p / Arya maQjuSriye kumAra BUtAya namaH
# # / / rgya gar skad du / / ma dhyan nta bi bham ga t'i k'a / / bod skad du / / dbus dang mtha' rnam-par-'byed-pa # 'i 'grel bshad /
uttama janaH hi prAyaSas gurum SradDA devatAm ca aByarcya karmasu pravartata / iti ayam api aham uttama janana mayam anuvartI maDya anta viBAga sUtra BAzyam
# 'jam dpal gzhon-nu # r gyur-pa #  la phyag 'tshal lo / / ya rabs dag ni phal-cher #  bla-ma #  dang dad-pa # 'i lha la mchod nas las rnams la 'jug ste / / dbus dang mtha' rnam-par-'byed-pa # 'i mdo rnam-pa # r bshad-pa # r 'dod-pa # s /
cikIrzuH tat praNetuH vaktuH ca pUjAm kRtvA tad arTa viBAgAya prayukta / iti pratipAdayan= Aha / SAstrasya asya praNetAram
# bdag la yang 'di ni ya rabs kyi tshul can no zhes shes-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir / / de mdzad-pa #  dang 'chad-pa #  la mchod nas / / de'i don rnam-par-dbye-ba # r zhugs so zhes rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / bstan-bcos #  'di ni rab mdzad-pa #  /
ityAdi / evam kRtvA kaH guNaH prApyate
# zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  smos so / / de-ltar #  byas-na #  yon-tan #  ci-zhig #  thob ce na /
guNavataH hita kAriNaH ca pUjayatAm ezAm puNyam upacIyate
# yon-tan-dang-ldan-pa #  dang phan 'dogs 'dogs-pa #  la mchod na bsod nams 'phel-ba # r 'gyur ro /
puNyaH upacite samAramBAt viGna vinAyakEH anupahata analpena prayAsena / samApayanti iti
# bsod nams 'phel na yang-dag-par #  rtsom pa la bar-chad #  dang bgegs kyis mi-tshugs-pa # r tshogs chung-ngu #  rdzogs-pa # r 'gyur ro /
aTavA praNetR praNeya pravacanAt sUtra praNetR vaktR vRttIzu / gOrava utpAdana arTam Aha / SAstrasya asya praNetAram / iti sarvam
# yang-na #  mdzad-pa # s gsungs-pa #  dang 'chad-pa # s bshad-pa #  yang-dag-par #  byin-pa # r bsnyad-pa # s / / mdzad-pa #  dang 'chad-pa #  dang mdo dang 'brel-ba #  la gus-pa-bskyed-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir / / bstan-bcos #  'di ni rab mdzad-pa #  /
tatra praNetR vacanAt sUtre gOravam utpadyate
# zhes-bya-ba #  thams-cad #  smos so / / de-la #  mdzad-pa # s bshad-pa # r bstan-pa # s mdo la gus-pa #  skye ste /
yasyAH asya kArikA SAstrasya Arya mEtreyaH praNetA
# 'di-ltar #  bstan-bcos #  tshig le'ur byas-pa # 'i mdzad-pa #  po ni 'phags-pa #  byams-pa #  ste /
sa ca eka jAti pratibanDAt sarva boDisattva aBijQA DAraNI pratisaMvid / samADi indriya kzAnti vimokzEH paramam pAram gataH sarvAsu / boDisattva BUmizu p / niHSezam api prahINa AvaraNaH
# de-yang #  skye-ba-gcig #  gis thogs-pa # 'i phyir / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i mngon-par-shes-pa #  dang gzungs dang so-so #  yang-dag-par #  rig-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang dbang dang bzod-pa #  dang rnam-par-thar-pa #  thams-cad-kyi #  dam-pa # 'i pha rol tu son pa / / byang-chub-sems-dpa'i-sa #  thams-cad-la #  sgrib-pa #  yang ma-lus-par-spangs-pa # 'o /
vaktR samAdAna dvAreNa vRttO gOravam utpadyate
# 'chad-pa # s yang-dag-par #  byin-pa # 'i sgo nas 'grel pa la gus-pa #  skye-bar-'gyur #  te /
vaktA punar atra AcAryA saFgaH tasmAt SrutvA AcArya danta vasu banDuH / tat BAzyam akarot
# 'di-la #  'chad-pa #  ni slob-dpon #  thogs med do / / de-la # s slob-dpon #  btsun pa dbyig gnyen gyis gsan nas 'di'i 'grel pa mdzad de /
tayoH uttaram aprajQAvatoH aBrAnti prativeDa DAraNa upadeSa sAmarTyAt / atra sUtra arTaH aBra antam upadizwaH iti vRttO gOravam utpadyate
# de gnyis kyang shes-rab #  mchog dang ldan-pa # s ma nor-ba # r rtogs-pa #  dang bzung-ba #  dang ston nus-pa # s 'dir mdo'i don ma nor-ba #  bstan to zhes 'grel pa la gus-pa #  skye ste /
evam ye pudgalam pramANIkurvanti tezAm sUtra vRttiH gOrava utpattiH
# de-ltar #  gang dag gang-zag #  tshad-ma # r byed-pa #  de-dag #  ni / / mdo dang 'grel pa la gus-pa #  skye'o /
ye ca Darma anusAriNaH tezAm sUtra vRttyoH SuBa arTA avaboDaH
# gang yang chos la ston-pa #  de-dag #  ni mdo dang 'grel pa'i don bzang-po #  khong du chud de /
jAte ca niScaye iyam praNetuH vaktuH ca pratItyA praBAvanA na tu
# nges-pa #  skyes na 'di mdzad-pa #  dang 'chad-pa #  yang rtogs-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba #  yin gyis /
tarka Agama mAtreNa praBAvanA iti praNetR vaktR gOrava utpattiH
# rtog ge dang lung tsam gyis rab-tu-phye-ba # r ni zad do zhes mdzad-pa #  dang 'chad-pa #  la gus-pa #  skye'o /
idam idAnIm vaktavyam / kIdRSam SAstra rUpam / SAstram kim iti ced nAmapada vyaQjana kAya praBAsA vijQaptayaH
# da-ni #  bstan-bcos #  kyi rang-bzhin #  ci-'dra-ba #  dang ci'i-phyir #  bstan-bcos #  zhes-bya-ba #  'di bshad-par-bya # 'o / / ming dang tshig-dang-yi-ge # 'i tshogs su snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-rig-pa #  rnams ni bstan-bcos #  so /
SAstram / aTa vA loka uttara jQAna prApaka Sabda viSeza praBAsA vijQaptayaH / SAstram / kaTam vijQaptayaH praNIyantaH ucyante vA
# yang-na #  'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i ye shes thob-par-byed-pa # 'i sgra'i khyad-par #  du snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-rig-pa #  rnams bstan-bcos #  so / / rnam-par-rig-pa #  rnams ji-ltar #  mdzad cing brjod ce na /
praNetR vijQapti praBa vat prajQaptInAm na atra dozaH / Sizya DArmikaH hi SIla samADi prajQA viSeza utpAdAt
# mdzad-pa #  dang 'chad-pa # 'i rnam-par-rig-pa #  las nyan-pa # 'i rnam-par-rig-pa #  rnams skye-ba # s 'di-la #  nyes-pa #  med do / / slob-ma #  'chos-pa # 'i phyir bstan-bcos #  te / / slob-ma # 'i 'chos-pa #  ni tshul-khrims #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang shes-rab #  kyi khyad-par #  bskyed-pa # 'i phyir /
kAya vAc manasA aMBAra anutpatI karmaNaH nivartate samBAra utpatti karmANi / ca pravartate
# lus dang ngag dang yid tshogs-pa # r mi-'byung-ba # 'i las las bzlog-pa #  dang tshogs-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i las la 'jug-pa # 'o /
aTa vA SAstra lakzaNasya SAsanAt SAstram
# yang-na #  bstan-bcos #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  du 'thad-pa # 'i phyir bstan-bcos #  te /
sva lakzaNam yat upadeSaH BAsamAna sarva kleSa prahANAya / nirantara dIrGa viviDa tIvra duHKa BItyAH ca durgateH BavAn ca
# lung-mnos-pa #  goms-par-byas-pa # s bag-chags-dang-bcas-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa-spong-ba # r 'gyur-ba #  dang-ba # r chad-med-pa #  yun-ring-ba # 'i sdug-bsngal-drag-po #  sna-tshogs #  kyis 'jigs-pa # 'i ngan-song #  rnams dang srid-pa #  las skyob pa gang-yin-pa #  de ni bstan-bcos #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  do /
santrAyate / tasmAt kleSa ripu SAsanAt Bava durgati santArAt ca SAstra lakzaNam
# de'i-phyir #  nyon-mongs-pa # 'i dgra 'chos-pa #  dang ngan-'gro #  dang srid-pa #  las skyob pas bstan-bcos #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  de /
etat ca dvayam api sarvasmin mahAyAne sarvasmin= ca tat vyAKyAne / vidyate na anyatra iti / atas etat SAstram / Aha ca / yat SAsti ca kleSa paripUn aSezAn
# de gnyis kyang theg-pa-chen-po #  thams-cad #  dang de bshad-pa #  thams-cad-la #  yod kyi gzhan la med de de'i-phyir #  'di ni bstan-bcos #  so / / de-la #  smras-pa #  / / nyon mongs dgra rnams ma lus 'chos-pa #  dang /
santrAyate durgatitaH BavAn ca
# ngan-'gro #  srid las skyob pa gang-yin-pa #  /
tad SAsanA tttrANa guNAt ca SAstram
# chos skyob yon-tan #  phyir na bstan-bcos #  te /
etat dvayam ca anya matezu na asti / asya iti
# gnyis po 'di dag gzhan gyi lugs la med / / 'di ni zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
kriyA anadvAreNa sapta vastu saFgrahasya
# theg-pa-gsum #  gyi sgo nas dngos-po #  bdun du bsdus-pa #  /
kleSa jQeya AvaraNa prahANa prApakasya maDya anta viBAga kArikA SAstrasya / hRdi sTita tvAt asya iti pratyakza upadeSaH
# nyon-mongs-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  spong-ba #  thob-pa #  dang bstan-bcos #  dbus dang mtha' rnam-par-'byed-pa # 'i tshig le'ur byas-pa #  'di ni sems-la-gnas-pa # 'i phyir dang 'di zhes mngon-sum-du #  bstan to /
praNetArm iti kartAram
# rab mdzad-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni byed-pa-po # 'o /
yadi api ayam DAtuH prApaNa arTaH taTA api praSabda saMyogAt / viSeza arTakaH drazwavyaH / uktam hi p / upasargeNa DAtvarTaH balAt anyaH pratIyate
# skad kyi dbyings 'di thob-par-byed-pa #  yin mod kyi / / 'on-kyang #  rab kyi sgra dang sgrogs na byed-pa # r lta ste / / skad dbyings don gyi stobs ldan yang / / nye-bar #  bsgyur-ba # s zil non 'gyur /
gaFgA salila mADuryam sAgareNa yaTA amBasA
# gang g'a'i chu ni mngar mod kyi / / rgya-mtsho # 'i chu ni ji bzhin no / / zhes bshad do /
sugata Atmajam iti
# bde gshegs nyid skyes zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
suzWu gataH sa vAsana kleSa AvaraNAt jQeya AvaraNAt ca apratizWitam / virvANam iti sugataH
# bag-chags-dang-bcas-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  las mi-gnas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # r shin-tu #  gshegs-pa # s bde-bar-gshegs-pa # 'o /
sa ca sarva vAsanA AvaraNa prahINaH sarvaTA sarva Darma avaboDa svarUpaH
# de-yang #  bag-chags #  kyi sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  spangs-pa #  / / chos-thams-cad #  rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  thugs-su-chud-pa # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo 'byor-ba #  thams-cad-kyi #  gnas-su-gyur-pa #  /
sarva viBUti ASraya BUta Niratna vat acintya praBAva vigrahaH / sarva sattvAnAm anABogena sarva arTa raNa samarTaH
# yid bzhin gyi nor-bu-rin-po-che #  ltar bsam-gyis-mi-khyab-pa # 'i mthu mnga' ste / / sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi don-thams-cad #  lhun-gyis-grub-pa # r mdzad-par-spyod-pa #  /
nirvikalpaka jQAna viSeza AtmakaH sugataH tat janita tvAt nirvikalpasya / jQAnasya / tasmAt tasmin vA jAtaH sugata AtmajaH
# rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyi khyad-par #  gyi bdag-nyid #  ni bde-bar-gshegs-pa # 'o / / de'i-bdag-nyid #  ni rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i deb zhin nyid de / / de-la # s rnam bar mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes-rab #  tu byung-ba # 'i phyir de-la # s sam / / der skye-ba # s na bde gshegs nyid skyes so /
aTavA sugata AtmanA jAtaH iti sugata AtmajaH
# yang-na #  bde-bar-gshegs-pa #  nyid-du #  skyes-pa # s / / bde gshegs nyid skyes te /
yaTA uktam sUtra antare jAtaH Bavati taTAgata vaMSe tad AtmakaH tu / pratilABAt iti
# mdo gzhan-las #  de'i-bdag-nyid #  kyi chos rab tu rnyed-pa # s / / de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # 'i gdung du skyes-pa #  yin no zhes ji-skad #  gsungs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
evam sati boDisattvasya daSamyAm BUmO pratizWitasya sarva AkAram / jQeyam vastu kara tala sTam iva Amalakam / tattvaMSuka avacCAdita locanasya iva ABAsam AyAti
# de-lta-bas-na #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  sa bcu pa la rab-tu-gnas-pa #  ni / / shes-bya'i-dngos-po # 'i rnam-pa-thams-cad #  sgyu ru ra lag-mthil #  du gzhag-pa #  / / dar lva srab mos g-yogs pa'i mig la snang-ba #  bzhin no /
BagavataH punar apanIta locana AvaraNasya iva iti ayam viSezaH
# bcom-ldan-'das #  kyi ni mig gi sgrib-pa #  bsal-ba #  bzhin te / / 'di ni khyad-par #  ro /
atra hi sugata Atmajasya SAstra praNetuH avaboDa sampad pradarSitA / lABa satkAra nirapekzasya SAstra praNetR tvena karuNA sampad
# 'dir ni bde-bar-gshegs-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  las skyes-pa # s / / bstan-bcos #  mdzad-pa #  de-kho-na #  thugs-su-chud-pa #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa # r bstan-pa #  dang rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  la mi-lta-ba # r bstan-bcos #  mdzad-pa # s /
prajQA sampad ca / vaktAram iti vyAKyAnasya kartAram / aByarhi eti sambaDyate / sugata Atmajam iti api iti apare / sa punar AryA asaFgaH / tasya hi idam SAstram aBivyaktam AKyAtam ca arya mEtreya aDizWAnAt / DarmasantAnena / ca iti samuccaye pAdapUraNe aDika vacane vA / anyAn api budDa boDisattvAn arcayitvA na kevalam praNetAram / vaktra AraQca iti / keByaH vaktAram / asmat AdiByaH iti / vayam AdiH yezAm te amada AdayaH teByaH asmad AdiByaH / anena AtmanaH upadeSasya amRzA tvam vyajyate / aByarhi eti aByarcya
# thugs rje phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  dang shes-rab #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa # r bstan-pa # 'o / / 'chad-pa #  ni bshad-pa # r byed-pa #  ste / / mngon-pa # r mchod ces bya-ba #  dang sbyar ro / / kha-cig #  na re bde gshegs nyid las skyes-pa #  zhes kyang bya'o zhe'o / / de ni 'phags-pa #  thogs med do / / de-la #  ni 'phags-pa #  byams-pa # 'i byin rlabs kyis na / / chos kyi rgyun gyis bstan-bcos #  'di mngon du gyur cing bshad do / / su la 'chad-pa #  zhe na / / bdag sogs la zhes-bya-ba #  ste / / bdag thog-mar #  byas-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  ni bdag la-sogs-pa #  ste / / 'di ni bdag-nyid-kyi #  mi-slu-ba #  las lung-mnos-pa # r ston to / / yang zhes-bya-ba #  ni bsdu-ba # 'am / / rtsa ba bskangs pa'am / / lhag-pa # 'i tshig ste / / mdzad-pa #  dang 'chad-pa #  nyi tshe la ma yin gyi / / sangs-rgyas #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  gang-yang-rung-ba #  dag la mchod-pa # r bya'o / / mngon mchod ces bya-ba #  ni rjed pa'o /
aBitas puratas sAkzAt iva sTitam
# mngon-pa # r zhes-bya-ba #  ni mdun nam mngon-sum #  dang 'dra-bar #  gnas-pa # 'o /
arhitvA arcayitvA kAya vAc manoBiH
# mchod-pa #  ni lus dang ngag dang yid kyis rjed pa'o /
SAstrasya praNetAram vaktAram ca aByarcya kim karizyasi iti Aha / yatIzye arTa vivecane iti / yatnam Arapsye arTa vivecane arTa vivareNe pRTak BAva karaNe vA / iyam ca nimitta arTA saptamI / arTa vivecana nimittam iti arTaH p / arTaH punar atra SAstra SarIram iti / ete saptArTAH hi asmin SAstre upadiSyante iti vacanAt / kim arTam idam SAstram praNItam
# bstan-bcos #  mdzad-pa #  dang 'chad-pa #  la mngon-pa # r mchod nas ci-zhig #  bya zhe na / / don rnams dbye phyir 'bad-pa # r bya / / zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / don dbye-ba # 'i phyir ram; don dgrol ba'i phyir ram / / so-so # r dbye-ba # 'i phyir bsgrim-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  'di ni rgyu'i don te / / don rnam-par-dbye-ba # 'i rgyur zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / don ni 'dir bstan-bcos #  kyi lus yin te zhes-bya-ba #  don bdun po 'di dag bstan-bcos #  'di-las #  'chad do zhes 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
budDAnAm BagavatAm samyak nirvikalpa jQAna utpAdana arTam / Darma nErAtmya deSanatayA nirvikalpa jQAna utpAdAt tad aByAsAt ca / niHSeza savAsana kleSa jQeya AvaraNa prahANam avApyate / ayam punar Darma nErAtByasya viroDa vAdaH yat sarva Darma rahita tA
# ci'i-phyir #  bstan-bcos #  'di bshad ce na sangs-rgyas #  bcom-ldan-'das #  rnams kyi rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes bskyed-pa # 'i phyir te / / chos-la-bdag-med-pa #  bstan-pa # s rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes bskyed-pa #  dang de goms-pa # s bag-chags-dang-bcas-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  ma-lus-par-spangs-pa #  thob-pa # r 'gyur ro /
Darma nErAtmyam / antar vyApAra puruza rahita tA ca Darma nErAtmyam iti atas tat pratizeDena
# chos-la-bdag-med-pa #  yang chos-thams-cad #  med-pa #  nyid chos-la-bdag-med-pa #  dang nang na byed-pa # 'i skyes-bu #  med-pa #  nyid chos-rnams #  la bdag-med-pa # 'o zhes mi-mthun-par-smra-ba #  de-dag #  bkag-pa # s /
taTABUta nErAtmya pratipAdana arTam SAstra AramBaH
# chos-la-bdag-med-pa #  yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  bstan-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir bstan-bcos #  brtsam mo /
lakzaNa AvaraNa Adizu apratipanna vipratipannAnAm samyak avaboDa utpAdanAt / apratipatti vipratipatti apanayana arTam iti anye / aTa vA paQcAkAra jQeyam lokaDAtu sattva Darma vineya upAya DAtu Atmake
# gzhan dag na re mtshan-nyid #  dang sgrib-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ma-rtogs-pa #  dang log-pa # r rtogs-pa #  rnams yang-dag-par-rtogs-pa #  skyed-pa # s ma-rtogs-pa #  rnams dang log-pa # r rtogs-pa #  bsal-ba # 'i phyir ro zhe'o / / yang-na #  'jig-rten-gyi-khams #  dang sems-can #  dang chos dang 'dul-ba #  dang thabs kyi bdag-nyid #  de /
pratyekam ananta praBeda tvAt durvijQeyam iti boDisattvAnAm
# shes-bya #  rnam lnga re-re #  la yang rab-tu-dbye-ba #  mtha'-yas-pa # 'i phyir shes-pa # r bya dka'o snyam-du #  /
yaH citta saFkocaH tat apanayana arTam Aha
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi sems-zhum-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de bstsal-ba # 'i phyir /
lakzaNam hi AvRtiH tattvam iti
# mtshan-nyid #  dang sgrib-pa #  dang de-kho-na #  zhes-bya-ba #  dag smos so /
tatra Aditas SAstra SarIram vyavasTApyate iti
# de-la #  thog-ma-kho-nar #  bstan-bcos #  kyi lus rnam-pa # r gzhag ste zhes-bya-ba #  la /
tatra iti SAstrasya arTa vivecane SAstre p / vA / Aditas iti praTamatas iti / SAstram vivaraNam
# de-la #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni bstan-bcos #  kyi don rnam-par-'byed-pa #  de-la # 'am / / bstan-bcos #  la'o / / thog-ma-kho-nar #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / dang-po-kho-nar #  ro / / bstan-bcos #  ni bshad-pa # r zad do /
tat SarIram saMkzepaH piNXa arTaH vA ASraya arTena vA SarIram
# de'i lus ni mdor-bsdus-pa # 'am / / don bsdus-pa # 'o / / gnas kyi don ni lus so /
yaTA hi bAhya ADyAtmika Ayatana ASrayaH kAyaH SarIram iti ucyate evam
# dper-na #  phyi dang nang gi skye-mched #  kyi gnas ni khog-pa #  ste / / lus zhes-bya-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  /
yAn arTAn niScitya SAstram pravartate te arTAH tasya SarIram / te ca saptyArTAH lakzaNa AdayaH / vyavasTApyate iti prajQApyate AKyAyate iti arTaH
# don gang dag la gnas te / / bstan-bcos #  la 'jug-pa'i-don #  de rnams ni de'i lus so / / de-dag #  kyang don bdun po dag ste / / mtshan-nyid #  la-sogs-pa #  dag go / / rnam-pa # r gzhag ces bya-ba #  ni bcas-pa #  ste /
nanu SAstra avaBoDena eva tat SarIram vijQAsyate iti nirarTakam AdO / tat vyavasTApanam
# bshad ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / bstan-bcos #  khong-du-chud-pa #  nyid kyis de'i lus shes-pa # r mi 'gyur ram / / de-bas-na #  thog-ma #  de rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  ni don med do /
na nirarTakam SizyA anugraha arTa tvAt
# slob-ma #  rnams la phan-gdags-pa # 'i phyir don-med-pa #  ma yin no /
gata arTaH hi SizyaH suKam vistaram ucyamAnam pratipAdyate / dRzwA BUmiH niHSaFkam aSva vAhanena iva na anyaTA / iti ete saptArTAH hi asmin SAstre upadiSyante
# slob-ma # s don khong du chud na rgyas-pa # r brjod kyang bde blag tu khong-du-chud-pa # r 'gyur te dkyus kyis bstan-pa # 'i rta thags-thogs #  med-pa # r rgyug-pa #  bzhin te / / gzhan-du #  ma yin no zhes-bya-ba #  don bdun po 'di dag bstan-bcos #  'di-las #  'chad do zhes-bya-ba #  la zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
itiH SAstra SarIra samApti arTaH / ete iti ye lakzaNa AdayaH uddizwAH / saptA iti saMKyA paryanta aDigama arTam upAdAnam / arTyante iti arTAH aDigamyante iti yAvat
# bstan-bcos #  kyi lus rdzogs so zhes-bya-ba #  ni tha-tshig #  go / / shes-par-bya-ba #  yin-pas #  don de khong-du-chud-pa # r bya-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / bdun po zhes-bya-ba #  ni grangs so / / 'di dag ces bya-ba #  ni mtshan-nyid #  la-sogs-pa #  smos-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  rnams so /
asmin SAstre iti maDya anta viBAga saMjQake
# bstan-bcos #  'di-las #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni dbus dang mtha' rnam-par-'byed-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
upadiSyante iti AKyAyante viniSciyante vA / yat uta iti taTA arTa pratipAdana nipAtaH / lakzaNam iti / lakzyante anena iti lakzaNam
# 'chad ces bya-ba #  ni bstan-pa # 'am gtan-la-'bebs-pa # 'o / / 'di-lta-ste #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni de'i don khong-du-chud-pa # r byed-pa # 'i tshig gi phrad do / / mtshan-nyid #  ces bya-ba #  ni / / 'dis mtshon par byed-pa # s mtshan-nyid #  do /
tat ca dviviDam saFkleSa lakzaNam vyavadAna lakzaNAn ca
# de-yang #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  te / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do /
tatra saFkleSa lakzaNam navaviDam
# de-la #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni rnam-pa #  dgu ste /
aBUta parikalpaH asti / iti AraBya yAvat / saptaDA BUta kalpanAt iti / SezeNa arDena vyavadAna lakzaNam AKyAtam / yadi lakzyante anena iti laksaNam iti evam sati lakzaNasya
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / ces bya-ba #  nas-bzung-ste #  / / rnam bdun yang dag min rtog las / / zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du # 'o / / lhag-ma #  ni rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  du bstan to / / gal-te #  'dis mtshon par byed-pa # s mtshan-nyid #  ces bya na /
saFkleSa vyavadAna BedaH Bavet iti na etat evam / svaBAvaH eva hi BAvAnAm lakzaNam
# de lta na ni mtshan-nyid #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  dang tha-dad-pa # r 'gyur ro zhe na / / de ni de lta ma yin te dngos-po #  rnams kyi rang-bzhin #  nyid mtshan-nyid #  de /
tat yaTA pRTivI DAtuH Kara lakzaNaH na ca Kara tvAt pRTivI DAtuH / pRTak asti iti / aTa vA lakzyate tat iti lakzaNam
# dper-na #  sa'i-khams #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  ni sra-ba #  ste / / sra-ba-nyid #  las sa'i-khams #  gud-na #  med-pa #  lta-bu # 'o; / / yang-na #  des mtshon par bya-ba # s mtshan-nyid #  de /
evam hi saFkleSaH vyavadAnaQca saFkleSa vyavadAna Atma tvena lakzyate iti / lakzaNam
# de-ltar #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  yang kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i bdag-nyid-kyis #  mtshon par bya-ba # s mtshan-nyid #  du 'gyur ro /
aTa vA dvayoH saFkleSa vyavadAnayoH lakzaNam dviviDam sva lakzaNaQca / sAmAnya lakzaNaQca / AvaraNam iti / AvRNoti kuSalAn DarmAn Avriyante anena kuSala DarmAH utpatti vibanDAt / iti AvaraNam / tat punar tripaQcASat prakAram / tattvam iti
# yang-na #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  gnyis las mtshan-nyid #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  te / / rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  dang spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  do / / sgrib-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni dge-ba'i-chos #  rnams la sgrib-par-byed-pa # 'am / / 'dis dge-ba'i-chos #  rnams bsgrib-pa # s sgrib-pa #  ste / / skye-ba #  la bgegs-byed-pa # 'i phyir sgrib-pa # 'o / / de-yang #  lnga bcu rtsa gsum mo /
tat eva idam tat tasya BAvaH tattvam aviparyAsaH iti arTaH
# de-kho-na #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'di nyid de yin-pas #  de'o / / de'i dngos-po #  ni de-kho-na #  ste / / phyin ci ma log ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
tat ca daSa prakAram p / vipakza prahANa arTaH pakzaH pratipakzaH / sa sArgaH / tad aByAsaH BAvanA
# de-yang #  rnam-pa-bcu # 'o / / mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  spangs-pa # 'i phyir / / phyogs ni gnyen-po #  ste de ni lam mo / / de goms-par-bya-ba #  ni bsgom-pa # 'o; /
avasTA tasya eva santAna utpatti viSezaH
# gnas-skabs #  ni de nyid rgyun gyis skye-ba # 'i khyad-par #  ro /
sA punar ekAnna viMSati prakArA gotra avasTA AdikA
# de-yang #  rnam-pa # r bcu dgu ste / / rigs kyi gnas la-sogs-pa # 'o /
Palasya lABaH Pala prAptiH
# 'bras-bu #  thob-pa #  ni 'bras-bu #  rnyed-pa # 'o /
tat punar paQcadaSa prakAram vipAka Pala Adi / yAnAnuttarTam iti / gamyate anena iti yAnam / yAnat ca tadA anuttarya Qceti yAnAn uttaryam
# de-yang #  rnam-pa #  bco lnga ste / / rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / theg-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dis 'gro-ba # s theg-pa #  ste / / de ni theg-pa #  yang yin la bla-na-med-pa #  yang yin-pas #  theg-pa #  bla-na-med-pa # 'o /
tat punar triviDam pratipattya anuttarya Adi
# de-yang #  rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / bsgrub-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
saptamaH arTaH iti niyama arTam anukramArTaQca Aha / etAvantaH eva arTAH nirdiSyante na atas anyaH iti
# don bdun pa zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / nges-pa'i-don #  dang go-rims #  kyi don-du #  smos-pa #  ste / / don 'di rnams 'dir bshad kyi de-la # s gzhan ma yin no /
anukramaH punar ayam loka uttara jQAna anukUlya arTaH
# yang go-rims #  'di ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i ye shes dang mthun-pa # 'i phyir te /
taTA hi boDisattvena aDimukti caryA BUmi sTitena SIla pratizWitena
# 'di-ltar #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  mos-pas-spyod-pa #  la gnas-pa #  / / tshul-khrims #  la rab-tu-gnas-pa # s /
praTamam saFkleSa vyavadAna kuSalena Bavitavyam
# thog-mar #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  la mkhas-pa # r bya'o /
tatas kuSalAnAm DarmANAm yasya yat AvaraNam tasya tat jQeyam
# de'i-'og-tu #  dge-ba'i-chos #  rnams kyi gang-gis #  sgrib-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de shes-pa # r bya ste /
tasya aprahArANAt vimukteH asamBavAt avijQAnaQca prahAtum na Sakyate / doza darSanAt
# de ma spangs na rnam-pa # r grol mi srid la / / rnam-pa # r mi shes na yang nyes-pa #  ma-mthong-ba # s spong mi nus so /
tatas tad AvaraNAt yena Alambanena cittam vimucyate tattva tvam veditavyam
# de'i-'og-tu #  sgrib-pa #  de-la # s dmigs-pa #  gang-gis #  sems rnam-par-grol-ba # r 'gyur-ba #  de ni de-kho-na #  yin par khong-du-chud-pa # r bya'o /
tatas tena AlamBanena tad AvaraNasya yena prayogena kzayaH Bavati sA
# de'i-'og-tu #  dmigs-pa #  des sgrib-pa #  de sbyor-ba #  gang-gis #  zad-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  de gnyen-po-bsgom-pa # r shes-pa # r bya'o /
pratipakza BAvanA jQeyA / tatas tasyAm pratipakza BAvAyAm vipakza hAnyA pratipakza vRdDyA / cA avasTA jQeyA
# de'i-'og-tu #  gnyen-po-bsgom-pa #  ni de'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  'bri-ba #  dang gnyen-po #  'phel-ba #  la gnas-skabs #  su shes-pa # r bya ste / / rigs kyi gnas-skabs #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
tatas loka uttara Darma aBimuKIkaraNam PalAni srotaH apatti Pala AdIni / veditavyAni
# de'i-'og-tu #  'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i chos mngon-du-gyur-pa #  ni 'bras-bu #  rnams te / / rgyun-du-zhugs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  la-sogs-pa # r shes-pa # r bya'o /
sarvam api etat srottara tvAt SrAvaka AdiBiH sADAraNam boDisattvAnAm / yaTA uktam sUtre
# de-dag #  thams-cad #  kyang bla-ma #  dang bcas-pa # s byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams dang nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  dang thun mong ste / / mdo las ji-skad-du #  /
sa pravrajitaH SrAvaka SikzA AcAra gocara samudAcAram api Sikzate
# rab-tu-byung-ba #  de nyan-thos #  kyi bslab-pa #  dang cho-ga #  dang spyod yul dang yang-dag-par #  spyod-pa #  la yang slob po /
pratyekabudDa SikzA AcAra gocara samudAcAram api Sikzate
# rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi bslab-pa #  dang cho-ga #  dang spyod yul dang yang-dag-par #  spyod-pa #  la slob po /
boDisattva SikzA AcAra gocara samudAcAram api Sikzate
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i bslab-pa #  dang cho-ga #  dang spyod yul dang yang-dag-par #  spyod-pa #  la yang slob po zhes gsungs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
boDisattvAnAm tvA anuttaryam asADAraNam / saptamaH arTaH Anuttaryam
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi ni bla-na-med-pa #  thun-mong-ma-yin-pa #  ste don bdun pa bla-na-med-pa # 'o /
anyaH tu Aha / saFkleSa vyavadAna lakzaNe kOSala utpAdana arTam AdO laksaNam
# gzhan na re kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  la mkhas-par-bya-ba #  bskyed-pa # 'i phyir thog-mar #  mtshan-nyid #  do /
tatra yaH saFkleSaH tad AvaraNam
# de-la #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni / / sgrib-pa # 'o /
yat vyavadAnam tat tattvam
# rnam-par-byang-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni de-kho-na # 'o /
AvaraNa prahANam ca tattva aDigamAt Bavati iti atas AvaraNa tattvam
# de-kho-na #  nyid khong-du-chud-pa # s sgrib-pa-spong-ba # r 'gyur te / / de'i-phyir #  sgrib-pa #  dang de-kho-na # 'o /
tat prahANa upAya pradarSana arTam tatas sa parivAraH pratipakzaH mArgaH
# de spang-ba # 'i thabs bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / de'i-'og-tu #  gnyen-po #  'khor dang bcas-pa #  ni lam mo /
tasya mArgasya Adi maDya antezu mRdu maDya aDimAtra praBeda pradarSana arTam
# lam de'i thog-ma #  dang-ba # r ma dang tha-ma # l chung-ngu #  dang 'bring dang chen-po #  rab-tu-dbye-ba # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir de'i-gnas #  skabs so /
tatra avasTA / avasTA anurUpam Palam Avahati iti tat anantaram Palam
# gnas-skabs #  dang mthun-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  thob-par-byed-pa # s / / de'i-'og-tu #  'bras-bu # 'o /
etat ca sarvam boDisattvasya SrAvaka Adi sADAraNam iti
# de-dag #  thams-cad #  kyang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  dang nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  dang thun mong ste /
asADAraNa mahAyAna naya prakASana arTam yAnAn uttaryam iti / apare punar AhuH
# de-bas-na #  thun-mong-ma-yin-pa #  dang theg-pa-chen-po'i-tshul #  rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir bla-na-med-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  zer ro /
sat asat lakzaNa jQApana arTam praTamatas lakzaNam AKyAtam
# gzhan dag na re yod-pa #  dang med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir thog-mar #  mtshan-nyid #  bshad do /

# mtshan-nyid #  shes-nas #  sgrib-pa-spang-ba # r bya-ba #  dang de-kho-na #  mngon-sum-du-bya-ba # s de'i-'og-tu #  sgrib-pa #  dang de-kho-na # 'o /
tayoH ca prahANa sAkzAtkaraNayoH ayam upAyaH iti pratipakza BAvanA
# de gnyis spang-ba #  dang mngon du bya-ba # 'i thabs ni 'di yin te / / gnyen-po-bsgom-pa # 'o /

tat kRtaQca prahANam Palam
# des spang-bar-bya-ba #  ni 'bras-bu # 'o /
tat anantaram yAna anuttaryam iti prakASana arTam ayam anukramaH iti
# de'i-'og-tu #  theg-pa #  bla-na-med-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba # r rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir 'di ni go-rims #  so zhes zer ro /
anyat ca sattvasya sadasat Darma saMmoha apavAda samAropa prahANa arTam / lakzaNa nirdeSaH
# gzhan-yang #  sems-pa #  yod-pa #  dang med-pa # 'i chos la rmongs nas / / skur-pa-'debs-pa #  dang sgro-'dogs-pa #  spang-ba # 'i phyir mtshan-nyid #  bshad do /
prahINa saMmohasya AvaraNa kOSala arTam AvaraNam

# de-kho-na #  rab-tu-rtogs-pa #  bsgoms-pa # s sgrib-pa-spong-ba # r 'gyur-ba # s de-kho-na # 'i 'og-tu #  gnyen-po-bsgom-pa # 'o /
tat praBeda kOSala arTam avasTA
# de'i dbye-ba #  la mkhas-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir gnas-skabs #  so /

# gnas-skabs #  kyis 'bras-bu #  rab-tu-phye-ba # s de-la #  mkhas-par-bya-ba #  bskyed-pa # 'i phyir gnas-skabs #  kyi 'og-tu #  'bras-bu # 'o /
sarvam etat mahAyAnam Agamya iti yAnAn uttaryam ante nirdizwam / tatra lakzaNam AraByAha
# de-dag #  thams-cad #  kyang theg-pa-chen-po #  la brten-pa # s theg-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  tha-ma # r bshad do snyam mo / / de-la #  mtshan-nyid #  las brtsams nas /
aBUta parikalpaH asti dvayam tatra na vidyate / SUnyatA vidyate tu atra tasyAm api sa vidyate iti
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / de-la #  gnyis po yod ma yin / / stong-pa-nyid #  ni 'di-la #  yod / / de-la #  yang ni de yod do /
tatra iti lakzaNa AvaraNa Adi saptArTezu nirdizwezu lakzaNam aDikRtya uddiSya Aha / aBUtaparikalpaH asti iti / yaTA uddiSaH taTA nirdeSaH iti kRtvA / lakzaNaQca prAk uddizwa mataH tasya eva SezeByaH nirdeSaH prAc AraByate / kecid virunDanti sarva DarmAH sarvaTA niHsvaBAvAH SaSa viSANa vat
# zhes-bya-ba # r gsungs so zhes-bya-ba #  la / / de-la #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mtshan-nyid #  dang sgrib-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dngos-po #  bdun smos-pa #  dag gi nang nas mtshan-nyid #  las brtsams nas de'i dbang du mdzad de / / de'i-phyir #  / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / ces bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  gsungs so / / ji-ltar #  bstan-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  bshad de / / thog-mar #  mtshan-nyid #  bstan-pa # s de'i-phyir #  lhag-ma #  rnams pas de nyid bshad-pa #  sngar brtsam mo / / la-la #  dag chos-thams-cad #  ri-bong-gi-rva #  ltar rang-bzhin #  ye med do /
iti atas sarva apavAda pratizeDa arTam Aha
# snyam-du #  sems-pa #  de'i-phyir #  thams-cad-la #  skur ba dgag-pa # 'i don-du #  /
aBUta parikalpaH asti iti

svaBAvataH iti vAkyaSezaH
# rang-bzhin #  gyi zhes-bya-ba #  tshig gi lhag-ma # 'o /
nanu evam sUtra viroDaH sarva DarmAH SUnyAH iti SAstre vacanAt / na asti viroDaH yasmAt
# de-ltar-na #  mdo las chos-thams-cad #  stong-pa # 'o zhes bshad-pa # s / / mdo dang mi 'gal lam zhe na / / mi 'gal-te #  'di-ltar #  /
dvayam tatra na vidyate / aBUta parikalpaH hi grAhya grAhaka svarUpa rahitaH SUnyaH ucyate na tu / sarvaTA niHsvaBAvaH
# de-la #  gnyis po yod ma yin / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i ngo bo dang bral-ba # s stong-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i rang-bzhin #  ye med-pa #  ni ma yin te /
atas na sUtra viroDaH
# de'i-phyir #  mdo dang mi 'gal lo /
yadi evam dvayam SaSa vizANa vat sarvaTA na asti
# gal-te #  de-ltar #  gnyis po ni ri-bong-gi-rva #  ltar ye med la /
aBUta parikalpaH ca paramArTataH svaBAvataH asti evam / SUnyatA aBAva prasaFgaH
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun-tu-rtog-pa #  ni / / don-dam-pa # r rang-bzhin-gyis #  yod-na #  / / de lta na ni stong-pa-nyid #  med-pa # r 'gyur ro zhe na /
na etat evam yasmAt a / SUnyatA vidyate tu atra / iyam eva hi SUnyatA yA grAha grAhaka rahita tA BUta parikalpasya iti na / SUnya tAyAH nAstitvam Bavati
# de ni de lta ma yin te 'di-ltar #  / / stong-pa-nyid #  ni 'di-la #  yod / / yang dag ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  la gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  med-pa #  nyid gang-yin-pa #  de stong-pa-nyid #  yin-pas #  stong-pa-nyid #  med-pa # r mi 'gyur ro /
yat yat vayayA SUnyatA sA ca aBUta parikalpe asti kasmAt vayam amuktAH
# gal-te #  gnyis po med-pa #  stong-pa-nyid #  yin la / / de-yang #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun-tu-rtog-pa #  la yod-na #  / / ci'i-phyir #  bdag-cag #  ma grol /
vidyamAnA ca kasmAt na gRhyate iti saMSaya apanayana arTam / tasyAm api sa vidyate / iti Aha
# yod-na #  yang ci'i-phyir #  ma rtogs snyam pa'i dogs-pa #  bsal-ba # 'i phyir / / de-la #  yang ni de yod do / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs te /
yasmAt SUnyatAyAm api aBUta parikalpaH vidyate tasmAt BavantaH na / muktAH / atas eva ca samalatvAt na prasanna abDAta vat gRhyate / aTa vA citta cEtteByaH anyatra rUpa AdayaH dravya tvena santi iti yat darSanam / tat pratizeDa arTam Aha
# 'di-ltar #  stong-pa-nyid #  la yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  yod-pa # s de'i-phyir #  khyed ma grol lo / / de-bas-na #  dri-ma #  dang bcas-pa # s chu'i-khams #  dangs pa bzhin rtogs-pa # r mi rung ngo / / yang-na #  sems-can #  dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams dang gzugs dang rdzas nyid-du #  yod-pa # r gang dag lta-ba #  de dgag-pa # 'i phyir /
aBUta parikalpaH asti
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod /
dravyataH / na asti rUpam tat vyatiriktam dravyataH iti / kim kAraNam / yasmAt / dvayaMtatra na vidyate
# ces gsungs te de nyid rdzas su yod do / / gzugs ni de-la # s logs-shig #  na yang med la / / rdzas su yang med do / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
na hi aBUta parikalpaH kasyacid grAhakaH na api kenacid gRhyate
# 'di-ltar #  de-la #  gnyis po yod ma yin / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  ni ci la yang 'dzin-pa #  ma yin / / sus kyang gzung-bar-bya-ba #  ma yin gyi /
kim tarhi grAhya grAhaka tvam BAva mAtram eva
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  dang bral-ba # 'i dngos-po #  tsam nyid de /
yatas vijQAnAt bahI rUpa AdayaH na gRhyante / svapna Adi vat vijQAnam rUpa Adi ABAsam uta pdyate / na ca yat yasya kAraNam tat aBAve tasya utpattiH yujyate
# 'di-ltar #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  las phyi-rol #  na gzugs la-sogs-pa #  gzung-ba #  med-pa # r rmi-lam #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  / / gzugs la-sogs-pa # r snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung ngo / / gal-te #  rgyu yin na de med-pa # r de 'byung-ba # r mi rung ngo /
tasmAt nirAlambanam eva svapna AdO= iva
# de'i-phyir #  dmigs-pa-med-pa #  nyid de / / da rmi-lam #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin no /
anyatra api sva bIja paripAkAt arTa ABAsam vijQAnam utpadyate iti / avaseyam
# gzhan la yang rang-gi-sa-bon #  yongs-su-smin-pa #  las don-du #  snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung-ba # r shes-pa # r bya'o /
grAhya aBAve grAhakasya aBAvAt grAhye asati grAhakaH Bavitum na
# gzung-ba #  med na 'dzin-pa #  med-par-'gyur-ba # s gzung-ba #  med na 'dzin-pa #  yod-pa # r mi rung ste /
yujyate / tasmAt na rUpam aBUta parikalpAt pRTak asti
# de-bas-na #  gzugs ni yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun-tu-rtog-pa #  las gud-na #  yod-pa #  ma yin no /
yadi tarhi grAhya BAvaH tena viSudDi Alambana aBAvAt mokza aBAvaH
# gal-te #  gzung-ba #  med na de'i-phyir #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i dmigs-pa-med-pa # s thar-pa #  yang med-pa # r 'gyur ro zhe na /
na etat evam yasmAt / SUnyatA vidyate tu atra / tu SabdaH yasmAt arTaH
# de ni de lta ma yin te / / 'di-ltar #  / / stong-pa-nyid #  ni 'di-la #  yod / / ni zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni gang-gi-phyir #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
SUnyatA hi vuSudDyA AlambanA
# stong-pa-nyid #  ni rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ste /
sA ca grAhya grAhaka rahita tA aBUta prEkalpe asti iti na mokza aBAvaH
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  dang bral-ba-nyid #  de / / de-yang #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  la yod-pa # s thar-pa #  med-pa # r mi 'gyur ro /
yadi aBUta parikalpe asti sA vidyamAnA kimarTam na gRhyate
# gal-te #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun du rtog-pa #  la yod-na #  / / de yod-pa # s ci'i-phyir #  mi rtogs she na /
aBUta parikalpa AvRta tvAt na gRhyate AkASanEH mAlya vat na tu asattvAt / iti pratipAdayan= Aha
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # s bsgribs-pa # s nam-mkha' #  dri-ma-med-pa #  bzhin-du #  rtogs-pa # r mi rung gi med-pa #  ni ma yin no zhes bstan-pa # 'i phyir; de-la #  yang ni de yod do zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so /
tasyAm api sa vidyate iti / aTa vA sarva apavAda pratizeDa arTam Aha p / aBUtaparikalpaH asti iti / na sarvam asat na api sat Atmakam vijQAna pariNAmAt manA asti iti kRtvA
# yang-na #  thams-cad-la #  skur ba 'debs-pa #  dgag-pa # 'i phyir / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / ces bya-ba #  gsungs te / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  gyur ba'i bdag-nyid #  yod-pa # s / / thams-cad-med-pa #  yang ma yin bdag-nyid #  yod-pa #  yang ma yin no /
ye tu manyante yaTA eva rUpa AdayaH praKyAyante taTA iva aBUta parikalpAt / svaBAvataH pRTak vidyante iti tAn pratyAha
# gang dag sems-pa #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  ji-ltar #  snang-ba #  de-ltar #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  las logs-shig #  na rang-bzhin #  du yod do zhes /
aBUta samAropa pratizeDa arTam
# yod-pa-ma-yin-pa #  la sgro-'dogs-pa #  dgag-pa # 'i don-du #  de'i-phyir #  /
dvayam tatra na vidyate iti
# de-la #  gnyis po yod ma yin /
aBUta parikalpa mAtram vidyate iti aBiprAyaH
# zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  tsam yod-pa # r dgongs-pa # 'o /
kenacid dvayoH aBAvaH vaH vnaDyA putra vat Ceda rUpaH gRhyate / anyEH antar vyApAra puruza rahita tA DarmANAm SUnyate ati ucyate / atas SUnyatA apavAda pratizeDa arTam BUta nErAtmya KyApana arTa QcAha
# kha-cig #  gnyis po med-pa #  ni mo-gsham-gyi-bu #  bzhin-du #  dngos-po #  med de zhes chad-pa # 'i dngos-po # 'i ngo bor 'dzin-pa #  dang gzhan dag nang na byed-pa # 'i skyes-bu #  med-pa #  nyid ni / / chos-rnams #  kyi stong-pa-nyid #  do zhes smra-ba #  de'i-phyir #  / / stong-pa-nyid #  du skur-pa-'debs-pa #  dgag-pa # 'i don dang bdag-med-pa #  yang-dag-par-bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
SUnyatA vidyate tu atra iti
# stong-pa-nyid #  ni 'di-la #  yod ces bya-ba #  gsungs so /
yadi aBUta parikalpe SUnyatA asti evam sati sarva prANinAm aprayatnena / mokza prasaFgaH / na asya etat yasmAt / tasyAm api sa vidyate / na hi aviSoDitAyAm SUnyatAyAm mokzaH asti saFklizwA ca mahatA yatnena / viSoDyate iti na asti ayatnena mokzaH
# gal-te #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  la stong-pa-nyid #  yod-na #  de lta na ni / / bsgrim mi-dgos-pa # r srog-chags #  thams-cad #  thar bar 'gyur ro zhe na / / de lta ma yin te 'di-ltar #  / / de-la #  yang ni de yod do / / stong-pa-nyid #  kyang rnam-pa # r ma sbyangs kyi bar-du #  thar-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir te / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r gyur-pa #  ni / / 'bad-pa #  chen-po # s rnam-pa # r sbyang dgos-pa # s 'bad-pa #  ma-byas-pa # r thar-pa #  med do /
aTa vA lakzaNam saFkleSa vyavadAna aBiDAnAt anyat na asti iti atas / saFkleSa vyavadAna lakzaNa pradarSana arTam Aha
# yang-na #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  dag gi mtshan-nyid #  brjod-pa #  las gzhan med-pa # s de'i-phyir #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  bstan-pa'i-don #  du /
aBUta parikalpaH asti / iti vistaraH / aBUta parikalpa svaBAvaH saMkleSaH BrAnti lakzaNa tvAt
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / ces rgya-cher #  gsungs so / / 'khrul-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyi phyir / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'o /
kaTam etat jQAtavyam BrAnti lakzaNam iti
# 'di 'khrul-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  du ji-ltar #  shes-pa # r bya zhe na /
yena / dvayam tatra na vidyate
# 'di-ltar #  de-la #  gnyis po yod ma yin /
sva Atmani aviDyamena grAhya grAhaka AkAreNa pratyAnAt / BrAnti svarUpeNa jQayate
# bdag-nyid #  du med-pa # r gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r snang-ba # s 'khrul-ba # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du mngon ngo /
edAnim vyavadAna svarUpa pradarzane arTamAH / SUnyatA vidyate tu atra / iti / SUnya tA svaBAvaH hi vyavadAnam dvaya aBAva svaBAva tvAt / atra ca SUnyatA praBAvita tvAt mArga niroDayoH api grahaNam veditavyam
# da-ni #  rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i ngo bo brtag-pa # 'i phyir / / stong-pa-nyid #  ni 'di-la #  yod / / ces bya-ba #  gsungs so / / gnyis po med-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  yin pa'i phyir / / stong-pa-nyid #  kyi rang-bzhin #  ni rnam-pa #  byang-ba # 'o / / stong-pa-nyid #  kyis rab-tu-phye-ba # s lam dang 'gog-pa #  dag kyang 'dir bsdu-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
saFkleSa pakzAt eva vyavadAna pakzaH mArgayitavyaH na punar pRTaktvam / asyAH asti iti pradarSana arTam Aha atra iti
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i phyogs nyid las rnam-par-byang-ba'i-phyogs #  nyid btsal bar bya-ba # 'i rang-gi-rgyud #  gud-na #  med-pa # r rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir 'di-la #  zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so /
yadi dvayam na asti kaTam tasyAm vidyamAnAyAm lokaH BrAntaH iti Aha / tasyAm api sa vidyate iti
# gal-te #  gnyis po med na ci'i-phyir #  de yod-pa # r 'jig-rten #  'khrul-ba # r gyur zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  de-la #  yang ni de yod do zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs te /
grAhya grAhaka vikalpaH hasti Adi AkAra SUnya mAyAyAm iva / hasti AkAra AdayaH
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'o / / sgyu-ma #  ni gang po che la-sogs-pa # s stong yang / / glang-po-che #  la-sogs-pa # r snang-ba #  lta-bu # 'o /
aBUtam asmin dvayam parikalpyate anena vA iti aBUta parikalpaH
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  gnyis po de-la # 'am / / des yongs-su-rtog-pa # s yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  gnyis por yongs-su-rtog-pa # s yang dag ma yin kun rtog-pa # 'o /
aBUta vacanena ca yaTA ayam parikalpyate grAhya grAhaka tvena taTA / na asti iti pradarSayati / parikalpa vacanena tu arTaH yaTA parikalpyate taTA arTaH na viDyate iti / pradarzayati / evam asya grAhya grAhaka vinirmuktam lakzaNam paridIpitam Bavati / kaH punar asO
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i tshig gis ni / / ji-ltar #  'di-la #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r kun rtog-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  med-pa # r ston to / / kun rtog-pa # 'i tshig gis ni don ji-lta-bu # r kun rtog-pa #  don de-lta-bu # r yod-pa #  ma yin zhes ston te / / de-ltar #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  las rnam-par-grol-ba #  de'i mtshan-nyid #  bshad-pa #  yin no /
atIta anAgata vartamAnA hetu Pala BUtAH trEDAtukAH anAdi kAlikA / nirvANa paryavasAnAH saMsAra anurUpAH citta cEttA
# de-yang #  gang yin zhe na sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  dang da-ltar #  gyi dang rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # r gyur-pa #  dang khams-gsum-pa #  dang thog-ma-med-pa # 'i dus can dang mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i mthar-thug-pa #  dan / / 'khor-ba # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa #  dag ni /
aviSezeNa aBUta parikalpaH / viSezeNa p / tu grAhya grAhaka vikalpaH
# khyad-par-med-pa # r yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'o / / khyad-par #  ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'o /
tatra grAhya vikalpaH arTa sattva pratiBAsam vijQAnam
# de-la #  gzung-ba # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni; don dang sems-can #  du snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o /
grAhaka vikalpaH Atma vijQapti pratiBAsam
# 'dzin-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni bdag dang rnam-par-rig-pa # r snang-ba # 'o /
dvayam grAhyam grAha kaQceti / tatra grAhyam rUpa Adi
# gnyis po ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  gzung-ba #  ni gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'o /
grAhakam cakzUH vijQAna Adi
# 'dzin-pa #  ni mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
grAhya grAhaka BAvena virahita tA vivikta tA hi aBUta parikalpasya / SanyatA / na tu aBUta parikalpaH api aBAvaH yaTA SUnyA rajjuH sarpa svaBAvena atat / svaBAva tvAt sarva kAlam SUnyA na tu rajju svaBAvena taTA iha api
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i dngos-po #  dang bral-ba-nyid #  de / / dben-pa #  nyid ni yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i stong-pa-nyid #  yin gyi / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  yang med-pa #  ni ma yin te / / dper-na #  thag-pa #  ni sprul pa'i dngos-po #  stong ste / / de'i-rang-bzhin #  ma-yin-pa # s dus-thams-cad-du #  stong-pa-nyid #  yin gyi / / thag-pa # 'i dngos-po #  ni ma yin te / / 'dir yang de-bzhin #  no /
tasyAm api sa vidyate iti aBUta parikalpaH
# de-la #  yang ni de yod do zhes-bya-ba #  ni yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  ste /
evam hi Agantuka AvaraNa upaklizwa tvAt tat agrahaNam uktam ap DAtu Adi vat iti
# de-ltar #  glo-bur #  gyi sgrib-pa # s nyon-mongs-pa # 'i phyir / / de chu khams la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  rtogs-pa # r mi rung ngo zhes bstan-pa #  yin no /
evam yat yatra na asti tat tena SUnyam iti yaTABUtam samanupaSyati iti
# de-ltar #  gang na gang med-pa #  de ni / / des stong-pa # r yang-dag-par #  rjes su mthong ngo zhes-bya-ba #  la /
kim kutra na asti
# ci-zhig #  gang na med ce na /
aBUta parikalpe dvayam
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  la gnyis po ste /
atas aBUta parikalpam dvayena SUnyam paSyati
# de'i-phyir #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  la gnyis kyis stong-pa # r mthong ngo /
yat punar atrA avaSizwam tat sat / kim punar iha avaSizwam
# 'di-la #  lhag-ma #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni yod-pa #  de 'di-la #  lhag-ma #  gang yin zhe na /
aBUta parikalpaH SUnyatA ca / tat uBayam iha asti iti anADyAya Aropa apavAdena paSyan yaTABUtam
# yang dag ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  stong-pa-nyid #  dang de-gnyi-ga #  yang 'dir yod-pa # r ma skur ba dang sgro-btags-pa #  med-pa # r mthong na yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  rab tu shes so /
prajAnAti / tatra aBUta parikalpe advaya darSanAt anaDyAropaH
# de-la #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  la gnyis po med-pa # r mthong-ba # 'i phyir sgro mi 'dogs so /
aBUta parikalpasya SUnyatAH ca astitva darSanAt anapavAdaH / aviparItam SUnyatA lakzaNam udBAvitam Bavati / yat SUnyam tasya sat BAvAt yena SUnyam tasya tatra aBAvAt / sarva BAve sarva aBAve vA na aviparItam SUnyatA lakzaNam / SUnyatAyAH eva aBAva prasaFgAt / na SUnya saMjQA asatyAm SUunyatAyAm yujyate / DarmatAyAH hi BAvAyAt tattvAt anitya tva Adi vat / dvayam asti iti SUnyatA BAvaH / yadi SaSa vizANa kalpanena dvayam kaTam tena aBUta parikalpasya / SUnyatA samBavaH / anyena hi anyasya SUunyatAH dRzwAH yaTA BikzuBiH vihArasya / na etat evam / yaTA rajjuH mAyA vA sva Atmani avidyamAnena sarpa AkAreNa puruza AdinA / praBAsate
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  dang stong-pa-nyid #  yod-pa # r mthong-ba # 'i phyir te / / skur-pa #  mi 'debs te / / stong-pa-nyid #  gang-yin-pa #  de yod-pa #  dang gang-gis-stong-pa #  de de-la #  med-pa # 'i phyir / / stong-pa-nyid #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r bstan-pa #  yin no / / thams-cad-med-pa # 'am thams-cad-yod-pa #  ni stong-pa-nyid #  kyang mtshan-nyid #  phyin-ci-log #  yin te / / stong-pa-nyid #  med-pa # r 'gyur ro / / stong-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  med na stong-pa-nyid #  du mi rung ste / / chos-nyid #  ni dngos-po #  la rag lus pa'i phyir mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin no / / gnyis po yod do zhe na / / stong-pa-nyid #  med-pa # r 'gyur ro / / gal-te #  gnyis po ni ri bong gi ra dang 'dren yang ji-ltar-de # s yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  stong ste /
tatra kasyacid grAha nirvartana arTam sarpa puruza AdiBiH ca SUnya iti ucyate / evam aBUta parikalpaH api sva Atmani avidyamAnena grAhya grAhaka AkAreNa / praKyAyamAnaH bAlAnAm tat grAha aBiniveSati Ajana arTam dvayena / SUnyam iti ucyate p / na SUnyam nA api ca AcA SUnyam / kim arTam asO SlokaH ArabDaH iti
# dper-na #  dge slong rnams kyis gtsug lag khang bzhin-du #  gzhan gyis gzhan stong-pa # r mthong zhe na; dper-na #  thag-pa #  la'am sgyu-ma #  la bdag-nyid-kyis #  med-pa # r sbrul gyi rnam-pa #  dang skyes-bu #  la-sogs-pa #  lta-bu # r snang-ba #  de-la #  kha-cig #  'dzin-pa #  bzlog-pa # 'i phyir / / sbrul dang skyes-bu #  la-sogs-pa # s stong ngo zhes brjod-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun du rtog-pa #  la yang bdag-nyid-kyis #  med-pa # r gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r snang-ba #  de-la #  byis-pa #  rnams 'dzin cing mngon-par-zhen-pa #  dor-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir gnyis kyis ston zhes bshad do / / stong-pa #  ma yin mi stong min / / zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshigs-su-bcad-pa #  'di ci'i-phyir #  brtsams she na /
sarvasya saMskRtasya asaMskRtasya ca dvaya rahita tA AjQApana arTam
# 'dus byas dang 'dus-ma-byas #  thams-cad #  gnyis dang bral-ba-nyid #  du shes-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro /
evam ca hi ekAnta pratikzepeNa sarvam idam na SUnyam na aSUnyam iti / prajQApAramitA pAWA aBiprAyata AvizkRtA Bavati / anyaTA pUrva apara virudDam etat syAt
# de-ltar #  mtha' gcig bkag-pa # s 'di thams-cad #  stong-pa #  yang ma yin mi stong-pa #  yang ma-yin-pa #  zhes shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i nang nas bshad-pa # 'i dgongs-pa #  bstan-pa #  yin no / / gzhan-du-na #  ltag 'og 'gal-ba # r 'gyur ro /
kiQca maDyamA pratipad prakASana arTam
# gzhan-yang #  dbu-ma'i-lam #  rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir te /
anyaTA ekAntika SUnyatA eva aSani antaH vA syAt
# gzhan-du-na #  ni gcig-tu #  stong-pa #  kho-na # 'am / / mi stong-pa # 'i mthar 'gyur ro /
apavAda samAropa pratizeDa upasaMhAra arTam vA asya AramBaH
# yang-na #  skur-pa-'debs-pa #  dang sgro-'dogs-pa #  dgag-pa #  bshad ma-thag #  pa mjug bsdu-ba # 'i don-du #  de brtsams so /
hetu pratyaya pratibadDa AtmalABAt aBUta parikalpaH saMskRtam
# rgyu-dang-rkyen #  dang 'brel-pa #  las skyes-pa # 'i phyir / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  ni 'dus byas te /
SUnyatA punar tat nirapekza tvAt asaMskRtam
# de-la #  mi ltos-pa # 'i phyir stong-pa-nyid #  ni 'dus-ma-byas #  so /
viDIyate prajQApAramitA Adi maDye paWyate
# bshad-pa #  ni shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i nang nas 'byung-ba # 'o /
sattvAt aBUta parikalpasya na saMskRtam SUnyam aBUta parikalpa Atma tvena / asatvAt dvayasya / grAhya grAhaka AtmanA SUnyam
# yod-pa # s zhes-bya-ba #  ni yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  ste / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyis #  'dus byas stong-pa #  ma yin no / / med-pa # s zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnyis po ste / / gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyis #  stong-pa # 'o /
SUnya AtAyAH tu sarvam aBUta parikalpe tat Darma tA iti kRtvA
# stong-pa-nyid #  ni yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  la de'i chos-nyid #  du yod de /
SUnyatAyAm api aBUta parikalpaH Darmi rUpeNa vidyate
# stong-pa-nyid #  la yang yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  chos-can #  gyi ngo bor yod do /
evam asaMskRtam api Darma tA rUpeNa na SUnyam
# de-ltar #  'dus-ma-byas #  kyang chos-nyid #  kyi ngo bos stong-pa #  ma yin te /
aBAva saMjQakena dvayena sva rUpa SUnyam
# dngos-po #  med ces bya-ba #  gnyis kyi ngo bos stong-pa # 'o /
sA ca maDyamA pratipad iti ratna kUwa Adi maDye asti iti kASya pAyam / ekaH antar / na asti iti ayam dvitIyaH antar / yat etayoH dvayoH antayoH maDyam iyam ucyate kASyapa maDyamA pratipad / DarmANAm BUta pratyavekzeti sA maDyamA pratipadevam anulomitA / sarvam iti saMskRtam asaMskRtaQca
# de ni dbu-ma'i-lam #  yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni dkon-mchog #  brtsegs pa la-sogs-pa # 'i nang nas / / 'od srungs yod ces bya-ba #  'di ni mtha' gcig go / / med ces bya-ba #  'di ni mtha'-gnyis #  te / / 'od srungs mtha'-gnyis #  po 'di dag gi dbus gang-yin-pa #  'di ni chos-rnams #  la yang-dag-par #  so-sor-rtog-pa # 'o zhes 'byung-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  ste / / de-ltar #  dbu-ma'i-lam #  de dang mthun-par #  byas-pa #  yin no / / thams-cad #  ces bya-ba #  ni 'dus byas dang 'dus-ma-byas #  so /
na ekAntena SUnyam iti aBUta parikalpasya tat SUnyatAyAH ca p / sadBAvAt
# gcig-tu #  stong-pa #  yang ma yin zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog dang de-la #  stong-pa-nyid #  kyang yod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na api ekAntena aSUnyam dvayasya aBAvAt
# gcig-tu #  mi stong-pa #  yang ma-yin-pa #  ni gnyis po med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sarva nAstitvam sarva astitvam vA antaH eva syAt / na maDyamA pratipad
# thams-cad-yod-pa # 'am thams-cad-med-pa #  ni mtha' nyid-du #  'gyur gyi / / dbu-ma'i-lam #  ma yin no /
evam aBUta parikalpasya sat lakzaNam asat lakzaNaQca KyApayitvA iti
# de-ltar #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i yod-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  brjod nas zhes-bya-ba #  'di /
idam sattvena lakzyate iti sattvam eva sat lakzaNam
# yod-pa # r nye-bar #  mtshon pas yod-pa-nyid #  / / yod-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  de /
aBUta parikalpaH vidyate iti anena aBUta parikalpasya sattvam / pradarSayati iti arTaH
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  yod ces bya-ba #  des yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  yod-pa # r ston zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
evam asattvena lakzyate iti asatvam eva asat lakzaNAt / tat punar yat grAhya grAhaka BAvena asattvam
# de-bzhin-du #  med-pa # r nye-bar #  mtshon pas med-pa #  nyid med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  de / / de-yang #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i dngos-po-med-pa #  ste /
yasmAt aBUta parikalpe dvayam na asti tasmAt aBUta parikalpaH api / dvaya AtmanA na asti iti uktam Bavati
# 'di-ltar #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  la gnyis po med-pa # s de'i-phyir #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  yang gnyis kyi bdag-nyid-kyis #  yod-pa #  ma yin no zhes bstan-pa #  yin no /
sva lakzaNam KyApayati iti / kaH viSezaH asti sat lakzaNa sva lakzaNayoH / sat lakzaNam hi sAmAnyam / sva lakzaNam tu viSezaH
# rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  brjod de zhes-bya-ba #  la yod-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  gnyis khyad-par #  ci yod ce na / / yod-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni spyi'i'o / / rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  ni bye-brag #  yin no /
yadi sva lakzaNam anAKyAtam atra kim syAt
# gal-te #  rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  ma bshad na ci-zhig #  tu 'gyur zhe na /
SarIram aBUta parikalpasya na uktam syAt
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i lus ma bshad-pa # r 'gyur te /
atas tat SarIra pratipAdana arTam ucyate
# de-bas-na #  de'i lus khong-du-chud-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir /
arTa sattva Atma vijQapti pratiBAsam prajAyate / vijQAnam na asti ca asya arTaH tad aBAvAt tad api asat iti
# don dang sems-can #  bdag rnam rig / / snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni / / rab tu skye'o de'i don med / / de med-pa # s na de-yang #  med /
aTa vA grAhya grAhaka rahita tA BUta parikalpa mAtrate asti / tasyAm aBUta parikalpa mAtra tAyAm indriya vizaya vijQAnam yaTA
# ces bya-ba #  gsungs so / / yang-na #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  med-pa # 'i yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  tsam nyid yod do zhes bstan-pa #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  tsam de-la #  /
vyavasTitam na jQAyata / aBUta parikalpa pratiBAsa Bedena tat vyavasTita jQApana arTam
# dbang-po #  dang yul dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  ji-ltar #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  mi-shes-pa # s yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i snang-ba #  tha-dad-pa #  de-la #  rnam-pa # r gzhag go zhes shes-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir /
aBUta parikalpasya sva lakzaNam KyApayati / arTa sattva Atma vijQapti pratiBAsam / iti vistaraH p
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  bshad de / / don dang sems-can #  bdag rnam rig / / snang-ba # 'i zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba # 'o; /
aTa vA BUta parikalpaH asti iti anena tat sattva mAtram jQAyate na tu / tat svaBAvaH / dvaya aBAve api yat grAhya grAhaka aBiniveSa kAraNam na vijQAyate dvayam / ca na asti iti yatas pratIyate tat api na uktam iti atas tat pratipAdana arTam
# yang-na #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  yod ces bya-ba #  des de yod-pa #  tsam du shes-pa # r byed kyi / / de'i-rang-bzhin #  ni ma-yin-pa #  dang gnyis po med-pa # r yang gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i rgyu gang-yin-pa #  rnam-pa # r mi-shes-pa #  dang gang-gi-phyir #  gnyis po med-pa # r yid-ches-pa # r bya-ba #  de-yang #  ma bshad-pa # s de bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
Aha / arTa sattva Atma vijQapti pratiBAsam
# don dang sems-can #  bdag rnam rig / / snang-ba # 'i zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
iti vistaraH / tatra vijQAna svaBAvaH aBUta parikalpaH
# de-la #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  no /
tat ca vijQAnam sa samprayogam aBipretam
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  de-yang #  'dir mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa # r dgongs-te #  /
praDAnena tu vijQAnam gRhItam
# gtso bor ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  gzung ngo /
saH eva grAhya grAhaka aBiniveSaH arTa sattva Adi pratiBAsa nibanDanaH / na asti ca asya arTaH tad aBAvAt tat api asat iti / dvaya aBAva kAraNam
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  de nyid kyi rgyu ni don dang sems-can #  la-sogs-pa # r snang-ba # 'o / / de'i don med de med-pa # s na de-yang #  med ces bya-ba #  ni gnyis po med-pa # 'i rgyu'o /
tatra arTa sattva pratiBAsam Alaya vijQAnam sa samprayogam
# de-la #  don dang sems-can #  du snang-ba # 'i kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  ste /
tat ca vipAka tvAt avyAkRtam eva
# de-yang #  rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i phyir lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  nyid do /
Atma pratiBAsam klizwam manaH sa saMprayogam
# bdag tu snang-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi yid mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'o /
tat ca nivRta avyAkRtam kleSa saMprayukta tvAt uktam
# de-yang #  bsgribs la lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  ste / / nyon-mongs-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i phyir bstan-pa # 'o /
vijQapti pratiBAsam kuSala akuSala avyAkRtam sa samprayigaQcakzuH / vijQAna Adi zawkam
# rnam-par-rig-pa # r snang-ba #  ni / / mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  drug-po #  mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'o /
tat etAni arTa sattva Atma vijQapti pratiBAsAni azwO vijQAnAni / sa samprayogANi samudaya satya saFgRhItAt sahakAri pratyaya apekzAt / AlayavijQAnAt yaTAsaMBavam paQcagatizu praBavanti / kaScid
# don dang sems-can #  dang bdag dang rnam-par-rig-pa # r snang-ba #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  brgyad po mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  de-dag #  ni kun-'byung-ba # 'i bden-pa # r bsdus-pa #  / / lhan-cig #  byed-pa # 'i rkyen-la-ltos-pa # 'i kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  las ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du 'gro-ba-lnga #  rnams su rab tu 'byung ngo /
kuSalA akuSala vyAkRta Darma vAsanA pariNAma viSezaH asti AlayavijQAnasya
# kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'i chos-kyis #  bag-chags #  'gyur-ba # 'i khyad-par #  'ga' zhig yod de /
yadA ADipatyena paraspara Binna ABAsam vijQAnam prajAyate
# de dbang gis phan tshun tha-dad-pa # r snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rab tu skye'o /
kaTam asati arTa AdO vijQAnam tad ABAsam utpadyate / na hi puruze asati sTANuH puruza ABAsaH Bavati iti / na eza dozaH
# don la-sogs-pa #  med-pa #  der-snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ji-ltar #  skye ste / / mi med na sdong-po #  mi-snang-ba # r mi-'gyur-ba #  lta-ba # 'o zhe na /
arTa Adi ABAsam hi vijQAnam bAlA vijQAnAt pRTak / arTa astitvena aBiniviSante tEmirikasya keSoNXuka Adi vat
# de ni nyes-pa #  ma yin te / / don la-sogs-pa # r snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  la byas-pa #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  las don gud-na #  yod-pa # r mngon-pa # r zhen te / / rab-rib #  can la skra shad 'dzings pa la-sogs-pa #  bzhin no /
tasmAt tad aBiniveSa tyAjana arTam ucyate / vijQAnam eva idam arTa Adi ABAsam utpadyate tEmirikANAm iva
# de'i-phyir #  de-la #  mngon-par-zhen-pa #  spangs-pa # 'i phyir / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  'di nyid don la-sogs-pa # r snang-ba # r 'byung ste /
keSa UrNXuka Adi ABAsam vinA api arTa sattva AdinA iti
# rab-rib #  can la skra shad 'dzings pa la-sogs-pa #  snang-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  med-pa # r yang don dang sems-can #  la-sogs-pa # r snang ngo zhes brjod do /
evam ca azwa vijQAna vastukaH paratantraH aBUta parikalpaH iti uktam Bavati
# de-ltar-na #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  brgyad kyi dngos-po #  can / / gzhan gyi dbang ni yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun du rtog-pa # r bshad-pa #  yin no /
rUpAt aBAvena iti rUpa Sabda ganDa rasa sprazwavya Darma svarUpeNa / pratiBAsam tad AkAreNa utpanna tvAt
# gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i dngos-po # r zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg-pa #  dang chos kyi ngo bor snang-ba #  ni de'i rnam-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
sattva pratiBAsam yat paQca indriya tvena sva para santAnayoH / pratiBAsaH iti aDikRtam / aDika sakti sTAna tvAt paQcasu indriyezu sattva AKyA / tEH tezu vA sajjate iti sattvaH / tad AkAra utpattitAm upAdAya vijQAnam tad ABAsam iti / Atma pratiBAsam klizwam manaH Atma moha Adi samprayogAt iti klizwasya
# sems-can #  du snang-ba # 'i dbang-po-lnga # r bdag-dang-gzhan #  gyi rgyud la gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / snang-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  dang sbyar ro / / dbang-po-lnga #  la sems-can #  zhes-bya-ba # r lhag-par-chags-pa # 'i gnas-su-gyur-pa #  ste / / de-dag #  gis sam / / de-dag #  la chags-pa # s sems-can #  te / / de'i rnam-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i phyir / / de snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
manasaH Atma mohena Atma dRzwyA Atma tRzNAyA smimAnena ca nityam / samprayukta tvAt p / tezAm Atma Alambana tva Adi uktam Atma pratiBAsa tvam klizwasya manasaH / vijQapti pratiBAsam zaX vijQAnAni iti
# bdag tu snang-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  dang bdag tu snang-ba #  ni bdag tu rmongs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i phyir / / nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi yid do zhes-bya-ba #  la nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi yid ni bdag tu rmongs-pa #  dang bdag-tu-lta-ba #  dang bdag-la-chags-pa #  dang nga'o-snyam-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  dang rtag-tu #  mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang de-dag #  kyang bdag tu dmigs-pa # 'i phyir nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi yid ni bdag tu snang-ba # r rigs so /
vizama grAhaka rUpeNa praKyAnAt tad AkAra utpattim upAdAya / vijQapti pratiBAsam / na asti ca asya arTaH iti catuzwayasya AkArasya iti
# rnam-par-rig-pa # r snang-ba #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  drug rnams so zhes-bya-ba #  ni yul 'dzin-pa # 'i ngo bor snang-ba # s de'i rnam-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i phyir rnam-par-rig-pa #  snang ngo / / de'i don med ces bya-ba #  ni rnam-pa-bzhi #  char gyi'o /
arTa sattva pratiBAsasya anAkAra tvAt Atma vijQapti pratiBAsasya ca / vitaTa pratiBAsa tvAt iti arTa sattva pratiBAsasya anAkAra tvAt / Atma vijQapti pratiBAsasya ca vitaTa pratiBAsa tvAt iti / arTa sattva pratiBAsayoH grAhya rUpeNa praKyAnAt / vitaTa pratiBAsa tva asamBavAt anAkAra tvam eva arTa aBAve kAraNam / na tu anyayoH grAhaka rUpeNa praKyAnAt anAkAraH / vitaTa pratiBAsa tvem eva arTa aBAve kAraNam uktam / AkAraH hi Alambanasya anitya Adi rUpeNa grahaNa prakAraH / sa ca anayoH na asti grAhya rUpeNa praKyAnAt / atas anAkAratvAt agrAhaka tvAt iti arTaH / Alambana sampedanam vAkAraH / tat ca tayoH na asti iti upalabDi aBAvAt anAkAraH / yadi uBayam api anAkAram paraspara Binna svarUpa= ca rUpa Adi vat
# don dang sems-can #  du snang-ba #  rnam-pa #  med-pa #  dang bdag dang rnam-par-rig-pa # r snang-ba #  ni log-pa # r snang-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni don dang sems-can #  du snang-ba #  gnyis gzung-ba # 'i ngo bor snang-ba # s / / log-pa # r snang-ba #  mi srid-pa # 'i phyir / / rnam-pa #  med-pa #  nyid ni don-med-pa # 'i rgyu'o / / gzhan dag ni 'dzin-pa # 'i ngo bor snang-ba # s rnam-pa #  med-pa #  ma yin te / / log-pa # r snang-ba #  nyid ni don-med-pa # 'i rgyu'o zhes bshad do / / rnam-pa #  ni dmigs-pa #  la mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i ngo bor 'dzin-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  yin na / / de-yang #  de-dag #  la med de / / gzung-ba # 'i ngo bor snang-ba # s de'i-phyir #  rnam-pa #  med-pa #  ni 'dzin-pa #  ma yin no zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / yang-na #  dmigs-pa #  yang-dag-par #  tshor-ba #  la rnam-pa #  zhes bya ste / / de-yang #  de-dag #  la med-pa # s dmigs-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir rnam-pa #  med do / / gal-te #  gnyis-ka #  yang rnam-pa #  med-pa #  dang phan tshun tha-dad-pa # 'i ngo bo yin te / / gzugs la-sogs-pa #  dang mig la-sogs-pa #  bzhin no /
cakzuH Adi vat ca evam sati loka SAstra prasidDeByaH / rUpa AdiByaH cakzuH AdiByaH ca vijQAnasya kaH asO= Atma atiSayaH yatas tAn / nirAkritya tEH aBinna rUpam vijQAnam gRhyate tat / avyatiriktasya arTasya asamBavAt / etat evam vyavasTApyate / yasmAt BinnarTa svarUpam Asanna picitta AsantAn apratiniyamena sva bIjAt
# de lta yin na ni 'jig-rten #  dang bstan-bcos #  las grags-pa # 'i gzugs la-sogs-pa #  dang mig la-sogs-pa #  las rnam-par-shes-pa #  rang-bzhin #  bye-brag #  tu gyur-pa #  ci yod-na #  / / 'di-ltar #  de-dag #  ni gsal la / / de-dag #  dang tha-dad-pa #  med-pa # 'i ngo bo rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni yongs su bzung zhe na / / de-la # s lhag-pa'i-don #  mi srid-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de ni 'di-ltar #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ste / / 'di-ltar #  tha-dad-pa # 'i don gyi ngo bo med kyang sems-kyi-rgyud #  so-sor-nges-pa # s /
pratyeka Atma grahItam Binna arTa Adi pratiBAsam vijQAnam prasUyate
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid so-so # s zin-pa #  tha-dad-pa # 'i don la-sogs-pa # r snang-ba # r rang-gi-sa-bon #  las rab tu 'byung ste /
taTA hi pretAH apaH pUya purIza mUtra Adi pUrNA DRta daNXa pANiBiH / uBayatas purusEH saMrakzyamANAH paSyanti manuzYa AdayaH punar / su acCa SItala udaka paripUrNAH nirvibanDAH iti upalaBante / yoginaH ca aSuBa manasikAra Adi aByastA nirantaram pRTivIm / kaFkAla pUrNAm paSyanti
# 'di-ltar #  yi dags rnams kyis chu rnag dang phyi-sa-dang-gcin #  la-sogs-pa # s gang-ba #  dang skyes-bu #  la gan dbyig-pa-thogs-pa #  rnams kyis dogs gnyis bsrung-ba # r mthong la / / mi la-sogs-pa # s ni chu dang-ba #  dang bsil ba dang bkrur rung-ba #  dang btung du rung-ba #  dang 'jug tu rung-ba # s gang zhig bgegs-byed-pa #  med-pa # r shes so / / rnal-'byor-pa #  mi-sdug-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  goms-pa # s ni / / rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  sa la keng-rus #  kyis gang-ba # r mthong ngo /
taTA pRTivI Adi kRtsnezu sarvam pRTivI AdiBiH vyAptam paSyati
# de-bzhin-du #  sa la-sogs-pa #  zad-pa # r la thams-cad #  sa la-sogs-pa # s khyab-pa # r mthong ngo /
na ca arTa pratibudDa Atma lABasya arTam antareNa arTa svarUpAt vA / Binna AkArasya vijQAna asya prasUtiH yuktA
# don la rag las te bdag-nyid #  thob-pa #  ni don-med-pa # r ram / / don gyi rang-gi #  ngo bo tha-dad-pa # 'i rnam-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung-ba # r mi rigs so /
tasmAt tat arTam antareNa sarvam arTa sattva Adi nirBAsam vijQAnam eva / prasUyate iti niScIyate
# de-bas-na #  don-med-pa # r yang don dang sems-can #  la-sogs-pa #  thams-cad-du #  snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid rab tu 'byung ngo zhes-bya-ba # r nges so /
grAhya aBAve dvayoH Atma vijQapti pratiBAsayoH grAhaka AkAreNa / praKyAnAt vitaTa pratiBAsa tvam
# gzung-ba #  med-pa # r bdag dang rnam-par-rig-pa # r snang-ba #  gnyis 'dzin-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r snang-ba # s log-pa # r snang-ba #  nyid do /
aTa vA yaTA vijQAnena arTaH parikalpyate taTA arTasya aBAvaH / vyAGra Adi Sruti Adizu iva vitaTa Alambana tvAt vitaTa pratiBAsa tA
# yang-na #  ji-ltar #  rnam-par-shes-pa # s don yongs su brtags-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  bdag dang rnam-par-rig-pa # r don med de stag la-sogs-pa #  thob-pa #  ltar / / log-pa # r dmigs-pa # 'i phyir /
taTA hi vijQaptiH api vijQapti antara parikalpitena AtmanA SUnyA iti / sidDAntaH
# log-pa # r snang-ba #  nyid do / / 'di-ltar #  rnam-par-rig-pa #  yang rnam-par-rig-pa #  gzhan gyis kun-brtags-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyis #  stong ngo zhes grub-pa # 'i mtha' las 'byung ngo /
atas ca arTa sattva vijQAnasya iva Atma vijQapti pratiBAsasya api arTa aBAvaH
# de'i-phyir #  don dang sems-can #  du snang-ba #  bzhin-du #  / / bdag dang rnam-par-rig-pa # r snang-ba # 'i don yang med do /
arTa aBAvAt tat vijQAnam asat / vijAnAti iti vijQAnam grAhya aBAve vijAnana api ayuktam
# don-med-pa # s rnam-par-shes-pa #  de-yang #  med do / / rnam-par-rig-pa # s na rnam-par-shes-pa #  ste / / de-yang #  gzung-ba #  med na rnam-par-shes-pa #  por mi rigs te /
tasmAt arTa aBAvAt vijQAtR tvena vijQAnam asat na p / tu arTa sattva Atma vijQapti pratiBAsa tayA
# de-lta-bas-na #  don-med-pa # 'i phyir rnam-par-shes-pa #  kho-nar #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  med kyi don dang sems-can #  dang bdag dang rnam-par-rig-pa # r snang-ba # s na med-pa #  ma yin no /
tat asattve hi sarvaTA aBAva prasaFgaH / tat avyatirekeNa vijQAna svaBAvAt nirdeSAt / tat Binna svaBAve sati tat vijQAnam kaTam yujyeta kaTam parasparam / Binnam Bavet
# de med du zin na de ma-gtogs-par #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  ma bstan-pa # 'i phyir ye med-pa # r thal-ba # r 'gyur ro / / de dang tha-dad-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  yin na ni de ji-ltar #  rnam-par-shes-pa # r rung / / ji-ltar #  phan tshun tha-dad-pa # r 'gyur /
evaMgrAhya grAhaka aBAvAt tat pratiBAsa vijQAna sadBAvAt ca yat / pUrvam pratijQAtam / aBUta parikalpaH asti dvayam tatra na vidyate / iti tat prasidDam iti pradarSayan= Aha / aBUta parikalpa tvam sidDam asya Bavati atas / aBUta parikalpa tvaQca tezAm AturANAm vijQAnAnAm sidDam
# de-ltar #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  ni med la de snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni yod-pa # s / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  ni yod / / gnyis po ni de na yod-pa-ma-yin-pa # r sngar dam-bcas-pa #  de grub po zhes rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog-pa #  / / de ni de phyir grub-pa #  yin / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  bzhi-po #  de-yang #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun du rtog-pa #  grub-pa #  yin no /
atas iti anantara uktAt hetoH arTa aBAvAt tat api asat iti punar api
# de phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni bshad ma-thag #  pa'i rgyu de'i-phyir #  te / / don-med-pa # s na de-yang #  med ces bya'o /
aBUta parikalpAH titvapra sADana arTam dvaya aBAva prasADana arTaQcA Aha / na taTA sarvaTA aBAvAt / ityAdi / aTa vA atas iti vakzyamANAt vetoH / tam eva pradarzayan= Aha / na taTA sarvaTA aBAvAt / iti / na taTA astitvAt na ca sarvaTA na astitvAt tat
# yang yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  yod-pa # r bsgrub-pa #  dang gnyis po med-pa # r rab tu bsgrub-pa # 'i phyir / / de-bzhin #  ma yin ye med min / / zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  gsungs so / / yang-na #  de'i-phyir #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'og nas 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de nyid rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / de-bzhin #  ma yin ye med min / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs te / / de-bzhin-du #  yod-pa-ma-yin-pa #  dang ye med-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
grAhya grAhaka pratiBAsam utpadyate
# gang-gi-phyir #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r snang-ba #  de skye-ba #  ste /
tatra catur prakAre api anAkAra tvAt vitaTa AkAra tvAt ca yaTAsamBavam / grAhaka tva aBAvaH
# de-la #  rnam-pa-bzhi-po #  de-yang #  rnam-pa #  med-pa #  dang log-pa # r snang-ba # 'i phyir ji-ltar-mthun-pa # r 'dzin-pa #  nyid-du #  med do /
vijQapti antara parikalpitAna ca AtmanA sarvasya SUnya tvAt / grAhya tva aBAvaH
# rnam-par-rig-pa #  gzhan gyis kun-brtags-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyis #  thams-cad #  stong bas gzung-ba #  nyid-du #  med do /
na ca sarvaTA aBAvaH BrAnti mAtrasya utpAdAt iti Atma tvena aBAvaH na tu
# 'khrul-pa #  tsam 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ye med-pa #  yang ma yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni bdag-nyid-kyis #  med kyang /
yad AkAreNa pratiBAsate tena BrAntiH ucyare mAyAvat
# rnam-pa # r snang-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni 'khrul-pa #  zhes bya ste / / sgyu-ma #  bzhin no /
mAtra SabdaH tad aDika vyavacCeda arTaH / etat uktam Bavati
# tsam zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni de-la # s lhag-ma #  rnam bar gcad-pa # 'i tha-tshig #  ste /
BrAnti vijQAnasya sadBAvAt na sarvaTA aBAvaH iti
# de ni 'di-skad-du #  'khrul-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  yod do /
kim arTa punar tasya BrAnti vijQAnasya aBAvaH eva na izyate / grAhya grAhaka aBAvavat / na hi kenacid tasya astitvam kalpayitum Sakyate / sarva avijQAna vizaya atikrAnta tvAt iti aBipretam iti ced / yasmAt
# ye med-pa #  ma yin no zhes bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro / / 'khrul-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  de gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  med-pa #  bzhin-du #  med-pa #  nyid-du #  ci'i-phyir #  mi 'dod / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  thams-cad-kyi #  yul las 'das-pa # 'i phyir / / sus kyang de yod-pa-nyid #  du brtag-pa # r mi nus so zhes bsams-pa # 'o zhe na 'di-ltar #  /
tat kzayAt muktiH izyate
# de zad nas ni grol bar 'dod /
atas asya aBAvaH eva na izyate / kim tarhi saFkleSa vyavadAna pakza sAmarTAt tat astitvam anumIyate a
# de'i-phyir #  de med-pa #  nyid-du #  mi 'dod do / / de ji lta zhe na kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba'i-phyogs #  kyi mthus de yod-pa # r rjes su dpag go /
anyaTA iti yadi tasya sarvaTA aBAvaH eva izyate na banDaH na mokzaH iti
# gzhan-du-na #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni gal-te #  ye med-pa #  nyid-du #  'dod na ni bcings-pa #  yang med ces bya ste /
BrAnti mAtre api asati saFkleSa aBAvAt banDaH api na asti
# 'khrul-pa #  tsam yang med du zin na / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa # s bcings-pa #  yang med do /
pUrvam badDaH mucyate iti kRtvA muktiH api na syAt / aTa vA kaTam na yaTA praKyAti taTA BAvena izyate sarvaTA
# sngar bcings-pa #  las grol lo zhes bya na grol ba yang med-pa # r 'gyur / / yang-na #  de ji-ltar #  snang-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  yod-pa # 'am /
vA aBAvaH iti para aBiprAya vyudAsa arTam Aha
# yang-na #  ye med-pa # r ci'i-phyir #  mi 'dod ces gzhan de snyam-du #  sems-pa #  bsal-ba # 'i phyir /
tat kzayAt muktiH izyate / tasmin= ca aparikzINe banDaH iti arTAt uktam Bavati
# de zad nas ni grol bar 'dod / / ces gsungs te / / de ma zad na bcings-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
anyaTA hi na banDaH na mokzaH iti saFkleSa vyavadAna apavAda dozaH syAt
# de gzhan-du-na #  bcings-pa #  dang grol ba med do zhes de-skad #  bshad-pa # r 'gyur te / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la skur ba 'debs-pa # 'i nyes-pa # r 'gyur ro /
yaTA grAhya grAhaka tvena BrAntiH udBAsitA api yadi taTA syAt / paramArTataH evam sati nityaH saFkleSaH syAt
# gal-te #  ji-ltar #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  nyid-du #  phyugs yan-chad-la #  snang-ba #  yang gal-te #  de-bzhin-du #  don-dam-pa # r 'gyur na ni / / de-ltar #  yin-du-zin #  na rtag-par #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r 'gyur te /
taTA ca nirvANa aBAvaH / evam ca BrAnti mAtrasya api aBAve saFkleSa aBAvaH nityaQca vyavadAnam / prasajyeta
# de-ltar-na #  mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  yang med-pa # r 'gyur ro / / de-ltar #  'khrul-pa #  tsam med na yang kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa # r 'gyur te / / rtag-tu #  rnam-par-byang-ba # r 'gyur ro /
evam ca uBayaTA api mokza arTinAm vyarTaH yatnaH syAt / atas avaSyam aBUta parikalpa BAvaH aByupagantavyaH dvaya aBAvaH ca
# de-ltar-na #  gnyi-ga # r yang thar-pa #  tshol-ba #  rnams kyi 'bad-pa #  don-med-par-'gyur-ba # s de'i-phyir #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  yod-pa #  dang gnyis po med-pa # r gdon-mi-za-bar #  khas-blang-ba # r bya'o /
saFgraha lakzaNam KyApayati iti saFgrahaH eva lakzaNam
# bsdu-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ston te zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / bsdu-ba #  nyid mtshan-nyid #  do /
aTa vA yena saFgrahaH lakzyate tat saFgraha lakzaNam / tat ca kim arTam uktam
# yang-na #  gang-gis #  bsdu-ba # r mtshon pa de bsdu-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do / / de-yang #  ci'i-phyir #  bshad ce na /
atra hi grAhya grAhaka rahitam aBUta parikalpa mAtram eva asti iti ayuktam
# 'dir ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  dang brla ba yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  tsam nyid yod do zhes smras la /
sUtra antarezu punar trayaH svaBAvAH paWyante / atas sUtra antarEH aviroDa pradarSana arTam tezAm iha saFgrahaH ucyate / atas eva vRtti kAraH Aha
# mdo gzhan dag las ni / / ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum gsungs-pa # s mdo dag dang mi-'gal-ba # r rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir de-dag #  'dir bsdu-ba # r brjod de / / de-lta-bas-na #  'grel pa mdzad-pa # s /
aBUta parikalpa mAtre sati iti vistareNa
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  tsam du zad na zhes-bya-ba #  rgya-cher #  smos so /
kalpitaH paratantraH ca parinizpannaH eva ca
# brtag-pa #  dang ni gzhan dbang dang / / yongs-su-grub-pa #  nyid kyang ngo /
arTAt aBUta kalpAt ca dvaya aBAvAt ca deSitaH iti
# don phyir-yang #  dag min rtog phyir / / gnyis po med-pa # 'i phyir bshad do / / zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
grAhyam grAhakam ca svaBAva SUnya tvAt aBUtam api astitvena / parikalpyataH iti p / parikalpitaH ucyate / sa punar dravyataH Asan= api vyavahArataH asti iti svaBAvaH ucyate / paratantraH paravaSaH hetu pratyaya pratibadDa janmaka tvAt / Aha ca
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  rang-bzhin-gyis #  stong-pa #  las yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # r yang yod-pa # r yongs-su-rtog-pa # s kun-brtags-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / de ni rdzas su med kyang tha-snyad #  du yod-pa # s ngo-bo-nyid #  ces bya'o / / gzhan gyi dbang ni rgyu-dang-rkyen #  la rag las te skye-ba # s gzhan gyi kha na las pa'o / / smras-pa #  /
akalpitaH pratyayacaH anaBilApyaH ca sarvaTA
# brtags min rkyen las skyes-pa #  dang / / rnam-pa #  kun-tu #  brjod med-pa #  /
paratantra svaBAvaH hi SudDa lOkika gocaraH
# gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  / / 'jig-rten-pa #  yi spyod yul lo /
yA BUta parikalpasya dvaya rahita tA sa parinizpannaH svaBAvaH / tasyAH asaMskRta tvAt nirvikAra tvena parinizpanna tvAt / Aha ca / kalpitena svaBAvena tasya yA atyanta SUnya tA
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  nyid-gnyis #  dang bral-ba-nyid #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  de / / de ni 'dus-ma-byas #  pas mi-'gyur-ba # r yongs-su-grub-pa # 'o / / brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  te / / shin-tu #  stong nyid gang-yin-pa #  /

evam aBUta parikalpAt dvaya aBAvAt ca iti vaktavyam
# de-ltar #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i phyir dang gnyis po med-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes brjod-pa # r bya'o /

aBUta parikalpaH paratantraH svaBAvaH iti / parEH hetu pratyayEH tantryate janyate na tu svayamBavatI iti paratantraH

atra hi aBUta parikalpasya dvaya rahita tA grAhya grAhaka aBAvaH uktaH

na tu dvayasya aBAva mAtram

# dmigs-pa #  la ni brten-nas #  su / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog-pa #  la de mtshon pa'am / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'o / / gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  gnyis med-pa #  nyid ni med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do /
