utpadyamAnam anutpannam vA vijQAnam vizayam Alambeta
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  skye-ba'i-tshe # 'am / / skye sa zin-pa # s yul la dmigs-pa # r 'gyur grang na /
tatra utpadyamAnam vizayam na Alambate utpadyamAnasya asattvAt
# de-la #  skye-ba'i-tshe #  ni med-pa # s skye-ba'i-tshe #  yul la dmigs-pa # r mi rung ngo /
na utpannam api vizaya pratiBAsa AtmanA utpanna tvAt
# yul du snang-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  du skyes-pa # 'i phyir / / skyes-pa # s kyang ma yin te /
na ca vizaya pratiBAsa AtmanA utpattim uktvA vijQAnasya anyA kriyA asti / yAm kriyAm kurvat vijQAnam vizayam AlambanaH iti ucyate
# yul du snang-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  du skye-ba #  ma-gtogs-par #  / / gang byed na rnam-par-shes-pa #  yul la dmigs-pa # 'o zhes-bya'o #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bya-ba #  gzhan med do /
yadi vA Alambanasya vartamAnaH eva vijQAne vyApAraH na utpadyamAne evam / Alambana pratyayaH na vijNyAna utpAdakaH / tat parikalpanam nirarTakam
# gal-te #  yang da-ltar #  gyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid kyi dmigs-pa #  byed-pa #  yin gyi / / skye-ba'i-tshe #  ni ma yin no zhe na / / de lta na ni dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i skye-ba #  ma yin te / / der yongs-su-rtog-pa #  don med do /
vartamAna Alambana grahaNe kzaNa Beda dozaH Bavati
# da-ltar #  gyi dmigs-pa #  'dzin na ni skad-cig-pa #  'jig-pa # 'i gnod-pa # r 'gyur ro /
na ca Atma atiSaya BAve pUrvavat vijQAnena Alambana grahaNam yujyate
# rang-bzhin #  bye-brag #  tu gyur-pa #  yang med-pa # s snga-ma-bzhin #  te / / rnam-par-shes-pa # s dmigs-pa #  'dzin-pa # r mi rung ngo /
aTa Alambana grahaNa kAle tasya AtmA atiSayaH izyate evam api / Atma atiSayasya anyatas eva darSanAt anyat eva utpannam Alambanam gRhNAti iti / prasajyate / anyaH manyate
# 'on te dmigs-pa #  'dzin-pa # 'i dus na / / de-la #  rang-bzhin #  bye-brag #  tu gyur-pa # r 'dod na / / de-lta-na-yang #  rang-bzhin #  bye-brag #  tu gyur-pa #  gzhan nyid-du #  snang-ba # s / / byung-ba #  gzhan nyid kyis dmigs-pa #  'dzin-pa # r thal-ba # r 'gyur ro /
niruDyamAnaH arTaH eva utpadyamAnasya vijQAnasya Alambana pratyayaH
# gzhan ni 'gag-pa # 'i tshe'i don nyid skye-ba'i-tshe # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  nyid yin te /
sa ca sva AkAra pratiBAsa jQAna kAraNa tvena SezeByaH pratyayeByaH / viSizyata / p
# de-yang #  rang-gi #  rnam-pa # r snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rgyu yin-pas #  rkyen lhag-ma #  rnams las khyad-par-can #  no snyam-du #  sems te /
iti / tena api rUpa Adi paramANavaH tat samUhaH vA Alambana tvena parikalpyate / uBayaTA api ca Alambana aBAvaH
# des kyang gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i rdul-phra-rab #  bam / / de 'dus-pa #  la dmigs-pa #  kho-nar #  kun-tu #  brtag grang na / / de-gnyi-ga #  yang dmigs-pa # r mi 'gyur te /
sarvam eva hi vijQAnam Gawa pawa Adi pratiBAsam utpadyate na tu / paramANu pratiBAsam
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  thams-cad #  ni bum-pa #  dang snam-bu #  la-sogs-pa # r snang-ba #  'byung gi / / rdul-phra-rab #  tu snang-ba #  ni ma yin no /
na ca A arTa AkArasya anya nirBAsasya vijQAnasya anyat Alambanam
# don gyi rnam-pa #  gzhan-du #  snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni gzhan ma yin te /
cakzuH AdInAm api Alambana tva prasaFgaH iti
# mig la-sogs-pa #  yang dmigs-pa #  nyid-du #  thal-ba # r 'gyur ta re /
yaH api manyate samuditAH paramANavaH Alambanam na pratyekam tasya api ayam / aparihAraH
# gang gzhan-yang #  rdul-phra-rab #  sil bu so-so #  la dmigs-pa #  yin pa snyam-du #  sems-pa #  de'i 'di yang lan du mi rung ste /
samuditAH api hi te pratyekam eva Alambana tvena izYante na tat samudAyena
# sil bu de ni de-dag #  so-so #  nyid la dmigs-pa # r 'dod kyi /
tatra paramANUnAm pratyeka pratiBAsam jQAnam na utpadyate na api tat
# de-dag #  gi 'dus-pa #  la ni ma yin no / / der rdul-phra-rab #  so-so # r snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni mi 'byung gi /
samudAya pratiBAsam
# 'di-ltar #  de-dag #  gi 'dus-pa # r snang-ba #  ste /
tasmAt na paramANUnAm Alambana tvam samBavati
# de-bas-na #  rdul-phra-rab #  rnams la dmigs-pa #  mi srid do /
na api paramANu samUhaH Alambanam prajQapti sutaH kAraNa tva asamBavAt
# brtags-pa # r yod-pa #  ni rgyur mi srid-pa # 'i phyir / / rdul-phra-rab #  'dus-pa #  yang dmigs-pa #  ma yin na /
vijQAna kAraNam hi samanantara Adi pratyaya vat Alambana pratyayaH api izyate
# de-ma-thag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rkyen ltar dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  yang-dag-par #  shes-pa # 'i rgyur 'dod de /
tasmAt na niruDyamAnaH api Alambanam
# de'i-phyir #  'gag-pa # 'i tshe yang dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  du mi srid do /
aTa ca nirudDaH Alambanam evam satya atIta anAgatam vizayaH syAt / svapna AdO tu vijQAnam anAlambanam iti sidDam
# ji ste yang 'gag-pa #  nyid dmigs-pa #  yin na / / de lta na ni 'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  yul du 'gyur-pa #  dang rmi-lam #  la-sogs-pa #  la yang rnam-par-shes-pa #  dmigs-pa-med-pa # r grub po /
nA na Alambanam svapna Adi vijQAnam nimitta Alambana tvAt iti
# la-la # n re rmi-lam #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  yang mtshan-ma #  la dmigs-pa # 'i phyir dmigs-pa-med-pa #  ma yin no /
nimittam punar arTa pratibimbam viprayukta saMskAra svaBAvam
# mtshan-ma #  ni don gyi gzugs-brnyan #  te ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  kyi rang-bzhin #  no zhe'o /
na hi svapnAt Avasati arTe tad nimittam yujyate muKa Adi aBAve tat / pratibimba vat
# rmi-lam #  la-sogs-pa #  don-med-pa #  la de'i mtshan-ma #  mi rung ste / / bzhin la-sogs-pa #  med-pa # r de'i gzugs-brnyan #  mi 'grub-pa #  bzhin no /
utpadyamAnam utpannam vA Alambanam vijQAna nimittam aBAvAt niroDAt / ca iti pUrvam uktam
# 'byung-ba # 'i tshe'am byung zin-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # s kyang mtshan-ma #  la dmigs-pa #  ma yin te / / med-pa #  dang dgag-pa #  sngar bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vijQAnam eva arTa pratiBAsa tvAt arTa pratibimbam / atas na viprayukta saMskAra Atmakam nimittam yujyate
# de'i-phyir #  ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  kyi rang-bzhin #  mtshan-ma # r mi-rung-ba # s / / rnam-pa # r shes ba nyid don-du #  snang-ba #  don gyi gzugs-brnyan #  te /
avaSyam ca arTa AkAram vijQAnam aByupagantavyam
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid don gyi rnam-pa # r gdon-mi-za-bar #  khas blang dgos so /
anAkAre hi tasmin grAhya grAhaka niyamaH eva na syAt
# rnam-pa #  med na ni de-la #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  nges-pa #  nyid-du #  mi 'gyur ro /
anyaH tu apratiGam rUpam eva svapne yoginAm ca aSuBa AdO= Alambanam manyate / tasya api varNa saMsTAna Adi Atmaka tvAt apratiGa tvam
# gzhan ni thogs-pa-med-pa # 'i gzugs nyid rmi-lam #  dang rnal-'byor-pa #  rnams kyi mi-sdug-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r dmigs-pa # 'o snyam-du #  sems te / / de'i yang kha-dog #  dang dbyibs la-sogs-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin-pas #  /
manaH mAtra vizaya tvaQca viruDyate
# thogs-pa-med-pa #  nyid dang yid 'ba'-zhig #  gi yul du 'gal lo /
na ca avijQapti mAtrAt anyat apratiGam rUpam SAstre varNyate
# rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa #  tsam ma-gtogs-par #  yang-thog # s pa med-pa # 'i gzugs gzhan bstan-bcos #  las mi bshad-pa # s /
tasmAt kalpanA mAtram eva
# de'i-phyir #  de nyid kyang rtog-pa #  tsam nyid do /
aparaH tu anuBUta arTam eva svapne vijQAna vizaya tvena icCati jAti anDena / svapne nIla Adi rUpa agrahaNAt
# gzhan dag ni dmus long gi rmi-lam #  na sngon-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gzugs mi-'dzin-pa # 'i phyir / / don myong-ba #  ni rmi-lam #  gyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i yul nyid-du #  'dod do /
na jAti anDaH svapne rUpam na gRhNAti
# dmus long gi rmi-lam #  na gzugs mi-'dzin-pa #  yin te /
avyutpanna saFketa tvAt tu nAmataH na jAnAti atas na anyasya Acazwe
# brda mi-shes-pa # s ming rnam-pa # r mi-shes-pa # 'i phyir gzhan la bsnyad mi nus so /
yadi ca anuBUtasya eva svapne darSanam evam jAti anDasya api rUpa darSanam / kim na izyate
# gal-te #  yang myong-ba #  nyid rmi-lam #  du mthong na de lta na dmus long gis kyang gzugs mthong-ba # r ci'i-phyir #  mi 'dod /
tena api pUrva janmasu rUpam upalabDam eva
# des kyang tshe-rabs #  snga-ma #  dag la gzugs dmigs-pa #  nyid do /
na ca p / vartamAna janmani upalabDam eva svapne pratiBAsate
# de-ltar #  gyi tshe la dmigs-pa #  nyid rmi-lam #  du snang-ba #  yang ma yin te /
na hi atIta anAgata vartamAna anuBave suptasya jAgrataH ca kaScid / viSezaH asti
# 'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  dang da-ltar #  gyi 'dzin-pa # r yang rmi-lam #  dang gnyid kyis ma-log-pa # r khyad-par #  med do /
tasmAt parikalpa mAtram eva etat anuBUta arTa vizayam svapne vijQAnam iti
# de-lta-bas-na #  don myong-ba #  de ni rmi-lam #  gyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i yul lo zhes-bya-ba #  ni kun rtog-pa #  tsam nyid do /
atItasya ca aBAvAt nirvizayam vijQAnam eva svapne arTa ABAsam / utpadyate iti niScayaH / evam vijQapti mAtra tvena upalamBAt arTA anupalabDiH BAvya iti
# 'das-pa #  yang med-pa # r yul med-pa # r rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid rmi-lam #  du don-du #  snang-ba #  'byung-ba # r nges so / / de-ltar #  rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam du dmigs-pa # s yul mi dmigs-pa # r bsgom mo /
yaH / arTAH anupalabDim niScitya vijNaptimAtrasya api anupalabDiH jAyate iti
# don mi dmigs-pa #  la brten-nas #  / / rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam yang mi dmigs-pa #  skye ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
yaTA a na vijNyanAt bahis parikalpitam grAhyam asti iti / vijQapti mAtra tA balena manaH grAhya aBAvam praviSati taTA / grAhya BAva balena vijQapti mAtrasya api aBAvam pratipadyate / na grAhya aBAve grAhaka tvam yujyate / grAhyam apekzya tat grAhakasya vyavasTApanAt / evam asat lakzaNam grAhya grAhakayoH parikalpita rUpayoH praviSati / na aBUta parikalpasya iti darSanam Bavati / kim arTam punar praTamatas eva vijQapti mAtrasya eva aBAvam na / viBAvayati / grAhya pratibadDa tvAt hi grAhakasya upalaBya arTa aBAve suKam praveSaH
# ji-ltar #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  las phyi-rol #  na kun-brtags-pa # 'i gzung-ba #  med-pa # s rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam nyid kyi stobs kyis gzung-ba #  med-pa # r 'jug-pa #  de-ltar #  gzung-ba #  med-pa # 'i stobs kyis rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam yang med-pa # r khong du chud do / / gzung-ba #  nyid la ltos te de 'dzin-pa # r rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i phyir / / gzung-ba #  med na 'dzin-pa # r mi rung ngo / / de-ltar #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  kun-brtags-pa # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo dag gi med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  la 'jug gi / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  ni ma yin no zhes bstan-pa #  yin no / / ci'i-phyir #  thog-ma #  nyid-du #  rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam nyid med-pa # r rnam-pa # r mi gzhag ce na / / 'dzin-pa #  ni gzung-ba #  la rag-las-pa # 'i phyir dmigs-par-bya-ba # 'i don med na /
syAt Alambana svaBAva vinASAt / anyaTA BAva apavAdam eva kuryAt / grAhya grAhakayoH paraspara nirapekza tvAt
# dmigs-pa # 'i ngo bo'i dngos-po #  'jig-pa # s bde blag tu 'jug-pa # r 'gyur gyi / / gzhan-du-na #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  gnyis phan tshun ltos-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir /
imAQca grAhya grAhaka vikalpa atItAm jQAna BUmim saMBArezu / nirantaram pravartamAnaH praTama kalpa asaMKyeya parisamAptO pravizati
# dngos-po #  la skur-pa-'debs-pa #  nyid-du #  'gyur ro / / rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  tshogs rnams la zhugs te / / bskal-pa-grangs-med-pa #  dang-po #  yongs su rdzogs na; gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  las 'das-pa # 'i ye shes kyis 'dir chud de /
taTA hi vijQaptimAtram idam niSritya rUpa anupalamBa anukUlaH / lokottara mArge praTamaH uzma gata AKyaH sa parivAraH samADiH muKI / Bavati / tasya anantaram mUrDa AKyaH
# 'di-ltar #  rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam 'di-la #  brten-nas #  / / gzugs la-sogs-pa #  med-pa # r bsgom-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam gyi thog-ma # 'i rang-bzhin #  dro-bar-gyur-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  'khor dang bcas-pa #  mngon du 'gyur ro / / de'i-'og-tu #  rtse mo zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
tasya anantaram aSeza grAhya anupalamBAt grAhaka anupalaBa anukUlaH / kzAntya AKyaH samADiH / tasya anantaram arTa anupalabDim niSritya vijQapti mAtrasya api anupalabDim / BAvayan lOkika agrya Darma AKyaH prajQA Adi sahitaH sa parivAraH samADiH / AmuKIBavati / tat anantaram darSana mArgaH
# de'i-'og-tu #  gzung-ba #  ma-lus-par #  mi dmigs-pa # s 'dzin-pa #  mi dmigs-pa #  dang mthun-pa #  bzod-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  to / / de'i-'og-tu #  don mi dmigs-pa #  la brten-te #  / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  tsam yang mi dmigs-pa # r bsgom zhing 'jig-rten-gyi-chos #  kyi mchog ces bya-ba #  shes-rab #  la-sogs-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  'khor dang bcas-pa #  mngon du 'gyur ro /
tatra eva ca sarvatraga Darma DAtu aDigamAt praTamAm BUmim praviSati iti / ayam ca tattvamanaskAraH na avimukti manaskAraH apramANa Adi vat / upalabDiH upalabDi tvena asidDA / aBUta arTa pratiBAsa tayA tu upalabDiH iti ucyate anupalabDi svaBAvA api api / satI p / upalabDeH anupalabDi svaBAva tvam iti pradarSayan= Aha / upalabDeH tatas sidDAH na upalabDi svaBAva tA iti
# de'i-'og-tu #  mthong-ba'i-lam #  ste / / de-nyid-la #  yang chos-kyi-dbyings #  kun-tu #  'gro-ba # r rtog-pa # s sa dang-po #  la 'jug ces bya'o / / 'di ni de-kho-na #  yid-la-byed-pa #  yin gyi / / tshad-med-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  mos-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa #  ni ma yin te / / dmigs-pa #  mi dmigs-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  gyi phyir ro zhes rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / de yi phyir na dmigs-pa #  ni / / mi dmigs ngo-bo-nyid #  du grub / / ces bya-ba #  gsungs so / / yang-na #  rnam-pa #  'dis so-so #  rang-gis #  rig-pa # 'i phyir /
aTa vA yat pUrvam pratijQAtam aBUta parikalpe dvayam na asti iti tat / anena AkAreNa pratyAtma vedya tvAt sidDam iti pradarSayan= Aha / upalabDeH tatas sidDAH na upalaBi svaBAva tA iti / tatas iti / upalaBya arTa aBAve upAlabDi aBAvAt
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  la gnyis med do zhes gang sngar dam-bcas-pa #  de grub po zhes rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / de yi phyir na dmigs-pa #  ni / / mi dmigs ngo-bo-nyid #  du grub / / ces bya-ba #  gsungs so / / de'i-phyir #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / dmigs-par-bya-ba # 'i don gyi dngos-po-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
upalabDiH iti BAva kartR karaNAnAm anyatamat parikalpyate / etat tritayam api aBAvAt na yujyate / upalabDeH tatas sidDAH na upalabDi svaBAva tA / atas eva vRtti kAraH Aha / upalaBya arTa aBAvaH upalabDi ayogAt iti / tasmAt ca samatA jQeyA na upalamBa upalamBayoH
# dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni dngos-po #  dang byed-pa-po #  dang byed-pa #  gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhig tu brtag grang na / / las med-pa # s de gsum char yang mi rung ste / / de'i-phyir #  dmigs-pa #  mi dmigs-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du grub po / / de nyid kyi phyir 'grel pa mdzad-pa # s dmigs-par-bya-ba # 'i don med na dmigs-pa # r mi-rung-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / de-lta-bas-na #  dmigs-pa #  dang mi dmigs-pa #  mnyam-pa # r shes-pa # r bya /
yasmAt upalabDiH anupalabDi svaBAvA tasmAt samatA tulya tA jQeyA
# 'di-ltar #  dmigs-pa #  ni mi dmigs-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du gyur te / / de'i-phyir #  mnyam mo /
arTa anupalamBasya vijQapti mAtra tA upalamBasya ca asattvAt aviSezatas / upalabDi anupalabDi SabdayoH paraspara virudDa tva apanaya na arTam Aha / aBUta arTa pratiBAsa tayA tu upalabDiH iti ucyate / na tu tayA kiQcid upalaByte arTa aBAvAt iti / atas paramArTataH anupalabDi svaBAvA api sati iti na asti viroDaH / aparaH Aha
# don mi dmigs-pa #  dang rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam du dmigs-pa #  yang med-pa # r bye-brag-med-pa # 'i phyir mtshungs-pa #  nyid-du #  shes-pa # r bya'o / / dmigs-pa #  dang mi dmigs-pa # 'i sgra dag phan tshun 'gal-ba #  bsal-ba # 'i phyir / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i don-du #  snang-ba # s dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / don-med-pa # s 'dis ni ci-yang #  mi dmigs so / / de'i-phyir #  don-dam-pa # r mi dmigs-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyang yin-pas #  'gal-ba #  med do /
yaH ca bAlAnAm asatya arTe arTa upalamBaH yaH ca AryANAm arTa anupalamBaH / tayoH dvayoH tulya lakzaNa tvAt samatA jQeyA sarpa BrAnti anupalabDi vat / atas eva bravIti aBUta arTa pratiBAsa tayA tu upalabDiH iti / ucyate anupalabDi svaBAvA api sati iti sarpa BrAntI anupalabDi vyapadeSa vat iti / anyaH punar Aha
# gzhan dag na re byis-pa #  rnams don-med-pa #  la don-du #  dmigs-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  dang 'phags-pa #  rnams don mi dmigs-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de gnyis mtshan-nyid #  mtshungs-pa # s mnyam-pa # r shes-pa # r bya ste / / sbrul du 'khrul-pa #  mi dmigs-pa #  bzhin no / / de nyid kyi phyir sbrul du 'khrul-pa #  mi dmigs-pa # r bshad-pa #  bzhin-du #  / / mi dmigs-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  yin yang / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i don-du #  snang-ba # 'i phyir dmigs-pa #  zhes bshad do zhes zer ro /
yaH ca bAlAnAm grAhaka upalamBaH yaH ca AryANAm arTa aBAvAt / grAhaka anupalamBaH tayoH dvayoH upalamBa anupalamBayoH ubahyataH api
# gzhan dag na re byis-pa #  rnams kyis 'dzin-pa # r dmigs-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  dang don-med-pa # 'i phyir-'phags-pa #  rnams kyis 'dzin-pa #  mi dmigs-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  dang dmigs-pa #  dang mi dmigs-pa #  de gnyis ni gnyi-ga #  yang gzung-ba #  med na /
sama tA jQeyA grAhye asati grAhaka aBAva aviSezAt / atas eva Aha aBUta arTa pratiBAsatayA iti vistaraH
# 'dzin-pa #  med-pa # r bye-brag-med-pa # 'i phyir mnyam-pa # r shes-pa # r bya ste / / de'i-phyir #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i don-du #  snang-ba # s zhes rgya-cher #  smos so zhe'o /
kecid tu manyante samAropA apavAda pratipakzeNa Aha / tasmAt ca samtA jQeyA na upalamBa upalamBayoH iti / arTa aBAvAt upalabDeH upalabDi svarUpa tvena aBAvAt svarUpeNa tat / aBAvaH ucyate
# yang kha-cig #  sems-pa #  sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r de-lta-bas-na #  dmigs-pa #  dang mi dmigs mnyam-pa # r shes-pa # r bya / / zhes gsungs so snyam ste / / don-med-pa # 'i phyir dmigs-pa #  ni dmigs-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  du med-pa # s / / ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  de med-pa #  zhes bya ste /
upalamBaH upalabDi svaBAvaH na apanIyate na api anupalabDi svaBAvaH / prakzipyate / kim tarhi samam etat uBayam nirvikalpa tayA
# dmigs-pa #  la dmigs-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  bsal-bar-bya-ba # 'am / / mi dmigs-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  yang gzhag-pa # r bya-ba #  med de / / de gnyis-ka #  yang rnam-pa # r brtag-tu #  med-pa # s mnyam-pa-nyid #  do; /
tasmAt na upalamBa upalamBayoH samAropa apavAda nirapekzeNa pratyAtma samatA / jQeya iti
# de-lta-bas-na #  sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-pa #  la mi ltos-pa # r dmigs-pa #  dang mi dmigs-pa #  gnyis so-so #  rang-gis #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  du shes-pa # r bya'o / / smras-pa #  /
Aha ca / na apaneyam atas kiQcid prakzeptavyam na kiQcana
# 'di-las #  bsal bya gang yang med / / gzhag-pa # r bya-ba # 'ang ci-yang #  med /
drazwavyam BUtataH BUtam BUta darSI vimucyate p / yadi evam kaTam vijQaptiH upalabDiH iti ucyate
# yang dag nyid la yang ngag lta / / yang dag mthong-ba #  rnam-pa # r grol / / gal-te #  de lta na ci'i-phyir #  rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam la dmigs-pa #  zhes bya zhe na / / mi dmigs-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  yin yang /
aBUta arTa pratiBAsa tayA loke SAstre ca taTA pratIta tvAt / anupalabDi svaBAvA api sati iti
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i don-du #  snang-ba # s / / 'jig-rten #  dang bstan-bcos #  las kyang de-bzhin-du #  grags-pa # 'i phyir ro /
praBeda lakzaNam KyApayati
# rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ston te zhes-bya-ba #  la /
kAma rUpA rUpya DAtu Atmakam aBUta parikalpasya praBedaH / nAnA prakAra tA / praBedaH eva lakzaNam iti praBeda lakzaNam anena / praBedena aBUta parikalpasya lakzaNAt
# 'dod-pa #  dang gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa'i-khams #  kyi bdag-nyid #  ni yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ste / / rnam-pa-tha-dad-pa #  nyid do / / rab-tu-dbye-ba #  nyid mtshan-nyid #  yin-pas #  / / rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  de / / rab-tu-dbye-ba #  'dis yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  mtshon pa'i phyir ro /
praBeda lakzaNaQca kim arTam KyApyate
# rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyang ci'i-phyir #  bshad ce na /
aBUta parikalpa mAtre kAma rUpaDAtu urayogAt
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  tsam la 'dod-pa #  dang gzugs-kyi-khams #  mi rigs te /
yaH ayam DAtu BAvena vipakza pratipakza Beda adrya pudgala Adi BedaH sa na / prApnoti iti mahAn SAsana upaplavaH prasajyate iti ASaFki udAsa arTam / praBeda lakzaNam AKyAtam / aTa vA yatra vitarka vicArOH tatra eva aBUta parikalpaH asti na
# khams tha-dad-pa # s mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang gnyen-po #  tha-dad-pa # 'i phyir-'phags-pa # 'i gang-zag #  la-sogs-pa # r tha-dad-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de thob-pa # r mi 'gyur te / / de-bas-na #  bstan-pa #  la nyes-pa #  chen-po # r 'gyur ro snyam pa'i dogs ba bsal-ba # 'i phyir rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  bshad do / / yang-na #  / / gang rtog-pa-dang-dpyod-pa #  yod-pa #  de nyid na /
tu anyatra iti yaH manyate tat apanayana arTam praBedalakzaNam ucyate / aBUta parikalpaH tu citta cEttAH tri DAtukAH
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  yod kyi gzhan ni ma yin no snyam ste / / de-bas-na #  de bsal-ba # 'i phyir / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog ni / / sems dang sems byung khams-gsum-pa #  / / zhes rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  brjod de gang na rtog-pa-dang-dpyod-pa #  yod-pa #  nyi tshe la ni ma yin no /
na tu yatra eva vitarka vicArO= iti / yaTA rUpam BUtAni BOtikaQcaH evam aBUta parikalpaH api cittam / cEttAH ca na kevalam cittam eva
# dper-na #  gzugs ni 'byung-ba #  rnams dang 'byung-ba-las-gyur-pa #  yin pa bzhin-du #  / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  yang sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  yin gyi / / sems 'ba'-zhig #  ni ma yin no /
te ca tri DAtuka svaBAvAH
# de-dag #  kyang khams-gsum-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  de /

# de-la #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun-tu-rtog-pa #  de-la # s sems-can #  dmyal-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  nyi shu gang dag 'byung-ba #  de ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  so /
ye saptadaSa prakArAH brAhkamAyika Adi AkArAH te rUpaDAtuH
# tshangs-rigs #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa-bcu #  bdun gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  ni gzugs-kyi-khams #  so /
yaH AkASa AnantyAya Ayatana Adi AkArAH catur prakArAH te ArUpya DAtuH / anyaH punar Aha aprahINakAma rAgAH aviBUta ArUpya saMjQAH ca / kAma avacaraH kAmaDAtuH / prahINa kAma rAgAH aviBUta ArUpya saMjQAH ca rUpa avacaraH rUpaDAtuH / prahINakAma rUpa rAgAH viBUtAH rUpya saMjQAH ca ArUpya avara / ArUpya DAtuH / kAma rAga anuSayitAH kAmaDAtuH
# nam-mkha' #  mtha' yas la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa-bzhi-po #  gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  ni gzugs-med-pa'i-khams #  so / / gzhan na re 'dod-pa-la-'dod-chags #  ma-spangs-pa #  dang gzugs-kyi-'du-shes #  dang ma-bral-ba #  rnams ni 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa # 'o / / 'dod-pa-la-'dod-chags #  spangs la gzugs-kyi-'du-shes #  dang ma-bral-ba #  rnams ni gzugs-kyi-khams #  so / / 'dod-pa #  dang gzugs la 'dod-chags #  spangs-shing #  gzugs-kyi-'du-shes #  dang yang bral-ba #  rnams ni gzugs-med-pa #  na spyod-pa # 'o zhes zer ro / / gzhan dag ni 'dod-pa-la-'dod-chags #  rgyas-pa # r gyur-pa #  rnams ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  so /
rUpa rAga anuSayitA rUpaDAtuH
# gzugs la 'dod-chags #  rgyas-pa # r gyur-pa #  rnams ni gzugs-kyi-khams #  so /
ArUpya rAga anuSayitAH ArUpya DAtuH iti anye p
# gzugs-med-pa #  la 'dod-chags #  rgyas-pa # r gyur-pa #  rnams ni / / gzugs-med-pa'i-khams #  so zhes smra'o /
satata cikzepakaH cEtasika duHKa prakArAH kAmaDAtuH
# kha-cig #  ni rtag-tu #  g-yeng ba dang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i sdug-bsngal-gyi-rnam-pa # 'i gnas-su-gyur-pa #  rnams ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  so /
samAhitA vigata cEtasika duHKa prakArAH rUpaDAtuH / samAhitAH prahINa muKa duHKa prakArAH ArUpa DAtuH iti apare
# mnyam-par-gzhag-pa #  la sems-las-byung-ba # 'i sdug-bsngal-gyi-rnam-pa #  dang bral-ba #  rnams ni gzugs-kyi-khams #  so / / mnyam-pa # r gzhag la bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  gyi rnam-pa #  spangs-pa #  rnams ni / / gzugs-med-pa'i-khams #  so zhes smra'o /
aprahINa ganDa rasa tad vijQAna abnhAsAH kAmaDAtuH
# kha-cig #  ni dri dang ro dang de-dag #  tu snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ma-spangs-pa #  rnams ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  so /
prahINa ganDa rasa tad vijQAna ABAsA rUpaDAtuH
# dri dang ro dang de-dag #  tu snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  spangs-pa #  rnams ni gzugs-kyi-khams #  so /

# khams bco lngar snang-ba #  spangs-pa #  rnams ni gzugs-med-pa'i-khams #  so zhes smra'o /
tezu sarvezu vyAKyAnezu katame te iti avaSyam pUrva vyAKyAna uktAH eva / vaktavyAH iti sa AkAFkzANi eva etAni vyAKyAnAni / aBUta parikalpa aDikAre
# bshad-pa #  de-dag #  thams-cad-la #  de-dag #  gang yin zhe na / / thog-mar #  bshad-pa #  las brjod-pa #  nyid bshad-par-bya #  ba ste / / de-ltar-na #  bshad-pa #  'di dag ni ltos-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  nyid do / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i skabs yin bzhin-du #  yang /
punar aBUta parikalpa grahaNam anupalabDi antarita tvAt iti / paryAya lakzaNaQca iti
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  smos-pa #  ni mi dmigs-pa # s bar-du #  bcad-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rnam-grangs #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  kyang ston te zhes-bya-ba #  ni /

# sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams kyi bye-brag #  rab-tu-bstan-pa # s / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i rnam-grangs #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  kyang ston to / / ji lta zhe na /
aBUparikalpya vastunaH svaBAva viSeza parikalpanayA citta cEttAnAm / pravRtta tvAt
# sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams yang-dag-pa #  ma yi pa kun rtog-pa # 'i dngos-po # 'i rang-bzhin #  dang khyad-par #  la rtog-pa # r zhugs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
arTa svarUpa viSeza dRzwiH citta cEttA aBUta parikalpaH ca iti / paryAya antarBUtAH
# don gyi rang-gi #  ngo bo dang bye-brag #  mthong-ba #  sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams dang yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rnam-grangs #  su gtogs-pa #  ste; don la ni khyad-par #  med do /
tatra arTa mAtre dRzwiH vijQAnam iti / mAtra SabdaH viSeza nirAsa arTaH
# de-la #  don tsam mthong-ba #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la tsam zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni /
tena agRhIta viSezAH vastu svarUpa mAtra upalabDiH iti arTaH
# khyad-par #  sel-ba # 'i phyir te khyad-par #  mi 'dzin gyi dngos-po # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo tsam dmigs so zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /

strI puruza Adi vyavahAra lakzaNaH yaH arTa viSezaH tat grahaNam saMjQA
# bud-med-dang-skyes-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r tha-snyad #  gdags-pa # 'i mtshan-ma #  don gyi khyad-par #  gang-yin-pa #  de 'dzin-pa #  ni 'du-shes #  so /

# de-ltar #  de-dag #  kyang gnas-pa #  dang dmigs-pa #  dang dus dang rdzas mtshungs-pa #  nyid kyis mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  yin gyi /

# rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang khyad-par-med-pa # r thal-ba # r 'gyur-ba # s rnam-pa # r mtshungs-pa # s ni ma yin no / / kha-cig #  ni 'dir sems-kyi-bye-brag #  nyid sems-las-byung-ba # r dgongs-pa # r shes te /
tet eva vijQAnam tAdRSa svarUpa AdinA vicitra pratiBAsam utpadyate / mayUra candrika vat / kaTam ekam vicitraQca
# rma-bya # 'i mdongs ltar rnam-par-shes-pa #  de nyid / / de-lta-bu # 'i ngo bo la-sogs-pa # r snang-ba #  sna-tshogs #  su 'byung ngo zhe'o / / ji-ltar #  na gcig-pu #  yang yin la sna-tshogs #  kyang yin / / gcig-pu #  du-ma # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du 'gyur du 'ong zhes /
na ekam hi lakzaNam loke vicitram izyate / mA BUt ekam aneka svaBAvam iti syAt eza p / dozaH yadi Darma svaBAvaH syAt / BrAnti mAtre tu na eza dozaH / kva taTA sarvaTA BAvAt / iti vacanAt
# 'jig-rten #  ni gcig la mi-mthun-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  sna-tshogs #  su mi 'dod do zhe na / / gal-te #  chos-kyi-ngo-bo-nyid #  yongs-su-grub-pa # r gyur na ni / / 'di yang nyes-pa # r 'gyur ro / / nor pa tsam la ni nyes-pa #  'di med de / / de-bzhin #  ma yin ye med min / / zhes bshad-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na etat evam sUtra vacana viroDAt / yA vedanA yA saMjQA yat cittam yat vijQAnaQca saMsRzwvA amI / DarmAH na visaMsRzwAH iti / saMsargaH ca nAma satAm yugapad ca Bavati iti
# de ni de lta ma yin te / / mdo las tshor-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  dang 'du-shes #  gang-yin-pa #  dang sems gang-yin-pa #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  ste chos 'di rnams ni 'dres-pa #  ste / / ma yin no zhes 'byung-ba #  dang 'gal-ba # 'i phyir ro / / 'dres-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni yod-pa #  rnams cig-car #  phrad-par-'gyur-ba #  la bya'o /
yaH hi Darma svaBAvam aparinizpannam icCati tasya etat sUtram / asmin= arTe ajQApakam iti
# gang chos-kyi-ngo-bo-nyid #  yongs-su-ma-grub-pa # r 'dod-pa #  de-la #  / / mdo de ni don 'dir khungs su mi rung ngo /
aBUta parikalpa mAtre anyasya ca aBAve hetu Pala praBA idam na vijQAyata / iti tat pratipAdana arTam pravRtti lakzaNaQca KyApayati / anena hetu Pala BAvenA BUta parikalpaH iti lakzaNam / pravRttiH eva lakzaNam pravRtti lakzaNam / pravRttiH punar divDA kzaNa paramparA pravRttiH yat Adi patyena
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  tsam du zad la gzhan-yang #  med-pa # s rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  rab-tu-dbye-ba #  rnam-pa # r mi-shes-pa # s de rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir 'jug-pa'i-mtshan-nyid #  kyang ston te / / 'dis yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # 'i dngos-po # r mtshon pa'o / / 'jug-pa #  nyid mtshan-nyid #  yin-pas #  'jug-pa'i-mtshan-nyid #  de / / 'jug-pa #  yang rnam-pa-gnyis #  so / / skad-cig #  brgyud mar 'jug-pa #  ste /
pratyutpannaH upaBoga saFkleSaH janma antara pravRttiH ca
# de'i dbang gis da-ltar-byung-ba # 'i nye-bar-spyod-pa # 'i kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang tshe-rabs-gzhan-du #  'jug ste /
yadA ADipatyena AyatyAm kleSa karma janma saFkleSaH

janma antara pravRttim saFkleSa lakzaNatvena KyApayizyati
# tshe-rabs-gzhan-du #  'jug-pa #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  du 'og nas 'chad do /
ekam pratyaya vijQAnam
# gcig ni rkyen gyi rnam-pa # r shes /
iti vistaraH / tatra ekam iti Alaya vijQAnam SezANAm saptAnAm vijQAnAnAm

hetu pratyaya BAvena hetuH iti pratyaya vijQAnam / dvitIyam OpaBogikam iti
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  lhag-ma #  bdun rnams kyi rgyu'i-rkyen #  gyi dngos-po # 'i rgyu yin-pas #  rkyen gyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o / / gnyis-pa #  nye-bar-spyod-pa #  can zhes-bya-ba #  ni /

# rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # r snyegs te /

vijQAna tvAt eka yogakzema tvAt ca
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang grub-pa-dang-bde-ba #  gcig pa'i phyir ro /

# kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  gzhan dag ni rgyu'i-rkyen #  yin-pas #  rkyen gyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
AlIyante sarve sa AsravAH DarmAH tatra Pala BAvena tat ca tezu
# zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i chos-thams-cad #  der 'bras-bu'i-dngos-po # r sbyor-ba #  dang de-yang #  de-dag #  la rgyu'i-dngos-po # r sbyor-ba # s kun-gzhi # 'o /

# sems-can #  dang snod-kyi-'jig-rten #  de-ltar #  snang-ba # s rnam-par-rig-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o / / de-yang #  cig tu rnam-par-smin-pa # s lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  nyid do /
sarvezAm sa AsravANAm DarmANAm bIjam anubaDnAti anyezAQca / pravRtti vijQAnAnAm hetu pratyayaH Bavati iti pratyaya vijQAnam
# zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i chos-thams-cad #  kyi sa-bon #  rjes-su-'brel-ba #  dang 'jug-pa #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  gzhan dag gi rgyu'i-rkyen #  yin-pas #  rkyen gyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o /
tat pratyayam pravRtti jQAna namaH upaBogikam iti
# de-la # s byung-ba #  'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni nye-bar-spyod-pa #  can no zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
tasmAt AlayavijQAnAt pratyeti iti tat pratyayam utpadyate iti arTaH / kaTam utpadyate
# kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  de-la # s byung-ba #  ste / / de'i rkyen gyis skye zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / ji-ltar #  'byung zhe na /
pravRtti vijQAnam hi AlayavijQAnAt pravartamAnam anutpannasya tat / jAtIyasya pravRtti vijQAnasya utpAdakam bIjam AlayavijQAne
# 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung-ba #  na de dang rigs gcig pa 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ma-byung-ba #  'byung-bar-byed-pa # 'i sa-bon #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la brtas-pa # r byed de /
paripuzNAti / tasmAt paripuzwa bIjAt pariNAma viSeza prAptAt punar tat jAtIyam / pravRtti vijQAnam utpadyate iti evam tat pratyayam pravRtti vijQAnam / Bavati / nanu AlayavijQAnam api OpaBogikam pravRtti vijQAna paQca
# sa-bon #  brtas nas 'gyur-ba # 'i bye-brag #  rnyed-pa #  de-la # s yang de dang rigs gcig la 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung ste / / de-ltar-na #  de'i rkyen gyis 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # r 'gyur ro / / bde-ba #  yang ma yin sdug-bsngal-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa # 'i tshor-ba # 'i nye-bar-spyod-pa # 'i gnas-su-gyur-pa #  dang kun kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la bag-chags #  bsgo-ba # 'i phyir / / kun-gzhi # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  yang nye-bar-spyod-pa #  can du 'gyur la /
pratyaya vijQAnam prasajyate aduHKa asuKa vedanA upaBoga ASraya tvAt / AlayavijQAne ca vAsanA BAvanAt / na pratyaya BAva vyatirekeNa anyA vAsanA aBAvanA asti / yaTA uktam aBiDarma sUtra gATAyAm / sarva DarmAH hi AlInAH vijQAne tezu tat taTA / anyonyam Pala BAvena hetu BAvena sarvadA iti / na prasajyate tat vedanAyAH durupalakzYa tvAt
# 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  yang rkyen gyi rnam-par-shes-pa # r 'gyur-ba # r thal-ba # r mi 'gyur ram / / rkyen gyi dngos-po #  ma-gtogs-par #  bag-chags #  bsgo-ba #  gzhan med de / / chos-mngon-pa # 'i mdo las tshigs-su-bcad-pa #  las ji-skad-du #  / / phan tshun 'bras-bu'i-dngos-po #  dang / / rgyu yi dngos-po # r rtog tu yang / / rnam-pa # r shes la chos kun sbyor / / de-yang #  de-bzhin #  de-dag #  la'o / / zhes gsungs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o zhe na / / thal-ba # r mi 'gyur te ci'i-phyir #  zhe na / / de'i tshor-ba #  shes-par-dka'-ba # s 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  bzhin-du #  nye-bar-spyod-pa #  can du mi shes sos /
na tad OpaBogika tvena lakzyate pravRtti vijQAna vat / prakarza gatam vA jQeyam sUrya vat / taTA hi upaBoga triviDa vedanA Sraya tvam pravRtti vijQAnasya eva na / tva Alaya vijQAnasya iti / hetu pratyayaH ca atra vivakzitaH na pratyaya mAtram / taTA hi kuSala akuSala Darma ADipatyAt AlayavijQAnam / vipAka nizyanda Pala vAsanAm parigRhNAti / avyAkRta Darma ADipatyAt ca nizyanda Pala vAsanAm eva iti / atas AlayavijQAnam niravaSezANAm sa asra vaDarmANAm hetu pratyayaH / pravRtti vijQAnam tu AlayavijQAnasya aDipati pratyayaH iti na asti / pravRtti vijQAnasya pratyaya tva prasaFgaH / upaBogaH vedanA iti / tri prakArA api upaBukzyate iti upaBogaH anuBUyate iti arTaH / Bava rasa sArasa rUpA vedanA / tasmE bAlAH tat saMvedana arTam vizayam aBiniviSante / na kevalam vedanA arTa upalabDiH api upaBogaH iti anye / tat ca naH upaBogaH vedanA iti BAzya viroDAt / arTa upalabDiH ca na vijQAnAt anyA iti na tasyAH ca etat tvam prayujyate / vedita paricCedaH saMjQA suKa Adi viSeza udgrahaNa Atmaka tvAt / upaBoge saMjQAyAn ca prerakAH saMskArAH vijQAnasya / cetanAmanaH kAra AdayaH p
# yang-na #  nyi-ma #  ltar khyad zhugs-pa # r shes-pa # r bya ste / / 'di-ltar #  nyes-par-spyod-pa #  tshor-ba #  rna pa gsum po'i gnas ni 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid yin gyi / / kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni ma yin no; / / 'dir ni rgyu'i-rkyen #  du 'dod kyi rkyen tsam du ni ma yin te / / 'di-ltar #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  kyi dbang gis rnam-par-smin-pa #  dang rgyu-mthun-pa'i-'bras-bu # 'i bag-chags #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'i chos kyi dbang gis rgyu-mthun-pa'i-'bras-bu # 'i bag-chags #  yongs su 'dzin to / / de'i-phyir #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i chos ma-lus-pa #  rnams kyi rgyu'i-rkyen #  to / / 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bdag-po'i-rkyen #  te / / rgyu'i-rkyen #  ma-yin-pa # s 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rkyen du thal-ba # r 'gyur-ba #  med do / / nye-bar-spyod-pa #  ni tshor-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la / / rnam-pa-gsum #  char yang nye-bar-spyod-pa # s nye-bar-spyod-pa #  ste / / myong-ba # r byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / srid-pa # 'i ro bro ba'i snying-po #  'dra-ba #  ni tshor-ba #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  byis-pa #  rnams de kun-tu #  myong-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir yul rnams la chags so / / kha-cig #  na re tshor-ba #  'ba'-zhig-tu #  ma zad kyi don-la-dmigs-pa #  yang nye-bar-spyod-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  zhes zer te /
aTa vA / upaBogaH vedanA iti yaTAsvam Alambana anuBAvAt / suKa Adi vedanIya karma anuBavanAt ca / evam vizaya karmaNoH upaBuktiH vedanA iti upaBogaH / vizaya cihnam vyavahAra nimittam paricCinnam karoti iti paricCedaH saMjQA / vijQAna antara AlambanaH ABogaH saMskArAH / tatas cetanA Adi ADipatyAt vijQAnam Alambana anantaram Bajate / Adi Sabdena CanDa AdayaH gRhyante / uktam yatas yAdRSaH yat arTA ca pravRttiH iti / tatra CAdanAt avidyayA yaTA BUta darSana avabanDanAt / ropaNAt saMskArEH vijQAne karma vAsanAyAH pratizWApanAt / nayanAt vijQAnena upapatti sTAna saMprApaNAt / samparigrahaNAt nAma rUpeNa Atma BAvasya / pUraNAt zaXa Ayatanena / tri paricCedAt sparSena / upaBogAt vedanayA / karzaNAt tRzNayA karma Akziptasya punar Bavasya / nibanDanAt upAdAnEH vijQAnasya utpatti anukUlezu kAma Adizu / ABimuKyAt Bavena kRtasya karmaNaH puarnBave / vipAka dAnAya aBimuKIkaraNAt
# bshad-pa #  las nye-bar-spyod-pa #  ni tshor-ba #  zhes 'byung-ba #  dang 'gal-ba # s de ni ma yin no / / don-la-dmigs-pa #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  las gzhan ma-yin-pa # s de sems-las-byung-ba # r mi rung ngo / / bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bye-brag #  'dzin-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  phyir tshor-ba #  yongs-su-spyod-pa #  ni 'du-shes #  nye-bar-spyod-pa #  dang 'du-shes #  la rnam-par-shes-pa #  'jug-par-byed-pa #  dag ni 'du-byed-rnams #  te / / sems-pa #  dang yid-la-byed-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / yang-na #  nye-bar-spyod-pa #  ni tshor-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / rang-gi #  dmigs-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  myong-ba # 'am / / bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  myong-bar-'gyur-ba # 'i las myong-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de-ltar #  yul dang las la spyod-pa #  ni tshor-ba #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  nye-bar-spyod-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / yul gyi don rtags tha-snyad #  kyi mtshan-ma #  yongs su gcod-par-byed-pa # s yongs gcod ni 'du-shes #  so / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  dmigs-pa #  gzhan la 'jug-par-byed-pa #  dag ni 'du-byed-rnams #  te / / de-ltar-na #  sems-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dbang gis rnam-par-shes-pa #  dmigs-pa #  gzhan la brten to / / sogs-pa # 'i sgras ni 'dun-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bsdu'o / / gang nas ci 'dra gang-gi-phyir #  'jug-pa #  ni bshad-zin #  to /
duHKhanA jantyA jarA maraNena ca parikliSyate jagat / saFkleSa lakzaNaQca KyApayati iti kleSa karma janma saFkleSAH yaTA
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyang ston to zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  dang las dang tshe'i kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams ji-ltar #  'byung-ba #  na /
pravartamAnAH jagataH parikleSAya Bavanti tat saFkleSa lakzaNam
# 'gro-ba #  yongs su nyon-mongs-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  de ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do /
taTA AcA sati api Atmani BUta parikalpa mAtrAt saMsAraH prajAyate / pradarSa nATam KyApyate / CAdana adropaNAt ca eva nayanAt samparigrahAt / iti vistaraH / saH ayam pravRtti pakzam aDi dvAdaSa aFgaH pratItyasamutpAdaH darSitaH / tatra CAdanAt
# de ni bdag-med-pa # r yang yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  tsam las 'khor-ba #  rgyas-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  / / rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir bshad de / / sgrib-pa # 'i phyir dang 'debs-pa # 'i phyir / / khrid pa'i phyir dang kun 'dzin phyir / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so / / rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba #  yan-lag-bcu-gnyis #  pa 'di yang 'jug-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi dbang du mdzad do / / de-la #  sgrib-pa # 'i phyir te /
kliSyate jagat iti anta vacanam sarveNa sambaDyate
# 'gro-ba #  nyon-mongs-pa # r byed do zhes tha-ma # r smos-pa #  ni thams-cad #  dang sbyar ro /
kena CAdanAt kaTam vA CAdanAt kliSyate iti
# gang-gis #  sgrib-pa #  ji-ltar #  sgrib-pa # 'i phyir nyon-mongs-pa # r byed ce na /
atas Aha / avidyayA yaTA BUta darSana vibanDAt iti
# de'i-phyir #  ma-rig-pa # s yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  mthong-ba #  la bgegs-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
avidyayA hi adarSana Atmaka tvAt BUta darSana vizaye pracCAdite
# ma-rig-pa #  ni mi mthong-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin-pas #  yang-dag-pa #  mthong-ba # 'i yul la rab tu sgrib-pa # 'i phyir /
BUta darSanam na utpadyate atas BUta darSana utpatti vibanDanAt avidyA / BUta darSana vibanDaH / BUta darSanam punar prADAnyena lokottara prajQA tat pRzWa udBava tvAt
# yang-dag-pa #  mthong-ba #  mi skye ste / / de'i-phyir #  yang-dag-pa #  mthong-ba #  skye-ba #  la bgegs-byed-pa # s ma-rig-pa #  ni yang-dag-pa #  mthong-ba #  la bgegs-byed-pa # 'o / / yang-dag-pa #  mthong-ba #  yang dngos su ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i shes-rab #  po /
tat pRzWa lABAt tat avagamAt ca tat prayogaH iti / Sruta cintA BAvanA mayI BUta darSanam iti ucyate
# de'i-rjes-la # s byung-ba # 'i phyir de'i-rjes-la # s thob-pa #  dang de'i rtogs-pa # 'i phyir de sbyong-bar-byed-pa #  thos-pa #  dang sems-pa #  dang bsgom-pa-las-byung-ba #  yang yang-dag-pa #  mthong-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  /
BUta darSana vibanDAt avidyA saMskArANAm pratyayaH iti evam CAdanAt
# yang-dag-pa #  mthong-ba # 'i bgegs-su-gyur-pa # s / / ma-rig-pa #  ni 'du-byed-rnams #  kyi rkyen zhes bya ste /
avidyayA kliSyate jagat iti p
# de-ltar #  sgrib-pa # 'i phyir ma-rig-pa # s 'gro-ba #  nyon-mongs-pa # r byed do /
ropaNAt kliSyate jagat iti sambaDyate
# 'debs-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  yang 'gro-ba #  nyon-mongs-pa # r byed ces bya-ba #  dang sbyar ro /
kena ropaNAt kva kasya vA iti atas Aha saMskArEH vijQAne karma vAsanAyA iti
# gang-gis #  gang-du #  ci 'dabs she na; de'i-phyir #  'du-byed-rnams #  kyis rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-la # s kyi bag-chags #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tatra saMskArAH yat kAyikam karma vAcikam mAnasam ca / puNya apuNya aniQjya svarUpam tat punar Bavam aBisaMskaroti iti saMskAraH / apraNihitam rohayati iti arTaH
# de-la #  'du-byed-rnams #  ni lus dang ngag dang yid-kyi-las #  bsod nams dang bsod nams ma-yin-pa #  dang mi g-yo-ba # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  gang-yin-pa # 'o / / de ni yang-srid-pa #  mngon-par-'du-byed-pa # s 'du-byed #  de / / ma btab-pa #  'debs zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
tat eva ca saMskAra Sabdena ucyate na tu sarvam / tat ca abidya ADipatyAt punar Bavam Akzeptum samarTam Bavati na
# de nyid-du #  'du-byed #  kyi sgrar bshad kyi thams-cad #  ni ma yin no / / de-yang #  ma-rig-pa'i-dbang #  gis yang-srid-pa #  'debs nus-pa # r 'gyur gyi /
sattA mAtreNa iti avidyA pratyayAH saMskArAH iti ucyate / taTA hi tAni anutpanna vidyasya punarBavam saMskurvanti na utpanna vidyasya
# yod-pa #  tsam gyis ni ma-yin-pa # s / / ma-rig-pa # 'i rkyen gyis 'du-byed-rnams #  zhes bya ste / / 'di-ltar #  ma-rig-pa #  ma skyes na de-dag #  yang-srid-pa #  'du-byed #  kyi /
na ca ADipatya mAtreNa eva avidyA saMskArANAm pratyayaH ucyate sAmAnyena / sA samutTAna pratyaya upari / aviDyA hi samprayuktvA aDyaTA sarva klezAnAm sAmAnyena / samutyAna pratyayaH tayA tat samudtyA nAm cetanAnAm api
# rig-pa #  skyes na ni ma yin no / / bdag-po #  tsam gyis ni ma-rig-pa #  'du-byed #  kyi rkyen zhes mi bya'i / / spyi'i rkyen yin-pas #  kun nas 'byung-ba #  na yang yin te / / 'di-ltar #  ma-rig-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-thams-cad #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i phyir / / ji-ltar #  nyon-mongs-pa #  kun nas 'byung-ba #  rnams kyi spyi'i rkyen yin pa de-bzhin-du #  de-la # s byung-ba # 'i sems-pa #  rnams kyi yang yin no /
api saMskArANAm Bava Boga Beda prArTanA anvayAnAm samutTAne tat
# bsod nams kyi 'du-byed #  srid-pa #  dang longs-spyod #  bye-brag #  can la smon-pa # 'i rjes-su-'gro-ba #  rnams kyi yang yin te /
saha BUtA avidyA sAmAnya pratyayaH
# kun nas 'byung-ba #  ni de dang lhan-cig-'byung-ba # 'i ma-rig-pa #  ni spyi'i rkyen yin no /
AniQjyAnAm api tat BUmi niHsara na dRzwi samutTAnAnAm tat / saha BUtA avidyA sAmAnya pratyayaH iti saMskArANAm pratyayaH uktaH
# mi g-yo-ba #  de-la #  nges-par-'byung-ba # r lta-ba #  kun-'byung-ba #  rnams kyi yang yin te / / de dang lhan-cig-'byung-ba # 'i ma-rig-pa #  ni spyi'i rkyen yin-pas #  / / 'du-byed #  kyi rkyen zhes bshad do /
vijQAnaH iti atra AlayavijQAnam aBipretam na tu pravRtti vijQAnam
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  la zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / 'dir kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la dgongs-pa #  yin gyi / / 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni ma yin te /
vyuparata pravRtti vijQAnasya utpatti sTAna nayanA samBavAt kuSala klizwayoH / ca samavaDAna aBAvAt saMskArEH tatra karma vAsanAyAH / pratizWApana aBAvAt
# rgyun-chad-pa #  dang 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # s skye-ba'i-gnas #  su khrid mi srid-pa #  dang dge-ba #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gnyis 'grogs mi srid-pa # s / / 'du-byed-rnams #  kyis de-la #  las kyi bag-chags #  gzhom mi srid-pa # 'i phyir ro /
karma vAsanAyAH iti / kA punar iyam karma vAsanA nAma
# las kyi bag-chags #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-la # s kyi bag-chags #  zhes-bya-ba #  'di gang yin zhe na /
anAgatasya janmanaH bIjam hetu BAvaH
# ma-'ongs-pa # 'i sa-bon #  te rgyu'i-dngos-po # 'o /
tat yaTA brIhi Palam BUmi Basma purIza Adi pratyaya viSezam apekzya
# dper-na #  'bru'i 'bras-bu #  sa dang thal-ba #  dang lung la-sogs-pa #  rkyen-gyi-bye-brag #  la ltos te /
pariNamat aFkura utpattO hetu BUtam bIjam iti
# 'gyur-ba #  las myu-gu #  'byung-ba # 'i rgyu'i-dngos-po #  ni sa-bon #  zhes-bya-ba #  lta-bu # 'o /
pratizWApanAt iti ropaNam eva paryAya antareNa Acazwe
# 'jog-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'debs-pa #  nyid kyi rnam-grangs #  gzhan bshad-pa # 'o /
pratizWApanam punar atra vijQAna santAne tat praTamatas tat bIjasya api
# 'jog-pa #  yang rnam-par-shes-pa'i-rgyud #  'di-la #  des thog-ma #  kho-na # 'i sa-bon #  de rgyas-par-byed-pa #  yin te /
Ayanam / na hi kasyacid sa Asravasya Darmasya anAsravasya iva apUrvam bIjam ADIyate
# zag-pa-med-pa # 'i ltar zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i chos ni 'ga' tsam gyis kyang sa-bon #  sngon ma-bskyed-pa #  med de /
evam saMskArEH vijQAne punarBAva bIja ADAnAt jagat kliSyate / nayanAt jagat kliSyate iti / kena nayanAt kva kasya vA iti na vijQAyate iti Aha vijQAnena utpatti
# 'di-ltar #  'du-byed-rnams #  kyis rnam-par-shes-pa #  la yang-srid-pa # 'i sa-bon #  skyed-pa # 'i phyir 'gro-ba #  nyon-mongs-pa # r byed do / / khrid pa'i phyir 'gro-ba #  nyon-mongs-pa # r byed do zhes-bya-ba #  gang-gis #  gang-du #  gang khrid pa mi shes-nas #  /
sTAna saMprezaNAt iti / karma pariBAvitena vijQAnena santAna vRttyA cyuti sTAnAt
# de'i-phyir #  rnam-par-shes-pa # s skye-ba'i-gnas #  su phyin par byed-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / las kyis yongs-su-bsgos-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rgyun-chags-su #  'jug-pa # s 'chi'o /
upapatti sTAne punar Bava bIja BUtAyAH vAsanAyAH prApaNam nayanam
# gnas nas skye-ba'i-gnas #  su yang-srid-pa # 'i sa-bon #  du gyur ba'i bag-chags #  phyin par byed / / khrid par byed do /
taTA ca sati na pratisanDi vijQAnam saMskAra pratyayam
# de-ltar #  byas-na #  nyid mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rkyen ni 'du-byed #  ma yin gyi /
pUrva kAla Bava vijQAnam eva p / saMskAra pratyayam iti pradarSitam Bavati
# sngon-gyi-dus #  kyi srid-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid kyi rkyen 'du-byed #  yin par rab-tu-bstan-pa #  yin te /
nahi vinazwAt kAraNAt kArya utpattiH yujyate
# rgyu zhig-pa #  las 'bras-bu #  'byung-ba # r mi rung ngo /
ArUpya samApa tIrABinaH hi yatra eva cyavante tatra eva utpadyante iti kaTam / ArUpyezu upapatti sTAna prApaNam iti tat yaTAyogam veditavyam / nAma rUpavat / samparigrahAt jagat kliSyate iti / kena samparigrahAt kasya vA iti atas Aha / nAma rUpeNa Atma BAvasya iti / nAma rUpam hi paQcaskanDAH
# gzugs-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  rnyed-pa #  rnams ni gang shi-ba #  de nyid-du #  skye-ba # s gzugs-med-pa #  rnams su ji-ltar #  skye-ba'i-gnas #  su phyin par byed ce na / / de ni ci-rigs-par #  shes-pa # r bya ste / / ming-dang-gzugs #  bzhin no / / kun 'dzin phyir 'gro-ba #  nyon-mongs-pa # r byed do zhes-bya-ba #  gang-gis #  gang-du #  gang yongs su 'dzin zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  ming-dang-gzugs #  kyi lus so zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / ming-dang-gzugs #  ni phung-po #  lnga'o /
te ca pratisaNDim upAdAya kalala arbuda peSI Gana praSAKa avasTA / anutpannaza Xa AyatanAH vijQAna pratyayam nAma rUpam iti
# de-dag #  kyang nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba #  nas-bzung-ste #  / / nur-nur-po #  dang mer-mer-po #  dang nar nar po dang gor gor po dang rkang-lag-'gyus-pa # 'i dus dang skye-mched-drug #  ma dod kyi bar-du #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rkyen gyis ming-dang-gzugs #  zhes bya ste /
tat BAvita viSezeNa hi anatarezu nikAya saBAgezu tat viSizwa tvam siDyati
# 'di-ltar #  de-la #  bsgos-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis rigs mthun-pa #  gzhan dag tu de bye-brag #  can du grub po /
tasmin= ca utpanne manuzya tiryak Adi nikAya sa BAga bedAt Atma BAvaH Bidyata / iti nAma rUpeNa Atma BAvaH parigRhItaH iti ucyate / aTa vA amaraNAt sarvam eva Atma BAvam parigRhNAti tat praTamatas / sarvasya hetu BAvena vyavasTAnAt iti / aTa vA aBinne api nAma rUpeNa ati tat praTamatas sarvasya hetu BAvena / vyavasTAnAt iti / aTa vA aBinne api nAma rUpeNa Atma BAvaH yaTA parigRhyeta tat pRTaktvena
# de skyes nas kyang mi dang dud-'gro #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rigs mthun-pa #  tha-dad-pa # 'i phyir lus kyang tha-dad-pa # s ming-dang-gzugs #  kyis lus yongs su 'dzin zhes-bya'o #  / / yang-na #  'chi-ba #  la thug gi bar-du #  lus thams-cad #  yongs-su-'dzin-pa #  ste / / de thog-ma-kho-nar #  thams-cad-kyi #  rgyu'i-dngos-po # r rnam-par-gnas-pa # 'i phyir / / yang-na #  dbyer med kyang ming gzugs kyis lus yongs su 'dzin to zhes 'di tha-dad-pa # r ston to /
darSayati yaTA sarvam saMskRtam paQcaBiH skanDEH saFgRhItam iti / OpapAdukAnAm tu vijQAna pratyayam zaXa Ayatanam eva iti atas / vijQAna pratyayam nAma rUpam yaTAsamBavam veditavyam
# dper-na #  'dus byas thams-cad #  phung-po #  lnga rnams kyis kun bsdus so zhes-bya-ba #  lta-bu # 'o / / rdzus te skye-ba #  rnams ni rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rkyen gyis skye-mched-drug #  nyid do / / de'i-phyir #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rkyen gyis ming-dang-gzugs #  ci-rigs-par #  shes-pa # r bya'o /
pUraNAt kliSyate iti / kena pUraNAt kasya vA iti / zaXa Ayatanena / nAma rUpa saFgRhItam SarIram / nAma rUpa avasTAyAm hi SarIram aparipUrNam ucyate cakzuH Adi / Ayatana aBAvAt
# rdzogs byed phyir 'gro-ba #  nyon-mongs-pa # r byed do zhes-bya-ba #  gang-gis #  gang-du #  gang rdzogs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir zhe na / / skye-mched-drug #  gis ming-dang-gzugs #  su bsdus-pa # 'i lus te 'di-ltar #  ming-dang-gzugs #  kyi tshe ni / / mig la-sogs-pa # 'i skye-mched #  med-pa # 'i phyir lus ma-rdzogs-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
asti ca tasyAm avasTAyAm kAya Ayatanam manA ayatanaQca tat api / aparipUrNam eva ASrita ASraya paripUrya BAvAt
# de'i tshe na lus kyi skye-mched #  dang yid kyi skye-mched #  yod mod kyi 'on-kyang #  brten-pa #  dang gnas yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r med ba'i phyir yongs-su-ma-rdzogs-pa #  nyid do /
zaXa Ayatana avasTAyAm punar cakzuH Adi aBinirvRttaH ASritaH paripUrNaH / Bavati
# skye-mched-drug #  gi dus na ni mig la-sogs-pa #  mngon-par-grub-pa # s gnas yongs-su-rdzogs-pa #  yin no /
kAya Ayatanam ca paripUrNam Bavati tat cakzuH Adi ASritAnAm / paripUrNa tvAt
# mig la-sogs-pa #  de-la #  brten-pa #  rnams yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # s lus kyi skye-mched #  kyang yongs-su-rdzogs-pa #  yin no /
kaTam tat cakzuH Adi ASritam / tat pratibadDa vRtti tvAt
# ji-ltar #  mig la-sogs-pa #  la brten zhe na de-la #  rag las te 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
manAayatanam api zaXu vijQAna saFgRhItam tadAnIm
# yid kyi skye-mched #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  drug gis bsdus-pa #  ste /
niravaSeza ASraya paripUritAt paripUrNam Bavati
# de'i tshe gnas-ma #  lus par yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # 'i phyir yongs-su-rdzogs-pa #  yin no /
aFga pratyaFga paripUritAH ca zaXa Ayatana avasTAyAm eva
# yan-lag #  dang nyid lag yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # 'i phyir skye-mched-drug #  gi dus nyid na /
ASraya paripUraNAt zaXa Ayatanena kliSyate jagat iti veditavyam
# gnas yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # s skye-mched-drug #  gis 'gro-ba #  nyon-mongs-pa # r byed ces bya'o /
tri paricCedAt jagat kliSyate iti sambaDyate / trayANAm hi indriya vizaya vijQAna sannipAte indriyasya
# gsum gcod phyir 'gro-ba #  nyon-mongs-pa # r byed do zhes-bya-ba #  dang sbyar ro / / gsum ni dbang-po #  dang yul dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  'dus so /
suKa Adi vedanA utpatti anukUlaH yaH tri prakAraH vikAraH tat paricCedaH sparSaH
# bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i tshor-ba #  'byung-ba #  dang mthun-pa #  dbang-po # 'i 'gyur-ba #  rnam-pa-gsum #  gang-yin-pa #  de yongs su gcod-pa #  ni reg-pa # 'o /
atas eva ayam indriya vikAra sAdyam spRSati tad AkAra tayA iti sparSaH ucyate a
# de-bas-na #  dbang-po # 'i 'gyur-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de'i rnam-pa #  dang 'dra-bar #  reg-par-byed-pa # s reg-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
aTa vA zaXa Ayatana pratyayaH sparSaH indriyasya suKa Adi vedanA anukUlam / triviDam vikAram prasUte / upaBogAt vedanayA iti / vedanA hi tRzNayA upaBujyate AsvAdyate iti arTaH
# yang-na #  skye-mched-drug #  gi rkyen gyis reg-pa #  ni bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa # r tshor-ba #  dang mthun-pa #  dbang-po # 'i 'gyur-ba #  rnam-pa-gsum #  skyed do; / / nye-bar-spyod-pa #  ni tshor-ba # s so zhes-bya-ba #  la / / tshor-ba #  ni srid-pa # s nye-bar-spyad-pa #  ste / / ro-myong-ba # r byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
puNya Adi karma upaBogAt vA vedanA upaBogaH
# yang-na #  bsod nams la-sogs-pa # 'i las la nye-bar-spyod-pa # s tshor-ba #  ni nye-bar-spyod-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
aTa vA upaBogaH atra vedanAyAH anuBavaH
# yang-na #  'dir nye-bar-spyod-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni tshor-ba #  myong-ba #  ste /
suKa Adizu ca anuBUyamAnezu tatra suKa Adi paripozaNAt
# bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  myong-ba #  na der bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  rgyas-pa # r gyur-pa # 'i phyir /
anurAga pratiGa mohEH kliSyate jagat / karzaNAt iti / karzaNAt kena kasya vA iti na vijQAyate iti atas Aha tRzNayA / karma Akziptasya punar Bavasya iti
# rjes-su-chags-pa #  dang khong-khro-ba #  dang gti-mug #  rnams kyis 'gro-ba #  nyon-mongs-pa # r byed do / / sdud-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  gang-gis #  gang sdud-pa #  mi shes so / / de'i-phyir #  las kyis btab-pa # 'i yang-srid-pa #  sred-pa # s so zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
saMskArEH vijQAne bIja paripozaNena Akziptasya punar Bavasya udaka / kalpayA tRzNayA sarva gatizu aviSezeNa Atma BAva aBilAzayA
# 'du-byed-rnams #  kyis yang-srid-pa # 'i sa-bon #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la gso-ba # 'i phyir btab-pa #  / / yang-srid-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i sa-bon #  chu dang 'dra-ba # 'i sred-pa #  /
yadA ArdrIkRtaH puar Bave utpattO= upayuFkte utpattim ca avasTApayati / tat karzaNam / nibanDanAt
# 'gro-ba #  thams-cad-du #  bye-brag-med-par #  lus 'dod-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # s brlan nas yang-srid-pa #  'byung-ba # r nye-bar #  sbyor zhing 'byung-ba #  nges-par #  'jog-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni sdud-pa # 'o /
kena nibanDanAt kva kasya vA iti praSna avakASe svayam eva Aha upAdAnEH / vijQAnasya upapatti anukUlezu kAma Adizu iti
# sbyor-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  la gang-gis #  gang-du #  gang zhig sbyor-ba #  dri-ba # r bya-ba # 'i skabs su bdag-nyid-kyis #  len-pa #  rnams kyis rnam-pa # r shas pa skye-ba #  dang mthun-pa #  'dod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rnams su'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
Candara Agala kzaNEH caturBiH upAdAnEH karma Akziptam vijQAnam / utpatti anukUlezu kAma dRzwi SIla vrata Atma vAdezu nibaDnAti avasTApayati
# mngon-pa # r zhan-pa #  dang 'dun-pa # 'i 'dod-chags #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  nye-bar-len-pa #  bzhi-po #  dag gis las kyis btab-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  skye-ba #  dang mthun-pa #  'dod-pa #  dang lta-ba #  dang tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  dang bdag-tu-lta-ba #  dag tu sbyor-ba # r byed 'jog-par-byed #  de /
ca vijQAnam hi cCanda rAga vaSAt tatra vartate
# 'di-ltar #  'dun-pa # 'i 'dod-chags #  kyi dbang gis rnam-par-shes-pa #  der gnas so /
ABimuKyAt iti atra api para praSna avakASe svayam eva ha Bavena kRtasya / karmaNaH punar Bava vipAka dAnAya aBimuKIkaraNAt iti
# mngon du'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  'dir yang gzhan gyis yongs-su-dri-ba # r bya-ba # 'i skabs su bdag-nyid-kyis #  las byas-pa # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa # s yang-srid-pa # r 'byin-pa # r mngon-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
yaTA nibanDanam vijQAnasya pUrva kRtam karma pOnarBavikam / vAsanA avasTAm vipAka Palam prati vRtti lamBanAt BavaH sat BUta / Akzipta BavaH ca nirvRttaye aBimuKIBavati evam Bavena aBimuKIkaraNAt / jagat kliSyate / duHKitAt jAtyA jarA maraNena ca / kim / kliSyate jagat iti
# ji-ltar #  sngon-byas-pa # 'i las rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rgyu yang-'byung-ba # s bag-chags #  kyi dus-su #  gyur-pa #  rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu # 'i phyir / / 'jug-pa #  rnyed-pa # s srid-pa #  yod-pa # r gyur cing srid-pa #  btab-pa #  'grub-pa # r mngon-du-gyur-pa #  ste / / de-ltar-na #  srid-pa # s mngon du'i phyir 'gro-ba #  nyon-mongs-pa # r byed do / / sdug-bsngal #  phyir ni skye-ba #  dang rga shis 'gro-ba #  nyon-mongs-pa # r byed-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
evam BavAt punarBava aBinirvRttO satyAm Aditas eva garBADAne / Sukra SoNite vijQAna sammUrcCanAt kliSyate
# de-ltar #  srid-pa #  las yang-srid-pa #  mngon-par-'grub-pa #  yod-pa #  thog-ma #  nyid-du #  mngal du zhugs-pa #  na khu-ba-dang-khrag #  gi nang na rnam-par-shes-pa #  myos-pa # s nyon-mongs-pa # r byed do /
taTA mAtuH AmASaya pakvASayayoH antarAle parivartanAt kliSyate
# de-bzhin-du #  ma'i-mngal #  du zhu-ba #  dang ma-zhu-ba # 'i gnas kyi bar na 'gre ldog-pa # s nyon-mongs-pa # r byed do /
taTA ca mAtuBojana caryayoH saFkawa Gunora parityAgAt api kliSyate
# yang de-ltar #  ma'i kha-zas #  dang spyod-pa #  nyam-nga-ba #  dang ya-nga-ba #  ma-spangs-pa # s kyang nyon-mongs-pa # r byed do /
taTA samBADe a aSucinA mArgeNa nirgacCati
# de-bzhin-du #  dog pa mi gtsang ba'i lam nas 'byung-ba # s nyon-mongs-pa # r byed do /
kliSyate jagat jAtam punar jarayA KAlitya pAli ityAdi lakzaNayA maraNena / ca nAma rUpa Beda lakzaNena priyAByAm yOvana jIvitAByAm BraSyamAnam / kliSyate jagat iti / gacCati iti jagat / saBA gAvakASAt kzaNa avakASam p / gacCati iti arTaH
# skyes nas kyang spyi cer dang skra skya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  rga-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang ming-dang-gzugs #  'jig-pa # 'i 'chi-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang lang-tsho #  dang srog phangs pa las nyams-pa # s 'gro-ba #  nyon-mongs-pa # r byed do / / 'gro-bar-byed-pa # s na 'gro-ba #  ste / / rigs mthun-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  nas skad-cig #  gi gnas-skabs #  su rab tu 'gro zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
kliSYataH iti jAti jarA vyADi maraNa AdiBiH trEDAtuke / kzaNa paramparayA aja aQjavIBAvena ca pIXyate iti arTaH / kliSyate iti na vyavadAyate iti apare
# nyon-mongs-pa # r byed ces bya-ba #  ni / / skye-ba #  dang rga-ba #  dang na-ba #  dang 'chi-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s khams-gsum #  du skad-cig-gcig #  nas gcig-tu #  brgyud-pa #  'ong zhing 'gro-ba # r gyur-pa # s nyen zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / kha-cig #  na re rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i ma-yin-pa # s nyon-mongs-pa #  zhes bya zhe'o /
evam ayam saFkleSa lakzaNaH dvAdaSa aFgaH / pratItyasamutpAdaH CAdana Adi ekAdaSaBiH arTEH vyavadAna vipakzaH
# de-ltar #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba #  yan-lag-bcu-gnyis #  pa 'di ni sgrib-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  don rnam-pa-bcu #  gcig gis rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  su 'gyur ro /
avidyA Adi utpatti kramaH pUrva pUrvasya uttara uttara AvAhanAt / treDA saFkleSaH kleSa saMkleSaH karma saFkleSaH janma saFkleSaH ca / tatra kleSa saFkleSaH avidyA tRzNA upAdAnAni / karma saFkleSaH saMskArAH BavaH ca / janma saMkleSaH SezANi aFgAni / dveDA saMkleSaH hetu saMkleSaH Pala saMkleSaH ca / tatra hetu saMkleSaH kleSa karma svaBAvEH aFgEH / Pala saMkleSaH ca SezEH / saptaDA saMkleSaH saptaviDaH hetuH viparyAsa hetuH Akzepa hetuH / upanaya hetuH parigraha hetuH upaBoga hetuH AkarzaNa hetuH udvega hetuH ca / tatra viparyAsa hetuH avidyA / Akzepa hetuH saMskArAH / upanaya hetuH vijQAnam / parigraha hetuH nAma rUpa zaXa Ayatane / upaBoga hetuH sparSa vedane / AkarzaNa hetuH tRzNA upAdAna BavAH / udvega hetuH jAti jarA maraNe / sacaScEza saMkleSaH aBUta parikalpAt pravartate iti / kativiDaH punar anena dvAdaSa aFgena na pratItyasamutpAdena samAsatas / saMkleSaH pradarSitaH iti atas eva idam ucyate saH ayam dvAdaSa aFgaH / pratItyasamutpAdaH / treDA dveDA ca saMkleSaH saptaDA iti / ca SabdaH samuccaya arTaH parivarta arTaH ca / kleSaH eva saMkleSaH iti kleSa saMkleSaH / evam karma janma saMkleSO / kleSaH hi pravartamAnaH sva para AtmanoH vyAbADaka tvAt saMkleSaH / yaTA uktam sUtre api raktaH rAga parItaH Atma vyAbADAya api cetayate / para vyAbADAyAH api cetayate / uBaya vyAbAdAya api cetayate / evam dvezaH mohaH ca api veditavyaH iti / karma janma saMkleSayoH ca utpAdaka tvAt saMkleSaH / taTA hi kleSa ADipatyena karma janma Akzipati dRzwa satyasya sati api karmaNi / punar Bava Akzepa aBAvAt kleSa samudAcAreNa punar Bava bIjasya / BavIkaraNAt klizwa cittasya ca punarBava pratisanDi banDAt janma / saFkleSena eva hetunA / tatas arhataH pratisanDi banDa aBAvaH klizwa citta aBAvAt / karma ca SuBa aSuBam tadAtve kAya cittayoH AyAsa nimitta tvAt / Ayati AQca vipAka dAnAt saFkleSaH / janmA api sarva upadrava Aspada tvAt saFkleSaH iti / treDA saFkleSaH / hetoH dviDA BedAt / kleSa saFkleSaH vidyA tRzNA upAdAnAni iti tritayam api kleSa Atmaka tvAt / karma saFkleSaH saMskArAH BavaH ca iti p / dvayam api karma Atmaka tvAt / ayantu viSezaH / svarUpa avasTam karma saMskArAH bIja avasTam BavaH iti / janma saMkleSaH SezANi aFgAni iti / vijQAna nAma rUpa zaXa Ayatana sparSa vedanA jAti jarA maraNAni ezAm / janma saFgRhIta tvAt / dveDA saMkleSaH hetu PalAByAm praBidyate / hetu saMkleSaH kleSa karma svaBAvEH aFgEH / Pala saMkleSaH ca SezEH aFgEH iti / tatra hetu saMkleSa tvam karma kleSAnAm vijQAna Adi vedanA paryantam / jAti Atmakam jarA maraNa AdIn avajanma sampAdayitum aBipravRtta tvAt / Pala saMkleSaH ca SezEH vijQAna AdiBiH karma kleSa Pala tvAt / punar saH eva pratItyasamutpAdaH saptaDA saMkleSaH iti / viparyAsa Akzepa upanaya parigraha upaBoga AkarzaNa udvega hetutvAt saptaviDaH

 lhag-ma #  rnams te / / de-dag #  ni tshe'i nang-du #  'dus-pa # 'i phyir ro / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnam gnyis ni rgyu mi dbye-ba # r byas-pa #  ste / / rgyu'i kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  dang las-kyi-ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi yan-lag #  rnams kyis so / / 'bras-bu # 'i kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  ni yan-lag #  lhag-ma #  rnams kyis so / / de-la #  las dang nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  tshor-ba #  la thug-pa #  skye pa'i bdag-nyid-can #  dang rga shi'i nyes-dmigs #  can gyi tshe skyed-pa # r rab tu zhugs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / 'bras-bu # 'i kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  ni lhag-ma #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rnams kyis te / / las dang nyon-mongs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  yin pa'i phyir ro / / rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba #  de nyid kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnam-pa #  bdun zhes bya ste / / phyin-ci-log #
