hetuH / tatra viparyAsa hetuH avidyA iti / avidyA gataH hi tattva sammohAt anitya AdIn nitya Adi rUpeNa viparyasyati iti
# rgyu bdun po de lta ma-rig-pa #  ni phyin-ci-log #  gi rgyu'o zhes-bya-ba #  la / / ma-rig-pa # r gyur-pa #  ni de-kho-na #  nyid la rmongs-pa # 'i phyir / / mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la rtag-pa # 'i ngo bor mthong-ba # s phyin-ci-log #  ces bya'o /
Akzepa hetuH saMskArAH iti vijQAne caturaFga Atma janma bIjasya / pratizWApanAt
# 'du-byed-rnams #  ni 'debs-pa # 'i rgyu'o zhes-bya-ba #  la / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  la yan-lag #  bzhi'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  tshe'i sa-bon #  'jog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
upanaya hetuH vijQAnam iti iha cyutasya upapatti viza Ye upanayanAt
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni nye-bar #  khrid pa'i rgyu'o zhes-bya-ba #  la 'dir shi-'phos-nas #  skye-ba # 'i yul du nye-bar #  khrid pa'i phyir ro /
parigraha hetuH nAma rUpa zaXa AyatanaH iti upanItasya / nAma rUpa zaXa AyatanAByAm nikAya saBAga parigrahAt / pUrvam nAma rUpeNa eva parigrahaH uktaH jarAyu ja AdikAm yonim aBipretya / idAnIm upapAdukam aDikRtya zaXa Ayatanena api parigrahaH uktaH / aTa vA nAma rUpeNa tat praTamatas Atma BAva mAtrasya saFgrahaH
# ming-dang-gzugs #  dang skye-mched-drug #  ni kun 'dzin-pa # 'i rgyu'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni khrid par gyur-pa #  ming-dang-gzugs #  dang skye-mched-drug #  gi ris-mthun-pa #  kun 'dzin-pa # 'i phyir ro / / sngar mngal nas skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i skye-gnas #  la dgongs nas ming-dang-gzugs #  kyis kun 'dzin-pa # r bshad do / / da-ni #  brdzus te skye-ba # 'i dbang du mdzad de skye-mched-drug #  gis kyang 'dzin to zhes bshad do /
vivakzitaH / iha tu aparipUrNasya paripUrNasya ca iti na asti viroDaH
# yang-na #  ming-dang-gzugs #  kyis thog-ma #  nyid-du #  lus tsam 'dzin-pa # r brjod-pa # r bzhed-pa # 'o / / 'dir ni yongs-su-ma-rdzogs-pa #  dang yongs-su-rdzogs-pa #  'dzin-pa # s 'gal-ba #  med do /
upaBoga hetuH sparSa vedanaH iti
# reg-pa #  dang tshor-ba #  ni nye-bar-spyod-pa # 'i rgyu'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
sa kAraNena anuBavena kuSala akuSala karma vipAkasya upaBogAt
# rgyu-dang-bcas-pa # 'i myong-ba # s dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba'i-las #  kyi rnam-par-smin-pa #  la nye-bar-spyod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
AkarzaNa hetuH tRzNA upAdAna BavAH iti
# sred-pa #  dang len-pa #  dang srid-pa #  ni sdud-pa'i-rgyu # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
saH upaBukta karma vipAkaH bAlaH tasyAm tasyAm vedanAyAm tRzyati
# byis-pa #  las kyi rnam-par-smin-pa #  la spyod-pa #  de tshor-ba #  de-dang-de #  la sred-pa # r byed de srid-pa #  'phel nas /
vivRdDa tRzNaH ca tat saMyoga tRzNayA kAma AdIn upAdatte
# yang de dang ldan zhing mi-'bral-ba # r sred-pa # s 'dod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  len to /
tat upAdAnAt ca asya pUrva BUtam pOnarBavikam karma vAsanA avasTam / pariNatam yaTA Akzipta vipAka dAnayA pravRttim labDvA BavaH Bavati
# de blangs-pa # s kyang de'i las sngon byung-ba #  yang-srid-pa #  / / bag-chags #  su gnas-pa #  yongs su gyur na ji-ltar #  btab-pa #  bzhin-du #  rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i 'byin-pa # 'i phyir; 'jug-pa #  rnyed nas srid-pa # r 'gyur ro /
sa ca tRzNA upAdAna BavaH saMskAra AkziptaH punar Bava aBinirvRttaya / AkRzyate aBimuKIkriyate iti tRzNA upAdAna BavAH AkarzaNa hetuH
# de-yang #  'du-byed #  kyis btab-pa # 'i yang-srid-pa #  mngon-par-grub-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir / / srid-pa #  dang len-pa #  dang srid-pa #  rnams kyis sdud cing mngon-pa # r 'du-byed #  ces bya-ba # s / / sred-pa #  dang len-pa #  dang srid-pa #  rnams ni sdud-pa'i-rgyu # 'o /
aTa vA tRzNA vaSena cCanda rAga anurUpAni atara karma vAsanA aBimuKAt / tRzNA upAdAna BavAH AkarzaNa hetuH / udvega hetuH jAti jarA maraNe iti evam atra jarma AkarzaNAt tasmin= tasmin
# yang-na #  sred-pa # 'i dbang gis 'dun-pa # 'i 'dod-chags #  dang mthun-pa #  gang-yang-rung-ba # 'i las kyi bag-chags #  mngon-du-byed-pa # 'i phyir / / sred-pa #  dang len-pa #  dang srid-pa #  ni bsdus-pa # 'i rgyu'o / / skye-ba #  dang rga shi ni skye-ba'i-rgyu # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
sattva nikAye jAti jarA maraNa duHKam anyat ca / Soka parideva duHKa dOrmanasya upAya asaduHKam ananta praBA idam anuBavati iti
# de-ltar #  'di ni tshe drangs bas sems-can #  gyi rigs de-dang-der #  skye-ba #  dang rga shi'i sdug-bsngal #  dang mya-ngan #  dang smre-sngags-'don-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  dang yid-mi-bde-ba #  dang 'khrugs-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal #  rab-tu-dbye-ba #  mtha'-yas-pa #  gzhan-yang #  myong-ba # r 'gyur ro /
p / tatra triDA saFkleSA aBiDAnena kleSa karmaNaH
# de-la #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  du brjod-pa # s nyon-mongs-pa #  dang las ni /
sADAraNa asADAraNa hetu tvam darSitam
# tshe'i rgyu thun mong dang thun mongs ma-yin-pa #  rab tu bstan to /
kleSaH hi janma aFkurasya sADAraNa kAraNam BUmi Adi vat
# nyon-mongs-pa #  ni sa la-sogs-pa #  ltar tshe'i myu-gu # 'i thun mong gi rgyu'o /
karma tva sADAraNa kAraNam aFkurasya iva bIjam tat Bedena jana BedAt iti / aTa vA na atra pUrva anta aparAnta maDyAntAni trINi kANXAni kim tarhi
# las ni thun mong ma yin te / / myu-gu # 'i sa-bon #  ltar de tha-dad-pa # s tshe tha-dad-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yang-na #  'dir sngon-gyi-mtha' #  dang phyi-ma'i-mtha' #  dang-ba # r gyi mtha' zhes-bya-ba #  rabs gsum du ni ma yin gyi /
karma kleSa PalAni iti pradarSayati
# las dang nyon-mongs-pa #  dang 'bras-bu #  yid zhes rab tu ston to /
dviviDa aBiDAnena hetu Pala mAtram eva idam na atra anyaH saFkliSyate
# rnam-pa-gnyis #  su brjod-pa # s 'di nyid rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  tsam du zad de / / 'di-la #  byed-pa-po # 'am /
kArakaH vedakaH vA iti pradarSayati / aTa vA atra karma kleSa mAtram eva hetuH / tayoH BAva aBAvAt janma BAva aBAva darSanAt / atas tat Palam eva janma
# tshor-ba #  po kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  gzhan med do zhes rab tu ston to / / yang-na #  'dir las dang nyon-mongs-pa #  tsam nyid rgyu ste / / de-dag #  yod-pa #  dang med-pa # s tshe yod-pa #  dang med-pa # r snang-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de'i-phyir #  tshe ni de'i 'bras-bu-nyid #  do /
tasmAt na atra hetuH Palam vA sarvatra paQca skanDikA avasTA iti / pradarSayati
# de-lta-bas-na #  'di-la #  rgyu 'am 'bras-bu #  ni med kyi dus skabs thams-cad-du #  yang phung-po #  lnga nyid do zhes rab tu ston to /
saptaDA hetu nirdeSena punar dviviDaH pratItyasamutpAdaH pradarSitaH / Akzepa lakzaNaH aBinirvRtti lakzaNaH ca iti / tatra Akzepa lakzaNaH pratItyasamutpAdaH saptyaBiH aFgEH nirdizwaH / yena akzIpyate yaTA Akzipyate yat ca Akzipyate tat pradarSanAt
# rgyu rnam-pa #  bdun bshad-pa # s ni 'phen-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang mngon-par-'grub-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  du yang rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  su rab tu bstan to / / de-la #  'phen-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni gang-gis #  'phen-pa #  dang ji-ltar #  'phen-pa #  dang gang 'phen-pa #  de rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
aBinirvRtti lakzaNaH paQcaBiH aFgEH tasya Akziptasya yena aBinirvRttiH / yaTA aBinirvRttiH yA ca aBinirvRttiH tasya aQca yaH AdIn avaH iti
# rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba # 'i yan-lag #  bdun gyis bstan to / / mngon-par-'grub-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni 'phags-pa #  de gang-gis #  mngon-par-'grub-pa #  dang ji-ltar #  mngon-par-'grub-pa #  dang gang mngon-par-'grub-pa #  dang de'i nyes-pa #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir yan-lag-lnga # s so /
kena akzIpyate / avidyA pratyayEH saMskArEH yaTA tattvam mugDvA viparItam saMjAnAti
# gang-gis #  'phen zhe na ma-rig-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  kyis te / / ji-ltar-de #  kho-na #  la rmongs nas phyin-ci-log #  tu shes te /
kuSala akuSala aniQjyAn saMskArAn aBisaMskAroti
# dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  dang mi g-yo-ba # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  mngon-pa # r byed do /
kaTam Akzipyate tEH saMskArEH
# 'du-byed #  de-dag #  gis ji-ltar #  'phen zhe na /
vijQAne bIja pozaNAt utpatti Bavya tAyAm avasTApanAt / kim Akzipyate
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  las sa-bon #  gsos pas skye-ba # r nus-pa # r gnas-pa # 'i phyir ro / / ci gzhig 'phen zhe na /
pOnarBavikam nAma rUpam zaXa Ayatanam sparSaH vedanA ca yaTAyogam
# yang-srid-pa #  ba'i ming-dang-gzugs #  dang skye-mched-drug #  dang reg-pa #  dang tshor-ba #  ste ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
tat evam Akziptam kena aBinirvartyate
# de-ltar #  'phangs-pa #  de gang-gis #  mngon-par-'grub-pa # r byed ce na /
yaTA ukta krameNa pUrva Akzipta Adi hotpannAm vedanAm pratItya yA / tRzNA utpannA tat pratyayena upAdAnena
# ji-skad #  bshad-pa # 'i rim-gyis #  snga-ma #  'phangs-pa # s 'dir skyes-pa # 'i tshor-ba #  la brten-nas #  sred-pa #  skyed-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  byung-ba # 'i len-pa # s so /
kaTam tena aBinirvartyate
# ji-ltar-de # s mngon-pa # r 'grub ce na /
tasya vijQAne vAsanA avasTasya karmaNaH tena BavIkaraNAt
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  la bag-chags #  su gnas-pa # 'i las de / / des srid-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
bahuviDA hi vijQAne karma vAsanA vartate / vicitra saMskAra pariBAvita tvAt
# 'du-byed #  sna-tshogs #  kyis yongs-su-bsgos-pa # 'i phyir / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-la # s kyi bag-chags #  rnam-pa #  mang-po #  gnas te /
upAdAna viSeza parigraheNa yena atra punar Bavatvam vartate saH atra Bava / ucyate / kA punar sa aBinivruttiH
# len-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis yongs-su-gzung-ba # 'i phyir / / gang-gis #  'di-las #  yang-srid-pa #  gnyis-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  de ni 'dir srid-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / mngon-par-'grub-pa #  de gang yin zhe na /
yA tasya Akziptasya nAma rUpa Adikasya AyatyAm jAtiH / tasyAam punar satyAm kaH AdInavaH
# ming-dang-gzugs #  la-sogs-pa #  'phangs-pa #  des phyis skye-ba #  gang-yin-pa # 'o / / de yod-pa # s nyes-par-'gyur-ba #  gang yin zhe na /
jarA maraNam priya yOvana jIvita BraMSA Adi iti / atra tu upanaya hetuH nirarTam iti ced na nirarTakaH / vicCinna maraNAt Bava upapatti Bava pravRtti aDigamanirA karaNa arTam / sarve ca ete saFkleSAH aBUta parikalpAt pravartante iti / citta cEtta ASraya tvAt saFkleSasya / uktam hi tat / aBUta parikalpaH ca citta cEttAH tri DAtukAH / iti p / aBUta parikalpa piNXa arTaH / piNXa arTaH punar aBUta parikalpasya navaviDam lakzaNam paridIpitam / Bavati / sat lakzaNam asat lAkzaNam sva lakzaNam saFgraha lakzaNam / asat lakzaNA anupraveSa upAya lakzaNam praBeda lakzaNam paryAya lakzaNam / pravRtti lakzaNam saMkleSa lakzaNaQca / piNXa arTaH punar aBUta parikalpasya iti vistareNa arTa nirdeSaH / suKa avaboDa arTam piNXa arTa nirdeSaH avismaraNa arTa Qca / tatas atra arTa dvayam uktam / sat lakzaNam / aBUtaparikalpaH asti iti / asat lakzaNam / dvayam tatra na vidyate iti
# rga shi de-la # ng tsho dang srog phangs pa 'jig-pa # 'i phyir ro / / 'dir nye-bar #  khrid pa'i rgyu ni don med do zhe na don-med-pa #  ma yin te / / 'chi-ba'i-srid-pa #  chad nas skye-ba'i-srid-pa #  'byung-ba # r rtog-pa #  bsal-ba # 'i phyir ro / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  'di dag thams-cad #  ni yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  las 'byung ngo zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i gnas yin pa'i phyir te / / de-yang #  / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog ni / / sems dang sems byung khams-gsum-pa #  / / zhes bshad-pa #  yin no / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i don bsdus-pa #  ni zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / don rgyas-par-bshad-pa #  bde blag tu khong-du-chud-pa # r bya-ba #  dang mi-brjed-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir don bsdus-pa #  bstan to / / de'i-phyir #  'dir ni don gnyi-ga #  yang bshad do / / yod-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / ces bya'o / / med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni / / de-la #  gnyis po yod ma yin / / zhes-bya-ba # 'o / / rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  ni /
sva lakzaNam / arTa sattva Atma vijQapti pratiBAsam prajAyate / vijQAnam iti / saFgraha lakzaNam / kalpitaH paratantraH ca parinizpannaH eva ca iti
# don dang sems-can #  bdag rnam rig / / snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni / / rab tu skye'o zhes-bya-ba # 'o / / bsdu-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni / / rtag ba dang ni gzhan dbang dang / / yongs-su-grub-pa #  nyid kyang ngo /
asat lakzaNa anupraveSa upAya lakzaNam
# zhes-bya'o #  / / med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  la 'jug-pa # 'i thabs kyi mtshan-nyid #  ni /
upalabDim samASritya na upalabDiH prajAyate / ityAdi / praBeda lakzaNam
# dmigs-pa #  la ni brten-nas #  su / / mi dmigs-pa #  ni rab tu skye / / zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni /
aBUta parikalpaH ca citta cEttAH tri DAtukAH iti / paryAya lakzaNam
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog ni / / sems dang sems byung khams-gsum-pa #  / / zhes-bya-ba # 'o / / rnam-grangs #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  ni /
tarTa arTa dRzwiH vijQAnam tat viSeze tu ca etasAH iti / pravRtti lakzaNam
# de-la #  don mthong rnam-pa # r shes / / de yi bye-brag #  sems las byung / / zhes-bya'o #  / / 'jug-pa'i-mtshan-nyid #  ni /
ekam pratyaya vijQAnam dvitIyam OpaBogikam iti / saMkleSa lakzaNam / CAdanAt ropaNAt ca eva nayanAt samparigrahAt / ityAdi
# gcig ni rkyen gyi rnam-pa # r shes / / gnyis-pa #  nye-bar-spyod-pa #  can / / zhes-bya'o #  / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni / / sgrib-pa # 'i phyir dang 'debs-pa # 'i phyir / / khrid pa'i phyir dang kun 'dzin phyir / / zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
evam aBUta parikalpam nava prakAram KyApayitvA yaTA SUnyatA / vijQeyA tat nirdeSati iti kaH atra aBisambanDaH
# de-ltar #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  rnam-pa #  dgur brjod nas stong-pa-nyid #  ji-ltar #  shes-par-bya-ba #  de ston te zhes-bya-ba #  'dir ji-ltar #  sbyar zhe na /
dvayam anena pratijQAtam aBUta parikalpaH SUnyatA ca p / saMkleSa pUrvakam ca vyavadAnam / Darma avaboDa ASraya Qca Darma tA avaDAraNam / iti atas aBUta parikalpa nirdeSa anantaram yaTA SUnyatA vijQeyA taTA / nirdiSati / lakzaNaQcA aTa paryAya / iti vistaraH
# 'dis yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  dang stong-pa-nyid #  dang sngar kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  la rnam-par-byang-ba #  dang chos khong-du-chud-pa #  la brten-nas #  chos-nyid #  nges-par-'dzin-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  gnyis dam-bcas-pa #  yin te / / de'i-phyir #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  / / stong-pa-nyid #  ji-ltar #  shes-par-bya-ba #  de-ltar #  'chad de / / mtshan-nyid #  dang ni rnam-grangs #  dang /
tatra lakzaNam hi BAva aBAva pratizeDa Atma tA sarvatra / SUnyaTApraBeda vyApaka tvAt
# zhes rgya-cher #  ro / / de-la #  mtshan-nyid #  ni dngos-po #  dang dngos-po-med-pa #  dgag-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  de / / stong-pa-nyid #  kyis rab-tu-dbye-ba #  thams-cad-la #  khyab-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nAma antaram paryAyaH
# ming gzhan ni rnam-grangs #  so /
paryAya anuguNam paryAya pravRtti nimittam paryAya arTaH / AkASa vat aBinna lakzaNa tvAt nirvikalpa tve api
# rnam-grangs #  dang mthun-pa #  rnam-grangs #  'jug-pa'i-rgyu #  ni rnam-grangs #  kyi don to / / nam-mkha' #  ltar tha-mi-dad-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyi phyir /
Agantu kopa kleSa saMyoga viyoga avasTA BedAt BedaH
# rnam-pa # r mi rtog kyang glo-bur #  gyi nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang phrad-pa #  dang bral-ba # 'i dus-tha-dad-pa # s dbye-ba # 'o /
anyaH ca pudgala Darma samAropa BedAt BedaH zoXa SaviDaH
# gzhan-yang #  gang-zag #  dang chos su sgro-'dogs-pa #  tha-dad-pa # s dbye-ba #  rnam-pa-bcu #  drug go /
sADanam SUnyatA praBeda pradarSane yuktiH
# sgrub-pa #  ni stong-pa-nyid #  kyi rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ston-par-byed-pa # 'i rigs-pa # 'o /
kim punar kAraNam yat eBiH prakArEH SUnyatA vijQAtavyA
# ci'i-phyir #  rnam-pa #  de-dag #  gis stong-pa-nyid #  shes-pa # r bya zhe na /
viSudDi Alambana tvAt viSudDi arTiBiH lakzaNataH vijQeyA
# rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  yin-pas #  na / / rnam-par-dag-pa #  'dod-pa #  rnams kyi mtshan-nyid-shes-pa # r bya'o /
sUtra antarezu paryAya nirdeSezu asammoha arTam paryAya arTaH
# mdo gzhan dag las rnam-grangs #  bshad-pa #  rnams la mi rmongs-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir rnam-grangs #  so /
paryAya arTA avaboDa arTAt SUnyatAyAH viSudDi Alambana tvena / niScita tvAt paryAya arTaH / saMkleSe nirAkRte sA viSudDa iti tat saMkleSa prahANAya / yatna utpAdana arTam BedataH / Beda sADana avaboDAt vikAra aBAve sati api Bedam suKam pratipadyata / iti Beda sADanataH api vijQeyA iti / pRTaktve sati DarmAt anyA Darma tA iti na yujyate anitya tA duHKa tAvat / ekatve sati viSudDi Alambanam jQAnam na syAt sAmAnya lakzaNaQca / etena tat tvA anyatva vinirmuktam lakzaNam paridIpitam Bavati / kaTam lakzaNam vijQeyam iti lakzaNam hi prAk uddizwam iti atas tat eva / praTamatas pRzwam / dvayA aBAvaH hi aBAvasya BAvaH SUnyasya lakzaNam p / iti vijQeyam / dvayasya grAhyasya grAhakasya ca aBUta parikalpe aBUta parikalpena vA / parikalpita Atmaka tvAt vastu rUpeNa aBAvaH aBAvaH
# rnam-grangs #  kyi don khong-du-chud-pa # r gyur na stong-pa-nyid #  la rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  nyid-du #  nges-pa # 'i phyir rnam-grangs #  kyi don to / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  bsal na / / de rnam-pa # r dag go zhes kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  de spangs-pa # 'i phyir 'bad-pa #  skyed-pa # 'i don-du #  dbye-ba # 'o / / dbye-ba # 'i sgrub-pa #  khong du chud na / / 'gyur-ba #  med kyang dbye-ba #  bde blag tu rig-pa # 'i phyir dbye-ba # 'i sgrub-pa #  yang shes-pa # r bya'o / / mtshan-nyid #  ji-ltar #  shes-pa # r bya zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / mtshan-nyid #  sngar smos-pa # s de'i-phyir #  de nyid dang-por #  'dri ste / / gnyis dngos med-pa # 'i dngos-po #  yi / / dngos-po #  stong-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do / / zhes-bya-ba # r shes-pa # r bya'o / / gnyis ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  la'am / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # s kun-brtags-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin-pas #  dngos-po # 'i ngo bor med do /
tasya ca dvaya aBAvasya yaH BAvaH etat SUnya tAyAH lakzaNam
# gnyis-pa #  dngos-po-med-pa #  de'i dngos-po #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni stong-pa-nyid #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  do /
kArikA anuguNyAt ca atra BAva pratyaya lupta nirdeSaH drazwavyaH
# tshig le'ur byas-pa #  dang mthun-par #  byas-pa # 'i phyir 'dir yang dngos-po # 'i rkyen ma smos-pa # r bstan-pa # r lta-ba # 'o /
aBAvasya BAvaH iti kim etat
# dngos-po-med-pa # 'i dngos-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  de-dag #  gang yin /
aBAvasya Atma tvam astitvam / anyaTA dvaya BAvasya astitvam eva syAt / tat BAvasya BAvataH avidyamAnatvAt / atas eva Aha / iti aBAva svaBAva lakzaNa tvam SUnya tAyAH paridIpitam Bavati na / BAva rUpa lakzaNam iti / BAva pratizeDa vAcaka tvAt aBAva Sabdasya
# dngos-po-med-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  ni yod-pa-nyid #  do / / gzhan-du-na #  de'i dngos-po-med-pa # 'i dngos-po #  stong-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gnyis kyi dngos-po-yod-pa #  nyid-du #  'gyur ro / / de'i-phyir #  de-ltar #  dngos-po-med-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  stong-pa-nyid #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  du yongs-su-bstan-pa #  yin no zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / dngos-po # 'i ngo bo'i mtshan-nyid #  du ni ma yin no / / dngos-po-med-pa # 'i sgra ni dngos-po #  dgag-pa # 'i tshig yin na /
BAva Sabda aBAve api ezaH arTaH avagamyate iti BAva SabdaH atra aDikaH na aDikaH
# dngos-po # 'i sgra med kyang don 'di khong-du-chud-pa # r 'gyur-ba # s / / dngos-po # 'i sgra ni 'dir lhag go /
dvaya aBAvaH SUnyatA lakzaNam iti iyati nirdiSyamAne dvaya aBAvasya / svAtantryam eva atra gamyate SaSavizANa aBAva vat na duHKa tA Adi vat
# lhag-ma #  ma yin te gnyis kyi dngos-po-med-pa #  stong-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do zhes de tsam zhig bshad na / / gtsor gnyis kyi dngos-po-med-pa-nyid #  du ri-bong-gi-rva #  dngos-po-med-pa #  dang 'dra-bar #  khong du chud de / / sdug-bsngal #  nyid la-sogs-pa #  ltar chos-nyid #  kyi ngo bor mi rung ngo /
Darma tA rUpa tA / tasmAt evam ucyate dvaya aBAvaH SUnyatA / tasya ca aBAvasya aBAvasya BUta parikalpe BAvaH SUnyate asti
# de-lta-bas-na #  'di skad ces bya ste / / gnyis kyi dngos-po-med-pa #  ni stong-pa-nyid #  do / / dngos-po-med-pa #  de ni yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  la yod de /
aBAvasya BAva lakzaNa parigRhIta tvAt Darma tA rUpa tA pradarSitA / aTa vA dvaya aBAvaH SUnyatA iti aBAva Sabdasya sAmAnya vAcitAn na
# stong-pa-nyid #  ces bya-ba #  ste dngos-po-med-pa # 'i dngos-po # 'i mtshan-nyid #  yongs-su-gzung-ba # 'i phyir chos-nyid #  kyi ngo bor bstan-pa #  yin no / / yang-na #  gnyis kyi dngos-po-med-pa #  stong-pa-nyid #  ces bya-ba #  la /
vijQAyate katamaH atra aBAvaH aBipretaH iti atyantA aBAva pradarSana arTam / ucyate aBUta parikalpe dvaya aBAvasya BAvaH iti / na hi prAk aBAva praDvaMsa aBAvO svopadAnAt anyatra AKyAtum yujyete / anyonya aBAvasvasya ca eka aSra tvam na yujyate uBaya ASrita tvAt
# med-pa # 'i sgra ni thun mong yin-pas #  'dir med-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  gang-la # s dgongs-pa #  mi-shes-pa # s / / gtan med-pa # r rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir-yang #  dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  la / / gnyis po'i dngos-po-med-pa # 'i dngos-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  brjod do / / snga na med-pa #  dang zhig-nas #  med-pa #  gnyis ni rang-gi #  nye-bar-len-pa #  las gzhan-du #  bshad-pa # r mi rigs so / / gcig-la-gcig #  med-pa #  yang gnyi-ga #  gnas yin pa'i phyir / / gcig-tu #  gnas-pa # r mi rigs so /
tasmAt BAvasya aBAva lakzaNa upAdAnAt grAhya grAhakayoH atyanta aBAva / eva SUnyatA iti etat jQApitam Bavati
# de'i-phyir #  dngos-po # 'i dngos-po-med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  nye-bar #  bzung-ba # s / / gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  dag gtan dngos-po-med-pa-nyid #  stong-pa-nyid #  ces bya-ba # r de shes-pa # r byas-pa #  yin no /
yadi aBAva AtmikA SUnyatA kaTam paramArTaH ucyate
# gal-te #  med-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  stong-pa-nyid #  yin na / / don-dam-pa #  zhes ji-skad-du #  bya zhe na /
parama jQAna vizaya tvAt anitya tAvat na tu vastu tvAt / api ca aBAva svaBAvaH na ezaH / yasmAt yavA asO tat aBAva svaBAvaH sa / na BAvaH nA api ca eva / kaTam na BAvaH / yasmAt dvayasyA aBAvaH
# ye-shes-dam-pa # 'i yul yin-pas #  mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  bzhin-du #  ste / / dngos-po # 'i phyir ni ma yin no / / de lta mod kyi de ni dngos-po-med-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyang ma yin te / / 'di-ltar #  de'i dngos-po-med-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni / / yod-pa #  ma yin med-pa # 'ang min / / ji-ltar-yod-pa #  ma yin zhe na / / 'di-ltar #  gnyis po'i dngos-po-med-pa #  ste /
BAva tve hi na dvaya BAvasya atyanta aBAvaH syAt
# yod-pa #  ni gnyis kyi dngos-po #  gtan med-pa # r yang mi 'gyur la /
nA aBUta parikalpa Darma tA / kaTam na aBAvaH
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i chos-nyid #  du yang mi 'gyur ro / / ji-ltar #  med-pa # 'ang ma yin zhe na /
yasmAt dvaya aBAvasya BAvaH
# 'di-ltar #  gnyis po'i dngos-po-med-pa # 'i dngos-po #  ste /
na hi dvaya aBAvaH dvaya aBAva svarUpeNa aBAvaH
# gnyis kyi dngos-po-med-pa #  ni gnyis kyi dngos-po-med-pa # 'i ngo bor med-pa #  ma yin te /
saH aBAvaH ced dvayasya astitvam syAt na ca syAt aBUta parikalpasya
# de med du zin na gnyis yod-pa-nyid #  du 'gyur zhing / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i chos-nyid #  du yang mi 'gyur te /
DarmatA yaTA nitya duHKa tA
# dper-na #  mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  nyid bzhin no /
sattvasya viparyAsa tvena samAropitasya / nitya suKa BAva aBAva svarUpa tvAt na BAvaH na api aBAvaH iti ucyate
# sems-can #  phyin-ci-log #  tu gyur-pa # s sgro-btags-pa # 'i rtag-pa #  dang bde-ba # 'i dngos-po # 'i dngos-po-med-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  yin-pas #  / / yod-pa #  yang ma yin med-pa #  yang ma yin zhes-bya'o #  /
yadi punar aBUta parikalpasya SUnyatA Darma tA asti kim asO tasmAt anyaH / vaktavyaH uta ananyaH iti atas bravIti
# gal-te #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa # 'i stong-pa-nyid #  chos-nyid #  yin na / / ci ste de-la # s gzhan zhes-bya-ba # 'am / / 'on te gzhan ma yin zhe na /
etat ca SUnyatAyAH lakzaNam iti / aBAvasya svarUpam eva p
# de'i-phyir #  de ni stong-pa-nyid #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  do zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / dngos-po-med-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kho-na # 'o /
aTavA BAvaH eva aBAva pratizeDa AtmakaH
# yang-na #  dngos-po #  kho-na #  dngos-po-med-pa #  dgag-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  kho-na # 'o /
tasmAt aBUta parikalpAt / na pRTaktvA eka lakzaNam / pRTaktve sati DarmAt anyA Darma tA iti na yujyate / kaH punar ayogaH
# de-lta-bas-na #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  dang tha dad gcig pa'i mtshan-nyid #  min / / tha-dad-pa #  yin na ni chos-nyid #  las chos-nyid #  gzhan yin pa mi rung ste /
DarmAt viBinna lakzaNa tvAt Darma tA Darma antaram eva Bavati tat / anya Darma vat / na ca Darma antaram Darma antarasya Darma tA Bavitum arhati tatra punar / Darma antaram anvezwavyam iti anavasTA prasaFgAt / anitya tA duHKa tAvat iti / yaTA anitya tA anityeByaH na anyA duHKa tA ca duHKAt eva SUnyatA api na
# ji-ltar #  mi rung zhe na chos las mtshan-nyid-tha-dad-pa # s chos-nyid #  chos gzhan nyid-du #  'gyur te / / de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i chos bzhin no / / chos gzhan ni chos gzhan gyi chos-nyid #  du mi rung ste / / de-la #  yang chos gzhan btsal dgos-pa # s thug-pa #  med-pa # r 'gyur ro / / mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  nyid bzhin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / ji-ltar #  mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  mi-rtag-pa #  rnams las gzhan ma-yin-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  nyid kyang sdug-bsngal-ba #  las gzhan ma-yin-pa #  de-ltar #  stong-pa-nyid #  kyang stong-pa #  las gzhan ma-yin-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
SUnyAt anyA iti / ekatve sati viSudDi Alambanam na syAt sAmAnya lakzaNaQca iti
# gcig pa yin-du-zin #  na ni rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  dang spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  du mi 'gyur ro /
viSudDyate anena iti viSudDiH mArgaH Darma sva lakzaNAt ananyatvAn
# 'dis rnam-par-dag-pa # r byed-pa # s rnam-par-dag-pa #  ni lam mo / / chos kyi rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  las gzhan ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
mArga Alambanam na syAt Darma sva lakzaNa vat / tasmAt ca na sAmAnya lakzaNam yujyate / sva lakzaNAt ananyatvAt
# chos kyi rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  bzhin-du #  lam gyi dmigs-pa # r mi 'gyur ro / / de'i-phyir #  rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  las gzhan ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir / / spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  du yang mi rung ngo /
tasya api Darma sva rUpa vat parasparataH BedaH iti sAmAnya tA hIyate / aTa vA sva lakzaNasya tasmAt anya tvAt BAva svarUpa vat Beda aBAvaH
# de-yang #  chos kyi rang-gi #  ngo bo dang 'dra-bar #  phan tshun tha-dad-pa # s mnyam-pa-nyid #  nyams-pa # r 'gyur ro / / yang-na #  rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  de-la # s gzhan ma-yin-pa # s dngos-po # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo tha-dad-pa #  med do /
tatas ca sAmAnya lakzaNasya api aBAvaH Beda apekza tvAt
# de'i-phyir #  spyi yang med-pa # r 'gyur te / / spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  ni tha-dad-pa #  la ltos-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sAmAnya lakzaNasya / aTa vA viSudDi arTam Alambanam viSudDi Alambanam na BAva sva lakzaNam / AlambyamAnam viSudDim Avahati sarva sattva viSudDi prasaFgAt / yadi anyAn anyatvena avaktavyA kaTam nirgranTa vAdaH nA AlambitaH Bavati / yaH hi BAvasya sataH tattva anya tvena vyAkaroti tena nirgranTavAt / Alambyate / SUnya tA tu na BAvaH iti na asti ayam dozaH
# yang-na #  rnam-par-dag-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir dmigs-pa #  ni rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i dmigs-pa # 'o / / dngos-po #  ni rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  la dmigs-pa # s rnam-par-dag-pa #  thob-pa #  med de / / sems-can-thams-cad #  rnam-par-dag-pa # r thal-ba # r 'gyur ro / / gal-te #  gzhan dang gzhan ma-yin-pa # r mi brjod na / / gcer-bu #  ba smra-ba #  la 'chel bar de-ltar #  mi 'gyur / / dngos-po-yod-pa #  la de nyid dam gzhan-du #  lung mi ston-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de gcer-bu-pa # 'i smra-ba #  la 'chel bar 'gyur ro / / stong-pa-nyid #  ni dngos-po-med-pa # s skyon du 'gyur-ba #  'di med do /
etena SUnyatA sat lakzanA aBAva sva rUpa lakzaNA dvaya lakzaNA
# de-ltar #  stong-pa-nyid #  'di ni med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang dngos-po-med-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  dang mi gnyis-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  de /
tattvAni atva vinirmukta lakzaNA ca paridIpitA
# de nyid dang gzhan-las #  rnam-par-grol-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  yongs-su-bstan-pa #  yin no /
uktam SUnyatA lakzaNam / paryAyaH idAnIm ucyate / taTatA BUtakowiH api nimittam / DarmaDAtuH ca paryAyAH SUnyatAyAH samAsatas iti
# stong-pa-nyid #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  bshad-zin #  to / / de ni rnam-grangs #  brjod-pa # r bya'o / / stong-pa-nyid #  ni mdor-bsdu-na #  / / de-bzhin-nyid #  dang yang dag mtha' / / mtshan-ma #  med dang don dam dang /
paryAyaH nAma ekasya arTasya Binna SabdEH pratyAyanam / paryAya arTa aBiDAnam iti paryAyaH ucyate
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  ni rnam-grangs #  so / / zhes-bya-ba #  la / / rnam-grangs #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni don gcig la sgra tha-dad-pa # r grag-pa #  ste rnam-grangs #  kyi don brjod-pa # s rnam-grangs #  zhes-bya'o #  /
tAni aBiDAnAni sUtra antarezu SUnyatA eva nirdiSyante
# brjod-pa #  de rnams ni mdo gzhan dag las stong-pa-nyid #  du ston to /
etat ca paryAya paQcakam yaTApraDAnam gATAyAm uktam evam anye api / paryAyAH iha anuktAH pravacanAt upaDAryAH p
# rnam-grangs #  lnga po de-dag #  gtso bo yin par tshigs-su-bcad-pa #  las ji-skad #  smos-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  rnam-grangs #  gzhan 'dir ma smos te / / gsung-rab #  las khong-du-chud-pa # r bya-ba #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  /
tat yaTA advayatA avikalpaDAtuH Darma tA anaBilapyatA aniroDaH / asaMskRtam nirvANa Adi / kaTam paryAya arTaH vijQeyaH iti etat darSayati / na ete SabdAH gONAH kim tarhi anvarTAH iti
# mi gnyis-pa #  nyid dang rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i dbyings dang chos-nyid #  dang brjod-du-med-pa #  nyid dang mi 'gag-pa #  nyid dang 'dus-ma-byas #  pa dang mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / rnam-grangs #  kyi don ji-ltar #  shes-pa # r bya zhe na / / de ston te sgra de-dag #  ni brtags-pa #  ma yin gyi / / don-dang-ldan-pa #  rnams zhes bya ste /
ananyaTA aparyAsatan niroDa Arya gocarEH
# gzhan min phyin-ci-log #  ma yin / / de 'gag 'phags-pa # 'i spyod yul dang /
hetu tvAt ca Arya DarmANAm paryAya arTaH yaTAkramam iti
# 'phags-pa # 'i chos kyi rgyu yi phyir / / rnam-grangs #  don de go-rims #  bzhin / / zhes-bya'o #  /
ananyaTA arTena taTatA iti avikAra arTena iti arTaH / tat eva pradarSana arTam Aha nityam taTA eva iti kRtvA / nityam sarvadA saMskRta tvAt na vikriyataH iti arTaH / aviparyAsa arTena BUtakowiH / BUtam satyam aviparItam iti arTaH / kowiH paryantaH yatas pareNAni ajjQeyam na asti iti atas BUtakowiH / BUta paryantaH ucyate / kaTam taTatA jQeyam ucyate
# de-la #  gzhan ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir de-bzhin-nyid #  de zhes-bya-ba #  ni mi-'gyur-ba # 'i don to zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / de nyid bstan-pa # 'i phyir rtag-tu #  de-bzhin #  pa'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / rtag-par #  dus-thams-cad #  'dus-ma-byas #  pa yin-pas #  mi 'gyur zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / phyin-ci-log #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir-yang #  dag-pa # 'i mtha' ste zhes-bya-ba #  la yang-dag-pa #  ni bden-pa #  dang ma nor-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / mtha' zhes-bya-ba #  ni mu-med-pa #  ste / / gang phan chad nas shes-par-bya-ba #  gzhan med-pa # 'i phyir-yang #  dag-pa # 'i mtha' ste / / yang-dag-pa # 'i mu zhes-bya'o #  / / ji-ltar-de #  bzhin nyid shes-par-bya-ba #  mu zhes bya zhe na /
jQeya AvaraNa viSoDana jQAna gocara tvAt
# shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i ye shes kyi spyod yul yin pa'i phyir ro /
aviparyAsa arTena iti anaDyA ropa anapavAda arTena
# phyin-ci-log #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur ba 'debs-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
atra eva kAraNam Aha viparyAsA vastu tvAt iti
# 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  phyin-ci-log #  gi gzhi ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ste /
viparyAsaH hi vikalpaH
# phyin-ci-log #  ni rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'o /
vikalpA Alambana tvAt na viparyAsavaH tu
# rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ma-yin-pa # s phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'o /
nimitta niroDa arTena animittam iti
# mtshan-ma #  'gog-pa # 'i phyir mtshan-ma-med-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
atrA nimitta tvam nimitta niroDaH ucyate
# 'dir mtshan-ma-med-pa #  la mtshan-ma #  'gog-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
etat eva pradarSana arTam Aha / sarva nimitta aBAvAt iti
# 'dir rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir mtshan-ma-thams-cad #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
sarvEH eva saMskRta asaMskRta nimittEH SUnyatA SUnyA iti animittam ucyate / sarva nimittA aBAvAt animittaH / animittam eva animittaH
# 'dus byas dang 'dus-ma-byas #  kyi mtshan-ma-thams-cad #  kyi stong-pa-nyid #  stong-pa # s mtshan-ma-med-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / mtshan-ma-thams-cad #  med-pa # 'i phyir mtshan-ma-med-pa #  ste / / mtshan-ma-med-pa-nyid #  mtshan-ma-med-pa # 'o /
Arya jQAna gocara tvAt paramArTaH iti paramam hi loka uttara jQAnam / tat arTaH paramArTaH / etat eva pradarSayan= Aha parama jQAna gocara tvAt iti / Arya Darma hetu tvAt DarmaDAtuH
# 'phags-pa # 'i ye shes kyi spyod yul yin-pas #  don-dam-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  la / / dam-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i ye shes te / / de'i don ni don-dam-pa # 'o / / 'phags-pa # 'i chos kyi rgyu yin-pas #  chos-kyi-dbyings #  te zhes-bya-ba #  la / / chos kyi sgra ni 'dir 'phags-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  te /
Darma Sabdena atra Arya DarmAH samyak dRzwi AdayaH samyak / vimukti jQAna paryantAH ca iti
# yang-dag-par-lta-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dang yang-dag-par #  rnam-par-grol-ba #  dang ye shes la thug-pa #  rnams la bya ste /
tad hetutvAt DAtuH
# de-dag #  gi rgyu yin-pas #  dbyings so /
tat eva viBAvayan= Aha Arya DarmANAm tat Alambana praBa tvAt iti
# de nyid bstan-pa # 'i phyir-'phags-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  ni de-la #  dmigs-pa # s byung-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
sva lakzaNa upAdAya rUpa DAraNe api ayam DAtu SabdaH vartate iti Aha / hetvarTaH hi atra DAtvarTaH / tat yaTA p / suvarNa DAtuH tAmra DAtuH rOpya DAtuH
# rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  dang rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  'dzin-pa #  la yang khams kyi sgra 'di 'jug-pa #  de'i-phyir #  / / 'dir dbyings kyi don ni rgyu'i don to zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / dper-na #  gser khung dang zangs khung bzhin no /
sUtra antarezu anye paryAyAH uktAH api anena eva nyAyena sva arTe / nirdezwavyAH
# mdo gzhan-las #  rnam-grangs #  gsungs-pa #  gzhan dag kyang 'di'i tshul du don bdag-gis #  brtag-pa # r bya'o /
SUnyatAyAH grAhya grAhaka aBAva rUpa tvAt Bedam asamBAvayan pRcCati
# stong-pa-nyid #  ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  med-pa # 'i ngo bo yin-pas #  tha-dad-pa #  mi srid de /
aTavA paryAya arTa anantaram BedaH vijQeyaH iti uktam atas
# 'dri-ba # 'am yang-na #  rnam-grangs #  kyi don gyi 'og-tu #  dbye-ba #  shes-par-bya-ba # r bstan-pa # s /
tad nirdeSa anantaram pRcCati kaTam SUnya tAyAH praBedaH vijQeyaH iti
# de'i-phyir #  de bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  stong-pa-nyid #  kyi rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ji-ltar #  shes-pa # r bya zhe na zhes dris so /
aBUta parikalpaH hi saMkleSaH tasya prahANam viSudDiH ucyate
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'o / / de spangs na rnam-par-dag-pa #  zhes bya ste /
saFkleSa viSudDi kAle ca SUnyatA avyatiriktam anyat na asti yat saFkliSyate / viSudDyate vA
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i dus na yang stong-pa-nyid #  ma-rtogs-pa # r gang kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'am / / rnam-par-byang-ba # r 'gyur-ba #  gzhan med do /
tasmAt saMkleSa viSudDi kAlayoH SUnyatA eva saFkliSyate viSudDyate ca iti / pradarSana arTam Aha / saFklizwA ca viSudDA ca / iti asyAH praBedaH / kadA saFklizwA kadA nirmala iti anavaboDAt pRcCati kasyAm / avasTAyAm saMklizwA kasyAm ca viSudDa iti / samalA nirmalA ca sA / iti vistaraH
# de-lta-bas-na #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa #  gnyis kyi dus na yang / / stong-pa-nyid #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa # 'o zhes rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro / / kun nas nyon mongs rnam-pa # r dang / / ces bya-ba #  ste / / de'i rab tu dbye'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / gang-gi-tshe #  nyon mongs la / / gang-gi-tshe #  dri-ma-med-pa #  khong du-ma #  chud nas / / gang-gi-tshe #  kun nas nyon mongs la / / gang-gi-tshe #  rnam-pa # r dag ce na zhes dris-pa #  dang de ni dris bcas dri-ma #  med /
ASrayA aparAvRtti parAvRtti apekzayA samalA ca prahINa malA ca / vyavasTApyate
# ces rgya-cher #  ro / / gnas-gyur-pa #  dang ma-gyur-pa #  la ltos-pa # s / / dri-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  dang dri-ma #  spangs-pa # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
yezAm aviduzAm grAhya grAhakA aBiniveSa rAga Adi kleSa malinAnAm / citta santAnAnAm apratipatti vipratipatti dozAt SUnyatA na praKyAti / tAn prati samalA p / vyavasTApyate
# ma-rtogs-pa #  dang log-pa # r rtogs-pa # 'i nyes-pa # s mi-mkhas-pa #  gang dag gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  la mngon-pa # r zhen cing / / 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa # s sems-kyi-rgyud #  dri-ma-can #  du gyur-pa #  la / / stong-pa-nyid #  mi-snang-ba #  de-dag #  dri-ma #  dang bcas-pa # 'o zhes rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
yezAm AryANAm tattva jQAnAt aviparIta cetasAm SUnya tA nirantaram / AkASa vat virajaskA praKyAti tAn prati prahINa mala iti ucyate
# 'phags-pa #  gang dag de-kho-na #  mkhyen-pa # s phyin-ci-log #  gi sems med-pa #  la stong-pa-nyid #  nam-mkha' #  ltar rdul-med-pa #  ste rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  snang-ba #  de-dag #  ni dri-ma #  spangs-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
evam SUnya tAyAH ApekzikA saMkleSa viSudDiH drazwavyA na
# de-ltar #  stong-pa-nyid #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa #  la ltos-pa #  can yin par blta ste /
malina svarUpa tvena prakRtyA praBAsvara tvAt
# rang-bzhin-gyis #  'od-gsal-ba # 'i phyir ngo-bo-nyid #  dri-ma-can #  du ni ma yin no /
yadi samalA BUtvA iti vistaraH
# gal-te #  dri-ma #  dang bcas-pa # r gyur la zhes-bya-ba #  rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  ni /
na hi avasTA BedaH vikAram antareNa dRzwaH / vikAraH ca utpAda vinASAByAm anusyUtaH iti
# 'gyur-ba-med-pa # r gnas-skabs #  tha-dad-pa #  ma mthong la / / 'gyur-ba #  ni skye-ba-dang-'jig-pa #  dang rjes-su-'brel-ba #  ste /
atas Aha kaTam vikAra DarmiNI tvAt anityA na Bavati iti
# de'i-phyir #  'gyur-ba # 'i chos-can #  yin-pas #  ji-ltar #  mi-rtag-pa # r mi 'gyur zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  smos so /
na hi saFklizwa avasTAtaH SUnyatA viSudDA avasTAyAm anyaH vikAraH / tattvaH titA tu svaBAva antaram anApadyamAnAyAH Agantu kamala apagamAt / yasmAt / ap DAtu kanaka AkASa SudDi vat SudDiH izyate
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  las stong-pa-nyid #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  su 'gyur-ba #  gzhan med kyi / / de-kho-na #  nyid-du #  gnas-pa # r rang-bzhin #  gzhan-du-'gyur-ba #  med-pa #  ste / / glo-bur-gyi-dri-ma #  dang bral pa'i phyir 'di-ltar #  / / chu khams gser dang nam-mkha' #  rnams / / dag-pa #  bzhin-du #  dag-pa # r 'dod /
tasmAt anityA na Bavati iti / yaTA eva hi abDAtu kanaka AkASAnAm atatsvaBAva tvAt / mala svaBAva tA aBAve api Agantu kamala vat tvam / Agantu kamalA apagame ca te viSudDAH eva / svaBAva antara pratipattim antareNa api / evam SUnyatA api Agantu kamalEH saFkliSyate avikRta svarUpA api tat / vigamAt ca viSudDyati iti
# de'i-phyir #  mi-rtag-pa # r mi 'gyur ro / / dper-na #  chu'i-khams #  dang gser dang nam-mkha' #  rnams de'i-rang-bzhin #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir / / dri-ma # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  yin par ma gyur kyang / / glo-bur-gyi-dri-ma # s dri-ma-can #  kho-na #  dang glo-bur-gyi-dri-ma #  dang bral na yang rang-bzhin #  gzhan-du-'gyur-ba #  med bzhin-du #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  nyid do / / de-bzhin-du #  stong-pa # 'i glo-bur-gyi-dri-ma #  rnams kyis kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r gyur yang / / 'gyur-pa #  med-pa # 'i ngo bo yin la / / de dang bral na rnam-par-dag-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
yaH hi tam eva BAvam pUrvam saFkleSa lakzaNam paScAt viSudDi svaBAvam
# dngos-po #  de nyid sngar kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang phyis rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  du gang rnam-par-'jog-pa #  de ni /
vyavasTApayati tasya vikAra Darma nivRttiH na Bavati / vikAra svaBAva tvAt na tu yatra api Agantukam tat uBayam / tasmAt na asO vikAra Darma tAm spRSati iti p
# rang-bzhin #  gzhan-du #  gyur bas 'gyur-ba # 'i chos bzlog-pa # r ma gyur gyi / / gang-la #  de-gnyi-ga #  yang glo-bur #  yin pa la ni ma yin te / / de-lta-bas-na #  de 'gyur-ba # 'i chos-nyid #  la reg-pa #  med do /
praBeda nirdeSa aDikAre sarve SUnyatA praBedAH vaktavyAH iti atas Aha
# rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i skabs yin-pas #  stong-pa-nyid #  kyi rab-tu-dbye-ba #  thams-cad #  brjod dgos te /
ayam aparaH praBedaH iti / zoXa SaviDA SUnyatA iti vastu Bedena zoXa SaviDA Bavati
# de'i-phyir #  gzhan-yang #  rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ni stong-pa-nyid #  rnam-pa-bcu #  drug-po #  'di-lta-ste #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / dngos-po #  tha-dad-pa # s rnam-pa-bcu #  drug tu 'gyur te /
dvaya aBAva svarUpe tu BedaH na asti
# gnyis kyi dngos-po-med-pa # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo la ni tha-dad-pa #  med do /
sA zoXa SaviDA SUnyatA prajQApAramitAyAm paWyate / aDyAtma SUnyatA yAvat aBAva svaBAva SUnyatA iti / sA ezA samAsatas veditavyA
# nang stong-pa-nyid #  ces bya-ba #  nas dngos-po-med-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  ces bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  stong-pa-nyid #  rnam-pa-bcu #  drug-po #  de ni shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  las byung ngo /
BoktR Bojana tat deha pratizWA vastu SUnyatA / iti evam Adi / sAmAnya lakzaNam SUnyatAyAH sarva DarmasyAH advaya svarUpa tvam
# de-yang #  mdor bsdu-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / za-ba #  bza' dang de yi lus / / gnas kyi gzhi yi stong-pa-nyid #  / / ces bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  la / / chos-thams-cad #  gnyis med-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi phyir stong-pa-nyid #  ni spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  do /
na anyaTA tat nAnAtvam Sakyate darSayitum iti atas vastunAnAtvena tat / nAnAtvam darSayati
# gzhan-du-na #  de ni tha-dad-pa # r bstan-pa # r mi nus te / / de'i-phyir #  gzhi tha-dad-pa # s de tha-dad-pa # r ston to /
pUrvam tAvat BoktA viBAvayitavyaH tat sneha aBiniveSa tyAjana arTam
# gzhan-du-na #  de ni tha-dad-pa # r bstan-pa # r mi nus so / / de-la #  chags-pa #  dang mngon-par-zhen-pa #  de spangs-pa # 'i phyir /
tat sneha aBiniveSaH hi budDa tva vimokza prApti pratibanDakaH Bavati
# thog-mar #  zab gzhig-pa # r bya'o / / de-la #  chags-pa #  dang mngon-par-zhen-pa #  de ni sangs-rgyas #  su 'grub-pa #  dang rnam-par-thar-pa #  thob-pa # 'i bgegs-su-gyur-pa # 'o /
tat anantaram tat Bojanam / tat anantaram tayoH aDizWAnam SarIram / tat anantaram tat aDizWAnasya SarIrasya pratizWA BAjana lokaH
# de'i-'og-tu #  de'i bza'-ba # 'o / / de'i-'og-tu #  de gnyis kyi gnas te lus so / / de'i-'og-tu #  za-ba #  la phan-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir /
viBAvayitavyaH BoktuH upakAraka tvAt / AtmIya sneha grAha vyAvartana arTam / etat catuH viDam vastu tat SUnyatA vastuSUnyata iti ucyate
# bdag-gi # r chags-pa #  dang 'dzin-pa #  bzlog-pa # 'i phyir / / de'i-gnas #  te lus kyi rten snod-kyi-'jig-rten #  gzhig-pa # r bya'o / / gzhi rnam-pa-bzhi-po #  'di'i stong-pa-nyid #  de ni gzhi stong-pa-nyid #  ces bya'o /
tatra BoktR SUnyatA ADyAtmikAni AyatanAni AraBya iti
# de-la #  za-ba #  stong-pa-nyid #  ni nang gi skye-mched #  rnams las brtsams so zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
tAni ca cakzUra AdIni yAvat manaH paryantAni
# de-dag #  kyang mig la-sogs-pa #  nas yid la thug-pa'i-bar-du # 'o /
tat anyasya BoktuH aBAvAt / cakzUra AdIn ca vizaya upaBoga pravRtti darSanAt lokasya cakzuH Adizt eva / BoktR aBimAnaH iti atas cakzUra Adi Ayatana SUnyatA BoktR SUnyatA iti ucyate
# za-ba #  de-la # s gzhan med-pa # s mig la-sogs-pa #  yul la nye-bar-spyod-pa # r 'jug-pa # r mthong-nas #  mig la-sogs-pa #  nyid kyis za-ba # r 'jig-rten #  mngon-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  byed-pa # s de'i-phyir #  / / mig la-sogs-pa # 'i skye-mched #  stong-pa-nyid #  la za-ba #  stong-pa-nyid #  ces bshad do /
Bojana SUnyatA bAhyAni iti rUpa AdIni yAvat Darma paryantAni
# bza'-ba #  stong-pa-nyid #  ni phyi-rol #  gyi rnams so zhes-bya-ba #  la / / gzugs la-sogs-pa #  nas chos la thug-pa'i-bar-du # 'o /
tAni vizaya aBAvena Bujyante iti Bojanam atas bAhya Ayatana SUnyatA / Bojana SUnyatA iti ucyate p / tayoH BoktR BojanayoH SarIre parasparA aviBAgenA avasTAnAt tat / dehaH SarIram iti atas tat SUnyatA aDyAtma bahirDA SUnyatA iti ucyate
# de-dag #  la yul-gyi-dngos-po # r bza'-ba # r bya-ba # s na-bza' #  ba ste / / de'i-phyir #  phyi-rol-gyi-skye-mched #  stong-pa-nyid #  ni bza'-ba #  stong-pa-nyid #  ces bshad do / / za-ba #  dang bza'-ba #  de gnyis ni lus dang phan tshun tha dad du mi-'jug-pa # r gnas / / de'i lus ni khog-pa # 'o zhes bya ste / / de-bas-na #  de'i stong-pa-nyid #  ces bya'o /
pratizWAvaH tu BAjana lokaH sarvatra sattvAnAm pratizWA vastu tvena / prajAnAt
# gnas kyi gzhi ni snod-kyi-'jig-rten #  te / / thams-cad-du #  sems-can #  rnams kyi gnas kyi gzhi rab tu 'dogs-pa # s /
atas eva Aha tasya vistIrNa tvAt tat SUnyatA mahASUnyatA ucyate iti
# de nyid kyi phyir de rgya-che-ba # 'i phyir de stong-pa-nyid #  ni chen-po #  stong-pa-nyid #  ces bya'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
vastu SabdaH pratyekam aBisambaDyate
# gzhi'i sgra ni re-re #  dang yang sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
tasya evam yoginaH boDisattvasya caturviDa jQeya vastu SUnya tAyAm
# de-ltar #  shes-bya'i-dngos-po #  rnams gzhi'i stong-pa-nyid #  la rtog-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i tshul-bzhin #  yid-la-byed-pa # s yid-la-byed-pa #  na /
sa vitarkeNa yoni SomanaskAreNa manaskriyamANAyAm ayam anyaH nimitta grAha
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnal-'byor #  ba de-la #  mtshan-mar-'dzin-pa #  gzhan 'di nye-bar-gnas-pa # r 'gyur ro /
upatizWate yena idam SUnyatA jQAnena ADyAtmika bAhya Ayatana Adi SUnyam / dRzwam tatra yaH grAhya grAhaka aBiniSeSaH ayam eva ca atra parama arTa AkAraH / yaTA tat Sruta ajQAnena dRzwam iti vikalpaH / tasya dvi prakArasya yogi BUmi BrAnti nimittasya vikalpasya / viBAvana arTam SUnyta SUnyata parama arTa SUnyatA ca yaTAkramam / jQanakAra lopam kRutvA nirdizwA / SUnyaTAvizaya tvAt vA tat jQAnam SUnyatA iti uktam
# stong-pa-nyid #  shes-bya #  gang-gis #  nang dang phyi'i skye-mched #  la-sogs-pa #  'di stong-pa # r mthong-ba #  de-la #  / / gang gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r mngon-par-zhen-pa #  dang ji-ltar-de # 'i stong-pa-nyid #  shes-pa # s mthong-ba #  'di nyid kyang 'dir don-dam-pa # 'i rnam-pa # 'o snyam-du #  rnam-par-rtog-pa #  la rnal-'byor #  gyi sa'i 'khrul-pa # 'i mtshan-ma # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  rnam-pa #  de gnyis gzhig-pa # 'i phyir / / stong-pa-nyid #  stong-pa-nyid #  dang don-dam-pa #  stong-pa-nyid #  de go-rims #  bzhin no / / shes-pa #  dang rnam-pa #  ni ma smos-pa # r byas te bshad do / / yang-na #  stong-pa-nyid #  yul yin-pas #  shes-pa #  dang stong-pa #  zhes bshad-pa #  yin no /
tasya grAhya grAhaka BAvena SUnyatA SUnyatA aSUnyatA / ADyAtmikA ayatana Adikam ca tena SUnyatA ajQAnena yaTA dRzwam saH atra
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i dngos-po # s de stong-pa-nyid #  ni stong-pa-nyid #  do / / nang gi skye-mched #  la-sogs-pa #  yang stong-pa-nyid #  shes-pa #  des ji-ltar #  mthong-ba #  de /
paramArTaH iti parama arTa AkAreNa tasya SUnyatA parama arTa SUnya tA / kim kAraNam / parama arTaH hi SUnyaH parikalpitena svaBAvena iti
# 'dir don-dam-pa # 'o snyam pa'i rnam-pa #  des stong-pa-nyid #  ni don-dam-pa #  stong-pa-nyid #  do / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na / / stong-pa-nyid #  ni don-dam-pa #  ste kun-brtags-pa # 'i rang-bzhin-gyis #  stong-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
ayam anyaH api nimitta grAhaH SUnyatA BAvanA upaplava BUtaH yad arTam
# mtshan-mar-'dzin-pa #  gzhan 'di ni stong-pa-nyid #  bsgom-pa # 'i nyes-pa # r gyur-pa #  ste /
boDisattvaH SUnyatAm pratipadyate tasya BAva svarUpa tvam samAropayati
# gang-gi-phyir #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  stong-pa-nyid #  sgrub-pa #  de-yang #  dngos-po # 'i ngo bor sgro-btags-pa #  ste /
tat viBAvana arTam saMskRta SUnyatA AdayaH sarva Darma SUnyatA paryantAH / SUnyatA nirdizwAH p
# de gzhig-pa # 'i phyir 'dus byas stong-pa-nyid #  ces bya-ba #  nas chos-thams-cad #  stong-pa-nyid #  ces bya-ba #  la thug-pa # 'i bar gyi stong-pa-nyid #  bshad do /
kim arTaQca pratipadyate
# ci'i-phyir #  sgrub-pa # r byed ce na /
SuBa dvayasya prApti arTam / yAvat budDa DarmANAm viSUdDi arTam SUnyatAm pratipadyate SUnyatAm / praBAvayati iti arTaH / SuBa dvayam hi saMskRtam asaMskRtaQca mArgaH nirvANaQca / tAByAm sambaDyate yaTAkramam saMskRta SUnya tA saMskRta SUnya tA / sadA sattva hitAya ca / iti sarva AkAram sarva kAlaQca mayA sattva hitam kartavyam iti tat / CUnyatA atyanta SUnya tA / saMsArA tyajana arTaQca / iti sattva arTam mayA saMsAraH na parityajyaH / saMsAre hi parityakte alabDvA boDisattva boDi SrAvaka boDO / vyavatizWate / tasya SUnya tA anavara agra SUnyatA / kim arTam punar tasya SUnyatA deSyate iti atas Aha anavarAgrasya hi / saMsArasya SUnya tAm apaSYan KinnaH saMsAram parityajeta iti / kuSalasya akzayAya ca iti / mayA kuSala mUlAni na kzIyante nirupADi Seze nirvANe api iti / na avakirati iti etat eva Acazwe na utsRjati iti / yadi evam kaTam tarhi nirupaDi SezaH nirvANa DAtuH sidDi ati / sa asra vaDarma vipAka kAya aBAvAt / anAsrava BUta Darma kAyasya tu budDasya BagavataH nirupaDi Seze / nirvANa DAtO= api na vyuparamAt iti sidDAntaH / atas tat SUnyatA anavakAra Sunya tA iti ucyate p / gotrasya ca viSudDi arTam tasya SUnyatA prakRti SUnya tA / atra eva kAraNam Aha gotram hi prakRtiH iti / kutas etat / atas Aha svABAvika tvAt iti / svaBAvikam anAdi kAlikam anAgantukam iti arTaH / yaTA anAdO saMsAre kiNcid cetanam kiQcid acetanam evam iha api kiQcid / zaXa Ayatanam budDa gotram kiQcid SrAvaka Adi gotram iti / na ca Akasmika tvam gotrasya anAdi paramparA gata tvAt cetana acetana viSeza vat iti / sarva sattvasya taTAgata gotra tvAt atra gotram iti taTAtvam jQeyam iti / anye / lakzaNa vyaQjana Aptaye / iti atas sa anuvyaQjanAnAm mahApuruza lakzaNAnAm SUnya tA / lakzaNa SUnyatA iti ucyate / kiQca / SudDaye budDa DarmANAm boDisattvaH prapadyate / ante prapadyate iti aBiDAnAt sarvatra SuBa dvayasya prApti arTam / boDisattvaH prapadyate / sadA sattva hitAya ca boDisattvaH prapadyate iti yojyam / katarezAm budDa DarmANAm iti atas bravIti bala vESAradyAveNikA AdInAm iti / saMkzepataH sarva budDa DarmANAm prAptaye mayA prayatitavyam iti / pratipadyate / tasmAt SUnyatA aviBAvanayA sarva Darma SUnyatA ucyate / kIdRSI viBAvanA iti / jQeye jQAnasya avyAvahita pravRttiH / evam tAvat caturdaSAnAm aDyAtma SUnyatA AdInAm / sarva Darma SUnyatA paryantAnAm vyavasTAnam veditavyam p / kA punar atra Boktra AdO SUnyatA katamat svarUpam iti atas Aha / pudgalasya aTa DarmANAm aBAvaH SUnyatA atra hi / tat aBAvasya sadBAvaH tasmin sA SUnyatA aparA iti / tatra yaTA uktAnAm Boktra AdInAm pudgala DarmA aBAvaH ca SUnyatA / tat aBAvasya ca sadBAvaH SUnyatA / tatra pudgala DarmayoH asadBAvaH aBAva SUnyatA / tat aBAvasya sadBAvaH aBAva SUnyatA / kim arTam punar ezA dviviDA SUnyatA ante vyavasTApyate / atas Aha SUnyatA lakzaNa KyApana arTam iti / kim arTam punar SUnyatA AKyApanam atas Aha pudgala Darma samAropasya tat / CUnyatA apavAdasya ca parihAra arTam yaTAkramam / pudgala Darma samAropasya parihAra arTam aBAva SUnya tAm vyavasTApayati / tat SUnyatA apavAda parihAra arTaQcA BAva svaBAva SUnyatAm / yadi aBAva SUnyatA na ucyeta parikalpita svarUpayoH Darma pudgalayoH / astitvam eva prasajyeta / yadi aBAva svaBAva SUnya tA na ucyeta SUnya tAyAH aBAvaH eva prasajyeta

 thams-cad #  thob-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir bdag-gis #  'bad-pa # r bya'o zhes sgrub-par-byed-pa # s de'i-phyir #  rnam-par-bsgom-pa #  zhes bya ste / / de'i stong-pa-nyid #  ni chos-thams-cad #  stong-pa-nyid #  ces bya'o / / 'dir rnam-par-bsgom-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ji-lta-bu #  zhen /
tat aBAvAt ca pudgala DarmayoH pUrvavat BAvaH syAt / tatra ADyAtmikezu Ayatanezu vipAka vijQAna svaBAvezu bAlAnAm / BoktR sammatezu BoktR pudgalasya kalpita lakzaNAnAm ca cakzuH AdInAm / aBAvaH tat aBAvasya ca sadBAvaH aDyAtma SUnya tA / bAhyezu Ayatanezu rUpa Adi vijQapti ABAsa svaBAvezu bAlAnAm / Bogya sammatezu Bojanasya AtmIyasya parikalpita lakzaNAnAm ca
# shes-par-bya-ba #  la shes-pa #  bar-chad-med-pa # r 'jug-pa #  ste / / de-ltar #  re-zhig #  nang stong-pa-nyid #  la-sogs-pa #  nas / / chos-thams-cad #  stong-pa-nyid #  la thug gi bar-du #  stong-pa-nyid #  bcu bzhi rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r shes-pa # r bya'o / / za-ba-po #  la-sogs-pa #  'di-la #  stong-pa-nyid #  gang yin / / ngo-bo-nyid #  ni ji-lta-bu #  zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  / / gang-zag #  dang ni chos-rnams #  kyi / / dngos-po #  med 'dir stong-pa-nyid #  / / de dngos-po-med-pa # 'i dngos yod-pa #  / / de-la #  de nyid stong nyid gzhan /
rUpa AdInAm aBAvaH tat aBAvasya ca sadBAvaH bahirDA SUnyatA / tat dehe SarIre BoktR pudgalasya bAla jana parikalpitAnAm rUpa AdInAm / dehasya ca aBAvaH tat aBAvasya ca BAvaH aDyAtma bahirDA SUnyatA / BAjana loke sattva lokA aBAvaH tat parikalpita svarUpa aBAvaH tat / aBAvaH tat aBAva sadBAvaH ca mahASUnyatA / SUnyatA jQAne parama arTa kAre ca jQAtuH AkAra grahItR pudgalasya / parikalpita lakzaNa Sunya tA parama arTa AkArasya ca aBAvaH tat aBAvaH / aBAvasya ca sadBAvaH yaTAkramam SUnyatA aSUnyatA paramArTa SUnyatA / ca / yat arTam boDisattvaH pratipadyate tezu saMskRta Adizu / sarva budDa Darma paryantezu p / boDisattva pratipattavyezu pudgalasya parikalpita lakzaNAnAm ca DarmANAm / aBAvaH tat aBAvasya ca sadBAvaH yaTAkramam saMskRta SUnya tA yAvat / sarva Darma SUnyatA iti / taTA hi na asti saMskRtasya svAmI vA prayoktA vA pudgalaH na api / saMskRtam bAla jana parikalpitena AtmanA / saMkzepataH sarva vikalpa grAha pratipakza arTam / sarva sUtra anta aBisanDi vyAkaraNa arTam ca etAH boDisattvAnAm SrAvakEH / asADAraNAH zoXa SaSUnya tA nirdizwAH / atra ca BagavatA SUnyatA vizayaH SUnyatA svaBAvaH / SUnyatA BAvanA prayojana Qca darSitam / tatra SUnyatA vizayaH BoktR Adi arTaH yAvat budDa Darma paryantaH / tat pradarSanam punar SUnyatAyAH sarva Darma vyApaka tva jQApana arTam / SUnyatA svaBAvaH aBAva svaBAvaH aBAva BAva svaBAvaH ca / SUnyatA svaBAva pradarSanam punar aDyAropa apavAda parti pakzeNa / sarva dRzwi niHsaraNa Atmaka tva jQApana arTam / SUnyatA BAvanA prayojanam SuBa dvayasya parapti arTam iti AraBya / budDa DarmANAm prAptayaH iti paryantam / tat pradarSanam punar sva para AtmanaH rUpa Darma kAya sampad prakarzaH / SUnyatA BAvanAt eva prApya iti pradarSana arTam iti / evam SUnyatAyAH praBedaH vijQeyaH iti sama lAva sTAyAm saMklizwA / nirmala avasTAyAm viSudDa iti
