'i dgongs-pa #  thams-cad #  lung bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / nyan-thos #  dang thun-mong-ma-yin-pa #  / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi stong-pa-nyid #  bcu drug-po #  'di dag bshad do / / 'dir ni bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis stong-pa-nyid #  kyi yul dang stong-pa-nyid #  kyi rang-bzhin #  dang stong-pa-nyid #  bsgom-pa # 'i dgos-pa #  yang rab tu bstan to / / de-la #  stong-pa-nyid #  kyi yul ni za-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i don nas sangs-rgyas-kyi-chos #  la thug gi bar-du # 'o / / de rab-tu-bstan-pa #  yang stong-pa-nyid #  kyis chos-thams-cad #  la khyab-pa # r shes-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / stong-pa-nyid #  kyi rang-bzhin #  ni dngos-po-med-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  dang dngos-po-med-pa # 'i dngos-po # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  do / / stong-pa-nyid #  kyi rang-bzhin #  rab-tu-bstan-pa #  yang sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r lta-ba #  thams-cad-la # s nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  du shes-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / stong-pa-nyid #  bsgom-pa # 'i dgos-pa #  ni dge-ba #  gnyis thob-par-bya-ba #  nas brtsams te / / sangs-rgyas-kyi-chos #  thob-par-bya-ba # 'i bar-du # 'o / / de bstan-pa #  yang bdag-dang-gzhan #  gyi gzugs dang chos kyi sku phun-sum-tshogs-pa # 'i mchog ni stong-pa-nyid #  bsgom-pa #  las 'thob po zhes rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
aDyAtma SUnyatA Adi zoXa SaprakAra BedaH anantara uktaH veditavyaH / Beda uddeSa anantaram tat sADanam uddizwam iti atas tad nirdeSa anantaram / pRcCati kaTam sADanam vijQeyam iti
# de-ltar #  stong-pa-nyid #  kyi rab-tu-dbye-ba #  shes-pa # r bya'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni dri-ma #  dang bcas-pa # 'i dus na kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang dri-ma-med-pa # 'i dus na rnam-pa # r dag go zhes-bya-ba #  dang nang stong-pa-nyid #  la-sogs-pa #  bcu drug tu gyur-pa # 'i dbye-ba #  bshad ma-thag #  pa'i rnam-pa #  yin par shes-pa # r bya'o / / dbye-ba #  smos-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  de sgrub-pa #  smos-pa # s dbye-ba #  bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  / / sgrub-pa #  ji-ltar #  shes-pa # r bya zhe na zhes dris so /
atra kim sADyate
# 'dir ci-zhig #  pa sgrub-pa # r bya zhe na /
Agantu kopa kleSa saMklizwa tA svaBAva viSudDa tA ca
# glo-bur #  gyi nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # s kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  nyid dang rang-bzhin-gyis #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  nyid do /
tatra saMklizwa asADam aDikRtya Aha / saMklizwA ced Bavet nA asO muktAssyuH sarva dehinaH p / iti
# de-la #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  nyid bsgrub-pa # 'i dbang du mdzad de / / gal-te #  nyon mongs de ma gyur / / lus can thams-cad #  grol bar 'gyur / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so /
muktiH saMkleSa prahANam
# rnam-par-grol-ba #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  spangs-pa # 'o /
tat saMkleSa prahANAn ca mArga BAvanAtaH
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  spangs-pa #  de-yang #  lam bsgoms-pa # s so /
tatra yadi DarmANAm SUnyatAH AgantukEH upakleSEH anutpanne api
# de-la #  gal-te #  gnyen-po #  ma-skyes-pa # r yang chos-rnams #  kyi stong-pa-nyid #  glo-bur #  gyi nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams kyis zhes-bya-ba #  la /
pratipakze api SabdAt utpannaH iva na saMklizwA Bavet evam sati
# yang gi sgra ni skyes-pa-dang-'dra-ba # r kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r mi 'gyur na /
saMkleSa aBAvAt ayatnataH eva muktAH sarva sattvAH BaveyuH
# de-ltar-gyur-na #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa # s 'bad-pa-med-pa # r sems-can-thams-cad #  grol bar 'gyur ro /
atyatnataH eva iti pratipakzam antareNa eva
# 'bad-pa-med-pa # r zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnyen-po #  med-pa #  nyid-du #  ste /
na tu pratipakzam antareNa prANinAm asti mokzaH iti avaSyam pRTak
# gnyen-po #  med-pa # r ni srog-chags #  rnams thar-pa #  med do / / de'i-phyir #  so-so'i-skye-bo # 'i dus na /
jana avasTAyAm taTA tAyAm AgantukEH malEH / saMklizwa tA aByupagantavyA iti
# de-bzhin-nyid #  la glo-bur-gyi-dri-ma #  rnams kyis kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  nyid-du #  gdon-mi-za-bar #  khas blang dgos te /
evam SUnyatAyAH saMklizwaH praBedaH sADitaH Bavati
# de-ltar #  stong-pa-nyid #  kyi rab-tu-dbye-ba #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  bsgrubs-pa #  yin no /
idAnIm viSudDi praBedam sADayan= Aha
# da-ni #  rab-tu-dbye-ba #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  sgrub-pa # 'i phyir /
viSudDA ced Bavet nA asO vyAyAmaH nizPalaH Bavet / dehinAm iti sambaDyate / aTa utpanne api pratipakze api SabdAt anutpannaH iva na viSudDAH Bavet evam / sati mokza arTaH AramBaH nizPalaH Bavet pratipakza BAvanayA api / tad malasyA avigamAt samalasya vimokza anupapatteH ca / na tu mokza arTaH AramBaH nizpahat izyate
# gal-te #  rnam dag de ma gyur / / 'bad-pa #  'bras-bu-med-pa # r 'gyur / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so / / lus can rnams dang sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / ci ste gnyen-po #  skyes kyang zhes-bya-ba #  la / / kyang gi sgra ni ma-skyes-pa #  dang 'dra-bar #  rnam-par-dag-pa # r mi 'gyur na / / de-ltar-gyur-na #  ni thar-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir rtsom pa 'bras-bu-med-pa # r 'gyur te / / gnyen-po #  bsgoms kyang dri-ma #  de dang bral-ba # r mi-'gyur-ba #  dang dri-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  ni grol bar mi 'thad-pa # 'i phyir ro / / thar-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir 'bras-bu-med-pa # r mi-'dod-pa # s /
tasmAt avaSyam pratipakza aByAsAt Agantu kopa kleSa vigamAt SUnyatAyAH / viSudDiH aByupagantavyA iti
# de'i-phyir #  gnyen-po #  goms-pa # r byas-na #  / / glo-bur #  gyi nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang bral-ba # s / / stong-pa-nyid #  kyi rnam-par-dag-pa #  gdon-mi-za-bar #  khas blang dgos te /
evam SUnyatAyAH viSUdDi praBedaH sADitaH Bavati
# de-ltar #  stong-pa-nyid #  kyi rab-tu-dbye-ba #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  bsgrubs-pa #  yin no /
atra saMkleSa Darma upAdAnAt saMkleSaH viSudDi Darma grahaNAt viSudDiH
# 'dir kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i chos nye-bar #  bzung-ba # s kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  la / / rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i chos nye-bar #  bzung-ba #  rnam-pa # r dag gi /
na tu SUnya tAyA sAkzAt saMkleSaH viSudDiH vezyate / Darma paratantra tva aDarma tAyAH / atas eva AH / muktAH syuH sarva dehinaH iti
# stong-pa-nyid #  la mngon du kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  'am / / rnam-par-dag-pa # r mi mi 'dod de / / chos-nyid #  ni chos kyi kha na las pas / / de'i-phyir #  / / lus can thams-cad #  grol bar 'gyur /
atas hi dehinaH iti tat upAdAnam eva uktam
# zhes gsungs te / / 'dir lus can zhes-bya-ba #  ni de'i rgyu nyid-du #  bshad-pa #  yin no /
anyaTA vA yadi SUnyatAyAH sAkzAt samklezaH vizuddadiH vA Bavet
# gzhan-du-na #  gal-te #  stong-pa-nyid #  la mngon du kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'am / / rnam-par-dag-pa # r gyur du zin na ni /
tatas kaH sambanDaH dehiBiH Bavet yena SUnyatA viSudDiH ca dehinAm / viSudDiH SUnyatA asaMkleSaH ca saMkleSaH ucyate
# de'i-phyir #  lus can rnams dang 'brel-pa #  ci yod-na #  / / 'di-ltar #  stong-pa-nyid #  rnam-par-dag-pa # s lus can rnams rnam-par-dag-pa #  dang stong-pa-nyid #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # s kyang / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  zhes bya /
yadA ca SUnyatA ca klizwA pRTagjana avasTAyAm SudDA / cAri avasTAyAm Bavati atas eva idam sidDam Bavati / na klizwA na api ca eva sA klizwA SudDA aSudDA na ca eva / kaTam na klizwA nA api ca api / SudDA eva dvaya SudDyA prakRta gamaka tvAt / atra eva Agamam Aha prakRtyA eva / praBAva svara tvAt cittasya iti
# gal-te #  so-so'i-skye-bo # 'i dus na / / stong-pa-nyid #  nyon mongs la / / 'phags-pa # 'i dus na dag-pa #  yin na ni / / de'i-phyir #  / / nyon mongs ma yin mi mongs min; / / de ni dag dang ma dag min / / zhes-bya-ba #  'di grub-pa #  yin no / / ji-ltar #  nyon-mongs-pa # r gyur-pa #  ma yin la ma-dag-pa #  yang ma yin zhe na / / dgag-pa #  gnyis kyis skabs su khong-du-chud-pa # r byed-pa # s dag-pa #  nyid de / / 'dir lus dang sems rang-bzhin-gyis #  'do gsal-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes 'byung ngo /
atra ca citta Darma tA eva citta Sabdena uktA cittasya evam lakzaNa tvAt
# 'dir ni sems kyi chos-nyid #  la sems kyi sgar bshad de / / sems nyid ni dri-ma # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyi phyir ro /
kaTam nA aklizwA na viSudDA kim tarhi klizwA eva iti
# ji-ltar #  nyon-mongs-pa # r ma-gyur-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  yang ma yin la rnam-par-dag-pa #  yang ma yin zhe na /
pratizeDa dvayAt pratipAdayati / sA
# nyon-mongs-pa #  nyid yin par dgag-pa #  gnyis kyis khong-du-chud-pa # r byed do /
kleSasya Agantuka tvataH / klizwAH na tu prakRtyA iti darSayati
# de-yang #  glo-bur #  gyi nyon-mongs-pa # s nyon-mongs-pa #  yin gyi rang-bzhin-gyis #  ni ma yin zhes ston to /
sA ca AgantukEH upakleSEH upakliSyate iti atra api AgamaH
# de-yang #  lung las glo-bur #  gyi nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams kyis nye-bar #  nyon mongs so zhes 'byung ngo /
saFklizwa viSudDa tayA dviDA BedaH ukte kimarTam punar caturDA Beda
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa #  gnyis su bye ste bshad na / / ci'i-phyir #  dbye-ba #  rnam-pa-bzhi # r bshad ce na /
ucyate / lOkikAt loka uttarAt ca mArgAt viSeza arTam iti ekaH
# kha-cig #  na re 'jig-rten-pa #  dang 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam las khyad-par #  du bstan-pa # 'i phyir te /
lOkikaH hi mArgaH sva BUmikEH malEH klizwaH na tu aDarEH tat / pratipakza tvAt
# 'jig-rten #  gyi lam ni rang-gi #  sa'i dri-ma #  rnams kyi nyon mongs kyi / / de'i gnyen-po # 'i phyir 'og mas ni ma yin no /
loka uttaraH tu mArgaH mRdu maDya Adi BedAt aSudDaH anAsrava tvAt SudDaH
# 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam ni chung-ngu #  dang 'bring-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis ni ma dag gi / / zag-pa-med-pa # s ni dag-pa #  ste /
na evam SUnyatA iti
# stong-pa-nyid #  ni de lta ma yin no zhe'o /
na klizwa iti uktvA punar cakzuH AdiByaH viSeza arTam ucyate na aSudDa iti anye
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  ma yin no zhes bshad-pa #  la / / gzhan dag na re mig la-sogs-pa #  dang bye-brag #  yod-pa # s ma-dag-pa #  yin no /
cakzuH AdayaH hi anivRttA avyAkRta tvAt na klizwAH na ca tezAm sArava tvAt / prakRti viSudDiH iti aSudDa iti
# mig la-sogs-pa #  ni ma-bsgribs-pa # 'i lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  yin-pas #  nyon-mongs-pa #  ma yin la / / de-dag #  gi zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # s rang-bzhin-gyis #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # s / / ma-dag-pa #  yang ma yin zhes bshad do /
evam na api sA klizwA iti CeduCyate a zudDA iti kuSalasA AsravAt / viSezaNa arTam AmAH
# de-bzhin-du #  nyon-mongs-pa-med-pa #  yang ma yin zhes bshad-pa #  la / / dag-pa #  ma yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i dge-ba #  dang bye-brag #  yod-pa # 'i phyir te /
kuSala sa Asravam hi saMsAra paryApanna tvAt nA aklizwam
# zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i dge-ba #  ni 'khor-ba # r gtogs-pa # s nyon-mongs-pa-med-pa #  ma yin la /
izta vipAka tvAt ca SudDam na eva Darma tA / sA hi klizwA avasTAyAm aSudDA eva iti
# rnam-par-smin-pa #  yid-du-'ong-ba # s dag-pa #  ste / / chos-nyid #  ni de lta ma yin no / / de ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i dus na nyon-mongs-pa-can #  yin la ma-dag-pa #  nyid ces bshad do /
evam SUnyatAyAH saFkleSa viSudDyA uddizwaH praBedaH sADitaH Bavati / p
# de-ltar #  stong-pa-nyid #  kyi rab-tu-dbye-ba #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa #  bstan-pa #  'di bsgrubs-pa #  yin no /
SUnyatA piNXu arTaH
# stong-pa-nyid #  kyi don bsdus-pa #  ni /
SUnyatA piNXda arTaH lakzaNa tAm vyavasTAnataH ca iti veditavyaH / tatra lakzaNataH aBAva lakzaNataH BAva lakzaNataH ca iti dvaya aBAvaH / hi ativacanAt aBAva lakzaNataH aBAvasya ca BAvaH iti vacanAt / BAva lakzaNataH / BAva lakzaNataH ca na BAvaH nA api ca aBAvaH iti vacanAt
# mtshan-nyid #  dang rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / de-la #  mtshan-nyid #  ni dngos-po-med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang dngos-po # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do zhes-bya-ba #  la gnyis kyi dngos-po #  med do zhes bshad-pa # s dngos-po-med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do / / dngos-po-med-pa # 'i dngos-po #  zhes bshad-pa # s dngos-po # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do / / dngos-po # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyang yod-pa #  ma yin med-pa # 'ang ma yin zhes bshad-pa # s /
BAva aBAva vinirmukta lakzaNataH tattvAni tva vinirmukta lakzaNaH ca iti / etat ca SUnyatAyAH lakzaNam
# dngos-po-yod-pa #  dang dngos-po-med-pa #  las rnam-par-grol-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang de nyid dang gzhan la rnam-par-grol-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  de 'di ni stong-pa-nyid #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  do /
tasmAt aBUta parikalpAt na pRTak tu eka lakzaNam iti vacanAt
# de-bas-na #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  dang tha dad gcig pa'i mtshan-nyid #  min zhes bshad do /
evam lakzaNataH piNXa arTaH
# de-ltar-na #  mtshan-nyid #  kyi don bsdus-pa # 'o /
kaTam vyavasTAnataH piNXda arTaH veditavyaH iti ete Aha
# rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i don bsdus-pa #  ji-ltar #  gzhag-pa # r bya zhe na /
vyavasTAnam punar paryAya Adi vyavasTAnataH veditavyam
# de'i-phyir #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  ni rnam-grangs #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
paryAyataH tad arTaH tad aBedaH tat sADanaQca iti arTaH
# rnam-grangs #  dang de'i don dang de'i dbye-ba #  dang de sgrub-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
etayA catur prakAra deSanayA caturviDA upakleSa pratipakzeNa sva lakzaNam
# mtshan-nyid #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-pa-bzhi-po #  'di dag bstan-pa # s nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnam-pa-bzhi # 'i gnyen-po # r /
karma lakzaNam saFkleSa vyavadAna lakzaNam yukti lakzaNa QcodBAvitam Bavati
# rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  dang las-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  dang kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang rigs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  brjod-pa #  yin no /
tatra sva lakzaNam vikalpasya pratipakzeNa tasya hi
# de-la #  rnam-pa # r rtog ba'i gnyen-po # r rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  de /
BAvA aBAva uBaya pRTaktvA ekatva grAha Atmaka tva tvAt
# de ni dngos-po #  dang dngos-po-med-pa #  dang gnyi-ga #  dang tha dad gcig pa nyid-du #  'dzin-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  do /
karma lakzaNam anaDimuktAnAm SUnya tA lakzaNa aSra tyAtrAsasya asya / pratipakzeNa / aBrAntitaTatA karmA viparyAsakarma / sarva loka uttara jQAna vizaya tvAt avasTAna karma / pratilabDa Arya Darma hetu BAva karma ca / evam SUnyatA svarUpa karma SravaNena prApta grahANAm kusIdinAm / kOsIdya apanana arTam praBeda lakzaNam
# stong-pa-nyid #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  thos-nas #  ma-mos-pa #  rnams kyis skrag-par-'gyur-ba #  de'i gnyen-po # r las-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  de / / ma nor bde-bzhin-nyid #  kyi las dang phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i las dang mtshan-ma-thams-cad #  spangs-pa # 'i las dang 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i ye shes thams-cad-kyi #  yul nyid-du #  gnas-pa # 'i las dang dmigs-pa #  na 'phags-pa # 'i chos kyi rgyu'i-dngos-po # 'i las so / / de-ltar #  stong-pa-nyid #  kyi rang-gi #  ngo bo dang las thos-pa #  tsam gyis chog-par-'dzin-pa #  le-lo-can #  rnams kyi le-lo #  bsal-ba # 'i phyir / / rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do /
kaTam sA saFkleSaH Bavati vyavadAnam ca iti saMSayinAm / saMSaya apanayana arTam yukti lakzaNam / maDya anta viBAga SAstre lakzaNa paricCedasya praTamasya wIkA / AvaraNa paricCedaH dvitIyaH / p / tatra vyApi kleSa jQeyA avaraNam boDisattva gotrakANAm sAkalyAt / prAdeSikam kleSAH AvaraNam SrAvaka Adi gotrakANAm / udriktam tezAm eva rAga Adi caritAnAm / samam sama BAga caritAnAm / saMsArA AdadAna tyAgA avaraNam boDisattva gotra kAraNam / apratizWita nirvANA AvaraNAt
# de ji-ltar #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r 'gyur rnam-par-dag-pa # r 'gyur snyam pa'i som nyi za-ba #  rnams kyi the-tshom #  bsal-ba # 'i phyir rigs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do / / bstan-bcos #  dbus dang mtha' rnam-par-'byed-pa # s mtshan-nyid #  kyi le'ur bcad-pa #  ste dang-por #  'grel bshad do / / mtshan-nyid #  bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  sgrub-pa #  bshad-pa # 'i skabs yin te / / de'i-'og-tu #  snos pas de'i-phyir #  sgrib-pa # 'i dbang du mdzad de zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / khyab dang nyi tshe lhag-pa #  dang / / mnyam-pa #  dang len-pa #  dang spong-ba #  ni /
iti etat yaTAyogam uBayezAm AvaraNam AKyAtam / boDisattva gotrakANAm SrAvaka Adi gotrakANAn ca
# gnyis kyi sgrib-pa # r bstan-pa #  yin / / gnyis po dag gi sgrub-pa #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i rigs can rnams dang nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rigs can rnams kyi sgrib-pa # 'o /
lakzaNa nirdeSa anantaram na AvaraNa nirdeSA vasaraH / tad anantaram uddizwa tvAt iti Aha AvaraNam aDikRtya Aha / vyApi prAdeSika udrikta samAdAna vivarjanam / dvaya avaranam AKyAtam / dvaya AvaraNam boDisattva gotrakANAm SrAvaka Adi gotrakANAn ca AvaraNam / AvaraNIya arTa Bedena AvaraNasya Binna tvam pradarSayitum ayam Sloka / ArabDaH / tatra vyApi kleSa jQeya AvaraNam boDisattva gotrakANAm iti / vyApnoti iti vyApi sakala arTa AvaraNAt / sakala arTaH hi sva arTaH para arTaH ca / aTavA dviviDam kleSam jQeyam ca AvaraNam boDisattvasya / vyApnoti iti upacArAt vyApyucyate / kleSaH eva AvaraNam iti AvaraNasya kleSa Darma tvena sArUpya Adi ha upakleSaH api / kleSa Sabdena gRhyate / anyaTA / navaDA kleSa lakzaNam p / iti atra IrzyAmAt sarye na gRhya tAm tayoH upakleSa tvAt
# bsgrib-pa # r bya-ba # 'i don tha-dad-pa # s sgrib-pa #  tha-dad-pa # r rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir le'u 'di brtsams so / / de-la #  khyab-pa #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i rigs can rnams kyi nyon-mongs-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni khyab-par-byed-pa # s khyab-pa #  ste / / don mtha'-dag #  la sgrib-pa # 'i phyir ro / / don mtha'-dag #  gi don dang gzhan-gyi-don #  to / / yang-na #  nyon-mongs-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam gnyis btags-pa # s byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi sgrib-pa #  la khyab-par-byed-pa # s khyab-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / nyon-mongs-pa #  nyid sgrib-pa # s ni sgrib-pa # 'o / / nyon-mongs-pa #  nyid kyi chos kho-nar #  'dra-ba # s / / 'dir ni nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  yang nyon-mongs-pa # 'i sgrar gzung ngo / / gzhan-du-na #  ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  rnam-pa #  dgu zhes-bya-ba # r phrag-dog-dang-ser-sna #  gnyis gzung-ba # r mi 'gyur te / / de gnyis nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
jQeyaH eva AvaraNam iti jQeya AvaraNam / tena jQeya prAvRta tvAt jQAnasya vizayaH eva na asti
# shes-bya #  ba la sgrib-pa # s shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  ste / / des shes-bya #  rab tu bsgribs-pa # s shes-pa # 'i yul du mi 'gyur ro / / yang-na #  shes-bya #  la ye shes kyi sgrib-pa #  yin te /
jQAne vA jQeya AvaraNam jQeyasya jQAna utpatti pratibanDaka tvAt iti / jQeya AvaraNam iti atra maDyama pada lopaH drazwavyaH / tEla pAtram iva / tat punar aklizwam ajQAtam
# shes spar bya-ba #  la ye shes skye-ba # 'i bgegs-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / shes-bya #  dang sgrib-pa # 'i bar gyi tshig ma smos-pa # r mar gyi bum-pa #  bzhin no / / de-yang #  nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i mi-shes-pa # 'o; / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i rigs can rnams kyis /
boDisattva gotrakANAm asvapara arTa sampad prakarza lABAya / budDa tva prAptaye puNya jQAna samBAram sarvaTA sarvatra anutizWatAm / tat dvayam api pratibanDaka BUtam / iti atas tad AvaraNam vyavasTApyate boDisattva gotrakANAm / tatra vyApi sarva vizayam sakalam sarvaTA vyApnoti
# bdag-dang-gzhan-gyi-don #  phun du byung-ba #  thob-pa # s sangs-rgyas #  nyid thob-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir bsod nams dang ye-shes-kyi-tshogs #  rnams pa thams-cad #  kun la nan-tan-du #  bya-ba #  de-la #  gnyi-ga #  yang bgegs su gyur bas de'i-phyir #  de byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i rigs can rnams kyi sgrib-pa # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go / / de-la #  khyab-pa #  ni thams-cad #  yul yin la mtha'-dag #  ces bya-ba #  ni rnam-pa # r thams-cad-la #  bya na /
kaTam sakalam vyApnoti iti jQAyate iti ced sAkalyAt AvaraNam / vyApIti ucyate iti hetu nirdeSAt / aTa vA vyApi SabdaH niravaSeza arTaH iti pradarSanAya sAkalya Adi vacanam
# ji-ltar #  mtha'-dag-gis #  khyab-pa # r shes-par-byed-pa # r 'gyur zhe na / / mtha'-dag #  gi phyir de khyab-pa # 'i sgrib-pa # r brjod de rgyur bstan-pa # s 'gyur ro / / yang-na #  khyab-pa # 'i sgra ni ma-lus-pa # 'i don-du #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir mtha'-dag #  gi phyir ro zhes smos so /
prAdeSikam kleSa AvaraNam SrAvaka Adi gotrakANAm iti
# nyi-tshe-ba #  ni nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rigs can rnams kyi nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
sva arTa mAtra AvaraNAt upacArAt avyApi tvAt ca prAdeSikA AKyA
# bdag-gi-don #  tsam la sgrib-pa # s sgrib-pa # r btags-pa #  dang khyab-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir nyi-tshe-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  /
kim SrAvaka pratyekabudDAnAm aklizwam ajQAnam na asti yasmAt tezAm / kleSa AvaraNam eva vyavasTApyate iti / Bavatu na tu tad AvaraNam tezAm tasmin vidyamAne
# nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  rnams la nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i mi-shes-pa #  med dam zhe na / / 'di-ltar #  de-dag #  la nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  nyid rnam-pa # r gzhag ce na / / yod mod kyi de ni de-dag #  gi sgrib-pa #  ma yin te /
SrAvaka pratyekabudDa boDi prApteH
# de yod-bzhin-du #  nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi byang-chub #  'thob-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nanu ajQAnam duHKa Adi satya vizaye jQAna utpatti pratibaMDaka tvam eva / SrAvaka AdInAm
# mi-shes-pa #  ni sdug-bsngal #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bden-pa # 'i yul la / / nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i shes-pa #  skye-ba # 'i bgegs-su-gyur-pa #  yang ma yin nam /
tatas tezAm api dvaya AvaraNam Bavet
# de-bas-na #  de-dag #  la yang sgrib-pa #  gnyi-ga #  yod-pa # r 'gyur ro /
tasmAt na vaktavyam kleSa AvaraNam SrAvaka Adi gotrakANAm iti
# de'i-phyir #  nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  la ni nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  kho-na # 'o zhes brjod-pa # r mi bya'o zhe na /
na etat evam ajQAnam hi klezwam jQAna pratipakza BUtam saMsAra mUlam ca
# de ni de lta ma yin te ma-rig-pa #  ni nyon mongs spar gyur-pa #  dang rig-pa # 'i mthun-pa # 'i phyogs su gyur-pa #  dang 'khor-ba # 'i rtsa bar 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir /
kleSza AvaraNam eva iti vyavasTApyate na tu jQeya AvaraNam saMSayaH iva
# nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  nyid-du #  rnam-pa # r gzhag gi / / shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  ni ma yin te / / so ma nyi bzhin no /
yaTA vimatiH hi duHKa Adi satya vizaye vicikitsA kleSaH ca ucyate na tu / vizaya antare
# dper-na #  sdug-bsngal #  gyi tshogs kyi rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir / / de-dag #  gi sgrib-pa #  ni shes nyon-mongs-pa #  zhes bya'i yul gzhan la ni ma yin no /
vizaya antare hi saMSayaH eva na kleSaH na vicikitsA
# yul gzhan la ni som nyi nyid de / / nyon-mongs-pa #  yang ma yin the-tshom #  yang ma yin no /
eva vam duHKa satya Adi vizaye eva ajQAnam avidyA kleSaH ca ucyate na tu / vizaya antare
# de-bzhin-du #  sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i yul nyid la mi-shes-pa #  ni ma-rig-pa #  dang nyon-mongs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i yul gzhan la ma yin no /
vizaya antare tu ajQAnam eva na ca A vidyA na eva / tasmAt tasya jQeya jQAna mAtra pravRttO= AvaraNa tvAt tad jQeya AvaraNam / ucyate na hi kleSa karma janmanAm api tAni ca utpadyantaH eva avidyAyAH eva
# yul gzhan la ni mi-shes-pa #  nyid yin te / / ma-rig-pa # 'am ma yin nyon-mongs-pa # 'am ma yin no / / de-lta-bas-na #  de ni shes-par-bya-ba #  la ye shes tsam 'jug-pa #  la sgrib-pa # 'i phyir / / shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  zhes bya ste / / ma-rig-pa #  ltar nyon-mongs-pa #  dang las dang tshe rnams kyang 'byung rba ni yin no /
yadi evam boDisattvAnAm AvaraNam na vyavasTApyate
# gal-te #  de lta na byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi sgrib-pa # r rnam-pa # r mi gzhag go zhe na /
na etat evam boDisattvAnAm hi Sruta samBAra praBAvita tvAt
# de ni de lta ma yin te / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams ni thos-pa # 'i tshogs kyi rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir /
tezAm AvaraNam jQeya AvaraNam / tat uktam
# de-dag #  gi sgrib-pa #  ni shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  ste / / de-skad #  du /
AryhaH api agyUH paQca vidyA padAni / nAraBya syAt kadApi sarvajQaH / tatas anyezAm nigrahA anugraha arTam
# rig-pa'i-gnas #  lnga dag la brtson par ma-byas-pa # r / / 'phags mchog cis kyang thams-cad #  mkhyen nyid mi 'gyur te / / de-bas #  gzhan dag tshar gcod rjes su gzung phyir ram /
sva jQAna arTam vA AraBet tatra yatnam iti
# rang-gis #  shes-pa # r bya phyir de-la #  de brtson byed / / ces bshad do /
udRktam tu mRdu api rAga Adi vastu tezAm eva boDisattva gotrakANAm / rAvakA diS otra kANaQcA aDimAtram aBIkzNam ca pravartitam
# lhag-pa #  ni 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dngos-po #  chung yang byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i rigs can dang nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rigs can de-dag #  la shas-che-ba #  dang rgyun-du #  'byung-ba # 'o /
rAga Adi caritAnAm Avaranam iti / yezAm p
# 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  spyod-pa #  rnams kyi sgrib-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
mRdO= api vizaye rAga AdInAm anyatamat aDimAtram aBIkzNyam ca / pravartate te rAga Adi caritAH
# su dag yul ngan-pa #  la yang 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  gang-yang-rung-ba #  shas-che-ba #  dang rgyun-du #  'byung-ba #  de-dag #  ni 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  spyod-pa # 'o /
samam punar tezAm eva boDisattva gotrakAraNam / SrAvaka Adi gotra kANAn ca AvaraNam / samam hi prakAra dvi tva aBAvAt
# mnyam-pa #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i rigs can dang nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rigs can de-dag-nyid #  kyi sgrib-pa #  ste / / mnyam-pa #  ni de-gnyi-ga # 'i rnam-pa #  yang med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sama BAga caritAnAm AvaraNam iti yezAm vizaya sAdRSye sAmIpye kleSa
# cha mtshungs-pa # r spyod-pa #  rnams kyi sgrib-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / su dag yul-dang-'dra-ba # r nyon-mongs-pa #  skye'i /
utpadyate na tu aBIkzNam te sama BAga caritAH
# rgyun-du #  ni ma-yin-pa #  de-dag #  ni cha mtshungs-pa # r spyod-pa # 'o /
saMsAra AdAna tyAga AvaraNam ityAdi
# 'khor-ba #  len-pa #  dang gtong-ba # 'i sgrib-pa #  ni zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni /
Bodi sattvaH hi kAruNya ADipattyAt saMsAram upAdatte prajQA ADipattyAt / ca saMsAra dozam yaTABUtam dRzwvA tyajati
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i snying-rje # 'i dbang gis 'khor-ba #  nye-bar-len-pa #  dang shes-rab #  kyi dbang gis 'khor-ba # 'i nyes-pa #  yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  mthong-ste #  /
tatas kleSa aBAve api sattva akicanAt janma parigrahaH apratizWatam nirvANam
# stong-pa # s de'i-phyir #  nyon-mongs-pa-med-pa # r sems-can-la-lta-ba # s skye-ba #  yongs-su-'dzin-pa #  ni / / mi-gnas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  ste /
saMsAra nirvANayoH dvayoH apratizWata tvAt
# 'khor-ba #  dang mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  gnyis la mi-gnas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tadA AvaraNantu kleSa aBiBUtena yaTA saMsAram upAdAya / yaTA BUta doza adarSanAt ca kRpayA
# de'i sgrib-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa # s non bzhin-du #  'khor-ba #  nye-bar-len-pa #  dang nyes-pa #  yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  mthong-nas #  snying-rje-med-pa # r 'khor-ba #  yongs-su-gtong-ba # 'o /
ajQAnam iha AvaraNam ucyate kRpA prajQayoH pratibanDaka tvAt iti anye
# gzhan dag na re snying-rje #  dang shes-rab #  gnyis kyi bgegs-su-gyur-pa # 'i phyir mi-shes-pa #  ni 'dir sgrib-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  zhe'o /
aTavA yaTA uktam mahA ratnakUwe a ASayena nirvANe tizWati saMsAre / ca prayogeNa tizWati iti
# yang-na #  ji-ltar #  dkon-mchog #  brtsegs pa chen-po #  las / / de'i bsam-pa #  mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la yang gnas la / / 'khor-ba #  na yang sbyor-ba # r gnas-pa #  zhes bstan-pa #  lta-bu #  ste /
etat hi boDisattvAnAm apratizWitam nirvANam
# 'di ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi mi-gnas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'o /
tatra nirvANa pRzWI BAvAt ASaya prayogAByAm saMsAram upAdatte
# de-la #  mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la rgyab kyis bltas-pa # 'i phyir / / bsam-pa #  dang sbyor-ba # s 'khor-ba #  la len te /
agotra sTa sattvaH iva / taTA ca saMsAra pRzWIBAvAt nirvANa gatAByAm ASaya prayogAByAm
# rigs-med-pa # 'i sems-can #  bzhin no / / de-bzhin-du #  'khor-ba #  la rgyab kyis bltas-pa # 'i phyir / / mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # r song-ba # 'i bsam-pa #  dang sbyor-ba #  gnyis kyis 'khor-ba #  yang yongs su gtong ste /
saMsAram tyajati SrAvaka Adi gotrakAH iva
# nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rigs can rnams ji-lta-ba #  bzhin no /
evam saMsAra AdAnam tat parityajanam ca / boDisattva gotra kANAma pratizWita nirvANa AvaraNam
# de-ltar #  'khor-ba #  len-pa #  dang de gtong-ba #  yang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi mi-gnas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la sgrib-pa #  ste /
saMsAra nirvANayoH ekAnta patita tvAt
# 'khor-ba #  dang mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  gnyis las mtha' gcig-tu #  ltung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
boDisattvAH tu taTAgata tva prApti kAle kleSa jQeya AvaraNa prahANAt / saMsAre na tizWanti nirupaDi Seze nirvANe ca Darma kAya prabanDAn na
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # r gyur-pa # 'i dus na nyon-mongs-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  spangs-pa # 'i 'khor-ba #  la mi-gnas-pa #  dang phung-po # 'i lhag-ma #  med-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  na yang chos kyi sku rgyun-mi-'chad-pa # 'i phyir /
tizWanti nirvANe SrAvaka Adi vat
# nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la mi gnas te /
tatas saMsAra nirvANayoH uBaya atra api na pratizWanti iti
# de-ltar-na #  'khor-ba #  dang mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  gnyi-ga #  la yang mi gnas so /
atra boDisattvasya SrAvaka AdIn ca mArge tezAm prayoge Pale / apratizWita nirvANam ca pratibanDaka tvAt etAni / paQcaviDAni AvaraNAni AKyAtAni / iti etat yaTAyogam iti yaTAsamBavam
# 'dir byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  dang nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i lam dang de gnyis kyi sbyor-ba #  dang 'bras-bu #  dang mi-gnas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la bgegs-byed-pa # 'i phyir sgrib-pa #  rnam-pa-lnga-po #  'di dag grangs bzhin no / / de-ltar #  'di dag ni ci-rigs-par #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du'o /
tatra praTamam antyam ca boDisattva gotrakANAm AvaraNam
# de-la #  dang-po #  dang tha-ma #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i rigs can rnams kyi sgrib-pa # 'o /
praTama Adavaram SrAvaka Adi gotrakANAm AvaraNam / itarat dvayam punaruBayezAm AvaraNam AKyAtam / tatra ca jQeya AvaraNam boDisattvAnAm AvaraNam uktam / tat ca aklizwam ajQAnam iti / nava saMyojanAni kleSa AvaraNam / kasya etAni AvaraNam / anunaya saMyojanam saMvegasya AvaraNam / pratiGa saMyojanam upekzAyAH tena hi p / pratikUlam api pratiGavaH tu upekzitum na Saknoti / SezANi tattva darSanasya AvaraNam / kaTam kRtvA / tAni hi yaTAkramam / saMkleSasya parijQAne saMyojanAni AvaraNam Bavanti / mAnam saMyojanam hi satkAya dRzwi parijQAne bahu ati AvaraNam / aBisamaya kAle sAntara vyantarA smimAna samudAcAra vaSena tat aprahANAt / avidyA saMyojanam satkAya dRzwi vastu parijQAne / tena upAdAna skanDA aparijQAnAt / dRzwi saMyojanam niroDa satya parijQAne satkAyAH anta grAha dRzwi BAntat / uttrAsAt miTyA dRzwyA ca apavAdAt / parAmarSa saMyojanam mArga satya parijQAne anyaTA apraSudDi parAmarSanAt / vicikitsA asaMyojanam ratna traya parijQAne tat guNAH anaBiSradDAnAt / IrzyA saMyojanam lABa satkAra parijQAne tat dozA adarSanAt / mAtsarya saMyojanam saMleKa parijQAne parizkArA aDyavasAnAt p / mAna Adi Bedena

r bshad de / / de-yang #  nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i mi-shes-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba # r shes so / / gnyi-ga # 'i sgrib-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  la rnam-pa #  du yod-pa #  dang rang-bzhin #  ji-lta-bu #  dang gang-gi #  bgegs-su-gyur-pa #  mi shes te / / de'i-phyir #  / / nyon mongs mtshan-nyid #  rnam dgu'o / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs te / / sgrib ces bya-ba #  dang sbyar ro / / nyon-mongs-pa # s kun du sbyor-ba #  rnams so / / sdug-bsngal #  sna-tshogs #  kyang 'dod-pa #  dang gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa # r gtogs-pa # 'i lus te / / sdug-bsngal-gyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid dang 'gyur-ba'i-sdug-bsngal #  nyid dang 'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid de khams-gsum #  dang ci-rigs-su #  sbyar ro / / de-yang #  rjes-su-chags-pa # 'i kun du sbyor-ba #  nas / / ser-sna # 'i kun du sbyor-ba # 'i bar-du # 'o / / de-la #  khong-khro-ba #  ni zhe-sdang #  ngo / / phrag-dog #  ni gzhan gyi phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  la mi-bzod-pa # 'o / / ser-sna #  ni yo-byad #  kun 'dzin-pa #  ste / / de gsum ni 'dod-pa # r gtogs-pa # 'o / / rjes-su-chags-pa #  zhes rgya-cher #  smos so / / yid-mi-bde-ba # 'i rgyu yin-pas #  mi-mthun-pa # 'o / / khong-khro-ba # 'i gzhi ste khong-khro-ba # 'i rgyu la btang-snyoms #  su byed cing mngon du mi-byed-pa # r mi nus so / / rjes-su-chags-pa # 'i gzhi ni mi-mthun-pa-med-pa # s btang-snyoms #  su mi-nus-pa #  ni / / rigs kyi khong-khro-ba # 'i gzhi ni mi-mthun-pa #  la yang khong-khro-ba #  ste; btang-snyoms #  su byed mi-nus-pa # s de'i-phyir #  / / rjes-su-chags-pa #  bas sdig che-ba # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir-yang #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / mnyam-par-'jog-pa #  na gal-te #  'du-byed #  kyi btang-snyoms #  thob na / / de-ltar #  de'i sems-mnyam-pa # r 'gyur ro / / gal-te #  de'i khong-khro-ba # 'i kun du sbyor bshas-che-ba # r 'gyur na ni / / de'i dbang gis khong-khro-ba # 'i rgyu de-la #  btang-snyoms #  mi thob ste / / de byung na bdag-gi #  dmigs-pa #  la gdon-mi-za-bar #  dmigs-pa # r 'gyur ro / / de-ltar #  rjes-su-chags-pa # 'i kun du sbyor-ba # s ni dben-pa #  nyid mi 'thob po / / khong-khro-ba # 'i kun du sbyor-ba # s ni dben-pa # r gyur kyang ting-nge-'dzin #  mi 'thob po / / lhag-ma #  bdun po ni de-kho-na #  mthong-ba #  la sgrib ces bya-ba #  ni / / ma nor-ba # r mthong-ba #  la sgrib po / / ji lta zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  ni mi shes te dri-ba # 'o / / de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  ni go-rims-bzhin-du #  / / 'jig-tshogs #  lta dang de'i gzhi dang / / zhes-bya-ba #  rgya-cher #  gsungs so / / nga-rgyal #  gyi kun du sbyor-ba #  ni 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  la bsgrib-pa #  yin no / / de-la #  'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  la brten-nas #  sems khengs-pa #  ni nga-rgyal #  te / / de-yang #  nga-rgyal #  las kyang nga-rgyal #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-pa #  bdun no /
Atma AtmIya grAhya grAhaka tva vivekena / bAla jana parikalpita Darma svaBAva vivekena ca yat satkAyadrzwiH darSanam
# 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  la bdag dang bdag-gi #  dang gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  las dben-pa #  dang byis-pa # 'i skye-bo # s kun-brtags-pa # 'i chos kyi rang-bzhin-gyis #  dben-pa # r mthong-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni /
tat satkAyadRzwi parijQAnam
# 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  yongs-su-shes-pa # 'o /
tasya mAna saMyojanam Bavati AvaraNam tat utpatti vibanDAt / kutra kaTam iti Aha aBisamyakAle / sAntara vyantarA smi mAnasam udAcAra vaSena tat aprahANAt iti
# de'i sgrib-pa #  ni nga-rgyal #  gyi kun du sbyor-ba #  yin te / / de skye-ba #  la ba gegs-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-yang #  gang-gi-tshe #  ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / mngon-par-rtogs-pa # 'i dus na nga'o-snyam-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  bar-chad #  dang bcas-pa #  dang-ba # r chad-med-pa # r kun du 'byung-ba # 'i dbang gis de ma-spangs-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
satya aBisamaya kAle nirveDa BAgIya avasTAyAm
# bden-pa #  mngon-par-rtogs-pa # 'i dus ni / / nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i dus so /
tatra sAntaraH pratipakza vyavahitaH vyantaraH pratipakzA avyavahitaH / sa ca aDimAtre mRdO ca pratipakze veditavyaH
# de-la #  bar-chad #  dang bcas-pa #  ni gnyen-po # s bar-du-chod-pa # 'o / / bar-chad-med-pa #  ni gnyen-po # s bar-du-ma-chod-pa #  ste / / de-yang #  gnyen-po #  che-ba #  dang chung-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
yAvat sAntareNa vyantareNa ca asmin yena samudAcarati na tAvat / satkAya dRzwEH prahANam asti
# ji-srid #  du nga'o-snyam-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  bar-chad #  dang bcas-pa #  dang-ba # r chad-med-pa #  kun du 'byung-ba #  de srid du 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  spong-ba #  med de /
satkAya dRzwi balena eva asmin apravRttitaH
# 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba # 'i stobs kyis nga'o-snyam-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
avidyA saMyojanam satkAya dRzwi vastu parijQAne AvaraNam iti sambaDyate / satkAya dRzweH vastu paQca upAdAna skanDAH tat AlambanataH / yaTA uktam sUtre ye kecid SramaNAH brAhmaNAH vE AtmA AtmA iti
# ma-rig-pa # 'i kun du sbyor-ba #  ni / / 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba # 'i gzhi yongs-su-shes-pa #  la sgrib po / / 'jig-tshogs #  la lta pa'i gzhi ni nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga rnams te / / de-la #  dmigs-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / mdo'i-sde #  las kyang ji-skad-du #  /
samanupaSyantaH samanupaSYanti aBiniviSamAnAH aBiniviSante te imAn eva / paQca upAdAna skanDAn upAdAya iti / kim punar tat parijQAnam p / Atmani Atma SUnyatAyAH skanDezu
# dge-sbyong #  bram-ze #  gang-la #  la bdag dang bdag-gi #  rjes su lta-ba #  na / / nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga po 'di dag nyid la brten-nas #  rjes su blta'o / / mngon-par-zhen-pa #  na mngon-pa # r zhen to zhes gsungs so / / yongs-su-shes-pa #  de-yang #  ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
bAla jana parikalpita Darma svaBAva SUnyatAyAH ca yat darSanam anityataH / duHKataH SUnyataH anAtmataH samudAya Aditas vA yat darSanam tat tezAm
# phung-po #  rnams la bdag dang bdag-gis #  stong-pa-nyid #  dang byis-pa # 'i skye-bo # s kun-brtags-pa # 'i chos kyi rang-bzhin-gyis #  stong-pa-nyid #  du mthong-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  dang mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  nyid dang bdag-med-pa #  nyid dang kun-'byung-ba #  la-sogs-pa # r mthong-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni de-dag #  yongs-su-shes-pa # 'o /
parijQAnam / atra eva kAraNam Aha tena upAdAna skanDA aparijQAnAt iti
# 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  des nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  rnams yongs su mi-shes-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
avidyayA hi nitya Adi prakAra AvRtezu skanDezu tat parijQAnA aBAvAt
# ma-rig-pa # s brtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  rnams kyis bsgribs-pa # 'i phung-po #  rnams la de yongs-su-shes-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir /
avidyA skanDa parijQAna AvaraNam
# ma-rig-pa #  ni phung-po #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  la sgrib po /
dRzwi saMyojanam niroDa satya parijQAne AvaraNam iti vartate
# lta-ba # 'i kun du sbyor-ba #  ni / / 'gog-pa # 'i bden-pa #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  la sgrib po /
dRzwi saMyojanam hi tisraH dRzwayaH satkAya anta grAha miTyA dRzwayaH
# lta-ba # 'i kun du sbyor-ba #  ni lta-ba #  la gsum ste; 'jig-tshogs #  dang mthar 'dzin-pa #  dang log-pa # r lta-ba #  rnams so /
tatra satkAya dRzwiH paQca sUpAt AnaskanDezu AtmataH AtmIyataH vA iti / darSanam / anta grAha dRzwiH hi tasmin= eva Atma aBikalpita BAve SASvata darSanam / ucCeda darSanam vA
# de-la #  'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  ni / / nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga rnams la bdag gam bdag-gi # r lta-ba # 'o / / mthar-'dzin-par-lta-ba #  ni bdag tu mngon-pa # r brtag-pa'i-dngos-po #  de-nyid-la #  rtag-par-lta-ba # 'am / / chad-pa # r lta-ba # 'o /
yena darSanena hetum vA Palam vA kriyA vA sat vA vastu apavadate / miTyA vA parikalpayati tat miTyA dRzwiH
# lta-ba #  gang-gi #  rgyu'am 'bras-bu # 'am byed-pa # 'am / / yod-pa'i-dngos-po #  la skur-pa-'debs-pa #  dang log-pa # r kun du rtog-pa #  de ni log-pa # r lta-ba # 'o /
niroDa satya parijQAnam SAnta AdiBiH AkarEH
# 'gog-pa # 'i bden-pa #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  ni zhi-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  rnams so /
kaTam punar tat tasya AvaraNam iti atas Aha / satkAya anta grAha dRzwi BAnta duttrAsAt miTyAdRzwyA ca apavAdAt iti
# ji-ltar-de #  ni de-la #  sgrib can / / de'i-phyir #  'jig-tshogs #  dang mthar-'dzin-par-lta-ba #  gnyis kyis de-la #  skrag-pa #  dang log-pa # r lta-ba # s de-la #  skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tatra satkAya anta grAha dRzwiByAm aham tatra na BavizyAmi iti niroDAt / uttrasyati miTyA dRzwyA ca apavadate na asti eva niroDaH
# de-la #  'jig-tshogs #  dang mthar-'dzin-par-lta-ba #  dag gis bdag der med-pa # r 'gyur ro zhes 'gog-pa #  la skrag-pa # r 'gyur ro; / / log-pa # r lta-ba # s kyang 'gog-pa #  med do zhes skur-pa #  'debs so /
tatra satkAya anta grAha dRzwiByAm SAntataH praNItataH nissaraNataH ca na
# de-la #  'jig-tshogs #  dang mthar 'dzin-pa # r lta bdag-gis #  zhi-ba #  dang gya-nom-pa #  dang nges-par-'byung-ba # r yongs su mi shes la /
parijAnAti miTyA dRzwyA niroDataH na parijAnAti / evam dRzwi saMyojanam niroDa parijQAne AvaraNam
# log-pa # r lta-ba # s 'gog-par #  yongs su mi shes te de-ltar #  lta-ba # 'i kun du sbyor-ba #  ni 'gog-pa #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  la sgrib-pa # 'o /
parAmarSa saMyojanam mArga satya parijQAne / tatra parAmarSa saMyojanam dRzwi parAmarSaH SIla vrata parAmarSaH ca
# mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i kun du sbyor-ba #  ni / / lam gyi bden-pa #  la yongs-su-shes-pa #  la sgrib ste zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i kun du sbyor-ba #  ni / / lta-ba #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  dang tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  mchog-tu #  'dzin ba'o; / / de-la #  lta-ba #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  ni /
tatra dRzwi parAmarSaH dRzwO dRzwi ASrayezu ca paQca sUpa AdAna skanDezu / yat utkarzAditaH darSanam / SIla vrata parAmarSaH SIlam vratam tat uBayam tad ASrayAn vA
# lta-ba #  dang lta-ba # 'i gnas nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga rnams la mchog la-sogs-pa # r lta-ba #  gang-yin-pa # 'o / / tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  ni / / tshul-khrims #  sam / / brtul-zhugs #  sam / / de-gnyi-ga # 'am /
paQca upAdAna skanDAn SudDitaH muktitaH nEryANikataH vA samanupaSyataH yat / darSanam tat SIla vrata parAmarSaH
# de-dag #  gi gnas nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga rnams la / / dag-pa #  dang grol ba dang nges-par-'byin-pa # r yang-dag-par #  rjes su lta-ba # 'i lta-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # 'o /
mArgasya parijQAnam punar nEryANika AdiBiH AkArEH
# lam yongs-su-shes-pa #  yang nges-par-'byin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  rnams su shes-pa # 'o /
kaTam punar parAmarSa saMyojanam mArga parijQAnaH AvaraNam iti atas Aha / anyaTA praSudDi parAmarSanAt iti
# ji-ltar #  na mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i kun du sbyor-ba #  lam yongs-su-shes-pa #  la sgrib ce na / / de'i-phyir #  rnam-pa #  gzhan gyis dag-pa # r mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
SIla vrata mAtrakeNa vA kAma suKa Alayena vA duzkara caryayA vA
# tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  tsam gyis sam / / 'dod-pa'i-bde-ba # 'i gnas kyis sam / / dka'-ba-spyod-pa # s sam /
sAMKya Adi jQAnena vA SudDi parAmarSanAt
# grangs can la-sogs-pa # 'i shes-pa # s dag-pa # r mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
dRzwi parAmarSena tu yena eva SudDim pratyeti tat eva agratas parAmRSati
# lta-ba #  la mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # s kyang gang-gis #  dag-pa # r yid-ches-pa #  de nyid dam-pa # r mchog-tu #  'dzin to /
evaMparA AmarSa saMyojanena mArgam tyajati anyaTA ca SudDim parAmRSati iti
# de-ltar-na #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i kun du sbyor-ba # s lam bor-te #  rnam-pa #  gzhan gyis dag-pa # r mchog-tu #  'dzin to /
vicikitsA saMyojanam ratnatraya parijQAne AvaraNam iti vartate / kaTam iti atas bravIti tat guNA anaBiSradDAnAt iti / vicikitsA saMyojanam sati aratnezu vimatiH
# the-tshom #  gyi kun du sbyor-ba #  ni dkon-mchog-gsum #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  la sgrib ste / / ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / de'i yon-tan #  la mngon-pa # r yid-mi-ches-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / the-tshom #  gyi kun du sbyor-ba #  ni bden-pa #  de dang dkon-mchog #  rnams la yid-gnyis-za-ba #  ste /
prakarzeNa apanIta sarva guNa dozasya paryanta ASraya tvena budDa ratne / parijQAnam p
# sangs-rgyas #  dkon-mchog #  la yon-tan #  dang nyes-pa #  thams-cad #  phul du phyin pa dang bsal-ba # 'i mthar-thug-pa # 'i gnas su yongs-su-shes-pa # 'o /
saMsAra sAgara uttaraka tvena sarva sa hetuka duHKA atyanta viyoga Atmaka tvena tat / pratipAdaka tvena ca Darma ratne parijQAnam
# chos dkon-mchog #  la 'khor-ba # 'i rgya-mtsho #  las sgrol ba dang rgyu-dang-bcas-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal #  dang gtan-du #  bral-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  de / / de khong-du-chud-pa # r byed-pa # r yongs-su-shes-pa # 'o /
SrAmaNya pala sTa tvena anuttara dakziNIya kzetra tvena ca AsaFGa ratne / parijQAnam
# dge-'dun #  dkon-mchog #  la dge-sbyong-gi-'bras-bu #  la gnas-pa #  dang der zhugs-pa #  dang bla-na-med-pa # 'i sbyin-gnas #  kyi zhing yin par yongs-su-shes-pa # 'o /
satya darSanAt prahINa vicikitsaH ca avetya prasAda lABena / ratnatraya guNe aBiSraddatte nA aprahINa vicikitse iti
# bden-pa #  dang mthong-ba #  dang the-tshom #  spang-ba # 'i phyir shes-nas-dad-pa #  rnyed-pa # s dkon-mchog-gsum #  gyi yon-tan #  la mngon-pa # r yid ches kyi the-tshom #  ma-spangs-pa #  ni ma yin no /
atas vicikitsA saMyojanam ratnatraya parijQAnaH AvaraNam uktam
# de'i-phyir #  the-tshom #  gyi kun du sbyor-ba #  ni dkon-mchog-gsum #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  la sgrib ces bya'o /
IrzyA saMyojanam lABa satkAra parijQAnaH AvaraNam
# phrag-dog #  gi kun du sbyor-ba #  ni rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  la sgrib ces bya'o /
atra eva kAraNam Aha tat dozA adarSanAt iti
# 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  / / de'i nyes-pa #  mi mthong-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya'o #  /
IrzyA saMKyA yojanam hi lABa satkAra raktaH anya sampad pratiGa aMSikaH cetasaH / vyArozaH
# phrag-dog #  gi kun du sbyor-ba #  ni rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  la chags-pa #  ste / / gzhan gyi phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  la zhe-sdang #  gi char gtogs-pa # s sems khong nas 'khrug-pa # 'o /
sarva anarTa ASraya tvAt avaboDaH lABa satkAra parijQAnam
# rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  la gnod-pa #  thams-cad-kyi #  gnas yin par khong-du-chud-pa #  ni yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya'o /
IrzyayA tu lABa satkAram sarva guNa vipakza BUta tvena / viviDA anarTa mUla tvena ca na parijAnAti iti atas lABa satkAra / parijQAnaH AvaraNam irzyA saMyojanam
# phrag-dog #  gis ni rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  yon-tan-thams-cad #  kyi mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  su gyur-pa #  dang gnod-pa #  sna-tshogs #  kyi rtsa bar gyur-pa # r mi-shes-pa # s / / de'i-phyir #  phrag-dog #  gi kun du sbyor-ba #  ni rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  la sgrib po /
mAtsarya saMyojanam saMleKa parijQAna AvaraNam iti / kaTam iti atas Aha / parizkArA aDyavasAnAt iti
# ser-sna # 'i kun du sbyor-ba #  ni yo-byad-bsnyungs-pa #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  la sgrib po / / ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  yo-byad #  la lhag-par-zhen-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / ser-sna #  ni yo-byad #  rnams la lhag-par-chags-pa #  ste /
mAtsaryam parizkAre ezu avyavasitaH rAga aMSikaH cetasaH upakaraNezu AgrahaH / saMleKaH parizkArEH vivekaH
# 'dod-chags #  kyi char gtogs-pa # s 'tshog-chas #  rnams la sems kun du 'dzin-pa # 'o / / yo-byad-bsnyungs-pa #  ni yo-byad #  rnams las lhag-pa # r dben-pa # 'o /
tasya sarva guNa ASraya vastu tvena avaboDaH parijQAnam
# de-la #  yon-tan-thams-cad #  kyi gnas-kyi-dngos-po # r yongs su rtogs-pa #  ni yongs-su-shes-pa # 'o /
na tu mAtsaryeNa parizkArA aDyavAsAnAt sarva guNa ASraya tvena / parijAnAti iti atas saMleKa parijQAne mAtsarya AvaraNa tvam uktam
# ser-sna #  ni yo-byad #  rnams la lhag-par-chags-pa # s / / yon-tan-thams-cad #  kyi gnas su yongs su mi shes te / / de'i-phyir #  yo-byad-bsnyungs-pa #  la sgrib po zhes bshad do /
tatra anunaya pratiGa saMyojane tattva aDigama prayoga AvaraNe
# de-la #  rjes-su-chags-pa #  dang khong-khro-ba # 'i kun du sbyor-ba #  ni de-kho-na-rtogs-pa # r byed-pa # r sbyor-ba #  ni sgrib kyi / / lhag-ma #  rnams ni ma yin no /
SezANi tu prayuktasya tattva darSanasya AvaraNAni tasmAt eva tezAm / anukramaH / tat yaTA avaSyam praTamam eva mumukzUNAm saMsArAt citttam / udvejayitavyam
# lhag-ma #  rnams ni de-kho-na-rtogs-pa # r byed-pa # r zhugs-pa # r byed-pa #  la sgrib po / / de nyid kyi phyir de-dag #  gi go-rims #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / thar-pa-'dod-pa # s thog-ma #  nyid-du #  gdon-mi-za-bar #  'khor-ba #  la sems-skyo-ba # r bya'o; /
tatas sarvatas upekzeNa Bavitavyam
# de nas thams-cad-la #  btang-snyoms #  su bya'o /
tatas sarvA anarTa mUla tvAt satkAyadRzwiH parijQeyA
# de nas gnod-pa #  thams-cad-kyi #  rtsa ba yin-pas #  'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya'o /
tat anantaram dukH samudaya Atmaka tvena tat vastu parijQeam
# de'i-'og-tu #  de'i gzhi la sdug-bsngal #  dang kun-'byung-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  du yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya'o /
tatas tad niroDaH vijQeyaH
# de nas de 'gog-pa-shes-pa # r bya'o /
tat anantaram lABa mArgaH vijQeyaH
# de'i-'og-tu #  thob-pa # 'i lam-shes-pa # r bya'o /
tatas satya darSanAt ratnatraye tat guNAH avaboDAt avetya prasAda lABaH
# de nas bden-pa-mthong-ba #  dang yon-tan #  de-dag #  rtog-pa # 'i phyir dkon-mchog #  la shes-nas-dad-pa #  'thob po /
satya darSana balena eva ca lABa satkAra saMleKayoH doza guNa darSI
# bden-pa-mthong-ba # 'i stobs nyid kyis kyang rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  dang yo-byad-bsnyungs-pa #  gnyis kyi nyes-pa #  dang yon-tan #  mthong-ba #  yin no /
Bavati iti evam AvaraNIya Darma krama hetunA tad AvaraNa kramaH veditavyaH
# de-ltar #  bsgrib-pa # r bya-ba # 'i chos kyi go-rims #  kyi rgyus de'i sgrib-pa # 'i go-rims #  kyang rig-par-bya # 'o /
nanu sarvasya api sarvatra AvaraNa tvena saMBavAt
# thams-cad-la #  yang thams-cad #  sgrib-pa #  nyid-du #  srid-pa # 'i phyir /
vastu pratiniyamena AvaraNa nirdeSaH na yuktaH
# gzhi so-sor-nges-pa # s sgrib-pa # r bshad-pa #  ni mi-rigs-pa #  ma yin nam zhe na /
na eva atra vastu pratiniyamaH kriyate kintarhi pratyAsat titaH prADAnya eza / nirdeSaH / boDisattva AvaraNam p
# 'dir gzhi so-sor-nges-pa # r bya-ba #  ni ma yin gyi / / so-so # r nye-bar-gnas-pa # 'i phyir gtso bor byas te 'di bstan to / / ci sgrib-pa #  de zad dam zhe na /
kim etat eva AvaraNam / etat tu sAmAnyam boDisattva SrAvaka AdInAm / boDisattvAn antvAvaraNam / SuBa AdO daSaDA aparam / AvaraNam / ke ca SuBa AdayaH iti na jQAyate / atas Aha / aprayogaH anAyatane ayoga vihitaH ca yaH / iti evamAdya AvaraNam / SuBa AdayaH punar / SuBam boDiH samAdAnam
# de ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  dang nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i spyi thun no / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi sgrib-pa #  ni / / dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  bcu la gzhan sgrib-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  dang dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  yang gang yin mi shes te / / de'i-phyir #  / / sbyor-ba #  med dang skye-mched #  min / / rnal-'byor #  min pas gang bskyed dang / / zhes gsungs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ni sgrib-pa # 'o / / dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni / / dge dang byang-chub #  yang dag 'dzin /
ityAdi daSa arTAH
# zhes-bya-ba #  la sgos-pa #  don bcu'o /
tatra SuBam hi boDi hetu BUtam sarva kuSala mUlam
# de-la #  dge-ba #  ni byang-chub #  kyi rgyur-gyur-pa #  ste dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba thams-cad #  do /
boDiH tu tat Palam
# byang-chub #  ni de'i 'bras-bu # 'o /
tatra SuBam sAmAnyatas uddizwam praBedataH svaBAvataH ca na vijQAyata / iti atas tat pratipAdana arTam AraByate / samAdAnam DImattA aBra antya na AvRtI / na anyatra asaH amatsari tvam vaSitvam ca / iti etat SuBam iti
# de-la #  dge-ba #  ni spyir bstan-pa #  bas rab-tu-dbye-ba #  dang rang-bzhin #  mi shes-nas #  de'i-phyir #  de khong-du-chud-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir rtsom ste / / yang dag 'dzin / / blo ldan 'khrul med sgrib-pa #  med / / bsngo dang mi skrag ser-sna #  med / / ces bya-ba #  de-dag #  ni dge bzhes-bya'o #  /
boDiH api vacana mAtreNa svaBAvataH na vijQAyate iti asyAH viBu tvam
# byang-chub #  kyang smos-pa #  tsam gyis rang-bzhin #  mi shes te / / de'i-phyir #  de ni dbang ngo zhes ston to /
darSayati / SuBasya boDeH ca samAdAna AdInAm iva svAtantryeNa AvaraNa nirdeSAt / svAtantryam eva atra vijQAyate na tat deSa nirdeSa BAvaH iti eke / utpatti AvaraNam hi SUBe vyavasTApyate tat ca boDi citta AdInAm
# kha-cig #  na re dge-ba #  dang byang-chub #  dang yang-dag-par-'dzin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  sgrib-pa #  rang-gi-rgyud #  yod-pa # r bshad-pa # s / / 'dir rang-gi-rgyud #  yod-pa-nyid #  du shes kyi / / bstan-pa-dang-bshad-pa # 'i dngos-po # r ni ma yin no zhe'o / / skye-ba #  la sgrib-pa #  ni dge-ba #  la rnam-pa # r gzhag go / / de-yang #  byang-chub #  kyi sems la-sogs-pa #  rnams kyi spyi thun yin gyi /
sAmAnyam tasyAH SuBa utpAdya tvAt
# dge-ba #  ni bskyed-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro /
DRti Adya AvaraNantu samAdAna Adi AvaraNam samAdAna Adizu / vRtti Adi arTa BedAt boDiH api ekopyA prAptavyA ca iti atas tasyAH
# yang-dag-par-'dzin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la sgrib-pa #  dang rten la-sogs-pa #  la sgrib-pa #  ni yang-dag-par-'dzin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rnams kyi sgrib-pa #  ste tha dad do / / byang-chub #  ni mi 'khrug-pa #  dang thob-par-bya-ba #  yin-pas #  de'i-phyir #  /
sTiti AvaraNam prApti AvaraNam ca vyavasTApyate / tasmAt na asti atra svAtantrya prasaFgaH iti
# de'i-gnas #  pa la sgrib-pa #  dang thob-par-bya-ba #  la sgrib-pa #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ste / / de-bas-na #  de rang-gi-rgyud #  du yod-pa # r mi 'gyur ro /
kramaH ca tezAm samAsatas kuSala mUlam niravaSezam nizpAdya boDiH / prAptavyA
# de-dag #  gi go-rims #  kyang mdor-na #  dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba ma-lus-par #  bsgrubs-nas #  byang-chub #  thob-pa # r bya'o /
vyAsataH punar praTamatas eva boDi cittam utpAdayitavyam / sva para arTa sampadADAra BUta tvAt / tatas citta utpAdanA anurUpA dAna Adizu pratipattiH yayA boDisattva / iti AKyAm laBate / tatas asaMKyeya kalpena aByasyataH puNya jQAna samBAra saQcayAt
# rgyas-pa # r ni thog-ma #  nyid-du #  byang-chub #  kyi sems-bskyed-pa # r bya ste / / bdag-dang-gzhan-gyi-don #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa # 'i gzhir gyur ba'i phyir ro / / de nas sems-bskyed-pa #  dang mthun-par #  sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bsgrub-pa # r bya ste / / des byang-chub-sems #  dpar mngon no / / de nas bskal-pa-grangs-med-pa # r goms-pa # r byas te /
ASaya viSoDana arTam pudgala Darma BrAnti pratipakzeNa aBrAnti AtmakaH AtmakaH AtmakaH / darSana mArgaH utpAdayitavyaH
# bsod nams dang ye-shes-kyi-tshogs #  bsags-pa # s bsam-pa # r rnam-pa # r sbyang-ba # 'i phyir / / gang-zag #  dang chos la nor-ba # 'i gnyen-po # r ma nor-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  mthong-ba'i-lam #  bskyed-pa # r bya'o /
tatas ca AvaraNa vigama praBAvitaH BAvanA mArgaH prakarzam netavyaH / viSudDi viSeza yoga arTam p
# de nas rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i khyad-par #  dang ldan-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir sgrib-pa-dang-bral-ba # s rab-tu-phye-ba #  bsgom-pa'i-lam #  mthar-phyin-pa # r bya'o /
tatas SrAvaka Adi atikramaNa prayogeNa yaTA upacitAni sarvANi etAni / lOkika kalka uttarANi kuSala mUlAni boDO pariNAmayitavyAni
# de nas nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  las 'da' bar sbyor-ba # s 'jig-rten #  dang 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba ji-ltar #  bsags-pa #  de-dag #  thams-cad #  byang-chub #  tu yongs-su-bsngo-ba # r bya'o /
tatas ca nAma vasTAm AgataH mahA boDya ASaya tvAt budDa boDisattvAnAm / gamBIra udArezu nirdeSezu na trasyati
# de nas gnas de thob-pa #  dang byang-chub-chen-po # r bsam-pa # r mi-byed-pa # s / / sangs-rgyas #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi bstan-pa #  zab cing rgya-che-ba #  rnams la skrag-pa # r mi 'gyur ro /
tatas bahu Sruta pratipatti yuktaH udAram Darmam nirdiSati / sattva paripAcana arTam
# de nas mang-du-thos-pa #  dang rtogs-pa #  dang ldan nas sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir chos rgya-cher #  ston to /
tatas paripakva vineyezu tad vimocana arTam vaSitvam budDa tvam avApnoti iti
# de nas 'dul-ba #  yongs su smin nas de-dag #  rnam-par-dgrol-ba # 'i phyir dbang ste / / sangs-rgyas #  nyid thob po /
atra hi triMSat AvaraNAni uktAni AvaraNIya arTAH SuBa AdayaH daSa / ca iti atas pRcCati ezAm tu SuBa AdInAm kasya katyA AvaraNAni / vijQeyAni iti / atas Aha / trINi trINi ca etezAm jQeyAni AvaraNAni hi iti
# 'dir sgrib-pa #  sum cu dang bsgrib-pa # r bya-ba #  dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i don bcu bshad bas de'i-phyir #  dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  de rnams la gang-la #  sgrib-pa #  du yod-pa #  mi shes-nas #  dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  / / de-dag #  gi ni sgrib-pa #  rnams / / gsum gsum dag tu shes-pa # r bya /
kuSalasya trINi AvaraNAni iti / aprayogaH anAramBaH
# zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so / / de-la #  sgrib-pa #  gsum zhes-bya-ba #  la sbyor-ba #  med-pa #  ni rtsom pa med-pa # 'o /
kim atra AvaraNam
# 'di-la #  sgrib-pa #  gang zhe na /
yena kleSena na prayujyate pramAdena kOsIdyena vA yasmin= avasTA viSeze
# bag-med-pa # 'ang le-lo # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  gang-gis #  mi sbyor-ba #  ste /
kleSa bIja anugate avyAkRte klizwe vA na prayujyate / na prayujyate nityam gOravAt vA alapa tvAt vA iti apratyogaH ucyate na tu / prayoga aBAvAt tasmin= AvaraNA anupapatteH
# nyon-mongs-pa # 'i sa-bon-dang-ldan-pa #  lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'am / / nyon-mongs-pa # r gyur-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  kyi bye-brag #  gang-du #  mi sbyor-ba # 'o / / rgyun-du #  ma chud-pa # 'am gus-par #  mi sbyor-ba #  ste / / chung-ba # s na sbyor-ba #  med-pa #  zhes bya'i / / sbyor-ba #  med-pa #  ni ma yin te / / de-la #  sgrib-pa # r mi 'thad-pa # 'i phyir ro / / skye-mched #  ma-yin-pa #  la sbyor-ba #  ni /
anAyatana prayogaH boDeH boDya AvAhakAnAn ca kuSala mUlAnAm yat / pravacanam utpatti dvAram tad Ayatanam tasmAt anyat anAyatanam
# byang-chub #  dang byang-chub #  thob-par-byed-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba rnams skye-ba # 'i sgo gsung-rab #  gang-yin-pa #  de skye-mched #  de / / de-las-gzhan-pa #  ni skye-mched #  ma yin no /

# der sbyor-ba #  ni 'di-las #  phyi-rol-pa-rnams #  skye-mched #  ma-yin-pa #  la sbyor-ba # 'o / / de-la #  sgrib-pa #  gang zhe na / / mi-shes-pa # 'am lta-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  gang-gis #  skye-mched #  ma-yin-pa #  la sbyor-ba #  ste / / sbyor-ba #  de-nyid-la #  ni sgrib-pa # 'o / / tshul-bzhin-ma-yin-pa #  la sbyor-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la tshul-bzhin #  ni thabs te /
yasya yaH upAyaH tasmAt anyaTA prayogaH ayoni SaH prayogaH

# yang-na #  gnas-skabs #  kyi bye-brag #  gi tshe dge-ba #  la skye-ba #  la sgrib-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de nyid byang-chub #  kyi sgrib-pa #  yang yin te /
