# snying-rje-med-pa #  ni sems-can-gyi-don #  gyis skyo-bar-'gyur-ba # 'am sgyid-lug-pa # r 'gyur ro / / blo-dang-ldan-pa #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  nyid de zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
svaBAvena SrAvaka Adi gotrakeByaH tIkzNa indriya tvAt sarvaTA / sarva jQeya upakarza aDikAri tvAt gamBIra udAra DarmA aDimukteH ca / boDisattvaH eva DImAn nA anyaH / boDisattva tA viparyastA para arTa parA pratipattiH
# rang-bzhin-gyis #  nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rigs can rnam-pa # s dbang-po-rno-ba #  dang shes-par-bya-ba #  thams-cad-kyi #  rnam-pa-thams-cad #  la nye-bar-rtog-pa # 'i skabs yin pa dang chos zab cing rgya-che-ba #  la mos-pa # s / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  nyid blo ldan yin gyi gzhan ni ma yin no / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  nyid ni gzhan-gyi-don #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r sgrub-pa # 'o; /
pratipatteH vEDuryam pAramita Adizu apravRttiH / boDisattvaH hi pratipatti vRttaH jQeyaH
# sgrub-pa #  dang mi ldan zhes pa ni pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la mi-'jug-pa # 'o / / sgrub-pa #  la gnas-pa #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  shes so /
kujanaH mUrKa janaH iti aparIkzaka janaH iti arTaH
# skye-bo #  ngan-pa #  ni skye-bo #  blun po'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni yongs su mi-rtog-pa # 'i skye-bo #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  ste /
kujanaH hi pratipatti yuktam api boDisattva upamitam na jAnIte
# skye-bo #  ngan-pa #  ni sgrub-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  la 'de'o zhes mi-shes-pa # 'o /
duzwa janaH pratihataH iti boDisattva dveziNaH / te hi ranDrA anvayitvA boDisattvasya BUtAn guNAn na paSyanti
# skye-bo #  sdang-ba #  ni zhe-'gras-pa #  rnams so zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  la zhe-sdang-ba #  rnams te / / de-dag #  glags-tshol-ba # s byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i yon-tan-yang-dag-pa #  rnams ni mi mthong la /
asat doza darSanAt pratiGa rOdra cittAt vA BUtAn guNAn / pracCAdyA aDyAropyA asBUtAn dozAn prakASayanti
# nyes-pa-med-pa #  ni mthong-ba # 'am zhe-sdang #  gis gnod-pa # r sems-pa # s yon-tan-yang-dag-pa #  rnams bcas te / / sgro btags-nas #  med-pa # 'i nyes-pa #  sgrogs-pa # 'o /
kim atra AvaraNam
# 'di-la #  sgrib-pa #  gang zhe na /
dAna pAramitA Adi vipakzaH ajQAnam pradvezaH ca iti / aBrAnteH trINi
# sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang mi-shes-pa #  dang zhe-sdang-ba # 'o / / 'khrul-pa-med-pa # 'i sgrib-pa #  gsum ni zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
aDyAropa apavAdAt BrAntiH tat pratipakzaH tu BrAti aBAvaH / darSana mArgaH
# sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i phyir 'khrul-pa # 'o / / gnyen-po #  ni 'khrul-pa-med-pa #  ste / / mthong-ba'i-lam #  mo /
viparyAsa dOzWulyam grAhya grAhakA aBiniveSa vAsanA paripuzwiH iti
# kha-cig #  na re phyin-ci-log #  gi gnas-ngan-len #  ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i bag-chags #  brtas-pa # 'o zhe'o /
kecid / sarvezAm darSana heyAnAm anuSayAnAm
# gzhan dag na re mthong-ba # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i bag-la-nyal #  thams-cad #  dam /
sarvatraga Darma DAtu boDa pratibudDasya p / vA aklizwasyA ajQAnasya Alaya vijQAna sannivizwa bIja paripozaH iti anye
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  thams-cad-du-'gro-ba # r khong-du-chud-pa # r bya-ba # 'i gegs su gyur-pa #  nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i mi-shes-pa # 'i sa-bon #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la gnas-pa #  yongs su gsos pa'o zhe'o /
Atma Adi aBAvaH Atma Adi vikalpaH hi viparyAsaH iti apare
# gzhan dag na re bdag la-sogs-pa #  med-pa # r bdag la-sogs-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni phyin-ci-log #  go zhe'o /
kleSa Adi AvaraNa trayAt anyatamA avaSiztata iti
# nyon-mongs-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sgrib-pa #  gsum las lhag-ma #  gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  /
tatra kleSa AvaraNam yaH tIvra Ayata kAla samudAcAri kleSaH rAga AdikaH tat
# nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  ni shas-che-ba #  dang yun-ring-po-nas #  'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  kun du 'byung-ba #  ste /
pratipakza prayogA anavakASAt aBra anteH AvaraNam
# de'i gnyen-po #  la sbyor-ba # 'i skabs mi 'byed-pa # s 'khrul-pa-med-pa #  la sgrib po /
karma AvaraNam anantara Adi karma yat apAya niyamanam
# las-kyi-sgrib-pa #  ni mtshams-med-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i las ngan-song #  du nges-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
vipAka AvaraNam apAya AdayaH tatra utpannasya Arya Darma utpatti BAgaH na asti
# rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i sgrib-pa #  ni ngan-song #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / der skyes-pa #  la 'phags-pa # 'i chos skye-ba # 'i skal-ba #  med do /
tezAm kleSa karma janmanAm anyatamam api aviSIzwam AvaraNam na punar
# nyon-mongs-pa #  dang las dang tshe de-dag #  las lhag-ma #  gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhig sgrib-pa #  yin gyi zad-pa # r ni ma yin no /
kRtsnam / vimukti paripAcinyAH prajQAyAH aparipakvatA ca iti
# rnam-par-grol-ba # 'i yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-pa # 'i shes-rab #  yongs-su-ma-smin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
vimuktyA vAhikAyAH prajQAyAH akarmaNya tA
# rnam-par-grol-ba #  thob-par-byed-pa # 'i shes-rab #  las-su-mi-rung-ba # 'o /
nirveDa BAgIya avasTAyAH aprApti tvAt iti kecid
# kha-cig #  na re de ni nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i gnas-ma #  thob-pa # 'i phyir zhe'o /
anyetvA AhuH nirvikalpA atra prajQA vimukti paripAcinI tat prayogikA ca / dvitIyA / tayoH aparipakvatA tattva aDigamA ayogya tA tat upanizad BAvA ayogyatA / cA paripUrNaMBAra tvAt yaTAkramam
# gzhan dag na re rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  dang de-la #  sbyor-ba #  can gnyis ni / / 'dir rnam-par-grol-ba #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-pa # 'i shes-rab #  po / / de gnyis yongs-su-ma-smin-pa #  ni tshogs yongs-su-ma-rdzogs-pa # 'i phyir de-kho-na-rtogs-pa # 'i 'os ma-yin-pa #  dang de'i rgyu'i-dngos-po # 'i 'os ma-yin-pa #  ste go-rims #  bzhin no zhe'o /
kim atra AvaraNam
# 'di-la #  sgrib-pa #  gang zhe na /
darSana heya kleSasya puzwa vAsanA kleSa AvaraNa AdInAm anyatamA avaSizwa tA / prajQA paripAka vibanDa BUtam ajQAnam samBArA aparipUrNa tA ca
# mthong-ba # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa # 'i bag-chags #  brtas-pa #  dang nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i lhag-ma-gzhan #  gang-yang-rung-ba #  dang shes-rab #  yongs-su-smin-pa # 'i gegs su gyur-pa #  mi-shes-pa #  dang tshogs yongs-su-ma-rdzogs-pa # 'o /
AvaraNa prahANam anAvaraNam iti / AvaraNam prahIyate anena iti AvaraNa aprahANam AvaraNa pratipakzAt / anAvaraNam BAvanA mArgaH / tasya trINi
# sgrib-pa #  spangs-pa #  ni sgrib-pa-med-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dis sgrib-pa-spong-ba # r byed-pa # s sgrib-pa-spong-ba #  ste / / sgrib-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  yin-pas #  sgrib-pa-med-pa #  ni bsgom-pa'i-lam #  mo / / de'i sgrib-pa #  gsum ni lhan-cig-skyes-pa # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
sahajam dOzWulyam BAvanA Aheya kleSA anuSayaH / sahajam vA Atma dRzwi AdInAm / DarmaDAtu sparSa arTa Adi prativeDa vibanDakasya asyA
# bsgom-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa # 'i bag-la-nyal #  lo / / yang-na #  bdag-tu-lta-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  lhan-cig-skyes-pa #  rnams dang chos-kyi-dbyings #  mchog gi don la-sogs-pa #  rtogs-pa # 'i gegs-byed-pa #  nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i mi-shes-pa # 'i sa-bon #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la gnas-pa #  yongs su gsos pa'o /
paripuzwa bIjam / kOsIdyam moha aMSikA dAlasyAt cittA aByutsAhaH
# le-lo #  ni snyom-las #  te gti-mug #  gi char gtogs-pa # s sems mngon-pa # r mi spro-ba # 'o /
pramAdaH ca vizaya vyAsaFgaH kuSale ca
# bag-med-pa # s ni yul la rnam-par-chags-pa #  dang dge-ba #  la mi-'jug-pa # 'o /
samADeH AsvAdinA atra pramAdaH iti eke
# kha-cig #  na re ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi ro myang-ba #  ni bag-med-pa # 'o zhe'o /
tatra dOzWulyAt ca mArgam na BAvayati
# de-la #  gnas-ngan-len #  dang le-lo # s ni lam mi bsgom mo /
pramAdAt akuSalAt cittAm na rakzati
# bag-med-pa # s ni mi-dge-ba #  las sems mi srung-ba # 'o /
kim atra AvaraNam / etat eva trayam
# 'di-la #  sgrib-pa #  gang zhe na / / gsum po de nyid do /
pariNAteH trINi yEH anyatra cittam pariNAmayati iti / tatra pariNatiH utpannAnAm kuSala mUlAnAm budDa tvam eva cittena / niyamanam / tasyAH trINi AvaraNAni
# yongs-su-bsngo-ba # 'i sgrib-pa #  gsum ni gang dag gis sems gzhan-du #  sngo-ba # r byed kyi bla-na-med-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa'i-byang-chub #  tu mi bsngo zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  bsngo-ba #  de ni dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba skyes shing byung-ba #  rnams sangs-rgyas #  nyid-du #  sems-kyis #  nges-par-byed-pa # 'o / / de-la #  sgrib-pa #  gsum ste /
katamAni trINi yEH anyatra budDa tvAt saMsAre SrAvaka Adi boDaH vA / cittam pariNAmayati nA anuttarAyAm samyaksambanDO / tAni punar Bava saktiH Boga sakti lIna citta tA ca
# gsum gang zhe na / / gang dag gis sangs-rgyas #  nyid las gzhan-du #  'khor-ba # 'am / / nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i byang-chub #  tu sems yongs su sngo-ba # r byed kyi / / bla-na-med-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa'i-byang-chub #  tu mi bsngo'o / / de-dag #  kyang-srid-pa #  la chags-pa #  dang longs-spyod #  la chags-pa #  dang sems-zhum-pa #  dang /
BavaH paQca upAdAna skanDAH
# srid-pa #  ni nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga rnams so /
Bujyante iti BogAH rUpa AdayaH vizayAH / tayoH aBizvaFgaH saktiH
# spyad-par-bya-ba #  na / / longs-spyod #  de gzugs la-sogs-pa #  yul rnams so / / de-dag #  la rnam-par-chags-pa #  ni chags-pa # 'o /
lIna citta tA anudAra citta tA kva budDa tvam kva ca madviDa / iti Atmani asamBAvanA
# sems-zhum-pa #  ni sems rgya chung-ba #  ste / / sangs-rgyas #  nyid-du #  ga la 'grub / / bdag lta-bu # s ga la zhig ces bdag la mi srid-pa # r sems so /
tatra ca Bava saktyA Boga saktyA ca sugatO cittam pariNAmayati
# de-la #  srid-pa #  la chags-pa #  dang longs-spyod #  la chags-pa # s ni bde-'gro # r sems sngo-ba # r byed do /
lIna citta tatyA SrAvaka Adi yAne pariNAmayati kim atra AvaraNam
# sems-zhum-pa # s ni nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa # r sngo-ba # r byed do / / 'di-la #  sgrib-pa #  gang zhe na /
Bava Boga tRzNA kOsIdyam akAruNya Qca p / atra Asasya trINi / kaH ayam atra asaH
# srid-pa #  dang longs-spyod #  la sred-pa #  dang le-lo #  dang snying-rje-med-pa # 'o / / mi-skrag-pa # 'i sgrib-pa #  gsum ni zhes-bya-ba #  la / / mi-skrag-pa #  gang zhe na /
SUnyatAyAm gamBIra udArezu ca budDa boDisattva Darmezu aDimuktiH / aBIrutA
# stong-pa-nyid #  dang sangs-rgyas #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i chos zab cing rgya-che-ba #  la mos shing mi-'jigs-pa # 'o /
asamBAvanA pudgale mahAyAna naya aBiDyAyinaH pudgalasya / BrAntyA avagamaH vacanaQca SIla samADi prajQA Adi guNasya / vA sampratyayaH
# gang-zag #  la mi srid snyam pa ni theg-pa-chen-po'i-tshul #  mngon-par-brjod-pa # 'i gang-zag #  la ma nor par khong du chud cing 'chad-pa #  dang tshul-khrims #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang shes-rab #  la-sogs-pa #  yon-tan #  la yid-mi-ches-pa # 'o /
anaDimuktiH Darme gamBIra udAra naya pratipAdake / budDa vacana tvena aviparItA arTena ca / yaTA ruta vicAraNA arTe
# chos la mi mos-pa #  ni sangs-rgyas-kyi-gsung-rab #  la tshul zab cing rgya-che-ba #  khong-du-chud-pa # r byed-pa #  dang don ma-log-pa # 'o zhes yid-mi-ches-pa # 'o /
anutpannA anirudDa Adi SAnta Adi arTa yaTASabdam eva pratipadyate na / ca aBiprAyika arTa tattvam avagacCati
# don la sgra bzhin-du #  spyod-pa #  ni ma-skyes-pa #  dang ma 'gags-pa #  dang gzod-ma-nas #  zhi-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i don la sgra ji bzhin kho-nar #  rtog-pa # r byed cing dgongs-pa'i-don #  gyi de-kho-na #  khong du mi chud-pa #  ste /
tasmAt anutpanna Adi arTA anaDimuktiH
# de'i-phyir #  ma-skyes-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i don la mi mos so /
kim atra AvaraNam
# 'di-la #  sgrib-pa #  gang zhe na /
vicikitsA prajQA samADi vipakza BUta jQAnam aBiprAyika arTam iti rota vicAraNA / vipakza BUta QcA iti / amAtsaryasya trINi
# the-tshom #  dang shes-rab #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  su gyur-pa #  mi-shes-pa #  dang dgongs-pa'i-don #  la spyod-pa #  mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  su gyur-pa # 'o / / ser-sna #  med-pa # 'i sgrib-pa #  gsum ni zhes-bya-ba #  la /
amAtsaryam yatas sadDarma sTitaye anya anugraha arTam vA Darma deSanA / sadDarme agOravam acitrI kAraH
# ser-sna #  med-pa #  ni gang-gis #  dam-pa'i-chos #  gnas-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ram / / gzhan rjes su gzung-ba # 'i phyir chos-ston-par-byed-pa # 'o / / dam-pa'i-chos #  la ched cher mi-'dzin-pa #  ni gces su mi-'dzin-pa #  ste /
tena anyasantAnA anA prApaNAt cira sTitikam sat Darmam na
# des gzhan-gyi-sems #  kyi rgyud la go-ba # r mi-byed-pa #  dang dam-pa'i-chos #  yun-ring-du-gnas-pa # r mi-byed-pa # 'o /
lABa satkAra pUjAyAm gOravam citrIkAraH sadDarma gOrave mA anyaH api / mad tulyaH aDikaH vA Bavizyati iti ASaFkA
# rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  dang mchod-pa #  la ched cher mi-'dzin-pa #  ni gces su mi-'dzin-pa # 'o / / dam-pa'i-chos #  la ched cher 'dzin-kyang #  / / bdag-dang-gzhan #  mtshungs sam lhag gi dogs te /
tasmAt lABa Adi vyavaDAnam Bavizyati iti BItyA Darmam na deSayati
# de'i-phyir #  rnyed-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bar-chad-du-'gyur-ba # s 'jigs nas chos mi 'chad-pa # 'o /
lABa satkAra aDyavasAne avidyamAne api sattvezu akAruQaQca iti sattvena ezu
# rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  la lhag-par-zhen-pa #  med kyang sems-can #  rnams la snying-rje-med-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
karuNa aBAvAt na deSayati
# sems-can #  rnams la snying-rje-med-pa # s chos mi 'chad de /
na hi akAruNikaH sattva duHKena apakriyate / kim atra AvaraNam
# snying-rje-med-pa #  ni sems-can #  gyi sdug-bsngal-gyi-gnod-pa # r mi 'gyur ro / / 'di-la #  sgring [?] pa gang zhe na /
agOravam lABa sakAra saktiH akAruQaQca iti / vaSitvasya trINi AvaraNAni iti arTaH
# ched cher mi-'dzin-pa #  dang rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  la chags-pa #  dang snying-rje-med-pa # 'o / / dbang gi sgrib-pa #  gsum ni zhes-bya-ba #  la /
vaSitvam hi sarvezAm citta vaSi tvAnAm prAptiH budDa tvam / tasya trINi AvaNAni punar na jQAyante iti atas Aha yEH viBu tvam na / laBate iti
# dbang ni sems kyi dbang rnam-pa-thams-cad #  thob-pa # s sangs-rgyas #  nyid dbang ngo / / de'i sgrib-pa-gsum-po-dag #  mi-shes-pa # s de'i-phyir #  / / gang dag gis dbang-byed-pa #  mi-'thob-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
citta vaSi tva pratibanDAt vaSitvasya yEH vaSitvam na laBate tAni eva / vaSItvasya AvaraNAni iti Aha
# dbang-byed-pa #  ni sems kyi dbang la rag lus pa'i phyir / / gang dag gis dbang-byed-pa #  mi-'thob-pa #  de nyid dbang gis sgrib-pa # 'o zhes brjod do /
viBu tvam punar jQAna prahANa praBAva sampanna tA / aTa vA vaSi tva paryAye nirdizwa tva AdyEH vaSi tvam na laBate iti
# dbang-byed-pa #  ni ye shes dang spong-ba #  dang mthu phun-sum-tshogs-pa # 'o / / yang-na #  gang dag gis dbang-byed-pa #  mi-'thob-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni dbang gi rnam-grangs #  su bstan-pa #  ste /
vRdDa tvam na laBate iti arTaH
# sangs-rgyas #  nyid mi 'thob ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
Sruta vyasanam sat Darma SravaNenA atyanta viyogaH
# thos-pa # s phongs-pa #  ni dam-pa'i-chos-nyan-pa #  dang gtan-du #  bral-ba #  ste /
banDuBiH atyanta viyogaH banDu vyasanam / tat punar Sruta vyasanam sat Darma vyasana samAvartanIya karma praBavanAt
# rtsa lag rnams dang gtan-du #  bral-ba #  la rtsa lag gis phongs-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  lta-bu # 'o / / thos-pa # s phongs-pa #  de-yang #  chos-kyis #  phongs-pa # r 'gyur-pa # 'i las skyes-pa # s 'gyur te /
Bavati / sva darSana parAmarSa sTita tvAt akalyANa mitra ASrita tvAt vA yEH
# rang-gi #  lta-ba #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  la gnas-pa # 'i phyir ram / / mi-dge-ba'i-bshes-gnyen #  la brten-pa # 'i phyir /
avipratisArEH mahAyAna sUtrAntaH pratikziptaH mAra BAzitaH ayam
# 'gyod-pa-med-pa #  gang dag gis theg-pa-chen-po # 'i mdos de-la #  / / 'di ni bdud kyis smras-pa #  dang ngan-song-gi-rgyu #  ste /
apAya hetuH ca nA api ambudDa BAzitaH iti anyAn api tasmAt vicCindayanti p / liKitam ca unmRzanti dAhayanti pAvayanti ityAdi prakArEH / sadDarma vyasana samAvartanIya karma utpadyate / sadDarma SravaNa viDura Atma BAva paripuzwitaH / asati Sruta vyasane alpa Sruta tvam jQAna samBArasyA aparipUritA AvaraNam / iti prakRtam / alpa SrutaH he na Saknoti DarmAn pravivektum
# 'di ni sangs-rgyas #  kyis gsungs-pa #  ma yin no zhes spong-ba #  dang gzhan dag kyang de-la #  mos-pa #  bzlog-pa #  dang yi-ge # r bris pa 'phyi ba dang sreg-pa #  dang chur skyur-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  rnams kyis dam-pa'i-chos-nyan-pa #  dang mi-ldan-pa # 'i las kyi sa-bon #  yongs su gsos pas / / dam-pa'i-chos #  kyis phongs-par-'gyur-ba # 'i las rab tu skye'o / / thos-pa # s phongs-pa # r ma gyur-na-yang #  thos-pa #  nyung ste / / ye-shes-kyi-tshogs #  yongs-su-ma-rdzogs-pa # s sgrib po zhes sbyar ro / / thos-pa #  nyung-ba #  ni chos rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa #  mi nus so /
bahu Srutasya api samADeH aparikarm tvac AvaraNam iti sambanDaH
# mang-du-thos-pa # r gyur kyang ting-nge-'dzin #  yongs-su-sbyong-ba #  ma-byas-pa #  nyid kyang sgrib po zhes sbyar ro /
Canda AdInAm anyatamA BAvAt aparipUrNa tvAt / vA azwAnAm prahANa saMskArANAm anyatama aBAvAt samADeH
# 'dun-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  las gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhig med-pa # 'i phyir ram / / spong-ba'i-'du-byed #  brgyad po dag las gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhig med-pa # s / / bsgom-pa #  yongs-su-ma-rdzogs-pa # 'i phyir ting-nge-'dzin #  yongs-su-sbyang-ba #  ma-byas-pa # 'o /
aparikarmita tvam / vajra upama AdInAm vA budDa samADInAm aparinizpanna tvam aparikarmita tvam
# yang-na #  sangs-rgyas #  kyi ting-nge-'dzin #  rdo-rje #  lta-bu #  la-sogs-pa #  yongs su mi sgrub-pa #  ni yongs-su-sbyang-ba #  ma-byas-pa # 'o /
kim atra AvaraNam Darma vyasana samAvartanIya karma alpa Sruta tvam
# 'di-la #  sgrib-pa #  gang zhe na / / chos-kyis #  phongs-par-gyur-pa # 'i las dang thos-pa #  nyung ste /
duzprajQa tA samADi pratyanIkaH ca upakleSaH laya OdDati AdikaH iti / daSa kAraNAni
# 'chal pa'i shes-rab #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang mi-mthun-pa # 'i bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # 'o /
p / tat punar etat AvaraNam aprayoga Adikam
# sgrib-pa #  'di ni zhes-bya-ba #  ni sbyor-ba #  med-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
SuBa AdO vaSi tva paryanta daSaviDe vastuni
# dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / dbang la thug gi bar-du #  dngos-po #  rnam-pa-bcu # 'o /
yatra arTe daSa kAraNAni Bavanti iti utpatti AdO prApti paryante / yasmin= arTe tad AvaraNa viparyayeNa prayoga AdIni
# don gang-la #  byed-rgyu #  rnam-pa-bcu # r 'gyur-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  nas / / 'thob-pa #  la thug gi bar gyi don gang-la #  sgrib-pa #  de bzlog na /
samADi parikarmitatvA avasAnAni daSa kAraNAni Bavanti
# sbyor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  nas ting-nge-'dzin #  yongs-su-sbyang-ba #  byas-pa #  la thug-pa #  rnams ni byed-rgyu #  bcur 'gyur ro /
atra ca utpatti Adi kAraNatvA viSezAt Binnasya api pratyekam api / aBeda nirdeSaH
# 'dir ni so-so #  tha dad kyang skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyu nyid-du #  khyad-par-med-pa # 'i phyir bye-brag-med-par #  bstan to /
tat arTa aDikAreNa iti utpatti Adi arTa ADipatyena iti arTaH tezAm hi / SuBa AdInAm utpatti Adi kAraNa vibanDam vartamAnam utpatti Adi AvaraNam
# don de'i skabs kyis zhes-bya-ba #  ni skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i don gyi dbang-du-byas #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  de-dag #  skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyu la gegs su gyur-pa # 'i tshe na /
ucyate tat yaTA kuXya Adikam Alokam AvRnvat kAryasya cakzuH / vijQAnasya AvaraNam ucyate
# skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  la sgrib po zhes bya ste / / dper-na #  rtsig pa la-sogs-pa # s snang-ba #  bsgribs na / / de'i 'bras-bu #  mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la yang sgrib po zhes-bya-ba #  lta-bu # 'o /
evam kRtvA ezAm daSAnAm DarmANAm triMSat AvaraNa viparyayeNa triMSat
# de-ltar #  byas-na #  chos bcu po de-dag #  gi sgrib-pa #  sum cu po bzlog na byed-rgyu #  sum cu bstan-pa #  yin no /
kAraNam veditavyam / tatra SuBa utpatti kAraNam trINi prayogaH Ayatana prayogaH yoniSas prayogaH / ca / tat yaTA cakzuH AdayaH iti atra eva dRzwAntaH
# de-la #  dge-ba #  skye-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  gsum ni sbyor-ba #  dang skye-mched #  la sbyor-ba #  dang tshul-bzhin #  la sbyor-ba # 'o / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / mig la-sogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dir dpe ste /
cakzuH AdayaH vijQAnasya utpatti kAraNam eva sTiti Adi kAraNam
# mig la-sogs-pa #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  nyid yin gyi / / gnas-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni ma yin no /
tatra aprayoga AdayaH prayoga AdInAm sAkzAt vibanDe vartamAnAH / paramparayA SuBa utpatteH api pratibanDakAH / evam utpatti AvaraNam SuBe drazwavyam iti Aha tasya utpAdanIya tvAt iti / SuBe sTiti Adi asamBavAt utpatti AvaraNam eva etat iti darSayati / sTiti kAraNam boDO
# de-la #  sbyor-ba #  med-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  sbyor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  la mngon du gegs su gyur-pa #  na gcig-nas-gcig-tu #  brgyud de dge-ba #  skye-ba #  la yang gegs-byed-pa # s de-bzhin-du #  skye-ba #  la sgrib-pa #  ni dge-ba #  la sgrib-pa #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  de bskyed-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / dge-ba #  la gnas-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  mi srid-pa # s skye-ba # 'i sgrib-pa #  nyid yin no zhes ston to / / byang-chub #  la ni gnas-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  yod de /
ASraya parAvRttiH boDiH ASrayaH nirmala taTatA
# byang-chub #  ni gnas-gyur-pa # 'o / / de-bzhin-nyid #  dri-ma-med-pa #  ni gnas-pa # 'o /
atra kAraNam Aha akopya tvAt iti
# 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  / / mi-'khrugs-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
yAvat lokaH tAvat avasTAnAt akopya tvam nA anyaTA Bavati vinivartate / vA
# 'jig-rten #  ji-srid-pa #  de srid du gnas-pa # s mi-'khrugs-pa #  ste / / gzhan-du-mi-'gyur-ba #  dang rnam-pa # r mi-ldog-pa # 'o /
SrAvaka AdInAn tu boDiH sva santAnaH eva kRtArTa tvAt vyAvartate
# nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i byang-chub #  ni bdag-gi #  rgyu nyid kyi don byas-na # s rnam-pa # r ldog go /
boDisattvAH hi sarva sattva hita suKa aDyASayena samBArezu pravartamAnA p
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni sems-can-thams-cad #  la phan-pa-dang-bde-ba # r bya-ba # 'i lhag-pa'i-bsam-pa # s tshogs rnams la 'jug-pa #  na /
ASraya parAvRtti lakzaNa tvAt boDeH yAvat sattvAH tAvat avatizWanti iti
# gnas-par-gyur-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  byang-chub-sems #  ji-srid-pa #  de srid du gnas-pa # r smon te /
ucyate na tu anutpatti mAtra tvAt SrAvaka Adi vat / utpattim vinA BAvita tvAt tu sTiteH utpattiH api atra Bavati
# nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  ltar mi-skye-ba #  tsam gyi phyir ni ma yin no / / gnas-pa #  ni skye-ba #  med-par-mi-'gyur-ba # s 'dir yang skye-ba #  yod-pa # r 'gyur ro /
tasmAt boDi sTiti kAraNam eva ucyate na utpatti kAraNam / na ca anya anyat tat vyatirekeNa sTiti kAraNam asti iti atas etat eva uktam / viSudDa taTatA vA boDiH
# de-bas-na #  byang-chub #  kyi gnas-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  nyid brjod kyi skye-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni ma yin no / / de ma-gtogs-par #  gzhan gnas-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  med-pa # s de'i-phyir #  de nyid bshad do / / yang-na #  de-bzhin-nyid #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  ni byang-chub #  ste /
na taTA tAyAH svaBAvavuSudDa tvAt utpattiH asti
# de-bzhin-nyid #  ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  rnam-par-dag-pa # s skye-ba #  med de /
kintarhi Agantuka amlA apagamAt anyantam eBiH kAraNEH sTitiH eva ucyate / na utpattiH
# glo-bur-gyi-dri-ma #  med-pa # r gyur na byed-rgyu #  de-dag #  gis gtan-du #  gnas-pa-nyid #  ces brjod kyi skye-ba #  ni ma yin no /
sTiti kAraNAni punar boDeH kuSala utpAdaH manasikAraH paripUrNa samBAraH / ca / atra ca SuBAn utpatti AdayaH kuSala utpatya Adi vibanDe vartamAnAH boDeH / sTitim kurvanti iti sTiti AvaraNam uktAH
# byang-chub #  kyi gnas-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba skye-ba #  dang yid-la-byed-pa #  dang tshogs yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # 'o / / 'dir yang dge-ba #  la mi-skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni / / dge-ba #  skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gegs su gyur-pa # s byang-chub #  kyi gnas-pa #  la gnod-pa-byed-pa # 'i phyir gnas-pa # 'i sgrib-pa #  zhes bshad do /
tat yaTA catvAraH AhArAH sattvAnAm iti atra eva nidarSanam
# gnas-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni dper-na #  sems-can #  rnams kyi zas gzhi lta-bu # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / 'dir dpe'o /
na hi kavaXa AkAra AdiBiH AhArEH apUrvAH sattvAH utpadyante / purA utpannAH tu vyavasTApyante eva
# kham gyis za-ba # 'i zas la-sogs-pa #  ldan med-pa # 'i sems-can #  skyed-par-byed-pa #  ni ma yin gyi / / sngar skyes-pa #  rnams gnas-par-byed-pa #  nyid do /
DRti kAraNam iti / DRtiH boDi cittam sarva kuSala Darma ADAra BUta tvAt / atra eva nidarSanam yat yasya ADAra BUtan tatra tasya DRtiH / DAryate anena iti kRtvA / tat yaTA BAjana lokaH sattva lokasya iti
# rten-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  zhes-bya-ba #  la rten ni byang-chub #  kyi sems te / / dge-ba'i-chos #  thams-cad-kyi #  gzhir-gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gang-gi #  gnas su gang gyur-pa #  de ni de'i rten te / / 'dis 'dzin-pa # s dper-na #  sems-can-gyi-'jig-rten #  gyi snod-kyi-'jig-rten #  lta-bu # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dir dpe'o /
tat kAraNam gotram kalyANa mitra sampanna tA cittA pariKedatA ca
# de'i byed-rgyu #  ni rigs dang bshes-gnyen #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  dang sems yongs-su-mi-skyo-ba # 'o /
tatra DRti kAraNa virudDa tvAt gotra vEDurya Adi kanDRteH api AvaraNam / uktam
# de-la #  rigs-dang-mi-ldan-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ni rten-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  dang 'gal-ba # s rten la yang sgrib-pa # r bshad do /
etat eva Aha DRti AvaraNam samAdAnaH AvaraNam

# gsal-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni blo ldan byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i sgrib-pa #  ste / / rab-tu-bstan-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir ro /
tat ca pratipatti sampad su jana vAsaH duzwa janA vAsaH ca
# de-yang #  sgrub-pa #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  dang skye-bo #  rung-ba #  dang 'grogs-pa #  dang skye-bo #  gnod-pa # r mi sems-pa #  dang 'grogs-pa # 'o /
atra DImattve pratipatti vEDuryAt ayaH aBivyakti AvaraNa tvena ucyante
# 'dir sgrub-pa #  dang mi-ldan-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ni blo ldan gsal-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  dang 'gal-ba # s gsal-ba # 'i sgrib-pa #  zhes bya ste /

tat yaTA AlokaH rUpasya iti atra eva nidarSanam
# dper-na #  gzugs kyi snang-ba #  lta-bu # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dir dpe'o /

# snang-ba #  ni gzugs 'ba'-zhig #  gsal-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  nyid yin te / / skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni ma yin no / / 'gyur-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni 'khrul-ba #  med-pa # 'i rgyu ste /

# sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-pa #  'khul pa ldog-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin-pas #  'khrul-pa-med-pa #  ni mthong-ba'i-lam #  mo / / 'khrul-pa-med-pa # 'i 'gyur-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ste /
tat yaTA Basma AdayaH kAzWa AdInAm / tasya trINi kAraNAni viparyAsa dOzWulya upaGAtaH / kleSa Adi AvaraNAnAm trayANAm aBAvaH p / vimukti paripAcinyAH prajQAyAH paripakva BAvaH / tat yaTA agni AdayaH pAki AdInAm iti
# dper-na #  shing sha ba la-sogs-pa # 'i thal-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o / / de'i byed-rgyu #  gsum ni phyin-ci-log #  gi gnas-ngan-len #  bcom ba dang nyon-mongs-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sgrib-pa #  gsum med-pa #  dang rnam-par-grol-ba #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-pa # 'i shes-rab #  yongs-su-smin-pa # 'o /
pAkyaH hi odana AdikaH taNXula Adi vilakzaNaH tat santAna antarBUtaH / tat kAraNam ca agni Adi
# dper-na #  btso ba la-sogs-pa # 'i me la-sogs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'bras-chan #  la-sogs-pa #  dang mi-'dra-ba #  ste / / de'i rgyud du gtogs-pa # 'o / / 'bras la-sogs-pa # r 'gyur ro zhes-bya-ba #  de'i byed-rgyu #  ni me la-sogs-pa # 'o /
viSleza kAraNam anAvaraNe
# 'bral-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni sgrib-pa-med-pa # 'i rgyu ste /
darSana mArga praheyAt AvaraNAt Sezam AvaraNam anena prahIyata / iti anAvaraNam BAvanA mArgaH / tasya trINi kAraNAni sahaja dOzWulya upaGAtaH vIryam apramAdaH ca
# mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyis spangs bar bya-ba # 'i sgrib-pa #  las lhag-ma #  dag 'dis spong-ba # s sgrib-pa-med-pa #  ni bsgom-pa'i-lam #  mo / / de'i byed-rgyu #  gsum ni lhan-cig-skyes-pa # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  bcom-pa #  dang brtson 'grus dang-ba # g yod-pa # 'o /
tezAm aQca viSleza kAraNa pratipakza tvAt

# ci'i-phyir #  zhe na bsngo-ba #  ni byang-chub-chen-po # r sems yongs-su-bsngo-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyi phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / yid-ches-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni mi-skrag-pa # 'i rgyu ste /
tat ca pudgala samBAvanA DarmA aDimuktiH ABiprAyika arTA aDigamaH ca
# de-yang #  gang-zag #  la srid do snyam pa dang chos la mos-pa #  dang dgongs-pa'i-don #  khong-du-chud-pa # 'o /

# chos de rnams kyi yid-ches-pa # r 'gyur-ba # s de'i-phyir #  yid-ches-pa # 'i byed-rgyu # 'i gegs yin-pas #  yid-ches-pa #  la sgrib-pa #  ni mi-skrag-pa #  la sgrib ste / / 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  / / yid-mi-ches-pa # s skrag-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya'o #  /
asampratyayena hi Darmasya trasyati / sampratyAyana karaNam amatsaritve

atra eva kAraNam Aha DarmA matsari tvena para sampyAyanAt iti

# dam-pa'i-chos #  ched cher mi-'dzin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s chos la ser-sna-byed-pa # r 'gyur ro / / chos la ser-sna-byed-pa # s kyang gzhan rnams la chos-'chad-pa # r mi-byed-pa # s de'i-phyir #  / / yid-ches-pa # r byed-pa #  la sgrib-pa # s ni ser-sna #  med-pa #  la sgrib-pa # 'o /
vaSitvasya trINi kAraNAni Darma vyasana saMvartanIya karmA aBAvaH / bahu Sruta tvam samADi parikarmita tvaQca
# 'thob-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  gsum ni chos-kyis #  phongs-par-'gyur-ba # 'i las med-pa #  dang mang-du-thos-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  yongs-su-sbyong-ba # r byas-pa # 'o /
tad virudDa tvAt cu tavya sana Adikam vaSitva AvaraNam vyavasTApyate / atra eva kAraNam Aha tasya vaSitvasya viBu tva prApti lakzaNa tvAt iti
# de dang 'gal-ba # s thos-pa # s phongs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ni dbang gi sgrib-pa # r rnam-pa # r gzhag ste / / 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  / / dbang de-la #  dbang-byed-pa #  'thob-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyi phyir ro zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
kecid tu SuBa AdInAm evam anukrame kAraNam AhuH
# kha-cig #  na re dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i go-rims #  kyi rgyu ni 'di-lta-bu #  ste /
kuSala Darma upavazwabDa satatiH boDiH prAptavyA
# dge-ba'i-chos #  kyi sems-kyi-rgyud #  nye-bar #  bstan-pa # s byang-chub #  'thob-pa # 'i skal-ba #  yod de /
tatas Aditas SuBam uktam
# de'i-phyir #  thog-mar #  dge-ba #  bshad do /
tat anantaram boDiH uktA
# de'i-'og-tu #  byang-chub #  bshad do /
boDi citta paQcAgamya etat uBaya sampAdane samarTaH Bavati A boDeH / boDi cittasya sarva kuSala Darma ADAra BUta tvAt atas tat anantaram / boDicittam uktam
# byang-chub #  kyi sems ni chos dge-ba'i-chos #  thams-cad-kyi #  gzhir-gyur-pa # s byang-chub #  kyi sems la brten-nas #  / / byang-chub #  la thug gi bar-du #  de-gnyi-ga #  sgrub nus-pa # r 'gyur te / / de'i-phyir #  de'i-'og-tu #  byang-chub #  kyi sems bshad do /
utpAdita boDi cittasya zaz pAramitAsu prayogaH kujana duzwa janAByAm ca / parihAraH
# byang-chub #  kyi sems bskyed nas pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  drug la rab tu sbyor-ba #  dang skye-bo #  ngan-pa #  dang skye-bo #  sdang-ba #  yongs su spong ste /
evam asya boDisattva BAvaH prakASIBavati p
# de-ltar #  'di'i byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i dngos-po #  bstan-pa #  yin no /
atas samAdAna anantaram DImatvam uktam
# de'i-phyir #  yang-dag-par-'dzin-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  blo-dang-ldan-pa #  bshad do /
eva Qca prayujyamAnaH viparyAsam prajahAti aviparyastam ca jQAnam / utpAdayati / atas DImatvAn antaram aBrAntiH uktA sa punar darSana mArgaH / tat aByasanena AvaraNam vijahAti iti atas tat anantaram AvaraNa prahANam / anAvaraNam uktam
# de-ltar #  rab tu sbyor-ba #  na phyin-ci-log #  spong zhing phyin-ci-log #  med-pa # 'i ye shes kyang skyed-pa # r byed de / / de'i-phyir #  blo ldan gyi 'og-tu #  'khrul-pa-med-pa #  bshad do / / de ni mthong-ba'i-lam #  ste / / de-la #  goms-pa # s sgrib-pa #  rnams spong-ba # s de'i-phyir #  / / de'i-'og-tu #  sgrib-pa-spong-ba # 'i sgrib-pa-med-pa #  bshad do /
nirAvaraNasya Bava Boga sakti aBavAt budDa tve eva mAnasam pariNAmayati / na anyatra iti / atas tat anantaram na tiruktA
# sgrib-pa #  med na srid-pa #  dang longs-spyod #  la chags-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir / / sangs-rgyas #  nyid-du #  yid kyis yongs su sngo-ba # r byed kyi gzhan-du #  ma yin no / / de'i-phyir #  de'i-'og-tu #  bsngo-ba #  bshad do /
evam BUtasya ca sugamBIrezu api budDa Darmezu prAmodya utpatIra trAsa / iti atas tat anantaram atra AsaH uktaH / evam Darma pratyakzeNa yena yena upAyena sattva vinayam paSyati / tat tam eva upAya mBa jata iti tasya kutas mAtsaryam Bavet iti atra asAntaram / amAtsaryam uktam
# de-lta-bu # r ni sangs-rgyas-kyi-chos #  shin-tu #  zab-mo #  rnams la mchog-tu-dga'-ba #  skye ste / / mi-skrag-pa # s de'i-phyir #  de'i-'og-tu #  mi-skrag-pa #  bshad do / / de-ltar #  chos mngon-sum-du-gyur-pa #  thabs gang-dang-gang-gis #  sems-can #  'dul-ba # r mthong-ba # 'i thabs de-dang-de #  la brten-pa # s / / de-la #  ser-sna #  'byung-ba # r ga la 'gyur-ba # s / / mi-skrag-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  ser-sna #  med-pa #  bshad do /
evam prahINa AvaraNaH paripUrNa Sukla DarmA ca boDisattvaH citta vaSi tve / pravartate iti atas tat anantaram vaSitvam uktam / ezaH anukramaH iti
# de-ltar #  sgrib-pa #  spangs-pa #  dang dkar-po'i-chos #  rnams yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # 'i byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni sems-la-dbang #  bar 'gyur-ba # s de'i-phyir #  de'i-'og-tu #  dbang bshad de / / go-rims #  ni 'di'o zhe'o /
asmin paricCede AvaraNa prasaFge iti atas SuBa AdInAm utpatIkAraNAni
# le'ur bcad-pa #  'dir sgrib-pa # 'i skabs yin-pas #  de'i-phyir #  dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i skye-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  rnams ni /
AvaraNa vat sUtritAni / prasaFga AgatAnAm antara Slokena saFgrahaH kriyate
# sgrib-pa #  bzhin-du #  mdor mdzad-pa # s skabs nas 'byung-ba #  rnams par gyi tshigs-su-bcad-pa # s sdud-pa # r mdzad do /
kAraNam daSaDA utpattO sTitO DRtyAm prakASane
# byed-rgyu #  bcu ni skye-ba #  dang / / gnas-pa #  brten dang bstan bya dang /
vikAra viSlezaNa tipratyaya prAyaNa Aptizu
# 'gyur dang 'bral dang gzhan-du #  dang / / yid ches go byed 'thob rnams la /
eza dvitIyaH antara SlokaH udAharaNa saFgraha arTam
# de ni dper brjod bsdu-ba # 'i phyir / / bar gyi tshigs bcad gnyis-pa #  ste /
cakzuH AhAra BU dIpa vahni AdiH tat udAhRtiH
# mig dang zas sam mar-me #  dang / / me la-sogs-pa #  de yi dpe /
dAtra Silpa jQa tA DUma hetu mArga AdayaH apare / iti p / boDi pakzya pAramitA BUmizu AvaraNAni
# zor ba bzo shes du-ba #  dang / / rgyu dang lam la-sogs-pa #  gzhan / / zhes-bya-ba # 'o / / phyogs dang pha rol phyin sa la / / sgrib-pa #  dag ni gzhan yin no /
pUrvam hi aviSezeNa SuBam nirdizwam tadA AvaraNaQca
# sngar ni dge-ba #  dang de'i sgrib-pa #  bye-brag #  tu ma phye-ba # r bshad do /
idAnIntu pakzyA ityAdi Bedena sADAraNA sADAraNa Bedena ca SuBam / nirdiSati
# da-ni #  phyogs dang zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bye-brag #  dang thun mong dang thun-mong-ma-yin-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis ni dge-ba #  bshad do /
vastu akOSala kOsIdyam
# gzhi la mi-mkhas #  le-lo #  dang /
ityAdi Bedena ca pakza AdInAm AvaraNam / tatra sADAraNam boDi pakzAH SrAvaka boDisattvayoH aviSezeNa / tatra akArAt avikArAt
# zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis ni phyogs la-sogs-pa # 'i dge-ba #  la sgrib-pa #  bshad do / / der gtogs-pa # s nyan-thos #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  gnyi-ga # 'i bya-ba #  bye-brag-med-pa # 'i phyir / / de-la #  byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  ni thun-mong-ba # 'o /
asADAraNantu pAramitA BUmayaH boDisattvAnAm karaNam boDisattvAnAm
# pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  dang sa rnams ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi bya-ba #  thun-mong-ma-yin-pa #  ste /
eva tad ADipatyAt / pUrvaQca SuBa Adi hetu AvaraNa dvAreNa Pala AvaraNam uktam iha tu sAkzAt
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams nyid de-la #  lhag-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / sngar ni dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyu la sgrib-pa # 'i sgo nas 'bras-bu #  la sgrib-pa # r bshad do /
Pala AvaraNam eva iti pUrvasmAt anyat ucyate
# 'dir ni 'bras-bu #  la dngos su sgrib-pa #  nyid de / / de-bas-na #  snga-ma #  las gzhan zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
aTa vA aprayoga AdiByaH vastu akOSala Adikam anyat eva iti tat anyat ucyate
# yang-na #  sbyor-ba #  med-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  las gzhi la mi-mkhas-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  gzhan nyid de / / de gzhan zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
aTavA SuBam boDiH ca iti atra boDisattvasya eva upAya sahitayoH caryA PalayoH / aprayoga Adikam AvaraNam uktam iha tu SuBasya eva / sADAraNasyA asADAraNasya ca boDi pakza Adi viBAgena
# yang-na #  dge-ba #  dang byang-chub #  ces bya-ba #  ni / / 'dir byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  nyid kyi thabs-dang-bcas-pa # 'i spyod-pa #  dang 'bras-bu #  la sbyor-ba #  med-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  sgrib po zhes bshad do / / 'dir ni byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-par-'byed-pa # s /
vastu akOSala Adikam aprayoga AdikAt anyat AvaraNam veditavyam / tatra SrAvaka Adi Bedena boDitrayam tad anurUpeNa smRti upasTAna AdayaH / mArga paryantAH boDi pakzAH iti ucyate daSa pAramitAH daSa ca BUmayaH / yaTA sUtram
# gzhi la mi-mkhas-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ni / / sbyor-ba #  med-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  las / / dge-ba #  thun mong dang thun-mong-ma-yin-pa # 'i sgrib-pa #  gzhan-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / de-la #  nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  tha-dad-pa # s byang-chub #  gsum ste / / de-dag #  dang mthun-pa # s dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  nas lam la thug gi bar dag ni byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  rnams zhes-bya'o #  / / pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bcu dang sa bcu rnams ni mdo las ji-skad-'byung-ba #  bzhin no /
smRti upasTAnezu vastu akOSalam AvaraNam iti / tAni punar p
# gzhi la mi-mkhas-pa #  ni dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  rnams la sgrib po zhes-bya-ba #  la /
kAya vedanA citta Darma smRti upasTAnAni catvAri
# de-dag #  ni lus dang tshor-ba #  dang sems dang chos dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  dang bzhi'o /
tezAm punar vastu kAya vedanA citta DarmAH tat vizaya tvAt / tatra ASrayam aBiniveSa vastu kAyaH
# de-dag #  gi gzhi ni lus dang tshor-ba #  dang sems dang chos-rnams #  te / / de'i yul yin pa'i phyir ro / / de-la #  gnas su mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i gzhi ni lus so /
Atma pariBoga aBiniveSavaH tu vedanA
# bdag-gi #  longs-spyod #  du mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i gzhi ni tshor-ba # 'o /
Atma aBiniveSavaH tu cittam
# bdag tu mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i gzhi ni sems so /
Atma saFkleSa vyavadAna aBiniveSavaH tu DarmaH iti
# bdag kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # r mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i gzhi ni chos-rnams #  so /
kAya Adizu yaH sva sAmAnya lakzaNA avaboDaH sa tatra akza kOSalam
# lus la-sogs-pa # 'i rang-dang-spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  khong du-ma #  chud-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni de-la #  mi-mkhas-pa # 'o /
tatra sva lakzaNam aneka aSuci dravyeNa saFgRhIta Atmaka tvam kAyasya
# de-la #  lus kyi rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  ni mi gtsang ba du-ma # 'i rdzas 'dus-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  do /
suKa Adi svaBAvaH vedanAyAH / vizaya prativijQaptiH vijQAnasya
# tshor-ba # 'i ni bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  no / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni yul las so-so # r rnam-par-rig-pa # 'o /
DarmANAm yaTAsamBavam
# chos-rnams #  kyi ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
sAmAnya lakzanam punar nitya duKa SUnya
# spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  ni mi-rtag-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  dang stong-pa #  dang bdag-med-pa'i-rnam-pa # 'o /
aTavA kAya Adizu aSuci duHKa hA anityA Atma AkAreNa pratipattiH
# yang-na #  lus la-sogs-pa #  la mi gtsang ba dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  dang mi-rtag-pa #  dang bdag-med-pa'i-rnam-pa # r ma rtog-pa # 'am /
Suci suKa nitya Atma AkAreNa vA vikalpaH vastu akOSalam yasmAt ajQAnam
# gtsang ba dag bde-ba #  dang rtag-pa #  dag / / bdag-gi #  rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni gzhi la mi-mkhas-pa #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  mi-shes-pa # 'am /
darSaNam vA smRti upasTAnezu AvaraNam / prajQAsmRti svABAvye sati smRti upasTAnAnAm kasmAt vastu akOSalam
# lta-ba #  ni dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  rnams la sgrib-pa # 'o / / dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  rnams ni shes-rab #  dang dran-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  yin na /
eva AvaraNam ucyate na tu vastu asmaraNam api iti
# ci'i-phyir #  gzhi la mi-mkhas-pa #  ni sgrib-pa #  zhes brjod kyi / / gzhi mi dran-pa #  ni ma yin zhe na /
prajQA aDIna pravRtti tvAt / taTA hi darSana Atmaka tvAt prajQAyAH prajQA pRzWa labDaH Alambane
# shes-rab #  kyi kha na las te 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / 'di-ltar #  shes-rab #  ni mthong-ba # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  phyir te /
smRti AdayaH pravartante na tu svAtantryeNa prajQA vat / tasmAt nA asmaraNam atra AvaraNam uktam iti / sampyak prahANezu kOzIidyam / kim / AvaraNam iti prakRtam
# shes-rab #  kyi rjes-las-thob-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  la dran-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rab tu 'jug gi / / shes-rab #  bzhin-du #  rang-gi-rgyud #  yod-pa #  ni ma yin te / / de'i-phyir #  mi dran-pa #  ni sgrib-pa #  zhes mi bshad do / / le-lo #  ni yang-dag-par-spong-ba #  rnams la sgrib bo /
vIryam hi atra utpannA anutpanna vipakza prahANA anutpAtaye / utpanna pratipakzasya BUyas BAva utpAdAya ca pravartamAnam / samyak prahANa AKyAm pratilaBate / tat punar Beda aBAve api Pala BedAt caturDA vyavasTApyate iti smRtiH / atas samyak prahANAnAm vIrya Atmaka tvAt Alasyam AvaraNam uktam / RdDi pAdezu samADeH dvaya hIna tA AvaraNam iti / anenadDaryataH iti RdDiH
# brtson 'grus kyi mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  skyes-pa #  dang ma-skyes-pa #  spong-ba #  dang mi-skyed-pa #  dang gnyen-po #  skyes-pa #  dang ma-skyes-pa #  phyir-zhing-'byung-ba #  dang skyed-pa # 'i phyir 'jug-pa #  ni yang-dag-par-spong-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i ming 'thob bo / / de ni dbyer med kyang 'bras-bu #  tha-dad-pa # 'i phyir rnam-pa-bzhi # r gzhag go / / de-bas-na #  yang-dag-par-spong-ba #  rnams brtson 'grus kyi bdag-nyid #  yin-pas #  le-lo #  ni sgrib-pa # r bshad do / / gnyis kyis ting-nge-'dzin #  nyams-pa #  dang zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  rnams la sgrib po / / 'dis rdzu-'phrul #  byed-pa # s rdzu-'phrul #  te /
sA ca cCanda vIrya cittam imAm asAsamADiH
# de-yang #  'dun-pa #  dang brtson 'grus dang sems dang dpyod-pa'i-ting-nge-'dzin #  to /
sA eva RdDi pAdaH AkASa gamana nirmANa Adi kAyAH RdDeH pratizWA BUta tvAt
# de nyid rdzu-'phrul #  gyi rkang ba ste / / nam-mkha' #  la 'gro-ba #  dang sprul pa la-sogs-pa #  rdzu-'phrul #  gyi gnas su gyur ba'i phyir ro /
gamanam vA RdDiH AkASa gamana AdikA samRdDiH iti arTaH
# yang-na #  'gro-ba # s rdzu-'phrul #  te / / nam-mkha' #  la 'gro-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  'byor-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
tasyAH pAdAH RdDi pAdAH tad ADAra tvAt
# de'i rkang-pa #  ni rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  ste / / de'i gzhi-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sA eva cCanda samADi Adi caturviDA samADiH
# 'dun-pa'i-ting-nge-'dzin #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-pa-bzhi-po #  de nyid ni ting-nge-'dzin #  to /
tatra= Canda samADO Canda prADAnyam tat dvAreNa samADi lABAt
# de-la #  'dun-pa'i-ting-nge-'dzin #  la 'dun-pa #  gtso bo ste / / de'i sgo nas ting-nge-'dzin #  'thob-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na tu vIrya AdayaH tatra na santi Canda sahAya tvAt apraDAnAH tu te
# brtson 'grus la-sogs-pa #  yang de na med-pa #  ni ma yin te / / 'dun-pa # 'i grogs-byed-pa # 'i phyir /
tatra iti na te prakASitAH
# de-dag #  ni der gtso bo ma-yin-pa # s de-dag #  mi bshad do /
evam vIrya citta mImAMsA samADizu vAcyam
# de-bzhin-du #  brtson 'grus dang sems dang dpyod-pa'i-ting-nge-'dzin #  rnams kyang brjod-pa # r bya'o /
samADeH dvaya hIna tAvaraNam uktam
# gnyis kyis ting-nge-'dzin #  nyams-pa #  sgrib-pa # r bshad-pa #  de mi shes te /
na tat jQAyate atas Aha aparipUryA ca cCanda vIrya cittam imAnAm / anyatama vEkalyAt BAvanayA ca prahANa saMskAra vEkalyAt iti
# de'i-phyir #  'dun-pa #  dang brtson 'grus dang sems dang dpyod-pa #  rnams las gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhig ma-tshang-ba #  yongs-su-ma-rdzogs-pa #  dang spong-ba'i-'du-byed #  bsgom-pa #  ma-tshang-ba # s zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tatra paripUrihIna tA tAsAm CandavIrya citta mImAMsAnAm / anyatama vEkalyAt tad ADipatyasya samADeH aBAvAt BAvanA hIyata
# de-la #  'dun-pa #  dang brtson 'grus dang sems dang dpyod-pa #  de-dag #  las gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhig ma-tshang-ba # s yongs su bskal-pa #  nyams te / / de'i dbang gis ting-nge-'dzin #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
iti azwa prahANa saMskArANAm anyatama vEkalyam
# sgom-pa #  nyams-pa #  ni spong-ba'i-'du-byed #  brgyad po dag las ma-tshang-ba # 'i phyir ro /
te punar SradDAt CandavIrya praSrabDi smRti samprajanya cetanA upekzA AtmakAH
# de-dag #  ni dad-pa #  dang 'dun-pa #  dang brtson 'grus dang shin-tu-sbyangs-pa #  dang dran-pa #  dang shes-bzhin #  dang sems-pa #  dang btang-snyoms #  kyi bdag-nyid #  do /
ezAm hi prahANa saMskArANAm BAvanayA samADO vaSitvam avApyate
# spong-ba'i-'du-byed #  'di dag bsgoms na ting-nge-'dzin-la-dbang #  thob ste /
na anyaTA iti atas ezAm vEkalyAt BAvanA hIna tA iti na samADO vaSitvam / avApyate
# gzhan-du #  ma yin no / / de-bas-na #  de-dag #  ma tshang na sgom-pa #  nyams-pa #  zhes bya ste / / ting-nge-'dzin-la-dbang #  mi thob bo /
kim atra AvaraNam
# 'di-la #  sgrib-pa #  gang zhe na /
Canda Adi pratipakzANAm prahANa saMskArANAn ca vipakza upakleSaH yat uta
# 'dun-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang spong-ba'i-'du-byed #  kyi mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # 'o /
kOsIdyatm Alambana sampramozaH laya Oddatye asaMkAraH saMskAraH ca iti
# 'di-lta-ste #  / / le-lo #  dang dmigs-pa #  brjed-pa #  dang bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  dang 'du mi-byed-pa #  dang 'du-byed #  pa'o /
indriyezu mokza BAgIyAnAm aropaNam iti / saMsArAt uttrastaH mokzam aDikRtya p
# thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  rnams mi-skyed-pa #  ni dbang-po #  rnams la sgrib po zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'khor-ba # s skrag ste /
kuSala mUlam aBisaMskaroti tena mokza lABa niScayAt mokza BAgIyam ucyate / tasmin ca Aropite SradDA AdayaH indriya AKyAm pratilaBante na anyaTA iti atas
# thar-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-nas #  dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba gang mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  des thar-pa #  rnyed-pa # r nges-pa # s / / thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / de bskyed na dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dbang-po # 'i ming 'thob-pa # r 'gyur te /
mokza BAgIyAnAm aropaNam indriyezu AvaraNam uktam
# gzhan-du #  ma-yin-pa # s thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  mi-skyed-pa #  ni dbang-po #  rnams la sgrib-pa # r bshad do /
kim atra AvaraNam
# de-la #  sgrib-pa #  gang zhe na /
yena upakleSena mokza BAgIyam na rocyate
# nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  gang-gis #  thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  mi-skyed-pa #  ste /
sA punar Bava saktiH nirvANa BItiH ca / balezu tezAm eva indriyANAn dOrbalayam
# de ni yang-srid-pa #  la chags-pa #  dang mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # s 'jigs-pa # 'o / / dbang-po #  de-dag #  gi nyam-chung-ba #  ni stobs rnams la sgrib po /
AvaraNam iti prakRtam / kaTam punar indriyANAn dOrbalyam iti atas Aha vipakza vyavakiraNAt iti
# dbang-po #  rnams kyi nyam-chung-ba #  ji-lta-bu #  zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang 'dre-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
ASraddya kOsIdyam uzita smRti vikzepa duzprajQA Atmakena / vipakzeNa aBiBUta tvAt iti arTaH / indriyANi hi uzma gata mUrDAnAByAm praBAvitAni
# mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  ma-dad-pa #  dang le-lo #  dang brjed-ngas-pa #  dang g-yeng ba dang 'chal-ba'i-shes-rab #  kyi bdag-nyid-kyis #  zil gyis mi gnon zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / do par gyur-pa #  dang rtse mos rab-tu-phye-ba #  dag ni dbang-po #  rnams so /
etat ca dviviDam api nirveDa BAgIyAn durbalam / aSradDi Adi vipakza aBiBavAt / atas eva tasmAt parihANisamBavaH
# nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  po 'di ni mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  ma-dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s zil-gyis-non-pa # 'i phyir nyam-chung-ba #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  'di-las #  yongs-su-nyams-pa #  srid do /
nirjita vipakza tvAt tu SradDA AdIni kzAnti agra Darma avasTAyAm / balA AKyAmpratilaBante
# mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  thul bas bzod-pa #  dang 'jig-rten-pa # 'i chos kyi mchog gi dus na dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  stobs kyis ming 'thob po /
tasmAt yat tezAm eva SradDA AdInAm uzma gata mUrDAna avasTAyAm / vipakzA aBiBavAt dOrbalyantat balAnAm AvaraNam / tasmin sati balA avasTA avasTA asamBavAt iti
# de'i-phyir #  dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  de-dag-nyid #  dro-bar-gyur-pa #  dang rtse mo'i dus na mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyis zil gyis non nas nyam-chung-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni stobs rnams la sgrib ste / / de yod-na #  stobs kyi bye-brag #  mi srid do /
kim atra AvaraNam
# 'di-la #  sgrib-pa #  gang zhe na /
saH eva aSradDi AdikaH vipakzaH
# ma-dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  de nyid do /
boDi aFgezu dRzwi dozaH / AvaraNam iti prakRtam / boDiH hi atra darSana mArgaH aBipretaH / tasyAH tAni
# lta-ba # 'i nyes-pa #  ni byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  rnams la sgrib po / / byang-chub #  ni 'dir mthong-ba'i-lam #  la dgongs-pa #  ste /
smRti Darma pravicaya vIrya prIti apraSrabDi samADi upekza AtmakAni / sapta boDyaFgAni darSana heya kleSa prahANa kAle utpadyante iti aFgAni iti
# de'i dran-pa #  dang chos-rnam-par-'byed-pa #  dang brtson 'grus dang dga'-ba #  dang shin du sbyangs-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang btang-snyoms #  kyi bdag-nyid #  byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  bdun po de-dag #  ni mthong-ba # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa-spong-ba # 'i dus na 'byung-ba # s yan-lag #  rnams zhes-bya'o #  /
ucyate / yadi tu boDeH anukUla tvAt aFgAni syuH evam smRti upasTAna AdInAm api / boDyaFgatvam prasajyeta / kaTam idam boDi aFgezu dRzwi dozaH AvaraNam iti atas Aha tezAm
# gal-te #  byang-chub-dang-mthun-pa # s yan-lag #  tu 'gyur ro zhe na / / de lta na ni dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  rnams kyang byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  nyid-du #  thal-ba # r 'gyur ro / / lta-ba # 'i nyes-pa #  ni byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  rnams la sgrib po zhes-bya-ba #  de ji lta zhe na /
darSana mArga praBAvita tvAt iti darSana mArga vyavasTApita tvAt iti / arTaH
# de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyis rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / mthong-ba'i-lam #  du rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
kaH punar anya dRzwi dozaH
# lta-ba # 'i nyes-pa #  'di gang zhe na /
parikalpitAH paQca dRzwayaH vicikitsA avidayA tad AlambanAzu ca rAga AdayaH / sa samprayogAH kleza upaklezAH / nanu vicikitsA dayA upya attrA AvaraNam / AvaraNamBavatu
# kun-brtags-pa # 'i lta-ba #  rnam-pa-lnga #  dang the-tshom #  dang ma-rig-pa #  dang de-la #  dmigs-pa # 'i 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  rnams so / / the-tshom #  la-sogs-pa #  yang 'dir sgrib-pa #  ma yin nam zhe na /
iha tu praDAna vivakzayA dRzwi doza upadeSaH iti na tezAm anupadeSaH / viruDyate
# sgrib-pa #  yin-du-zin #  kyang 'dir gtso bor brjod-pa # r bzhed-pa # s lta-ba # 'i skyon smos-pa # 'i phyir de-dag #  ma smos kyang 'gal-ba #  med do /
tezAm aQca dRzwi AdInAm AlayavijQAna sannivizwam bIjam eva / darSana mArga praheya tvAt tat AvaraNam ucyate
# lta-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  de rnams kyi sa-bon #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la gnas-pa-nyid #  mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyis spong-ba # 'i phyir de'i sgrib-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
mArga aFgezu samyak / dRzwi saMkalpa karmAnta AjIva vyAyAma smRti samADi AKyezu dOzWulya doza / AvaraNam iti prastutam
# gnas-ngan-len #  gyi nyes-pa #  ni lam gyi yan-lag #  yang-dag-par-lta-ba #  dang rtog-pa #  dang ngag dang las-kyi-mtha' #  dang 'tsho-ba #  dang; rtsol ba dang dran-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  rnams la sgrib ste /
atra eva kAraNam Aha tezAm mArga aFgAnAm / BAvanA mArga praBAvita tvAt iti BAvanA mArga vyavasTApita tvAt
# 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  / / lam gyi yan-lag #  de-dag #  bsgom-pa'i-lam #  gyis rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ste / / bsgom-pa'i-lam #  la rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kaH sa dOzWulya dozaH
# gnas-ngan-len #  gyi nyes-pa #  de gang zhe na /
vyAsataH satkAya anta grAha dRzwI sahaje sa samprayoge tadA AlambanA / vizaya AlambanAH ca rAga AdayaH kleSa upakleSAH sa samprayogAH
# rgyas-pa # r bya-ba #  na ni 'jig-tshogs #  dang mthar 'dzin-pa # 'i lta-ba #  lhan-cig-skyes-pa #  mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  dang de-la #  yang dmigs-pa #  yul la yang dmigs-pa #  'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  rnams te /
tezAm AlayavijQAna sannivizwam yat bIjantat dOzWulyam
# de-dag #  gi sa-bon #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la gnas-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni gnas-ngan-len #  to /
saFkzepataH tu darSana prahAtavyAt anyA sa AsravA tad SaktiH
# mdor-bsdu-na #  mthong-ba # s spang-bar-bya-ba #  las gzhan-pa #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  ste /
AlayavijQAna sannivizwA dOzWulyam
# de'i nus-pa #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la gnas-pa #  ni gnas-ngan-len #  to /
tat ca BAvanA mArga praheya tvAt mArga aFgezu AvaraNa tvena / vyavasTApyate / uktam boDi pakzezu AvaraNam p
# de ni bsgom-pa'i-lam #  gyis spang-bar-bya-ba #  yin-pas #  lam gyi yan-lag #  gi sgrib-pa # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go / / byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  rnams la sgrib-pa #  ni bshad-zin #  to /
pAramitAsu AvaraNAni / tat anantaram apara AramitAsu vaktavyam iti atas Aha pAramitAsu AvaraNam
# de'i-'og-tu #  pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams kyi bshad dgos-pa # s de'i-phyir #  / / pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams la sgrib-pa #  ni /
ESvaryasyA aTa sugateH sattvA atyAgasya ca AvRtiH / iti vistaraH
# phyug-po #  dang ni bde-'gro #  dang / / sems-can #  mi gtong sgrib-pa #  dang / / zhes rgya-cher #  smos so /
atra daSAnAm pAramitAnAm yasyAH pAramitAyAH yat Palam tad AvaraNena / tasyAH AvaraNam udBAvitam
# 'di-la #  pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bcu po dag gi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  gang-gi #  'bras-bu #  gang-yin-pa #  de-la #  sgrib-pa # s de'i sgrib-pa #  zhes brjod-pa #  yin no /
kim atra kAraNam yat mAtsarya AdayaH vastutas dAna Adi vibanDe vartamAnaH tat / Pala AvaraNa tvena ucyante na punar pAramitA AvaraNa tvena iti
# 'di-la #  ser-sna #  la-sogs-pa #  sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la dngos su gegs-byed-pa #  bzhin-du #  ci'i-phyir #  de'i 'bras-bu #  la sgrub-pa # r brjod la / / pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams la sgrib-pa # r ni ma bshad ce na /
tat Pala arTena dAna AdO sarvaH pravartate / tasmAt mAtsarya Adi prahANaH Adara utpAdana arTam Pala AvaraNam uktam na / pAramitAvaraNam iti
# de'i 'bras-bu # 'i don-du #  sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la thams-cad #  'jug ste / / de-bas-na #  ser-sna #  la-sogs-pa #  spang-ba # r nan-tan #  bskyed-pa # 'i phyir 'bras-bu #  la sgrib-pa # r bshad de / / pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnam la sgrib-pa # r ni ma yin no /
aTavA mAtsarI Adikam AvaraNam ESvarya Adi vipakza BUtam / dAridrya Adi Palam janayat ESvarya Adi Pala pratibanDAt tad AvaraNam ucyate / kintAsAmPalam
# yang-na #  ser-sna #  la-sogs-pa #  sgrib-pa #  phyug-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  su gyur-pa #  dbul-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  bskyed-pa #  na phyug-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  la gegs-byed-pa # s de'i sgrib-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / de-dag #  gi 'bras-bu #  gang zhe na /
tatra dAna pAramitAyAH Palam prADAnyena ESvarya ADipatyam / SIlapAramitAyAH sugatiH
# de-la #  sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni gtso bor ni phyug-po #  dang bdag-po # 'o / / tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni bde-'gro # 'o /
kzAnti pAramitAyAH sattvA aparityAgaH / vIrya pAramitAyAH doza guNa hAni vRdDI
# bzod-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni sems-can #  yongs-su-mi-gtong-ba # 'o / / brtson 'grus kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni nyes-pa #  dang yon-tan #  'bri-ba #  dang 'phel-ba # 'o /
DyAna pAramitAyAH SAsane sattva avatAraNam / prajQApAramitAyAH guru vimocanam
# bsam-gtan #  gyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni bstan-pa #  la sems-can #  'dzud-pa # 'o / / shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni btsud pa de rnams rnam-par-grol-ba # r byed-pa # 'o /
upAya kOSalya pAramitAyAm boDi pariNAmanayA kuSalA akzaya tvam / prANi DAna pAramitayAH SuBanEH antar yam
# thabs-la-mkhas-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni byang-chub #  tu yongs-su-bsngo-ba # s dge-ba #  mi-zad-pa # 'o / / smon-lam #  gyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni dge-ba #  rgyun-mi-'chad-pa # 'o /
bala pAramitAyAH kuSala Darma niyatIkaraNam
# stobs kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni dge-ba'i-chos #  nges-par-'byed-pa # 'o /
jQAna pAramitAyAH Darma upaBogaH sattva paripAcanaQca
# ye shes kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni chos la longs-spyod-pa #  dang sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-pa # 'o /
ESvarya ADipatya AvaraNam iti / tatra ESvaryam Dana upakaraNa bahulatA
# phyug-po #  dang bdag-po #  la sgrib ces bya-ba #  la / / de-la #  phyug-po #  ni nor dang yo-byad #  mang-ba # 'o /
ADipatyam p / tat upaBoga vaSi tvam
# bdag-po #  ni longs-spyod #  de-la #  dbang-ba # 'o /
asya uBayasya AvaraNam AvaraNam dAna pAramitAyAH tat Pala tvAt / kim punar tat / mAtsaryam
# de-gnyi-ga #  la sgrib-pa #  ni sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i sgrib-pa #  ste / / de'i 'bras-bu #  yin pa'i phyir ro / / de gang zhe na ser-sna # 'o /
sugati AvaraNam iti
# bde-'gro #  la sgrib ces bya-ba #  la /
SoBanA gatiH sugatiH manuzyaH devaH ca
# mdzes-pa # r 'gro-ba #  ni bde-'gro #  ste mi dang lha'o /
tasya AvaraNam AvaraNam SIla pAramitAyAH tat PalatvAt / tat punar dOSIlyam kutsitam kAya vAc karma / sattvA aparityAgaH iti / upakAri vat apakAri sattva upAdAnam
# de-la #  sgrib-pa #  ni tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i sgrib-pa #  ste / / de'i 'bras-bu #  yin pa'i phyir ro / / de ni 'chal-ba'i-tshul-khrims #  te / / lus-dang-ngag-gi-las #  ngan-pa # 'o / / sems-can #  yongs-su-mi-gtong-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni sems-can #  gnod-par-byed-pa #  la yang phan-'dogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  'dzin-pa #  ste / / de-yang #  bzod-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu # 'o /
etat ca kzAnti Palam tad AvaraNam kroDaH / doza guNa hAni budDI iti
# de'i sgrib-pa #  ni khro-ba # 'o / / nyes-pa #  dang yon-tan #  'bri zhing 'phel-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  la /
sva parA apakAra prayuktAnAm utpannAnAm prahANam / anutpannA anAQcA anutpAdaH dozANAm hAniH
# bdag-dang-gzhan #  la gnod-pa #  rab tu zhugs-pa #  skyes-pa #  rnams spong-ba #  dang ma-skyes-pa #  rnams mi-skyed-pa #  ni nyes-pa #  rnams 'bri-ba # 'o /

# bdag-dang-gzhan #  la phan-pa # r zhugs-pa #  skyes-pa #  rnams phyir-zhing-'byung-ba #  dang ma-skyes-pa #  rnams skyed-pa #  ni yon-tan #  rnams 'phel-ba # 'o / / 'di-la #  sgrib-pa #  gang zhe na le-lo # 'o /
vineya avatAraNa AvaraNam iti

vineyAnAm SAsane avatAraNam / svargA apavarga lABa kAraNa tvena aByupagamAt
# 'dul-ba #  rnams bstan-pa #  la 'dzud-pa #  ni mtho-ris #  dang byang grol rnyed-pa'i-rgyu # r khas-len-pa # 'i phyir ro /
upaSAntyA gOravaH utpadyamAne sattvAH san jalpa RdDi apryatnena / SAsanampratipadyante / atra ca vikzepaH AvaraNam / vimocana AvaraNam iti / vimocanam kleSa prahANam / tat ca anuSAsanyA Bavati anuSAsanI ca prajQA nA anyaTA iti atas / prajQApAramitA Palam vimocanam / tad AvaraNam klizwa prajQA mohaH duzprajQA vA / dAna Adi akzayatva AvaraNam iti
# nye-bar-zhi-ba # s gus-pa #  skye ste sems-can #  kun brjod-pa #  dang rdzu-'phrul #  gyis bsgrib mi-dgos-pa # r bstan-pa #  rtogs-pa # r byed do / / 'di-la #  sgrib-pa #  ni g-yeng ba'o / / rnam-par-grol-ba # r byed-pa #  la sgrib ces bya-ba #  la rnam-par-grol-ba # r byed-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-spong-ba #  ste / / de-yang #  rjes-su-bstan-pa # s 'gyur ro / / rjes-su-bstan-pa #  ni shes-rab #  kyis te / / gzhan gyis ma yin no / / de'i-phyir #  shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni rnam-par-grol-ba # r byed-pa # 'o / / de'i sgrib-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi shes-rab #  bam / / gti-mug #  gam / / 'chal pa'i shes-rab #  po / / sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  mi-zad-pa #  la sgrib ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni sbyin-pa #  dang tshul-khrims #  la-sogs-pa #  mi-zad-pa #  la sgrib-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni /
dAna SIla AdInAm akzaya tve yat AvaraNam tat upAya pAramitAyAH AvaraNam

tad AvaraNam mahA boDi pariNAmanA lakzaNA anupAya jQa tA iti eke

# ji lta zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  smon-lam-gyi-dbang #  gis de dang mthun-pa # 'i skye-ba #  yongs-su-'dzin-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
praNiDAvaSena hi dAna AdInAm nErantarya pravRttyA anuguNAm upapattim / parigRhNAti
# smon-lam-gyi-dbang #  gis sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  'byung-ba #  dang mthun-pa # 'i skye-ba #  yongs su 'dzin to /
tasya AvaraNam dAna Adi anukUla upapattO= apraNiDAnam
# de-la #  sgrib-pa #  ni sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dang mthun-par #  smon-lam #  mi 'debs-pa # 'o /
tasya eva kuSalasya niyatIkaraNa AvaraNam iti / pratidinam pratikzaNam vA niyatIkaraNam niScayaH
# dge-ba #  de nyid nges-par-byed-pa #  la sgrib ces bya-ba #  ni nyin re'am skad-cig-re-re-la #  gcig-tu #  byed-pa #  ni nges-par-byed-pa # 'o /
atra eva kAraNam Aha pratisaMKyAna BAvanA balAByAm / vipakzA anaBiBavAt iti
# 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  / / so-sor-brtags-pa #  dang bsgoms-pa # 'i stobs kyis mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyis zil gyis mi gnon-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
atra pratisaMKyAna balam DErya sahitA prajQA
# de-la #  so-sor-brtags-pa'i-stobs #  ni bstan-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i shes-rab #  bo /

# brtan-pa #  ni btags-pa # 'i chos te; brtson 'grus dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang shes-rab #  gsum lhan-cig-skyes-pa #  la btags-pa # 'i phyir ro /

kim atra AvaraNam
# 'di-la #  sgrib-pa #  gang zhe na /

# so-so # r ma-brtags-pa #  dang bsgom-pa #  nyam-chung-ba # 'o /

# bdag-dang-gzhan #  chos la longs-spyod-pa #  dang yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-pa #  la sgrib ces bya-ba #  ni longs-spyod-pa # 'i 'khor-gyi-dkyil-'khor #  du rnam-pa # r gnas te /

# theg-pa-chen-po # 'i chos zab cing rgya-che-ba #  la longs-spyod-pa #  dang sprul pa rnam-pa-sna-tshogs #  kyi las kyis tshes ston-pa # s sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-pa #  ni 'bras-bu # 'o /

atra ca dravyataH zax pAramitAH nAmataH daSa / prajQApAramitA praBAvita tvAt catasRNAm pAramitAnAm
# 'di-la #  rdzas su ni pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  drug go / / ming du ni bcu ste / / pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bzhi ni shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  las rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
tatra prajQApAramitA loka uttara nirvikalpa jQAnam / tena jQAnena krameNa sarva AvaraNa prahANam
# de-la #  shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes te / / ye shes des sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  rim-gyis #  spang ngo /

# thabs dang smon-lam #  dang stobs dang ye shes kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam gyi rjes-las-thob-pa # 'i ye shes kyis bsdus so /
jQAna pAramitA prakRzwA satI kaTam na nirvikalpaH iti
# ye shes kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  mchog yin na ji-ltar #  rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  ma yin zhe na /
jQAna pAramitA hi nirvikalpa jQAna pRzwa labDa jQAnam
# ye shes kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  na rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyi rjes-las-thob-pa # 'i ye shes te /

# ye shes des khong-du-chud-pa #  yongs su bcad nas bdag-nyid #  kyang chos la longs-spyod-pa #  rab tu myong la / / gzhan dag kyang yongs-su-smin-pa # r byad pa yin te /
tat ca etat nirvikalpe dvayam api na asti iti atas na nirvikalpA / jQAna pAramitA iti / uktam pAramitAnAm AvaraNam / BUmizu AvaraNAni p / tat anantaram BUmizu vaktavyam iti atas Aha BUmO punar yaTAkramam
# 'di gnyi-ga #  yang rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  la med-pa # s de'i-phyir #  ye shes kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  ma yin no / / pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams kyi sgrib-pa #  ni bshad-zin #  to /

# de'i-'og-tu #  sa rnams kyi brjod dgos-pa # s de'i-phyir #  / / sa rnams la yang go-rims #  bzhin te / / kun du 'gro don mchog gi don /

# zhes rgya-cher #  smos so / / de-la #  sa ni bcu ste /

# rab-tu-dga'-ba #  dang dri-ma-med-pa #  dang 'od byed-pa #  dang 'od 'phro can dang shin-tu #  sbyang dka' dang mngon du gyur ba dang ring-du-song-ba #  dang mi g-yo-ba #  dang legs-pa # 'i blo-gros #  dang chos kyi sprin no /
tatra Darma ADAtoH sarvatra ga Adi arTe aDigamAt / avakASa viSeza uttara uttara pratipatti sTAna rUpeNa tat / utpanna guNa vastu rUpeNa ca BUmayaH ucyante / DarmaDAtoH sarvatragAt yaTe yena yena vihAreNa boDisattvaH bahulam / viharati tasmin tasmin vihAre avasTAna arTena BUmI AKyet pare / vyavasTAnam punar BUmiBiH pramuditAyAm darzana mAga utpatti tvAt
# de-la #  chos-kyi-dbyings #  la kun-tu #  'gro-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i don-du #  khong-du-chud-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  kyi khyad-par #  rnams ni gong-nas-gong-du #  khong-du-chud-pa # 'i gnas-pa'i-tshul #  dang de-la # s skyes-pa # 'i yon-tan #  gyi gzhi'i tshul gyi sa rnams zhes-bya'o #  / / gzhan dag na re chos-kyi-dbyings #  kun du 'gro-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i don la gnas-pa #  gang-dang-gang-gis #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  mang-du-gnas-pa # 'i gnas-pa #  de-dang-de #  la gnas-pa # 'i phyir sa zhes-bya'o #  zhe'o / / sa rnams kyi rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  ni rab-tu-dga'-ba #  la mthong-ba'i-lam #  skye-ba # 'i phyir byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  chos-mngon-pa # r rtogs so /

# chos-mngon-pa # r rtogs-nas #  dri-ma-med-pa #  la rang-gi-ngang-gis #  'byung-ba #  lhag-pa'i-tshul-khrims #  bslab-pa # 'i khyad-par #  sgrub ste /
nizpAdayati sarva sUkzma apatIdOH SIlya vigamAt

# de-dag #  ni ma spangs kyang spangs-pa #  bzhin te / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams la kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r byed-pa #  ma yin no / / don de nyid kyi dbang du mdzad de tshigs su bcad de gsungs-pa #  / / thabs chen rnams dang ldan-pa #  la / / nyon mongs byang-chub #  lan lag 'gyur /

taTA hi SrAvakAH pratyeka budDAH ca tasmin sati eva mucyante na tu / boDisattvAH iti atas asADAraNam / etat BUmizu AvaraNam uktam na tu etat eva BUmizu AvaraNam iti kRtvA
# 'di-ltar #  nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  rnams la de yod kyang grol bar 'gyur la / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams ni ma-yin-pa # s de'i-phyir #  thun mong ma yin no / / de sa rnams la sgrib-pa # r bshad kyang / / sa rnams la sgrib-pa #  de-kho-na # r ma zad de /
kleSaH tu SrAvaka AdiBiH boDisattvAnAm samAnaH iti tasya AvaraNa tvena / boDisattva BUmizu na viDiH na pratizeDaH iti tasyAH avavacane api AvaraNam na / nivartate
# nyon-mongs-pa # 'i nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams la 'dra-ba # s byang-chub-sems-dpa'i-sa #  rnams la de'i sgrib-pa # r gzhag-pa #  yang med bkag-pa #  yang med de / / de ma bshad kyang sgrib-pa #  las ldog-pa # r mi 'gyur ro /
anyaH Aha aklizwam ajQAnam SrAvaka AdiBiH boDisattvAnAm samAnam iti / BUmInAm viSezeNa AvaraNam ucyate / kleSaH tvA anuzaFgikaH iti na uktam
# gzhan na re nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams la 'dra-ba # s nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i mi-shes-pa #  ni sa rnams la sgrib-pa #  khyad-par #  du bshad kyi /
kleSaH api SrAvaka AdiBiH boDisattvAnAm samAnaH eva iti asO= AnuzaFgikaH na / syAt iti
# nyon-mongs-pa #  ni zhar la yod-pa # s ma smos so zhes zer te / / nyon-mongs-pa #  yang nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams la 'dra-ba #  nyid yin-pas #  de zhar la yod ces bya-ba # r mi rung ngo /

sAmAnya lakzaNena ekatra yaTA sarvatra api taTA iti sarvatra ga tvAt / sarvatragaH
