# rang-bzhin-gyis #  'od-gsal-ba # r mthong-ba # 'i phyir chos-kyi-dbyings #  rab tu rtogs so zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro /
yena asi asya evam Bavati tasmAt tarhi asmABiH samAne aBinirhAre / sarva AkAra pariSoDana aBinirhAraH eva yogaH karaNIyaH iti Agamam darSayati
# des de-'di-snyam-du #  sems te / / de-lta-bas-na #  sgrub du mtshungs-pa #  la bdag-gis #  rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  yongs-su-sbyong-ba #  mngon-pa # r bsgrub-pa #  nyid la brtson par bya'o snyam mo zhes lung las bshad do /
sUtre hi uktam yasmAt iti daSa kuSalAH karma paTAH prajQAkAreNa / pratiBAvyamAnAH yAvat SrAvaka yAnam saMvartayanti
# mdo las kyang 'di skad ces de-bas-na #  dge-ba #  bcu'i las-kyi-lam #  de-dag #  shes-rab #  kyi rnam-pa # r yongs su bsgoms na nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa # 'i bar-du #  'gyur ro /
tatas uttaram pariSoDitAH yAvat pratyeka budDyAnam saMvartayanti
# de-bas #  gong-du #  yongs su sbyangs-pa # s rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi theg-pa # 'i bar-du #  'gyur ro /
tatas uttaram pariSoDitAH yAvat / boDisattva BUmi pariSudDi pAramitA pariSudDi caryA vipula tvAya / saMvartante / tatas uttaram pariSudDitara tvAt yAvat daSa bala tvAya saMvartante / tasmAt tarhi asmABiH samAne aBinirhAraH iti vistaraH
# de-bas #  gong-du #  yongs su sbyangs-pa # s byang-chub-sems-dpa'i-sa #  yongs-su-dag-pa #  dang pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  yongs-su-dag-pa #  dang spyod-pa #  rgyas-pa # 'i bar-du #  'gyur ro / / de-bas #  gong-du #  yongs-su-dag-pa # s stobs-bcu # 'i bar-du #  'gyur ro / / de-lta-bas-na #  bsgrub tu mtshungs-pa #  la bdag-gis #  zhes rgya-cher #  bshad do /
yasmAt etat asya eva Bavati dvitIyAyAm BUmO tasmAt tarhi ityAdi / tasmAt dvitIyayA agra arTam prativiDyati iti vijQAyate
# gang-gis #  'di-ltar #  de-'di-snyam-du #  sems te / / sa gnyis-pa #  la de-lta-bas-na #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / de-bas-na #  gnyis-pa #  la mchog gi don-du #  rab-tu-rtogs-pa # r mngon no /
aBinirhAraH prayatnaH kRtyam vA
# mngon-pa # r bsgrub-pa #  ni 'bad-pa # 'am bya-ba # 'o /
sarva AkAra pariSoDanam DarmaDAtO klizwA aklizwa moha nirAkaraNam
# rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  yongs-su-sbyang-ba #  ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  la nyon-mongs-pa-can #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i rmongs-pa #  sel-ba # 'o /
tasmAt tasyAm BUmO SIla pAramitA tiriktatarA
# de-bas-na #  sa de-la #  tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  lhag-pa # r che-ba #  yin te /
viSizwa arTa prArTanayA sutarAm Atma mAtrIkaraNAt / tRtIyayA tat nizyanda agra arTam / prativiDyati iti prakRtam / DarmaDAtu prativeDa praBAvita tvAt budDa vacanasya
# khyad-par-du-'phags-pa # 'i don la smon-pa # s bdag shin-tu #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i snod du byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gsum-pa #  la ni de'i rgyu-mthun-pa #  don-gyi-mchog #  tu rtogs te / / sangs-rgyas #  kyi gsung ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  rab-tu-rtogs-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
yasmAt sarva AkAra pariSudDa DarmakAya saMjQakena Darma DAtu vaSena / praBAvitaH DarmaDAtu nizyandaH sUtra AdikaH deSanA DarmaH
# 'di-ltar #  rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  yongs-su-dag-pa #  chos kyi sku zhes-bya-ba # 'i chos-kyi-dbyings #  kyi dbang gis chos-kyi-dbyings #  kyi rgyu-mthun-pa #  mdo la-sogs-pa #  bstan-pa # 'i chos rab-tu-byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
Darma DAtu agra tayA tat nizYanda deSanA Darma agra tayA / Darma DAtu pariSudDi nimitta tvAt ca
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  mchog yin-pas #  de'i rgyu-mthun-pa # s bstan-pa # 'i chos kyang mchog yin pa dang chos-kyi-dbyings #  yongs-su-dag-pa # r bya-ba # 'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
tena Darma DAtu nizyandasya p / Srutasya agra tAm viditvA iti vistaraH
# des chos-kyi-dbyings #  kyi rgyu-mthun-pa #  thos-pa #  mchog-tu #  rig-nas #  shes-pa #  rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  la /
tena iti prativiDha DarmaDAtunA
# des zhes-bya-ba #  ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  rab-tu-rtogs-pa # s so /
Srutasya iti Sruta sUtra Adi Darmasya tasyAH agra tA viditvA iti nirvikalpena / jQAnena taTA pratyAtmam jQAtvA iti arTaH
# thos-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mdo la-sogs-pa # 'i chos thos-pa # 'o / / de-la #  mchog-tu #  rig-nas #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyis de-bzhin-du #  so-so # r rang-gis #  shes zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
tat arTam iti budDa vacana SravaNa arTam
# de'i-phyir #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni sangs-rgyas #  kyi gsung mnyan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tri sAhasra mahA sAhasra pramANAyAm api agni kaNXAyAm AtmAnam prakzipet iti / uktam hi sUtre a ced idam kaScid evam brUyAt evam aham tuByam idam / Darma padam samyak sambudDa upanItam boDisattva caryA pariSoDanam / saMSrAvayeyam sa ced tvam mahatyAm agni KaXAyAm samprajvalitAyAm / eka jvAlIBUtAyAm AtmAnam prapAtayeH mahAntam ca / duHKa vedanA upakramam sva SarIreNa upAdadyAt yAH / tasya evam Bavati utsahe aham ekasya api Darma padasya / samyaksambudDa upanItasya boDisattva caryA pariSoDanasya arTAya / tri sAhasra mahA sAhasra lokaDAtO= agni paripUrNe brahma lokAt AtmAnam / utsrazwum / kim punar prAkRtAyAm agni KaXAyAm / api tu Kalu punar sarvEH nirayApAya duHKa saMvAsEH api asmABiH / sarva budDa DarmAH paryezitavyAH kim punar manuzya duHKa saMvAsEH iti / atas eva asyAm BUmO kzAnti pAramitA tiriktatarA Bavati Sruta arTam / sarva kleSa sahana AdiBiH api aBedya tvAt
# me'i 'obs stong-gsum #  gyi stong-chen-po # 'i tshad tsam du yang bdag-nyid #  mchong zhes-bya-ba #  ni mdo las gsungs-pa #  / / gal-te #  la-la-zhig #  de-la #  'di skad ces zer te / / gal-te #  khyod me'i 'obs chen-po #  'bar-ba #  / / kun du 'bar-ba #  / / kun du rab tu mched cing 'bar-ba #  / / me-lce #  gcig-tu #  gyur-pa # 'i nang-du #  bdag rab tu mchong zhing sdug-bsngal-gyi-tshor-ba #  chen-po #  myong-bar-'gyur-ba #  rang-gi-lus #  kyis nyams su len na ngas khyod-la #  chos-kyi-tshig #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa # 'i sangs-rgyas #  kyis bstan-pa #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i spyod-pa #  yongs-su-sbyong-ba #  'di bshad-par-bya # 'o zhe na yang de-'di-snyam-du #  sems te / / yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa # 'i sangs-rgyas #  kyis bstan-pa #  / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i spyod-pa #  yongs-su-sbyong-ba # 'i chos-kyi-tshig #  gcig gi don-du #  yang stong-gsum #  gyi stong-chen-po # 'i 'jig-rten-gyi-khams #  mas rab tu gang-ba # r tshangs-pa'i-'jig-rten #  nas bdag-gis #  bdag dor-ba # r mos na me'i 'obs tha-ma # l bar bdag dor-ba #  lta-ci-smos #  / / sems-can #  dmyal-ba # 'i sdug-bsngal-thams-cad #  nyams su bab kyang bdag-gis #  sangs-rgyas-kyi-chos #  thams-cad #  btsal bar bya na / / mi'i sdug-bsngal #  dang 'grogs-pa #  lta-ci-smos #  kyi snyam nas zhes-bya-ba # 'o / / de-bas-na #  sa de-la #  bzod-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  lhag-pa # r che-ba #  yin te / / thos-pa # 'i ched du nyon-mongs-pa-thams-cad #  la mi 'byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
caturTyA nizparigraha arTam DarmaDAtoH prativiDyati iti prakRtam / caturTyam BUmO sama tvAt anAtmIya tvam Darma DAtoH prativiDyati
# bzhi-pa #  la ni yongs-su-gzung-ba #  med-pa # 'i don-du #  ste / / chos-kyi-dbyings #  rab tu rtogs so zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro / / sa bzhi-ba #  la-la #  ni mnyam-pa # 'i phyir chos-kyi-dbyings #  bdag-gi #  ba med-pa # r rab tu rtogs te /
yasmAt na Darma DAtoH kasyacid samatA asti iti / aTavA sarva viparyAsA vizaya tvAt na kasyacid parigrahaH
# 'di-ltar #  chos-kyi-dbyings #  la bdag gang yang med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yang-na #  phyin-ci-log #  thams-cad-kyi #  yul-ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir su'i yongs-su-bzung-ba #  yang ma yin no /
svayam avizaya tvAt nA atra kaScid parigrahaH / yasmAt Darma tRzNA api vyAvartate iti Agama vacanam
# bdag-nyid-kyis #  phyin-ci-log #  ma-yin-pa # s 'di-la #  yongs-su-bzung-ba #  gang yang med de / / 'di-ltar #  chos la sred-pa #  yang ldog go zhes lung las 'byung ngo /
evam arcizmatyAm nizprapaQcena jQAnena DarmaDAtu aDigamAt / boDipakza Darma prAtpiH
# de-ltar #  'od 'phro ba can ni spros-pa #  med-pa # 'i ye shes kyi dbyings khong-du-chud-pa # 'i phyir byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  kyi chos thob ste /
boDisattvasya yA api sUtra Adi Darma tRzNA pUrvam AsIt sA api / vyAvartate / DyAna samADi samApattiH DarmatRzNA iti anye / tasmAt tasya aBUme vIrya pAramitA tiriktatarA Bavati / aBIkzNam vAc manaH jalpa samatikrAnte boDi pakzEH viharaNAt / paQcamyA santAna aBeda arTam / DarmaDAtoH prativiDyati iti aDikRtam / atItA anAgata vartamAnAnAm sarva budDAnAm paramparataH / boDisattvAn AQca santAnEH AtmanaH p / santAnA aBedam paSyati / daSaBiH citta ASaya viSUdDi samatABiH iti Agamam darSayati / atIta budDa Darma viSudDi ASaya samatayA ca / anAgata budDa Darma viSudDi ASaya samatayA ca
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  mdo-sde #  la-sogs-pa # 'i chos la sred-pa #  snga-nas #  yod-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de-yang #  ldog go / / gzhan dag na re bsam-gtan #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  ni chos la sred-pa # 'o zhe'o / / de-bas-na #  sa de-la #  brtson 'grus kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  lhag-pa # r che-ba #  yin te / / lus dang ngag dang yid kyi spyod-pa #  las 'das-pa # r rgyun-du #  byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  rnams kyis gnas-pa # 'i phyir ro / / lnga pa la ni rgyud tha-dad-pa #  med-pa # 'i don-du #  ste / / chos-kyi-dbyings #  rab tu rtogs zhes-bya-ba #  dang sbyar ro / / 'das-pa #  dang ma byon pa dang da-ltar #  gyi sangs-rgyas #  bcom-ldan-'das #  thams-cad #  nang dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i rgyud rnams dang bdag tha mi dad cing mtshungs-pa # r mthong ngo / / sems dang bsam-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  bcus zhes-bya-ba #  ni lung gis ston te /
pratyutpanna budDa Darma viSudDi ASaya samatayA ca / SIla viSudDi ASaya samatayA ca citta viSudDi ASaya samatayA ca / dRzwi kAFkzA vimati vileKA apanayana viSudDi ASaya samatayA ca / mArgA mArga jQAna viSudDi ASaya samatayA ca / pratipad prahANa jQAna viSudDi ASaya samatayA ca sarva boDi sAkzika / Darma uttara uttara viBAvana viSudDi ASaya samatayA ca / sarva sattva paripAcana viSudDi ASaya samatayA ca / ABiH samatABiH sarva budDAnAm santAnA aBedam prativiDyati / AlayavijQAna parAvRtti lakzaNa Darma kAyasyA aBinnatvAt / tasmAt tasyAm BUmO DyAna pAramitA tiriktatarA / paramArTataH satya AkAra BAvanA bahula tvAt / zazWyAH nizsaFkleSa viSudDi arTam / Darma DAtoH prativiDyati iti sambaDyate / pratItyasamutpAda lakzaNaH saFkleSaH tasmin= AgantukAt prakRtyA na / saFkliSyate / prAkRtika viSudDeH na viSudDi ati / evam sva saMvedya AkAreNa nirvikalpena jQAnena DarmaDAtum / prativiDyati iti atra eva Agamam darSayati / pratItyasamutpAde na asti sa kaScid DarmaH yaH saFkliSyate vA viSudDyate / vA iti prativeDAt
# 'das-pa # 'i sangs-rgyas-kyi-chos #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  la bsam-pa #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  dang ma byon pa'i sangs-rgyas-kyi-chos #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  la bsam-pa #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  dang da-ltar-byung-ba # 'i sangs-rgyas-kyi-chos #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  la bsam-pa #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  dang tshul-khrims #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  la bsam-pa #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  dang sems-can #  rnam-par-dag-pa # s bsam-pa #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  dang lta-ba #  dang the-tshom #  dang yid-gnyis #  dang 'gyod-pa #  sel-ba # s rnam-par-dag-pa #  la bsam-pa #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  dang lam dang lam ma-yin-pa #  shes-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  la bsam-pa #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  dang lam-shes-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  la bsam-pa #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  dang byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  kyi chos-thams-cad #  gong-nas-gong-du #  rnam-pa # r 'jig-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  la bsam-pa #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  dang sems-can-thams-cad #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  la bsam-pa #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  ces bya-ba #  ste / / mnyam-pa-nyid #  'di dag gis sangs-rgyas-thams-cad #  kyi rgyas thams-cad-kyi #  rgyud tha-mi-dad-pa # r rab tu rtogs te / / kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  gnas-gyur-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  chos kyi sku tha-mi-dad-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-bas-na # s de-la #  bsam-gtan #  gyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  lhag-pa # r che-ba #  yin te / / don-dam-pa # r bden-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r bsgoms-pa #  mang-ba # 'i phyir ro / / drug-pa #  la ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  ma-yin-pa # 'i don-du #  ste / / chos-kyi-dbyings #  rab tu rtogs zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro / / rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  ni de-la #  glo-bur-du #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir rang-bzhin-gyis #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  ma yin no / / rang-bzhin-gyis #  rnam-par-dag-pa # s rnam-par-dag-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  ma yin no / / de-ltar #  rang-gis #  rig-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyis chos-kyi-dbyings #  rab tu rtogs so zhes lung de-nyid-la # s ston te / / rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba #  la gang kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'am / / rnam-par-dag-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i chos de-gang-yang #  med-pa # r rab-tu-rtogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
zazWyAm BUmO boDisattvaH pratItyasamutpAdam viDyati / tatra na kasyacid Darmasya saFkleSam vyavadAnam vA prativiDyati
# sa drug-pa #  la ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba #  la rnam-pa # r rtogs te / / chos-kyi-dbyings #  rang-bzhin-gyis #  'od-gsal-ba # 'i phyir de-la #  yang chos gang-la #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'am /
DarmaDAtoH prakRti praBA svara tvAt pratItyasamutpAda aFgaQca / saFkleSa mAtra tvAt na ca tat vyatiriktaH anyaH AtmA asti AtmIyaH vA yasmin / saFkleSaH saFkalpyate viSudDiH vA
# rnam-par-byang-ba #  med-pa # r rtogs so / / rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba # 'i yan-lag #  rnams ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  tsam du zad-pa # 'i phyir gang-la #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'am / / rnam-par-dag-pa # r kun du rtogs-pa #  de-la #  gtogs-pa # r bdag gam bdag-gi #  med do /
tasmAt vA asyAm BUmO prajQApAramitA vE tiriktatarA / nissaFkleSa viSudDi arTena pratItyasamutpAda gAmBIryA avaboDAt iti / saptamyA anAnAnArTa tvam
# de'i-phyir #  sa de-la #  shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  lhag-pa # r che-ba #  yin te; kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa #  med-pa # 'i don-du #  rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba #  za-ba #  mo khong-du-chud-pa # 'i phyir ro / / bdun pa la ni tha-dad-pa #  med-pa # 'i don-du #  ste /
DarmaDAtoH prativiDyati iti aDikRtam
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  rab tu rtogs zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro /
tasyAm BUmO boDisattvaH aBiBavati sarva nimitta samudAcAra aBAvAt / nimitta samudAcAra dvArakaMH ca nAnA tva samudAcAraH iti / atas nimitta samudAcArA aBAvAt saptamyA anAtva arTam Darma DAtoH / prativiDyati iti ucyate
# sa de-la #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  mtshan-ma-thams-cad #  mi-'byung-ba # s zil gyis non te / / mtshan-ma #  'byung-ba # 'i sgo nas tha-dad-pa #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de-bas-na #  mtshan-ma-med-pa # 'i phyir bdun pa la tha-dad-pa #  med-pa # 'i don-du #  rab tu rtogs so zhes-bya'o #  /
imam eva arTam pradarSayan= Aha nirnimitta tayA / sUtra Adi Darma nimitta nAnAtvA samudAcArAt iti
# don de nyid rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir mtshan-ma-med-pa # s mdo la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  tha-dad-pa #  mi-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
yEH sUtra Adi Darma nimittEH DarmaDAtum praviSati p / tAni balAn nAnAtvena tat praveSatat pRzwa labDayoH aBimuKIBavanti / yAvat zazWI BUmiH
# sa drug-pa # 'i bar-du #  ni mdo la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-kyi-mtshan-ma #  gang-gis #  chos-kyi-dbyings #  la 'jug-pa #  de-dag #  shugs kyis de-la #  'jug-pa #  dang de'i-rjes-la # s thob-pa # 'i shes-pa #  gnyis kyis tha-dad-pa #  nyid-du #  mngon du 'gyur ro /
saptamyA antu BUmO sarva nimitta eka rasa AkAreNa jQanena Darma DAtoH / nimitta aBAva tvam prativiDyati iti tAni tAni nimittAni na / samudAcaranti / tasmAt tasyAm BUmO= upAya paramitA tiriktatarA Bavati yatas
# sa bdun pa la ni mtshan thams-cad #  ro gcig pa'i rnam-pa # 'i ye shes kyis chos-kyi-dbyings #  mtshan-ma-med-pa # r rab-tu-rtogs-pa #  mtshan-ma #  de-dag #  mi 'byung ngo / / de'i-phyir #  sa de-la #  thabs kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  lhag-pa # r che-ba #  yin te /
sarva nimittAni animitta tvena prativiDyati nimitta kRtam ca vyavahAram na / viroDayati
# 'di-ltar #  mtshan-ma-thams-cad #  ma med-pa #  nyid-du #  yang rab tu rtogs la / / mtshan-ma # r byas-pa # 'i tha-snyad #  kyang mi 'gog ste /
tat prativeDAt ca tasyAm eva vaSitvam pratilaBate / azwamyA ahInaDikA arTam / Darma DAtoH prativiDyati iti sambaDyate
# de rab rtogs-pa # s kyang de-nyid-la #  dbang-byed-pa #  rab tu thob-pa # 'i phyir ro / / brgyad pa la ni bri-ba #  med cing 'phel-ba #  med-pa # 'i don-du #  ste / / chos-kyi-dbyings #  rab tu rtogs so zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro /
DarmaDAtoH prakRti pariSudDa tvAt samalA amalA avasTayoH / viSezA aBAvAt / atas eva asO nityam taTA eva iti kRtvA taTatA iti ucyate
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  rang-bzhin-gyis #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i phyir dri-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  dang; dri-ma-med-pa # 'i dus na yang khyad-par-med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-bas-na #  rtag-tu #  de-bzhin #  kho-na #  bas de-bzhin-nyid #  ces bya'o /
nimittA aBAve kvacid api hIna tA na asti
# mtshan-ma #  dang bral-ba #  na gang-la #  yang bri-ba #  yang med la /
sa nimitta tve kvacid api aDika tvam na asti / taTA hi nimittam eva animittam iti kiQcid
# mtshan-ma #  yod-pa #  na yang gang-la #  yang 'phel-ba #  yang med do / / la-la # n re 'di-ltar #  mtshan-ma #  nyid mtshan-ma-med-pa # 'o zhe'o /
anutpattika Darma kzAnti lABAt iti atra eva kAraNam
# 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  / / mi-skye-ba'i-chos #  la bzod-pa #  thob-pa # s zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
azwamyAm hi BUmO boDisattvaH anutpattika Darma kzAnti pratilamBAt / DarmaDAtoH aByuccayA aBAva tvam apacayA aBAva tvam ca evam / prativiDyati / saFkleSe vyavadAne vA kasyacid Darmasya / hAni vRdDi adarSana Aditya pUrva DarmA
# sa brgyad pa la byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  mi-skye-ba'i-chos #  la bzod-pa #  thob-pa # s chos-kyi-dbyings #  la bri-ba #  med-pa #  dang lhag-ma #  med-pa #  nyid-du #  de-ltar #  rab tu rtogs so / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  ni bri-ba #  med-pa # 'am / / rnam-par-byang-ba # s na 'phel-ba # 'i chos gang yang med de / / sngon med-pa # 'i chos mi-skye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
caturTA vaSitA nirvikalpa vaSitA kzetra pariSudDi vaSitA jQAna vaSitA / karma vaSitA ca / tatra nirvikalpa vaSita ASraya tvam Darma DAtoH veditavyam / anABogena sarva nimitta samudAcArA aBAvAt
# dbang rnam-pa-bzhi #  ste / / rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  la dbang-ba #  dang zhing yongs-su-dag-pa #  la dbang-ba #  dang ye shes la dbang-ba #  dang las la dbang-ba # 'o / / de-la #  lhun-gyis-grub-pa # r mtshan-ma-thams-cad #  mi-'byung-ba # s chos-kyi-dbyings #  ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes la dbang-ba # 'i gnas su rig-par-bya # 'o /
saptamyAm api nimitta samudAcAra aBAvaH samBavati aBisaMskAreNa
# bdun pa yang mtshan-ma #  mi-'byung-ba #  yod mod kyi / / mngon-par-'du-byed-pa # s yin gyi /
iha tu anaBisaMskAreNa iti viSezaH
# 'dir ni lhun gyi grub-pa #  yin-pas #  bye-brag #  yod do /
kzetra pariSudDi vaSitA ASraya tvam ca azwamyA prativiDyati iti prakRtam / kzetra pariSudDi vaSita ASraya tvam Darma DAtoH yaTezwam
# ji-ltar-bzhed-pa #  bzhin-du #  sangs-rgyas-kyi-zhing #  dang 'khor-gyi-dkyil-'khor #  kun du bstan-pa # 'i mthu brnyes-pa # s chos-kyi-dbyings #  ni zhing yongs su dag la dbang-ba # 'i gnas su rig-par-bya # 'o /
budDa kzetra parzad maNXa lasat darSana Sakti pratilamBAt / tasmAt tasyAm BUmO praNiDAna pAramitA tiriktatarA / nirvikalpa kzetra vaSitA lABena kuSala nirantara prayogAt
# de-bas-na #  sa de-la #  smon-lam #  gyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  lhag-pa # r che-ba #  yin te / / rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  dang bzhin la dbang-ba #  thob-pa # s dge-ba #  la bar-chad-med-pa # r sbyor-ba # 'i phyir ro / / dgu pa la ni ye shes la dbang-ba # 'i gnas nyid-du #  ste / / ci zhe na /
jQAna vaSitA ASraya tvam navamyA / DarmaDAtoH prativiDyati iti prakRutam / kaTame tat vijQayate navamyA jQa navazita ASraya tvam prativiDyati iti / atas Aha pratisaMvid lABAt / asyAm hi BUmO Darma arTa nirukti pratiBAna pratisaMvidaH anyEH
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  rab tu rtogs zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro / / dgu pa la ni ye shes la dbang-ba # 'i gnas te / / rab tu rtogs so zhes-bya-ba # r ci mngon zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  so-so #  yang-dag-par #  rig-pa #  thob-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / sa 'di-la #  chos-dang-don #  dang nges-pa'i-tshig #  dang spobs-pa #  so-so #  yang-dag-par #  rig-pa #  gzhan dag gis mi-'jigs-pa #  rab tu thob po /
aparyAntAH pratilaBate / atas atra jQAna vaSita ASraya tvam Darma DAtoH pratividDam iti vijQAyate / tasmAt tasyAm BUmO balapAramitA tiriktatarA
# de-bas-na #  'dir ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  ye shes la dbang-ba # 'i gnas te / / rab tu rtogs so zhes-bya-ba # r mngon no / / de'i-phyir #  sa de-la #  stobs kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  lhag-pa # r che-ba #  yin te /
prajQA bala viSeza yogAt p
# shes-rab #  kyi stobs kyi khyad-par #  dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
karma vaSita ASraya tvam daSamyA prativiDyati iti sambaDyate
# sa bcu pa la ni las la dbang-ba # 'i gnas nyid-du #  rtogs so / / de ci mngon zhe na /
kartum etat gamyate / atas Aha yaTecCam nirmANEH sattva arTa karaNAt iti
# de'i-phyir #  ji-ltar-bzhed-pa #  bzhin-du #  sprul pa rnams kyis sems-can-gyi-don #  mdzad-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
niScayena anena daSamyAm BUmO Darma DAtoH karma vaSita ASraya tvam
# 'di ni sa bcu pa la chos-kyi-dbyings #  las la dbang-ba # 'i gnas su rab tu rtogs so /
prativiDyati tena taTAgata karma sva ADipatyam pratilaBate
# des de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # 'i phrin-las #  rnams la dbang-byed-pa #  rab tu brnyes te /
taTA hi sugata tvAt daSa diS ananta loka DAtu sTitAnAm sattvAnAm / nirmANakAyEH yaTezwam yasya yaTA yasmin kAle yat kartavyam tasya / taTA tasmin kAle tat karoti
# 'di-ltar #  bde-bar-gshegs-pa #  bzhin-du #  phyogs-bcu # 'i 'jig-rten-gyi-khams #  mtha'-yas-pa #  na gnas-pa # 'i sems-can #  dag la sprul pa'i sku rnams kyis ji-ltar-'dod-pa #  bzhin-du #  gang-la #  ji-ltar #  gang-gi-tshe #  gang bya-ba #  la / / de-ltar #  de'i tshe de mdzad do /
tasmAt asyAm BUmO jQAna pAramitA tiriktatarA
# de-bas-na #  sa 'di-la #  ye shes kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  lhag-pa # r che-ba #  yin te /
Darma pariBoga sattva paripAka viSeza yogAt iti
# chos la longs-spyod-pa #  dang sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r mdzad-pa # 'i khyad-par #  dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
evam AsAm yaTA uktAnAm boDisattva BUminAm / daSaviDa Darma DAtu prativeDa sarva AkAra parizoDana viBanDa bUtam yat
# de-ltar #  byang-chub-sems-dpa'i-sa #  bcu ji-skad-du #  bshad-pa #  de-dag #  la chos-kyi-dbyings #  rnam-pa-bcu #  rab-tu-rtogs-pa #  rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  yongs-su-sbyang-ba #  la gegs su gyur-pa #  /
aklizwam ajQAnam ekEkAyAm api BUmyAm AvaraNam tat pratipakzA / boDisattvAnAm daSa BU mayaH vyavasTitAH navamyAH daSamyAH ca BUmeH / Palena viSezaH paridIpitaH na AvaraNa Beda prativeDa viSezeNa tat vihArasya / kAm api anirUpyA avasTAm gata tvAt
# nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i mi-shes-pa # s re-re #  la yang sgrib-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de'i gnyen-po # r byang-chub-sems-dpa'i-sa #  bcu rnam-pa # r gzhag go / / sa dgu pa dang sa bcu pa dag gi khyad-par #  ni 'bras-bu # s bstan-pa #  yin gyi / / dmigs-pa #  tha-dad-pa #  rab tu rtog-pa # 'i khyad-par #  gyis ni ma yin te / / gnas-pa #  cir yang dpyad du med-pa # 'i gnas su phyin pa'i phyir ro /
sarvatraga Adi arTa prativeDa prayojanam daSa BUmizu daSAnAm pAramitAnAm / viSeza gatiH yaTAkramam
# kun du 'gro-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i don-du #  rtogs-pa # 'i dgongs-pa #  ni sa cu rnams su pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bcu go-rims-bzhin-du #  khyad-par-du-'gro-ba # 'o /
tasmAt etat eva uktam BUmyAvaraNam pAramitA viSeza gati AvaraNam iti
# de'i-phyir #  'di skad ces sa la sgrib-pa #  ni pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams khyad-par-du-'gro-ba #  la sgrib-pa # 'o zhes bshad do /
aTavA sUtra uktam eva samADi samApatti Adikam uttara uttara BUmi viSizwam / sarva AkAram nAnA avasAnam Palam sarvatraga Adi arTa prativeDa prayojanam / iti
# yang-na #  mdo las ting-nge-'dzin #  brgya-la #  snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s gong-nas-gong-du #  khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  mchog rnams kyi ye shes kyi mthar-thug-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  gsung pa nyid kun du 'gro-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i don-du #  rab-tu-rtogs-pa # 'i dgongs-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
AvaraNa samAsaH / prAk uktAni bahuviDAni sarva AvaraNAni dvaya AvaraNa antar gatAni iti / pradarSana arTam Aha samAsena punar / kleSa AvaraNam AKyAtam jQeya AvaraNam eva ca / kaTam etat gamyate / samAsatas dvayam eva na punar tRtIyam api asti iti
# sgrib-pa #  rnam-pa-du-ma #  gong-du #  ma bshad-pa #  thams-cad #  ni sgrib-pa #  gnyis kyi nang-du #  'dus-pa # r rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir mdor-bsdu-na #  / / nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  nyid-du #  bstan zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / mdor-bsdu-na #  gnyis kho-na #  ste / / gsum du med do zhes-bya-ba #  de ci mngon zhe na /
atas Aha / sarvAn AvaraNAni iha iti
# de'i-phyir #  / / der ni sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  de / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs te /
atra antargatAni iti vAkyaSezaH
# nang-du #  'dus so zhes-bya-ba #  ni tshig gi lhag-ma # 'o /
sarva AvaraNAni dvaya AvaraNa antargatAni na anyat tRtIyam asti iti gamyate
# sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  sgrib-pa #  gnyis kyi nang-du #  'dus-pa # s gsum-pa #  gzhan med-pa # r mngon no /
yatas ca sarva AvaraNAni atra eva antargatAni atasya eva / sarva AvaraNa saFgrAhakasya kleSa jQeya AvaraNa dvayasya kzayAt
# gang-gi-phyir #  sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  'di nyid kyi nang-du #  'dus-pa #  de'i-phyir #  sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  sdud-pa #  nyon-mongs-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  po 'di zad na /
sarva AvaraNeByaH muKtiH izyate sarva AvaraNAnA prahANa miti arTaH / budDabUmyAH varaNe na AKyAte kaTam atra eva antar BAvaH
# sgrib-pa #  thams-cad-la # s grol bar 'dod de / / sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  spong zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / sangs-rgyas #  kyi sa'i sgrib-pa #  ma bshad-pa # r de nyid kyi nang-du #  'dus-pa # r ji-ltar #  'gyur /
na hi aBiDAnAt antarBAvaH kin tarhi svaBAvAt
# brjod-pa # s de'i nang-du #  gtogs-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  yang ma yin te / / rang-bzhin-gyis #  'dus so /
api ca vyApya AvaraNa vacanAt tat api uktam eva
# de lta mod kyi khyab-pa # 'i sgrib-pa #  bshad-pa # 'i phyir de nyid bshad-zin #  to /
anyaTA ca pradeSa AvaraNam eva Bavati iti
# gzhan-du-na #  ni nyi-tshe-ba # 'i sgrib-pa #  nyid-du #  'gyur ro /
aTavA budDa BUmi AvaraNa saFgraha arTam Aha
# yang-na #  sangs-rgyas #  kyi sa'i sgrib-pa #  bsdu-ba # 'i don-du #  /
sarvANi AvaraNAni iha yat kzayAt muktiH izyate p
# der ni sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  de / / ce zad nas ni grol bar 'dod /
budDa AvaraNA akzaye na muktiH asti iti / atas Seza AvaraNa vat tat api AvaraNam iti pratipAditam Bavati
# ces bya-ba #  gsungs so / / sangs-rgyas #  kyi sa'i sgrib-pa #  ma zad-pa # r grol ba med de / / de'i-phyir #  sgrib-pa #  lhag-ma #  ltar de'i sgrib-pa #  yang bstan-pa #  yin no /
sOkzmya prakarza avasTam tu aklizwam ajQAnam kleSa vAsanAH ca / budDa BUmeH AvaraNam ucyate
# nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i mi-shes-pa #  rab tu phra-ba # 'i gnas-skabs #  dang nyon-mongs-pa # 'i bag-chags #  ni sangs-rgyas #  kyi sa'i sgrib-pa #  zhes bya ste /
tasmAt sOkzmya prakarzAt anyaTA prekzitum na Sakyate iti evam AKyAnam / Bavati
# de-bas-na #  shin-tu-phra-ba # 'i phyir gzhan-du #  brtag mi-nus-pa # s de-skad #  ces bshad-pa # r 'gyur ro /
AvaraNa piNXa arTaH / mahA varaNam yat vyApi kleSa jQeya AvaraNam boDisattva gotrANAm
# sgrib-pa #  chen-po #  ni khyab-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni bya-ba #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i rigs can rnams kyi nyon-mongs-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa # 'o /
pratanvAvaraNam prAdeSikam kleSa AvaraNam eva SrAvaka Adi gotrANAm
# sgrib-pa #  chung-ngu #  ni nyi-tshe-ba #  gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rigs can rnams kyi nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  nyid do /
prayoga AvaraNam yat udriktam iti tezAm eva rAga Adi caritAnAm tEH
# sbyor-ba # 'i sgrib-pa #  ni lhag-ma #  gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  spyod-pa #  de-dag-nyid #  kyi ste /
prayogA aprApteH
# des sbyor-ba #  nyid mi 'thob po /
prApti AvaraNam yat samam iti sama BAga caritAnAm tat hi prApti vibanDe
# 'thob-pa #  la sgrib-pa #  ni mnyam-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni cha mtshungs-pa # r spyod-pa #  rnams kyi ste; de 'thob-pa # 'i bgegs su 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
vartate / prApti viSeza AvaraNam yat AdAna vivarjane iti boDisattva gotrANAm
# thob-pa #  khyad-par-can #  la sgrib-pa #  ni len-pa #  dang spong-ba #  gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i rigs can rnams kyi ste /
aDigama viSeza AvaraNa tvAt
# thob-par-bya-ba #  khyad-par-can #  la sgrib-pa # 'i phyir ro /
apratizWitam nirvANam aDigama viSezaH
# mi-gnas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  ni thob-par-bya-ba #  khyad-par-can #  te /
eza ca eva Pala viSezaH veditavyAH
# de nyid 'bras-bu # 'i khyad-par #  du yang rig-par-bya # 'o /
samyak prayoga AvaraNam yat navaDA kleSa lakzaNam iti nava / saMyojanAni AvaraNam iti vacanAt
# yang-dag-par-sbyor-ba #  la sgrib-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  rnam-pa #  dgu gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni kun du sbyor-ba #  dgu ni sgrib po zhes bshad-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tAni samyak prayogasya AvaraNam Bavanti yaTA taTA uktam
# de-dag #  yang-dag-par-sbyor-ba #  la ji-ltar #  sgrib-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  bshad-zin #  to /
hetu AvaraNam yat SuBa AdO daSaviDet vaDi kArAt iti
# rgyu la sgrib-pa #  ni dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  rnams pa bcu la sgrib-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  ste /
tat hi SuBa Adi hetu vibanDa dvAreNa AvaraNam Bavanti iti hetu AvaraNam ucyate
# rgyu'i don gyi skabs kyi phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyu la gegs-byed-pa # 'i sgo nas sgrib-pa # r 'gyur-ba # s rgyu la sgrib-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
tattva pravezA AvaraNam yat boDi pakzyezu iti / tEH hi tattvam praviSati
# de-kho-na #  la 'jug-pa #  la sgrib-pa #  ni byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  rnams la sgrib-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-dag #  gis de-kho-na #  la 'jug-pa # r byed do /
SuBa anuttarya AvaraNam yat pAramitAsu tatas uttari SuBa aBAvAt
# dge-ba #  bla-na-med-pa #  la sgrib-pa #  ni / / pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams la sgrib-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni de'i bla na dge-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tat viSeza gati AvaraNam yat BUmizu iti pAramitAH eva hi / loka uttara viSeza ASraya BUtAH BUmayaH ucyante
# de khyad-par-du-'gro-ba #  la sgrib-pa #  ni sa rnams la sgrib-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la / / pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  nyid 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i khyad-par #  gyi gnas-su-gyur-pa #  ni sa rnams zhes-bya'o #  /
saFgraha AvaraNam yat samAsatas dviviDam iti kleSa AvaraNam / jQeya AvaraNaQcaH etena sarva AvaraNa saFgrahAt / piNXa arTa vacanam suKa udgrahaNa DAraNa arTam / piNXIkRtam hi suKam udgRhyate DAryate ca iti / Agama anusAriNyAm mADyanta viBAga wIkAyAm AcArya BadantasTi / ramati vyAKyAtAyAm AvaraNa paricCedaH dvitIyaH samAptaH / tattva paricCedaH tRtIyaH / p / AvaraNa nirdeSa anantaram tattva nirdeSa avasaraH tat anantaram uddizwa tvAt / iti atas tattvam aDikRtya Aha iti Aha
# bsdus-pa # 'i sgrib-pa #  ni mdor-bsdus-pa #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  po gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  ste / / de-dag #  gis sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  bsdus-pa # 'i phyir ro / / des bde blag tu len-pa-dang-'dzin #  par bya-ba # 'i phyir don bsdus-pa #  bshad do / / bsdu-ba #  byas-pa # s bde blag tu len to / / 'dzin to / / bstan-bcos #  dbus dang mtha' rnam-par-'byed-pa #  las sgrib-pa # 'i le'ur bcad-pa #  ste gnyis-pa # 'i 'grel bshad do / / sgrib-pa #  bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  de-kho-na #  bshad-pa # 'i skabs yin te / / de'i-'og-tu #  smos-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-bas-na #  de-kho-na # 'i dbang du mdzad de gsungs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tattvasya ca bahuviDa tvam vidyate / atas tad Bedana vaboDe tattva svarUpam duravagamam iti atas tattva praBedam / eva adO pratipAdayan= Aha / mUla lakzaNa tattvam
# de-kho-na #  yang rnam-pa-du-ma #  yod de / / de'i-phyir #  de'i dbye-ba #  khong du-ma #  chud-pa # r de-kho-na # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo khong-du-chud-pa # r dka'-bas #  de'i-phyir #  de-kho-na # 'i dbye-ba #  nyid dang-por #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / rtsa ba mtshan-nyid #  de-kho-na #  /
iti vistareNa daSaviDam tattvam / tatra mUla tattve anya tattva antar BAva sandarSana arTam mUla tattva vacanam
# zhes de-kho-na #  bcu rgya-cher #  gsungs so / / kha-cig #  na re rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  de-la #  de-kho-na #  gzhan 'dus-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  bshad do /
mUla tattve parijQAna prahANa sAkzAt karaNa samprayuktasya / doza prahANa arTam lakzaNa tattva vacanam
# rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  la yongs-su-shes-pa # r byed-pa #  dang spong-ba #  dang mngon-sum-du-byed-pa #  la zhugs-pa # 'i nyes-pa #  gzhom-pa # 'i phyir mtshan-nyid #  kyi de-kho-na #  bshad do /
saMsArAt udvega upAya pradarSana arTam aviparyAsa tattva vacanam
# 'khor-ba #  la skyo-bar-bya-ba # 'i thabs rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  bshad do /
udvignasya SrAvaka yAna niryANa sandarSana arTam Pala hetu tattva vacanam
# skyo nas nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa # s nges-par-'byung-ba #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir 'bras-bu #  dang rgyu'i de-kho-na #  bshad do /
SrAvakaH hi catur Arya satya prativeDa BAvanAByAm niryAti / sarva AkAra jQAna pratipatti upAya sandarSana arTam OdArika tattva vacanam / sarva varaNa prahANa upAya sandarSana arTam sUkzma tattva vacanam / suvyavasTita Darma nirdeSa upAya sandarSana arTam sarva para pravAdi nigraha upAya sandarSana arTan ca prasidDa tattva vacanam / same api DarmaDAtO p
# nyan-thos #  ni 'phags-pa'i-bden-pa-bzhi #  rab-tu-rtogs-pa #  dang bsgom-pa #  gnyis kyis nges-par #  'byung ngo / / rnam-pa-thams-cad #  shes-pa #  bsgrub-pa # 'i thabs bstan-pa # 'i phyir rags-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  bshad do / / sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  spang-pa # 'i thabs bstan-pa # 'i phyir phra-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  bshad do / / legs-par-gnas-pa # 'i chos-bstan-pa # 'i thabs bstan-pa #  dang phas-kyi-rgol-ba #  thams-cad #  tshar-gcod-pa # 'i thabs bstan-pa # 'i phyir grags-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  bshad do /
gotra indriya ASaya Bedena viSudDi Beda sandarSana arTam / viSudDi gocara tattva vacanam
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  su mtshungs kyang rigs dang dbang-po #  dang bsam-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis rnam-par-dag-pa #  tha-dad-pa #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i spyod yul gyi de-kho-na #  bshad do /
sarva AkAra saFkleSa vyavadAna praveSa upAya sandarSana arTam / saFgraha tattva vacanam
# rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  la 'jug-pa # 'i thabs bstan-pa # 'i phyir bsdu-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  bshad do /
taTatAm AraBya sarva sandeha vinirvartana sAmarTya sandarSana arTam / praBeda tattva vacanam / sarva prakAra Atma grAham nivartya
# de-bzhin-nyid #  las brtsams te som nyi thams-cad #  rnam-pa # r ldog-pa # 'i mthu bstan-pa # 'i phyir rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  bshad do / / bdag-tu-'dzin-pa #  rnam-pa-thams-cad #  bzlog-ste #  /
nErAtmya vyavasTAna sAmarTya nandana arTam kOSalya tattva vacanam iti
# bdag-med-pa #  rab tu gzhag-pa # 'i thabs bstan-pa # 'i phyir mkhas-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  bshad do zhe'o /
anye punar AhuH mUla tattvam boDisattvasya asADAraNam
# gzhan dag na re rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i ste / / thun-mong-ma-yin-pa # 'o /
tatra eva miTyA prayoga pratipakza tvAt dvitIyam
# de-kho-na #  gnyis-pa #  ni de-nyid-la #  log-pa # r sbyor-ba # 'i gnyen-pa # 'o /
samyak yoga anukUla tattvam tRtIyam
# de-kho-na #  gsum-pa #  ni yang-dag-pa # 'i rnal-'byor #  dang mthun-pa # 'o /
SrAvaka pratyekabudDa sADAraNa tattvam caturTam
# de-kho-na #  bzhi-ba #  ni nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  dang mthun-pa # 'o /
partipatyi upAya tattvam paQcamam
# de-kho-na #  lnga pa ni sgrib-pa # 'i thabs so /
loka sADAraNa tattvam zazWam
# de-kho-na #  drug-pa #  ni 'jig-rten #  dang thun mong ngo /
tat asADAraNa tattvam saptamam
# de-kho-na #  bdun pa ni de dang thun mong pa yin pa'o /
jQeya samAsa tattvam azwamam
# de-kho-na #  brgyad pa ni shes-bya #  mdor bsdu-ba # 'o /
prakRti tattvam navamam
# de-kho-na #  dgu pa ni rang-bzhin #  no /
saFkleSa mUla nirGAtana tattvam daSamam iti
# de-kho-na #  bcu pa ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rtsa ba 'joms pa'o zhe'o /
etAni samAsatas daSa tattvAni taTAgatAnAm / sarva aBisanDi vacana ASraya BUtam / vistareNa tattvam aprayem / atra tat tvA nukUlyAt saMvRtiH api tattvam iti uktam iti eke / sarvANi eva etAni yahoktEH prakArEH avisamvAdAt tattvAni iti anye / yadi enaprakAreNa na visamvadati tat taTA tattvam iti kRtvA / mUla tattvam
# mdor-bsdus-pa #  de-kho-na #  bcu po de-dag #  ni de-bzhin-gshegs-pa #  rnams kyis ldem-po # r dgongs-te-gsungs-pa # 'i gnas su gyur ba'o / / rgyas-pa # r bya na de-kho-na #  dpag tu med do / / kha-cig #  na re 'di-la #  de-kho-na #  dang mthun-pa # s kun-rdzob #  kyang de-kho-na #  zhes bstan zhe'o / / gzhan dag na re de-dag #  thams-cad #  ni ji-skad #  bshad-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  rnams kyis mi bslu-ba # 'i phyir de-kho-na #  rnams zhes-bya-ba #  ste / / gang rnam-pa #  gang-gis #  slu-bar-mi-byed-pa #  de ni de-bzhin #  bas de-kho-na #  zhes-bya'o #  zhe'o /
tatra mUla tattvam / svaBAvaH triviDaH / iti etat aprasidDam iti atas Aha parikalpitaH paratantraH parinizpannaH / ca iti / yena p
# de-la #  rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  ni ngo-bo-nyid #  rnam-pa-gsum #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  de ma grags-pa # s de'i-phyir #  / / kun-brtags-pa #  dang gzhan gyi dbang dang yongs-su-grub-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
kAraNena svaBAvaH triviDaH mUla tattvam iti ucyate tat pradarSayan= Aha / tatra anya tattva vyavasTApanAt iti
# ci'i-phyir #  ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum la rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  zhes brjod can / / de rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir de-la #  de-kho-na #  gzhan rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
tatra anyasya lakzaNa Adi tattvasya antargata tvam iti arTaH
# der mtshan-nyid #  la-sogs-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  gzhan 'dus so zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
kim arTam svaBAvaH triviDaH upaDAryate
# ci'i-phyir #  ngo-bo-nyid #  rnam-pa-gsum #  nye-bar #  gzung zhe na /
vyavahAra paramArTa tat ASraya pradarSana arTam iti eke
# kha-cig #  na re tha-snyad #  dang don-dam-pa #  dang de'i-gnas #  rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro zhe'o /
viparyAsa tad nimitta tad pratipakza Alambana pradarSana arTam iti anye
# gzhan dag na re phyin-ci-log #  dang de'i rgyud dang de'i gnyen-po # 'i dmigs-pa #  rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro zhe'o /
boDisattvAnAm AvaraNa visaMyoga arTam prahANa parijQA sAkzAt / kriyA vastu pradarSana arTam iti anye
# gzhan dag na re byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi sgrib-pa-dang-bral-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir spang-ba #  dang yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba #  dang mngon-sum-du-bya-ba # 'i dngos-po #  rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro zhe'o /
prakRtyAH gamBIrasya prajQApAramitA rUpasya / tri svaBAva dvAreNa aBrAnti pratipatti arTam iti anye / evam hi uktam aBiDarma putra grAha dvaye
# gzhan dag na re shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i tshul rang-bzhin-gyis #  zab-pa #  ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum gyi sgo nas ma nor-ba # r rtogs-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro zhe'o / / de-skad #  du chos-mngon-pa # 'i mdo'i nang nas tshigs-su-bcad-pa #  gnyis las /
mAyA Adi deSanAm BUte kalpitAn na asti deSanA
# byung rten sgyu-ma #  la sogs bstan / / rtags la brten-nas #  med-pa #  bstan /
caturviDa viSudDeH tu parinizpanna deSanA
# rnam dag rnam-pa-bzhi # r brten-nas #  / / yongs-su-grub-pa #  bstan-pa #  yin /
SudDiH prakRti vEmalyam na Argata Alambanan taTA / viSudDAnAm hi DarmANAm caturDA grahaNam matam iti
# dag-pa #  de ni rang-bzhin #  dang / / dri-ma #  med dang lam dang dmigs / / rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i chos kyi rnams / / rnam-pa-bzhi-po # s bsdus-pa #  yin / / zhes gsungs so / / byung-ba #  gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  la ltos nas mdo las sgyu-ma #  la-sogs-pa #  bstan te / / de ni sgyu-ma #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  log-pa # r snang-ba # 'i phyir ro / / med-pa #  kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  la ltos nas med-pa #  bstan to / / rnam-par-dag-pa #  rnam-pa-bzhi #  la ltos nas yongs-su-grub-pa # r bstan to / / rnam-par-dag-pa #  rnam-pa-bzhi #  la rang-bzhin-gyis #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  ni dri-ma #  dang bcas-pa # 'i dus kyi de-bzhin-nyid #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / dri-ma-med-pa # s rnam-par-dag-pa #  ni de-dag-nyid #  dri-ma-med-pa # 'i dus na'o / / stong-pa-nyid #  la-sogs-pa #  'thob-pa # 'i lam rnam-par-dag-pa #  ni byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / lam skyed-pa # 'i phyir dmigs-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  kyi rgyu-mthun-pa #  bstan-pa # 'i chos mdo'i-sde #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / de-la #  brten-nas #  lam skye-ba # 'i phyir ro / / 'di-ltar #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  'di bzhis rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i chos-thams-cad #  bsdus te tshigs-su-bcad-pa #  gnyis kyi don-mdor-bsdus-pa # 'o /
lOkika lokottara tad pRzWa labDa jQAna vizaya tva pradarSana arTam / yaTAsamBavam traya upAdAnam svaBAvatam iti anye
# gzhan dag na re 'jig-rten-pa #  dang 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  dang de'i-rjes-la # s thob-pa # 'i ye shes kyi yul yin par rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir ci-rigs-par #  ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum gzung ngo zhe'o /
kim atra svaBAva traye tattvam izyate iti / aviparIta arTaH hi tattva arTaH
# ci'i-phyir #  'dir ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum la de-kho-na #  zhas bya-ba # r 'dod ce na zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-kho-na'i-don #  ni ma nor-ba # 'i don yin na /
kim atra svaBAva traye aviparIta tvam iti yasmAt svaBAva traye tattvam / izyate iti pRcCA aBiprAyaH
# ci'i-phyir #  'dir ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum la ma nor-ba #  zhes bya / / 'di-ltar #  ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum la de-kho-na #  zhes bya snyam-du #  dri-ba # r bsams-pa # 'o /
svaBAvaH triviDaH asat ca nityam / ityAdi vistaraH
# ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum rtag med ces bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  rgya-cher #  smos-pa #  la /
parikalpita lakzaNam nityam asat iti yatra hi bAlAnAm
# kun du brtags-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni rtag-tu #  med-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
grAhya grAhaka vAcya vAcaka aBiniveSaH svapne iva pravartate / asat ca sa svarUpa aBAvAt kalpita svaBAvaH
# gang-la #  byis-pa #  rnams kyis gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  dang smra-ba #  dang smra-ba # r bya-ba # r mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i rmi-lam #  ltar rab-tu-'byung-ba #  de ni rang-gi #  ngo bor med-pa # 'i phyir brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  do /
tasmAt asat Atmaka tvAt aBra antvAt ca parikalpita lakzaNam asattvam
# de'i-phyir #  med-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin pa dang 'khrul-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir med-pa #  nyid kun-brtags-pa'i-mtshan-nyid #  do /
etat parikalpita svaBAve asattvam eva tattvam ucyate
# de'i-phyir #  kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  la med-pa #  nyid kyi de-kho-na #  zhes brjod do /
aviparIta tvAt iti aviparIta arTaH atra tattva arTam iti darSayati / paratantra lakzaNam sat ca na ca tattvataH iti
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i don ni 'dor de-kho-na'i-don #  du ston to / / gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan-nyid #  ni yod kyang yang-dag-par #  na ma yin te zhes-bya-ba #  la /
grAhya grAhaka Adi kalpita vyavahAra ASraya tvAt sattvam
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  brtags-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  de tha-snyad #  kyi gnas yin-pas #  yod do /
grAhya grAhaka Adi Atmaka tvena asattvAt na taTA tattvataH iti
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  du med-pa # s yang-dag-par #  na de-bzhin-du #  ma yin no /
etat eva pratipAdayan= Aha BrAnti mAtra tvAt iti
# de nyid bstan-pa # 'i phyir 'khrul-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
etat uktam Bavati yat KyAti mAyA upAdAna vat tat asti
# de ni 'di-skad-du #  sgyu-ma # 'i rgyu ltar snang-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni yod do /
yaTA KyAti grAhya grAhaka AkAreNa na etat eva mAyA puruza Adi vat / atas BrAntiH iti
# ji-ltar #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r snang-ba #  de ni de lta ma yin te / / sgyu-ma # 'i skyes-bu #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin no / / de'i-phyir #  'khrul-pa #  zhes bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro /
iti etat paratantra svaBAve tattvam anyaTA vidyamAnasya sva Atmani / avidyamAnena AkAreNa praKyAnam / atra api aviparIta tvAt iti prakRta tvAt sambaDyate p / parinizpanna lakzaNam sat asat tattvataH ca iti
# de ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  la de-kho-na #  ste / / gzhan-du #  yod-pa #  bdag-nyid #  la med-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r snang ngo / / skabs yin-pas #  'dir yang phyin ci ma log go zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro / / yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni / / yod dang med-pa #  kho-na #  ste /
sat asat ca tattvam parinizpanna lakzaNam
# zhes-bya-ba #  ni yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  dang de-kho-na #  ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  de /
dvayA aBAva BAva Atmaka tvAt sattvam
# gnyis-pa #  med-pa #  yod-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin-pas #  yod-pa # s so /
dvayA aBAva Atmaka tvAt asattvaQca
# gnyis po med-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin-pas #  med-pa # 'o /
viSudDi Alambana tvAt tattvam
# rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  yin-pas #  de-kho-na # 'o /
etat parinizpanne svaBAve tattvam / aviparIta tvAt iti sambaDyate / lakzaNa tattvam
# 'dir ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  la de-kho-na #  ste / / phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  dang sbyor ro /
svaBAva trayasya tattvam uktam na tu lakzaNam iti atas pRcCati
# ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum gyi de-kho-na #  ni bshad na / / mtshan-nyid #  ma bshad de /
aTavA mUla tat tvA nantaram lakzaNa tattvam uktam tat ca
# de'i-phyir #  dris-pa # 'am yang-na #  rtsa ba'i de-kho-na # 'i 'og-tu #  mtshan-nyid #  kyi de-kho-na #  bshad la /
pRcCati lakzaNa tattvam katamat iti
# de-yang #  ma grags-pa # s na mtshan-nyid #  kyi de-kho-na #  gang zhe na zhes dris te /
atas Aha / samAropA apavAdasya Darma pudgalayoH iha / iti vistaraH
# de'i-phyir #  / / 'di-la #  chos dang gang-zag #  dang / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
pudgala DarmayoH samAropA apavAda darSanam yasya jQAnAt na pravartate / tat parikalpita svaBAve tattva lakzaNam iti
# gang shes-nas #  gang-zag #  dang chos gnyis la sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-par #  lta-ba #  mi-'byung-ba #  de ni kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi de-kho-na'i-mtshan-nyid #  do zhes-bya-ba #  la /
Atma rUpa AdayaH ca DarmAH tat pratiBAsa vijQAna vyatiriktasya / tad Alambana BUtAH paramArTataH santi iti aBiniveSaH samAropadarSanam
# bdag dang gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  de-dag #  tu snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ma-gtogs-par #  de'i dmigs-pa # r gyur-pa #  don-dam-pa # r yod do zhes mngon-par-zhen-pa #  ni sgro-'dogs-pa # r lta-ba # 'o /
vyavahAra arTaH api na santi iti apavAda darSanam
# tha-snyad #  du yang med do zhes-bya-ba #  ni skur-pa-'debs-par #  lta-ba # 'o /
anyaH AhuH / pudgala Darma pratiBAsa vijQAna parihAraH apavAda darSanam iti / grAhA apakzepaH iti cintyam etat
# gzhan dag na re gang-zag #  dang chos su snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  spong-ba #  ni skur-pa-'debs-par #  lta-ba # 'o zhes zer te / / 'dzin-pa #  spong-ba #  'di ni bsam dgos-pa # 'o /
pudgala DarmayoH samAropA apavAda darSanam yasya lakzaNasya paricCedAt na / pravartate tat parikalpita svaBAve tattva lakzaNam samAropa apavAda varjitam / veditavyam / tat ca vyavahAreNa tattvam na tu svaBAvena yasmAt
# mtshan-nyid #  gang yongs su gcad-pa # s gang-zag #  dang chos gnyis la sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-par #  lta-ba #  de ni kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi de-kho-na'i-mtshan-nyid #  de / / sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur ba 'debs-pa #  spangs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / de'ang tha-snyad #  du de-kho-na #  yin gyi ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  ni ma yin no /
parikalpitA avaboDAt Darma pudgalayoH samAropa apavAda darSanam na / pravartate
# gang-gi-phyir #  kun-brtags-pa #  khong du chung na gang-zag #  dang chos gnyis la sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-par #  lta-ba #  mi-'byung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mi skye'i zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
na jAyate iti arTaH / grAhya grAhakayoH samAropa apavAda darSanam iti vistaraH
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  gnyis la sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-par #  lta-ba #  zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  la /
grAhya grAhaka pratiBAsa BrAntiH yA DarmeNa pudgalena ca gRhyate sA / yadi tattvena eva asti iti aBiniviSate evam grAhya grAhaka samAropaH
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r snang-ba # 'i 'khrul-pa #  gang-la #  chos dang gang-zag #  tu 'dzin-pa #  de gal-te #  kho-na #  nyid-du #  yod do zhes mngon-pa # r zhen na de-la #  bu ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r sgro-'dogs-pa # 'o /
aTa grAhyasya iva grAhaksya api aBAvam aBiniviSate evam / grAhya grAhaka apavAdaH
# ji ste gzung-ba #  bzhin-du #  'dzin-pa #  yang med do zhes mngon-pa # r zhen na / / de-lta-bu #  ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  la skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'o /
yasya lakzaNasya jQAnAt grAhya grAhakayoH samAropA apavAda darSanam na / pravartate tat paratantra svaBAve tattva lakzaNam samAropa apavAda varjitam / jQAtavyam / tat punar kalpitayA grAhya grAhaka AtmatayA asattvam tat
# mtshan-nyid #  gang shes-nas #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  gnyis la sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-par #  lta-ba # r mi-'byung-ba #  de ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  de / / sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-pa #  spangs-pa # r shes-pa # r bya'o / / de-yang #  brtags-pa #  ste gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  du med-pa # 'o /
vyavahAra ASraya tvena ca sattvam
# de'i tha-snyad #  kyi gnas yin pa'i phyir yod-pa # 'o /
evam hi parijQAnAt p / paratantre samAropA apavAda darSanam na pravartate
# de-ltar #  yongs su shes na gzhan gyi dbang la sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-par #  lta-ba #  mi 'byung ngo /
BAvA aBAva samAropa apavAda darSanam iti vistaraH / kecid AhuH yadi SUnyatAm BAvaH eva iti samanupaSYati evam
# dngos-po #  dang dngos-po-med-pa # r sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-par #  lta-ba #  zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  la kha-cig #  na re / / gal-te #  stong-pa-nyid #  dngos-po-yod-pa #  nyid do zhes yang-dag-par #  rjes su lta na /
BAva samAropa darSanam Bavati / aTa aBAvaH eva iti evam aBAva darSanam / etat uBayam api BAva aBAva darSanam / yasya lakzaNasya jQAnAt na te BAva aBAva darSane pravartete tat
# de lta ni dngos-po # r sgro-'dogs-pa # r lta-ba # r 'gyur ro / / ji ste med-pa #  nyid do zhe na / / de-lta-bu #  ni dngos-po-med-pa # r lta-ba # 'o / / mtshan-nyid #  gang shes-nas #  dngos-po #  dang dngos-po-med-pa # r lta-ba #  de gnyis mi-'byung-ba #  ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi de-kho-na'i-mtshan-nyid #  do /
parinizpanna svaBAve tattva lakzaNam iti / tat ca BAvA aBAva avimukta svaBAvam
# kha-cig #  na re de-yang #  dngos-po #  dang dngos-po-med-pa #  las rnam-par-grol-ba # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  yin la /
tat jQAnAt hi parinizpanne svaBAve BAvA aBAva pradarSanam na / pravartate iti eke
# de shes-nas #  yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  la dngos-po #  dang dngos-po-med-pa # r lta-ba #  mi 'byung ngo zhe'o /
anye punar AhuH dvaya aBAva svarUpa eva SUnyatA iti aBAva samAropAntaH / BAvA aBAva vimukta Atmaka tve BAva svarUpa samAropaNAt / BAvA aBAva vimuktena dvayA BAva svarUpeNa / nirvikalpa jQAna gocareNa asO= na asti iti aBAva vAda antaH
# gzhan na re dngos-po #  dang dngos-po-med-pa #  las rnam-par-grol-ba # 'i bdag-nyid-can #  la / / dngos-po # 'i ngo bor sgro-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir gnyis po med-pa #  ni rang-gi #  ngo bos stong-pa-nyid #  do zhe na / / dngos-po # r sgro-'dogs-pa # 'i mthar 'gyur ro / / de dngos-po #  dang dngos-po-med-pa #  las rnam-par-grol-ba #  gnyis-su-med-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyi spyod yul du yang med do zhe na / / dngos-po-med-pa # r skur ba 'debs-pa # 'i mthar 'gyur ro zhes zer ro /
BAvA aBAvayoH pratyekam samAropA apavAda darSanasya aBisambanDAt / cintyam etat vyAKyAna advayam iti aparaH
# gzhan na re dngos-po #  dang dngos-po-med-pa #  gnyis la so-so # r sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-par #  lta-ba #  dang sbyar-ba # s bshad-pa #  'di gnyis kyang bsam dogs-pa # 'o zhe'o /
BAvaH atra dvayA aBAvasya BAvaH
# 'dir dngos-po #  ni gnyis po med-pa # 'i dngos-po #  ste /
tam yadi BAvam eva gRhNAti evam BAvaH samAropitaH Bavati
# gal-te #  de-la #  dngos-po #  nyid-du #  'dzin na de lta na ni dngos-po # r sgro-'dogs-pa # r 'gyur ro /
yadi aBAvam eva gRhNAti evam apoditaH Bavati
# ji ste dngos-po-med-pa-nyid #  du 'dzin na de lta na ni skur-pa-'debs-par #  'gyur ro /
BAvaH api dvaya aBAva sTam yadi ucCedataH gRhNAti evam / BAvaH atyanta aBAva tvena samAropitaH Bavati
# 'dir ni dngos-po-med-pa #  na ni gnyis po'i dngos-po-med-pa #  ste / / gal gte de-la #  chad-pa #  nyid-du #  na de lta na ni dngos-po-med-pa # 'ang shin-tu #  med-pa #  nyid pas sgro-'dogs-pa # r 'gyur ro /
aTa dvayataH eva gRhNAti evam apoditaH Bavati yasmAt etat dvaya aBAvena / praBAvitam
# ji ste gnyis po nyid-du #  'dzin na de lta na ni skur-pa # r 'gyur te / / 'di-ltar #  de ni gnyis kyi dngos-po-med-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba #  yin no /
aTavA tam BAvA aBAva svarUpeNa gRhNAti evam samAropitaH Bavati / aTa aBAvam eva gRhNAti evam saMkleSaH vyavadAnaQcA apoditam / etat anta dvaya viDAtanam parinizpanna tve tattva lakzaNam / nanu pUrvam api tri svaBAva lakzaNam uktam / arTAt aBUta kalpAt ca dvaya aBAvAt ca deSitaH iti / tatra svaBAvaH lakzaNam iha tu cihnam iti na asti punarukta tA / yat jQAnAt na pravarteta tat hi tattvasya lakzaNam
# yang-na #  gal-te #  dngos-po # 'i ngo bor 'dzin na de lta na ni sgro-btags-pa # r 'gyur ro / / ji ste dngos-po-med-pa-nyid #  du 'dzin na de lta na ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  la yang skur-pa #  'gyur te / / mtha'-gnyis #  spangs-pa #  'di ni yongs-su-grub-pa #  nyid kyi de-kho-na'i-mtshan-nyid #  do / / don phyir-yang #  dag min rtogs phyir / / gnyis po med-pa # 'i phyir bshad do / / zhes ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum gyi mtshan-nyid #  sngar yang bshad ma zin na ma zhe na / / der ni ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  do / / 'dir ni gang shes-nas #  mi-'byung-ba #  de ni de-kho-na'i-mtshan-nyid #  do /
iti pudgala Adi samAropa apavAda darSanam yat jQAnAt na pravartate tat / mUla tattvasya lakzaNam
# zhes-bya-ba # 'i mtshan-ma #  yin-pas #  zlog-pa #  med do / / gang shes-nas #  gang-zag #  la-sogs-pa # r sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-par #  lta-ba #  mi-'byung-ba #  de ni rtsa ba'i de-kho-na'i-mtshan-nyid #  do /
aviparyAsa tattvam p / lakzaNa tattva anantaram aviparyAsa tattvam vaktavyam tat anantaram / uddizwa tvAt iti atas Aha aviparyAsa tattvam iti vistaraH
# de'i-'og-tu #  bshad-pa # 'i phyir mtshan-nyid #  kyi de-kho-na # 'i 'og-tu #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  brjod-pa # r bya ste / / de'i-phyir #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  ni zhes bya cher smos so /
anitya duHKa SUnyA Atma tas hi / nitya suKa SudDa Atma viparyAsa pratipakza tvAt aviparyAsa tattva tvam iti ucyate
# mi-rtag-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  dang stong-pa #  dang bdag-med-pa #  ni rtag-pa #  dang bde-ba #  dang gtsang ba dang bdag tu phyin-ci-log-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  yin-pas #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  zhes-bya'o #  /
mUla tattve tat anyat tvA antarBAvaH pUrvam pratijQAtaH iti atas pRcCati
# rtsa ba'i de-kho-na # 'i nang-du #  de-kho-na #  gzhan 'dus so zhes sngar dam-bcas-pa # s de'i-phyir #  /
mUla tattve kaTam iti vistaraH
# rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  der ji-ltar #  zhen zhes rgya-cher #  dris so /
anityAt iti eti / anitya AdayaH ye anitya duHKa SUnyA Atma prakArAH te anitya AdayaH
# mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  nyid ces bya-ba #  ni mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  gang dag yin pa mi-rtag-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  dang stong-pa #  dang bdag-med-pa'i-rnam-pa #  de-dag #  mi-rtag-pa #  la sgos-pa # 'o /
tat BAvaH anitya Adi tA
# de'i dngos-po #  ni mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  nyid do /
mUla tattve aviparyAsa tattvasya antar BAva pradarSana arTam Aha
# rtsa ba'i de-kho-na # 'i nang-du #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  'dus-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
asat arTaH hi anitya arTa / iti vistaraH
# mi rtag don ni med don dang / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
triviDaH hi anitya arTaH asadarTaH utpAda vyArTaH samala amala tA arTaH / ca
# mi-rtag-pa'i-don #  ni rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / med-pa # 'i don dang skye zhing 'jig-pa # 'i don dang dri-ma #  dang bcas shing dri-ma-med-pa # 'i don do /
yaH sarvadA taTA asti sa nityaH
# gang-du # s thams-cad-du #  de-bzhin-du #  yod-pa #  de ni rtag-pa #  ste /
tat viparItaH anityaH
# de-las-bzlog-pa #  ni mi-rtag-pa #  ste /
tezu yaTAkramam iti / tatra sarvadA asat arTA anitya arTena parikalpita svaBAvaH anityaH
# de-dag #  tu go-rims #  bzhin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-la #  dus-thams-cad-du #  med-pa # 'i don mi-rtag-pa'i-don #  gyis kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  ni mi-rtag-pa # 'o /
asat nityam anityam iti nirutti nyAyena veditavyam iti anye
# gzhan dag na re nges-pa'i-tshig #  gi tshul du na rtag-pa #  med-pa #  ni mi-rtag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o zhe'o /
pratikzaNam utpAda vyaha lakzaNena anitya arTena anityaH paratantra svaBAvaH
# gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  ni skad-cig-re-re-la #  skye zhing 'jig-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  yin te / / mi-rtag-pa # 'i phyir mi-rtag-pa # 'o /
tasya pratyaya utpAdya tvAt vinASe ca ahetuka tvAt / samalAmalatA arTa lakzaNena Agantukena iti / parinizpanna svaBAvaH iti
# de ni rkyen las byung-ba #  dang 'jig-pa #  la rgyu-med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  mi 'gyur-pa # 'i chos yin-du-zin #  kyang dri-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  dang dri-ma-med-pa #  nyid kyi don gyi mtshan-nyid #  glo-bur #  gyi don mi-rtag-pa # 'o /
duHKam AdAna lakzma AKyam
# sdug-bsngal #  len dang mtshan-nyid #  dang /
iti vistaraH / duHKam api triviDam upAdAna duHKam lakzaNa duHKam sambanDa duHKaQca
# zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  la sdug-bsngal-ba #  la yang rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / nye-bar-len-pa # s sdug-bsngal-ba #  dang mtshan-nyid #  kyis sdug-bsngal-ba #  dang 'brel-ba # s sdug-bsngal-ba # 'o /
tatra kalpita svaBAvaH upAdAnataH duHKam
# de-la #  brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  ni nye-bar-len-pa # s sdug-bsngal #  te /
aparijQAtena iha amutra vA duHKam upAdIyate iti duHKam
# yongs-su-ma-shes-pa # s 'di'am gzhan na sdug-bsngal #  nye-bar-len-pa # s sdug-bsngal #  lo /
yaTA ca tena tena aparijQAtena duHKam upAdIyate tat pradarSayan= Aha
# ji-ltar #  na de yongs-su-ma-shes-pa # s sdug-bsngal #  nye-bar-len-pa #  de bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
pudgala Darma aBiniveSa upAdAnAt iti
# gang-zag #  dang chos la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
tat BAva grAha dvAreNa pudgala Darmam aBiniviSataH iti / pudgala Darma aBiniveSaH
# des dngos-po # r 'dzin-pa # 'i sgo nas gang-zag #  dang chos su mngon-par-zhen-pa # s na gang-zag #  dang chos la mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'o /
sa ca dvaya patita tvAt parikalpitaH svaBAvaH
# de-yang #  gnyis su lhung-ba # 'i phyir kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  de /
parikalpita svaBAvA aBiniveSAt duHKa prabanDaH iti evam uktam na punar
# kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  ni sdug-bsngal-gyi-rgyu # n gyi rgyu yin-pas #  de-skad #  bshad kyi /
parikalpitaH eva duHKam / tat aBAvAt
# kun-brtags-pa #  nyid ni sdug-bsngal #  ma yin te / / de med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aTavA parikalpita svaBAvaH pudgala Darma aBiniveSena
# yang-na #  kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  gang-zag #  dang chos la mngon-pa # r zhen nas dngos-po # 'i ngo bor nye-bar-len-pa #  ste /
vastu rUpeNa upAdIyate iti evam upAdAnataH kalpitaH svaBAvaH duHKam
# de-ltar #  nye-bar-len-pa # s brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  ni sdug-bsngal #  lo /
paratantraH svaBAvaH lakzaNataH duHKam iti sambaDyate / tisraH hi duHKa tA duHKa duHKa tA vipariNAmadaH KatA saMskAra duHKa tA / ca
# gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  ni mtshan-nyid #  kyi sdug-bsngal #  zhes-bya-ba #  dang sbyar ro / / mtshan-nyid #  kyi sdug-bsngal-ba #  ni sdug-bsngal #  nyid rnam-pa-gsum #  ste; sdug-bsngal-gyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid dang 'gyur-ba'i-sdug-bsngal #  nyid dang 'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid do /
tAH ca tisraH api duHKa tAH paratantra duHKa tAH iti lakzaNataH duHKam
# sdug-bsngal-rnam-pa-gsum #  po de-dag #  ni gzhan gyi dbang gi sdug-bsngal #  te / / mtshan-nyid #  kyi sdug-bsngal-ba # 'o /
parinizpannaH svaBAvaH sambanDataH duHKam
# yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  ni 'brel-pa # s sdug-bsngal-ba # 'o /
ca SabdaH samuccarya arTaH / kaTam sambanDataH
# yang zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni bsdu-ba # 'i don to / / ji lta zhe na / / 'brel-pa # 'i phyir te /
iti atas Aha duHKa sambanDAt iti
# de'i-phyir #  sdug-bsngal-dang-'brel-pa # 'i phyir bya-ba #  smos so /
paratantra svaBAvaH duHKam
# gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  ni sdug-bsngal #  te /
tat Darmasya parinizpannasya api duHKa sambanDAt duHKam ucyate
# de'i chos-nyid #  yongs-su-grub-pa #  yang sdug-bsngal-dang-'brel-pa # 'i phyir sdug-bsngal #  zhes-bya'o #  /
atra eva mUla tattve yaTAkramam iti tatra upAdAnataH duHKam parikalpitaH / lakzaNataH paratantraH
# rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  nyid kyi nang-du #  go-rims #  bzhin no zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  / / nye-bar-len-pa # s sdug-bsngal #  ni kun-brtags-pa # 'o / / mtshan-nyid #  kyis ni gzhan gyi dbang ngo /
sambanDataH parinizpannaH
# 'brel-pa # s ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'o /
aBAvaH ca api atadBAvaH prakRtiH SUnya tA matA iti
# dngos med de yi dngos ma yin / / rang-bzhin-gyis #  ni stong-pa # r 'dod / / ces bya-ba #  la stong-pa-nyid #  ni rnam-pa-gsum #  ste /
triviDA SUnyatA amAvaSUnyatA atadBAva SUnyatA prakRti SUnyatA / ca
# dngos-po-med-pa # s stong-pa-nyid #  dang de-ma-yin-pa # s stong-pa-nyid #  dang rang-bzhin-gyis #  stong-pa-nyid #  do /
tatra aBAva SUnyatA parikalpatasya svaBAvasya
# da la dngos-po-med-pa # s stong-pa-nyid #  ni kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  de /
etat pratipAdayan= Aha parikalpita lakzaNam p / SaSa vizANa Adi svarUpa vat BrAntyA na kenacid prakAreNa yena api sattvam / grAhyam na asti iti aBAvaH eva asya SUnyatA iti / atadBAva SUnya tA paratantrasya
# de nyid bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / kun-brtags-pa'i-mtshan-nyid #  ni ri-bong-gi-rva #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  ltar mngon-sum #  dang rjes-su-dpag-pa #  rnam-pa #  gang-gis #  kyang yod-pa # r gzung du med de / / dngos-po-med-pa-nyid #  pas de'i stong-pa-nyid #  do zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / de-ma-yin-pa # s stong-pa-nyid #  ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  de /
etat eva pratipAdayan= Aha paratantra lakzaNam taTA na asti yaTA / bAlEH dvaya AtmanA parikalpyate
# de nyid bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan-nyid #  ni ji-ltar #  byis-pa #  rnams kyis gnyis kyi bdag-nyid #  du kun-brtags-pa #  de-ltar #  med kyi /
na tu sarvaTA na asti yaTA ca a asti / SudDa lOkika jQAnena aDigamyate
# ji-ltar #  dag-pa #  'jig-rten-pa # 'i ye shes kyis rtog-pa # r 'gyur-pa #  lta-bu #  yang ye med-pa #  ni ma yin te /
tasyAH tad BAvaH SUnyatA iti
# de-bas-na #  de-ma-yin-pa # s de'i stong-pa-nyid #  do zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
prakRti SUnyatA parinizpannasya
# rang-bzhin-gyis #  stong-pa-nyid #  ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  de /
atas eva Aha parinizpanna lakzaNam dvaya aBAva svaBAva tvAt
# de'i-phyir #  yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni gnyis po med-pa # 'i dngos-po # 'i ri bo 'di yin pa'i phyir stong-pa-nyid #  kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  do /
CUnyatA svaBAvam eva iti / tasmAt prakRtiH eva svaBAvaH eva asya SUnyatA / alakzaNaQca nErAtmyam / iti vistaraH / triviDam nErAtmyam alkzaNanEH Atmyam vilakzaNa nErAtmyam / sva lakzaNa nErAtmya Qca / tatra parikalpitasya svaBAvasya lakzaNA aBAvAt alakzaNam eva / nErAtmyam / atas eva Aha parikalpitasya svaBAvasya lakzaNam eva na asti iti alakzaNam
# de-bas-na #  rang-bzhin #  kho-na #  ste ngo-bo-nyid #  kho-na # s de'i stong-pa-nyid #  do zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / mtshan-nyid-med-pa # s bdag med dang / / zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  la bdag-med-pa #  yang rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / mtshan-nyid-med-pa # s bdag-med-pa #  dang mi-mthun-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyis bdag-med-pa #  dang rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  kyis bdag-med-pa # 'o / / de-la #  kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  ni mtshan-nyid #  kyis dngos-po-med-pa # s mtshan-nyid-med-pa #  nyid bdag-med-pa #  ste /
eva asya nErAtmyam na anyena prakAreNa iti darSayati / paratantrasya vilakzaNanEH Atmyam yasmAt paratantrasya asti lakzaNam
# de'i-phyir #  kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  ni mtshan-nyid #  kyis med-pa # 'i phyir mtshan-nyid-med-pa #  nyid de'i bdag-med-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / rnam-pa #  gzhan gyis ni ma-yin-pa # r ston to / / gzhan gyi dbang ni mi-mthun-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyis bdag-med-pa #  ste /
vastu rUpam / na tu tat yaTA bAlEH parikalpyate dvaya tvena / tat vilakzaNam iti parikalpita lakzaNena asadRSam / paratantra lakzaNam tat nErAmyam
# 'di-ltar #  gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan-nyid #  ni dngos-po # 'i ngo bor yod kyang des byis-pa #  rnams kyis gnyis su ji-ltar #  kun-brtags-pa #  de-ltar #  ni yod-pa #  ma yin no / / de dang mi-mthun-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ces bya-ba #  ni kun-brtags-pa'i-mtshan-nyid #  dang mi-'dra-ba #  ste / / gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan-nyid #  de'i bdag-med-pa # 'o /
evam parikalpitena AtmanA nErAtmyam asya darSItam Bavati
# de-ltar-na #  kun-brtags-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyis #  de'i bdag-med-pa # r bstan-pa #  yin no /
sva lakzaNam nErAtmyam parinizpannasya
# rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  kyis bdag-med-pa #  ni yongs-su-grub-pa #  ste /
yatas parinizpannaH svaBAvaH grAhya grAhaka aBAva rUpa tvAt nErAtmyam / eva iti sva lakzaNam asya nErAtmyam iti parinizpannasya Darmasya / nErAtmya svaBAva tAm darSayati / kaH punar anayoH SUnyatA na Atma tayoH viSezaH
# 'di-ltar #  yongs-su-grub-pa #  ni ngo-bo-nyid #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i dngos-po-med-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  yin pa'i phyir bdag-nyid #  med-pa # s de-bas-na #  rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  de'i bdag-med-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i chos-la-bdag-med-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du ston to / / stong-pa-nyid #  dang bdag-med-pa #  'di gnyis la khyad-par #  ci yod ce na /
yadi atra na asti tat tena SUnyam
# kha-cig #  na re gang na gang med-pa #  de ni des stong la /
yat tu yasya AtmA svaBAvaH na Bavati tat tena tena na Atma iti ayam / iti eke
# gang zhig gang-gis #  bdag ste ngo-bo-nyid #  ma-yin-pa #  de ni bdag-med-pa #  ste / / 'di gnyis kyi khyad-par #  ni 'di yin no zhe'o /
arTataH kaH api viSezaH na asti vyavasTAna Bedena tu BedaH / yasmAt yat yatra na asti tena tasya niHsvaBAvatAm upAdAya nErAtmyam / itarasya tu tatra anizpanna svaBAva tAm upAdAya SUnya tvam iti p / triviDe mUla tattve samAropa apavAda antayoH / pratipakzeNa Agantu kamala pradarSanena ca yaTAkramam triviDA anitya tA
# kha-cig #  na re don-du #  khyad-par #  gang yang med mod kyi rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis tha dad de; 'di-ltar #  gang na gang med-pa #  des de'i-ngo-bo-nyid #  med-pa # 'i phyir bdag-med-pa #  dang cig shos ni de-la #  yongs-su-ma-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi phyir stong-pa-nyid #  do zhe'o / / sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i mtha'-gnyis #  kyi gnyen-po #  dang glo-bur-gyi-dri-ma #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  rnam-pa-gsum #  la go-rims-bzhin-du #  mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  rnam-pa-gsum #  yongs su bstan te /
paridIpitA / sA asat arTa anitya tA utpAda BaFgA anitya tA samala nirmalA anitya tA ca
# med-pa # 'i don mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  dang skye zhing 'jig-pa #  mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  dang dri-ma #  dang bcas shing dri-ma-med-pa # 'i mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  do /
evam yAvat triviDam nErAtmyam iti uktam aviparyAsa tattvam
# de-bzhin-du #  bdag-med-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  gyi bar-du #  bstan-pa #  ni phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i de-kho-na # 'o /
Pala hetu tattvam / tat anantaram Pala hetu tattvam vaktavyam iti atas Aha Pala hetum ayantattvam
# de'i-'og-tu #  'bras-bu #  dang rgyu'i de-kho-na #  brjod dgos te / / de'i-phyir #  'bras-bu #  dang rgyu'i de-kho-na #  nyid la zhes rgya-cher #  smos so /
mUla tattvam iti vistaraH / tatra saFkleSa pakzam aDikRtya duHKa satyam Pala tattvam
# de-la #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i phyogs kyi dbang du mdzad de / / sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  ni 'bras-bu # 'i de-kho-na # 'o /
samudaya satyam hetu tattvam vyavadAna pakze api niroDa satyam Pala tattvam
# kun 'byung gi bden-pa #  ni rgyu'i de-kho-na # 'o / / rnam-par-byang-ba'i-phyogs #  la yang 'gog-pa # 'i bden-pa #  ni 'bras-bu # 'i de-kho-na # 'o /
mArga satyam hetu tattvam
# lam gyi bden-pa #  ni rgyu'i de-kho-na # 'o /
evam duHKa AdIni catvAri satyAni Pala hetu tattvam
# de-ltar #  sdug-bsngal #  la-sogs-pa #  bden-pa-rnam-pa-bzhi #  ni 'bras-bu #  dang rgyu'i de-kho-na # 'o /
mUla tattve duHKa samudaya niroDa mArga satyam iti uktam
# rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  nyid la sdug-bsngal #  dang kun-'byung-ba #  dang 'gog-pa #  dang lam gyi bden-pa #  rnams so zhes bshad na /
tat ca na vijQAyate kaTam mUla tattvam duHKa Adi satya svaBAvam iti atas
# de-yang #  ji-ltar #  na rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  sdug-bsngal #  la-sogs-pa #  bden-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  yin pa mi shes na / / de'i-phyir #  /
pRcCati kaTam triviDam mUla tattvam duHKa Adi satyam iti / atas Aha yatas tat anitya Adi lakzaNam
# ji-ltar #  rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  rnam-pa-gsum #  la sdug-bsngal #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bden-pa #  zhes bya zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  dris-pa #  dang; de'i-phyir #  'di-ltar #  de mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyis te /
duHKa satyam tatas matam iti
# de'i-phyir #  sdug-bsngal #  bden-pa # r 'dod ces bya-ba #  smos te /
anitya duHKa SUnya anAtma tAyAH duHKa satya lakzaNa tvAt tat ca samastam / pratyekam kalpita Adizu asti iti vistareNa uktam
# mi-rtag-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  dang stong-pa #  dang bdag-med-pa #  nyid ni sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  pas de-dag #  thams-cad #  kun-brtags-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  re-re #  la yod-pa # r rgyas-pa # r bstan te /
atas kalpita AdayaH pratyekam duHKa satya tvena aBipretAH iti
# de'i-phyir #  kun-brtags-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  re-re #  la sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  nyid-du #  'dod do /
triviDena samudayA arTena mUla tattvam samudaya satyam yaTAkramam
# kun-'byung-ba # 'i don rnam-pa-gsum #  gyis rtsa ba'i de-kho-na # r kun-'byung-ba # 'i bden-pa # 'i go-rims #  bzhin no /
saH eva samudayaH na jQAyate iti atas Aha triviDaH samudaya arTaH
# kun-'byung-ba # 'i de nyid mi-shes-pa # s de'i-phyir #  / / kun-'byung-ba # 'i don rnam-pa-gsum #  ni /
vAsanA aTa samutTAnam avisaMyogaH eva ca iti
# bag-chags #  dang ni kun nas 'byung / / ma-bral-ba #  yang de-bzhin #  no / / zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
triviDaH samudayaH vAsanA samudayaH samutTAna samudayaH / avisaMyoga samudayaH ca
# rnam-pa-gsum #  ni bag-chags #  kyi kun-'byung-ba #  dang kun nas byung-ba # 'i kun-'byung-ba #  dang ma-bral-ba # 'i kun-'byung-ba # 'o /
tatra vAsanA samudayaH parikalpita svaBAvaH veditavyaH
# de-la #  bag-chags #  kyi kun-'byung-ba #  ni kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du shes-pa # r bya ste /
atas Aha parikalpita svaBAva aBiniveSa vAsanA iti
# de'i-phyir #  kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i bag-chags #  so zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
asti hi parikalpite svaBAve asti iti aBiniveSam upAdAya lOkikA DarmA / vikalpa kleSa vAsanAm vyavasTApayanti na tu vigata aBiniveSAH loka uttarAH
# kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # r yod do zhes mngon-par-zhen-pa #  nye-bar-bzung-nas #  'jig-rten-gyi-chos #  rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i bag-chags #  'jog-par-byed #  kyi / / mngon-par-zhen-pa #  med-pa #  'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  dag ni ma yin te /
tatas parikalpita svaBAvaH vAsanA samudayaH ucyate / samutTAna samudayaH paratantraH / samutTAnaH Atma lABaH / sa yatas Bavati sa samutTAna samudayaH p / samudeti asmAt iti kRtvA
# de-bas-na #  kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  la bag-chags #  kyis kun-'byung-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  / / kun nas byung-ba # 'i kun 'byung ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  do / / kun nas byung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni bdag thob-pa #  ste / / de gang-la # s byung-ba #  de ni de-la # s 'byung ngo zhes-bya-ba # 'i phyir kun nas 'byung-ba # 'o /
sa punar kiMsvarUpaH iti atas Aha karma kleSAH iti
# de-yang #  rang-bzhin #  ji-lta-bu #  zhe na de'i-phyir #  las dang nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams so zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
te ca vastu svarUpa tvAt paratantra svaBAvaH / avisaMyoga samudaya sTatAyAH iti / kaTam iti atas Aha AvaraNA visaMyogaH
# de-dag #  kyang dngos-po # 'i rang-bzhin #  yin-pas #  gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  do / / ma-bral-ba # 'i kun-'byung-ba #  ni de-bzhin-nyid #  la bya ste / / ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / sgrib-pa #  dang ma bral zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / de ni 'di-skad-du #  /
etat uktam Bavati yAvat AvaraNEH na visaMyuktA taTatA tAvat / samudeti duHKam iti
# de-bzhin-nyid #  ji-srid #  du sgrib-pa #  rnams dang ma-bral-ba #  de srid du sdug-bsngal #  kun 'byung zhes-bya-ba # 'am /
AvaraNEH avisaMyuktA vA taTatA samudaya Darma tA iti samudayanAm amla ABa
# sgrib-pa #  rnams dang ma-bral-ba # 'i de-bzhin-nyid #  ni kun-'byung-ba # 'i chos-nyid #  yin-pas #  kun-'byung-ba # 'i ming 'thob po zhes-bya-ba # r bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro /
iti / triviDena niroDena mUla tattvam niroDa satyam / tat ca na vijQAyate iti atas Aha triviDaH niroDaH
# 'gog-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  gyis rtsa ba'i de-kho-na # r 'gog-pa # 'i bden-pa #  yin na de-yang #  mi shes-nas #  de'i-phyir #  /
svaBAva dvayana utpattiH mala SAnti dvayam matam iti
# 'gog-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  ni; ngo-bo-nyid #  dang gnyis mi skye / / dri-ma #  zhi-ba #  gnyis su 'dod / / ces bya-ba #  smos so /

# de-la #  ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  mi-skye-ba #  ni kun-brtags-pa #  ste / / de ni mo-gsham-gyi-bu #  bzhin-du #  ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # s gtan-du #  mi skye ste /
grAhya grAhakayoH anutpattiH paratantrasya
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  gnyis mi-skye-ba #  ni gzhan gyi dbang ste /
tasya api grAhya grAhaka svarUpAByAm atyanta rahita tvAt / dvayaBrAnti AtmanA
# de-yang #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  gnyis kyi rang-bzhin #  dang gtan bral-ba # 'i phyir 'khrul-pa #  gnyis kyi bdag-nyid #  du mi-skye-ba # 'o /
mala SAnti dvayam parinizpannaH / ca SabdaH samuccaya arTaH

tat punar na vijQAyate iti atas Aha pratisaMKyA niroDa taTatA AKyam iti
# de-yang #  mi shes-nas #  de'i-phyir #  so-sor-brtags-pa # 'i 'gog-pa #  dang de-bzhin-nyid #  ces bya-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
malam dviviDam rAga Adi AvaraNam parikalpitaH ca

# de-la #  zag-pa-med-pa # 'i ye shes kyi sa-bon #  gnas nas bton te / / 'dod-chags #  la sog pa'i dri-ma #  rnams gtan mi-skye-ba # 'i bdag-nyid-kyis #  zhi-ba #  ni so-sor-brtags-pa # 'i 'gog-pa # 'o /
taTatA gocareNa advAda jQAnena parikalpita malasyA anutpAda AtmikA SAntiH / taTatA
# de-bzhin-nyid #  du spyod yul pa gnyis-su-med-pa # 'i ye shes kyis kun-brtags-pa # 'i dri-ma #  mi-skye-ba # 'i bdag-nyid-kyis #  zhi-ba #  ni de-bzhin-nyid #  do /

# 'gog-pa #  rnam-pa #  'di gsum ni brtags-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rtsa ba'i de-kho-na # r go-rims-bzhin-du #  shes-pa # r bya'o /

uktaH niroDa satyasya mUla tattve antar BAvaH

# de'i-'og-tu #  lam gyi bden-pa #  bsdu-ba # r bya ste; de'i-phyir #  lam gyi bden-pa #  rtsa ba'i de-kho-na # r rnam-pa-gsum #  du ji-ltar #  rab tu gzhag ce na zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  / / yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  gsungs so / / kun-brtags-pa #  ni yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
parikalpitataH atyantam asat deva iti tasya parijQAnam eva na prahANam / na hi asataH prahANam yujyate / paratantrasya parijQAne prahANe ca
# kun-brtags-pa #  ni gtan med-pa #  nyid pas de ni yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba # r zad kyi spang du med de med-pa #  ni spang-ba # r mi rung ngo / / gzhan gyi dbang ni yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba #  dang spang-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
paratantraH hi yaTA KyAti taTA asattvam vijQeyam na tu
# gzhan gyi dbang ni ji-ltar #  snang-ba #  de-ltar #  med-pa # r shes-pa # r bya'i /
sarva Atma tvena asattvam kalpita vat
# brtags-pa #  bzhin-du #  thams-cad-kyi #  bdag-nyid-kyis #  med-pa # r ni ma yin no /
karma kleSayoH BAva Atma tvAt prahAtavyaH ca
# las dang nyon-mongs-pa #  ni dngos-po # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin-pas #  spang-bar-bya-ba #  yang yin no /
parinizpannasya prEjQAne prApti sAkzAtkaraNe ca iti
# yongs-su-grub-pa #  ni yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba #  dang thob-pa # r mngon-sum-du-bya-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
parinizpannaH hi BAva aBAva vinirmukta lakzaNam atas parijQeyaH / ASraya parAvRtti tAyAH ca
# yongs-su-grub-pa #  ni dngos-po #  dang dngos-po-med-pa #  las rnam-par-grol-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang gnas-gyur-pa #  nyid-du #  yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya zhing /
ASaya parAvRtti tA vinirmukta Darma kAya tvena sAkzAtkartavyA iti SUnyatA / parijQeyA / niroDaH sAkzAt kartavyaH prApti sAkzAt kriyayA
# gnas-par-gyur-pa #  nyid rnam-par-grol-ba #  chos kyi skur mngon-sum-du-bya-ba #  yin-pas #  stong-pa-nyid #  ni yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'o / / 'gog-pa #  ni thob-pa # r mngon-sum-du-byas-pa # s mngon-sum-du-bya-ba # 'o /
uBayam ca uBaTA iti anye / dviviDAH hi parijQA jQAna parijQA prahANa parijQA ca
# kha-cig #  na re gnyis la rnam-pa-gnyis #  gnyis te yongs-su-shes-pa #  rnam gnyis ni shes-pa # 'i yongs-su-shes-pa # 'i dang spong-ba # 'i yongs-su-shes-pa # 'o /
tatra jQAna parijQAya parijQeyam praTamam tRtIyaQca
# de-la #  dngos-po #  dang gsum-pa #  ni shes-pa # 'i yongs-su-shes-pa # s yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'o /
dvitIyam tu uBaya parijQeyam
# gnyis-pa #  ni gnyis-ka # s yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya'o /
sAkzAtkriyA api dviDA jQAna sAkzAt kriyA prApti sAkzAt kriyA ca iti

tatra jQAna sAkzAt kriyayA trayam api sAkzAt kartavyam
# de-la #  shes-pa # r mngon-sum-du-bya-ba # s ni gsum char yang mngon-sum-du #  bya'o /
prApti sAkzAt kriyayA tu tRtIyam eva
# thob-pa # r mngon-sum-du-bya-ba # s ni gsum-pa #  nyid do zhe'o /
evam atra mUla tattve parijQA prahANa sAkzAtkriyAyAm mArga satya / vyavasTAnam veditavyam na tu tatra antar BAvAt
# de-ltar #  rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  'dir yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba #  dang spang-bar-bya-ba #  dang mngon-sum-du-bya-ba #  rnams kyis lam gyi bden-pa #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'i /
atra ca satya catuzwayena yaH saFkleSaH yatas ca tayoH ca viSudDiH yA / yatas ca tat paridIpitam
# de'i khongs-su-gtogs-pa # r bsdu-ba #  ni ma yin no / / de-la #  bden-pa #  bzhis ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  dang; gang-la # s byung-ba #  dang de gnyis rnam-par-dag-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  dang gang-la # s 'gyur-pa #  de rnams yongs su brjod do /
anukramaH tu ezAm yaTA aBisamayam iti / OdArika sUkzma tattvam p / OdArika sUkzma tattvaQca iti / OdArika tattvam saMvRti satyam sUkzma tattvam tu paramArTa satyam / yatas AdO= OdArikeNa sattvAn paripAcayati paripakvAn= tu sUkzmeNa
# de-dag #  gi go-rims #  ni ji-ltar #  mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  bzhin-du # 'o / / rags-pa #  dang phra-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  ni zhes-bya-ba #  la / / rags-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  ni kun-rdzob-kyi-bden-pa # 'o; / / phra-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  ni don-dam-pa'i-bden-pa #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  dang-por #  rags-pa # s sems-can #  rnams yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed do / / yongs-su-smin-pa # r gyur nas phra-ba # s rnam-par-grol-ba # r byed de /
vimocayati atas pUrvam OdArikam paScAt sUkzmam / kArikA anuguNyAt viparyaya uktiH
