samAhita jQAna vizaya tvAt paramArTa satyam sUkzma tattvam
# mnyam-par-bzhag-pa # 'i shes-pa # 'i yul yin-pas #  don-dam-pa'i-bden-pa #  ni phra-ba # 'i de-kho-na # 'o /
aTavA vijQAna vizaya tvAt OdArikam
# yang-na #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i yul yin-pas #  na rags-pa # 'o /
jQAna vizaya tvAt sUkzmam / sarva tattvAnAm mUla tattve antarBAvaH pratijQAtaH iti atas pRcCati tat / mUla tattve kaTam veditavyam / iti atas Aha / prajQapti pratipattitaH / taTA udBAvanayA OdAram iti
# ye shes kyi yul yin-pas #  na phra-ba # 'o / / de-kho-na #  thams-cad #  rtsa ba'i de-kho-na # r bsdu-ba # r dam bcas bas na / / de'i-phyir #  de rtsa ba'i de-kho-na # r ji-ltar #  rig-par-bya #  zhe na zhes dris te de'i-phyir #  / / brtags-pa #  dang ni shes-pa #  dang /
prajQaptiH pratipatIH udBAvanA ca OdArika tattvam mUla tattve veditavyam
# de-bzhin #  brjod-pa #  rags-pa #  yin / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so / / brtags-pa #  dang shes-pa #  dang brjod-pa #  rnams ni rags-pa # 'i de-kho-na # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
etat eva pratipAdayan= Aha triviDAH hi saMvRtiH iti vistaraH
# de nyid bstan-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir kun-rdzob #  ni rnam-pa-gsum #  ste zhes rgya-cher #  smos so /
asataH arTasya rUpam GawaH pawaH ca iti vyavasTAnam prajQapti saMvRtiH
# don-med-pa #  la gzugs dang bum-pa #  dang snam-bu #  zhes-bya-ba # r rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  ni brtags-pa # 'i kun-rdzob #  po /
rUpa vedanA saMjQA Adi svaBAva viSezeNa nAma aBilApaH prajQapti saMvRtiH / iti anye
# kha-cig #  na re gzugs dang tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  dang bye-brag #  gi ming gis brjod-pa #  ni brtags-pa # 'i kun-rdzob #  bo zhe'o /
aBilApa apekzayA yat vyavahriyate rUpam vedanA iti vA tat / prajQapti saMvRtiH iti kecid
# kha-cig #  na re brjod-pa #  la ltos nas gzugs dang tshor-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # r tha-snyad-'dogs-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni brtags-pa # 'i kun-rdzob #  bo zhe'o /
tat ca etat asattvAt parikalpitaH svaBAvaH
# sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  bzhin-du #  med-pa # s na kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  do /
pratipatti saMvRtiH vikalpena yena rUpa AdayaH Gawa AdayaH ca p / vijQAna nirBAsAt abahiH BUtam api bahis BUtam iva vastu rUpeNa yaTA / vyavasTAnam aBiniviSate sa vikalpaH pratipatti saMvRtiH / udBAvanA saMvRtiH ca iti / caSabdaH samuccaya arTaH
# shes-pa # 'i kun-rdzob #  ni rnam-par-rtog-pa #  gang-gis #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  dang bum-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  snang-ba #  las; pha rol na med kyang phyi-rol #  na yod-pa #  bzhin-du #  ji-ltar #  rnam-par-gnas-pa #  ltar dngos-po # 'i ngo bor mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni shes-pa # 'i kun-rdzob #  po / / brjod-pa #  yang kun-rdzob #  po zhes-bya-ba #  la / / yang zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni bsdu-bar-bya-ba # 'i don te /
vikalpA aBilApa atikrAntasya api parinizpannasya SUnyatA taTatA samalA / nirmala iti evam AdiBiH paryAyEH sandarSanam udBAvanA saMvRtiH
# yongs-su-grub-pa #  ni rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang brjod-pa #  las 'das kyang stong-pa-nyid #  dang de-bzhin-nyid #  dang dri-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  dang dri-ma-med-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-grangs #  kyis bstan-pa #  ni brjod-pa # 'i kun-rdzob #  bo /
tayA triviDayA saMvRttyA saMvRti satya tvam mUla tattve yaTAkramam / veditavyam / saMvRtiH vyavahAraH
# kun-rdzob #  rnam-pa-gsum #  po des kun-rdzob-kyi-bden-pa #  nyid de / / rtsa ba'i de-kho-na # r go-rims-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / kun-rdzob #  ni tha-snyad #  do /
prajQaptiH iti aBiDAnam
# btags-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni brjod-pa #  ste /
arTa aBAve aBiDAna mAtreNa vyavahAraH prajQapti saMvRtiH
# don-med-pa # r brjod-pa #  tsam gyis tha-snyad #  du bya-ba #  ni btags-pa # 'i kun-rdzob #  bo /
atas eva arTa aBAvAt prajQapti saMvRtyA parikalpitaH saMvRti satyam
# de-bas-na #  don-med-pa # 'i phyir btags-pa # 'i kun-rdzob #  kyis kun-brtags-pa #  kun-rdzob-kyi-bden-pa # 'o /
avidyamAne arTe arTa aBiniveSaH pratipattiH tayA vyavahAraH / pratipatti saMvRtiH
# don med bzhin-du #  don-du #  mngon-pa # r zhen nas shes-pa #  des tha-snyad-'dogs-pa #  de ni shes-pa # 'i kun-rdzob #  ste /
sA punar aBiniveSa vikalpaH
# de ni mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'o /
tasmAt pratipatti saMvRtyA saMvRtti satyam paratantraH
# de-bas-na #  shes-pa # 'i kun-rdzob #  kyi gzhan gyi dbang kun-rdzob-kyi-bden-pa # 'o /
taTatA Adi SabdEH niraBilApyasya Darma DAtoH yA saMsUcanA / sa udBAvanA
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  brjod-du-med-pa #  la de-bzhin-nyid #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sgras brjod-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni brjod-pa #  ste /
tayA DarmaDAtoH vyavahAraH udBAvanA saMvRtiH
# des chos-kyi-dbyings #  la tha-snyad-'dogs-pa #  ni brjod-pa # 'i kun-rdzob #  bo /
atas ca udBAvanA saMvRtyA parinizpannaH saMvRti satyam / tatra prajQapti udBAvanA saMvRtyoH avasara saFgraha vyavasTAnam / veditavyam na tu svaBAvataH iti / uktam saMvRti satyam / idAnIm paramArTa satyam vaktavyam iti atas Aha / paramArTantu ekatas iti / kalpita paratantrayoH paramArTataH asamBava tvam / satyam punar ekasmAt p / parinizpannAt eva svaBAvAt veditavyam
# de-bas-na #  brjod-pa # 'i kun-rdzob #  kyis yongs-su-grub-pa #  kun-rdzob-kyi-bden-pa # 'o / / de-la #  brtags-pa #  dang brjod-pa # 'i kun-rdzob #  gnyis ni skabs su bsdus nas rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'i / / rang-bzhin-gyis #  ni ma yin no / / kun-rdzob-kyi-bden-pa #  bshad-zin #  to / / de ni don-dam-pa'i-bden-pa #  brjod-pa # r bya ste / / de'i-phyir #  / / dam-pa # 'i don ni gcig-pu # 'o / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so / / brtags-pa #  dang ni gzhan dbang gnyis ni don-dam-pa # r mi srid-pa # 'i phyir don-dam-pa'i-bden-pa #  ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  gcig-pu # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
sa punar parinizpannaH kena kAraNena paramArTaH ucyate / iti atas Aha / arTa prApti pratyayAH hi parama arTaH triDA mataH iti / triviDaH hi parama arTaH arTa paramArTaH prApti parama arTaH / prayati parama arTaH ca / tatra arTa parama arTaH taTatA / paramaH hi loka uttaram jQAnam tasya arTaH vizayaH iti kRtvA taTatA
# yongs-su-grub-pa #  de-yang #  ci'i-phyir #  don-dam-pa #  zhes bya zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  / / don dang thob dang sgrub-pa #  ni / / don dam rnam-pa-gsum #  du 'dod / / ces bya-ba #  gsungs so / / don-dam-pa #  ni rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / don-dam-pa #  dang thob-par-bya-ba #  don-dam-pa #  dang sgrub-pa #  don-dam-pa # 'o / / de-la #  don-dam-pa #  de-bzhin-nyid #  de / / dam-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i ye shes so / / de'i yul yin-pas #  don te /
paramArTaH iti ucyate indriya arTa vat / tat eva pradarSayan= Aha paramasya jQAnasya arTaH iti kRtvA iti
# dbang-po #  rnams kyi don bzhin-du #  / / de-bzhin-nyid #  ni dam-pa # 'i don / / zhes-bya'o #  / / de nyid bstan-pa # 'i phyir ye-shes-dam-pa # 'i don yin pa'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
Alambana BAvena vyavasTAnAt iti arTaH
# dmigs-pa'i-dngos-po # r rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
jQAnA pRTaktvAt tasmin kAle Alambanam na vartate
# ye shes dang tha-mi-dad-pa # 'i phyir de'i tshe dmigs-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  ni ma yin gyi /
vijQapti mAtra pratiBAsa vat
# rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam snang-ba #  bzhin te /
tat yaTA yezAm vijQapti mAtram kzamate na tezAm rUpa Adi vijQapti mAtram / muktvA rUpa Adi pratiBAsAH vidyante
# dper-na #  gang dag rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam du bzod-pa #  de-dag #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam ma-gtogs-par #  gzugs la-sogs-pa # r snang-ba #  ni med-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
prApti parama arTaH nirvANam ekAnta nirma taTatA ASraya parAvRtti lakzaNam / kaTam paramArTaH iti atas Aha paramaH arTaH iti kRtvA / paramaH ca asO= arTaH ca iti kRtvA paramArTaH
# thob-par-bya-ba #  don-dam-pa #  ni mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  ste / / shin-tu #  dri-ma-med-pa # 'i de-bzhin-nyid #  gnas-gyur-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do / / ji-ltar #  na don-dam-pa #  zhes bya zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  don-gyi-dam-pa #  yin pa'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / de ni dam-pa #  yang yin la don yang yin-pas #  na don-dam-pa #  ste /
tatra saMskRta asaMskRta Darma agra tvAt paramaH mArga prayojana tvAt arTaH
# de 'dus byas dang 'dus-ma-byas #  kyi chos-rnams #  kyi mchog yin-pas #  dam-pa # 'o / / lam gyi dgos-pa #  yin-pas #  na don to /
taTA hi mArgaH nirvANa prApti prayojanaH
# 'di-ltar #  mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  thob-par-bya-ba #  ni lam gyi dgos-pa #  ste /
nirvANantu arTaH sarva apakAra doza rahita tvAt / yasmAt doza sahitaH anarTaH iti ucyate
# gnod-pa # 'i nyes-pa #  thams-cad #  dang bral-ba # 'i phyir mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  ni don to / / 'di-ltar #  nyes-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  la ni don-med-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
pratipatti parama arTaH mArgaH / kim kAraNam / paramaH asya arTaH iti kRtvA / vizayaH prayojanam vA arTaH
# sgrub-pa #  don-dam-pa #  ni lam ste / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na / / de'i don ni dam-pa #  yin pa'i phyir ro / / don ni yul lam dgos-pa #  ste /
vizayaH taTatA prayojanam nirvANam
# yul ni de-bzhin-nyid #  do / / dgos-pa #  ni mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'o /
vizaya dvAreNa paramaH ucyamAne kaTam anyaH anya samarTanam na syAt / anyaH anya samarTanam ced kaH dozaH iti / niScaya aBAvaH / na evam Bavizyati anyonya samarTanAt siMha vana vat / kaTam asaMskRtam nirvANa AKyam saMskRtam ca mArga AKyam / parinizpanna svaBAvaH ucyate / paramArTa satyam hi parinizpanna svaBAvaH nirdizwam / mArgaH tu parinizpannot na yujyate / na pUrva apara BAgaBAvaH iti kRtvA / tasmAt na mArgaH parama arTa satyam na ca apar parinizpanne / paramArTa satya saMgrahaH iti / atas Aha / nirvikArA aparyAsa parinizpattitaH dvayam iti / aTavA kaTam asaMkRtam nirvANa AKyam saMskRtaQca mArga AKyam / parinizpanna svaBAva p / ucyate / parinizpannaH hi taTatA / ezA ca dvaya lakzaNa rahita tvam paratantrasya iti na nirvANa mArgayoH / parinizpanna tA yujyate / tat idam avAcyam yatas tatra dvaya aBAvaH parinizpannaH eva
# yul gyi sgo nas dam-pa #  zhes bya na / / ji-ltar #  na gcig-la-gcig-brten-pa # r mi 'gyur / / gcig-la-gcig-brten-pa # r gyur na ci nyes she na / / gtan la bab-pa #  med-pa # r 'gyur ro / / gcig-la-gcig #  brten du zin-kyang #  de-ltar #  mi 'gyur te / / seng-ge #  dang nags bzhin no / / don-dam-pa'i-bden-pa #  ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du bstan la / / lam la ni snga-ma-dang-phyi-ma # 'i cha med-pa-ma-yin-pa # s yongs-su-grub-pa # r mi rung ste / / de-bas-na #  lam ni don-dam-pa'i-bden-pa #  ma yin la / / yongs-su-ma-grub-pa # s kyang don-dam-pa'i-bden-pa # r bsdur mi rung na 'dus-ma-byas #  dang 'dus byas yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du ji-skad #  brjod ce na / / de'i-phyir #  / / 'gyur med phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  / / yongs-su-grub-pa #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so / / yang-na #  yongs-su-grub-pa #  ni de-bzhin-nyid #  de / / de-yang #  gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan-nyid #  gnyis dang bral-ba-nyid #  pas mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  dang lam-gnyis #  yongs-su-grub-pa #  nyid-du #  mi rung na mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  'dus-ma-byas #  dang lam zhes-bya-ba #  'dus byas gnyis yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  do zhes ji-skad-du #  bya zhe na / / 'di ni klan-ka # r mi rung ste / / 'di-ltar #  de-la #  gnyis po med-pa #  ni yongs-su-grub-pa #  nyid de /
na tu dvaya aBAvaH eva parinizpannaH iti tat anya pratizeDaH / atas tat anyat ca
# gnyis po med-pa #  nyid yongs-su-grub-pa #  zhes de-la # s gzhan dgag-pa # r mi byed de / / de-bas-na #  de-la # s gzhan-yang #  ste /
nirvikArA aparyAsa parinizpattitaH dvayam api parinizpannaH iti
# 'gyur-ba-med-pa #  dang phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r yongs-su-grub-pa #  gnyis kyang yongs-su-grub-pa #  zhes sbyar ro /
sambadDyate asaMskRtam nirvANam taTatA ca
# 'dus-ma-byas #  ni mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  dang de-bzhin-nyid #  de /
asaMskRtam ananyaTABAvAt avikAra parinizpattyA parinizpannam
# 'dus-ma-byas #  ni gzhan-du-'gyur-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir 'gyur-ba-med-pa # r yongs-su-'grub-pa # s yongs-su-grub-pa # 'o /
saMskRtam mArga saMgRhItam na anyatra
# 'dus byas ni lam gyis bsdus-pa #  la bya'i gzhan la ma yin te /
aviparyAsa parinizpattyA parinizpannam iti sambaDyate / kaTam iti atas abravIt punar jQeya vastu viparyAsAt iti
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r yongs-su-grub-pa # s yongs-su-grub-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro / / ji lta zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  / / shes-bya'i-dngos-po #  la phyin-ci-log #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
yasmAt na punar jQeye viparyAsam Apadyate tasmAt na mArgaH api / parinizpannaH iti atas ca dvayoH api saMskRta asaMskRtayoH parinizpanna tvam / pRTak aBiprAyAt iti aviroDaH / prasidDa tattvam / tatra / loka prasidDam ekasmAt iti / yaTA aBiDAnam asamBavAt parikalpitAt eva tat na anyasmAt tasya tu
# gang-gi-phyir #  shes-par-bya-ba #  la phyin-ci-log #  tu mi-'gyur-ba #  de'i-phyir #  lam yongs-su-grub-pa #  yin te / / de-bas-na #  bsam-pa-tha-dad-pa # 'i phyir 'dus byas dang 'dus-ma-byas #  gnyi-ga #  yang yongs-su-grub-pa #  yin-pas #  'gal-ba #  med do / / de-la #  / / gcig gis 'jig-rten #  grags-pa #  ste / / zhes-bya-ba #  ni ji-ltar-brjod-pa #  bzhin-du #  med-pa #  kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  te /
svarUpam na jQAyate iti atas Aha yasmin vastuni iti vistaraH
# de gzhan gyis ni ma yin no / / de'i rang-gi #  ngo bo mi-shes-pa # s de'i-phyir #  / / dngos-po #  gang-la #  zhes-bya-ba #  rgya-cher #  smos so; /
saMketaH saMjQA saMjQita sambanDa jQAnam
# brda-ni #  ming dang ming can 'brel-pa # r shes-pa # 'o /
saMstavaH tasya vAram vArampra yoga darSanam
# 'dris-pa #  ni de-la #  yang-dang-yang-du #  sbyor zhing lta-ba # 'o /
tatra anupravizwayA budDyA iti
# de-la #  rjes-su-zhugs-pa # 'i blo zhes-bya-ba #  la /
kaH punar budDeH saMketa saMstava anupraveSaH
# brda la 'dris-pa # 'i rjes la zhugs-pa # 'i blo gang zhe na /
tat smaraNAt
# de-dag #  dran-pa #  ste /
etat uktam Bavati saMketa saMstava anusmaraNa anugatatyA budDyA sarvezAm / lOkikAnAm SAstra vidAm tat avidAm ca vyAhRti BAve kvacid p / pRTyvyeveyam iti Adi vaMSa Adi darSana tulya tA iti / etat loka prasidDam tattvam / loka prasidDyA tat taTA eva iti kRtvA
# de ni 'di-skad-du #  brda la 'dris-pa # 'i dran-pa # 'i rjes-su-song-ba # 'i blos 'jig-rten-pa #  bstan-bcos-shes-pa #  dang de mi-shes-pa #  thams-cad-kyi # s tha-snyad #  du btags-pa # 'i dngos-po #  gang-la #  la 'di ni sa yin no zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # r lta-ba #  mthun-pa #  yin no zhes bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro / / de ni de-kho-na-bzhin-du #  'jig-rten #  du grags-pa # 'i phyir de ni 'jig-rten #  gyi grags-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  zhes-bya'o #  / / gsum gyis rigs-pa # 'i grags-pa # 'o /
trayAt yukti prasidDakam iti / triviDam api hi svaBAvam aDikRtya yuktiH kriyate iti / atas svaBAva trayeNa yukti prasidDa tvam vyavasTApyate / tat ca na vijQAyate iti atas pradarSayan= Aha yat satAm / yukta arTa paNXitAnAm ityAdi / tatra santaH ye yukta arTa paNXitAH
# zhes-bya-ba #  ni ngo-bo-nyid #  rnam-pa-gsum #  gyi dbang du mdzad de rigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # s na de'i-phyir #  ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum gyis rigs-pa # 'i grags-pa # 'i de-kho-na # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go / / de-yang #  mi shes te / / de-bas-na #  de bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / gang-zag #  dam-pa #  rigs-pa'i-don #  la mkhas-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  smos so / / de-la #  dam-pa #  dag ni gang dag rigs-pa'i-don #  la mkhas-pa #  dag go /
tArkikAH ye mImAMsakAH
# rtog-ge-pa #  dag ni gang dag dpyod-pa-can #  dag ste /
pUrvasya vyAKyA nASayasya paScAt nirdeSa uktiH / aTavA santaH anvezakAH kim kuSalam iti
# snga-ma #  bshad-pa # r bsams nas tshig phyi-ma #  brjod do / / yang-na #  dam-pa #  dag ni dge-ba #  ci zhes tshol-ba #  can dag go /
yuktA yuktA arTa paNXitA / apekzA kArya kAraNa upapatti Darma tA yukti catuzwayA virudDa arTa kRta kOSalAH
# rigs-pa'i-don #  la mkhas-pa #  dag ni ltos-pa #  dang bya-ba-byed-pa #  dang 'thad-pa #  dang chos-nyid-kyi-rigs-pa #  bzhi dang mi-'gal-ba # 'i don la mkhas-pa #  dag go /
tArkikAH tuhapa Uha samarTAH taTAgata pravacana samASrayeNa A / viparIta SAstra praNetAraH
# rtog ge ba dag ni rtog-pa #  dang sel nus-pa #  dag dang de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # 'i gsung-rab #  la brten-nas #  bstan-bcos #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r byed-pa # 'o /
mImAMsakAH sva para SAstra paNXitAH SreyaH doza parIkzakAH / kecid mImAMsakAH iti na paWanti / te evam AhuH satAm iti ukte ke punar santaH iti atas Aha / yukta arTa paNXitAH iti
# dpyod-pa-can #  dag ni bdag-dang-gzhan #  gyi bstan-bcos #  la mkhas-par-gyur-pa #  dang legs-pa #  dang nyes-pa #  dpyod-pa #  dag go / / kha-cig #  las ni dpyod-pa-can #  / / zhes mi 'byung ste / / de-dag #  'di-skad-du #  / / dam-pa #  zhes brjod-pa # 'i dam-pa #  de gang zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  / / rigs-pa'i-don #  la mkhas-pa #  dag / / ces bya-ba #  smos so /
te ca tarka BUmO BAvABUmO ca vyavasTita tvAt dviviDAH / tasmAt tArkikAH iti ucyante iti
# de-dag #  kyang rtog-ge-pa # 'i sa dang bsgom-pa # 'i sa la gnas-pa # 'i phyir rnam-pa-gnyis #  te / / de'i-phyir #  rtog-ge-pa #  dag ces bya-ba #  smos so zhes zer ro /
tezAm ca kaScid loka prasidDa anusArIzyataH Aha pramANa trayam niSritya iti / pramANa traya aviroDena
# de-dag #  las kyang kha-cig #  ni 'jig-rten #  gyi grags-pa # 'i rjes-su-'brang-ba # s na / / de'i-phyir #  tshad-ma #  gsum la brten-nas #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / tshad-ma #  gsum dang mi-'gal-ba # r zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
pramANa trayam punar pratyakzam anumAnam AgamaH ca
# tshad-ma #  gsum ni mngon-sum #  dang rjes-su-dpag-pa #  dang lung ngo [?] /
tatra pratyakzam paQca indriya jam mAnasam ca suKa duHKa Adi samvedanam
# de-la #  mngon-sum #  ni dbang-po-lnga #  las skyes-pa #  dang bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  la-sogs-pa #  myong-ba # 'i yid do /
tri rUpa liFgena anumeya arTa jQAnam anumAnam / Apta vAc AgamaH
# tshul gsum-pa # 'i rtags kyi rjes-su-dpag-pa # r bya-ba # 'i don la shes-pa #  ni rjes-su-dpag-pa # 'o / / yid ches bas bstan-pa #  ni lung ste /
AptAH punar anRta hetu vimuktAH
# yid-ches-pa # s ni brdzun-du-smra-ba # 'i rgyu dang mi-ldan-pa #  dag go /
aTavA pratyakza anumAna Agama prasidDena hetunA dRzwAntena ca tat / prasidDasya eva sADyasya param prati sADya tvAt pramANa trayam niSritya iti
# yang-na #  mngon-sum #  dang rjes-su-dpag-pa #  dang lung gis rab tu grub-pa # 'i gtan-tshigs #  dang dpes bsgrub-par-bya-ba #  sgrub-pa #  de nyid gzhan la sgrub-par-byed-pa # s tshad-ma #  gsum la brten-nas #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
upapatti sADana yuktyA prasidDam vastu iti
# 'thad-pa #  sgrub-pa # 'i rigs-pas-grags-pa # 'i dngos-po # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
upapattiH trirUpam liFgam sADya pratipAdana upAya tvAt
# 'thad-pa #  ni bsgrub-par-bya-ba #  rtogs-par-byed-pa # 'i thabs yin-pas #  tshul gsum-pa # 'i rtags so /
upapatteH sADanam upapatti sADanam trirUpa liFga AKyAnam tena tat / pratipAdanAt
# 'thad-pa # 'i sgrub-pa #  ni 'thad-pa #  sgrub-pa #  ste / / des rtogs-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir tshul gsum-pa # 'i rtags brjod-pa # 'o /
yuktiH upAyaH yena prayoga niyamena liFgasya trirUpyam AKyAyate / aTavA upapaAtiH ananyaTAsamBavaH / sADanyuktiH avayava sambanDaH / upapatteH sADana yuktiH iti vigrahaH / aTavA upapattiH eva sADana yuktiH iti vigrahaH / anya sADana yukteByaH vyavacCeda arTam upapatti grahaNam
# rigs-pa #  ni thabs te / / sbyor-ba #  nges-pa #  gang-gi #  rtags kyi tshul gsum brjod-pa # 'o / / yang-na #  'thad-pa #  ni gzhan-du #  mi srid-pa # 'o / / sgrub-pa # 'i rigs-pa #  ni cha'i sbyor-ba #  ste / / 'thad-pa #  sgrub-pa # 'i rigs-pa # 'o zhes tshig rnam-pa # r sbyar-ba # 'o / / yang-na #  'thad-pa #  nyid sgrub-pa # 'i rigs-pa #  yin par tshig rnam-pa # r sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / sgrub-pa # 'i rigs-pa #  gzhan dag las dbye-ba # 'i phyir 'thad-pa #  smos te /
evam pramANa trayam niSritya upapatti sADana yuktyA yat prasidDam vastu / trayANAm BAvanAm anyatamat tat yukti prasidDam ucyate
# de-ltar-na #  tshad-ma #  gsum la brten-nas #  'thad-pa #  sgrub-pa # 'i rigs-pas #  gang grags-pa # 'i dngos-po #  ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum gyi nang nas gang-yang-rung-ba #  ste rigs-pas-grags-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
uktam prasidDa tattvam
# grags-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  bshad-zin #  to /
viSudDi gocara tattvam / p
# de'i-'og-tu #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i spyod yul brjod dgos te /
tat anantaram tu viSudDi vizayam vaktavyam iti atas Aha / viSudDi gocara tattvam dviviDam iti
# de'i-phyir #  / / rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i spyod yul gyi de-kho-na #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  te zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tat tu yaTA dviviDam tat pradarSayan= Aha / kleSa AvaraNa viSudDi jQAna gocaram jQeya AvaraNa viSudDi jQAna gocaraQca iti / kleSa AvaraNa viSudDiH kleSa AvaraNa prahANam
# de-yang #  ji-ltar #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  su 'gyur-ba #  de bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i ye shes kyi spyod yul dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i ye shes kyi spyod yul lo zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  spangs-pa #  ste /
kleSa AvaraNa viSudDaye kleSa AvaraNa viSudDO vA jQAnam / kleSa AvaraNa viSudDi jQAnam
# nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir ram / / nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa # r byed-pa # 'i ye shes ni nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i ye shes te /
kleSa AvaraNa viSudDi prayojanam tat nimittam vA iti arTaH
# nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa # r bya-ba # r dgos-pa # 'am / / de'i rgyu zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
tasya kleSa AvaraNa viSudDi jQAnasya gocaram iti vizayaH iti arTaH
# nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i ye shes de'i spyod yul zhes-bya-ba #  ni yul zhes pa'i tha-tshig #  go /
evam jQeya AvaraNa viSudDi jQAnasya gocaram api vaktavyam
# de-bzhin-du #  shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i ye shes kyi spyod yul la yang brjod-pa # r bya'o /
tatra kleSa AvaraNam sarve darSana BAva nAma arga prahAtavyAH kleSa upakleSAH
# de-la #  nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  ni mthong-ba #  dang bsgom-pa'i-lam #  gyis spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  thams-cad #  do /
iti atas darSana BAvanA tat upacAra jQana vizayam SrAvaka pratyekabudDAnAm / yat tattvam duHKa samudaya niroDa mArga satyam ucyate tat
# de-bas-na #  mthong-ba #  dang bsgom-pa #  dang de dang nye-bar-spyod-pa # 'i ye shes kyi yul ni nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  rnams kyi de-kho-na #  gang-yin-pa #  sdug-bsngal #  dang kun-'byung-ba #  dang 'gog-pa #  dang lam rnams kyi bden-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ste /
kleSa AvaraNa viSudDi jQAnasya gocaram
# de ni nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i ye shes kyi spyod yul lo /
jQAtavyam jQeyam / tat ca sarva AtmanA paQca vidyA sTAnAni
# shes-par-bya-ba #  ni shes-bya #  ste / / de ni mdor-na #  rig-pa'i-gnas #  lnga dag go /
tAni punar aDyAtma vyAkaraNa hetu cikitsA sarva Silpa karma sTAna AKyAni
# de-dag #  ni nang dang brda-sprod-pa #  dang gtan-tshigs #  dang gso-ba #  dang bzo-dang-las-kyi-gnas #  zhes-bya-ba #  thams-cad #  do /
tatra jQAna vibanDa BUtam aklizwam ajQAnam jQeya AvaraNam
# de-la #  ye shes kyi-ge # gs su gyur-pa #  nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i mi-shes-pa #  ni shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa # 'o /
tat viSoDanam loka uttara jQAna anuloma aDimukti caryA BUmi saFgRhItam tat / pRzWalabDaQca jQAnam
# de rnam-par-sbyong-ba #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i ye shes kyi rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'i mos-pas-spyod-pa'i-sa # r bsdus-pa #  dang rab-tu-dga'-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  sa bcu gcig-tu-bsdus-pa #  dang de'i-rjes-la # s thob-pa # 'i ye shes so /
tat punar boDisattva taTAgata santAna vartim
# de-yang #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  dang de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # 'i thugs kyi rgyud la mnga'-ba #  ste /
tasya ca taTatA sarvatraga Adi arTa muKena Alambanam iti atas
# de ni kun du 'gro-ba # 'i don la-sogs-pa # 'i sgo nas de-bzhin-nyid #  la dmigs-pa # s de'i-phyir #  /
jQeya AvaraNa viSudDi jQAna gocarasya tattvam taTatA
# shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i ye shes kyi spyod yul gyi de-kho-na #  ni de-bzhin-nyid #  do /
Pala hetu tattva uktyA sUkzma tattva uktyA ca viSUdDi gocaram dviviDam api / nirdizwam eva iti punar asya viDAnam vyarTam / na vyarTam
# 'bras-bu #  dang rgyu'i de-kho-na #  bshad-pa #  dang phra-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  bshad-pa # s rnam bar dag-pa # 'i spyod yul rnam-pa-gnyis #  kyang bshad-zin #  na / / 'di brjod-pa #  don-med-pa # r mi 'gyur ram zhe na /
yatas tat Pala hetu tattvam sUkzmam ca vastu vyavasTAnataH uktam
# don-med-pa # r mi 'gyur te / / 'di-ltar #  'bras-bu #  dang rgyu'i de-kho-na #  dang phra-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  ni dngos-po #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i phyir bshad do /
atra tu AvaraNam yaTA viSudDyate taTA etat nirdizwam
# 'dir ni sgrib-pa #  ji-ltar #  rnam-par-dag-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  ste /
idam dviviDam viSudDi gocaram ekasmAt parinizpannAt eva svaBAvAt / kIrtitam
# de'i-phyir #  de-skad #  bstan to / / rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i spyod yul 'di rnam-pa-gnyis #  ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  gcig-pu # s brjod de /
atra eva kAraNam Aha na hi anyaH svaBAvaH viSudDi jQAna gocaraH / Bavati iti
# 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  / / ngo-bo-nyid #  gzhan ni rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i ye-shes-rnam-pa-gnyis #  kyi spyod yul ma yin no zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
kim kAraNam / aBUta parikalpasya dOzWulya mala dvayena samala BUta tvAt parikalpitasya / ca asattvAt
# ci'i-phyir #  zhe na yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  ni gnas-ngan-len #  gyi dri-ma #  gnyis kyis dri-ma-can #  du gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro / / kun-brtags-pa #  ni med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
dviviDa jQAna vizayasya tu DarmatAyAH viSudDi vizaya tattvam / parinizpannAt eva vyavasTApyate iti / uktam viSudDi gocara tattvam / saFgraha tattvam / p / tat anantaram tu saFgraha tattvam vaktavyam iti atas pRcCati kaTam
# ye-shes-rnam-pa-gnyis #  kyi yul ni chos-nyid #  yin-pas #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i spyod yul gyi de-kho-na #  ni yongs-su-grub-pa #  nyid kyis rnam-pa # r gzhag go / / rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i spyod yul gyi de-kho-na #  bshad-zin #  to / / de'i-'og-tu #  bsdu-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  brjod dgos te /
triviDe mUla tattve saFgraha tattvam veditavyam iti / saFgraha tattvam triviDe mUla tattve saMgRhItam pradarSayan= Aha
# de'i-phyir #  rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  rnam-pa-gsum #  du bsdu-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  ji-ltar #  rig-par-bya #  zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  rnam-pa-gsum #  du bsdu-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  'dus-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
nimittasya vikalpasya nAmnaH ca dvaya saMgrahaH / iti vistaraH
# rgyu dang rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang / / ming ni rnam-pa-gnyis #  su bsdu / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs te /
dvaye paratantre parikalpite ca saFgrahaH
# gzhan gyi dbang dang kun-brtags-pa #  gnyis su bsdu'o /
tatra saFgraha tattvam paQca vastUni iti atas Aha yaTAyogam paQca / vastUni AraBya iti
# de-la #  bsdu-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  ci-rigs-su #  sbyar ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni gar 'os-pa # r rtsa ba'i de-kho-na # r dngos-po #  lnga dag 'dus-pa # r rig-par-bya-ba # 'i go-rims-bzhin-du #  ni ma yin no /
yaTAyogam mUla tattve paQca vastUni saFgRhItAni veditavyAni na tu / yaTAkramam / paQca punar vastUni nimittam nAma vikalpaH taTatA samyak jQAnam ca iti / sarvasya jQeyasya asmin paQcaviDe vastuni saFgrahAt etat paQcaviDam
# dngos-po #  lnga ni rgyu mtshan dang ming dang rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang de-bzhin-nyid #  dang yang-dag-pa # 'i ye shes te / / shes-par-bya-ba #  thams-cad #  dngos-po #  rnam-pa-lnga-po #  'dir bsdu-ba # 'i phyir dngos-po #  rnam-pa #  'di lnga la bsdu-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  zhes-bya'o #  /
vastu saMgraha tattvam iti ucyate / tatra nimittam AlayavijQAnam klizwa manaH pravRtti vijQAnAni ca / anyaH anya nimitta BAvAt nimittam
# kha-cig #  na re de-la #  rgyu mtshan ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi yid dang 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams te / / phan tshun rgyu'i-dngos-po #  yin-pas #  rgyu mtshan no /
nAma yat tasya eva nimittasya anaBilApyasya api sataH akzi nikoca vat sUcakam
# ming ni rgyu mtshan-gang-yin-pa #  de nyid brjod du med du zin-kyang #  mig brda bzhin-du #  go-ba # r brjod-pa # 'o /
aBiDAnam / yaTA ukta nimitta svaBAva viSeza vikalpakAH trEDAtuka pratisaMyuktAH citta cEttA / vikalpaH / SUnyatA taTatA
# ji-skad-du #  smras-pa # 'i rgyu mtshan gyi rang-bzhin #  dang bye-brag #  tu rnam-par-rtog-pa #  khams-gsum-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  ni rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'o / / stong-pa-nyid #  ni de-bzhin-nyid #  do /
samyak jQAnam loka uttaram taTatA Alambanam
# yang-dag-pa # 'i ye shes ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  ste / / de-bzhin-nyid #  la dmigs-pa # 'o /
kramaH punar ezAm tatra saFkleSa prajQapti vastu tvAt nimittam AdO
# de-dag #  gi go-rims #  ni de-la #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r gdags-pa # 'i dngos-po #  yin-pas #  na dang-por #  rgyu mtshan no /
saFkleSa prajQapti tvAt anantaram nAma
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  zhes btags-pa # 'i phyir de'i-'og-tu #  ming ngo /
yaTA nAma taTA saFkleSa prajQapti vastu vikalpa tvAt tat anantaram / vikalpaH
# ming ji-lta-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r gdags-pa # 'i dngos-po #  la rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i phyir de'i-'og-tu #  rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'o /
sa ca saFkleSaH taTatA samyak jQAnena niruDyate iti tat anantaram / taTatA samyak jQAnaQca iti kecid
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  de-yang #  de-bzhin-nyid #  dang yang-dag-pa # 'i ye shes kyis 'gag-pa # r 'gyur-ba # s na de'i-'og-tu #  de-bzhin-nyid #  dang yang-dag-pa # 'i ye shes so zhe'o /
BrAnti nimittam BrAnti dOzWulyam tat nimittam iti / tasmAt BrAntiH tasya nimittam prakRti SamaH tatra jQAnam / iti anayA gATayA asya paQcaviDasya vastunaH arTaH iti anye
# gzhan dag na re / / 'khrul-pa # 'i rgyu ni 'khrul-pa #  ste / / de yi rgyu ni gnas-ngan-len #  / / de-bas #  'khrul-pa #  de yi rgyu / / rang-bzhin #  zhi bde shes-pa #  / / zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshigs-su-bcad-pa #  'dis dngos-po #  lnga'i don to zhe'o /
tatra ADyAtmika cakzuH Adi vijQAn saMgRhItAyAH BrAnteH nimittam / bAhya ADyAtmikA rUpa Adi cakzuH Adi saMgRhItA BrAntiH / tasyAH bAhya aDyAtimikAyAH BrAnteH nimittam dOzWulyam
# de-la #  nang gi mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # r bsdus-pa #  rnams kyi 'khrul-pa # 'i rgyu ni phyi nang gi gzugs la-sogs-pa #  dang mig la-sogs-pa # r bsdus-pa # 'i 'khrul-pa # 'o / / phyi nang gi 'khrul-pa #  de-dag #  gi rgyu ni gnas-ngan-len #  te /
tat punar AlayavijQAna vAsanA / tasyAH vAsanAyAH nimittam sA eva bAhya ADyAtmika BrAntiH / tasmAt tatra aBilApa pravRttiH
# de-yang #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bag-chags #  so / / bag-chags #  de'i rgyu ni phyi nang gi 'khrul-pa #  de nyid do / / de-lta-bas-na #  de-la #  brjod-pa #  'jug go /
aBilApa vaSAt ca vAsanAyAH avasTAnam Alaya vijQAne
# brjod-pa # 'i dbang gis kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la bag-chags #  gnas so /
prakRti SamaH iti taTatA
# rang-bzhin-gyis #  zhi-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-bzhin-nyid #  de /
prakRtyA klizwa tvAt Darma DAtoH
# rang-bzhin-gyis #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir chos-kyi-dbyings #  so /
tatra ca jQAnam iti taTatA Alambanam mArga saMgRhItam yat jQAnam
# de shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-bzhin-nyid #  la dmigs-pa #  lam-du #  gtogs-pa # 'i ye shes gang-yin-pa # 'o /
tatra nimitta vikalpayoH paratantreNa saFgrahaH hetu pratyaya utpAdita tvAt p
# de-la #  rgyu dang rnam-par-rtog-pa #  gnyis ni rgyu-dang-rkyen #  gyis bskyed-pa # 'i phyir gzhan gyi dbang du bsdu'o /
nAmnaH parikalpitena iti / yaTA nAma arTa aBAvAt nAmnaH parikalpitena saFgrahaH
# ming ni kun-brtags-pa # r zhes-bya-ba #  la ming ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  don-med-pa # s ming ni kun-brtags-pa # r bsdu'o /
evam aDikAra saFgrahaH parikalpitena nAmnaH na svaBAva saFgrahaH iti yat
# de-ltar-na #  skabs yin pa'i phyir kun-brtags-pa # r ming bsdus kyi / / ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  bsdus-pa #  ni ma yin no /
uktam nizsvaBAva sidDa tvAt parikalpitaH svaBAvaH / nimitta Adi paQcavastuBiH na saFgRhItaH iti tat na viruDyate tatra
# ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # r grub-pa #  las kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  ni rgyu la-sogs-pa #  dngos-po #  lngas ma bsdus so zhes gang bshad-pa #  dang 'gal-ba #  med do /
svaBAva saFgrahasya vivakzita tvAt / samyak jQAna sa tattvasya iti
# der ni ngo-bo-nyid #  bsdu-ba # r 'dod-pa'i-phyir #  ro / / yang dag ye shes-rab #  kho-na #  / / zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
sadA SoBanam vA tattvam sa tattvam taTatA SUnyatA AlambanAt vayajQAnam / tat pRzWa labDa SudDa lOkikam ca samyak jQAnam
# rtag-tu # 'am mdzes-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  ste de-bzhin-nyid #  do / / stong-pa-nyid #  la dmigs-pa #  gnyis-su-med-pa # 'i ye shes dang de'i-rjes-la # s thob-pa #  dag-pa #  'jig-rten-pa #  ni yang-dag-pa # 'i ye shes so /
taTatA samyak jQAnayoH avikArA viparyAsa parinizpattyA yaTAkramam / parinizpanna tvAt ekena eva parinizpannena svaBAvena saFgrahaH iti / tat uktam saFgrahatattvam
# de-bzhin-nyid #  dang yang-dag-pa # 'i ye shes de gnyis ni 'gyur-ba-med-pa #  dang phyin-ci-log #  med-pa # 'i yongs-su-grub-pa # s go-rims-bzhin-du #  yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i phyir yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  gcig-pu # s bsdus so / / bsdu-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  bshad-zin #  to /

# rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  la rnam-pa-du-ma #  yod-pa #  dang de rtsa ba'i de-kho-na # r ji-ltar #  bsdu-ba #  mi shes-nas #  de'i-phyir #  /
iti na vijQAyate iti atas pRcCati praBeda tattvam mUla tattve kaTam / veditavyam iti / atas Aha saptaviDam praBeda tattvam
# rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  rtsa ba'i de-kho-na # r ji-ltar #  rig-par-bya #  zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  / / rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  rnam-pa #  bdun te zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
kaTam iti atas Aha pravRtti tattvam lakzaNa tattvam iti vistaraH
# gang zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / 'jug-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  dang mtshan-nyid #  kyi de-kho-na #  zhes-bya-ba #  rgya-cher #  smos te /
yA eva ca sanDi nirmocara nasUtre saptaviDA taTatA nirdizwA / pravRtti taTatAyO= samyak pratipatti taTatA iti sA eva atra saptaviDam / praBeda tattvam iti uktA pravRtti tattvam yAvat samyak pratipatti tattvam iti
# dgongs-pa #  nges-par #  'grel pa las 'jug-pa # 'i de-bzhin-nyid #  nas yang-dag-par-sgrub-pa # 'i de-bzhin-nyid #  kyi bar-du #  de-bzhin-nyid #  rnam-pa #  bdun bka'-stsal-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de nyid 'dir 'jug-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  nas / / yang-dag-par-sgrub-pa # 'i de-kho-na # 'i bar-du #  rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  rnam-pa #  bdun du bshad do /
tatra pravRtti tattvam yA saMsArA anavara agratA sA eva ca pravRtti taTatA / yasmAt na jAtu tasya agra tA yogaH Bavati
# de-la #  'jug-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  ni gang 'khor-ba #  la thog-ma #  dang tha-ma #  med-pa # 'o / / de nyid 'jug-pa # 'i de-bzhin-nyid #  de / / 'di-ltar #  de ni nam yang-thog #  ma dang ldan-pa # r mi 'gyur ro /
lakzaNa tattvam pudgala Darma nErAtmyam p
# mtshan-nyid #  kyi de-kho-na #  ni gang-zag #  dang chos-la-bdag-med-pa #  ste /
ananyatvAt caturviDa lakzaNa taTatA
# gzhan-du-mi-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir de nyid mtshan-nyid #  kyi de-bzhin-nyid #  do /
vijQapti tattvam vijQapti mAtra tA DarmANAm
# rnam-par-rig-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  ni chos-rnams #  kyi rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam nyid do /
nirvikalpam jQAnam vijQapti ASraya BAvAt vijQpti tattvam iti apare
# kha-cig #  na re rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes sam / / rnam-par-rig-pa # 'i gnas 'di ni rnam-par-rig-pa # 'i de-kho-na # 'o zhe'o /
ananyaTABAva tvAt vijQapti tattvasya vijQapti taTatA ucyate
# rnam-par-rig-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  ni gzhan-du-'gyur-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir rnam-par-rig-pa # 'i de-bzhin-nyid #  ces bya'o /

# gnas-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  ni sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  ste / / 'du-byed #  rnam sdug-bsngal-bar-gnas-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de nyid rtag-par #  de-bzhin #  pas na de-bzhin-nyid #  do /

# log-pa # r sgrub-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  ni kun-'byung-ba # 'i bden-pa #  ste /

# de-yang #  gang 'du-byed #  de-dag #  la yon-tan-du-lta-ba # s 'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro /

# yang-dag-par-sgrub-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  dang rnam-par-rig-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  yang lam gyi bden-pa #  nyid do zhe'o / / de-kho-na #  gsum po 'di dag kyang rtag-tu #  de-bzhin #  bas de-bzhin-nyid #  ces bya-ba # r 'gyur ro /
tatra / pravRtti tattvam dviviDam
# de-la #  'jug-pa #  de-kho-na #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  /
mUla tattvam veditavyam parikalpita paratantra lakzaNam / tatra pravRttiH janma nAmana AdimAn prabanDaH / sA ca avidyamAna tvAt parikalpitaH svaBAvaH / yezAm tu sa prabanDazTe hetu praBAvita tvAt paratantraH svaBAvaH
# rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  kun-brtags-pa #  dang gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan-nyid #  du rig-par-bya # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  'jug-pa #  ni tshe'i rgyun thog-ma-med-pa #  can te / / de ni med-pa # s kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  do / / rgyun de su dag gi yin pa de-dag #  ni rgyus rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  de /
evam yezAm yA ca pravRttiH tat pravRtti tattvam iti nirdizwam Bavati
# de-ltar #  gang dag gis yin pa dang 'jug-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni 'jug-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  zhes bstan-pa #  yin no /
aTavA kleSa karma janma nAm anAdimAn utpAdaH saMsAra pravRttiH iti ucyate
# yang-na #  nyon-mongs-pa #  dang las dang tshe rnams kyi 'byung-ba #  thog-ma-med-pa #  can ni 'khor-ba # r 'jug-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
sA ca parikalpita svaBAva aBiniveSa praBAveta iti Aha / pravRtti tattvam dviviDam
# de-yang #  kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  / / 'jug ste kho-na #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  /

# rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / de-bzhin-du #  / / gnas-pa #  dang ni ngan-pa # r zhugs / / zhes-bya-ba #  la log-pa # r sgrub-pa #  ni ngan-pa # r zhugs-pa # 'o /
taTA eva dviviDam mUla tattvam iti duHKa samudayayoH / hetu pratyaya praBAta tvAt parikalpita vizaya tvAt ca / sanniveSa miTyA pratipatti tattvam dviviDe saMgRhItam
# de-bzhin-du #  rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  su'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni sdug-bsngal #  dang kun-'byung-ba #  gnyis rgyu-dang-rkyen #  gyis rab-tu-phye-ba #  dang kun rtog-pa # 'i yul yin pa'i phyir gnas-pa #  dang log-pa # r sgrub-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  su bsdu-ba # 'o / / mtshan-nyid #  rnam-pa # r rig dang dag /

# yang-dag-par-sgrub-pa # 'i de-kho-na # s ni shes-rab #  mnyam-pa # r bstan to / / smras-pa #  / / sems-can #  mnyam-pa # r gsum gyis brjod / / chos-rnams #  mnyam-pa #  gnyis kyis te / / de-ltar #  byang-chub #  blo mnyam-pa # r / / re-re #  rab-tu-bstan-pa #  yin /

# rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i de-kho-na # 'i 'og-tu #  mkhas-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  bshad de / / de-bas-na #  de bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / mkhas de-kho-na #  rnam bcu ni / / bdag-tu-lta-ba # 'i gnyen-po # 'o /
tat punar skanDa Adizu kaTam daSaviDam Atma darSanam iti na jQAyata

iti atas pRcCati kaTam ezu skanDa Adizu daSaviDam Atma darSanam iti / atas Aha
# de'i-phyir #  phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  la bdag-tu-lta-ba #  rnam-pa-bcu-po #  de-dag #  ji lta zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  /

# bdag-po # 'i don dang rtag-pa #  dang / / nyon-mongs-pa #  dang dag-pa # 'i gnas / / rnal-'byor #  can dang ma grol grol / / de-dag #  la ni bdag tu lta / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs te / / phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  la zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro /
eza tu daSaviDaH AtmA asat grAha p / iti AtmanaH asat asat grAhaH iti Aha

yadi AtmA na asti kaTam grAha paratantraH sannirvizayaH grAhaH pravartata

yatas skanDa Adi vyatiriktaH AtmA yuktyA parIkzyamANaH na upalaByate
# 'di-ltar #  phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  ma gtogs bar bdag ces bya-ba #  rigs-pas #  yongs su brtags na dmigs su med do /

# bdag-tu-smra-ba #  dag bdag-gi #  bya-ba #  dang rang-bzhin #  gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  thams-cad #  kyang phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  la 'jug ste / / de'i-phyir #  phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  nyid bdag-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i gzhi-yin-pa # r mngon no /
eBiH daSaviDEH Atma aBiniveSaH nAma Atma grAhaH pravartate na anyEH

pratipakzeNa skanDa kOSalyam

aTavA Atma tvAt sarvam pravartate iti ayam hetu tva grAhaH
# yang-na #  bdag-nyid #  las thams-cad #  'byung ngo snyam pa 'di ni rgyud 'dzin-pa #  ste /
yasya vezwam anizwaQca iha janmani Palam tasya SuBa aSuBasya karmaNaH AtmA / hetuH iti cetanA hetu tva grAhaH
# las dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de'i 'bras-bu #  tshe-'di-la #  'dod-pa #  dang mi-'dod-pa # 'i rgyu bdag yin par sems-pa #  ni rgyur 'dzin-pa # 'o /
BoktR tva grAhaH iti AtmA BoktA cetanatvAt

vyakta avyaktam tu Bojanam acetana tvAt
# gsal-ba #  dang mi-gsal-ba #  ni sems med-pa # 'i phyir bza'-ba # 'o /
aTavA yasya SuBam aSuBam karmaBiH utpadyate saH eva tat PalAnAm / BoktA iti BoktR tva grAhaH
# yang-na #  dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba'i-las #  rnams kyi bar-du #  skye-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de nyid de'i 'bras-bu #  la za-ba # r byed do snyam pa ni za-ba # r 'dzin-pa # 'o /
kartR tva grAhaH iti AtmA eva sukRta duzkRtAnAm karmaNAm kartA iti yaH grAhaH
# byed-pa # r 'dzin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni legs-par-byas-pa #  dang nyes-par-byas-pa # 'i las rnams bdag-nyid-kyis-byed-pa # r 'dzin-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
yaH vA karaNa Adi upetaH tAH tAH kriyAH karoti saH AtmA iti kartR tva grAhaH
# yang-na #  byed-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  gang zhig bya-ba #  de-dang-de-dag #  byed-pa #  ni bdag go zhes byed-pa # r 'dzin-pa # 'o /
svatantra grAhaH iti yat svEram vaSitvam saH AtmA yaH aDikAraH saH AtmA iti / yaH grAhaH
# rang dbang du 'dzin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rang-dgar #  dbang-byed-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni bdag go / / dbang de bya-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni bdag go zhes-bya-ba # r 'dzin-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
hetu anurUpasya eva vA Palasya utpattO vaSitvam asya iti svatantra grAhaH
# yang-na #  rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  'byung-ba #  la dbang byed do snyam pa ni rang dbang du 'dzin-pa # 'o /
aDipati tva grAhaH iti yaH aDipatiH praBuH ISvaraH saH AtmA iti
# bdag-po # r 'dzin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni bdag-po #  dang rje-bo #  dang dbang-phyug #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni bdag go snyam-du #  sems-pa # 'o /
Palasya eva vA anurUpeNa AcaraNam tat aDipati tvAt / AtmA iti aDipati tva grAhaH
# yang-na #  'bras-bu #  dang mthun-par #  de-la #  spyod-pa # 'i bdag-po #  ni bdag go snyam-du #  sems-pa #  ni bdag-po # r 'dzin-pa # 'o /
nitya tva grAhaH iti hetu Adi vastunA paQcaviDenA viSudDaH api AtmA / eva / anyaTA p
# rtag-par #  'dzin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgyu la-sogs-pa #  dngos-po #  rnam-pa-lnga # s rnam-pa # r ma dag kyang bdag rtag-pa #  kho-na # 'o /
tu akRta aByAgamaH kRtasya nASaH ca / taTA smRteH pratyaBijQAnasya ca aBAvaH prasajyate
# gzhan-du-na # m byas-pa #  dang phrad-pa #  dang byas-pa #  chud-zos-pa #  dang de-bzhin-du #  dran-pa #  dang so-so # r ngo shes-pa #  yang med-pa # r 'gyur ro /
saFklizwa vyavadAna tva grAhaH iti saFkleSa vyavadAna ASraya tvAt / yogi tva grAhaH iti Atmani manasaH DAraNam yogaH prANa manasoH vA nigrahaH
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # r 'dzin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i rten yin pa'i phyir ro / / rnal-'byor #  can du 'dzin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la / / bdag la yid 'dzin-pa #  ni rnal-'byor #  ro /
AtmanaH manasAm saMyoga viSezaH yogaH saH asyAH asti iti yogI
# yang-na #  dbugs dang yid 'gog-pa # 'o / / bdag dang yid sbyor-ba # 'i khyad-par #  ni rnal-'byor #  te / / de-la #  'di yod-pa #  ni rnal-'byor #  can no /
amukta mukta tva grAhaH ca iti AtamnaH banDAt vimuktiH iti yaH vikalpaH
# ma grol ba dang grol ba 'dzin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni bdag sngar bcings-pa #  las grol lo snyam-du #  rnam-par-rtog-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
kaTam idam daSaviDam kOSalya tattvam mUla tattve antar Bavati iti
# mkhas-pa #  rnam-pa-bcu-po #  'di dag rtsa ba'i de-kho-na # r ji-ltar #  'du-shes #  na zhes-bya-ba #  la /
kOSalyam hi skanDa Adizu vEcakzaNyam / tat kaTam trizu svaBAvezu antarBavati / asamBAvayataH praSnaH
# mkhas-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  la mkhas-pa #  yin na / / de ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum po dag tu ji-ltar #  'dus te / / mi srid do snyam nas dris-pa # 'o /
yatas trizu svaBAvezu te skanDa AdayaH antarBUtAH iti kOSalyavizayAH ete / kOSalya Sabdena udBAvitAH / na tu tasmin= eva kOSalyaH iti / atas akuSalya tattvasya api aDikArataH tatra antar BAvaH na tu svarUpataH iti
# 'di-ltar #  ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum du phung-po #  lnga la-sogs-pa #  de-dag #  'dus so zhes-bya-ba #  ni mkhas-pa # 'i yul la 'dir mkhas-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgrar brjod kyi mkhas-pa #  de nyid ma yin te / / de-lta-bas-na #  mkhas-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  skabs kyis der bsdu-ba'i-dngos-po #  ni ma-yin-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste /
veditavyam tat yaTA Pala hetu tattva mArga satyam trizu antarBUtam uktam iti / nanu evam api na eva vijQAyante yaTA antarBUtAH iti pRcCati kaTam / antarBUtAH iti atas ca Aha / parikalpa vikalpa arTa Darma tA arTena tezu te iti
# 'di-lta-ste-dper-na #  'bras-bu #  dang rgyu'i de-kho-na #  lam gyi bden-pa #  gsum du 'dus-pa # r bshad-pa #  lta-bu # 'o / / de nyid ji lta 'dus-pa # 'ang ma shes-nas #  / / ji-ltar #  'dus shes na zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  / / kun du rtog dang rnam rtog don / / chos-nyid #  don gyi de-dag #  der /
tezu trizu svaBAvezu te skanDa AdayaH antarBUtAH iti aDikRtam
# zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs te / / ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum du phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  de-dag #  'dus so zhes-bya-ba # 'i skabs yin no /
tatra DAtu AdiByaH pUrvam skanDAnAm antar BUta tvam prakASayitavyam / praTamam nirdizwa tvAt tatra api rUpasya iti p
# de-la #  khams la-sogs-pa #  pas sngar bstan-pa # 'i phyir phung-po #  rnams thog-mar #  bsdus la bshad-par-bya # 'o / / de-dag #  las kyang gzugs su bsdu-ba # r bya ste /
atas Aha triviDam rUpam / kaTam / parikalpitam rUpam vikalpitam rUpam Darma tA rUpa Qca / tatra kim parikalpitam rUpam / yaH rUpasya parikalpitaH svaBAvaH iti
# de'i-phyir #  gzugs la rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / gang zhe na kun-brtags-pa # 'i gzugs dang; rnam-par-brtags-pa # 'i gzugs dang chos-nyid #  kyi gzugs so / / de-la #  kun-brtags-pa # 'i gzugs gang zhe na /
tat ca yA anyatra nAmnA upalabDiH tatra vizaya svaBAvaH parikalpyate / saH atyantam asattvAt parikalpitaH iti ucyate
# gang gzugs kyi kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  do zhes-bya-ba #  ni da'ang gang ming du dmigs-pa #  ma-gtogs-par #  de-la #  yul gyi ngo bo dngos-po # r yongs-su-rtog-pa #  ste; de gtan med-pa # 'i phyir kun brtags zhes-bya'o #  /
vikalpitam rUpam yaH rUpasya paratantraH svaBAvaH iti / hetu pratyaya pratibadDaH iti arTaH
# rnam-par-brtags-pa # 'i gzugs ni gang gzugs ni gang gzugs gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  do zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgyu-dang-rkyen #  la rag las zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
kim arTam punar idam vikalpitam rUpam ucyate iti atas Aha tatra hi
# ci'i-phyir #  'di rnam-par-brtags-pa # 'i gzugs zhes bya zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  de-la #  gzugs su rnam-par-rtog-pa # r byed do zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
rUpa vikalpaH kriyate iti / yasmAt rUpa KyAta vijQAne adRzwa tattvEH aparijQAta rUpa saMjQa tvAt / rUpa aBiniveSaH kriyate yaTA skanDezu Atma grAhaH / tasmAt paratantre vikalpitam rUpam iti ucyate / Darma tA rUpam yaH rUpasya parinizpannaH svaBAvaH iti / tat vikalpa rUpa parikalpita rUpa vigata AtmikA SUnya tA / yaTA rUpam iti / yaTA rUpam triDA BittvA trizu svaBAvezu antar BAvitam evam / vedanA AdayaH skanDa DAtu AdayaH ca yojyAH iti / vedanA saMjQA saMskAra vijQAna skanDAH DAtu AyatanAni / pratItyasamutpAda aFgAni Ayatana anyatana aniindriyANi aDva trayam / satya catuzwayam yAna trayam saMskRta asaMskRtaQca iti etat api vedanA Adikam / DAtu Adi paQca pratyekam parikalpita vikalpita Darma tA svaBAva BedataH / triDA BittvA trizu svaBAvezu antar BAvayitavyam / tatra pratiBAsezu vedanA Adizu yaH atyantam asat BUtaH grAhya grAhaka BAvaH / rUpa pratiBAsezu yaTA grAhya BAvaH parikalpyate sA parikalpitA
# 'di-ltar #  de-kho-na #  ma-mthong-ba #  rnams kyis yongs su ma shes te / / gzugs su snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  la gzugs su 'du-shes #  nas gzugs la mngon-par-zhen-pa # r byed de / / dper-na #  phung-po #  la bdag-tu-'dzin-pa #  bzhin no / / de-bas-na #  gzhan gyi dbang la rnam-par-brtags-pa # 'i gzugs zhes-bya'o #  / / chos-nyid #  kyi gzugs ni gang gzugs kyis yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  do zhes-bya-ba #  de ni rnam-par-brtags-pa # 'i gzugs dang kun-brtags-pa # 'i gzugs de-dag #  dang bral-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  stong-pa-nyid #  do / / gzugs ji-lta-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs la gsum du phye ste ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum du bsdus-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i phung-po #  rnams dang khams dang skye-mched #  la-sogs-pa #  la yang sbyar-ba # r bya'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang 'du-byed #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i phung-po #  dang khams dang; skye-mched #  rnams dang rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba # 'i yan-lag #  rnams dang gnas dang gnas-ma-yin-pa #  dang dbang-po #  rnams dang dus-gsum #  dang bden-pa #  bzhi dang theg-pa-gsum #  dang 'dus byas dang 'dus-ma-byas #  te tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dang khams la-sogs-pa #  de-dag #  kyang kun-brtags-pa #  dang rnam-par-brtags-pa #  dang chos-nyid #  kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi bye-brag #  gis rnam-pa-gsum #  gsum du phye ste / / ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum du bsdu-ba # r bya'o / / de-la #  gzugs su snang-ba #  rnams la gzung-ba # 'i dngos-po # r rtog-pa #  bzhin-du #  tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa # r snang-ba #  de-la #  / / gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i dngos-po #  gtan med-pa #  bzhin-du #  yang kun rtog-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de kun-brtags-pa # 'i tshor-ba #  nas kun-brtags-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o /
vedanA yAvat parikalpitam vijQAnam / yasmin grAhya grAhekaH vikalpaH kriyate sA vikalpitA vedanA yAvat / vikalpitam vijQAnam / Darma tA vedanAH yaH vedanAyAH parinizpannaH svaBAvaH
# gang-la #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r rtog-par-byed-pa #  de ni rnam-par-brtags-pa # 'i tshor-ba #  nas rnam-par-brtags-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o / / chos-nyid #  kyi tshor-ba #  ni gang tshor-ba # 'i yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  de /
evam yAvat Darma tA vijQAnam veditavyam / evam DAtu Ayatana Adizu api yaTAsaMBavam vistareNa vaktavyam
# chos-nyid-kyi-rnam-pa # r shes-pa # 'i bar-du #  de-bzhin-du #  brjod-pa # r bya'o / / de-bzhin-du #  khams dang skye-mched #  rnams la yang ci-rigs-par #  rgyas-pa # r brjod-pa # r bya'o /
rUpa vedane yAvat saMskRta asaMskRtam iti yaH nAma aBiDeyaH BAvaH saH api / porikalpita paratantra parinizpanna svaBAvaH veditavyaH / kaTam
# gzugs dang tshor-ba #  nas 'dus byas dang 'dus-ma-byas #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  ming gis brjod-par-bya-ba # 'i dngos-po #  gang-yin-pa #  de-yang #  kun-brtags-pa #  dang gzhan gyi dbang dang yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra rUpa Adi svaBAva prajQapta tvAt parikalpitaH / prajQapti aDizWAna BAvAt paratantraH pratyaya paratantra tvAt tasya eva / rUpa Adi BAva atyanta vigata tvam parinizpannaH
# ji lta zhe na / / de-la #  gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du brtags-pa # 'i phyir kun-brtags-pa # 'o / / gdags-pa # 'i gnas-kyi-dngos-po #  yin-pas #  gzhan gyi dbang ste / / de nyid rkyen-gzhan #  la rag-las-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i dngos-po #  dang gtan dang bral-ba-nyid #  yongs-su-grub-pa # 'o; /
nanu paratantre eva manuzya Adi BAvena nAmnA ucyate na parikalpitaH iti / anarTaka / p / eva parikalpita vikalpaH / na anarTakaH
# gzhan gyi dbang nyid gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i dngos-po # r ming du brjod kyi kun-brtags-pa # 'i ni ma yin no / / kun-brtags-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  don-med-pa #  nyid-du #  mi 'gyur ram zhe na /
tatra manuzya Adi svaBAvasya aDyAropita tvAt
# don-med-pa #  ma yin te / / de-la #  gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du sgro-btags-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yaTA hi nAma arTe pravartate taTA taTA eva na asti / bAlaH tu tat svaBAvam aBiniviSanti tat ca miTyA aDyavasitam na tu / BUta arTena iti / kutas etat / nAma arTayoH sArUpye vErUpye ca vAcya vAcaka BAva vyAvRttitaH
# ji-lta-ji-lta #  bur don la ming 'jug-pa #  de lta de-lta-bu # r med mod kyi byis-pa #  rnams de'i-ngo-bo-nyid #  du mngon-pa # r zhen to / / de'ang log-pa # r mngon-par-zhen-pa #  yin gyi yang-dag-pa'i-don #  du-ma #  yin par ci mngon zhe na / / mthun nam mi mthun yang rung ste / / ming-dang-don #  gnyis kyis brjod-par-bya-ba #  dang rjod pa'i dngos-po #  ldog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yadi vRkza Adi SabdAnAm tat arTAnAm ca aBinna rUpa tA evam nAmnaH / tad arTam rUpA avyatirekAt vAcaka tvam vyAvartyate arTavat
# gal-te #  shing la-sogs-pa # 'i sgra dang de-dag #  gi don rnams tha-dad-pa # 'i ngo bo ma yin-du-zin #  na / / de lta na ni ming dang de-dag #  gi don gyi ngo bo tha-mi-dad-pa # 'i phyir don bzhin-du #  brjod-pa #  ldog-pa # r 'gyur ro /
arTasya api nAma svarUpA avyatirekAt vAcya tvam vihIyate / niyama hetu aBAvAt
# don kyang ming gi ngo bo dang tha mi dad na brjod-par-bya-ba #  las nyams-pa # r 'gyur te nges-pa # 'i rgyu-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
namnaH api vA anyat vAcaka arTasya ca vAcyam prasajyata / iti anavasTA prasaFgAT / ekasya ca arTasya nAma bahutve nAmnaH ca arTa bahutve aneka rUpa tA prasajyate / ekasya tu bahu svarUpa tvam na yujyate
# yang-na #  ming gis brjod-pa #  yang gzhan la don gyi brjod-par-bya-ba #  yang gzhan-du-'gyur-ba # s thug-pa #  med-pa # r 'gyur ro / / don gcig la ming mang-po # 'am / / ming gcig la yang don mang-po # r gyur na du-ma # 'i ngo bor 'gyur te / / gcig ni du-ma # 'i ngo bor mi rung ngo /
aBAva vAcakAnAm arTavatAm asattvam tat arTasya aBAva rUpa tvAt tat
# dngos-po-med-pa # 'i brjod-pa #  dag kyang don bzhin-du #  med-pa # r 'gyur te / / de'i don dngos-po-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
arTasya api vA sattvam nAmnaH astitvAt iti / vErUpye api Sabda anurUpyeNa arTa pratyaya aBAvaH / SabdaH eva hi tatra vRkzaH na arTaH
# yang-na #  ming yod-pa # 'i phyir de'i don kyang yod-pa # r 'gyur ro / / mi-mthun-pa #  yang sgra dang mthun-par #  don shes-pa #  med de / / de-la #  shing ni sgra nyid de don ni ma yin no /
arTaH tu na vRkzaH na api avRkzaH / tasmAt vRkza Sabda arTasya na vRkza jQAna vizaya tvam tat
# don ni shing yang ma yin shing ma-yin-pa # 'ang ma yin no / / de'i-phyir #  shing gi sgra'i don ni shing zhes pa'i yul du mi 'gyur te /
arTasyA avRkza Atmaka tvAt
# de'i don ni shing gi bdag-nyid #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tat viDaQca Sabda arTayoH vAcya vAcaka BAva vyAvRttiH / vElakzaNye ca vAcya vAcaka niyamaH na syAt niyama kAraNa aBAvAt
# de-ltar #  sgra dang don gnyis rjod pa dang brjod-par-bya-ba # 'i dngos-po #  las ldog go / / mi mthun na yang nges-pa # 'i rgyu-med-pa # 'i phyir rjod pa dang brjod-par-bya-ba #  nges-pa-med-pa # r 'gyur ro /
nAma ca arTam utpAdayet aBivyaQjayet vA
# ming gis don bskyed dam gsal-ba # r byed grang na /
tatra na utpAdayati utpanne arTe nAma karaNAt
# de-la #  skyed-par-byed-pa #  ni ma yin te / / skyes zin-pa # 'i don la ming 'dogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
utpannaH api punar punar utpAdayitavyaH iti prasaFga punar panar / nAmakaraNAt / na api aBivyaQjayati yasmAt arTam gRhItvA nAma kriyate na ca / gRhItasya aBivyaQjakam yuktam / tena eva nAmnA tam eva arTam anyaH na gRhNAti yaH tat na jAnAti / tat eva tasya eva arTasya aBivyaQjakam ca anaBivyaQja kaQcA iti na yuktam
# yang-dang-yang #  ming 'dogs-pa # s skyes zin-pa #  yang yang-dang-yang #  bskyed dgos-pa # r thal-ba # r yang 'gyur ro / / gsal-bar-byed-pa #  yang ma yin te / / 'di-ltar #  don rtogs-nas #  ming 'dogs na rtogs zin-pa #  la ni gsal-ba # r bya-ba #  mi rigs so / / ming de nyid kyis don de nyid yin par su de mi-shes-pa #  gzhan dag gis ni mi rtogs so / / de nyid don de nyid gsal-bar-byed-pa #  yang yin /
na aBivyaQjaka pradIpa AdayaH vyaFgyam arTam vyutpatti apekzAH vyaQjayanti
# gsal-ba # r mi-byed-pa #  yang yin zhes-bya-ba # r ni mi rung ste / / gsal-bar-byed-pa #  sgron-ma #  la-sogs-pa #  dag ni gsal-ba # r bya-ba # 'i don shes-pa #  la ltos nas gsal-bar-byed-pa #  ma yin no /
na ca vyaFgyezu Gawa pawa Adizu vyaQjaka niyamaH dRzwaH iti sarvaH arTaH / sarveNa nAmnA aBivyajyeta
# gsal-ba # r bya-ba #  bum-pa #  dang snam-bu #  la-sogs-pa #  la gsal-bar-byed-pa #  nges-pa #  yang ma-mthong-ba # s don-thams-cad #  la ming thams-cad-kyi # s gsal-bar-byed-pa # r 'gyur du 'ong ngo /
na ca ganDa Adizu niyama aBAvaH
# dri la-sogs-pa # s nges-pa #  yang ma yin te /
yatmAt kuTA rajala AdInAm ganDa Adi utpAdayitR tvam izwam na tu / vyaQjaka tvam p
# 'di-ltar #  ste'u dang chu la-sogs-pa #  ni dri la-sogs-pa # 'i skyed-pa #  por 'dod kyi gsal-bar-byed-pa #  ni ma yin no /
tasmAt vAcya vAcaka aBiniveSaH grAhya grAhaka aBiniveSa vat asat arTam / eva iti pratIyate
# de-bas-na #  rjod pa dang brjod-par-bya-ba #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  bzhin-du #  don-med-pa #  nyid-du #  mngon no /
evam trizu svaBAvezu skanDa AdInAm anantarBAvAt daSaviDam / kOSalya tattvam mUla tattvaH eva drazwavyam
# de-ltar-na #  ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum du phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  'dus-pa # 'i phyir mkhas-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  rnam-pa-bcu #  ni rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  nyid-du #  blta'o /
skanDa Adi kOSalyam idam idam
# bdag-tu-lta-ba # 'i gnyen-po # r phung-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i don ni bshad de /
yasmin tu arTe skanDa Adi kOSalyam vipakza Atma dRzwa pratipakzaH / skanDa Adi arTaH na uktaH iti atas saH idAnIm ucyate / skanDa arTaH / amekartva aBisaFkzepa paricCeda arTaH Aditas / Aditas iti AdO= ucyate iti sambaDyate / Aditas tAvat skanDAH ucyante / te ca triviDena arTena veditavyAH / aneka tva arTena yat kiQcid rUpam atIta anAgata pratyutpannam ADyAtmikam
# don gang-la #  phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  la mkhas-pa # 'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  bdag-tu-lta-ba #  phung-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i don ni ma bshad-pa # s de brjod-pa # r bya ste / / thog-mar #  du-ma #  nyid dang ni / / bsdus dang yongs su phye-ba # 'i don / / zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / thog-mar #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni dang-por #  brjod do zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro / / de-la #  thog-ma-kho-nar #  phung-po #  bshad de / / de-dag #  kyang don rnam-pa-gsum #  du rig-par-bya #  ste / / du-ma # 'i don ni gzugs gang-ci # 'ang rung ste /
vA bAhyam vA OdArikam vA sUkzmam vA hInam vA praNItam vA yat vA / dUre yat vA ntike iti evam aneka arTena bahUnAm
# 'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  dang da-ltar-byung-ba # 'am nang gi'am phyi'i'am rags-pa # 'am phra-ba #  'am ngan-pa # 'am gya-nom-pa # 'am rgyang-ring-po # 'am thag-nye-ba #  de-lta-bu #  dag ni du-ma # 'i don te /
dravyANAm skanDa Sabdena ukta tvAt / aBisaFkzipya iti vacanAt aBisaMkzepa arTena skanDaH iti / aBisaMkzipta iti ekIkRtya
# 'das-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rdzas mang-po #  dag la phung-po #  zhes brjod-pa # 'i phyir ro / / bsdus-pa # 'i don ni phung-po #  ste / / bsdus nas gcig-tu #  byas-pa # 'o /
paricCeda arTena ca skanDaH iti sambaDyate / caSabdaH samuccaya arTaH aneka arTa aBisaMkzepa arTa dvayasya api
# yongs su phye-ba # 'i don yang phung-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  dang sbyar te / / kyang zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni du-ma # 'i don dang bsdus-pa # 'i don gnyis kyang bsdu-ba # 'i don to /
atra kAraNam Aha skanDAnAm rUpa Adi lakzaNasya vedanA Adi lakzaNeByaH / pRTak vyavasTApanAt iti / pRTak paricCinnaH iti paryAyaH
# 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  / / gzugs kyi mtshan-nyid #  kyi phung-po #  ni tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  las tha dad du rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
kim atra kAraNam eBiH triBiH aFgEH skanDa arTaH vyavasTApyate
# tha-dad-pa #  yang yongs su phye-ba #  ni rnam-grangs #  su gtogs-pa # 'o / / 'dir ci'i-phyir #  na yan-lag #  'di gsum gyi phung-po # 'i don rnam-pa # r gzhag ce na /
rASi arTaH hi skanDa arTaH iti atas evam vyavasTApyate / eva Qca loke rASi arTaH dRzwaH / yaH anekaH aBisaMkzItaH paricCinnaH sa rASiH iti ucyate / yaTA rUpa skanDaH evam vedanA AdayaH api skanDAH veditavyAH / tatra yaH ayam eka Atma grAhaH yaTA puruzaH eva idam sarvam yat BUtam yat ca / BAvyam ityAdi tasya p / pratipakzeNa yaTA skanDa arTe kOSalyam kAryam taTA uktam / kaTam iti
# phung-po # 'i don ni spungs pa'i don te zhes-bya-ba # s na de'i-phyir #  de-ltar #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ste / / 'jig-rten #  na yang mthong-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de-ltar #  'jig-rten #  na yang du-ma #  dang bsdus-pa #  dang yongs su phye-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  ni spungs pa zhes brjod-pa # r mthong ngo / / gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  ji-lta-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  tshor-ba'i-phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  yang rig-par-bya # 'o / / de-la #  ji-ltar #  byung-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  dang 'byung-bar-'gyur-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  'di dag thams-cad #  ni skyes-bu #  yin no zhes bdag gcig-pu # r 'dzin-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de'i gnyen-po # r ji nas phung-po # 'i don la mkhas-par-bya-ba #  bshad de / / ji lta zhe na /
atIta Adi Binna rUpa Adizu EkaDyam aBisaMkziptezu / rUpa Adi skanDa prajQApanAt / etat ca triviDa sammoha pratipakzeNa triviDa skanDa vyavasTApanam
# 'das-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  tha-dad-pa # 'i gzugs la-sogs-pa # r gcig-tu-bsdus-pa #  rnams la gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i phung-po # r gdags-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-yang #  rmongs-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  gyi gnyen-po #  phung-po #  rnam gsum gzhag ste /
triviDaH sammohaH ekatva sammohaH saMvRti sammohaH lakzaNa saFkIrNa sammohaH / ca / DAtvarTaH / skanDa arTa anantaram DAtavaH uddizwAH
# rmongs-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  ni gcig-tu #  rmongs-pa #  dang bzlum pa la rmongs-pa #  dang mtshan-nyid #  'dres-pa #  la rmongs-pa # 'o / / phung-po # 'i 'og-tu #  khams rnams bstan te /
tasmAt skanDa arTa anataram DAtvarTam Aha
# de-bas-na #  phung-po # 'i don gyi 'og-tu #  khams-kyi-don #  gsungs-pa #  /
grAhaka grAhya tat grAha vIrya arTaH ca aparaH mataH iti
# 'dzin dang gzung dang de 'dzin-pa #  / / sa-bon #  don de gzhan-du #  'dod / / ces bya-ba # 'o /
apara SabdaH atra DAtO= eva sambaDyate skanDa anantaram uddizwa tvAt / atas eva BAzyakAraH api Aha katamaH aparaH / DAtuH iti
# gzhan zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni khams nyid dang sbyar te phung-po # 'i 'og-tu #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de'i-phyir #  bshad-pa #  byed-pa # s kyang / / gzhan gang zhe na /
bIja arTaH DAtu arTaH tat yaTA svarNaH sati svarNaDAtuH ucyate
# khams so zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / sa-bon #  gyi don ni khams-kyi-don #  te / / dper-na #  gser yod-pa # 'i rdo-rje #  la gser gyi khams zhes-bya-ba #  ste /
svarNa bIjam iti gamyate
# gser gyi sa-bon #  zhes-bya-ba # r mngon-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
sa ca Pala BedAt triDA Bidyate grAhaka DAtuH grAhya DAtuH tat / grAha DAtuH ca
# de-yang #  'bras-bu #  tha-dad-pa # s rnam-pa-gsum #  du dbye ste / / 'dzin-pa # 'i khams dang gzung-ba # 'i khams dang de 'dzin-pa # 'i khams so /
tatra grAhaka bIja arTaH cakzuH DAtu AdayaH / cakzuH DAtuH AdiH yezAm manaH paryantAH te cakzuH DAtu AdayaH
# de-la #  'dzin-pa # 'i sa-bon #  gyi don ni mig gi khams la-sogs-pa #  ste; gang dag mig gi khams nas yid kyi khams la thug gi bar gyi khams de-dag #  mig gi khams la-sogs-pa # 'o /
te ca rUpa Adi vizaya grAha ASraya BUta tvAt grAhakAH
# de-dag #  kyang gzugs la-sogs-pa #  yul 'dzin-pa # 'i gnas-su-gyur-pa # 'i phyir 'dzin-pa #  dag go /
sajAtIyAnAm cakzuH AdInAm hetu tvAt DAtavaH ucyante
# rigs mthun-pa # 'i mig la-sogs-pa #  dag gi rgyu yin pa'i phyir khams rnams zhes-bya'o #  /
grAhya bIja arTaH rUpa DAtu AdayaH Darma DAtu paryantAH
# gzung-ba # 'i sa-bon #  gyi don gzugs-kyi-khams #  la-sogs-pa #  nas chos-kyi-khams #  la thug gi bar dag go /
cakzuH Adi vijQAna vizaya tvAt grAhyAH
# mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i yul yin pa'i phyir gzung-ba #  dag go /
te api evam saBAgAnAm rUpa AdInAm hetu BAvAt DAtavaH ucyante
# de-dag #  kyang de-bzhin-du #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  mtshungs-pa #  rnams kyi rgyu'i-dngos-po #  yin-pas #  khams rnams zhes-bya'o #  /
tat grAha bIja arTaH cakzuH vijQAna DAtu AdayaH
# de 'dzin-pa # 'i sa-bon #  gyi don ni mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  la-sogs-pa #  ste /
rUpa Adi pratipatti svaBAva tvAt rUpa Adi grAhAH cakzuH vijQAna AdayaH / manaH vijQAna paryantAH
# gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la shes-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  yin-pas #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la 'dzin-pa #  mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  nas yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la thug gi bar dag go /
te api saBAgAnAm eva cakzuH Adi vijQAnAnAm hetu BUta tvAt DAtava / ucyante cakzuH vijQAna DAtu AdayaH manaH vijQAna DAtu paryantAH
# de-dag #  kyang mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  mtshungs-pa #  rnams kyi rgyur-gyur-pa # 'i phyir khams rnams zhes bya ste / / mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  nas yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  kyi bar dag go /
anye tu AhuH cakzuH Adi aBiniveSa karma vAsitam AlayavijQAnam / yaTAkramam cakzuH AdInAm bIjam
# kha-cig #  na re mig la-sogs-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i las kyi bag-chags #  bsgos-pa # 'i kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni mig la-sogs-pa # 'i sa-bon #  te go-rims #  bzhin no /
taTA rUpa Adi aBiniveSa karma vAsitam AlayavijQAnam yaTAkramam / rUpa AdInAm bIjam
# de-bzhin-du #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i las kyi bag-chags #  bsgos-pa # 'i kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i sa-bon #  te go-rims #  bzhin no /
taTA cakzuH Adi vijQAna aBiniveSa karma vAsitam AlayavijQAnam eva / cakzuH Adi vijQAnAnAm yaTAkramam bIjam iti
# de-bzhin-du #  mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i las kyi bag-chags #  bsgos-pa # 'i kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i sa-bon #  te go-rims #  bzhin no /
evam tu Alaya vijQAnam eva DAtu Sabda vAcyam na cakzuH AdayaH iti cintyam / etat
# de-ltar-na #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid la khams zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgrar brjod kyi / / mig la-sogs-pa #  la ni mi bya'o zhes te / / 'di ni bsam dgos-pa # 'o /
kartR kriyA karma sammoha vyAvartana arTam triviDe bIja arTe DAtuH / vyavasTApitaH
# byed-pa #  dang bya-ba #  dang las rnams la rmongs-pa #  ldog-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir sa-bon #  gyi don rnam-pa-gsum #  la khams rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
atra pUrva cakzuH AdayaH uttara cakzuH AdInAm eva hetavaH Bavanti na
# 'di-la #  mig la-sogs-pa #  snga-ma #  ni mig la-sogs-pa #  phyi-ma #  dag gi rgyur-gyur-pa #  yin gyi /
tatra anyaH kaScid AtmA anyaH vA hetu vidyate iti evam DAtu kOSalyAt / Atmani hetu grAha vyAvRttiH p
# 'di-la #  rgyu bdag ces bya-ba #  gzhan gang yang med do / / de-ltar-na #  khams la mkhas na bdag la rgyur 'dzin-pa #  ldog-pa # r 'gyur ro /
Ayatana arTaH / DAtvarTa anantaram AyatanAnAm arTaH vaktavyaH / atas Aha
# khams-kyi-don #  gyi 'og-tu #  skye-mched #  rnams kyi don brjod-pa # r bya ste / / de'i-phyir #  /
vedita arTa paricCeda BogAya dvArataH aparam iti
# tshor dang don rnams yongs gcod kyi / / nyer spyod 'byung sgo gzhan yin no / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so /
DAtoH aparANAm hi Ayatana pratItyasamutpAda AdInAm bahu tvAt / apara Sabdasya ca sAmAnya tvAt praSnaH kim aparam iti
# khams rnams las gzhan-pa #  ni skye-mched #  dang rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  mang zhig kyang yod-la #  / / gzhan zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni spyir brjod-pa # 'i phyir /
DAtuByaH anantaram uddizwa tvAt arTataH Ayatanezu eva ayam / apara SabdaH avatizWate iti jQApana arTam Aha Ayatanam iti
# gzhan gang yin zhes dris-pa #  dang khams rnams kyi 'og-tu #  bshad-pa # 'i phyir don-gyis-na #  skye-mched #  rnams las gzhan zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra 'di gnas-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / skye-mched #  do zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tatra vedita upaBogAya dvAra arTena zaXa ADyAtmikAni AyatanAni
# de-la #  nang gi skye-mched-drug #  po dag ni tshor-ba # 'i nye-bar-spyod-pa #  skye-ba # 'i sgo'i phyir ro /
arTa paricCeda upaBogAya dvAra arTena zakRt bAhyAni iti
# phyi'i drug-po #  dag ni don yongs su gcod-pa # 'i nye-bar-spyod-pa #  skye-ba # 'i sgo'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  la /
Aya dvAra arTam Ayatana arTaH
# skye-ba # 'i sgo'i don ni skye-mched #  kyi don to /
Aya AgamaH / tam vedita arTa paricCeda upaBogayoH tanvanti iti AyatanAni
# skye-ba #  ni 'byung-ba #  ste tshor-ba #  dang don yongs su gcod-pa # 'i nye-bar-spyod-pa #  gnyis kyi skye-ba #  de mched par byed-pa # s skye-mched #  do /
vedita saMjQa upaBogAya dvAra iBedana ADyAtmika bAhya praBedaH
# tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  kyi nye-bar-spyod-pa #  skye-ba # 'i sgo'i bye-brag #  gis phyi dang nang-du #  dbye ste /
veditam hi suKa duHKA aduHduHKA asuKam / tat eva upaBujyate iti upaBogaH
# tshor-ba #  ni bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  dang bde-ba #  yang ma yin sdug-bsngal #  yang ma-yin-pa # 'o / / de nyid nye-bar-spyod-pa # s na nye-bar-spyod-pa #  ste /
anuBUyate iti arTaH
# myong-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
tasya vedanA upaBogasya Aya dvAram ADyAtimkAni eva AyatanAni uktAni
# nang gi skye-mched #  rnams ni tshor-ba # 'i nye-bar-spyod-pa #  de skye-ba # 'i sgor bshad do /
sati api vizayANAm tat Aya dvAra BAve cakzuH AdInAm ASrayANAm / anugraha upaGAta tvena tat pravINa tvena ca asADAraNa tvena ASraya tvAt sati
# yul rnams kyang de skye-ba # 'i sgo yin mod kyi gnas mig la-sogs-pa #  ni phan-'dogs-pa #  dang gnod-pa-byed-pa #  dang de-la #  yang rab-tu-shes-pa #  dang thun-mong-ma-yin-pa # s gnas-su-gyur-pa # 'i phyir mig la-sogs-pa #  yod-na #  de'i sgo nas tshor-ba #  las spyod-pa # r 'gyur gyi /
cakzuH AdO tad dvAreNa vedanA upaBogAn na asti iti / arTa paricCedaH saMjQA arTa nimitta udgrahaNa Atmaka tvAt
# med na ni ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro / / don yongs su gcod-pa #  ni 'du-shes #  te / / don la mtshan-mar-'dzin-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  phyir ro /
sA eva arTa pratipatti Atmaka tvAt vizayam upaBuFkte / tat Aya dvAra BAvena bAhyAni AyatanAni uktAni na tu ADyAtmikAni / sati api tat Aya dvAra BAve yasmAt
# de nyid don rtogs-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin-pas #  yul rnams la nyer bar spyod do / / de skye-ba # 'i sngos po'i sgo yin-pas #  ni phyi-rol-gyi-skye-mched #  rnams bshad kyi / / nang gi rnams ni ma yin te /
vizaya aBAve arTa paricCeda upaBoga aBAvaH sati api ADyAtmike / cakzuH Adi Ayatane
# sgye ba'i sgo yin-du-zin #  kyang 'di-ltar #  yul-gyi-dngos-po #  med na nang gi mig la-sogs-pa # 'i skye-mched #  yod kyang don yongs su gcod-pa #  la nye-bar-spyod-pa #  med-pa # r 'gyur ro /
vedita arTa paricCedayoH sa samprayogayoH ayadvAra BAva tvAt / etAni AyatanAni veditavyAni / praDAnam hi dvaya grahaNam
# tshor-ba #  dang don yongs su gcod-pa #  mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  dag skye-ba # 'i sgo'i dngos-po #  yin pa'i phyir skye-mched #  'di dag rig-par-bya #  ste / / gtso bor ni gnyis gzung ngo /
grahaNa prADAnyam punar karma Pala upaBogAt arTa paricCeda Atmaka tvAt ca
# gtso bor gzung-ba #  ni las-kyi-'bras-bu #  la spyod-pa #  dang don yongs su gcod-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
vedita arTa paricCeda upaBoga muKena BoktR vikalpaH pravartate iti atas
# tshor-ba #  dang don yongs su gcod-pa #  la nye-bar-spyod-pa # 'i sgo nas za-ba-po # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  'byung ste /
dviviDena arTena Ayatane vyavasTAnam kRtam
# de'i-phyir #  don gnyis kyis skye-mched #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  byas so /
evam Ayatana kOSalyam BoktA aDyAtmikAni AyatanAni Bojanam / AyatanAni bAhyAni
# de-ltar #  skye-mched-la-mkhas-pa #  za-ba-po #  ni nang gi skye-mched #  rnams yin la / / bza'-ba # r bya-ba #  ni phyi'i rnams yin te /
na anyaH BoktA iti Atmani BoktR tva grAhaH vyAvartate
# za-ba-po # 'i bdag med do snyam nas bdag za pa por 'dzin-pa #  ldog-pa # r 'gyur ro /
yat uktam cakzuH adya AyatanAnAm anugraha upaGAtAt tat aDizWAnaH eva / BoktR tva vyavahAraH iti tat ayuktam
# mig la-sogs-pa # 'i skye-mched #  la phan-pa #  dang gnod-pa # 'i phyir de'i-gnas #  nyid za-ba-po # r tha-snyad #  btags so zhes gang bshad-pa #  de mi rigs te /
rUpa pratizeDena cakzuH AdInAm AyatanAnAm api asattvAt Atma vat iti / na eza / p / upAlamBaH
# gzugs bkag-pa # 'i phyir bdag bzhin-du #  mig la-sogs-pa # 'i skye-mched #  rnams kyang med-pa # 'i phyir ro zhe na / / 'di ni klan-ka # r mi rung ste /
yasmAt parikalpita rUpasya eva atra pratizeDaH kriyate na vikalpa tA rUpasya
# 'di-ltar #  kun-brtags-pa # 'i gzugs kho-na #  'dir dgag-pa # r bya'i / / rnam-par-brtags-pa # 'i gzugs ni ma yin no /
tatra cakzuH Adi prapaQca pariBAvita karma Akzipta tvena Alaya vijQAnam / pariNAma viSeza prAptam ADyAtmikam Ayatanam / tat nimittasya pravRtti vijQAnasya rUpa Adi pratiBAsam bAhya Ayatanam / yaH AlayavijQAnasya sADAraNa arTa pratiBAsaH yaH ca sattva pratiBAsaH
# de-la #  mig la-sogs-pa # r spros-pa # s bsgos-pa # 'i las kyis 'phags-pa # s kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  'gyur-ba # 'i khyad-par #  rnyed-pa #  ni nang gi skye-mched #  do / / rgyu-de-las-byung-ba #  'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  la gzugs la sog par snang-ba #  ni phyi'i skye-mched #  do /
saH api grAhya grAhaka pratiBAsasya / pravRtti vijQAnasya utpattO= aDipati pratyaya tvAt bAhyam Ayatanam ucyate / na tu tat vizaya tvAt iti
# kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  thun mong gi don-du #  snang-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  dang sems-can #  du snang-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de-yang #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r snang-ba #  'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  skye-ba # 'i bdag-po'i-rkyen #  yin pa'i phyir phyi'i skye-mched #  ces bya'i / / de yul du gyur-pa # 'i phyir ni ma yin no /
nanu evam dvayam ASritya cakzuH vijQAna AdayaH utpadyante iti sUtra vacanena / viruDyate
# de-ltar-na #  go mdo-sde #  las gnyis la brten-nas #  mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  skye'o zhes 'byung-ba #  dang mi 'gal lam /
rUpa Adi pratiBAsaH vijQAnAt BinnaH / na ca tat eva tasya eva utpatti pratyayaH yuktaH
# gzugs la-sogs-pa # r snang-ba #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  las tha dad na de nyid skye-ba'i-rkyen #  du de nyid 'gyur-ba # r ni mi rigs te /
utpannAn utpanna avasTayoH BAvAt aBAvAt ca sva Atmani vRtti viroDAt
# skyes-pa #  dang ma-skyes-pa # 'i dus na yod-pa #  dang med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / bdag-nyid #  la 'jug-pa #  'gal-ba # 'i yang phyir ro /
tasmAt avaSyam vijQAna nirBAsAt BinnAH rUpa AdayaH aByupagantavyAH iti / na ezaH api upAlamBaH
# de-lta-bas-na #  gdon-mi-za-bar #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  snang-ba #  las tha-dad-pa # r gyur-pa #  gzugs la-sogs-pa # r khas-blang-ba # r bya'o zhe na / / 'di yang klan-ka # r mi rung ste /
yasmAt pAdi nirBAsa vijQAn m saBAga vijQAna utpattaye pratyaya vijQAne / vAsanAm ADatte
# 'di-ltar #  gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni 'dra-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  skye-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir rkyen gyis rnam-par-shes-pa #  la bag-chags #  'jog go /
vasana apariNAmAt ca rUpa Adi ABAsam punar vijQAnam jAyate
# bag-chags #  yongs su gyur nas yang gzugs la-sogs-pa # r snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  skye ste /
evam vijQAna nirBAsa Atmaka tvena vAsanA hitaH vijQAna pratyayaH uktaH iti / na sUtra viroDaH
# de-ltar #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  gzugs la-sogs-pa # r snang-ba # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  bag-chags #  bskyed-pa #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rkyen yin par bshad-pa # s na mdo-sde #  dang 'gal-ba # r 'gyur-ba #  med do /
evam rUpa Adi nirBAsasya Alambana arTaH api upapannaH sva nirBAsa AkArasya / vijQAnasya pratyaya tvAt
# de-ltar-na #  rang snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rkyen yin pa'i phyir gzugs la sgos-pa # r snang-ba #  ni dmigs-pa # 'i don-du #  'thad do /
aTavA yaTA bAhya arTa vAdiBiH vijQAnena sahajaH Alambana pratyayaH / vyavasTApyate janya janaka vat aBAve api tad BAva aBAvAByAm
# yang-na #  ji-ltar #  phyi'i don-du #  smra-ba #  dag gis bskyed-par-bya-ba #  dang skyed-pa #  po lta-bu # r med kyang de yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  las rnam-par-shes-pa #  yod-pa #  dang med-par-'gyur-ba # 'i dbang-du-byas-nas #  /
vijQAna BAva aBAva avaDi kRtya evam iha api rUpa Adi nirBAsasya / vijQAnasya vA asati api janya janaka BAve tat BAva aBAvayoH / vijQAna BAva aBAva vyaBicArAt pratyaya pratyayi tvam vyavasTApyate / rUpa nirBAsa vijQAnayoH aBinna tvAt dRzwAntena muKyataH asAdRSyam iti / na Beda upacArAt
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang lhan-cig-skyes-pa #  ni dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  du 'jog-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  'dir yang gzugs la-sogs-pa #  snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  bskyed-par-bya-ba #  dang skyed-pa #  po'i dngos-po # r med kyang de yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  las rnam-par-shes-pa #  yod-pa #  dang med-par-'gyur-ba #  'khrul-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir rkyen dang rkyen can du rnam-pa # r gzhag go / / gzugs su snang-ba #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  gnyis tha-mi-dad-pa # 'i phyir / / dpe dang dngos su mi 'dre'o zhe na / / ma yin te /
tat yaTA grAhya grAhaka vikalpa aDizwHAna tvAt / svapna mAyA ganDarvanagara Adi vijQAnam paramArTataH aBinnam api
# tha-dad-pa # r gdags-pa # 'i phyir ro / / dper-na #  rmi-lam #  dang sgyu-ma #  dang dri-za # 'i grong-khyer #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  don-dam-pa # r tha mi dad mod kyi /
grAhya grAhaka AkAreNa Binnam iva vyavasTApyata / Alambya Alambaka BAva tvena taTA anyatra api na asti viroDaH
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa'i-gnas #  yin pa'i phyir gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r tha-snyad #  kyi tha-dad-pa #  lta-bu # r dmigs-par-bya-ba #  dang dmigs-par-byed-pa # 'i dngos-po # r rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  gzhan la 'gal-ba #  med do /
api ca Alambya Alambaka BAvaH sarvatra upacaryataH eva na muKyaH asti
# gzhan-yang #  dmigs-par-bya-ba #  dang dmigs-par-byed-pa # 'i dngos-po #  ni thams-cad-du #  yang gdags-pa #  nyid-du #  zad kyi dngos su med de /
nahi vijQAnam utpannam anutpannam vA vizayam Alambate
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni skyes-pa # 'am ma-skyes-pa # s kyang yul la dmigs-pa # r mi 'gyur te /
utpatti anantara vinASi tvAt kriyA kAle anavasTAnAt asattvAt ca
# skyes ma-thag-tu #  zhig-pa # 'i phyir dmigs-par-byed-pa # 'i tshe mi sdod-pa #  dang med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vizayaH ca utpannaH anutpannaH vA uBayaTA api Alambana tvena ayogyaH / utpannasyA anavasTAnAt anutpannasya ca asattvAt
# yul yang skyes-pa #  dang ma-skyes-pa #  gnyis-ka #  la yang dmigs su mi rung ste / / skyes-pa #  ni gnas-pa #  med-pa #  dang ma-skyes-pa #  ni med-pa # 'i phyir te /
nahi nirADArA Alambana kriyA yujyate
# gzhi-med-pa #  la ni dmigs-pa # r byar mi rung ngo /
yasya api sattA mAtreNa kArya kAraNa BAvaH eva Alambya Alambaka BAvaH / tasya api vartamAnasya vijQAnasya Alambanam nirarTakam p
# gang-gi #  ltar yod-pa #  tsam gyis rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # 'i dngos-po #  de nyid dmigs-par-bya-ba #  dang dmigs-par-byed-pa # r 'jog-pa #  de'i ltar na yang da-ltar #  gyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni don-med-pa # r 'gyur te /
Bavati tad Atma tvena sidDeH
# de'i-bdag-nyid #  du grub zin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
utpadyamAnasya api nirarTakam asattvAt
# skye-ba'i-tshe # 'ang don-med-pa # r 'gyur te / / med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na utpadyamAnasya nirarTakam yasmAt vizaya sadBAve vijQAnam tat / nirBAsam AtmAnam pratilaBate / yadi vizaya nirBAsaH vijQAnasya bAhya arTa nimittaH evam
# skye-ba'i-tshe #  don-med-pa # r mi 'gyur te / / 'di-ltar #  yul-gyi-dngos-po #  yod-na #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  der-snang-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  'thob-pa # 'i phyir ro zhe na / / gal-te #  yul du snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rgyu phyi-rol #  gyi don yin te /
atIta anAgata svapna Adi vijQAnasya nirAkAra tvam vartate / tat arTa aBAvAt vA sattvam / na vikalEH pratyayEH kAryam utpadyate atiprasaFgAt / na ca asataH pratyaya tvam yujyate
# de lta na 'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  dang rmi-lam #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnam-pa #  med-pa # r 'gyur ro / / yang-na #  de'i don-med-pa # s med-pa #  nyid-du #  'gyur ro / / rkyen ma-tshang-ba #  ni 'bras-bu #  'byung-ba # r mi rung ste / / ha-cang-thal-ba # r 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro / / med-pa #  ni rkyen du mi rung ngo /
na ca bAhya arTaH Alambana pratyayaH vijQAnasya tena vinA api BAvAt
# phyi'i don yang rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  du mi 'gyur te / / de med kyang-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
tasmAt sarvam eva vijQAnam tEmirika AdInAm iva / bAhya arTa Alambana nirapekzam eva aByupagantavyam
# de-bas-na #  rab-rib #  can la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  thams-cad #  phyi'i don dmigs-pa #  la mi ltos-pa #  nyid khas-blang-ba # r bya'o /
pratItyasamutpAda arTaH / AyatanA arTAn antaram pratItyasamutpAda arTaH vaktavyaH iti atas Aha / pratItyasamutpAda arTaH / punar hetu Pala AyAsA anAropA arAt anapavAdataH
# skye-mched #  kyi don gyi 'og-tu #  rten cing 'brel-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i don brjod dgos te / / de'i-phyir #  rten cing 'brel-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i don te / / rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  rtsol ba la / / sgro 'dogs med cing skur 'debs med /
nirIha anitya samarTa pratyaya utpAdana arTaH / yaTA uktam sUtre api etat asmin satI damBavati
# ces bya-ba #  smos so / / g-yo-ba #  med-pa #  dang mi-rtag-pa #  dang nus-pa # 'i rkyen las byung-ba # 'i don to / / mdo-sde #  las kyang 'di-skad-du #  / / 'di yod-pa # s 'di 'byung /
asya utpAdAt idam utpadyate yat uta avidyA pratyayAH saMskArAH iti vistaraH
# 'di skyes-pa # 'i phyir 'di skye-ba #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  ma-rig-pa # 'i rkyen gyis 'du-byed-rnams #  zhes-bya-ba #  rgya-cher #  gsungs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
ayam ca pratItyasamutpAdaH hetupa hala kriyANAm / samAropa apavAda pratizeDena izyate iti pratipAdayan= Aha
# 'di yang rten cing 'brel-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  dang byed-pa #  rnams la sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-pa #  dgag-pa # r 'dod-pa #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
hetu Pala kriyANAm asamAropa vAda arTaH pratItyasamutpAda arTaH iti
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  dang byed-pa #  rnams la sgro-'dogs-pa #  med-pa #  dang skur ba 'debs-pa #  med-pa # 'i don ni rten cing 'brel-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i don to zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
AyAsa Sabdena tu kriyA uktA
# rtsol ba zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni byed-pa # r bshad do /
tatra hetu samAropaH avidyA AdIn hitvA puruza ISvara aNu praDAna AdInAm / hetu tva kalpanAt
# de-la #  rgyu la sgro-'dogs-pa #  ni ma-rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bor nas skyes-bu #  dang dbang-phyug #  dang bdag dang gtso bo la-sogs-pa #  la rgyu nyid-du #  rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
etat eva pratipAdayan= Aha saMskAra AdInAm jarA maraNa paryantAnAm
