# de bstan-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir / / 'du-byed #  la-sogs-pa #  tha-ma #  rga shi la thug-pa #  dag gi mi-mthun-pa'i-rgyu #  la rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
vizama hetu kalpnAt iti / saMskAra AdInAm hi anityAnAm nityaH puruza AdikaH hetuH vizamaH visadRSa
# 'du-byed #  la-sogs-pa #  mi-rtag-pa #  rnams kyi rgyu skyes-bu #  la-sogs-pa #  rtag-pa #  ni mi-mthun-pa #  ste / / mi-'dra-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
iti arTaH / aTavA hetuH sva rUpa vikriyAH apekzaH bIja AdikaH aFkura AdInAm dRzwaH
# yang-na #  rgyu'i-rang-bzhin #  'gyur-ba #  la ltos nas sa-bon #  la-sogs-pa #  la myu-gu #  la-sogs-pa #  mthong-ste #  /
na ca nityasya sva rUpa vikriyA asti iti vizama hetO hetu tva kalpanAt / hetu samAropaH p
# rang-bzhin #  rtag-pa #  la ni 'gyur-ba #  med do / / mi-mthun-pa'i-rgyu #  nyid la rgyur rtog-pa # 'i phyir rgyu la sgro-'dogs-pa # 'o /
hetu apavAdaH nirhetuka tva kalpanAt iti saMskAra AdInAm / nirhetuka utpAda aByupagamAt avidyA AdInAm saMskAra Adi hetu tvam apoXam / Bavati
# rgyu la skur-pa-'debs-pa #  ni rgyu-med-pa #  can du rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'du-byed #  la-sogs-pa #  rgyu-med-pa # r skye-ba # r khas-blangs-pa # s 'du-byed #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyu-ma #  rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  gsal-ba #  yin no /
Pala samAropaH sAtmakAnAm saMskAra AdInAm / avidyA Adi pratyaya pravRtti kalpanAt iti
# 'bras-bu #  la sgro-'dogs-pa #  ni bdag dang bcas-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  la-sogs-pa #  ma-rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rkyen las 'byung-ba # r rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  la /
satya Atmani saMskAra AdInAm avidyA Adi pratyaya pravRtti tvam na tu asti iti / saMskAra Adi Palezu Atma samAropaH iti eke
# kha-cig #  na re bdag yod-na #  ni 'du-byed #  la-sogs-pa #  ma-rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rkyen rnams las 'byung gi / / med na ni ma yin no zhes 'bras-bu #  'du-byed #  la-sogs-pa # r bdag sgro 'dogs na 'bras-bu #  la sgro-'dogs-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  zhe'o /
Atma dravya samavAyi tvena tat anugraha upaGAta kartR tvena vA sAtmakAnAm / saMskAra AdInAm avidyA Adi pratyaya pravRtti kalpanAt Pala samAropaH iti apare
# gzhan dag na re bdag-gi #  rdzas dang ldan-pa # s sam / / de phan-pa #  dang gnod-pa-byed-pa # s bdag dang bcas-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  la-sogs-pa #  ni ma-rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rkyen las 'byung-ba # r rtog-pa # 'i phyir 'bras-bu #  la sgro-'dogs-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
Pala apavAdaH na santi avidyA Adi pratyayAH saMskAra dayaH iti kalpanAt iti / tat yaTA su carita duScarita para loka apavAdinAm na asti su caritam na asti / duScaritam na asti para loke iti
# 'bras-bu #  la skur-pa-'debs-pa #  ni 'du-byed #  la-sogs-pa #  ma-rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rkyen gyis 'byung-ba-med-pa # r rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / legs-par-spyad-pa #  yang med / / nyes-par-spyad-pa #  yang med / / 'jig-rten-pha-rol #  yang med do zhes med-pa #  rnams legs-par-spyad-pa #  dang nyes-par-spyad-pa #  dang 'jig-rten-pha-rol #  la skur-pa-'debs-par #  smra-ba # 'o /
kriyA samAropaH avidyA AdInAm saMskAra Adi utpattO vyApAra kalpanAt iti / yadi vastu rUpam arTa antara BUtam saMskAra Adi utpattO= avidyA AdayaH / kurvanti iti kalpyeta evam kriyA samAropaH / kriyA apavAdaH nissAmarTya kalapanAt iti
# byed-pa #  la sgro-'dogs-pa #  ni 'du-byed #  la sogs skye-ba #  la ma-rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  byed-pa # r rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni gal-te #  'du-byed #  la-sogs-pa #  skye-ba #  la ma-rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dngos-po # 'i rang-bzhin #  don-gzhan-du-gyur-pa #  zhig byed-pa # r rtog-pa #  de-lta-bu #  ni byed-pa #  la sgro-'dogs-pa # 'o / / byed-pa #  la skur-pa-'debs-pa #  ni nus-pa-med-pa # r rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  la /
avidyA AdInAm sattA mAtreNa saMskArANAm hi utpAdana samarTAnAm api / niHsAmarTya kalpanAt kriyA apavAdaH
# ma-rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yod-pa #  tsam gyis 'du-byed #  la-sogs-pa #  skye-ba # r nus-pa #  yin yang nus-pa-med-pa # r rtog-pa # 'i phyir-byed-pa #  la skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'o /
tat aBAvAt asamAropa anapavAdaH veditavyaH iti / tasya hetu Pala kriyANAm samAropa apavAdasya aBAvAt asamAra upAnapa vAdaH
# de med-pa # 'i phyir sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-pa #  med-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  dang byed-pa #  rnams la sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-pa #  de med-pa # 'i phyir sgro-'dogs-pa #  med-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-pa #  med-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
veditavyaH / evam idam pratItyasamutpAda kOSalyam avidyA divya tirekeNa Atmani anyasmin
# de-ltar #  rten cing 'brel-pa # r 'byung-ba #  la mkhas-pa #  'di ni ma-rig-pa #  las gzhan-pa #  bdag gam gzhan-yang #  rung ste /
vA yaH kartR tva grAhaH tasyAm pratipakzeNa veditavyam
# byed-pa # r 'dzin-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de'i gnyen-po #  yin par rig-par-bya # 'o /
na hi atra AtmA anyaH vA avidyA vyatirekeNa SuBa aSuBAnAm karmaNAm kartA
# 'di-la #  ma-rig-pa #  ma-gtogs-par #  dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba'i-las #  rnams byed-pa #  ni bdag gam gzhan-yang #  rung ste med do /
anyaH saMskAra vyatirekeNa vijQAnasya kartA na asti
# 'du-byed-rnams #  ma-gtogs-par #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i byed-pa #  gzhan med do /
evam sarvatra api yaTAyogam vaktavyam nirIheByaH anityeByaH / samarTeByaH ca avidyA AdiByaH saMskAra Adi utpattitaH / sTAnA AsTAna arTaH p / pratItyasamutpAda anantaram sTAnA sTAna arTaH vaktavyaH iti atas Aha / anizwa izwa viSudDInAm / iti vistaraH
# thams-cad-du #  yang ci-rigs-par #  brjod-pa # r bya ste / / ma-rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  g-yo-ba #  med-pa #  mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  nus-pa #  yod-pa #  dag las 'du-byed #  la-sogs-pa #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / rten cing 'brel-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i don gyi 'og-tu #  gnas dang gnas-ma-yin-pa # 'i don brjod dgos te / / de'i-phyir #  / / mi 'dod 'dod dang rnam dag dang / / mnyam-du #  'byung dang dbang byed dang / / 'thob dang kun du spyod-pa #  dag / / gzhan dbang nyid kyi don de gzhan / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so /
sTAna AsTAnam saptaviDa pAratantrya arTena veditam iti / tatra sTAnam hetuH asTAna mahetuH / yaTA uktam gATAyAm
# gnas dang gnas-ma-yin-pa #  ni gzhan gyi dbang nyid rnam-pa #  bdun gyi don-gyis #  rig-par-bya #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  gnas ni rgyu yin no / / gnas-ma-yin-pa #  ni rgyu-ma #  yin te / / ji-skad-du #  /
satyam vadet na ca krudDet dadyAt alpaH api yAcitaH
# bden-pa # r smra zhing khro-ba #  med / / slong la chung yang sbyin-pa # r bya /
eBiH triBiH iha shtAnEH devAnAm samitim vrajet / hetuBiH iti gamyate / aTavA sTAnam samBavaH asTAnam punar asamBavaH
# rnam-pa #  'di gsum gnas kyis ni / / lha yi nang-du #  skye-bar-'gyur #  / / zhes tshigs-su-bcad-pa #  las 'byung-ba #  lta-bu #  ste rgyu yin par mngon no / / yang-na #  gnas ni srid-pa # 'o / / gnas-ma-yin-pa #  ni mi srid do /
tat kOSalyam sTAna AsTAna kOSalyam / paratantrasya BAvaH pAratantryam
# de-la #  mkhas-pa #  ni gnas dang gnas-ma-yin-pa #  la mkhas-pa # 'o / / gzhan gyi dbang gi dngos-po #  ni gzhan gyi dbang nyid de /
parAyatta tA iti arTaH / tat ca saptaviDam api trizu antar Bavati karma kleSa janma pAratantryezu
# gzhan la rag las zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / rnam-pa #  de bdun yang las dang nyon-mongs-pa #  dang tshe'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid gsum du 'dus so /
tatra anizwe pAratantryam iti / anizwAH duargatayaH / tatra gamanam duScarita Ayatattvam pAratantrI aQcA iti pradarSayan= Aha
# de-la #  mi-'dod-pa # 'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni zhes-bya-ba #  la / / mi-'dod-pa #  ni ngan-'gro #  rnams te / / der 'gro-ba-gzhan #  gyi dbang nyid-du #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
duSaritena prANa atipAta AdinA kAya vAc manaH karma saNggRhItena / sa prayoga pRzWenA anicCataH api durgati gamAt iti / durgatayaH narakAH pretAH tiryaQcaH ca
# nyes-par-spyod-pa #  srog-gcod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  lus dang ngag dang yid-kyi-las #  su bsdus-pa #  sbyor-ba #  dang bcas-pa #  dang mjug gis mi-'dod-bzhin-du #  yang ngan-'gror-'gro-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tezAm ekAntena duHKa tvAt na kasyacid tatra gamana icCA Bavati
# ngan-'gro #  dag ni sems-can #  dmyal-ba #  dang yi dags dang dud-'gro # 'o / / de-dag #  ni shin-tu #  sdug-bsngal-ba # 'i phyir der 'gro-'dod-pa #  ni su yang med mod kyi /
karmaNAm balavat tvAt durgati getu tvAt ca duScaritasya anicCataH api tatra / karma vaSAt eva gamanam Bavati
# las rnams stobs dang ldan la ngan-'gro # 'i rgyu yang yin-pas #  nye-bar-spyod-pa #  ni mi-'dod-bzhin-du #  las kyi dbang gis der 'gro-ba # r 'gyur ro /
izwe pAratantryam su caritena sugati gamanAt iti / izwam sugati gamanam / sugatiH devAH manuSyAH ca
# 'dod-pa # 'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni legs-par-spyad-pa # s bde-'gror-'gro-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  la / / 'dod-pa #  ni bde-'gror-'gro-ba # 'o / / bde-'gro #  ni lha-dang-mi # 'o /
su caritam sa prayoga pRzWeByaH prANa atipAta AdiByaH viratiH / dAna mAna satkAra Adi kriyA SAstR guruNA anvita Adizu mEtrI karuNa AdayaH ca
# legs-par-spyod-pa #  ni srog-gcod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  sbyor-ba #  dang bcas-pa #  dang 'jug-pa #  rnams las log-pa #  dang; ston-pa #  dang bla-ma #  dang yon-tan-dang-ldan-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la sbyin-pa #  dang rim-gro #  dang bkur-sti #  la-sogs-pa #  byed-pa #  dang byams-pa #  dang snying-rje #  la-sogs-pa #  yon-tan #  gyi khyad-par #  rnams so /
guNa viSezAH / pAratantryam su caritam antareNa anyaTA prArTayatAm api / sugati gamana aBAvAt / su carita pratibadDa tA eva sugati utpatteH
# gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni legs-par-spyad-pa #  med-pa # r gzhan gyis ni 'dod du zin-kyang #  bde-'gror-'gro-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir te / / bde-'gror-skye-ba #  ni legs-par-spyad-pa #  la rag lus pa nyid do /
viSUdDO pAratantryam iti vistaraH / viSudDiH kleSa prahANam
# rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni ches-rgya #  cher 'byung-ba #  la rnam-par-dag-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-spangs-pa # 'o /
paQca nivaraNAni kAma= CandaH vyApAdaH styAnam idDam OdDatya kOkRtyam / vicikitsA ca / styAnam idDam ekIkRtya OdDatya kOkRtyaQca paQca Bavati / aBedena kuSala pakzam nivRNvanti iti nivaraNAni Bedena punar yaTAkramam / pravrajatyABiH atim tat anurUpe kAya vAc karmANi sabrahmacAriBiH samyak / coditasya samyak pratipattim SamaTa kAle alInatAm pragraha kAle avikzepam / SamaTa vipaSyana akAle svarasa vAditAm CAdayanti iti nivaraNAni / tAni aprahAya Agatya yAvat sapta boDi aFgAni aBAvayitvA iti
# sgrib-pa #  lnga ni 'dod-pa-la-'dun-pa #  dang gnod-sems #  dang rmugs pa dang; gnyid dang rgod-pa #  dang 'gyod-pa #  dang the-tshom #  mo / / rmugs pa dang gnyid gcig-tu #  bsdus / / rgod-pa #  dang 'gyod-pa #  gcig-tu #  bsdus te lngar 'gyur ro / / dge-ba'i-phyogs #  la sgrib-pa # r bye-brag-med-pa # s sgrib-pa #  rnams so / / bye-brag #  tu ni sgrib-pa #  rnams zhes mngon-par-dga'-ba #  dang lus-dang-ngag-gi-las #  mi cha-ba #  la tshangs-pa #  mtshungs-pa # r spyod-pa #  rnams kyis legs-par-blangs-pa #  la legs-par #  sgrub-pa #  dang zhi-gnas-kyi-dus #  na ma bying-ba #  dang rab-tu-'dzin-pa'i-dus #  na mi g-yeng ba dang zhi-gnas-dang-lhag-mthong #  gi dus na rang-gi-ngang-gis #  'jug-pa #  la rim-pa #  bzhin-du #  bsgribs-pa # s na sgrib-pa #  rnams zhes-bya'o #  / / de-dag #  ma spangs lags zhes-bya-ba #  ni ma-btang-ba # 'o / / byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  bdun gyi bar-du #  ma bsgoms na zhes-bya-ba #  la /
yAvat iti paryanta upadeSAt smRti upasTAna samyak / prahANa RdDi pAda indriya balAnAm api grahaNam
# bar-du #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mtha' brjod-pa #  ste / / dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  rnams dang yang-dag-par-spong-ba #  rnams dang rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  rnams dang dbang-po #  rnams dang stobs rnams kyang bsdu'o /
duHKasya antA karaNAt iti / duHKasya antaH p
# sdug-bsngal #  gyi mtha' mi-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  la /
yatra duHKam na asti tat ca nirvANam tasya akaraNam aprAptiH nirvANam na / prApnoti iti arTaH
# sdug-bsngal #  gyi mtha' ni gang na sdug-bsngal-med-pa #  ste / / de ni mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'o / / de mi-byed-pa #  ni mi-'thob-pa #  ste / / mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  mi 'thob po zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
aTavA duHKasya antaH yasmAt duHKAt anya duHKam na sanDIyate tat
# yang-na #  sdug-bsngal #  gyi mtha' zhes-bya-ba #  ni sdug-bsngal #  gzhan dang mtshams mi sbyor-ba # 'o /
tAdRSam duHKam na karoti iti apratisanDikam duHKam na karoti iti arTaH
# de ni sdug-bsngal #  de-lta-bu #  dang mtshams-sbyor-ba # r mi-byed-pa #  ste / / sdug-bsngal #  du mi-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
paQca nivaraNa prahANa pratibadDa tA viSudDO pAratantryam
# sgrib-pa #  lnga spangs-pa #  la rag lus pa'i phyir rnam-par-dag-pa #  gzhan gyi dbang nyid do /
sama utpattO pAratantryam dvayoH apUrva AcaramayoH iti sahitayoH iti arTaH / taTAgatayoH cakravartinoH ca ekasmin lokaDAtO= anutpAdAt iti
# mnyam-du #  'byung-ba # 'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni de-bzhin-gshegs-pa #  dang 'khor-los-sgyur-ba #  gnyis gnyis snga-phyi #  med-pa # r zhes-bya-ba #  ni lhan-cig #  ces pa'i tha-tshig #  go /
taTAgatayoH tri sAhasra mahA sAhasraH lokaDAtuH aBipretaH
# de-bzhin-gshegs-pa #  gnyis dang 'khor-los-sgyur-ba #  gnyis 'jig-rten-gyi-khams #  gcig-tu #  mi 'byung zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
cakravartinoH tu cAtuH dvIpakaH iti kecid / taTAgatayoH api cAtur dvIpakaH eva iti apare / budDAH hi BagavantaH DarmakAya ADipatyAt tri sAhasra mahA sAhasre
# kha-cig #  na re de-bzhin-gshegs-pa #  gnyis stong-gsum #  gyi stong-chen-po # 'i 'jig-rten-gyi-khams #  su mi-'byung-ba # r 'dod kyi / / 'khor-los-sgyur-ba #  ni gling-bzhi-pa # r 'byung-ba # r mi 'dod do zhe'o /
lokaDAtO pratyekam cAtuH dvIpakezu nirmANakAyena aBisambaH Dim / parinirvANam ca darSayanti / taTA hi yat ekasmiQca AtuH mahA dvIpake tuzitezu manuzyezu ca / cyuti janma parigrahaH boDisattvAnAm prayojanam / tad itarezu api cAtur dvIpakezu samAnam / tasmAt akanizWa BavanaH eva aBisambadDaH BagavAn nirmANakAyena
# gzhan dag na re de-bzhin-gshegs-pa #  gnyis kyang gling-bzhi-pa #  nyid-du #  mi 'byung ngo zhes zer te / / sangs-rgyas #  bcom-ldan-'das #  rnams ni chos kyi sku'i dbang gis stong-gsum #  gyi stong-chen-po # 'i 'jig-rten-gyi-khams #  su gling-bzhi-pa #  re-re # r yang sprul pa'i skus mngon-pa # r byang-chub #  pa dang yongs su mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  yang ston to / / 'di-ltar #  gling-bzhi-pa #  gcig-tu #  dga'-ldan #  dang mi rnams kyi nang-du #  yang tshe yongs-su-'dzin-pa #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyis dgongs-pa #  ste / / de ni gling-bzhi-pa #  gzhan-du # 'ang 'dra'o /
tri sAhasra mahA sAhasre vantargatezu sarva cAturdvIpakezu / tuzitezu upapattim manuzyezu ca janma parigraha Adikam sarvam darSayati iti / manyante
# de-lta-bas-na #  'og-min-gyi-gnas #  nyid-du #  bcom-ldan-'das #  mngon-pa # r sangs-rgyas #  nas sprul pa'i skus stong-gsum #  gyi stong-chen-po # 'i 'jig-rten-gyi-khams #  kyi khongs-su-gtogs-pa # 'i gling-bzhi-pa #  re-re # r yang dga'-ldan #  du skye-ba #  dang 'chi-'pho #  dang mi'i-nang-du #  tshe yongs-su-'dzin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  thams-cad #  ston to snyam-du #  sems so /
tatra ca sama saMvartanIya karma AyattatA budDa carkravartI utpatteH / sahaBAve pAratantryam
# 'di-la #  sangs-rgyas #  dang 'khor-los-sgyur-ba #  'byung-ba #  ni mnyam-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  ma-yin-pa # 'i las la rag lus pas lhan-cig-tu #  skye-bar-'gyur-ba #  gzhan gyi dbang nyid do /
ADipatye pAratantryam striyA cakravarti tva Adi akaraNAt iti / cakravarti saMvartanIyasya karmaNaH pumAtmaBAvaH eva / vipAka dAna sAmarTyAt / na hi strIH strI Adi ratna upaBoga samarTA / Adi Sabdena Sakra tvAt gRhyate
# dbang-byed-pa # 'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni bud-med #  'khor-los-sgyur-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  mi-byed-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'khor-los-sgyur-ba # r 'gyur-ba # 'i las kyi rnam-par-smin-pa #  ni skyes-pa'i-lus #  kyis smin-pa # r nus te / / bud-med #  la ni bud-med-rin-po-che #  la spyod-pa # 'i mthu-med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / sogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgras ni brgya byin la-sogs-pa #  bsdu'o /
samprAptO pAratantryam strI apratyeka anuttara boDi anaBisamboDAt
# 'thob-pa # 'i gzhan gyi dbang ni bud-med #  kyis rang byang-chub #  dang bla-na-med-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-par-byang-chub-pa # r mi-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  la /
prAptiH budDa pratyekabudDa tva aDigamaH
# 'thob-pa #  ni sangs-rgyas #  dang rang byang-chub #  nyid 'thob-pa # 'o /
tatra pAratantryam puruzasya prAptiH na tu striyaH
# de-la #  gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni skyes-pa # s 'thob-pa # r 'gyur gyi bud-med #  kyis 'thob-pa # r mi 'gyur te /
tasyAH hi saMsarga aBAvAt Ka Xgavat / tri BUmi SAstrI tva asamBavAt yaTAkramam
# de ni go-rims-bzhin-du #  bse ru lta-bu # r 'dre-ba #  med-pa #  dang sa gsum gyi ston-pa # r mi srid-pa # 'i phyir te /
sA punar sarva DUrta jana gamyA alpa prajQa tvAt / anAcAryaka aBisambaH DAya ugyA ca iti
# de'ang skye-bo #  g-yon can thams-cad-kyi #  spyod yul yin pa dang shes-rab #  chung-ba # s slob-dpon-med-par #  mngon-pa # r rdzogs-par-byang-chub-pa # 'i 'os ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
samudAcAre pAratantryam dRzwi sampannasya vaDa Adi asamavAcArAt
# kun du spyod-pa # 'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni lta-ba #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  gsod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  kun du mi spyod-la #  /
pRTagjanasya ca samudAcArAt iti / dRzwi sampannaH dRzwa satyaH
# so-so'i-skye-bo #  ni kun du spyod-pa # 'i phyir te zhes-bya-ba #  lta-ba #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  ni bden-pa-mthong-ba # 'o /
vaDaH prANa atipAtaH p / Adi Sabdena Adatta AdAna AdayaH saMgRhyante / te vaDa AdayaH kAya vAc kriyA svaBAvAH dRzwi sampannasya na samudAcaranti
# gsod-pa #  ni srog-gcod-pa #  yin; sogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgras ni ma-byin-par-len-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bsdus te / / gsod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  de-dag #  ni lus dang ngag gi bya-ba # 'i rang-bzhin #  no /
darSana mArgeNa vaDa Adi duScarita samutTApaka kleSa prahANAt pRTagjanasya
# mthong-ba'i-lam #  nyid kyi gsod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  nyes-par-spyod-pa #  kun-nas-slong-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  spongs pa'i phyir lta-ba #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  ni kun du mi spyod do /
samudAcaranti tat aprahANAt / tat aprahANam punar tat pratipakzeNa mArga anutpanna tvAt
# so-so'i-skye-bo #  ni de ma-spangs-pa # 'i phyir kun du spyod do / / de ma-spangs-pa #  yang de'i gnyen-po # r lam ma-skyes-pa # 'i phyir ro /
evam anizwa Adi pAratantrya anugatam asTAna kOSalyam puruza ISvara AdO / svAtantrya agrAhara pratipakzaH
# de-ltar #  mi-'dod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  gzhan gyi dbang nyid kyi rjes-su-song-ba #  / / gnas dang gnas-ma-yin-pa #  la mkhas-pa #  ni skyes-bu #  dang dbang-phyug #  la-sogs-pa #  rang dbang can du 'dzin-pa # 'i gnyen-po # 'o /
yadi hi svatantraH kaScid syAt na duScaritena durgatim gacCet
# gal-te #  rang dbang can 'ga' zhig yod-na #  ni nyes-par-spyad-pa #  las ngan-'gror-'gro-ba # r mi 'gyur ro /
evam anyatra api vAcyam
# de-bzhin-du #  gzhan dag la yang brjod-pa # r bya'o /
indriya arTaH / sTAna AsTAna arTa nirdeSa anantaram indriya arTaH vaktavyaH iti atas Aha
# gnas dang gnas-ma-yin-pa # 'i don bstan-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  dbang-po #  rnams kyi don brjod dgos-pa # s de'i-phyir #  dbang-po #  ni rnam-pa #  nyi shu rtsa gnyis te zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
indriyam dvAviMSativiDam iti cakzuH indriyam yAvat / AjQAtO= indriya avasAnam / atra punar ADipAti arTam indriya arTaH / kasya punar kva ADipatyam iti atas Aha
# mig-gi-dbang-po #  nas kun-shes-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i dbang-po #  la thug gi bar-du # 'o / / de-la #  dbang-po # 'i don ni dbang-byed-pa # 'i don to / / gang zhig gang-la #  dbang-byed-pa #  de mi shes-nas #  / / de'i-phyir #  /
grahaNa sTAna sanDAna Boga SudDi dvaya arTataH iti
# 'dzin dang gnas dang rgyun mi 'chad / / spyod dang dag-pa #  gnyis kyi phyir / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs te /
atra ca dvaya aDipatti arTataH iti yuktO kArikA anukUla arTam / ADipatya SabdaH luptaH drazwavyaH
# 'di-la #  gnyis-pa #  dbang-byed-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  rigs-pa #  las tshig le'ur byas-pa #  dang mthun-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni mi smos-pa # r blta'o /
tasmAt BAzyakAraH Aha tezu tad ADipatyAt iti
# de-bas-na #  bshad-pa #  byed-pa # s / / de-dag #  la de dbang-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
grahaNa arTena iti / arTa SabdaH atra prayojana vAcI / grahaNa prayojanam nimittam tatra indriyam iti darSayati
# 'dzin-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  la / / phyir zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni 'dir dgos-pa #  yin par brjod de / / 'dzin-pa # 'i dgos-pa #  ste ched yin la /
evam anyatra api yaTAyogam vaktavyam
# de-bzhin-du #  gzhan dag la yang ci-rigs-par #  brjod-pa # r bya'o /
tezu iti arTa grahaNa Adizu ADipatyam iti aDika praBuH tvam iti ADipatyam / hetu tvam iti arTaH
# de-dag #  la zhes-bya-ba #  ni don 'dzin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la'o / / dbang byed ces bya-ba #  ni lhag-pa # r dbang-ba # s na dbang-byed-pa #  ste rgyu zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
rUpa AdayaH Darma paryantAH rUpa Adi vizayAH
# gzugs la-sogs-pa #  chos la thug-pa #  dag ni gzugs la-sogs-pa #  yul rnams te /
tezAm grahaNam cakzuH Adi vijQAnam
# de-dag #  la 'dzin-pa #  ni mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o /
tatra cakzuH AdInAm zaNNAm ADipatyam / cakzuzaH niravaSeza rUpa praBeda vijQAna ASraya tvAt rUpa AdInAm / aDika praBu tvam iti indriyam ucyate / na tu nIla rUpam pIta rUpa Adi vijQAnasya Alambanam Bavati / evam Srotra Adizu api yaTAsamBavam vistareNa vAcyam / sTAne jIvita indriyasya iti
# de-la #  mig la-sogs-pa #  dbang-po #  drug dbang-byed-pa #  ni mig ni gzugs kyi bye-brag #  ma-lus-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rten yin-pas #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la lhag-pa # r dbang-byed-pa # s na dbang-po #  zhes bya ste / / gzugs sngon-po #  ni gzugs ser-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i dmigs-pa # r mi 'gyur ro / / de-bzhin-du #  rna-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  la yang ci-rigs-su #  rgyas-pa # r brjod-pa # r bya'o /
jIvita indriyam punar karma vAsanA viDam vipAka santAne asati / vicCitti pratyaye pUrvpUrva kzANa sarUpezu uttara uttara kzaNezu / pratisanDi sAmarTyam / sTAne jIvita indriyasya ADipatyam iti atra eva kAraNam Aha tat
# gnas-par-bya-ba #  la ni srog-gi-dbang-po #  dbang byed de zhes-bya-ba #  la; srog-gi-dbang-po #  ni sngon-gyi-las #  kyi bag-chags #  kyis 'phangs-pa # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa'i-rgyu # d la bar-du-gcod-pa # 'i rkyen med na skad-cig #  snga-ma # s 'dra-ba # 'i skad-cig #  phyi-ma-phyi-ma #  rnams su mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i mthu-yod-pa # 'o / / gnas-par-bya-ba #  la ni srog-gi-dbang-po #  dbang byed ces bya-ba #  la rgyu smos-pa #  /
ADipatyena maraNAt iti
# 'di'i dbang gis mi-'chi-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes bya ste /
amaraNam pUrva karma Akzipta nikAya saBA anuvRttiH / sati api sattva sTiti kAraNa tve na AhAra AdInAm indriya tvam
# mi-'chi-ba #  ni sngon-gyi-las #  kyis 'phangs rigs mthun-pa # 'i rjes su 'jug go / / kha-zas #  la-sogs-pa #  ni sems-can #  gnas-pa # 'i rgyu yin-du-zin #  kyang dbang-po #  ma yin te /
tat sadBAve api AyuzaH kzaye avasTAnA vA sadBAvAt
# de-dag #  yod-bzhin-du #  tshe-zad-pa #  gnas-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
rUpa ArUpya DAtO= asati api kavaXIkAra AhAre / jIvita indriya adevA avasTAna sadBAvAt
# gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa'i-khams #  na kham gyis za-ba # 'i zas rnams med kyang srog-gi-dbang-po #  nyid kyis gnas-pa-yod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na ca tatra sparSa AdInAm avasTAnaH ADipatyam yujyate
# de na reg-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ni gnas-pa # r dbang-byed-pa # r mi rung ste /
niroDA asaMjQi samApatti avasTAyAm AsaMjQike ca sparSa Adi aBAve api / sattvAnAm sTiti samBavAt iti
# 'gog-pa #  dang 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i gnas dang 'du-shes-med-pa #  dag la reg-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  med kyang sems-can #  rnams gnas-pa # r srid-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kula sanDAne strI puruza indriyayoH ADipatyam iti
# rigs 'tshob pa la pho dang mo'i dbang-po #  gnyis dbang byed de zhes-bya-ba #  la /
putra utpattO kulO= uparata tA vartate iti putra utpattiH kula sanDAnam / etat eva darSayan= Aha prasava ADipatyAt iti
# bu byung na rigs rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  'gyur-ba # s bu 'byung-ba #  ni rigs 'tshob pa'o / / de nyid bstan-pa # 'i phyir-'byung-ba # r dbang-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
kAya indriya pradeSaH eva kaScid ADipatya viSezAt strI puruza indriya AKyam / pratilaBate
# lus kyi dbang-po # 'i phyogs-'ga' #  nyid de / / dbang-byed-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis pho dang mo'i dbang-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  'thob po /
yatra stIndriyam puruza indriya QcaH taH tatra kula vyavasTAnam asti / tat vaSena kulaH na vyuparamate
# gang na pho'i-dbang-po #  dang mo'i dbang-po #  yod-pa #  de na rigs rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  yod de / / de'i dbang gis rigs rgyun mi 'chad do /
kAma avacarezu api ca devezu strI indriye puruza indriye ca sati / kula vyavasTAnam nA asatI iti
# 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa # 'i lha rnams la ni pho'i-dbang-po #  dang mo'i dbang-po #  yod-pa #  la rigs rnam-pa # r gzhag gi med-pa #  la ni ma yin no /
nahi ganDarva AdInAm tatra ADipatyam sati api ganDarva AdO paNXaka Adizu / strI puruza indriyayoH asat BAve putra prasava sAma arTi ABAvAt
# dri-za #  la-sogs-pa #  la dbang-byed-pa #  med de dri-za #  la-sogs-pa #  yod-du-zin-kyang #  / / pho dang mo'i dbang-po-med-pa #  ma-ning #  la-sogs-pa #  la bu 'byung-ba # 'i mthu-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
AhAra AdInAm punar sattve asaMKyAta tvAt sati api ADipatye na indriya tvam
# zas la-sogs-pa #  ni dbang-byed-pa #  yin yang sems-can #  gyi grangs su ma-gtogs-pa # s dbang-po #  zhes mi bya'o /
upaBoge vedanA indriyANAm / ADipatyam iti aDikRtam
# nye-bar-spyod-pa #  la ni tshor-ba'i-dbang #  po rnams te zhes-bya-ba #  ni dbang byed ces bya-ba #  dang sbyar te /
kaTam iti atas Aha kuSala akuSala karma Pala upaBogAt iti
# ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba'i-las #  kyi 'bras-bu #  la nye-bar-spyod-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
vedanA indriyANi paQca suKam duHKam sOmanasyam dOrmanasyam upekzA ca
# tshor-ba'i-dbang #  po ni lnga ste / / bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  dang yid-bde-ba #  dang yid-mi-bde-ba #  dang btang-snyoms #  so /
tarhi kuSala akuSala karma PalaH upaBujyate anuBava Atmaka tvAt
# de-dag #  ni myong-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin-pas #  dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba'i-las #  kyi 'bras-bu #  spyod kyi /
na nAma rUpasya tadA ADipatyam vedanA samBAra BAvAt
# ming-dang-gzugs #  ni de-la #  dbang-byed-pa #  ma yin te / / tshor-ba # 'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
tat samBAra BAvaH ca vedanA praDAna tvAt vipAkasya iti
# de'i rgyu'i-dngos-po #  ni tshor-ba #  rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i gtso bo yin pa'i phyir ro /
lOkika viSudDiH prahANam lOkika kleSAnAm
# 'jig-rten-pa # 'i rnam-par-dag-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams spang-pa # 'o /
tatra SradDA AdInAm iti / SradDA vIrya smRti samADi prajQA paQca indriyANAm / ADipatyam iti vartate
# de-la #  dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni dad-pa #  dang brtson 'grus dang dran-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang shes-rab #  kyi dbang-po #  dang lnga ste / / dbang byed ces bya-ba # r snyegs so /
tezAm aSradDa Adi pratipakzetvena lOkika mArga praBAvita tvAt
# de-dag #  ni ma-dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  yin pa dang 'jig-rten-pa'i-lam #  gyis rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
mokza BAgIya praBAvita tvAt iti apare
# gzhan na re thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro zhe'o /
loka uttara viSudDO= anAjQAnam AjQAsyAmi indriya AdInAm iti ADipatyam / iti vartate
# 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i rnam-par-dag-pa #  ni kun-shes-par-byed-pa # 'i dbang-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni dbang byed do zhes-bya-ba # r snyegs te /
loka uttara mArgeNa kleSAnAm prahANam loka uttara viSudDiH
# 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam gyis nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams spangs-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i rnam-par-dag-pa # 'o /
tatra anAjQAtam AjQAsyAmi indriya ajQa indriya ajQAtO= indriyANAm / trayANAm ADipatyam
# de-la #  kun-shes-par-byed-pa # 'i dbang-po #  dang kun-shes-pa'i-dbang-po #  dang kun-shes-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i dbang-po-gsum #  ni dbang-byed-pa #  ste /
tezAm darSana BAvanA SEkza mArgezu yaTAkramam saMgRhIta tvAt
# de-dag #  mthong-ba #  dang bsgom-pa #  dang mi-slob-pa # 'i lam-du #  rim-pa #  bzhin-du #  bsdus-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tatra SradDA AdInAm paQca manaH suKa sOmanasya upekzANi / ca anAgamya Adi ASrita viSezeNa samBavam aDikRtya etAni nava indriyANi / darSana mArge anAjQAtam AjQAsyAmi indriyam / BAvanA mArgaH AjQa indriyam / aSEkzaMArga ajQAtO= indriyam iti ucyate / yoga AcArANAm tu anyaTA vyavasTAnam p / anAjQAtam AjQAsyAmi indriya ajQa indriye dvaye daSa indriyANi / pUrvoktezu navasu dOrmanasyam aDikam prakzipya daSa Bavanti / AjQAtO= indriyan tu nava eva / tatra prayoga mArge nirveDa BAgIya Atmake paQcadaSasu ca / darSana mArga kzaNezu mana Endriyam paQca / SradDA AdIni anAgamya Adi ASrita viSezeNa yaTAsaMBavam / suKa sOmanasya dOrmanasya upekzA indriyANAm ca anyatamAt dOrmanasya indriyam
# de-la #  dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  lnga dang yid dang bde-ba #  dang yid-mi-bde-ba #  dang btang-snyoms #  rnams ni mi lcogs-pa #  med-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la brten-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis ci-rigs #  pa'i dbang-du-byas-te #  / / dbang-po #  dgu ni mthong-ba'i-lam #  la ni kun-shes-par-byed-pa # 'i dbang-po # 'o / / bsgom-pa'i-lam #  la ni kun-shes-pa'i-dbang-po # 'o / / mi-slob-pa # 'i lam la ni kun-shes-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i dbang-po #  zhes-bya'o #  / / rnal-'byor-pa #  rnams ni gzhan-du #  rnam-pa # r 'jog ste / / kun-shes-par-byed-pa # 'i dbang-po #  dang kun-shes-pa'i-dbang-po #  gnyis la ni dbang-po #  bcu ste / / sngar smos-pa #  dgu'i nang-du #  yid-mi-bde-ba #  bsnan na bcur 'gyur ro / / kun-shes-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i dbang-po #  la ni dgu nyid do / / de-la #  nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  sbyor-ba'i-lam #  dang mthong-ba'i-lam #  skad-cig #  bco lnga dag la ni yid-kyi-dbang-po #  dang dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  lnga dang mi lcogs-pa #  med-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la brten-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis ci-rigs-par #  bde-ba #  dang yid-bde-ba #  dang yid-mi-bde-ba #  dang btang-snyoms #  kyi dbang-po #  rnams las gang-yang-rung-ba # 'o /
punar prayoga kAle nirveDa BAgIya pRzWena uttara vimokza spRhA saFgRhItam / veditavyam / tat etat saMBavataH daSaviDam indriyam
# yid-mi-bde-ba # 'i dbang-po #  ni sbyor-ba # 'i dus na nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  thar-pa #  mchog 'dod-pa # s bsdus-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / dbang-po #  'di bcu ni ci-rigs-par-sbyar-bar #  bya ste /
anAjQAtam eva ajQAtum pravRtta tvAt anAjQAtam AjQAsyAmi indriyam / ucyate
# sngon kun mi-shes-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  kun-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir zhugs-pa # s mi-shes-pa #  kun-shes-par-byed-pa # 'i dbang-po #  zhes-bya'o #  /
tat eva daSaviDam indriyam zoXa SadarSana mArga kzaNa Adi vat vajra upamaH / samADiH iti etasmin SEkzamArgam AjQa indriyam iti ucyate
# mthong-ba'i-lam #  skad-cig-ma #  bcu drug nas rdo-rje #  lta-bu # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi bar-du #  slob-pa'i-lam #  de-la #  dbang-po #  rnam-pa-bcu-po #  de nyid kun-shes-pa'i-dbang-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  ste /
apUrva ajQAta ajQeya aBAvAt
# sngon mi-shes-pa #  shes-pa # r byar med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aSEkza mArge dOrmanasya indriya vyatiriktAni / SizwAni ajQAtO= indriya AKyAm pratilaBante
# mi-slob-pa # 'i lam la yid-mi-bde-ba # 'i dbang-po-ma-gtogs-pa # r lhag-ma #  rnams kun-shes-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i dbang-po # 'i ming 'thob po /
AjQAtO= indriyam iti AjQAtO= indriyam ucyate
# kun-shes-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i dbang-po #  yin-pas #  kun-shes-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i dbang-po #  zhes-bya'o #  /
evam indriya kOSalasya yaH puruza nArAyaNa ISvara Adizu aDipati grAhaH sa / vyAvartate / aDyArTaH / indriya arTa anantaram aDvatrayaH vaktavyaH iti atas Aha
# de-ltar-na #  dbang-po #  la mkhas-pa #  ni skyes-bu #  dang mthu bo che dang sred-med-kyi-bu #  la-sogs-pa #  la dbang-po # r 'dzin-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ldog-pa # r 'gyur ro / / dbang-po # 'i don gyi 'og-tu #  dus-gsum #  gyi don brjod dgos-pa # s / / de'i-phyir #  /
Pala hetu upayoga arTanA upayogAt taTA aparam iti
# 'bras-bu #  rgyu rnams spyad zin dang / / de-bzhin #  ma spyad gzhan yin no / / zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
tatra janma kAraNam hetuH / Palam janam asaMgRhItam / Pala dAnam hetoH upayogaH
# de-la #  rgyu ni skye-bar-byed-pa # 'i rgyu'o / / 'bras-bu #  ni tshes-pa #  sdus pa'o / / rgyu spyad-zin-pa #  ni 'bras-bu #  phyung zin-pa # 'o /
Palasya upAyogaH anuBUtasya parikzayaH / evam prakAraH ca atItaH hetuH tad Palam ca iti atas Palasya
# 'bras-bu-spyad-zin-pa #  ni myong nas yongs-su-zad-pa #  ste / / rnam-pa #  de-lta-bu # 'i rgyu dang de'i 'bras-bu #  ni 'das-pa # 'o /
tad hetoH ca upayoga arTena AnItaH aDvA
# de'i-phyir #  'bras-bu #  dang de'i rgyu spyad-zin-pa # 'i phyir 'das-pa'i-dus #  so /
tena eva prakAreNa Palasya hetoH ca anupayoga arTena anAgataH aDvA
# rnam-pa #  'di nyid kyi 'bras-bu #  dang rgyu-ma #  spyad-pa # 'i phyir ma-'ongs-pa # 'i dus so /
vartamAnaH punar aDvA vartamAnam janma / hetoH datta PalatvAt hetu upayoga arTena tat PalaQca vartamAnam
# da-ltar-byung-ba # 'i dus ni da-ltar #  gyi tshe'i rgyus 'bras-bu-byin-pa # 'i phyir rgyu spyad-pa # 'i don dang de'i 'bras-bu #  ni da-ltar #  gyi tshe rjes-su-'brang-ba #  nyid de /
janmA anuvartate eva iti PalA anuyoga arTena ca veditavyaH
# 'bras-bu #  ma-spyad-pa # 'i phyir da-ltar-byung-ba # 'i dus-su #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
BAva anAQca pratikzaNam hetu Pala BAva tvena kzaNa tvam / aDikRtyA aDva vyavasTAnam veditavyam
# dngos-po #  rnams kyi skad-cig #  so-so #  ni rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # 'i dngos-po #  yin-pas #  skad-cig #  nyid kyi dbang-du-byas-te #  dus rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra hetu upayogaH sva Palasya utpAdanAt
# de-la #  rgyu spyad-zin-pa #  ni rang-gi-'bras-bu #  bskyed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
Pala upayogaH Palasya janma anantara vinASAt / evam Pala hetu upayoga arTena atItaH aDvA Pala hetvoH / anupayoga arTena anAgataH UrDva iti prakRtam / kArya anutpAdAt anutpannasya ca vinASa aBAvAt Pala hetvoH anupayogaH
# 'bras-bu-spyad-zin-pa #  ni 'bras-bu #  skyes ma-thag-tu #  'jig-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-ltar #  'bras-bu #  dang rgyu-ma #  spyad-pa # 'i phyir ma-'ongs-pa # 'i dus te / / dgos-pa #  ma-bskyed-pa #  dang ma-skyes-pa #  la zhig-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir 'bras-bu #  dang rgyu-ma #  spyad-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
veditavyaH p / hetu upayoga Pala anupayoga arTena iti kArya utpAdanAt hetu upayogaH / kAryA vinASAt PalA anupayogaH / evam aDva kuSalasya nitya AtmA iti grAhaH vyAvartate / aDavya tiriktasya anyasyA anupalabDa tvAt / catur satya arTaH / aDvatraya arTa anantaram catur satya arTaH vaktavyaH iti atas Aha / vedanA nimitta arTa tat nimitta prapattitaH / iti vistaraH / vedanA duHKa arTaH iti loke rUXam
# rgyu spyad la 'bras-bu #  ma-spyad-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni dgos-pa #  bskyed-pa # 'i phyir rgyu spyad-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / dgos-pa #  ma-zhig-pa # 'i phyir 'bras-bu #  ma-spyad-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / de-ltar #  dus la mkhas-pa #  ni dus ma-gtogs-par #  gzhan mi dmigs-pa # 'i phyir bdag rtag-par #  'dzin-pa #  ldog-pa # r 'gyur ro / / dus-gsum #  gyi don gyi 'og-tu #  bden-pa #  bzhi'i don brjod dgos-pa # s / / de'i-phyir #  / / tshor-ba #  rgyu-dang-bcas-pa # 'i don / / de yi rgyu ni sgrub-pa #  yin / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so / / tshor-ba #  ni sdug-bsngal #  gyi don to zhes 'jig-rten #  na grags so / / bstan-bcos #  las kyang gang-ci #  tshor yang rung ste / / de ni 'dir sdug-bsngal #  lo zhe'o /
SAstre ca yat kiQcid veditam idam atra duHKasya iti vacanAt / satya vyavasTAyAm sarvA sa asravA sa nimittA suKA duHKA suKA duHKA
# bden-pa #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  ni zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  dang bde-ba #  yang ma yin sdug-bsngal #  yang ma-yin-pa # 'i tshor-ba #  rgyu-dang-bcas-pa #  thams-cad #  sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa # 'i don yin no zhes bstan-pa # 'i phyir bshad-pa #  byed-pa # s kyang /
ca vedanA duHKa satya arTaH iti pradarSayan BAzyakAraH Aha tatra / duHKa satyam vedanA nimitta arTena iti / sarvA vedanA duHKam iti kutas etat
# de-la #  sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  ni tshor-ba #  rgyu-dang-bcas-pa # 'i don zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / tshor-ba #  thams-cad #  sdug-bsngal #  yin par ci mngon zhe na /
atas Aha yat kiQcid veditam idam atra duHKasya iti kRtvA iti / sA ca vedanA duHKa duHKa tA vipariNAma duHKa tA saMskAra duHKa tABiH / yaTAsamBavam duHKA / saMskAra duHKa tayA eva vA duHKA / vedanA nimittam panar vedanA sTAnIyA DarmA veditavyA iti / suKa duHKA asuKa vedanIyA DarmA vedanA sTAnAni
# de'i-phyir #  gang-ci #  tshor yang rung ste / / de ni 'dir sdug-bsngal #  lo zhes-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / tshor-ba #  de-dag #  kyang sdug-bsngal-gyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid dang 'gyur-ba'i-sdug-bsngal #  nyid dang 'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid rnams su ji-ltar #  mthun du sbyar te / / sdug-bsngal-ba # 'o / / yang-na #  'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid kyi sdug-bsngal-ba # 'o / / tshor-ba # 'i rgyu ni tshor-ba # 'i gnas kyi chos-rnams #  su rig-par-bya # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la / / bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  ba dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  yang ma yin bde-ba #  yang ma yin myong-bar-'gyur-ba # 'i chos-rnams #  ni tshor-ba # 'i gnas rnams so /
evam paQca skanDAH duHKa satyam nirdizwam
# de-ltar #  phung-po #  lnga po dag ni sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa # r bstan-pa #  yin no /
tat nimitta pratipattitaH samudaya satyam iti
# de'i rgyu ni sgrub-pa #  yin / / kun-'byung-ba # 'i bden-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  la /
tat Sabdena duHKa satyam aBisambaDyate
# de'i zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  dang sbyar ro /
duHKam yayA pratipattyA janyate sA pratipattiH samudaya satyam
# sgrub-pa #  gang-gis #  sdug-bsngal #  skyed-pa #  ni bsgrub-pa #  ste kun-'byung-ba # 'o /
sA punar vedanAyAm vedanA sTAniyezu ca Darmezu tRzNA hetu pUrvikA / kAya vAc manaH pracala svarUpA / saMkzepataH ca Bava samudBavikam karma samudaya satyam iti uktam Bavati
# de-yang #  tshor-ba #  dang tshor-ba # 'i gnas kyi chos-rnams #  la sred-pa # 'i rgyu sngon-du #  song-ba # 'i lus dang ngag dang yid rab tu g-yo-ba # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  do / / mdor-na #  yang-srid-pa #  kun-nas-slong-ba # 'i las ni kun-'byung-ba # r bstan-pa #  yin no /
tayoH Sama arTena niroDasatyam iti
# de gnyis zhi-ba # 'i phyir 'gog-pa # 'i bden-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
tayoH iti duHKa samudaya satyayoH
# de gnyis zhes-bya-ba #  ni sdug-bsngal #  dang kun-'byung-ba # 'i bden-pa #  gnyis so /
Sama arTena iti utpAdana arTena
# zhi-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni mi-skye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
eva Qca sa hetuka duHKa anutpala kzaNa tvAt niroDaH dviviDaH uktaH
# de-ltar #  rgyu-dang-bcas-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal #  mi-skye-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir 'gog-pa #  la rnam-pa-gnyis #  su bstan-pa #  yin te /
samudaya Sama arTena sa upaDi SezaH duHKa upaSama arTena nirupADi SezaH iti
# kun-'byung-ba #  zhi-ba # 'i phyir phung-po # 'i lhag-ma #  dang bcas-pa # 'o / / sdug-bsngal #  zhi-ba # 'i phyir phung-po # 'i lhag-ma #  med-pa # 'o /
tayoH eva aDikRtayoH duHKa samudayayoH pratipakza arTena / duHKa samudaya niroDa gAminI pratipad mArga satyam
# de nyid kyi dbang-du-byas-nas #  sdug-bsngal #  dang kun-'byung-ba #  gnyis kyi gnyen-po # 'i phyir sdug-bsngal #  dang kun-'byung-ba #  'gog-par #  'gyur-ba # 'i lam ni lam gyi bden-pa # 'o /
tat evam satya kuSalasya saFkleSa vyavadAna mAtra avagata tvAt tad anyaH / saFkleSa vyavadAna grahaH vyAvartate tasya aBAvAt iti / yAna trayA arTaH p
# de-ltar #  bden-pa #  la mkhas-pa #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  tsam rtogs-nas #  de-dag #  las gzhan-pa #  la kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # r 'dzin-pa #  ldog-pa # r 'gyur te / / de med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
satya arTa anantaram yAna traya arTam pratipAdyataH iti atas Aha / guNa dozA avikalpena jQAnena / iti vistaraH
# bden-pa #  rnams kyi don gyi 'og-tu #  theg-pa-gsum #  gyi don bstan-pa # r bya ste / / de'i-phyir #  / / yon-tan #  skyon dang rnam mi rtog / / shes-pa # s gzhan-las #  bdag-gis #  ni / / nges-par #  'byung phyir gzhan zhes bya / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so /
jQAna SabdaH uBayatra sambaDyate / guNa doza jQAnena avikalpa jQAnena ca iti
# shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni yon-tan-dang-skyon #  shes-pa #  dang rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes zhes-bya-ba #  gnyis-ka #  dang sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
aTavA antare vikalpa SabdaH luptaH drazwavyaH / tatra guNa doza jQAnena paratas svayaQca iti atas eva Aha vRttO yaTAyogam iti
# yang-na #  bar-du #  rnam-pa # r rtog / / ces bya-ba # 'i sgra zhig ma smos-pa # r blta-bar-bya # 'o / / de-la #  yon-tan-dang-skyon #  shes-pa #  ni gzhan-las #  dang bdag-gis #  zhes phye ste brjod-pa # r bya'o / / rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyi ni bdag-nyid-kyis #  te / / de-bas-na #  'grel pa las ci-rigs-su #  sbyar-ba # r bya'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tatra nirvANa saMsArayoH guNa doza jQAnena iti
# de-la #  mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  dang 'khor-ba #  la yon-tan-dang-skyon #  du shes zhes-bya-ba #  la /
nirvANa Sabdena atra mArga niroDO saFgRhItO yaTA praSAnta SabdaH
# mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni 'dir lam dang 'gog-par #  gzung ste / / dper-na #  rab-tu-zhi-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra bzhin no /
tatra niroDe SAnta Adi AkArEH mArge nEryANika Adi AkArEH jQAnam / nirvANe guNa jQAnam
# de-la #  'gog-pa #  la ni zhi-ba # 'i rnam-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dang lam la nges-par-'byin-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r shes-pa #  ni mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la yon-tan #  du shes-pa # 'o /
saMsAraH api duHKa samudaya AtmakaH
# 'khor-ba #  ni sdug-bsngal #  dang kun-'byung-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  de /
tatra api anitya duHKa Adi AkArEH samudaya pratyaya Adya AkArEH ca jQAnam / saMsAre doza jQAnam
# de-yang #  mi-rtag-pa #  dag sdug-bsngal-ba # 'i rnam-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dang kun-'byung-ba #  dang rkyen gyi rnam-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r shes-pa #  ni 'khor-ba #  la skyon du shes-pa # 'o /
paratas SrutvA iti budDa boDisattva AdiByaH nirvANa saMsArayoH / guNAn yaTA ekAn dozAn= ca SrutvA iti
# gzhan-las #  thos zhes-bya-ba #  ni sangs-rgyas #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  la-sogs-pa #  las mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  dang 'khor-ba #  gnyis kyi yon-tan-dang-skyon #  ji-skad-du #  smos-pa #  thos-pa # 'o /
niryANa arTena iti saMsAra nirgama arTena
# nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'khor-ba #  las byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
SrAvaka yAnam iti para dGoza saMnirayeNa niryANAt SrAvakAyan mA iti
# nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzhan gyi sgra la brten-nas #  nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
pratyekabudDa yAnAt viSezam darSayati
# nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # s ni rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi theg-pa #  las bye-brag #  tu ston to /
tena eva iti nirvANa saMsArayoH guNa doza jQAnena svayam aSrutvA paratas / budDa boDa sattveByaH niryANa arTena pratyekabudDa yAnam
# de nyid kyis zhes-bya-ba #  ni mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  dang 'khor-ba #  gnyis la yon-tan-dang-skyon #  du shes-nas #  sangs-rgyas #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  gzhan-las #  ma-thos-pa # r bdag-gis #  nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i phyir rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi theg-pa # 'o /
svayam aSrutvA iti SrAvaka yAnAt viSezaNam
# gzhan-las #  ma-thos-pa # r bdag-gis #  shes-par-bya-ba #  ni nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa #  las bye-brag #  tu bstan to /
avikalpena jQAnena iti saMsAra nirvANayoH anaBilApya Darma tA prativeDAt / avikalpam jQAnam
# rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyis zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'khor-ba #  dang mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i chos gnyis brjod-du-med-pa # r rtogs-pa # 'i phyir rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes te /
svayam eva paratas SrutvA niryANa arTena mahAyAnam
# gzhan-las #  ma-thos-pa # r bdag-nyid-kyis #  nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i phyir theg-pa-chen-po # 'i /
atra hi jQAnena iti pratyekabudDa yAnAt viSezaH
# 'dir ni rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi theg-pa #  las ye shes kyis bye-brag #  tu byas so /
anye tu AhuH pudgala nErAtmya vizayeNa guNa dozA avikalpena jQAnena / paratas SrutvA niryANam SrAvaka yAnam
# gzhan dag na re gzhan-las #  thos-nas #  gang-zag #  la bdag-med-pa # 'i yul can yon-tan-dang-skyon #  du rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyis nges-par-'byung-ba #  ni nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa # 'o /
SravaNa nirapekzasya svayam niryANam pratyekabudDa yAnam
# mnyam-pa #  la mi ltos-pa # r bdag-nyid-kyis #  nges-par-'byung-ba #  ni rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi theg-pa # 'o /
Darma nErAtmya vizayeNa pratizWita nirvANa prApakena avikalpena jQAnena / svayam niryANam mahAyAnam ucyate / etat vyAKyAnam BAzyeNa viruDyate
# mi-gnas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  thob-par-byed-pa #  chos-la-bdag-med-pa # 'i yul can rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyi bdag-nyid-kyis #  nges-par-'byung-ba #  ni theg-pa-chen-po #  zhes-bya'o #  / / rnam-pa # r bshad-pa #  'di ni 'grel pa dang 'gal lo /
evam yAna traya kuSalasya yoga mAtra darSanAt AtmA yogI iti grAhaH / vyAvartate p / saMskRtA asaMskRta arTaH / idAnIm saMskRta asaMskRta arTam pratipAdayan= Aha / sa prajQapti sa hetukAt / nimittAt praSamAt sArTAt paScimam samudAhRtam iti / kim idam paScimam samudAhRtam / iti atas Aha saMskRtA asaMskRtam iti sarva paScAt udizwa tvAt
# de-ltar #  theg-pa-gsum #  la mkhas-pa #  ni rnal-'byor #  tsam du zad-pa # r mthong-ba # s bdag rnal-'byor #  can du 'dzin-pa #  ldog-pa # r 'gyur ro / / nga ni 'dus byas dang 'dus-ma-byas #  kyi don bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / btags bcas rgyur bcas rgyu mtshan dang / / rab-tu-zhi-ba #  don bcas ni / / tha-ma #  nyid-du #  bshad-pa #  yin / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so / / tha-ma # r bshad-pa #  de gang zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  / / 'dus byas dang 'dus-ma-byas #  so zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
tatra saMskRtam sa prajQaptikAt sa hetukAt ca nimittAt asaMskRtam punar
# thams-cad-kyi-tha-ma # r bshad-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-la #  'dus byas ni btags-pa #  dang bcas shing rgyu-dang-bcas-pa # 'i rgyu mtshan gyis rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
sArTAt praSamAt vyavasTApitam
# 'dus-ma-byas #  ni don dang bcas-pa # 'i rab-tu-zhi-ba # s rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
prajQapti hetu nimittam punar ajQAnAt / tat pradarSayan= Aha tatra sa prajQaptiH nAmakAya AdayaH iti
# btags-pa #  dang rgyu dang rgyu mtshan yang mi shes-nas #  de bstan-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir / / de-la #  btags-pa #  ni ming-gi-tshogs #  la-sogs-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
prajQapyete svaBAva viSezO BAvAnAm nAma pada kAyAByAm iti / nAmapadakayO prajQaptiH
# ming dang tshig gi tshogs kyi dngos-po #  dag gi ngo-bo-nyid #  dang khyad-par #  gnyis btags-pa # s na ming dang tshig gi tshogs gnyis ni btags-pa # 'o /
vyaQjana kAyaH tu tat uBaya aBivyaQjaka tvAt prajQaptiH
# yi-ge # 'i tshogs ni de-gnyi-ga #  gsal-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir btags-pa # 'o /
hetuH punar bIja saFgRhItam AlayavijQAnam iti / tat ca sarva sAhasra vaDa vAsanA anvitam adatta Palam / samudaya satya saFgRhItam / atas eva datta PalAt vyavacCeda arTam bIja saFgRhItam iti Aha
# rgyu ni sa-bon #  du bsdus-pa # 'i kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  de-yang #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i chos-thams-cad #  kyi bag-chags #  kyi rjes-su-song-ba #  'bras-bu-ma-byin-pa #  kun-'byung-ba # 'i bden-pa # r bsdus-pa #  nyid de / / 'bras-bu-byin-pa #  las rnam-par-dbye-ba # 'i phyir / / sa-bon #  du bsdus-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
nimittam pratizWA deha Boga saFgRhItam iti Alaya vijQAnam iti prakRtam
# rgyu mtshan ni gnas dang lus-dang-longs-spyod #  du bsdus-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro /
pravRtti vijQAna saFgRhItaH ca manadugraha vikalpaH iti / tatra pratizWA BAjana lokaH / tad ABAsam AlayavijQAnam
# 'jug-pa #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa # r bsdus-pa #  yid dang 'dzin-pa #  dang rnam-par-rtog-pa # r bsdus-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  gnas ni snod-kyi-'jig-rten #  te / / der-snang-ba # 'i kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o /
pratizWA AtmanA saFgRhItam iti pratizWA saFgRhItam
# gnas kyi bdag-nyid #  du bsdus-pa # s na gnas-su-bsdus-pa # 'o /
dehaH sa indriyam SarIram tad ABAsam AlayavijQAnam deha saFgRhItam
# lus su snang-ba # 'i rang-bzhin #  la lus su bsdus-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / lus ni dbang-po-dang-bcas-pa # 'i khog-pa #  lus der-snang-ba # 'i kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o /
deha AtmanA upagatam iti arTaH p
# lus su bsdus-pa #  ni lus kyi bdag-nyid #  dang ldan-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
Boga saFgRhIta tamaH deva uttaram uktam
# longs-spyod #  du bsdus-pa #  ni gong-du #  bshad-pa #  de nyid de /
tat dvayam SezANi vijQAnAni aDipati vastu tvena BuQjataH iti BogaH
# de gnyis la yang rnam-par-shes-pa #  gzhan dag dbang-byed-pa # 'i dngos-po # r longs-spyod-pa # s na longs-spyod #  do /
aTavA anna pAna AdikaH arTaH Bujyate iti BogaH
# yang-na #  bza'-ba-dang-btung-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i don la longs-spyod-pa # s na longs-spyod #  de /
tat nirBAsam vijQAnam Boga saFgRhItam
# der-snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni longs-spyod #  du bsdus-pa # 'o /
etat saprajQapti sa hetukam nimittam sa samprayogam / paratantra svaBAva saFgRhIta tvAt saMskRtam veditavyam
# btags-pa #  dang bcas shing rgyu-dang-bcas-pa # 'i rgyu mtshan de ni mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo bsdus-pa # 'i phyir 'dus byas su rig-par-bya # 'o /
samprayogaH ca etAH / tat saMskRtam na kevalam tat eva iti darSayati / kasya punar tad nimittam
# mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  ni sems-las-byung-ba #  ste / / 'dus byas de ni de nyid 'ba'-zhig #  ma-yin-pa # r bstan to / / de-yang #  gang-gi #  rgyu mtshan zhe na /
nAmakAya AdInAm / tezAm tat svaBAva viSeza saMsUcaka tvAt tad anusAreNa ca
# ming-gi-tshogs #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyu mtshan te / / de ni de-dag #  gi ngo-bo-nyid #  dang khyad-par #  rjod-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
svaBAva viSeza aBiniveSinAm citta cEttAnAm mad Odgraha vikalpa AKyAnAm / nimittam
# de-dag #  gi rjes-su-'brang-ba # s rang bzhen dang bye-brag #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  yid dang 'dzin-pa #  dang rnam-par-rtog-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  rnams kyi rgyu mtshan yang yin no /
mad Odgraha vikalpaH cAlaya vijQAnasya nimittam
# kha-cig #  na re yid dang 'dzin-pa #  dang rnam-par-rtog-pa #  yang kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rgyu mtshan te /
tasmin vAsana pozaNa tvAt iti eke
# de-la #  bag-chags #  brtas-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro zhe'o /
anye tu manyante svaBAva viSeza prajQApanAt prajQapteH nimittam / saMjQAm nimitta udgrahaNa AtmikA iti vacanAt
# gzhan dag ni rang-bzhin #  bye-brag #  tu 'dogs-pa # s na 'dogs-pa # 'i mtshan-ma #  ni 'du-shes #  te / / mtshan-mar-'dzin-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  phyir ro /
pratizWA deha Boga saMgRhItam AlayavijQAnam nidAna nimittam / vAsanA pozaNa tvAt
# gnas dang lus-dang-longs-spyod #  du bsdus-pa #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni bag-chags #  brtas-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir gzhi'i rgyu mtshan no /
Alambana nimitta paQca manaH udgraha vikalpAH Alambana nimittIkaraNa arTena / Alambana Alambana nimittam ca uBayaTA nimittIkaraNAt iti
# yid dang 'dzin-pa #  dang rnam-par-rtog-pa #  rnams ni dmigs-pa #  mtshan-ma # r byed-pa # 'i phyir dmigs-pa # 'i rgyu mtshan yang yin la / / gnyi-ga #  mtshan-ma # r byed-pa # 'i phyir dmigs-pa #  dang dmigs-par-byed-pa # 'i rgyu mtshan yang yin no snyam-du #  sems so /
tatra manaH yat nityam manyana AkAram iti
# de-la #  yid la gang rtag ru rlom sems-pa # 'i rnam-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
aham mama iti yat nityam manyate tat mataH ucyate
# bdag gam bdag-gi #  zhes-bya-ba #  gang rtag-par #  rlom sems-pa #  de ni yid ces bya ste /
tat ca samprayuktam Atma moha Atma dRzwi Atma sneha Atma mAnEH paQcaBiH ca / sarvatragEH vedanA saMjQA cetanA sparSa manaskArEH iti
# de ni bdag tu rmongs-pa #  dang bdag-tu-lta-ba #  dang bdag-la-chags-pa #  dang nga'o-snyam-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  dang kun du 'gro-ba-lnga-po #  tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang sems-pa #  dang reg-pa #  dang yid-la-byed-pa #  dag dang mtshungs-pa # r ldan no /
udgrahaH paQca vijQAna kAyAH iti vizaya svarUpa grahaNa lakzaNa tvAt
# 'dzin-pa #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs lnga po zhes-bya-ba #  ni yul gyi rang-bzhin #  gyi ngo bo 'dzin-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyi phyir ro /
sva saMvedyA iti AKyAtum aSakya tvAt udgrahaH ucyate
# rang rig-pa #  yin-pas #  brjod mi-nus-pa # 'i phyir 'dzin-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
vikalpaH manaH vijQAnam / tasya Darma sva sAmAnya lakzaNa vikalpaka tvAt iti
# rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  ste / / de ni chos-rnams #  kyi rang-dang-spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  la rnam-par-rtog-pa #  can gyi phyir ro /
etat sarvam sa prajQapti sa hetukam nimittam karma kleSAByAm / aBisaMskRta tvAt saMskRtam
# btags-pa #  dang bcas shing rgyu-dang-bcas-pa # 'i rgyu mtshan 'di-las #  nyon-mongs-pa #  gnyis kyis mngon-par-'dus-byas-pa # 'i phyir 'dus byas so /
asaMskRtam punar praSamaH ca niroDaH praSama arTaH ca taTatA iti yuktam
# 'dus-ma-byas #  ni rab-tu-zhi-ba # 'i 'gog-pa #  dang rab-tu-zhi-ba # 'i don de-bzhin-nyid #  de-bzhin-nyid #  de zhes-bya-ba #  la /
niroDasya praSama svarUpa tvam sannimitta duHKa praSama lakzaNAt
# rgyu-dang-bcas-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal #  rab-tu-zhi-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir 'gog-pa #  ni rab-tu-zhi-ba # 'i bar rung na /
kaTam taTatA praSama arTam ucyate iti / praSamasya arTaH iti kRtvA
# de-bzhin-nyid #  ji-ltar #  rab-tu-zhi-ba # 'i don ces bya zhe na / / rab-tu-zhi-ba # 'i don yin pa'i phyir ro /
nanu ca niroDena taTA tayA na kaScid sambanDaH asti kaTam praSama arTa tvam
# 'gog-pa #  dang de-bzhin-nyid #  gnyis 'brel-pa #  ci-yang-med-pa #  snyam na / / ji-ltar #  rab-tu-zhi-ba # 'i don zhes bya zhe na /
taTatAyAH mArga Alambana tvAt
# de-bzhin-nyid #  ni lam gyi dmigs-pa #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
mArgasya punar kaTam praSama tvam / tena praSamanAt
# ji-ltar #  na lam yang rab-tu-zhi-ba #  nyid ces bya zhe na / / des rab-tu-zhi-ba # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nirvANam praSamaH praSamanAt
# rab-tu-zhi-ba # 'i phyir mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  ni rab-tu-zhi-ba # 'o /
anena ca praSamanAt praSamaH mArgaH
# 'dis rab-tu-zhi-ba # r byed-pa # 'i phyir lam yang rab-tu-zhi-ba # 'o /
evam vigraha BedAt eka aBiDAnena nirvANa mArgayoH grahaNam praSamaH iti
# de-ltar-na #  tshig rnam-pa # r sbyar-ba #  tha-dad-pa # 'i phyir brjod-pa #  gcig gis mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  dang lam gnyi-ga #  rab-tu-zhi-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # r bzung ngo /
mArga satyam punar kim saMskRtam asaMskRtam / saMskRtam utpAdya tvAt
# ci lam gyi bden-pa #  'dus byas sam 'on te 'dus-ma-byas #  she na / / bskyed-par-bya-ba #  yin-pas #  'dus byas so /
yadi karma kleSAByAm anaBisaMskRtAt asaMskRtena ca praBAvitAt / asaMskRtam iti brUyAt na dozaH syAt iti
# gal-te #  las dang nyon-mongs-pa # s mngon-pa # r 'dus-ma-byas #  pa dang 'dus-ma-byas #  kyis rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir 'dus-ma-byas #  zhes brjod na nyes-pa #  med do /
iti etena arTena skanDa Adizu jQAnam skanDa Adi kOSalyam veditavyam iti p
# de-ltar #  don 'dis phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  shes-pa #  ni phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  la mkhas-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
aneka tva aBisaMkzepa paricCeda arTaH Aditas
# thog-ma #  du-ma #  nyid dang ni / / bsdus dang yongs su phye-ba # 'i don /
iti vistareNa sarvatra vAcyam / tattva piNXa arTaH / tattvasya piNXa arTaH / samAsatas dviviDam tattvam / vistareNa daSaviDam uktam / atas samAsatas dviviDam iti Aha AdarSa tattvam dRSya tattvaQca
# zhes-bya-ba #  ste / / rgyas-pa # r thams-cad-la #  brjod-pa # r bya'o / / de-kho-na'i-don #  bsdus-pa #  ni mdor-bsdu-na #  de-kho-na #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  so / / rgyas-pa # r ni rnam-pa-bcu # r bshad do / / de-bas-na #  mdor-bsdu-na #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  te zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / rnam-pa-gnyis #  po ji-lta-bu #  zhe na / / me long lta-bu # 'i de-kho-na #  dang snang-ba # 'i de-kho-na # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tatra mUla tattvam AdarSa tattvam
# de-la #  rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  de ni me long lta-bu # 'i de-kho-na #  ste /
tat punar trayaH svaBAvAH / kim arTam punar tat AdarSa tattvam iti ucyate / SezANAm lakzaNa tattva AdInAm tatra darSanAt
# de-yang #  ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum mo / / ci'i-phyir #  de-la #  me long lta-bu # 'i de-kho-na #  zhes bya zhe na / / mtshan-nyid #  kyi de-kho-na #  la-sogs-pa #  lhag-ma #  rnams der-snang-ba # 'i phyir ro /
dRSya tattvam yat lakzaNa tattva Adikam pUrva nirdizwam navaviDam / kimarTam tat dRzyatattvam iti ucyate
# snang-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  ni mtshan-nyid #  kyi de-kho-na #  la-sogs-pa #  sngar bstan-pa #  rnam-pa #  dgu gang-yin-pa # 'o / / ci'i-phyir #  de-dag #  snang-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  zhes bya zhe na /
tasya mUla tattve darSanAt niraBimAna dRSya tattvam lakzaNa tattvam
# rtsa ba'i de-kho-na #  la snang-ba # 'i phyir ro / / nga-rgyal-med-pa #  snang-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  ni mtshan-nyid #  kyi de-kho-na #  ste /
tena hi niraBimAnaH Bavati / pudgala DarmayoH grAhya grAhakayoH BAva aBAvayoH / cA samAropa anapavAda viparyAsa dRSya tattvam aviparyAsa lakzaNam
# gang-zag #  dang chos dang gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  dang dngos-po #  dang dngos-po-med-pa #  la sgro mi 'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-mi-'debs-pa # 'i phyir des nga-rgyal-med-pa # r 'gyur ro / / phyin-ci-log #  gi gnyen-po #  snang-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  ni phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  de /
tat hi nitya Adi viparyAsa pratipakza BUtam
# de ni rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r phyin-ci-log #  gi gnyen-por-gyur-pa # 'o /
SrAvaka yAna niryANa dRSya tattvam Pala hetu mayam tattvam
# nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa # s nges-par-'byung-ba #  snang-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  ni 'bras-bu #  dang rgyu'i de-kho-na #  ste /
catur Arya satya prativeDa BAvanayA SrAvaka niryANam
# 'phags-pa'i-bden-pa-bzhi #  rab tu rtogs shing bsgoms-pa # s nyan-thos #  nges-par #  'byung ngo /
mahAyAna niryANa drSyata tvam sUkzma OdArika tattvam
# theg-pa-chen-po # s nges-par-'byung-ba #  snang-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  ni phra-ba #  dang rags-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  ste /
OdArikena saMvRtisatyena sattva paripAcanAt sUkzmeNa paramArTa satyena / vimocanAt mahAyAnena niryAti
# rags-pa #  kun-rdzob-kyi-bden-pa # s sems-can #  rnams yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-pa #  dang phra-ba #  don-dam-pa'i-bden-pa # s rnam-par-grol-ba # r byed-pa # 'i phyir theg-pa-chen-po # s nges-par-'byung-ba # 'o /
para vAdini graha dRSya tattvam prasidDa tattvam
# phas-kyi-rgol-ba #  tshar-gcod-pa #  snang-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  ni grags-pa # 'i de-kho-na # 'o /
kaTam iti atas Aha dRzwAna sanniSrayeNa yuktyA nigrahAt iti
# ji lta zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  / / dpe la brten-te #  rigs-pas #  tshar-gcod-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
nigrahe loka prasidDaH dRzwAntaH / yukti prasidDa Sabda ASrayAt yuktiH
# tshar-gcod-pa #  la dpe ni 'jig-rten #  du grags-pa # 'o / / rigs-pa #  ni rigs-pas #  rab tu grub-pa #  la brten-pa # 'o /
mahAyAna aBidyotana dRSya tattvam viSudDi jQAna gocara tattvam
# theg-pa-chen-po #  mngon-par-brjod-pa #  snang-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  ni rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i ye shes kyi spyod yul gyi de-kho-na #  ste /
p / tat hi kleSa AvaraNa viSudDi jQAna gocarAt anyasya aBidyotakaH AgamaH / tat punar mahAyAnam
# des ni nyon-mongs-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i ye shes kyi spyod yul gyi lung gzhan mngon-par-brjod-pa #  ste / / de ni theg-pa-chen-po # 'o /
sarva AkAra jQeya praveSa dRSya tattvam saMgraha tattvam / tat ca paQca vastUni tatra sarva jQeya anupraveSAt / avitaTatA aBidyotana dRSya tattvam praBeda tattvam / tena hi BAvAnAm avitaTa taTatA nanyataTatayoH / Atma grAha vastu sarva aBisanDi praveSa dRSya tattvaQca iti kOSalaya tattvam / tena hi Atma grAhavaH tu sarva aBiprAya muKena praviSati iti yaTA pUrvam / uktam daSaBiH aBiprAyEH skanDa Adizu Atma grAha pravRtti tvam / tattva piNXa arTa vacanam suKa DAraNa arTam arTAt granTam Akarzati iti / asammoha apariKeda arTa Qca paridRzwa aDikAra paryantasya hi na pariKeda / upajQAyate na api sammohaH yaToddeSa nirdeSa aDigamAt uta pdyate / uktam tattvam / Agama anusAriNyAm maDya anta viBAga wIkAyAm AcArya BadantasTi / ramati uparacitAyAm tattva paricCedaH tRtIyaH samAptaH / pratipakza BAvanA avasTA Pala paricCedaH caturTaH / pratipakza BAvanA p / tattva pratipAdana anantaram pratipakza BAvanA vaktavyA tatra avasTA / Pala prAptiH ca
# shes-bya # 'i rnam-pa-thams-cad #  la 'jug-pa #  snang-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  la bsdu-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  dngos-po #  lnga ste / / de ni shes-par-bya-ba #  thams-cad-la #  'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro / / ma nor-ba #  de-bzhin-nyid #  mngon-par-brjod-pa #  snang-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  ni rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  ste / / des dngos-po #  rnams kyi ma nor-ba #  de-bzhin-nyid #  dang gzhan ma-yin-pa #  de-bzhin-nyid #  mngon-par-brjod-pa # 'i phyir ro / / bdag-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i gzhi la dgongs-pa #  thams-cad #  rtogs-pa # r snang-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mkhas-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  ste / / des bdag-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i gzhi la dgongs-pa #  thams-cad-kyi-sgo-nas #  rtogs te / / bsam-pa #  bcu po dag gis phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  la bdag-tu-'dzin-pa #  'jug-pa # r sngar ji-skad-du #  bstan-pa # 'o / / de-kho-na'i-don #  bsdus-pa #  smos-pa #  ni bde blag tu 'dzin-pa # 'i phyir te / / don-gyis #  tshig 'dren-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rmongs-pa-med-pa #  dang yongs su skyo-ba #  yang med-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir te / / skabs kyi mgo mjug yongs su mthong na yongs su skyo-ba #  mi skye'o / / ji-ltar #  bstan-pa #  bzhin-du #  bshad-pa #  rtogs-pa # s rmongs-pa #  yang mi 'byung ngo / / de-kho-na #  bshad-zin #  to / / bstan-bcos #  dbus dang mtha' rnam-par-'byed-pa #  las de-kho-na'i-le'u # r bcad-pa #  ste gsum-pa # 'i 'grel bshad do / / de-kho-na #  bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  gnyen-po-bsgom-pa #  dang de'i-gnas #  dang 'bras-bu #  thob-pa #  bshad dgos te /
atas tad pratipAdana arTam caturTa paricCeda AramBaH
# de-bas-na #  de bstan-pa # 'i phyir le'ur bcad-pa #  bzhi-pa #  brtsams so /
tattva anantaram uddizwa tvAt pratipakza BAvanA pratibadDa tvAt ca tat / avasTA Pala prAptyoH uddeSaH
# de-kho-na # 'i 'og-tu #  bstan-pa #  dang gnyen-po-bsgom-pa #  la rag lus pa'i phyir de'i-gnas #  dang 'bras-bu #  thob-pa #  gnyis kyang smos so /
sUtre pratipakaza tvena boDi pakzaH anumataH iti pradarSana arTam Aha / pratipakza BAvanA boDi pakzya BAvena iti / te hi yaTA ukta AvaraNa vipakza prahANAya BAvyamAnaH praBavanti iti / pratipakzAH ucyante
# bstan-pa # 'i mdor byas-pa #  las gnyen-po #  ni byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  su bzhed-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / gnyen-po-bsgom-pa #  ni byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  bsgom-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / de-dag #  bsgoms na mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  sgrib-pa #  ji-skad-bstan-pa #  rnams spang-bar-bya-ba #  la mthu-yod-par-'gyur-ba # s gnyen-po #  rnams zhes-bya'o #  / / de rnams kyang sum cu rtsa bdun te /
te punar saptatriMSat catvAri smRti upasTAnAni yAvat Arya azwa aFga
# dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  bzhi nas 'phags-pa'i-lam #  yan-lag-brgyad-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o /
mArgAH / tat BAvanA bRMhaNa AropaNAH aByAsaH bahulA kriyA iti paryAyAH
# de rnams bsgom-pa #  ni spel-ba #  dang bskyed-pa #  dang goms-par-bya-ba #  dang lan-mang-du-bya-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i rnam-grangs #  so /
sA idAnIm vaktavyA tattva anantaram uddizwa tvAt
# de-yang #  de-kho-na # 'o 'og-tu #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir de-yang #  brjod-pa # r bya'o /
kim kAraNam smRti upasTAna BAvanA eva pUrvam ucyate na anyA / boDipakza BAvanA / Aha tatra tAvat AdO / dOzWulyAt tarza hetu tvAt / iti vistaraH / tatra iti boDi pakza BAvanAyAm
# byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  bsgoms-pa #  la ci'i-phyir #  dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  bsgom-pa #  nyid thog-mar #  bshad kyi gzhan ni ma yin zhe na / / de-la #  re-zhig #  dang-por #  / / gnas-ngan-len #  phyir sred rgyu'i phyir / / zhes rgya-cher #  smos so / / de-la #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  bsgoms-pa #  la'o /
tAvat Sabda arTaH krama arTaH / AdO tAvat smRti upasTAna BAvanA ucyate / paScAt anyezAm api iti
# re-zhig #  ces bya-ba #  ni rim gyi don te / / thog-mar #  dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  bsgom-pa #  ji bshad la / / gzhan-yang #  phyis bshad do zhes-bya-ba # r 'gyur ro /
nirvANa saMsAroH guNa dozA anavaboDAt / saMskArezu suKa Suci nitya Atma aBiniveSena bAlAnAm Bava Boge aBivacanam p
# mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  dang 'khor-ba #  gnyis kyi yon-tan #  dang nyes-pa #  mo rtogs-pa # 'i phyir 'du-byed-rnams #  la bde-ba #  dang gtsang ba dang rtag-pa #  dang bdag tu mngon-par-zhen-pa # s byis-pa #  rnams srid-pa #  dang longs-spyod #  la mngon-pa # r dga' zhing mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # s skrag go /
nirvANa arTam trAsaH / sa ca guNa doza anavaboDaH suKa Adi aBiniveSaH ca satya darSanAt vinivartata
# yon-tan #  dang nyes-pa #  ma-rtogs-pa #  dang bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  de-yang #  bden-pa #  mthong-nas #  ldog-pa # r 'gyur te /
iti atas saMsArAt udvajana arTam nirvANe ca aBimuKIkaraNa arTam / catur satya avatArAya smRti upasTAna BAvanA eva AdO= uktA
# de'i-phyir #  'khor-ba #  la skyo-bar-bya-ba # 'i don dang mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  mngon-sum-du-bya-ba # 'i don-du #  bden-pa #  bzhi la 'jug-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  bsgom-pa #  nyid thog-mar #  bshad do /
kAyena hi dOzWulyam praBAvyate iti / dOzWulyam duHsTita tA
# lus-kyis #  ni gnas-ngan-len #  rab tu ston zhes-bya-ba #  la / / gnas-ngan-len #  ni ngan-pa # r gnas-pa #  ste /
taTA hi pratidinam aBisaMskriyamANaH vikriyate eva kAyaH iti kAyena
# 'di-ltar #  nyin gcig bzhin mngon-par-'dus-byas #  kyang lus 'gyur-ba #  nyid pas lus-kyis #  ni gnas-ngan-len #  rab tu ston to /
dOzWulyam praBAvyate / tatas ca kAya parIkzayA duHKa satyam avatarati
# de'i-phyir #  lus la yongs su brtags-pa # s sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  la 'jug go / / de-ci'i-phyir-zhe-na #  /
kim arTam etat iti Aha tasya sadA ozWulya saMskAra lakzaNa tvAt iti
# de'i mtshan-nyid #  ni gnas-ngan-len #  dang bcas-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  yin pa'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ste /
yasmAt duHKa satyasya sadA ozWulyAH saMskArAH lakzaNam svaBAvaH
# 'di-ltar #  sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ngo-bo-nyid #  ni gnas-ngan-len #  dang bcas-pa # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  yin la /
kAyena ca dOzWulyam praBAvyate tasmAt kAya parIkzayA duHKa satyam / avatarati / dOzWulyam na vijQAyate iti atas Aha dOzWulyam hi saMskAra duHKa tA iti
# lus-kyis #  kyang gnas-ngan-len #  du rab tu ston-pa # s / / de'i-phyir #  lus la yongs su brtags-pa # s sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  la 'jug go / / gnas-ngan-len #  mi-shes-pa # s de'i-phyir #  / / gnas-ngan-len #  ni 'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid de zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
saMskAraH BAvanAm utpattiH
# 'du-byed #  ni dngos-po #  rnams kyi skye-ba # 'o /
sa ca sarva viplavaH tu iti dOzWulya mAryANAm pratikUla tvAt ca duHKa tA / yaTA uktam
# de-yang #  gnod-pa #  thams-cad-kyi #  gzhi-yin-pa # s gnas-ngan-len #  yin la / / 'phags-pa #  rnams dang mi-mthun-pa # 'i phyir sdug-bsngal #  nyid de / / ji-skad-du #  /
anarTaH janma idam sati hi janane santi ripavaH
# skye 'di gnod yin pa skye-ba #  yod-na #  rga dang 'chi-ba #  dang /
jarA mRtyu vyADi vyasana banDa praBRtayaH / anarTAH te na syuH yadi na BavataH nASa viBavA
# nad dang phongs-pa #  gsod dang 'ching-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dgra rnams yod / / gal-te #  'jigs mad skye-ba #  med gyur gnod-pa #  de-dag #  med /
vajAte vRkze syAt na hi dahana dava vAyu cyutiH api
# shing skyes med na me dang rlung dang nags mes 'gyel mi 'gyur / / zhes-bya-ba #  lta-bu # 'o /
tayA iti saMskAra duHKa tayA na vipariNAma duHKa tA duHKa duHKa tAByAm / tayoH AvyApi tvAt saMskAra duHKa hata animitta tvAt ca
# des zhes-bya-ba #  'di 'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid kyis so / / 'gyur-ba'i-sdug-bsngal #  dang sdug-bsngal-gyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid-gnyis #  kyis ni ma yin te; de gnyis khyab-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  dang 'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
sarvam sa Asravam vastu AryAH duHKa tA paSyanti nA Asavam mArgasatyasya
# zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i dngos-po-thams-cad #  'phags-pa # s sdug-bsngal #  du gzigs kyi zag-pa-med-pa #  ni ma yin te /
janma utpatti pratipakza tvAt na tu pRTagjanAH viparyAsa sTAna ASraya tvAt
# lam gyi bden-pa #  na che'i gnyen-po #  yin pa'i phyir ro / / phyin-ci-log #  gi bsam-pa #  nyams-pa # 'i phyir so-so'i-skye-bo #  rnams kyis ni ma yin no /
sUtre api uktam samAsatas paQca upAdAna skanDAH duHKam iti / saMskAra duHKa tA karmaNi atra iti anye / na dOzWulyam akarmaNyAtA iti apare / kim kAraNam
# mdo'i-sde #  las kyang mdor-na #  nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga ni sdug-bsngal #  lo zhes gsungs so / / gzhan dag na re 'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid ni las-su-mi-rung-ba # 'o zhes zer ro / / gzhan na re las-su-mi-rung-ba #  ni gnas-ngan-len #  ma yin no /
akarmaNyAtAyAH sa Asrava tvAt avaSyam sa AsravatAm / bIja kAraNa utpannA
# ci'i-phyir #  zhe na / / las-su-mi-rung-ba # 'i zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i phyir nges-par #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  ni sa-bon #  gyi rgyu-las-byung-ba # r khas blang dgos na /
sA tu abIjA api arTa santAne kadAcid AhAra Adi apacArAt Bavati / na ca asO dOzWulyam Bavitum arhatya na Asrava tvAt iti
# de ni dgra-bcom-pa # 'i rgyud la sa-bon #  med kyang res-'ga' #  kha-zas #  dang gnas-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  drags-pa #  las 'byung ngo / / de ni zag-pa-med-pa #  yin pa'i phyir gnas-ngan-len #  zhes byar mi rung ngo zhes zer ro /
atas ca sa asra vaDarma bIjam AlayavijQAna sannivizwam / dOzWulyena atra izyate
# de-bas-na #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i chos-kyis #  sa-bon #  gnas-pa #  ni 'dir gnas-ngan-len #  du 'dod do /
ayam suKa duHKA asuKA duHKa sahitaH kAyaH tat Palam
# bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  yang ma yin bde-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa #  dang lhan-cig #  pa'i lus 'di ni de'i 'bras-bu # 'o /
tasmAt suKa Adi avakASa sahitena kAyena pratikzaNa BAvinA tat dOzWulyam / praBAvyate pratIyate iti arTaH / tat yaTA Kala vila antargatam bIjam aFkureNa iti
# de-bas-na #  bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  dang lhan-cig #  pa skad-cig-re-re-la #  'byung-ba'i-lus #  kyi gnas-ngan-len #  de rab tu ston te / / shes-pa # r byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / dper-na #  myu-gu # s g-yul gyi ser-ga # 'i nang-du-song-ba # 'i sa-bon #  mngon-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
tasmAt kAya parIkzayA duHKa satyam avatarati / atra kAraNam Aha p
# de'i-phyir #  lus la yongs su brtags-pa # s sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  la 'jug go / / 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  /
tasya sa dOzWulya saMskAra lakzaNa tvAt iti sa bIja saMskAra Atmaka tvAt / iti arTaH
# de'i mtshan-nyid #  ni gnas-ngan-len #  dang bcas-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  yin pa'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ste / / sa-bon #  dang bcas-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  kyi bdag-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
saMskAra duHKa tA hi vipariNAma duHKa tA duHKa duHKa tA dOzWulyAByAm / anugata tvAt kAraNa tvAt ca dOzWulyam iti aktA
# 'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid ni 'gyur-ba #  dang sdug-bsngal-gyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid ngag gnas-ngan-len #  gnyis kyi rjes-su-song-ba #  dang de'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir 'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  du bshad do /
atas eva saMskAra duHKa tayA sarva sAhasram vastu AryEH duHKa tvena Alokita
# de-bas-na #  'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid kyis zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i dngos-po-thams-cad #  'phags-pa #  rnams kyis sdug-bsngal #  nyid-du #  gzigs so /
evam kAya smRti upasTAnena duHKa satyam avatarati iti
# de-ltar-na #  lus dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa # s sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  la 'jug go /
tRzNA hetuH vedanA avidyA saMsparSa ja iti aBiprAyAt anAsravAyA atad / hetu tvAt
# sred-pa # 'i rgyu ni tshor-ba #  ste / / zhes-bya-ba #  ni ma-rig-pa # 'i 'dus-te-reg-pa #  las byung-ba # r dgos-pa #  ste / / zag-pa-med-pa #  ni de'i rgyu-ma #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
tatra suKA vedanA tat saMyoga aviyoga tRzNAyAH hetuH / duHKA tat asaMyoga viyoga tRzNAyAH hetuH
# de-la #  bde-ba'i-tshor-ba #  ni de dang ldan zhing mi-'bral-ba # r sred-pa # 'i rgyu'o / / sdug-bsngal #  ni de dang mi phrad-pa #  dang bral-ba # r sred-pa # 'i rgyu'o /
aduHKa suKA tat avasTABiH ati tRzNAyAH tat saMyoga aviyoga tRzNAyAH ca / kasyAMcid samAptO hetuH iti
# sdug-bsngal #  yang ma yin bde-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa #  ni snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  'ga' zhig la de'i-gnas #  skabs la mngon-par-dga'-ba # 'i sred-pa # 'i rgyu dang de dang phrad cing mi 'bral-pa # r sred-pa # 'i rgyu yin no /
sa duHKa vedanayA spRzwaH kAma suKam aBinandati iti vacanAt duHKA api / vedanA suKAyAH tRzNayA hetuH Bavati
# de sdug-bsngal-gyi-tshor-ba # s reg na 'dod-pa'i-bde-ba #  la mngon-pa # r dga'o zhes 'byung-ba # 'i phyir / / sdug-bsngal-ba # 'i tshor-ba #  yang bde-ba #  la sred-pa # 'i rgyur 'gyur te /
tat parIkzayA samudayasatyam avatarati
# de-la #  yongs su brtags-pa # s kun-'byung-ba # 'i bden-pa #  la 'jug go /
sa hi vedanAm svarUpataH kAraNataH kAryataH anityataH / duHKataH ca upaparIkzamANaH samudaya satyam avatarati tRzNAm tat / kAryatvena avagacCati iti arTaH
# de-la #  tshor-ba #  rnams la rang-bzhin #  dang 'bras-bu #  dang mi-rtag-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  nyid-du #  nye-bar #  yongs su rtog na kun-'byung-ba # 'i bden-pa #  la 'jug ste / / sred-pa #  ni de'i 'bras-bu # r khong du chud do zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
tRzNA hi sUtre samudayasatyam iti uktA
# mdo-sde #  las sred-pa #  ni kun-'byung-ba # 'i bden-pa # r gsungs te /
kaH duHKa samudayaH
# sdug-bsngal #  kun-'byung-ba #  gang zhe na /
paWyate tRzNA pOnarBavikA AnandA rAga saha gatA iti vistaraH
# yang-'byung-ba # 'i sred-pa #  dga'-ba # 'i 'dod-chags #  dang ldan-pa # 'o zhes rgya-cher #  'byung ngo /
evam vedanA mRtyu upasTAnena samudaya satyam avatarati
# de-ltar #  tshor-ba #  dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa # s kun-'byung-ba # 'i bden-pa #  la 'jug go /
Atma aBiniveSavaH tu cittam iti
# bdag tu mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i gzhi ni sems te zhes-bya-ba #  la /
anyasya nitya Adi guNa viSizwasya AtmanaH aBAvAt Atma aBiniveSa Alambanam / cittam eva
# rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i yon-tan #  khyad-par-can #  gyi bdag gzhan med-pa # s na bdag tu mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni sems nyid do /
tasmAt tat parIkzayA niroDasatyam avatarati SAnta tvena
# de-bas-na #  de yongs su brtags-pa # s 'gog-pa # 'i bden-pa #  la zhi-ba #  nyid-du #  'jug ste /
atra eva kAraNam Aha Atma ucCeda Baya apagamAt iti
# 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  / / bdag chad bar dogs-pa'i-'jigs-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ste /
citte hi anitya tva Adi parIkzayA Atma aBiniveSaH vyAvartate duHKa saMjQA / pravartate
# sems la mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r yongs su brtags-pa # s bdag tu mngon-par-zhen-pa #  ldog cing sdug-bsngal #  du 'du-shes #  'byung ngo /
atas ca Atma ucCeda Baya apagamAt duHKa mAtrasya ucCedAt niroDa satyam / SAntatvena avatarati iti / evam citta smRti upasTAnena niroDa satyam avatarati iti / Darma parIkzayA sa aFkleSika vyavadAnika Darma asaMmohAn mArga satyam / avatarati iti / tatra sa aFkleSikAH DarmAH kleSa upakleSAH / vyAvadAnikAH tu kleSa upakleSa pratipakza BUtAH prema mEtrI AdayaH
# de'i-phyir #  bdag chad-pa # 'i 'jigs-pa-med-pa # s sdug-bsngal-ba #  tsam zhig gcod-pa # 'i phyir 'gog-pa # 'i bden-pa #  la zhi-ba #  nyid-du #  'jug ste / / de-ltar #  sems dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa # s 'gog-pa # 'i bden-pa #  la 'jug ces bya'o / / chos la yongs su brtags-pa # s kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i chos la rmongs-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir lam gyi bden-pa #  la 'jug go zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams so / / rnam-par-byang-ba #  rnams ni nye-ba # 'i gnyen-por-gyur-pa #  rnams te / / mi-sdug-pa #  dang byams-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
tezAm sa aFkleSikAnAm vyAvadAnikA nAQca vipakza pratipakza BAvam / budDvA sarva upadrava atyanta prahANa upAye mArga satye aBimuKIBavati / evam Darma mRtyu pasTAnena mArga satyam avatarati iti / avatAraH atra pratyekam satye satya lakzaNa avaboDaH / tatra kAya smRti upasTAna BAvanA anityataH duHKataH SUnyataH anAtmataH api
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  de rnams la gnyen-po #  dang mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi ngo bor shes-nas #  gnod-pa #  thams-cad #  gtan-du #  spang-ba # 'i thabs lam gyi bden-pa #  la mngon-du-phyogs-pa # r 'gyur te / / de-ltar #  chos dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa # s lam gyi bden-pa #  la 'jug go / / 'jug-pa #  ni 'dir bden-pa #  so-so #  la bden-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  du rtogs-pa # 'o /
anekA aSuci dravya svaBAvataH api aSuci bIjataH api aSuci nizyandataH api / aSuci sTiti hetutaH api aSuci vikArataH api Pena BaFgaH iva asArataH api gatitaH api / yonitaH api
# de-la #  lus dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  bsgom-pa #  ni mi-rtag-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  dang stong-pa #  dang bdag-med-pa #  dang mi gtsang ba du-ma # 'i rdzas kyi rang-bzhin #  dang mi gtsang ba'i sa-bon #  dang mi gtsang ba'i rgyu-mthun-pa #  dang mi gtsang ba gnas-pa # 'i rgyu dang mi gtsang bar 'gyur-ba #  dang dbu-ba #  rdos pa bzhin-du #  snying-po-med-pa #  dang 'gro-ba #  dang skye-gnas #  yin par bsgom mo /
vedanA citta Darma smRti upasTAna BAvanA punar / anitya duHKa SUnyAn AtmataH api sva lakzaNataH api hetutaH api PalataH api / DAtu BUmi gatitaH api kuSala akuSala avyAkRtataH api vipakza pratipakzataH api / boDisattvAnAm punar smRti upasTAna BAvanAH eva QcAnu palamBa AkAreNa / ca vikalpa prahANa arTam / smRti upasTAnAnAm tu prajQAsvABAvye api smRti upasTAna vacanam / smRti balena upasTAnAt etAsAm prajQAnAm smRti upasTAnam ucyate p
# tshor-ba #  dang sems dang chos dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  rnams bsgom-pa #  yang mi-rtag-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  dang stong-pa #  dang bdag-med-pa #  dang spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  dang rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  dang rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  dang khams dang sa dang 'gro-ba #  dang dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  dang mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang gnyen-po #  yin par bsgom mo / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  bsgom-pa #  ni 'di-lta-bu #  yang yin la rnam-par-rtog-pa #  spangs-pa # 'i phyir mi dmigs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r yang bsgom mo / / dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  rnams shes-rab #  kyi rang-bzhin #  yin-du-zin #  kyang dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa # 'i tshig ni dran-pa'i-stobs #  kyis nye-bar-gnas-pa # 'i phyir ram / / 'di dag gis dran-pa #  nye-bar-gnas-pa # s dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
catvAri samyak prahANAni / smRti upasTAna BAvanA anantaram samyak prahANa BAvanA uktA / kim kAraNam atas Aha / yasmAt / parijQAte vipakze ca / iti vistaraH / smRti upasTAna BAvanayA iti
# dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  bsgom-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  yang-dag-par-spong-ba #  bsgom-pa #  bshad de / / de-ci'i-phyir-zhe-na #  / / de'i-phyir #  'di-ltar #  / / mi mthun phyogs dang gnyen-po #  rnams / / rnam-pa-thams-cad #  yongs shes-nas #  / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
aviSeza aBiDAne api Darma mRtyupa sTAna BAvanA eva iti veditavyam / DAtu BUmi avakASEH sAmAnya lakzaNa Adi AkArEH taTA
# dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  bsgoms-nas #  zhes khyad-par-med-pa # r brjod kyang chos dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  bsgom-pa #  nyid yin par rig-par-bya # 'o /
sa Asrava anAsrava naDAtu BUmi SEkzA SEkzA Adi AkArEH taTA / sa Asrava anAsrava DAtu BUmi SEkzA SEkza Adi Bedena ca vipakze pratipakze / ca sarva prakAra parijQAte / vipakzA AgamAya iti / vipakza apagamamaH atra utpannAnAm prabanDa= CedaH anutpannAnAm ca anutpAdaH / pratipakza upagamAya ca iti
# khams dang sa'i spangs-pa #  dang spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  dang de-bzhin-du #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa #  dang khams dang sa dang slob-pa #  dang mi-slob-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang gnyen-po #  rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  yongs su shes na mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  gsal-ba #  ni 'dir skyes-pa #  rnams kyi rgyun-chad-pa #  dang ma-skyes-pa #  rnams mi-skyed-pa # 'o / / gnyen-po #  bskyed-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  la /
pratipakza AgamaH utpannAnAm prabanDa anuvRttiH anutpannA anAQca utpAdaH / vIryam caturDA pravartate iti vipakza pratipakzayoH utpanAn utpanna Bedena / caturDA vIryasya pravRttiH / utpannAnAm pApakAnAm akuSalAnAm DarmANAm prahANAya iti vistara / iti idam Agamena vIryasya eva caturDA pravRttim darSayati
# gnyen-po #  bskyed-pa #  ni skyes-pa #  rnams kyi rgyun gyis rjes-su-'jug-pa #  dang ma-skyes-pa #  rnams skyed-pa # 'o / / brtson 'grus rnam-pa-bzhi #  rab tu 'byung zhes byang ni mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang gnyen-po #  gnyis skyes-pa #  dang ma-skyes-pa #  tha-dad-pa # s brtson 'grus rnam-pa-bzhi #  'byung ste / / sdig-pa #  mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  skyes-pa #  rnams spang-ba # 'i phyir zhe rgya-cher #  'byung ngo zhes-bya-ba #  'dis ni lung gis brtson 'grus nyid rnam-pa-bzhi #  'byung-ba # r ston to /
vistara vacanena Seza granTa aBisambanDaH / tatra AyAm SezaH granGaH prahANAya Candam janayati vyAyacCate vIryam
# rgya-cher #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni tshig lhag-ma #  dang sbyar-ba # 'o / / de-la #  'di ni tshig lhag-ma #  ste sdig-pa #  mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  skyes-pa #  rnams spangs-pa # 'i phyir 'dun-pa #  skyed do / / 'bad do /
AraBate cittam pragRhNAti samyak pradaDAti iti / evam anutpannAnAm pApakAnAm akuSalAnAm DarmANAm anutpAdAya / CandaQjanayati iti vistaraH
# brtson 'grus rtsom mo / / sems rab tu 'dzin to / / yang-dag-par #  rab tu 'jog go zhes-bya-ba #  dang de-bzhin-du #  sdig-pa #  mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  ma-skyes-pa #  rnams mi bskyed-pa # 'i phyir 'dun-pa #  bskyed do zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba # 'o /
evam anutpannAnAm kuSalAnAm DarmANAm utpAdaya CandaQjanayati iti / vistaraH
# de-bzhin-du #  dge-ba'i-chos #  ma-skyes-pa #  rnams bskyed-pa # 'i phyir 'dun-pa #  bskyed do zhes rgya-cher #  bya'o /
utpannAnAm kuSalAnAm DarmANAm sTitaye BUyas BAvatAyE / asampramozAya paripUraNAya CandaQjanayati vyAyacCate vIryam
