# dge-ba'i-chos #  skyes-pa #  rnams gnas-pa #  dang phyir-zhing-'byung-ba #  dang yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir 'dun-pa #  bskyed do / / 'bad do / / brtson 'grus brtsam mo /
AraBate cittam pragRhNAti / samyak pradaDAti / utpannAnAm sTitiH aparihANiH / BUyas BAvaH prabanDena utpAdaH / paripUriH prakarza gamanam
# sems rab tu 'dzin to / / yang-dag-par #  rab tu 'jog go zhes-bya-ba # 'o / / skyes-pa #  rnams gnas-pa #  ni yongs-su-mi-nyams-pa # 'o / / phyir-zhing-'byung-ba #  ni rgyun-du-skye-ba # 'o / / yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r bya-ba #  ni phul du phyin par 'gyur-ba # 'o /
CandaQjanayati iti sa gOrava udyakta vIrya samRdDim darSayati
# 'dun-pa #  skyed ces bya-ba #  ni gus-par #  brtson 'grus bsgom-pa # 'i sbyor-ba #  ston to /
vyAyacCataH iti kOsIdya prahANAya kAya citte aBimuKIkaroti iti arTaH
# 'bad ces bya-ba #  ni le-lo #  spangs-te #  / / lus dang sems mngon du byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
vIryam AraBate iti laya OdDatya apakarzaNa arTam
# brtson 'grus rtsom zhes-bya-ba #  ni bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  bsal-ba # 'i phyir ro /
kaTam AraBeta
# ji-ltar #  rtsom zhe na /
lInam cittam pragRhNAti samvejanIya pramodAnIya Darma manaskArEH / udDatam cittam tasmin= eva Alambane samyak pradaDAti / samvejanIya pramodanIya Darma manaskArEH DArayati iti arTaH / eva paQca p / samyak praDAnAni vIrya AtmakAni iti jQApitam Bavati / samyak eBiH kAya vAc manAMsi DArayanti iti samyak praDAnAni / catvAraH RdDi pAdAH / karmaQa tA sTiteH tatra
# yang-dag-pa #  shes-par-bya-ba #  dang dga'-bar-bya-ba # 'i chos yid-la-byed-pa # s bying-ba # 'i sems rab tu 'dzin to / / sems-rgod-pa # r gyur na dmigs-pa #  de-nyid-la #  yang-dag-par #  rab tu 'jog ste / / 'dzin zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / de-ltar #  yang-dag-par-spong-ba #  rnams ni brtson 'grus kyi rang-bzhin #  du bstan-pa #  yin te / / 'di rnams kyis lus dang ngag dang yid yang-dag-par-'dzin-pa # s na yang-dag-par-'dzin-pa #  rnams so /
iti vistaraH / tatra iti tasyAm vipakza pratipakzAya apagama vIrya BAvanAyAm
# der gnas las-su-rung-ba #  nyid / / ces rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  la der zhes-bya-ba #  ni mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  bsal-ba # 'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom pa de-la # 'o /
karmaNya tA citta sTiteH sarva arTa samRdDi yogya tA
# sems-gnas-pa # 'i las-su-rung-ba #  nyid ni don-thams-cad #  'byor-pa # r nus-pa #  nyid de-la # s su rung-ba #  nyid do /
sA ca karmaNya tA Canda vIrya cittamImAMsA ADipatya praBavA iti atas Aha
# las-su-rung-ba #  de-yang #  'dun-pa #  dang brtson 'grus dang sems-pa #  dang dpyod-pa # 'i dbang gis byung-ba # s na de'i-phyir #  /
karmaNya tA catvAraH RdDi pAdAH iti / sarvasya aBijQA Adikasya arTasya samRdDi RdDiH / tasyAH pratizWA arTena RdDi pAdAH RdDi hetavaH iti arTaH / atas eva Aha sarva arTa samRdDi hetutvAt iti / te punar candana samADiH prahANa saMskAra sama anvAgataH RdDi pAdaH / vIrya samADiH prahANa saMskAra sama anvAgataH RdDi pAdA citta samADiH / prahANa saMskAra sama nava AgataH RdDi pAdaH mImAMsA samADiH
# las-su-rung-ba #  nyid ni rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  bzhi-po #  dag ste zhes-bya-ba #  smos so; / / mngon-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  don-thams-cad-'grub-pa # r byed-pa #  ni rdzu-'phrul #  lo / / de'i-gnas #  yin pa'i phyir rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  zhes bya ste / / rgyu zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / de-bas-na #  don-thams-cad #  'byor-pa # 'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro zhes smos te / / de-dag #  kyang 'dun-pa'i-ting-nge-'dzin #  spong-ba'i-'du-byed #  dang ldan-pa # 'i rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  dang brtson 'grus kyi ting-nge-'dzin #  spong-ba'i-'du-byed #  dang ldan-pa # 'i rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  dang sems-kyi-ting-nge-'dzin #  spong-ba'i-'du-byed #  dang ldan-pa # 'i rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  dang dpyod-pa'i-ting-nge-'dzin #  spong-ba'i-'du-byed #  dang ldan-pa # 'i rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
prahANa saMskAra samanvAgataH RdDi pAdaH iti / tatra cCandsamADiH yadA Canda ADipatyAt vIrya BAvanAyAm sa gOravam
# de-la #  'dun-pa'i-ting-nge-'dzin #  ni gang-gi-tshe #  'dun-pa # 'i dbang gis brtson 'grus rtsom pa la gus-par #  'jug-pa #  na sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg-pa # 'o /
pravartamAnaH spRSati citta syaka agra tAm / vIrya samADiH yadA vIryam AraBamANaH sAtatya prayogAt spRSati / cittasya ekAgra tAm / citta samADiH yadA pUrva samADi bIjam Agamya cittaH eva cittam DArayan / spRSati cittasya ekAgra tAm / mImAmsA asamADiH yad Alambana pravicitaH anuspRSati cittasya ekAgra tAm iti / sTitiH atra citta sTitiH samADiH veditavyaH iti samADi grahaNam
# brtson 'grus kyi ting-nge-'dzin #  ni gang-gi-tshe #  brtson 'grus rtsom pa na rtag-par #  sbyor-ba # s sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg-pa # 'o / / sems-kyi-ting-nge-'dzin #  ni gang-gi-tshe #  sngon gyi ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi sa-bon #  la brten-nas #  sems 'dzin cing gang sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg-pa # 'o / / dpyod-pa'i-ting-nge-'dzin #  ni gang-gi-tshe #  dmigs-pa #  rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa #  na sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg-pa # 'o / / gnas-pa #  ni 'dir sems-gnas-pa #  ste / / ting-nge-'dzin #  du rig-par-bya # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
saMskRta lakzaNAt vyavacCeda arTam
# ting-nge-'dzin #  smos-pa #  ni 'dus-byas-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  las dbye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
yatas ArabDa vIryasya citta karmaNya tA catvAraH RdDi pAdAH Bavanti atas / samyak prahANa anantaram RdDi pAdAH nirdizwAH / sA punar karmaNya tA p / kim prayojanA kim hetukA ca iti atas Aha / paQca doza prahANAya azwa prahANa saMskAra BAvanA anvayA videtavyA iti / anvayaH hetuH / paQca dozAH
# 'di-ltar #  brtson 'grus brtsams pa ni sems-las-su-rung-ba #  nyid rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  bzhir gyur-pa #  de'i-phyir #  yang-dag-par-spong-ba # 'i 'og-tu #  rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  rnams bstan to / / las su rang ba de-yang #  dgos-pa #  ni gang / / rgyu ni gang zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / nyes-pa #  lnga spang-ba # 'i phyir 'du-byed #  bsgom-pa # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
te ca paQca dozAH na vijQAyante iti atas pRcCati katame paQca dozAH iti / tat pradarSayan= Aha / kOsIdyam avavAdasya sammozaH layaH udBavaH / iti vistaraH
# nyes-pa #  lnga po de-dag #  mi shes-nas #  / / de'i-phyir #  / / nyes-pa #  lnga po de-dag #  gang zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang de-dag #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / le-lo #  dag ni gdams-ngag #  rnams / / brjed dang bying dang rgod-pa #  dang / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so / / de-dag #  ni nyes-pa #  drug tu 'gyur ro snyam pa la / / de'i-phyir #  /
ete hi zaXdozAH iti atas Aha tatra laya OdDatyam ekaH dozaH kriyate iti / paQca Bavanti
# de-la #  bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  ni nyes-pa #  gcig-tu #  bsdu'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / de'i-phyir #  lngar 'gyur ro /
tatra kOsIdyam prayoga kAle dozaH tena aprayogAt

udyuktasya avavAda sammozaH dozaH tena citta samADAna BAvAt
# brtson pa'i tshe gdams-ngag #  brjed-pa #  ni nyes-pa #  ste / / des sems-mnyam-par-gzhag-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
samAhitasya laya OdDatyam dozaH tena citta karmaNya tA
# mnyam-par-gzhag-pa #  la bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  ni nyes-pa #  ste / / des sems-las-su-rung-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anaBisaMskAraH laya OdDatya praSamana kAle dozaH
# bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa # r gyur-pa # 'i tshe mngon-pa # r 'du mi-byed-pa #  nyes-pa # 'o /
anaBisaMskAraH upekzA tayA tat dvaya ASamanAt / aBisaMskAraH praSAntO dozaH iti / aBisaMskAraH cetanA
# mngon-pa # r 'du mi-byed-pa #  ni btang-snyoms #  te / / des de gnyis rab-tu-zhi-ba # r mi-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rab-tu-zhi-ba # 'i tshe ni mngon-par-'du-byed-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # r snyegs so / / mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  ni sems-pa # 'o /
laya OdDatya vigamAt hi samatA prApta tvAt praSAntam iti ucyate / azwO prahANa saMskArAH p / prahANa saMskArAH prahANAya saMskArAH / kasya prahANAya
# bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  dang bral-ba # s mnyam-pa-nyid #  du gyur-pa # 'i phyir rab-tu-zhi-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  / / spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i phyir 'du-byed-rnams #  ni spong-ba'i-'du-byed #  rnams so / / gang spang-ba # 'i phyir zhe na /
anantara uktAnAm paQcAnAm dozANAm prahANAya
# bshad ma-thag #  pa'i nyes-pa #  lnga rnams spang-ba # 'i phyir ro /
yadi evam tena vaktavyam ezAm prahANAya kaTam azwO prahANa saMskArA
# gal-te #  de lta na des de-dag #  spong-ba'i-'du-byed #  brgyad ji-ltar #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  brjod dgos so /
vyavasTApyante iti / tatra kOsIdya prahANAya catvAraH Canda vyAyAma SradDA prasrabDayaH

# de-la #  'dun-pa #  ni 'dod-pa # 'o / / rtsol ba ni brtson 'grus so / / dad-pa #  ni mgon par yid-ches-pa # 'o / / shin-tu-sbyangs-pa #  ni las-su-rung-ba #  nyid do /
kaTam punar ete kOsIdya prahANAya vyavasTApyante iti atas Aha te
# ji-ltar #  na le-lo #  spang-ba # 'i phyir de-dag #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ce na / / de'i-phyir #  /

# de-dag #  kyang go-rims-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya #  ste / / gnas dang de-la #  gnas-pa #  dang / / rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  nyid-du # 'o /
atas anyonya praBAvita tvAt ete kOsIdya prahANAya samvartante iti / darSayati ASrayaH CandaH vyAyAmasya ASritaH vyAyAmaH
# zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / de-dag #  gcig las gcig 'byung-ba # s na le-lo #  spong-bar-'gyur-ba #  ston to / / rtsol ba'i gnas ni 'dun-pa # 'o / / gnas-pa #  ni rtsol ba ste /
aBilAzasya vyAyAma pUrvakatvAt / tasya ASrayasya Candasya nimittam SradDA
# 'dod-pa #  ni rtsol ba'i sngon-du-'gro-ba # 'i phyir ro / / gnas 'dun-pa # 'i rgyu ni dad-pa #  ste /
kaTam iti atas bravIti sampratyaye sati aBilAzAt iti
# ji lta zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  / / yid-ches-pa # r gyur na 'dod-pa'i-phyir #  ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
SraddaDAnasya hi hetu Pale kriyA aBilAzaH Bavati
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  la dad-pa-dang-ldan-pa #  ni bya-ba #  la 'dod-pa # r 'gyur ro /
tasya ASritasya vyAyAmasya Palam prasrabDiH
# gnas-pa #  rtsol ba de'i 'bras-bu #  ni shin-tu-sbyangs-pa #  ste /
kaTam iti atas Aha prArabDa vIryasya samADi viSezAH aDigamAt iti
# ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / brtson 'grus brtsams na ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi khyad-par-thob-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
samADi viSeza gamanam hi prasrabDi nimittam
# ting-nge-'dzin #  khyad-par-du-'gro-ba #  ni shin-tu-sbyangs-pa # 'i rgyu'o / / de'i-phyir #  /
atas ArabDa vIryasya samADi viSeza gamanAt prasrabDiH vyAyAma Palam
# brtson 'grus brtsams pa'i ting-nge-'dzin #  khyad-par-du-'gro-ba # s shin-tu-sbyangs-pa #  ni rtsol ba'i 'bras-bu # r bshad do /
iti uktam / taTA hi ArabDa vIryasya dOzWulya vitarka Adi apakAla vigamAt pramoda
# de-ltar #  brtson 'grus brtsams pa gnas-ngan-len #  gyi rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i nyes-pa #  dang bral-ba # s dga'-ba #  skye'o /
utpadyate / manaH pramodAt kAya cittayoH prasrabDiH karmaNi atAlakzaNa tA
# yid-dga'-ba # s lus dang sems gnyis shin-tu #  sbyangs te las-su-rung-ba #  nyid kyi mtshan-nyid #  do /
tatas samADi viSeza gamanam iti
# de-bas-na #  ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi khyad-par-thob-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
atra ca vIryam sa hetukam saPalam ca kOsIdya pratipakzeNa uktam
# 'dir ni brtson 'grus rgyu dang bcas shing 'bras-bu-dang-bcas-pa #  le-lo # 'i gnyen-po # r bshad do /
caturNAm dozANAm yaTAsaMKyam pratipakzaH iti / tatra smRtiH avavAda sammozasya pratipakzaH / samprayojanyam laya OdDatyasya / cetanA anaBisaMskArasya
# nyes-pa #  bzhi'i gnyen-po # r grangs bzhin no zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  / / dran-pa #  ni gdams-ngag #  brjed-pa # 'i gnyen-po # 'o / / shes-bzhin #  ni bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa # 'i gnyen-po # 'o / / sems-pa #  ni mngon-pa # r 'du mi-byed-pa # 'i gnyen-po # 'o /
aBisaMskArasya upekzA iti saMskAra upekzA atra veditavyA
# btang-snyoms #  ni mngon-par-'du-byed-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  ste / / 'dir 'du-byed #  kyi btang-snyoms #  su shes-pa # r bya'o /
smRti AdInAm punar lakzaNa vivakzayA idam Aha te punar smRti AdayaH / veditavyA yaTAkramam iti
# dran-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  brjod-pa # r 'dod-pa'i-phyir #  / / de-dag #  kyang ngan-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rig-par-bya #  ste go-rims #  bzhin zhes-bya-ba #  'di smos so /
smRtiH Alambane asammozaH iti p
# dran-pa #  ni dmigs-pa #  ma brjed-pa # 'o zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  la /
vistarIkRtam Alambanam iti citta sTApanIyam avavAda vastu aBilapanam / iti ArtaH
# dran-pa #  ni dmigs-pa #  ma brjed-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni sems-gnas-par-bya-ba # 'i gdams-ngag #  yid kyis brjod ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
samprajanyam smRti asampramoze sati laya OdDatya avaboDaH iti / upasTita smRtiH hi samprajanyavAn Bavati eva iti atas Aha smRtya sampramoze / sati iti / anubudDyA laya OdDatyam SamaTa vipaSyane yuga nadDAt aprayatena
# shes-bzhin #  ni dran-pa #  ma brjed-pa # r gyur na bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  rtogs-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni dran-pa #  nye-bar-gnas-pa #  shes-bzhin #  dang ldan-pa # r 'gyur ro / / de'i-phyir #  dran-pa #  ma brjed-pa # r gyur na zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  rtogs-nas #  zhi-gnas-dang-lhag-mthong #  gnyis zung du 'brel-pa # r 'jug-pa # 'i phyir bsgrim mi-dgos-pa # r 'jug go zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
pravarteta iti arTaH / upekzA iti vizaya antara anaBisaMskAraH iti arTaH
# btang-snyoms #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni yul gzhan la mngon-pa # r 'du mi byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  ste /
etat uktam Bavati sUpa sTita smRtiH avavAde lInam cittam udDtam vA / yaTABUtam prajAnAti / laya OdDatya vigamAya ca tat aBisaMskaroti laya OdDatya vigamAt ca upekzAm / karoti iti / evam tasya citta praSaWatA karmaNya tA / atra ca karmaNi atAsTitiH iti sva arTe BAva pratyayaH sva pewa tva Adi vat
# de ni 'di-skad-du #  gdams-ngag #  la dran-pa #  shin-tu #  nye-bar-gnas-pa #  ni bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa # 'i sems yang-dag-pa #  ji-ltar-ba #  bzhin-du #  shes shing / / bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  dang 'bral-ba # 'i phyir de mngon-pa # r 'du-byed #  la / / bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  dang 'bral na yang btang-snyoms #  su byed do zhes bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro / / de-ltar-na #  de'i sems rnal du 'jug-pa #  las-su-rung-ba #  nyid yin no /
paQca indriyANi / RdDi pAda anantaram paQca indriyANi SradDA AdIn yuktAni iti sambaDyate
# rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  dbang-po-lnga #  rnams te / / dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni bstan zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro /
tezAm kaTam vyavasTAnam iti kena arTena iti aBiprAyaH / atas Aha
# de-dag #  ji-ltar #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ce na zhes-bya-ba #  ni gang-gi-phyir #  zhes dgongs-pa # 'o / / de'i-phyir #  /
ropite mokza BAgIye Canda yoga ADipatyataH / iti vistaraH
# thar-pa # 'i cha dang mthun bskyed na / / 'dun dang sbyor-ba #  dbang byed do / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
ADipatyate iti vartate iti anena cCanda yoga ADipatyata / iti atra ADipatya SabdaH prayuktaH uttaratra api anuvartate iti darSayati
# dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # r snyegs so zhes-bya-ba #  'dis ni 'dun-pa-dang-sbyor-ba #  dbang byed ces bya-ba # 'i sgra 'dir smos-pa #  'og ma rnams la yang snyegs so zhes ston to /
RdDi pAdEH karmaNi acittasya Aropite mokza BAgIye kuSala mUle iti / karmaNi acittasya vimokza BAgIyam kuSala mUlam citta sanDAne pratizWAm
# rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  rnams kyis sems-las-su-rung-ba #  thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba bskyed nas zhes-bya-ba #  ni sems-las-su-rung-ba #  sems-kyi-rgyud #  la thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba rab tu 'jog-pa #  'thob ste /
pratilaBate Canda ADipatyataH yAvat pravicaya ADipatyataH na tu / akarmaNya cittasya
# 'dun-pa #  ni dbang-byed-pa #  nas rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa #  ni dbang-byed-pa # 'i bar-du #  'gyur gyi / / sems las-su-mi-rung-ba #  la ni ma yin no /
sA ca citta karmaNya tA RdDi pAdEH Bavati
# sems-las-su-rung-ba #  nyid de-yang #  rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  rnams kyis 'gyur ro /
tasmAt RdDi pAda anantaram vimokza BAgIya kuSala mUla ropaNa ADipatyataH / paQca SradDA AdIni indriyANi iti vyavasTApyante
# de-bas-na #  rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba bskyed-pa #  la dbang-byed-pa # s dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dbang-po-lnga #  rnams rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
Canda ADipatyate iti kAraNe kArya upacArAH SradDDA eva atra / Canda Sabdena uktA tat yaTA daDatrapuzam sadyojvaraH iti
# 'dun-pa #  ni dbang byed zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgyu la 'bras-bu #  btags-nas #  dad-pa #  nyid la 'dir 'dun-pa # 'i sgrar bshad de / / dper-na #  zho dang ga gon la 'phral du rims zhes-bya-ba #  lta-bu # 'o /
aTavA astitva guNa Saktizu yaTAkramam aBisampratyaya prasAda aBilAzAH / SradDAyAH lakzaNam
# yang-na #  yod-pa-nyid #  dang yon-tan-can #  dang nus-pa #  rnams la go-rims-bzhin-du #  mngon-par-yid-ches-pa #  dang dang-ba #  dang 'dod-pa #  rnams ni dad-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do /
atas candana grahaNena atra aBilAza lakzaNA SradDA eva gRhyate na tu cCandaH iti
# de-bas-na #  'dun-pa #  smos-pa # s 'dir 'dod-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dad-pa #  smos-pa # r 'gyur gyi 'dun-pa #  ni ma yin no /
prayoga ADipatyate iti prayujyate anena iti prayogaH
# sbyor-ba #  ni dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dis sbyor-bar-byed-pa # s na sbyor-ba #  ste /
prayoga Sabdena vIryam aBipretam
# sbyor-ba # 'i sgra ni brtson 'grus la bya-ba # r dgongs-pa # 'o /
Alambana asampramoza ADipatyate iti smRti indriya ADipatyataH
# dmigs-pa #  mi-brjed-pa #  ni dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni dran-pa # 'i dbang-po #  dbang-byed-pa #  ste /
Almbana aBilapana lakzaNam smRti indriyam
# dmigs-pa #  gsal-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni dran-pa # 'i dbang-po # 'o /
avisAra ADipatyataH iti samADi indriya ADipatyataH / avisAraH hi samADi indriyam citta ekAgra tA lakzaNa tvAt
# mi-'phro-ba #  ni dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni ting-nge-'dzin-gyi-dbang #  po dbang-byed-pa #  ste / / sems rtse gcig pa'i mtshan-nyid #  yin-pas #  mi-'phro-ba #  ni ting-nge-'dzin-gyi-dbang #  po'o /
pravicaya ADipatyataH ca iti prajQA indriya ADipatyataH
# rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa #  ni dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni shes-rab #  kyi dbang-po #  dbang-byed-pa #  ste /
prajQA indriyasya Darma pravicaya Atmaka tvAt
# shes-rab #  kyi dbang-po #  chos-rnam-par-'byed-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
ca SabdaH vimokza BAgIya kuSala mUla ropaNa aDipattyAt p / yaTAkramam paQca SradDA AdIni indriyANi veditavyAni iti darSayati
# kyang zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba bskyed-pa #  la dbang-byed-pa # s dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dbang-po #  dag dang go-rims-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o zhes-bya-ba # r ston to /
SradDaDAnaH hi saMsAra cArakAn niHsaraNa arTam vIryam AraBate
# dad-pa # r gyur-pa #  ni 'khor-ba # 'i btson ra nas 'byung-bar-'gyur-ba # s de'i-phyir #  brtson 'grus rtsom mo /
ArabDa vIryasya triSikzA nizpattiH smRti samADi prajQa indriyANi / yaTAkramam
# brtson 'grus brtsams pa bslab-pa-gsum #  sgrub ste / / dran-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang shes-rab #  kyi dbang-po #  rnams go-rims #  bzhin no /
evam darSana mArga prayoga BUmO= indriyANAm prADAnyam izyate
# de-ltar #  mthong-ba'i-lam #  la sbyor-ba # 'i sa la dbang-po #  di rnams gtso bor 'dod do /
anye tu AhuH na mokza BAgIya kuSala mUla ropaNa ADipatyataH / SradDA AdInAm indriya tvam
# gzhan dag na re thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba bskyed-pa #  la dbang-byed-pa #  la dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dbang-po #  zhes mi bya'o /
kim tarhi ropite mokza BAgIya kuSala mUle Canda AdInAm ADipatyata / etAni indriyANi ucyante
# thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba bskyed nas 'dun-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la dbang-byed-pa # s na 'di dag dbang-po #  zhes-bya'o #  /
etat eva pradarSayan= Aha Canda ADipatyataH SradDAyAH indriya tvam iti / sambaDyate / prayogaH vyApAraH / asammozaH Alambana vipraNASaH / avisaraNam avisAraH / pravicayanam pravicayaH
# de nyid bstan-pa # 'i phyir 'dun-pa #  ni dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / dad-pa'i-dbang-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  dang sbyar ro / / sbyor-ba #  ni byed-pa # 'o / / mi-brjed-pa #  ni dmigs-pa #  chud-mi-za-ba # 'o / / 'phro ba med-pa # s na mi-'phro-ba # 'o / / rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa # s na rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa # 'o /
tezAm prayoga sammoza avisAra pravicayAnAm ADipatyAt / vIrya smRti samADi prajQA AKyaH cEttAH indriya AKyam Bavanti iti
# sbyor-ba #  dang mi-brjed-pa #  dang mi-'phro-ba #  dang rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa #  de-dag #  la brtson 'grus dang dran-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang shes-rab #  ces bya-ba # 'i sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams dbang-ba # s na / / dbang-po #  rnams zhes-bya-ba # r gyur zhes zer ro /
atra tu etat vaktavyam ropite mokza BAgIye kuSala mUle ropita avasTAtaH / candana Adi ADipatyasya SradDA AdIn ca kaScid viSizwa svaBAvaH na asti / yasmAt tad avasTAyAm tat ADipatyAt tezAm indriya tvam avasTApyata / iti
# 'dir ni ji-skad-du #  bshad-par-bya #  ste / / thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba bskyed-pa #  dang ma-bskyed-pa #  gnyis kyi dus na 'dun-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dbang-byed-pa #  dang dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rang-bzhin #  du bye-brag #  tu gyur-pa #  gang yang med de / / 'di-ltar #  de'i dus na dbang-byed-pa # s de-dag #  dbang-po # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
paQca balAni / tAni eva SradDA AdIni balavanti balAni ucyante indriya anantaram uktAni iti / tezAm punar balavat tvam kutas iti atas Aha / vipakzasya hi saMliKAt iti
# dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  de-dag-nyid #  stobs-dang-ldan-pa # r gyur-pa #  la stobs rnams zhes bya ste / / dbang-po # 'i 'og-tu #  bshad-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-dag #  stobs ldan ji-lta-bu #  zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  / / mi mthun phyogs ni bsrabs-pa # 'i phyir /
vipakzasya saMliKita tvAt / etat eva pradarSayan= Aha yadA tAni iti SradDA AdIn driyANi
# zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs te / / mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  srab mor gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de nyid bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / gang-gi-tshe #  de-dag-nyid #  ces bya-ba #  smos te / / dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dbang-po #  rnams so /
ASradDya AdiBiH vipakzEH iti / ASradDya kOsIdya vismRti vikzepa asamprajanyEH SradDA Adi vipakzEH na / vyavakIryante atyarTam tanu tvAt antara antarA samudAcAra aBAvAt na / vyAmiSryante iti arTaH tadA balAni ucyante
# ma-dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  rnams zhes-bya-ba #  ni ma-dad-pa #  dang le-lo #  dang brjed-pa #  dang g-yeng ba dang shes-bzhin #  med-pa #  rnams so / / mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  rnams dang dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  mi-'dre-ba #  ni rab tu srab-pa # 'i phyir te / / skabs skabs su kun du 'byung-ba-med-pa # s na skabs mi thod ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / de'i tshe na stobs rnams zhes-bya'o #  /
tAni indriyANi vipakzEH avakIryante tadA tat vipakzasya anirliKita tvAt / p
# de'i tshe na ni de-dag #  gis mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  ma bsrabs-pa # s dbang-po #  de-dag #  mi-mthun-pa # 'i phyir rnams dang 'dre'o /
yadi anirjita vipakzANi indriyANi tat kaTam kOSalya tattve / lOkika viSudDi ADipatyena SradDA AdInAm indriya tvam uktam
# gal-te #  mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  rnams ma thul bar dbang-po #  rnams zhes bya na / / ji-ltar #  mkhas-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  nyid las 'jig-rten-pa # 'i rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i dbang gis dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dbang-po # r bshad ce na /
tatra hi aBedena indriyANi aBipretAni atra tu nirveDa BAgIyasya / kuSala mUlasya Beda pradarSana arTam
# der ni dbang-po #  rnams la bye-brag-med-par #  dgongs-pa # 'o / / 'dir ni nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba'i bye-brag #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir bye-brag #  yod de /
tasmAt na asti viroDaH
# de-bas-na #  'gal-ba #  med do /
atra eva atra Aha etAni eva indriyANi balAni ucyante iti
# de'i-phyir #  / / 'dir dbang-po #  de-dag-nyid #  stobs rnams zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
SraddaDAnaH hi hetu Pale vIryam AraBate
# dad-pa # r gyur-pa #  de rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  la brtson 'grus rtsom ste /
ayam hetuH asya eva Palasya idaQca Palam asya eva hetoH iti evam / SraddaDAnaH Pala SradDayA tad hetO vIryam AraBate
# 'bras-bu #  'di nyid kyi rgyu ni 'di'o / / rgyu 'di nyid kyi 'bras-bu #  ni 'di'o zhes de-ltar #  dad-pa # r gyur-pa #  ni 'bras-bu #  la dad-pa # s de'i rgyu la brtsan 'grus rtsom mo /
AraBda vIryasya tat para tvAt smRtiH upatizWate
# brtson 'grus brtsoms [*brtsams?] pa ni dran-pa #  nye-bar #  gnas so /
upasTita smRteH vipakzepa aBAvAt cittam samADIyate ekAgram Bavati
# dran-pa #  nye-bar-gnas-pa #  ni g-yeng ba med-pa # 'i phyir sems-mnyam-pa # r 'jog ste / / rtse gcig par 'gyur ro /
samAhita cittaH yaTABUtam prajAnAti iti samADi anugRhItA prajQA / sPuwA Bavati
# sems-mnyam-par-gzhag-pa #  ni yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  rab tu shes te / / ting-nge-'dzin #  gyis rjes su bzung-ba # 'i shes-rab #  ni gsal-ba # r 'gyur ro /
avaropita mokza BAgIyasya indriyANi uktAni / mokza BAgIya anantaram nirveDa BAgIyAni iti indriya anantaraQca
# thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  bskyed-zin-pa #  la dbang-po #  rnams bstan na thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  ni nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  rnams dang dbang-po #  rnams kyi 'og-tu #  ni stobs rnams bstan na de'i-phyir #  /
balA anyatas vaktavyam nirveDa BAgIyAni kim indriya avasTAyAm / veditavyAni Ahosvit bala avasTAyAm
# nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  rnams kyi dbang-po # 'i dus na rig-par-bya-ba # 'am / / 'on te stobs kyi dus la rig-par-bya #  /
taTA kim nirveDa BAgIyAni nidriyANi bala svaBAvAni Ahosvit tat / vyatirikta svaBAvAni iti atas Aha / dvO dvO nirveDa BAgIyAni indriyANi balAni ca iti
# de-bzhin-du #  nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  rnams kyi dbang-po #  dang stobs kyi rang-bzhin #  nam / / 'on te de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  yin pa brjod dgos te / / de'i-phyir #  / / dbang-po #  rnams dang stobs rnams la / / nges 'byed cha mthun gnyis gnyis so / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so /
aTavA yaTA moksa BAgIyAni pratipakza BAvanA praBAvitAni
# yang-na #  ji-ltar #  thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  rnams gnyen-po #  rnams bsgoms-nas #  rab-tu-phye-ba # 'am /
SradDA Adi praBAvitAni vA Bavanti taTA nirveDa BAgIyAni api
# dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba # r gyur-pa #  de-ltar #  nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  rnams kyang ngo /
atas Aha ropita mokza BAgIyasya indriyANi uktAni iti vistaraH / atas Aha / dvO dvO nirveDa BAgIyO / iti sarvam / uzma gatAni mUrDAH ca indriyANi iti / mRdu tvAt ayukta tvAt ezAm kuSalAnAm ezu balAnAm indriyANi eva / kzAntayaH lOkikAH ca agraDarmAH balAni iti
# de'i-phyir #  thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  bskyed zin nas dbang-po #  rnams bstan na zhes bya bya rgya-cher #  smos so / / de'i-phyir #  / / nges 'byed cha mthun gnyis gnyis so / / zhes-bya-ba #  thams-cad #  gsungs so / / dro-bar-gyur-pa #  rnams dang rtse mo dag gi tshe ni dbang-po #  rnams so / / dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba de-dag #  chung-ba # 'i phyir te / / de-dag #  rnams su mi-rigs-pa # s de-dag #  dbang-po-nyid #  do / / bzod da [*pa?] dag dang 'jig-rten-pa # 'i chos kyi mchog rnams kyi tshe ni stobs rnams so zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-dag #  che-ba # 'i phyir te /
aDimAtra tvAt ezAm indiryANAm asamBavAt kzAntayaH agra DarmAH ca / balAni eva / mRdu maDya ADi mAtra Bedena hi triviDAni SradDA AdIni / tatra mRdUni maDyAni ca indriyANi / aDimAtrANi balAni / yAni mRdUni tAni Ayuzma gatAni / maDyAni mUrDAnaH / aDimAtrANi punar caturDA kriyante
# bzod-pa #  dang 'jig-rten-pa # 'i chos kyi mchog de-dag #  ni dbang-po #  rnams su mi rigs kyi stobs rnams nyid do / / chung-ngu #  dang 'bring-po #  dang chen-po # 'i bye-brag #  gis dang-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni rnam-pa-gsum #  mo / / de-la #  chung-ngu #  dang 'bring-po #  dag ni dbang-po #  rnams so / / chen-po #  dag ni stobs rnams so / / chung-ngu #  gang-yin-pa #  dag ni dro-bar-gyur-pa #  rnams so / / 'bring-po #  dag ni rtse mo rnams so / / chen-po #  la yang bzhir dbye ste /
tatra mRdu maDya aDimAtrANi yaTAkramam mRdu maDya aDimAtrAH kzAntayaH / aDimAtra aDimAtrANi lOkikAH agraDarmAH iti
# de-la #  chung-ngu #  dang 'bring-po #  dang chen-po #  rnams ni bzod-pa-chung-ngu #  dang 'bring-po #  dang chen-po #  dag go-rims #  bzhin no / / chen-po # 'i yang chen-po #  dag ni 'jig-rten-pa # 'i chos kyi mchog rnams so /
etAni ca nirveDa BAgIyAni sarvANi p / samADi prajQAsu aBAvAni sa saMprayogANi
# nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  'di dag thams-cad #  ni ting-nge-'dzin #  dang shes-rab #  kyi rang-bzhin #  te / / mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  rnams so /
tatra Uzma prakAraH uzma gatam
# de-la #  dro-ba # 'i rnam-pa #  ni dro-bar-gyur-pa #  ste /
yaTA araNiniH maTanAt tat dahana samarTasya agneH utpati cihnam pUrvam
# dper-na #  gtsub shing gtsubs pa las shing tshig-pa # r nus-pa # 'i me'i mtshan-ma #  thog-mar #  byung-ba #  ni dro-ba # r 'byung-ba # 'o /
Uzma utpadyate evam sarva kleSa inDana dahana samarTasya Arya mArga agneH / pUrvarUpa tvAt tat uzma gatam iti ucyate / cala kuSala mUleByaH mUrDa upagamana tvAt mUrDA / kzAntiH satya arTe kzamAvat tvAt
# de-bzhin-du #  'phags-pa'i-lam #  gyi mes nyon-mongs-pa-thams-cad #  kyi shing sreg-pa # r nus-pa # 'i thog-ma # 'i rang-bzhin #  yin-pas #  dro-bar-gyur-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba g-yo-ba #  rnams las rtse mor phyin-pas #  na rtse mo'o / / bden-pa # 'i don la rab tu bzod-pa # s na bzod-pa # 'o / / zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  yang yin la /
tat anyasA asra vaDarma SrezWa tvAt ca lOkikAH agra DarmAH iti ucyante
# zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i chos gzhan-pa # s dam-pa #  yin-pas #  na 'jig-rten-pa # 'i chos kyi mchog rnams zhes-bya'o #  /
tezAm tu agratA tat anantaram darSana mArga utpatteH / te ca kzaNikAH SezANi nirveDa BAgIyAni santAnavanti
# de ma-thag-tu #  mthong-ba'i-lam #  skye-ba # s na de-dag #  mchog ces bya ste / / de-dag #  ni skad-cig-pa # 'o / / nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  lhag-ma #  rnams ni rgyun can no /
tatra mokza BAgIyam kuSala mUlam saMsAra praBAvana Sakti GAta yogena / veditavyam
# de-la #  thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba ni 'khor-ba # r rab-tu-skye-ba # 'i mthu 'joms pa'i tshul du rig-par-bya # 'o /
nirveDa BAgIyam anAsrava Darma utpatti Sakti ADAna yogena iti / sapta boDi aFgAni
# nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i zag-pa-med-pa # 'i chos 'byung-ba # 'i mthu skyed-pa # 'i tshul du rig-par-bya #  ste /
agra Darma anantaram darSana mArga utpatteH tasya boDyaFga praBAvita tvAt / Aha balAnantaram boDyaFgAni iti
# chos kyi mchog gi 'og-tu #  mthong-ba'i-lam #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de-yang #  byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  gis rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir stobs kyi 'og-tu #  byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  rnams bshad do /
tezAm kaTam vyavasTAnam iti / kim arTam vyavasTAnam iti aBiprAyaH
# de-dag #  ji-ltar #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ce na zhes-bya-ba #  ni ci'i-phyir #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ces bya-ba # r dgongs-pa # 'o /
atas Aha / ASraya aFgam svaBAva aFgam / iti vistaraH
# de'i-phyir #  / / rang-bzhin #  yan-lag #  gnas yan-lag #  / / ces rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
darSana mArge boDa avaFgAni boDi aFgAni iti / adRzwa pUrvasya tattvasya tat praTamatas AlocanAt darSanam
# ma blong-ba # 'i lam la byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  tu gyur-pa #  dag ni byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  rnams so zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-kho-na #  nyid ma-mthong-ba #  las de thog-ma #  nyid-du #  mthong-ba # 'i phyir mthong-ba # 'o /
Arya BUmi prApaka tvAt mArgaH iti atas darSanamArgaH iti ucyate
# 'phags-pa # 'i sar phyin par byed-pa # 'i phyir lam zhes-bya-ba #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  mthong-ba'i-lam #  zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
nirveDa BAgIya avasTAyAm hi pelava vastra antaritAni iva upalakzyante / satyAni / darSana mArga avasTAyAm tad apanItaH iva iti
# nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i tshe na ni dar las chod-pa #  lta-bu # r bden-pa #  rnams rtogs so / / mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyi tshe na ni de bsal-ba #  lta-bu # r rtogs so /
tatra tattva aBisambaH DaH boDi nirvikalpam jQAnam tatra zaz smRwya AdIni / boDya anukUlAt tad aFgAni
# de-la #  de-kho-na #  mngon-pa # r rdzogs-par-byang-chub #  ba ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes so / / de-la #  dran-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  drug ni byang-chub-dang-mthun-pa # 'i phyir de'i yan-lag #  rnams so /
Darma pravicayaH tu avaboDa Atmaka tvAt boDiH itarezAm ca sahAya BAvAt / aFga tvam
# chos-rnam-par-'byed-pa #  ni rtogs-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  pas na byang-chub #  ste / / de-dag #  gis grogs-su-gyur-pa # s cha yan-lag #  go /
anyaH punar Aha Anantarya mArga gRhItaH Darma pravicayaH boDyaFgam
# gzhan na re-ba # r chad-med-pa # 'i lam-du #  gtogs-pa # 'i chos rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa #  ni byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  go /
vimukti mArga saFgRhItaH tu boDiH iti
# rnam-par-grol-ba'i-lam #  du gtogs-pa #  ni byang-chub #  ces bya'o zhes zer ro /
tatra boDeH ASrAFgam smRtiH smRtbalena tasmin= Alambane avikzepaNAt
# de-la #  dran-pa #  ni byang-chub #  kyi gnas kyi yan-lag #  ste / / dran-pa'i-stobs #  kyis dmigs-pa #  de-la # s mi g-yeng ba'i phyir ro /
svaBAva aFgam Darma pravicayaH jQAna svaBAva tvAt boDeH
# chos-rnam-par-'byed-pa #  ni rang-bzhin #  gyi yan-lag #  ste / / byang-chub #  kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
niryANa aFgam vIryam vIryeNa p / pRTagjana BUmi samatikramAt
# brtson 'grus ni nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i yan-lag #  ste / / brtson 'grus kyis so-so'i-skye-bo # 'i sa las shin-tu #  'da' ba'i phyir ro /
anuSaMsa aFgam prItiH taTA kAya citta anugrahAt
# dga'-ba #  ni phan yon gyi yan-lag #  ste / / des lus dang sems la phan-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
asaFkleSa aFgam triDA prasrabDi samADi upekzAH tAsAm / saFkleSa pratipakza BUta tvAt
# rnam-pa-gsum #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa # 'i yan-lag #  ste / / shin-tu-sbyangs-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang btang-snyoms #  so / / de-dag #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i gnyen-por-gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aTavA asaFkleSa nidAna ASraya svaBAva BedAt
# yang-na #  nyon-mongs-pa-med-pa # 'i gzhi dang gnas dang ngo-bo-nyid #  tha-dad-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kim arTam punar asaFkleSa aFgam triDA deSitam iti / kena arTena triDA deSA etam iti aBiprAyaH / atas Aha
# ci'i-phyir #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa # 'i yan-lag #  rnam-pa-gsum #  bstan zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  ni ci'i-phyir #  rnam-pa-gsum #  du bshad snyam-du #  bsams-pa #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  / / 'di-la #  gzhi dang gnas dang ni /
nidAnena ASrayeNa iha svaBAvena ca deSitam iti / asaMkleSasya nidAnam prasrabDiH / asaFkleSaH viSudDaH / nidAnam kAraNam
# ngo-bo-nyid #  du bstan-pa #  yin / / zhes gsungs so / / shin-tu-sbyangs-pa #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa # 'i gzhi ste / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa #  ni rnam-par-dag-pa # 'o / / gzhi ni rgyu yin no / / ji-ltar #  gzhi zhes bya zhe na /
kaTam nidAnam iti atas bravIti dOzWulya hetuka tvAt saFkleSasya tasyAH / ca tat pratipakza tvAt iti / etat uktam Bavati saFkleSa nidAna pratipakza BUta tvAt / asaFkleSa nidAnam iti
# de'i-phyir #  / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  ni gnas-ngan-len #  gyi rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'i phyir de ni de'i gnyen-po #  yin pa'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / de ni 'di-skad-du #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i gzhi'i gnyen-por-gyur-pa # 'i phyir kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa # 'i gzhi yin no zhes bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro /
kAya citta akarmaNya tA dOzWulyam / tasmin sati citta ekAgra tA samBavAt citta vikzepaH
# lus dang sems las-su-mi-rung-ba #  nyid ni gnas-ngan-len #  zhes bya ste / / de yod-na #  sems rtse gcig pa med-pa # 'i phyir sems g-yengs par 'gyur ro /
vikzipta cittasya ca rAga Adi saFkleSaH pravartate
# sems g-yengs pa la 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams 'byung ste /
evam dOzWulyam saFkleSasya hetuH
# de-ltar #  gnas-pa #  na len ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rgyu yin no /
tasya dOzWulyasya pratipakzaH prasrabDiH / kaTam iti
# gnas-ngan-len #  de'i gnyen-po #  ni shin-tu-sbyangs-pa # 'o / / ji-ltar #  zhe na /
prasrabDyA kAya cittayoH karmaNi tA ApAdanAt
# shin-tu-sbyangs-pa # s na lus dang sems gnyis las-su-rung-ba # r 'gyur te /
evam prasrabDiH asaFkleSa nidAnam vyavasTApyate
# de-ltar-na #  shin-tu-sbyangs-pa #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa # 'i gzhir rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
ASrayaH samADiH prasrabDi anugRhIta kAya cittasya cittam samADIyate / samAhite citte yaTABUtam prajAnAti
# ting-nge-'dzin #  ni gnas so zhes-bya-ba #  ni lus dang sems gnyis shin-tu-sbyangs-pa # s rjes su bzung-ba # s na sems-mnyam-pa # r 'jog go / / sems-mnyam-pa # r gzhag na yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  rab tu shes so /
yaTA BUta darSanAt kleSaH prahIyante
# yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  mthong-ba # s nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams spong ste /
evam asaFkleSasya samADiH ASrayaH
# de-ltar #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa # 'i gnas ni ting-nge-'dzin #  to /
svaBAvaH upekzA iti / saFklizwa vihAra anukUlAyAH citta sama tAyAH citta apraSaWa tAyAH citta ABoga avasTitatAyAH
# btang-snyoms #  ni ngo-bo-nyid #  do zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnas-pa #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r gyur-pa #  dang mthun-pa # 'i sems mi-mnyam-pa #  dang sems rnal du mi-'jug-pa #  dang sems rtsol ba dang bcas-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
ca pratipakza tvAt / evam upekzA aFkleSa svaBAvaH
# de-ltar-na #  btang-snyoms #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  do /
anye tu AhuH prahANEH mArgEH darSana heye saMkleSe prahINe tat / saFkleSa anubanDa vimuktA svaBAva viSudDA vimukti mArga saMgRhItA
# gzhan na de spong-ba # 'i lam rnams kyis mthong-ba # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams spangs-pa # s nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rjes su 'ching-ba #  dang bral-ba # 'i ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i rnam-par-grol-ba'i-lam #  du gtogs-pa # 'i shes-rab #  shes-bya #  la nges-pa #  skye-ba #  de 'dir btang-snyoms #  zhes bya ste /
jQeye su niScitAH yA prajQA sA atra prajQA upekzA iti ucyate kRtakRtya tvAt
# dgos-pa #  byas-pa # 'i phyir zad-pa #  la zad do snyam-du #  btang-snyoms-su-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro zhe'o /
kzaye kzaye iti upekzA karaNAt iti / azwO mArga aFgAni p / boDyaFga anantaram mArga aFgAni / tezAm kaTam vyavasTAnam iti / darSana mArga anantaram BAvanA mArgaH tatra ca mArga aFgAni iti atas / boDi aFgAn antaram mArga aFgAni iti ucyante
# byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  gi 'og-tu #  lam gyi yan-lag #  rnams te / / de-dag #  ji-ltar #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ce na zhes-bya-ba #  ni mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyi 'og-tu #  bsgom-pa'i-lam #  ste / / de-la #  lam gyi yan-lag #  rnams zhes-bya'o #  / / de'i-phyir #  byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  gi 'og-tu #  lam gyi yan-lag #  rnams brjod do /
tezAm kena arTena vyavasTAnam atas bravIti / paricCedaH aTa samprAptiH / iti vistaraH
# de-dag #  gang-gi #  don-du #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ce na / / de'i-phyir #  / / yongs su gcod dang go byed dang / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
miTyAdRzwi vipakzeNa yAvat miTyA samADi vipakzeNa samyak dRzwi AdInAm / azwAnAm mArga aFgAnAm yaTAkramam vyavasTAnam
# mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  log-pa # r lta-ba #  nas mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  log-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi bar gyis yang-dag-par-lta-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  lam gyi yan-lag-brgyad #  po dag go-rims-bzhin-du #  rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
kramaH punar ezAm kAritrA anukrameNa BAvanA mArgaH iti vistaraH
# yang de-dag #  gi go-rims #  ni byed-pa # 'i rim-gyis #  te / / bsgom-pa'i-lam #  zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba # 'o /
nizevaNa BAvanayA BAvyate iti BAvanA mArgaH
# brten-pa # r bsgom-pa # s bsgom-par-bya-ba #  yin-pas #  na bsgom-pa'i-lam #  mo /
tasmin BAva nAma arge darSana mArgasya prApti BAvanA BAvitasya / paricCeda aFgam samyak dRzwiH
# bsgom-pa'i-lam #  de-la #  mthong-ba'i-lam #  thob-pa # r bsgom-pa # s bsgom-pa #  yongs su gcod-pa # 'i yan-lag #  ni yang-dag-pa'i-lta-ba # 'o /
lOkikI iti sa vikalpa tvAt lOkikI tat utpatti sAmarTya lABAn / mArga samApannasya api sA vyavasTApyate / loka uttarAt tu nirvikalpAt nirvikalpasya sataH api samyak / dRzwi ASraya BUta tvAt samyak dRzzwiH ucyate / atas eva Aha lokottara pRzWa labDa iti / loka uttarasya darSana mArgasya pRzWena balena labDa utpannA iti arTaH
# 'jig-rten-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i phyir 'jig-rten-pa # 'i / / de 'byung-ba # 'i mthu rnyed-pa # s lam la mnyam-pa # r gzhag na yang de rnam-pa # r gzhag go / / 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'o / / rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # r gyur kyang yang-dag-par-lta-ba # 'i gnas-su-gyur-pa # s na / / yang-dag-par-lta-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  / / de'i-phyir #  'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i rjes-las-thob-pa #  zhes smos te / / 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyi rjes-las-thob-pa #  ni skyes zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
sA punar kiMvizayA iti atas Aha yayA sva aDigamam iti
# de'i yul gang zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  des rang-gis #  rtogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
darSana mArga aDigamam paricCinatti evam mayA aDigatam iti
# mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyis rtogs-pa #  la bdag-gis #  'di-lta-bu #  rtogs so zhes yongs su gcod-pa #  ste /
darSana mArgasya vizaya tvAt samyak dRzwiH iti ucyate / para samprApaNa aFgam iti vistaraH / tayA samyak dRzwyA paricCinnasya tattvasya samyak vAcA samyak / saFkalpena ca paratra prApaNAt samyak saFkalpaH samyak vAc ca / para samprApaNa aFgam
# mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyi yul yin-pas #  na yang-dag-par-lta-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  / / gzhan go-bar-byed-pa # 'i yan-lag #  ces bya-ba #  rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  ni yang-dag-pa'i-lta-ba #  des yongs-su-bcad-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  yang-dag-pa # 'i dag dang yang-dag-pa'i-rtog-pa # s gzhan la go-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir / / yang-dag-pa'i-rtog-pa #  dang yang-dag-pa'i-ngag #  ni gzhan-yid-ches-pa # r byed-pa # 'i yan-lag #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  /
atas eva Aha samutTAnayA vAcA tat prApaNAt iti
# kun-nas-slong-ba #  dang bcas-pa # 'i ngag gis de go-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
samyak saMkalpaH hi vAcaH samutTAnam na avitarkya na avicArya vAcam / BAzate iti sUtre vacanAt
# yang-dag-pa'i-rtog-pa #  ni ngag-kun-nas-slong-ba #  ste / / ma brtags ma dpyad-pa # r tshig mi smra'o zhes mdo las gsungs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
samAhitaH api tAByAm samanvAgataH veditavyaH tat utpatti lABAt na tu
# de 'byung-ba # 'i mthu rnyed-pa # 'i phyir mnyam-par-gzhag-pa #  na yang de gnyis dang ldan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'i /
samAhitaH saFkalpayati BAzate vA / para samBAvana aFgam triDA samyak vAc karmAntAjIvAH / kaTam iti atas Aha tEH hi samyak vAc karmAntAjIvEH yaTAkramam / dRzwO SIle aTa saMleKe parivijQaptiH izyate p / iti / tasya samyak vAcA iti vistaraH / kaTA iti Darma deSanA / sAMkaTya viniScayaH parEH saha aBisamayam AraBya codya parihAra kriyA / anena kaTA sAFkaTya niScayena prajQAyAm samBAvanA Bavati / parezAm niyogAt anena tattvam aDigatam taTA hi upaSama saMsaktam / suviniH catA virudDa arTam sPuwa arTam vacanam idam
# mnyam-par-gzhag-pa #  na yang-dag-par-rtog-pa # r byed-pa # 'am smra-ba #  ni ma yin no / / gzhan-yid-ches-pa # r byed-pa # 'i yan-lag #  ni rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / yang-dag-pa'i-ngag #  dang las-kyi-mtha' #  dang las kyi 'tsho-ba # 'o / / ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / de-dag #  go-rims-bzhin-du #  / / lta dang tshul-khrims #  yo-byad #  bsnyungs / / gzhan la rnam-par-rig-byed #  'dod / / ces bya-ba #  smos te / / yang-dag-pa'i-ngag #  dang las-kyi-mtha' #  dang 'tsho-ba #  dang go-rims #  bzhin no / / yang-dag-pa'i-ngag #  gis zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  la / / bsnyad-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni chos-bstan-pa # 'o / / 'brel-ba # 'i gtam rnam-par-nges-pa # s zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  las brtsams nas gzhan dag la rgol zhing lan-'debs-pa #  ste / / bsnyad-pa #  dang 'brel-ba # 'i gtam rnam-par-nges-pa #  'dis ni 'di-ltar #  'di thogs-pa-med-pa #  dang don shin-tu #  gtan la phab pa dang 'gal-ba #  med-pa #  dang don gsal-ba #  brjod-pa #  las na 'dis de-kho-na #  nges-par #  rtogs so zhes shes-rab #  la gzhan dag yid-ches-pa # r 'gyur ro /
samyak karma antena SIlasya iti / samBavanA Bavati iti vartate / kaTam iti atas Aha akRtya akaraNAt iti
# yang-dag-pa # 'i las-kyi-mtha' #  ni tshul-khrims #  la ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni yid-ches-pa # r 'gyur ro zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro / / ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / bya-ba-ma-yin-pa #  mi-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
samyak karmAntaH hi duScarita viroDi iti atas tena sambanDa AgataH jIvita hetoH
# yang-dag-pa # 'i las-kyi-mtha' #  ni nyes-par-spyod-pa #  dang mi-mthun-pa #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  de dang ldan na srog-gi-phyir #  yang bya-ba-ma-yin-pa #  mi byed do /
api akRtyam na karoti iti atas Arya kAnta SIlavAn ayam iti samBAvanA
# de'i-phyir #  'dir ni 'phags-pa #  dgyes-pa # 'i tshul-khrims #  dang ldan no zhes yid-ches-pa #  'byung ngo /
Bavati / samyak AjIvena saMleKa samBAvanA Bavati iti sambaDyate
# yang-dag-pa'i-'tsho-ba # s ni yo-byad-bsnyungs-pa #  la ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni yid-ches-pa # r 'gyur ro zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro /
kaTam iti atas Aha DarmeNa mAtrayA ca cIvara Adi ezaNAt iti
# ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / chos-kyis #  gos la-sogs-pa #  tshod-zin-pa # r tshol-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
kuhana Adi doza rahitaH jIvita upakaraNa arTaH kAya vAc samAcAraH / samyak AjIvaH
# 'tsho-ba'i-yo-byad #  kyi phyir tshul-'chos-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i nyes-pa-med-pa # 'i lus dang ngag gis kun du spyod-pa #  ni yang-dag-pa'i-'tsho-ba #  ste /
tena saMleKe samBAvanA Bavati niScayena asya upakaraNa tRzNA prahINA / taTA hi asO kevalam ASraya sTiti arTam eva nyAyena mAtrayA ca / cIvara AdIna paryezate / tatra samyak dRzwyA ABimAnikaH na Bavati yaTABUtam
# des 'di-ltar #  'di ni lus-gnas-pa #  tsam du bya-ba # 'i phyir rigs-pa #  dang tshod-zin-pa # r chos-gos #  la-sogs-pa #  tshol-ba # s na gdon-mi-za-bar #  'di ni yo-byad #  rnams la sred-pa #  spangs so zhes yo-byad-bsnyungs-pa # r yid-ches-pa # r 'gyur ro / / de-la #  yang-dag-pa'i-lta-ba # s ni mngon-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  med-pa # r 'gyur te /
sva aDigama parijQAnAt / samyak saFkalpena samutTApita vAcA siMhanAdam nadati samyak vAc / karmAnta AjIvEH svAm pratijQAm samudBavayati
# rang-gi-rtog-pa #  yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  yongs-su-shes-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yang-dag-pa'i-rtog-pa # s kun-nas-bslang-ba # 'i tshig gis ni seng-ge # 'i sgra sgrog go / / yang-dag-pa'i-ngag #  dang las-kyi-mtha' #  dang; 'tsho-ba #  rnams kyis ni rang-gis #  dam-bcas-pa #  yang-dag-par #  brjod do /
tatra vipakza pratipakza aFgam triDA eva
# de-la #  mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi gnyen-po # 'i yan-lag #  rnam gsum mi shes-nas #  de'i-phyir #  /
tat tu na jQAyate iti Aha samyak vyAyAmi smRti samADayaH iti
# yang-dag-pa # 'i rtsol ba dang dran ba dang ting-nge-'dzin #  to zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
te ca kasya vipakzasya pratipakzAH iti atas Aha ezAm punar yaTAkramam
# de-dag #  kyang mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  gang-gi #  gnyen-po #  yin zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  ni go-rims-bzhin-du #  /
kleSa upakleSa Butva vipakza pratipakzatA iti
# nyon mongs nye-ba # 'i nyon mongs dbang / / mi mthun phyogs kyi gnyen-po # 'o / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so /
tatra praTamasya samyak vyAyAmaH iti
# de-la #  dang-po # 'i gnyen-po #  ni yang-dag-pa # 'i rtsol ba ste zhes-bya-ba #  la /
BAvanA heyaH hi kleSaH praTamaH vipakzaH
# bsgom-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  ni mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang-po #  ste /
tasya samyak vyAyAmaH pratipakzaH
# de'i gnyen-po #  ni yang-dag-pa # 'i rtsol ba'o /
kaTam iti atas Aha tena iti samyak vyAyAmena mArga BAvanAt
# ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / des zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / yang-dag-pa # 'i rtsol bas lam bsgom-pa # 'i phyir ro /
samyak dRzwi parigRhItam laya OdDatya viagatam samADi avasTAyAm vIryam / samyak vyAyAmaH
# bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  dang bral-ba # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi dus kyi brtson 'grus yang-dag-pa'i-lta-ba # s bsdus-pa #  ni yang-dag-pa # 'i rtsol ba ste /
tena BAvanA prahAtavyAnAm kleSAnAm prahANAya tat pratipakzam / mArgam BAvayati iti samyak samADi pratipAdanAt samyak vyAyAmaH / praTamasya pratipakzaH ucyate
# des bsgom-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i phyir de'i gnyen-po #  lam bsgom mo / / de'i-phyir #  yang-dag-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  sgrub-pa # s yang-dag-pa # 'i rtsol ba ni dang-po # 'i gnyen-po #  zhes-bya'o #  /
tasyAm eva mArga BAvanAyAm laya OdDatya lakzaNasya dvitIyasya upakleSasya / samyak smRtiH iti / pratipakzaH iti prakRtam
# lam bsgom-pa #  de-nyid-la #  gnyis-pa #  nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni yang-dag-pa'i-dran-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnyen-po #  zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro /
kaTam iti atas bravIti SamaTa Adi nimittezu sUpa sTita smRteH / laya OdDatya aBAvAt iti
# ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / zhi-gnas #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyu rnams la dran-pa #  shin-tu #  nye-bar-gnas-pa # s bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
Adi Sabdena pragraha nimittam upekzA nimitta Qca veditavyam
# sogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgras ni rab-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i rgyu dang btang-snyoms #  kyi rgyu yin par shes-pa # r bya'o /
tatra vikzepa nimitta upaSamanAt SamaTaH
# de-la #  g-yeng ba'i rgyu nye-bar-zhi-ba # r byed-pa # s zhi-gnas #  so /
SamaTa Adi nimittam SamaTa Adi kAraNam
# zhi-gnas #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyu ni zhi-gnas #  la-sogs-pa # 'i byed-rgyu # 'o /
tara udDate cittaH OdDatya aBiSaFkini vA samvejanIya vastu manaskAraH / SamaTa nimittam
# de-la #  sems-rgod-pa # 'am rgod du dogs-pa #  zhig tu gyur na / / skyo-bar-'gyur-ba # 'i dngos-po #  yid-la-byed-pa #  ni zhi-gnas #  kyi rgyu'o /
lIne citte laya aBiSaFkini vA aBinandanIya vastu manaskAraH
# sems bying-ba # 'am / / bying du dogs-pa #  zhig tu gyur na / / mngon-par-dga'-ba # r gyur-pa # 'i dngos-po #  yid-la-byed-pa #  ni rab-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i rgyu'o /
pragraha nimittam SamaTa ekAntike vipaSya p / na ekAntike vA mArge yuga nadda vAhini vA tat
# zhi-gnas #  la gcig-tu-nges-pa # 'i lam mam / / lhag-mthong #  la gcig-tu-nges-pa # 'am / / zung du 'brel-ba # s 'jug-pa # 'ang rung ste /
uBaya upakleSa anupaklizwe anABoga manaskAraH upekzA nimittam
# nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  de gnyis kyis nye-bar-nyon-mongs-pa # r gyur-pa #  la lhun-gyis-grub-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa #  ni btang-snyoms #  kyi rgyu'o /
aBijQA Adi guNa svaBAvasya viBu tvasya yat vipakzaH
# mngon-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yon-tan #  gyi rang-bzhin #  gyi dbang 'byor-ba # 'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  gang-yin-pa #  ni /
samApatti AvaraNa Atmakam aklizwam ajQAnam tasya tRtIyasya samyak
# snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i sgrib-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i mi-shes-pa # 'o /
samADiH pratipakzaH iti prakRtam
# gsum-pa #  ni de'i yang-dag-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  te gnyen-po #  zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro /
kaTam iti atas Aha DyAna sanniSrayeNa aBijQA Adi guNa aBinirhArAt iti
# ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / bsam-gtan #  la gnas nas mngon-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yon-tan #  mngon-pa # r bsgrub-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes smos so /
DyAnam hi sarva viSizwa guNa aBinirhAra ASraya
# bsam-gtan #  ni yon-tan #  khyad-par-can #  thams-cad #  mngon-pa # r bsgrub-pa # 'i gnas yin te /
iti aBijQA Adi guNa aBinirhAra vipakza BUtasya samADi AvaraNasya
# de-bas-na #  mngon-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yon-tan #  mngon-par-sgrub-pa # 'i mthun-pa # 'i phyogs su gyur-pa #  ni /
pratipakzaH / tat evam samyak vyAyAmena kleSa AvaraNa visaMyogam KyApayati samyak smRtyA
# snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i sgrib-pa # 'i gnyen-po # 'o / / de-bas-na #  de-ltar #  yang-dag-pa # 'i rtsol ba ni nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  dang bral-ba #  ston to /
samADi pariSudDim samyak samADinA samApatti AvaraNena vizamam iti / pratipakza BAvanA praBedaH
# yang-dag-pa'i-dran-pa # s ni ting-nge-'dzin #  yongs-su-dag-pa # 'o / / yang-dag-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  gyis ni snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i sgrib-pa-dang-bral-ba # 'o /
sA ezA pratipakza BAvanA samAsena triviDA veditavyA
# gnyen-po-bsgom-pa #  mdor-bsdus-na #  rnam-pa-gsum #  du rig-par-bya #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
AramBa pratilamBa nizpatti Bedena / vyAsataH tvena ekaviDA / kaTam
# rtsom pa dang thob-pa #  dang grub-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis so / / rgyas-pa # r byas-na #  rnam-pa-du-ma #  yod do / / de ji lta zhe na /
anukUlA viparyastA / iti vistaraH
# rjes su mthun la phyin-ci-log #  / / ces rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  de-la #  /
tatra ara viparyAsa anukUlA viparyastA
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa #  la phyin-ci-log-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la /
aviparyAsaH darSana mArgaH tattva vizaya tvAt
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni mthong-ba'i-lam #  ste / / de-kho-na #  yul yin pa'i phyir ro /
tat anukUla tvAt aviparyAsa anukUlA
# de'i rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'i phyir phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'o /
iyaQca pRTagjana BAvanA iti atattva vizaya tvAt viparyastA pRTagjanasya
# 'di ni so-so'i-skye-bo # 'i sgom-pa #  yin-pas #  de-kho-na #  yul du-ma #  gyur-pa # 'i phyir phyin-ci-log #  ste /
niravaSezA prahINa kleSa tvAt
# so-so'i-skye-bo # s nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams ma-lus-pa #  ma-spangs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kaTam viparyastA satI aviparyAsa anukUlA Bavati
# ji-ltar #  na phyin-ci-log #  tu gyur-pa # 'i phyin-ci-log #  med-pa # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa # r 'gyur zhe na /
su viSudDa Darma DAtu nizyandAyAH / Sruta vAsanAyAH utpAdAt
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  shin-tu #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i rgyu-mthun-pa #  thos-pa # 'i bag-chags #  las byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
sA ca smRti upasTAna BAvanAm AraBya yAvat bala BAvanA iti
# de-yang #  dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  bsgom-pa #  nas brtsams te / / stobs bsgom-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o /
aviparyastA viparyAsa anubanDa iti / iyam hi SEkzANAm boDyaFga BAvanA mArga BAvanA ca
# phyin-ci-log #  med la phyin-ci-log #  rjes-su-'brel-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  'di ni slob-ma #  rnams kyi byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  bsgom-pa #  dang lam bsgom-pa #  ste /
tattva vizaya tvAt aviparyastA BAvanA prahAtavya kleSa sadBAvAt ca / viparyAsa anubanDA
# de-kho-na #  yul du gyur-pa # s na phyin-ci-log #  med-pa # 'o / / bsgom-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  yod-pa # 'i phyir phyin-ci-log #  rjes-su-'brel-ba # 'o /
aviparyastA viparyAsa niranubanDA iti / iyam aSEkza mArga BAvanA tattva vizaya tvAt aviparyastA
# phyin-ci-log #  kyang med la phyin-ci-log #  kyang rjes-su-'brel-ba #  yang med-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  'di ni dgra-bcom-pa #  mi-slob-pa # 'i bsgom-pa #  ste / / de-kho-na #  yul du gyur-pa # s na phyin-ci-log #  med-pa # 'o /
niravaSeza mala prahANAt arhatAm viparyAsa niranubanDA p
# dgra-bcom-pa # s ni dri-ma #  rnams ma-lus-par-spangs-pa # 'i phyir phyin-ci-log #  rjes-su-'brel-ba #  med do /
idAnIm SrAvaka AdiByaH boDisatvAnAm pratipakza BAvanAyAH / viSeza pradarSana arTam Aha boDisattvAnAm tu
# da-ni #  nyan-thos #  rnams las byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi gnyen-po-bsgom-pa #  khyad-par #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi ni /
Alambana manaskAra prAptitaH tat viSizwatA iti
# dmigs dang yid-la-byed-pa #  dang / / 'thob-pa # s de ni khyad-par #  'phags / / zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
tatra AlambanataH viSizwa tA SrAvaka pratyekabudDAnAm hi sva asAntAnikAH / kAya AdayaH
# de-la #  dmigs-pa #  khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  ni / / nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  rnams ni rang-gi-rgyud #  du gtogs-pa # 'i lus la-sogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ste /
kAya vedanA citta DarmA Alambanam
# lus dang tshor-ba #  dang sems dang chos-rnams #  la dmigs so /
boDisattvAnAm punar sva para sAntAnikAH kAya vedanA citta DarmA / Alambanam
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams ni bdag-dang-gzhan #  gyi rgyud du gtogs-pa #  rnams so zhes-bya-ba #  ni lus dang tshor-ba #  dang sems dang chos-rnams #  la dmigs so /
kim arTam Alambanam Binnam
# ci'i-phyir #  dmigs-pa #  tha dad ce na /
yasmAt SrAvaka AdInAm sva arTam eva aDikRtya / pratipakza BAvanA pravRttiH boDisattvAnAm punar sva pArTam aDikRtya iti
# 'di-ltar #  nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  ni rang-gi-don #  gyi dbang-du-byas-nas #  gnyen-po-bsgom-pa #  la 'jug go / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni bdag-dang-gzhan-gyi-don #  gyi dbang du mdzad-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anitya AdiBiH AkArEH iti anitya duHKa SUnya Atma AkArEH
# mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r zhes-bya-ba #  ni mi-rtag-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  dang stong-pa #  dang bdag-med-pa'i-rnam-pa # r ro /
kasmAt SrAvaka pratyekabudDAnAm anitya AdiBiH eva manaskAraH
# ci'i phir nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  rnams la-sogs-pa #  de-ltar #  yid la byed ce na /
teByaH udvega arTam / na hi anudvignaH tEH visaMyujyate
# de-dag #  la skyo-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir te / / skyo-ba # r ma-gyur-pa #  de-dag #  'bral-ba # r mi 'gyur ro /
boDisattvAH anupalamBa yogena iti / kalpita svaBAva anupalamBa prakAreNa iti arTaH kim arhtam evam manasi
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams ni dmigs-pa # 'i tshul du'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  dmigs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / ci'i-phyir #  de-ltar #  yid la mdzad ce na /
kurvanti / sarva vikalpa prahANa arTam
# rnam-par-rtog-pa #  thams-cad #  spang-ba # 'i phyir te /
eza hi tezu viSezaH ucyate na kevalam anupalamBa yogena eva manasi kurvanti
# 'di ni de-dag #  gi khyad-par #  zhes-bya'o #  / / mi dmigs-pa # 'i tshul 'ba'-zhig-tu #  yid la mdzad-pa #  yang ma yin gyi /
kim tarhi anitya AdiBiH api AkArEH
# mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r yang yid la mdzad de /
evam manasikAra viSezAt viSizwa tA
# de-ltar-na #  yid-la-byed-pa # 'i khyad-par #  gyis khyad-par #  gdu 'phags so /
yAvat eva kAya AdInAm visaMyogAya iti / kAya AdInAm visaMyogaH nirupaDi Seza nirvANam tadA Alambana kleSa prahANaQca / boDisattvAH na visaMyogAya nA avisaMyogAya / kim kAraNam
# ci nas kyang lus la-sogs-pa #  dang 'bral-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni lus la-sogs-pa #  dang bral-ba #  ni / / phung-po #  lhag-ma #  med-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  dang de-la #  dmigs-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa-spangs-pa # 'o / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams ni 'bral-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir-yang #  ma yin / / mi-'bral-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir-yang #  ma yin te / / de-ci'i-phyir-zhe-na #  /
ekAntena hi kAya AdiBiH visaMyuktAH ca / sattva arTa karaNa samarTAH na syuH kzINa kleSa itara sattva vat
# lus la-sogs-pa #  dang shin-tu #  bral-ba #  dang ma bral na yang sems-can-gyi-don #  bya-ba # r mi-nus-pa # r 'gyur te / / nyon-mongs-pa #  zad-pa #  dang sems-can #  phal ba bzhin no /
yadi na visaMyogAya kimarTam tarhi pratipakzam BAvayati iti atas Aha
# gal-te #  'bral-ba # 'i phyir-yang #  ma yin mi-'bral-ba # 'i phyir-yang #  ma yin na ci'i-phyir #  gnyen-po #  rnams bsgom zhen de'i-phyir #  /
yAvat eva pratizWita nirvANAya BAvayati iti
# ci nas kyang mi-gnas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i phyir bsgom mo zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
kim tat apratizWitam nirvANam
# mi-gnas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  de gang zhe na /
boDisattva avasTAyAm tAvat karma upapatti vaSitA Asan niSrayeNa / kAruNika tvAt saMsAra upapattiH prajQA balena tatra AsaFkleSaH
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i tshe na ni las dang skye-ba #  la dbang-ba #  la gnas nas snyong rje dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir 'khor-ba # r skye-ba #  yang shes-rab #  kyi stobs kyis der kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r mi 'gyur te /
tat idam boDisattvAnAm apratizWitam nirvANam viDIyate
# 'di ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i mi-gnas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  zhes brjod do /
saMsAra avasTitaH api pRTagjana vat saMklizwaH na vartate
# 'khor-ba #  na gnas kyang so-so'i-skye-bo #  bzhin-du #  nyon-mongs-pa # r yang mi 'gyur la /
na SrAvaka Adi vat nirupAdAnaH nirvANaH iti / taTAgata avasTAyAm api kleSa jQeya AvaraNa prahANAn na saMsAre / pratizWitaH nirupaDi Seze nirvANe na eva pratizWitaH
# nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  nye-bar-len-pa #  med-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # r yang mi 'gyur ro / / de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # 'i dus na yang nyon-mongs-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  spangs-pa # s 'khor-ba #  la mi gnas la /
DarmakAyasya anucCedAt sa amBogikanEH mANika kAya yoH vat lokaH tAvat / para arTa karaNAt
# chos kyi sku rgyun mi 'chad cing longs-spyod #  rdzogs-pa #  dang sprul pa'i sku gnyis kyis 'jig-rten #  ji-srid-pa #  de srid du gzhan-gyi-don #  mdzad-pa # 'i phyir /
evam ezA pratipakza BAvanA boDisattvAnAm SrAvaka AdiByaH / Alambana manaskAra Pala viSezEH viSizwA iti uktA pratipakza BAvanA / tatra avasTA vasTA
# phung-po #  lhag-ma #  med-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la yang mi gnas so / / de-ltar-na #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi gnyen-po-bsgom-pa #  'di ni dmigs-pa #  dang yid-la-byed-pa #  dang 'bras-bu # 'i khyad-par #  rnams kyis nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  las khyad-par #  du 'phags so /
pratipakza BAvanA anantaram tatra avasTA uktA iti atas pRcCati tatra ava sTA / katamA iti
# gnyen-po-bsgom-pa #  bshad-zin #  to / / gnyen-po-bsgom-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  de'i-gnas #  bshad de / / de'i-phyir #  de'i-gnas #  gang zhe na zhes dris so /
tatra iti tasyAm pratipakza BAvanAyAm / atas Aha / hetu avasTAvatAra AKyA / iti vistaraH
# de'i zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnyen-po-bsgom-pa #  de'i ste / / de'i-phyir #  / / rgyu yi gnas-skabs #  zhugs-pa #  dang / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
tatra hetu avasTA gotra sTasya pudgalasya iti
# de-la #  rgyu'i-gnas #  ni gang rigs-la-gnas-pa # 'i gang-zag #  go zhes-bya-ba #  la /
gotram hetuH bIjam iti arTaH
# rigs ni rgyu dang sa-bon #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
tatra yaH gotre eva vartate na citta utpAda Adizu sa gotra sTaH iha aBipretaH
# de-la #  gang rigs nyid-du #  gyur gyi sems-bskyed-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la ma yin te / / de ni 'dir rigs-la-gnas-pa # r 'dod do /
sa punar uttara avasTAsu anuvartate na nivartate
# de ni gong-ma # 'i gnas rnams su rjes su 'jug ste mi ldog go /
kecid tat ca gotram kuSala mUla svaBAvam iti varNayanti
# kha-cig #  na de rigs de-yang #  dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba'i rang-bzhin #  no zhes zer te /
kuSala mUlAni eva hi kAnicid SrAvaka gotram iti ucyante / evam yAvat kAnicid boDisattva gotram iti
# dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba nyid la kha-cig #  ni nyan-thos-kyi-rigs #  zhes-bya-ba #  nas de-bzhin-du #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i rigs kyi bar-du # 'o zhe'o /
pRTagjana avasTAm AraBya indriya BedaH gotram ucyate
# kha-cig #  na re so-so'i-skye-bo # 'i gnas las brtsams te / / dbang-po # 'i bye-brag #  la rigs zhes bya ste /
citta bIja SaktiH gotram iti etat api ekaH AhuH / tasmin sati pRTagjana avasTAyAm SEkza avasTAya aQca SrAvaka gotra / iti ucyate yAvat boDisattva gotraH iti / aSEkza avasTAyAm tu SrAvakaH iti ucyate pratyekabudDaH iti vA / na tat gotram tasya p / prakarza avasTAnAt
# sems kyi sa-bon #  gyi mthu la rigs zhes de-skad #  kyang zer te de yod-na #  so-so'i-skye-bo # 'i dus dang slob-pa # 'i dus na nyan-thos-kyi-rigs #  zhes-bya-ba #  nas byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i rigs kyi bar-du # 'o zhe'o / / mi-slob-pa # 'i dus na ni nyan-thos #  she'am / / rang-sangs-rgyas #  she 'am / / sangs-rgyas #  zhes bya ste / / de ni gnas-skabs #  kyi mthar-thug-pa # 'i phyir de ni rigs ma yin no /
tat ca SrAvaka Adi Bedena triDA aBidyate
# de-yang #  nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis gsum du dbye'o /
niyata aniyata praBedena zaXviDam Bavati
# nges-pa #  dang ma-nges-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis drug tu 'gyur ro /
avatAra avasTA utpAdita boDi cittasya iti / sA ca SrAvaka pratyekabudDa taTAgata gotrANAm yaTAkramam
# zhugs-pa # 'i gnas ni sems-bskyed-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  dang de-bzhin-gshegs-pa'i-rigs #  rnams dang go-rims-bzhin-du #  /
SrAvaka pratyekabudDa samyaksambudDa boDizu citta utpAdAt triviDA Bavati
# nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa # 'i sangs-rgyas #  kyi byang-chub #  tu sems-bskyed-pa # s rnam-pa-gsum #  du 'gyur ro /
tasya prayoga mUla BUta tvAt tasmin= utpanne prayoga avatAraH iti tat
# de ni sbyor-ba # 'i rtsa bar gyur-pa # 'i phyir de byung na sbyor-ba # r zhugs-pa #  yin-pas #  na /

# de bskyed-pa #  la sbyor-ba # r zhugs-pa # 'i gnas zhes-bya'o #  /
