# de'i-phyir #  sbyor-ba # 'i gnas ni sems bskyed nas 'bras-bu #  ma thob tshun chad do zhes-bya-ba #  ste /
utpAdita boDi cittasya dAna SIla AdikaH
# sems-bskyed-pa # 'i sbyin-pa #  dang tshul-khrims #  la-sogs-pa #  nas stobs bsgom-pa #  la thug gi bar-du #  /
bala BAvanA paryavasAna kuSala samAramBaH praTama Pala prApakaH upAyaH iti / sa prayogaH ucyate
# dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba yang-dag-par #  brtsams shing-thog #  ma'i 'bras-bu #  thob-par-byed-pa # 'i thabs yin-pas #  de-la #  sbyor-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  /
kaTam hetu avatAra avasTA boDipakza BAvanA avasTA iti ucyate
# ji-ltar #  rgyun-du-zhugs-pa # 'i gnas la byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  bsgom-pa # 'i gnas zhes bshad ce na /
tad hetutvAt / atas eva uktam uttarottaraPalam gotrAt citta utpAdaH iti evam Adi
# de'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir de-bas-na #  'di-skad-du #  rigs nas sems-bskyed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  phyi-ma-phyi-ma #  'bras-bu # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  bshad do; /
Pala avasTA prApte praTama Pale / Pala arTam hi prayujyate
# 'bras-bu # 'i gnas ni thob-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni dang-po # 'i 'bras-bu #  ste / / 'bras-bu # 'i phyir sbyor ro /
atas prayoga anantaram Pala avasTA / sa karaNIya avasTA hi SEkzasya / tasya PalAnAm / aparisamApta tvAt Pala anantara prApti pratikaraNIya sadBAvAt / akaraNIyA avasTA / aSEkzaH hi tri DAtuka vIta rAgAt / tasya PalAnAm parisamApta tvAt Pala antara prApti karaNIyA sadBAvAt / akaraNIya avasTA
# de-bas-na #  sbyor-ba # 'i 'og-tu #  'bras-bu # 'i gnas so / / bya-ba #  med-pa # 'i gnas ni mi-slob-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba # 'o / / khams-gsum #  gyi 'dod-chags #  dang bral pa'i phyir mi-slob-pa #  ste / / de'i 'bras-bu #  rnams yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # s na / / 'bras-bu #  gzhan thob-par-bya-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir bya-ba #  med-pa # 'i gnas so /
viSeza avasTA aBijQA Adi guNa viSeza samanvAgatasya iti / samAne arTattve aBijQA AdiBiH guNa viSezEH samanvAgataH itarasmAt
# khyad-par #  gyi gnas ni mngon-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yon-tan #  gyi khyad-par #  gyi khyad-par #  dang ldan-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni dgra-bcom-pa # r mtshungs-pa #  las mngon-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yon-tan #  gyi khyad-par #  rnams dang ldan-pa # s /
viSizwA aBijQA Adi guNa viSeza nizpanna avasTA viSeza avasTA iti ucyate
# gzhan-las #  khyad zhugs-pa # r mngon-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yon-tan #  gyi khyad-par #  bsgrub-pa # 'i gnas la khyad-par #  gyi gnas zhes-bya'o #  /
uttara avasTA SrAvaka pratyekabudDeByaH BUmi pravizwasya boDisattvasya
# bla-ma'i-gnas #  ni nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  bas / / sar zhugs-pa # 'i byang-chub-sems-dpa' # o zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
sva para arTa kArikasya loka uttarasya mArgasya uBaya nErAtmya prativeDasya / lABena tad anyayA uttara BUtAt tad avasTA uttara avasTA iti ucyate
# bdag-dang-gzhan-gyi-don #  byed-pa #  'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam bdag-med-pa #  gnyis rtogs-par-byed-pa #  thob-pa # s / / de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i theg-pa # 'i bla-mar-gyur-pa # s na / / gnas de-la #  bla-ma'i-gnas #  zhes-bya'o #  /
anuttara avasTAH budDasya / kim arTam
# bla-na-med-pa # 'i gnas ni sangs-rgyas #  te / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na de'i-phyir #  /
atas Aha tatas UrDvam avasTA aBAvAt iti
# de'i gong-na #  gnas med-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
sarva guNa doza prakarza nizWA aDizWAna tvAt budDasya tatas UrDvam anyA
# yon-tan #  dang nyes-pa #  thams-cad #  phul du phyin pa dang brtsal ba'i mthar-phyin-pa # s na sangs-rgyas #  su grub-pa #  ste /
viSizwA avasTA na vidyate iti sA eva anuttara iti ucyate
# de'i-gong-du #  khyad-par-can #  gyi gnas gzhan med-pa # s de-nyid-la #  bla-na-med-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
iyat uktam parisamAptA api niravaSezA avasTA boDisattvAnAm / ekAdaSa BUmi praBeda sandarSana arTam
# de snyed du bshad-pa # s gnas-ma #  lus par yongs su rdzogs kyang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi sa bcu gcig-tu #  rab-tu-dbye-ba #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
aDimukti cartya Adi avasTA aBizekADya vasta avasAnAH punar uktA / budDAnAm tu kAya traya praBeda pradarSana arTam prApti avasTA AdikAH
# mos-pas-spyod-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gnas nas / / dbang-bskur-ba # 'i gnas la thug gi bar-du #  yang bshad do / / sangs-rgyas #  rnams kyi sku gsum rab-tu-dbye-ba #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
punar tisraH nirdizwAH
# phyi-ma # 'i gnas la-sogs-pa #  yang gsum du bstan te /
tatra hetu avatAra avasTA boDisattva itara sADAraNA veditavyA / tatra aDimukti avasTA boDisattvAnAm sarvasyAm aDimukti caryA BUmO= iti / citta utpAdAt UrDvam yAvat na BUmi praveSaH atra antare adRzwa tattvaH api
# de-la #  rgyu dang zhugs-pa # 'i gnas ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  dang gzhan dag thun mong par rig-par-bya # 'o / / de-la #  mos-pa'i-gnas #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi mos-pas-spyod-pa'i-sa #  thams-cad #  do zhes-bya-ba #  ni sems bskyed nas sa la ma zhugs tshun chad de /
dRzwa tattvam iva p / budDa boDisattvezu aDimuktyA svaBAva traya muKena DarmAn pratipadyate
# bar der de-kho-na #  ma mthong yang de-kho-na #  mthong-ba #  dang 'dra-bar #  sangs-rgyas #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams la mos-pa # s ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum gyi sgo nas chos-rnams #  sgrub cing /
tad anya sattvAnAm duzkara dAna SIla Adizu budDa tva nizpAda samBArezu / pravartate iti atas iyam avasTA aDimukti praBAva tattvAt / aDimukti caryA iti ucyate / sA ca kalpa asaMKyeyam aDikam vA / praveSAvasTA praTamAyAm BUmO= iti / svaBAva trayasya avikalpena jQAnena tat praTamatas eva / tattva sva sampedana prativeDaH iti praveSA avasTA ucyate / ezA eva boDisattvasya darSana mArgaH niryANa avasTA tat uttarAsu zawsu / BUmizu iti
# de-las-gzhan-pa #  sems-can #  rnams kyi bya-dka'-ba #  sbyin-pa #  dang tshul-khrims #  la-sogs-pa #  sangs-rgyas #  su 'grub-pa'i-tshogs #  rnams la 'jug-pa #  ste / / de-bas-na #  gnas mos-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba #  yin-pas #  mos-pas-spyod-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / de-yang #  bskal-pa-grangs-med-pa # 'am de-bas #  lhag-pa # 'o / / 'jug-pa # 'i gnas ni sa dang-po # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum la rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyis / / dang-po-kho-nar #  de-kho-na #  rang-gis #  rig cing rtogs-pa # s na 'jug-pa # 'i gnas zhes bya ste / / 'di nyid ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i mthong-ba'i-lam #  mo /
BAvanA prahAtavyasya nimitta nAnA tva aBiniveSasya prahANa nizwa AgamanAt / sa ABoga prayoga nizWA gamanAt ca etAH BU mayaH niryANa avasTA iti ucyate / vyAkaraNa avasTA azwamyAm BUmO= iti
# des-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i gnas ni de'i gong-ma #  sa drug-po #  dag go zhes-bya-ba #  ni bsgom-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i mtshan-ma #  rnam-pa-sna-tshogs #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  spangs-pa # 'i mthar-thug-par-'gro-ba #  dang rtsol ba dang bcas-pa # 'i sbyor-ba # 'i mthar-thug-par-'gro-ba # 'i phyir / / sa 'di dag la nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i gnas zhes-bya'o #  /
sarvaTA sarva nimitta ABoga saMjQA vigamAt azwamyAm BUmO niyati patitaH / Bavati budDa tve iti budDEH BagavadBiH sammuKa vyAkaraNena vyAkriyate / kaTaka tva avasTAH navamyAm iti
# lung bstan-pa # 'i gnas ni sa brgyad pa'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni mtshan-ma-thams-cad #  la 'bad-pa #  dang 'du-shes #  rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  bral pas sa brgyad pa ni sangs-rgyas #  su 'grub-pa # r nges-pa #  yin te / / sangs-rgyas #  bcom-ldan-'das #  rnams kyis mngon-sum-du #  lung bstan-pa # s lung ston to /
navamyAm BUmO SrAvaka pratyekabudDeByaH prativiSizwAH catasraH / pratisamvidaH pratilaBate iti anuttaraH mahADArma kaTikaH Bavati
# brjod-pa # 'i gnas ni dgu pa'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni sa dgu par nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  rnam-pa # s so-so #  yang-dag-par #  rig-pa #  bzhi khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  rnyed-pa # s na bla-na-med-pa # 'i chos-chen-po #  brjod-pa #  yin no /
aBizeka avasTAH daSamyAm BUmO= iti / daSamyAm hi BUmO boDisattaH mArga nizWA gataH
# dbang-bskur-ba # 'i gnas ni bcu pa'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni sa bcu pa la byang-chub-sems-dpa'i-lam #  gyi mthar-phyin-pa # s na /
daSa diS lokaDAtu vyavasTitAnAm budDAnAm BagavatAm raSmINAm / aBizekeNa aBizicyate
# phyogs-bcu # 'i 'jig-rten-gyi-khams #  na rnam-pa # r bzhugs-pa # 'i sangs-rgyas #  bcom-ldan-'das #  rnams kyis 'od-zer #  dag gis mngon-pa # r dbang-bskur-ba # s dbang-bskur-ba # 'o /
prApti avasTA budDAnAm DarmakAyaH iti / sarva AvaraNa prahANAt tat pratipakzAna asra vaDa bIja pracayAt / ca ASraya parAvRttya AtmakaH sarva Darma vartyAna AlayaH iti budDAnAm / Darma kAyAH / tena Darma prativeDa nizWA aDigamanAt prApti avasTA iti ucyate
# phyin pa'i gnas ni sangs-rgyas #  rnams kyi chos kyi sku'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  spangs-pa #  dang de'i gnyen-po #  zag-pa-med-pa # 'i chos kyi sa-bon #  rab tu rgyas-pa # s gnas-gyur-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  chos-thams-cad #  la dbang-byed-pa #  / / kun-gzhi #  med-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  sangs-rgyas #  rnams kyi chos kyi sku'o / / des-na #  chos rtogs-par-bya-ba # 'i mthar-phyin-pa # s na phyin pa'i gnas zhes-bya'o #  /
anye tu niHSeza Agantuka mala apagamAt su viSudDaH DarmaDAtuH eva / DarmatA kAyaH DarmakAyaH iti varNayanti
# gzhan dag na re glo-bur-gyi-dri-ma #  ma-lus-par #  bstsal-ba # s chos-kyi-dbyings #  rab tu rnam-par-dag-pa #  nyid ni chos kyi sku yin-pas #  chos kyi sku'o zhes zer ro /
sarvasmin= api jQeye asakta apratihata pravRtti viSizwam jQAnam DarmakAya
# gzhan dag na re shes-bya-thams-cad #  la yang chags-pa-med-pa #  dang thogs-pa-med-pa # r 'jug-pa # 'i ye shes khyad-par-can #  ni chos kyi sku'o /
iti apare / anuSaMsA avasTA sAmBogikaH kAyaH iti / svABAvikaH yasmin kAye vyavasTite aBisambauDyate yena kAyena
# phan yon-gyi-gnas #  ni longs-spyod #  rdzogs-pa # 'i sku'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi sku ste / / sku gang-la #  bzhugs nas mngon-pa # r rdzogs-par-byang-chub #  ste /
nizWA gatEH boDisattvEH saha parzad maNXalena Darma saMgItim anuBavati / sa sAmBogikaH kAyaH
# sku de mthar-phyin-pa # 'i byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams dang lhan-cig-tu #  'khor-gyi-dkyil-'khor #  rnams ni chos kyi 'gro-ba #  myong-bar-'gyur-ba #  de ni longs-spyod #  rdzogs-pa # 'i sku'o /
kRtya nuzWAna avasTAH nirmANakAyaH iti / svABAvika kAya ASritaH sattva ASaya AlocanaH vineya arTam
# bya-ba-sgrub-pa # 'i gnas ni sprul pa'i sku'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi sku la brten-nas #  sems-can #  gyi bsam-pa #  la gzigs te /
prakriyA pravRttO= ananta praBedaH nErmANikaH kAyaH
# 'dul-ba # 'i phyir bya-ba #  la zhugs-pa #  dang rab-tu-dbye-ba #  mtha'-yas-pa #  ni sprul pa'i sku'o /
sarvA api ezA bahuviDA avasTA aBisamasya veditavyA / DarmaDAtO triDA punar iti / kaTam iti atas Aha / aSudDa SudDa SudDA ca viSudDA ca yaTArhataH iti
# gnas rnam-pa #  mang-po #  'di thams-cad #  kyang mdor-bsdu-na #  chos-kyi-dbyings #  la rnam-pa-gsum #  ste zhes-bya-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / ma dag ma dag dag-pa #  dang / / rnam-par-dag-pa #  ci-rigs #  sbyar /
tatra aSudDa avasTA hetu avasTAm upAdAya yAvat prayogAt iti p / hetu avatAra prayoga aDimukti avasTAH gRhyante / Asu avasTAsu Darma DAtoH aprahINa niravaSeza mala tvAt aSudDa avasTA iti / ucyate / aSudDa SudDa avasTA SEkzANAm iti / atra ca / Pala sakaraNIya viSeza uttara praveSa niryANa vyAkaraNa kaTikA aBizeka avasTA / gRhyante
# zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so / / de-la #  ma-dag-pa # 'i gnas ni rgyu'i-gnas #  nas nye-bar #  bzung-ste #  sbyor-ba # 'i bar-du # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgyu dang zhugs-pa #  dang sbyor-ba #  dang mos-pa'i-gnas #  rnams bzung ngo / / gnas de-dag #  ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  dri-ma #  ma-lus-par #  ma-spangs-pa # s na ma-dag-pa # 'i gnas zhes-bya'o #  / / ma-dag-pa #  dang dag-pa # 'i gnas ni slob-pa #  rnams so zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dir yang 'bras-bu # 'i khyad-par #  dang bcas-pa #  dang khyad-par-can #  dang bla-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  dang 'jug-pa #  dang nges-par-'byung-ba #  dang lung bstan-pa #  dang brjod-pa #  dang dbang-bskur-ba # 'i gnas rnams bzung-ste #  /
etAsu api avasTAsu Darma ADAtoH prahINa aprahINa kleSa tAm / upAdAya aSudDa SudDa avasTA iti ucyate
# gnas 'di dag na yang chos-kyi-dbyings #  la nyon-mongs-pa-spangs-pa #  dang ma-spangs-pa # 'i phyir ma-dag-pa #  dang dag-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
viSudDa avasTA SEkzANAm / iti akaraNIya viSezAn uttara prApti anuSaMsa AkRti anuzWAna avasTA / viSudDa avasTA iti ucyate aSEkzANAm niravaSeza kleSa prahANAt
# rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i gnas ni mi-slob-pa #  rnams so zhes-bya-ba #  ni bya-ba #  med-pa #  dang khyad-par-can #  dang bla-na-med-pa #  dang phyin pa dang phan yon dang bya-ba-sgrub-pa # 'i gnas rnams la rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i gnas zhes bya ste / / mi-slob-pa #  rnams ni nyon-mongs-pa #  ma-lus-par-spangs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
etAH ca avasTAH pRTagjana SEkzANAm vyavasTApyante
# gnas 'di dag ni so-so'i-skye-bo #  dang slob-pa #  dang mi-slob-pa #  rnams la rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
tezAm ca bahuDA vyavasTAnam kaTam vijQApanIyam iti atas Aha / pudgalANAm vyavasTAnam yaTAyogam atas matam iti / yaTAyogam iti yaTAsamBavam
# de-dag #  gi rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  rnam-pa #  mang-po #  de ji-ltar #  rnam-par-rig-pa # r bya zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / 'di-las #  ji-ltar #  'os 'os su / / gang-zag #  pa rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r 'dod / / ces bya-ba #  gsungs so / / 'di-las #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnas rab-tu-dbye-ba #  las zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / ji-ltar #  'os 'os su zhes-bya-ba #  ni ji-ltar-mthun-pa #  ste /
atas iti atas avasTA praBedAt iti arTaH / ayam gotra sTaH ayam avatIrNaH iti evam Adi / AditagrahaNAt ayam prayuktaH srotAapannaH sakRdAgAmI anAgAmI / arhan sa alaFkAraH boDisattvaH taTAgataH aDimukti cArI / SudDyA aDyASaya cArI niryAyI vyAkRtaH DArmikaTikaH aBiziktaH / boDi prAptaH BogI parArTa kRt iti / uktAH avasTAH / Pala prAptiH p / avasTAyAH Pala pUrvakatvAt avasTA anantaram Pala BAzaNa arTam / pRcCati Pala prAptiH katamet yatas Aha / BAjana tvam vipAka AKyam / iti vistaraH / tat idam samAsena paQcaviDam Palam BAjana tvam balam ruciH vRdDiH / viSudDiH ca iti / tatra BAjana tvam yaH kuSala anukUlaH vipAkaH iti
# 'di ni rigs-la-gnas-pa # 'o / / 'di ni zhugs-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / sogs-pa #  smos-pa # s ni 'di ni sbyor-ba # 'o / / rgyun-du-zhugs-pa # 'o / / lan-cig-phyir-'ong-ba # 'o / / phyir-mi-'ong-ba # 'o / / dgra-bcom-pa # 'o / / rgyan dang bcas-pa # 'o / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' # o / / de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # 'o / / mos-pas-spyod-pa # 'o / / lhag-pa'i-bsam-pa #  dag-pa #  la spyod-pa # 'o / / nges-par-'byung-ba # 'o / / lung-ston-pa # 'o / / chos-brjod-pa # 'o / / dbang-bskur-ba # 'o / / byang-chub #  thob-pa # 'o / / longs-spyod-pa # 'o / / gzhan-gyi-don #  mdzad-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  dag go / / gnas bshad-zin #  to / / gnas ni 'bras-bu # 'i sngon-du-'gro-ba # s gnas kyi 'og-tu #  'bras-bu #  bshad-pa # 'i phyir 'bras-bu #  thob-pa #  gang zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  / / snod gyur rnam-pa # r smin brjod dang / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so / / 'dir mdor-bsdu-na #  'bras-bu #  rnam-pa-lnga #  ste / / snod-du-gyur-pa #  dang stobs dang 'dod-pa #  dang 'phel-ba #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa # 'o /
sa punar azwa akzaNa prahANaH sa Asrava viSizwa zaXa AyatanaH / boDi pakza Darma vipAkaH sarva kuSala Darma utpatti ASraya tvAt BAjanam / ucyate / balam yAH BAjana tva ADipatyAt iti
# de-la #  snod-du-gyur-pa #  ni gang dge-ba #  dang rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-yang #  mi-khom-pa #  brgyad spangs-pa # 'i skye-mched-drug #  khyad-par-can #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  kyi chos kyi rnam-par-smin-pa #  ste / / dge-ba'i-chos #  thams-cad #  skye-ba # 'i gzhi-yin-pa # s snod ces bya'o /
ASraya kleSa upapattim anDa tAm upAdAya kuSala mUlasya aDimAtra tA / pRzwatA iti arTaH / idam ucyate balam
# stobs ni gang snod-du-gyur-pa # 'i dbang gis zhes-bya-ba #  ni lus-las #  nyon-mongs-pa #  skye-ba #  chung-ba # 'i phyir / / dge-ba #  shas-cher #  gyur-pa #  de rgyas-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / 'di ni stobs zhes-bya'o #  /
ruciH yA pUrva aByAsAt kuSale ruciH iti atItezu janmasu / kuSala Darma aByAsAt vartamAne janmani kuSala Darma aBiprAyaH / nadI srotaH nyAyena sA ruciH
# 'dod-pa #  ni gang sngon-goms-par-byas-pa # s dge-ba #  'dod-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'das-pa # 'i tshe-rabs #  rnams su dge-ba'i-chos #  goms-pa # 'i phyir / / da-ltar #  gyi tshe dge-ba'i-chos #  la sems-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni 'dod-pa # 'o /
vRdDiH yA pratyutpanna kuSala mUla Darma aByAsAt / apUrva viSizwa kuSala Darma utpattiH kuSala mUla paripuzwiH iti aBiprAyaH
# 'phel-ba #  ni gang da-ltar-byung-ba #  dge-ba'i-chos #  la goms-par-byas-pa # s sngon med-pa # 'i dge-ba'i-chos #  khyad-par-can #  skye-ba #  ste / / dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba rgyas-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba # r dgongs-pa # 'o /
trayam bala vRdDyoH viSezaH balam hi manda kuSala vipAka apekzyam dArXyam / vRdDiH punar kuSalasya uttara uttara viSezaH
# stobs dang 'phel-ba # 'i khyad-par #  ni 'di yin te / / stobs ni dge-ba #  chung-ngu # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  la yang lto sa nas mi-'gyur-ba # 'o / / 'phel-ba #  ni dge-ba #  rnams gong-nas-gong-du #  khyad-par-du-'gyur-ba # 'o /
anye punar kuSala mUla puzwiH iti viSizwa kuSala Darma vAsanA puzwiH / iha aBipreta iti manyante
# gzhan dag ni dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba rgyas zhes-bya-ba #  ni dge-ba'i-chos #  khyad-par-can #  gyi bag-chags #  la 'dir rgyas-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  snyam-du #  sems so /
viSUdDiH yadA AvaraNa prahANam iti / tatra SrAvaka budDa gotrANAm kleSa AvaraNa prahANam viSudDiH
# rnam-par-dag-pa #  ni gang sgrib-pa #  spangs-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-la #  nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas-kyi-rigs #  rnams ni nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  spangs-pa # s rnam-pa # r dag go /
sambudDa gotrANAm kleSa jQeya AvaraNa prahANam viSudDiH
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i rigs rnams kyi rnam-par-dag-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  spangs-pa # 'o /
etat yaTA arka mam paQcaviDam Palam iti / vipAka Palam yaH kuSala Darma anukUlaH vipAkaH
# 'di dag ni 'bras-bu #  rnam-pa-lnga #  dang go-rims #  bzhin te zhes-bya-ba #  la rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni gang dge-ba'i-chos #  dang mthun-par #  rnam-par-smin-pa # 'o /
aDipati Palam yA BAjana tva ADipatyAt kuSalasya aDimAtra tA
# bdag-po'i-'bras-bu #  ni gang snod-du-gyur-pa # 'i dbang gis dge-ba #  shas-cher #  gyur-pa # 'o /
nizyanda Palam yA pUrva aByAsAt kuSale ruciH
# rgyu-mthun-pa'i-'bras-bu #  ni gang sngon-goms-par-byas-pa # s dge-ba #  'dod-pa # 'o /
puruzakAra Palam yA pratyutpanna kuSala Darma aByAsAt kuSala mUla puzwiH
# skyes-bu #  byed-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni gang da-ltar-byung-ba #  na dge-ba'i-chos #  goms-par-byas-pa # s dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba rgyas-pa # 'o /
visaMyoga Palam yadA AvaraNa prahANam
# bral pa'i 'bras-bu #  ni gang sgrib-pa #  spangs-pa # 'o /
asya eva paQcaviDasya Palasya samAsa uktasya praBedaH samAsena nirdizwaH / uttara uttaram AdyaQca
# phyi-ma-phyi-ma #  thog-ma #  dang / / zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba # s ni 'bras-bu #  mdor bshad-pa #  lnga po nyid kyi rab-tu-dbye-ba #  mdor ston to /
iti vistaraH / uttara uttara Palam gotrAt citta utpAdaH citta utpAdAt prayogaH iti evamAdi / yaTA uktayA avasTA paramparayA veditavyam
# phyi-ma-phyi-ma #  'bras-bu #  ni rigs las sems-bskyed-pa #  dang sems-bskyed-pa #  las sbyor-ba #  dang de-lta-bu #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / gnas gcig-nas-gcig-tu #  brgyud-pa #  zhes ji-skad-du #  bshad-pa # s / / rig-par-bya # 'o /
Adi Palam praTamatas loka uttara Darma pratilamBa p / iti darSana mArga prAptiH
# thog-ma # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni dang-por #  'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i chos-thob-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / mthong-ba'i-lam #  thob-pa # 'o /
aByAsa Palam pareNa SEkza avasTAyAm iti
# goms-par-bya-ba # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni de'i-pha-rol #  slob-pa # 'i gnas so zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
darSana mArgAt pareNa SikzA avasTAyAm paQca pudgala praBAvitAyAm / sakRdAgAmi Palam anAgAmi PalaQca
# mthong-ba'i-lam #  phan chad slob-pa # 'i gnas la gang-zag #  lngas rab-tu-phye-ba #  lan-cig-phyir-'ong-ba # 'i 'bras-bu #  dang phyir-mi-'ong-ba # 'i 'bras-bu #  ste /
sa prayoga pRzWa BAva nAma arDa Atmaka tvAt aByAsa Palam
# sbyor-ba #  dang bcas-pa # 'i rjes la bsgom-pa'i-lam #  gyi rang-bzhin #  yin-pas #  na / / goms-par-byas-pa # 'i 'bras-bu # 'o /
samApti pahlam aSEkzA DarmA iti / te punar samyak
# rdzogs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni mi-slob-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  so zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
dRzwi saFkalpa vAc karmAntAjIva vyAyAma smRti samADi vimukti vimukti jQAna darSana AKyAH / sarva Pala paryanta avasTita tvAt samApti Palam iti ucyate / AnukRtya Palam upanizad BAvena uttarottara Palam eva veditavyam iti
# de-dag #  kyang yang-dag-pa'i-lta-ba #  dang rtog-pa #  dang ngag dang las-kyi-mtha' #  dang 'tsho-ba #  dang rtsol ba dang dran-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang rnam-par-grol-ba #  dang rnam-par-grol-ba # 'i ye-shes-mthong-ba # 'i zhes-bya-ba #  rnams te / / 'bras-bu #  thams-cad-kyi #  mtha' la gnas-pa # 'i phyir rdzogs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  zhes-bya'o #  /
upanizad BAvaH hetuH / tatra citta utpAdaH gotra anukUla tvAt citta utpAdaH Palam iti
# rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni rgyu dngos-po # s phyi-ma-phyi-ma # s 'bras-bu-nyid #  du rig-par-bya # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  sems-bskyed-pa #  ni rigs dang rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'i phyir sems-bskyed-pa #  ni 'bras-bu # 'o /
uttara uttara Pala AdInAm AnukUlya Pala AdInAm ca pRTak upadeSaH
# phyi-ma-phyi-ma #  'bras-bu #  la-sogs-pa #  dang rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  las /
yaTAkramam uddeSa nirdeSataH veditavyaH iti
# sogs-pa #  so-so # r smos-pa #  ni bstan-pa-dang-bshad-pa # r rim bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
vipakza Palam prahANa mArgaH yat eva Adi Palam
# mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi 'bras-bu #  ni spong-ba # 'i lam ste / / thog-ma # 'i 'bras-bu #  gang-yin-pa #  de nyid de /
vipakzaH eva Palam iti vipakza Palam prahANa mArgaH yena kleSeByaH / visaMyujyate
# mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  nyid 'bras-bu #  yin-pas #  na / / mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi 'bras-bu #  ste / / spong-ba # 'i lam des nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams dang 'bral lo /
Adi Palam yat pUrvam uktam praTamatas loka uttara Darma pratilamBaH iti
# thog-ma # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni gong-du #  bshad-pa # 'i thog-mar #  'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i chos-thob-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
vipakza SabdaH yadi api pratipakza vibanDana arTena AvaraNam ucyate atra tu
# mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi sgra ni gnyen-po # 'i gegs yin pa'i phyir / / sgrib-pa #  la byar zin-kyang #  /
vipakzaH pratipakzaH aBipretaH iti AvaraNa nirvAsa pakzaH vipakzaH iti vigrahAt
# 'dri ni mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  gnyen-po #  la bya-ba # r 'dod do / / sgrib-pa #  gzhom-pa # 'i phyogs yin-pas #  na / / gnyen-po #  zhes-bya-ba # r sbyor ro /
visaMyoga Palam aByAsa Palam samApti Palam ca kleSa visaMyogaH
# bral-ba'i-'bras-bu #  ni goms-par-byas-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  dang rdzogs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ste /
SEkzA SEkzANAm yaTAkramam iti / aByAsa Palam visaMyogaH sakRdAgAmi Pala pratipanna AdInAm paQcAnAm
# nyon-mongs-pa #  dang bral-ba #  ni slob-pa #  dang mi-slob-pa #  dang rim bzhin no zhes-bya-ba #  la goms-pa # s byas-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  bral-ba #  ni lan-cig-phyir-'ong-ba # 'i 'bras-bu #  la zhugs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  slob-pa #  lnga rnams te /
SEkzANAm Sizwa kleSa tvAt
# nyon-mongs-pa # 'i lhag-ma #  dang bcas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
samApti Palam visaMyogaH / aSEkzANAm parihANi Darma AdInAm zaNNAm api
# rdzogs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni yongs-su-nyams-pa # 'i chos-can #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mi-slob-pa #  rnams yin te /
trEDAtuka aSeza kleSa prahINa tvAt / pUrvam Bedena uktam idAnIm aBedena iti viSezaH
# de drug kyang khams-gsum #  gyi nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams ma-lus-par-spangs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gong-ma #  ni phye ste bshad-pa # 'o / / 'dir ni ma phye-ba #  ste khyad-par #  ro /
viSeza Palam aBijQA AdikaH guNa viSezaH iti / etat api aByAsa samApti Pala viSezaH eva veditavyam / kim kAraNam
# khyad-par #  gyi 'bras-bu #  ni mngon-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yon-tan #  gyi khyad-par #  ro zhes-bya-ba #  'di-la #  yang goms-par-byas-pa #  dang rdzogs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu # 'i khyad-par #  nyid-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
anAgAminAm arhatAm pratyekabudDAnAm boDisattvAnAm / taTAgata anAQca vESezika guNa lABasya vivakzita tvAt
# phyir-mi-'ong-ba #  rnams dang dgra-bcom-pa #  rnams yin te / / rang-sangs-rgyas #  rnams dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams dang de-bzhin-gshegs-pa #  rnams kyi yon-tan #  gyi khyad-par-can #  thob-pa #  brjod-pa # r 'dod-pa'i-phyir #  ro /
uttara Palam boDisattva BUmayaH
# bla-ma # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa'i-sa #  rnams te /
atra kAraNam Aha tat anyayA na uttara tvAt iti / boDisattva BUmayaH hi yadi api darSana BAva nAma arga Atmaka tvAt Adi Palam
# 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  / / de-ma-yin-pa # 'i theg-pa #  las bla-mar-gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba # 'o / / byang-chub-sems-dpa'i-sa #  rnams ni / / mthong-ba #  dang bsgom-pa'i-lam #  gyi rang-bzhin #  yin-pas #  /
aByAsa PalaQca taTA api SrAvaka pratyekabudDa yAna apekzayA
# thog-ma # 'i 'bras-bu #  dang goms-par-bya-ba # 'i 'bras-bu #  yin-du-zin #  kyang / / nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi theg-pa #  la ltos nas /
boDisattva BUminAm uttara Pala tvam nirvikalpa tvAt budDa gotraka tvAt
# rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  dang sangs-rgyas-kyi-rigs #  yin pa dang byang-chub-chen-po # 'i 'bras-bu #  yin-pas #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams ni bla-ma # 'i 'bras-bu #  yin par rig-par-bya # 'o /
mahA boDi Pala tvAt ca veditavyam / anuttara Palam budDa BUmiH iti
# bla-na-med-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni sangs-rgyas #  kyi sa'o zhes-bya-ba #  'di yang rdzogs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu-nyid #  yin-du-zin #  kyang /
etat api samApti Palam eva yatas sarva vAsanA kleSa upakleSa prahANAt / aklizwa ajQAna prahANAt ca tat uttara BUmi antara aBAvAt anuttara Palam / iti ucyate / etat anyat Palam samAsanirdeSataH vyAsataH tu aparimANam iti
# bag-chags-dang-bcas-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  thams-cad #  spangs-pa #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i mi-shes-pa #  spangs-pa # 'i phyir / / de'i gong-na #  gzhan med-pa # s bla-na-med-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  zhes-bya'o #  / / 'bras-bu #  gzhan 'di dag ni mdor bstan te / / rgyas-pa # r bya na dpag tu med do zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgyas-pa # r bya na /
vyAsataH SrAvaka pratyekabudDa boDisattva sambudDa PalAni / pratipAdyamAnAni aparimANAni Bavanti iti / pratipakza BAvanA piNxa arTaH p
# nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  dang yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa # 'i sangs-rgyas #  rnams kyi 'bras-bu #  rnams rab tu phye ste / / bshad na tshad-med-pa # r 'gyur ro /
pratipakza BAvanAyAH piNXa arTaH / vyutpatti BAvanA smRti upasTAna BAvanA catur Arya satya vyutpatti tvAt
# gnyen-po-bsgom-pa # 'i don bsdus-pa #  las byang-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir bsgom-pa #  ni / / dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  bsgom-pa #  ste; 'phags-pa'i-bden-pa-bzhi #  pa byang-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir ro /
nirleKa BAvanA samyakprahANa BAvanA akuSala DarmANAm nirleKAt / parikarma BAvanA RdDi pAda BAvanA tatra samADi parikarma karaNAt / paQca doza prahANAya azwa prahANa saMskAra AsevanAt
# bsrab-pa # 'i bsgom-pa #  ni yang-dag-par-spong-ba #  bsgom-pa #  ste / / mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  rnams bsrab-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yongs-su-sbyang-ba # r bya-ba # 'i bsgom-pa #  ni rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  bsgom-pa #  ste / / de-la #  ting-nge-'dzin #  yongs-su-sbyang-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir nyes-pa #  lnga spangs-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  brgyad brten-pa # 'i phyir ro /
uttara samAramBa BAvanA indriya BAvanA tasya
# gong-ma #  yang-dag-par #  brtsam pa'i bsgom-pa #  ni dbang-po #  bsgom-pa #  ste /
vimokza BAgIya kuSala mUla utpAdaka tvAt
# de ni thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba bskyed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
Slizwa BAvanA balA abala BAvanA darSana mArga SlezAt
# 'dre-ba # 'i bsgom-pa #  ni stobs bsgom-pa #  ste / / mthong-ba'i-lam #  dang 'dre-ba # 'i phyir ro /
pravizwa BAvanA boDyaFga BAvanA tatra tattva praveSAt / loka uttara Darma praveSAt Arya BUmi praveSAt vA
# zhugs-pa # 'i bsgom-pa #  ni byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  bsgom-pa #  ste / / der de-kho-na #  la zhugs-pa # 'i phyir ram / / 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i chos la zhugs-pa # 'i phyir ram /
utkRzwa BAvanA mArga BAvanA darSana mArgAt
# 'phags-pa'i-lam #  la zhugs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / mchog gi bsgom-pa #  ni lam bsgom-pa #  ste /
BAvanA mArgasya utkRzwa tvAt Adi BAvanA pRTagjana avasTAyAm / anukUla aviparyastA vA
# mthong-ba'i-lam #  pas bsgom-pa'i-lam #  mchog-tu-gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro / / thog-ma # 'i bsgom-pa #  ni / / so-so'i-skye-bo # 'i gnas-skabs #  te / / rjes su mthun la phyin-ci-log-pa # 'o /
maDya BAvanA SEkzya avasTAyAm aviparyastA viparyAsa sAnubanDA vA / paryavasAna BAvanA SEkzA avasTAyAm aviparyastA / viparyAsa niranubanDA
# bar-ma # 'i bsgom-pa #  ni slob-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  te / / phyin-ci-log #  med la phyin-ci-log #  rjes-su-'brel-ba # 'o / / mtha'i bsgom-pa #  ni mi-slob-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  te / / phyin-ci-log #  kyang med la phyin-ci-log #  rjes-su-'brel-ba #  yang med-pa # 'o /
sa uttarA BAvanA SrAvaka AdInAm
# bla-ma #  dang bcas-pa # 'i bsgom-pa #  ni nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
niruttarA ca BAvanA boDisattvAnAm yA
# bla-na-med-pa # 'i bsgom-pa #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi ste /
Alambana manaskAra prApti viSizwA iti / avasitaH BAvanAyAH piNXa arTaH / avasTAnAm piNXa arTaH / avasTAnAm piNXa arTaH / Bavya tA avasTA hetu avasTA / AramBa avasTA saha citta utpAdena prayogAt
# gang dmigs-pa #  dang yid-la-byed-pa #  dang thob-pa #  khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  zhes bstan-pa # 'o / / gnas-skabs #  rnams kyi don bsdus-pa #  ni skal-ba #  yod-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  ni rgyu'i-gnas #  skabs so / / rtsom pa'i gnas-skabs #  ni sems-bskyed-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i sbyor-ba # 'o /
aSudDa SudDa avasTA dve avasTe Pala avasTA sa karaNIyA avasTA ca p / viSudDa avasTA akaraNIya avasTA
# ma-dag-pa #  dang dag-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  ni gnas gnyis te / / 'bras-bu # 'i gnas dang bya-ba-dang-bcas-pa # 'i gnas so / / shin-tu #  dag-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  ni bya-ba #  med-pa # 'o gnas-skabs #  so /
sa alaFkAra avasTA viSeza avasTA / vyApti avasTA uttara avasTA
# rgyan dang bcas-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  ni khyad-par #  gyi gnas-skabs #  so / / khyad-par #  bya-ba # 'i gnas-skabs #  ni bla-ma'i-gnas #  skabs te /
boDisattvAnAm daSa BUmi vyApanAt vyApti avasTA iti ucyate
# byang-chub-sems-dpa'i-sa #  bcus khyab-pa # s na khyab-pa # r bya-ba # 'i gnas-skabs #  so zhes-bya'o #  /
anuttara avasTA ca budDAnAm BagavatAm tat uttara avasTA antara aBAvAt / sA ca prApti avasTA anuSaMsA avasTA kRtyA anuzWAna avasTA ca yAH / pUrvam uktAH / PalAnAm piNXa arTaH / PalAnAm piNXa arTaH saMgrahataH tad viSezataH pUrva aByAsataH / uttara uttara nirhArataH uddeSataH nirdeSataH ca iti / ezAm BAzya kAraH eva vyAKyAm karoti / tatra saMgrahataH vipAka Pala AdIni paQca PalAni tezu / sarva Pala saMgRhIta tvAt / tat viSezataH SezANi iti / tezAm eva paQcAnAm praBedaH SezANi uttara uttara PalAni veditavyAni / pUrva aByAsataH vipAka Palam iti / pUrva janma upacitAt kuSalAt pratyutpanna janmani vipAkaH / kuSala anukUla utpattiH iti atas uktam pUrva aByAsataH iti / uttara uttara nirhArataH tat anyAni catvAri iti / aDipati Palam nizyanda Palam puruzakAra Palam visaMyoga PalaQca / tatra vipAka nirhRtam balam / bala nirhRtA ruciH / ruCi nirhRtA vRdDiH / vRdDi nirhRtA viSudDiH / kecid AhuH uttarottara AKyAna praBAvita tvAt uttara uttara nirhRta tvam / iti ucyate / uddeSataH uttara uttara Pala AdIni catvAri iti / uttara uttara Palam Adi Palam aByAsa PalaMsam Apti PalaQca iti / nirdeSataH AnukUlya PlAdIni zax / tezAm eva caturNAm nirdeSAt iti

 ni bstan-pa-dang-bshad-pa # r rim bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi 'bras-bu #  ni spong-ba # 'i lam ste / / thog-ma # 'i 'bras-bu #  gang-yin-pa #  nyid mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  nyid 'bras-bu #  yin-pas #  na mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi 'bras-bu #  ste / / spong-ba # 'i lam des nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams dang 'bral lo / / thog-ma # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni gong-du #  bshad-pa #  thog-mar #  kyi theg-pa #  la ltos nas rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  dang sangs-rgyas-kyi-rigs #  yin pa dang byang-chub-chen-po #  'bras-bu #  la-sogs-pa #  'bras-bu #  lnga ste / / de-dag #  tu 'bras-bu #  thams-cad #  bsdus-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de'i bye-brag #  ni lhag-ma #  rnams so zhes-bya-ba #  la /
tatra anukUlya Palam uttara uttara Palasya nirdeSaH vipakza Palam Adi Palasya / nirdeSaH visaMyoga Palam aByAsa Palasya samApti Palasya ca nirdeSaH / viSeza Palam uttara Palam anuttara PalaQca samApti Palasya eva nirdeSaH / tatra eva sa alaFkArasya vivakzita tvAt / anye tu AhuH viSeza Palam aByAsa samApti PalayoH eva / nirdeSaH anAgAminaH api aBijQA Adi guNa saMBavAt / anuttara Palantu samApti Palasya nirdeSaH iti / Agama anusAriNyAm maDya anta viBAgawIkAyAm Arya sTiram ati aparat / itAyAm Pala nirdeSa UnAm caturTaH paricCedaH samAptaH / yAnAH anuttarya paricCedaH paQcamaH / triviDA anuttaryam nuttaryam / lakzaNa AvaraNa Adi zawpada arTa uddeSa anantaram yAnAnuttaryam uddizwam atas / tad nirdeSAt param yAnAn uttara nirdeSaH prakRtaH / atas Aha yAnAnuttaryam idAnIm vaktavyam / tat ucyate iti
# 'bras-bu #  lnga po de-dag-nyid #  kyi rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'o / / lhag-ma #  rnams ni phyi-ma-phyi-ma #  'bras-bu #  la-sogs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / sngon-goms-par-byas-pa #  ni rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu # 'i zhes-bya-ba #  ni sngon-gyi-tshe-rabs #  su dge-ba #  bsags-pa #  da-ltar #  gyi tshe la rnam-par-smin-pa #  ste / / dge-ba #  dang mthun-par #  skye-ba # s na / / de'i-phyir #  sngon-goms-par-byas-pa #  zhes bshad do / / gong-nas-gong-du #  sgrub-pa #  ni de-ma-yin-pa #  gzhan bzhi'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / bdag-po'i-'bras-bu #  dang rgyu-mthun-pa'i-'bras-bu #  dang skyes-bu #  byed-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  dang bral-ba'i-'bras-bu # 'o / / de-la #  rnam-par-smin-pa # s sgrub-pa #  ni stobs so / / stobs kyis sgrub-pa #  ni 'dod-pa # 'o / / 'dod-pa # s sgrub-pa #  ni 'phel-ba # 'o / / 'phel-ba # s sgrub-pa #  ni rnam-par-dag-pa #  pa'o; / / kha-cig #  na re gong-nas-gong-du #  bshad-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba # s na gong-nas-gong-du #  sgrub-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  zhe'o / / bstan-pa #  ni phyi-ma-phyi-ma #  'bras-bu #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhi'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni phyi-ma-phyi-ma #  'bras-bu #  dang thog-ma # 'i 'bras-bu #  dang goms-par-byas-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  dang rdzogs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu # 'o / / bshad-pa #  ni rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  la-sogs-pa #  drug ste / / bzhi-po #  de-dag-nyid #  bshad-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  / / rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni phyi-ma-phyi-ma #  'bras-bu # 'i bshad-pa # 'o / / mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi 'bras-bu #  ni / / thog-ma # 'i 'bras-bu # 'i bshad-pa # 'o / / bral-ba'i-'bras-bu #  ni goms-par-byas-pa #  dang rdzogs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu # 'i bshad-pa # 'o / / khyad-par #  gyi 'bras-bu #  dang bla-ma # 'i 'bras-bu #  dang bla-na-med-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni rdzogs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu-nyid #  kyi bshad-pa #  ste / / de-nyid-la #  rgyan dang bcas-pa # r brjod 'dod-pa'i-phyir #  ro / / kha-cig #  na re khyad-par #  gyi 'bras-bu #  ni goms-par-byas-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  dang rdzogs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  gnyis kyi bshad-pa #  ste / / phyir-mi-'ong-ba #  la yang mngon-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yon-tan #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / bla-na-med-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni rdzogs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu # 'i bshad-pa # 'o zhe'o / / bstan-bcos #  dbus dang mtha' rnam-par-'byed-pa #  las gnyen-po-bsgom-pa # 'i le'ur bcad-pa #  ste bzhi-pa # 'i 'grel bshad do / / mtshan-nyid #  la-sogs-pa #  dngos-po #  drug bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  theg-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  bstan-pa # s de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  theg-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  bshad-pa # 'i skabs su bab ste / / de'i-phyir #  / / de ni theg-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  bshad dgos-pa # s de brjod do zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
idAnIm iti lakzaNa Adizawka nirdeSa anantaram iti arTaH tat anantaram
# da-ni #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mtshan-nyid #  la-sogs-pa #  drug bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
uddizwa tvAt iti aBiprAyaH
# de-dag #  gi 'og-tu #  bshad-pa # 'i phyir ro snyam-du #  dgongs-pa # 'o /
aTa vA pratipad saBA vana avasTA Pala prAptayaH SrAvaka AdInAm / boDisattvEH sADAraNAH nirdizwAH
# yang-na #  gnyen-po-bsgom-pa #  dang gnas dang 'bras-bu #  thob-pa #  dag ni nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi thun mong yin par bshad do /
asADAraNa prasaFgena yAnAn uttaryantu boDisattvAnAm SrAvaka AdiBiH / asADAraNam iha ca prADAnyena ucyate iti pradarSayan= Aha
# thun-mong-ma-yin-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  su bab-pa # s na theg-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams dang nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # r thun mong ma yin te / / 'dir gtso bor bshad do zhes bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
yAna anuttaryam idAnIm vaktavyam tat ucyate iti
# da-ni #  theg-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  bshad dgos-pa # s de-la #  brjod do zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
na asmAt uttaram asti iti anuttarya SabdaH viSizwa tva prayAyaH / kim punar etat / mahAyAnam
# 'di-las #  gong-na-med-pa # s na bla-na-med-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ni khyad-par-du-'phags-pa # 'i rnam-grangs #  su gtogs-pa # 'o / / de-yang #  gang zhe na theg-pa-chen-po #  ste /
taTA hi SrAvaka pratyekabudDa yAnAByAm mahAyAnam viSizwam / na eva mahAyAnAt anyat viSizwataram asti
# ji-ltar #  nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi theg-pa #  dag las theg-pa-chen-po #  khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  de-ltar #  theg-pa-chen-po #  las ni khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  dam-pa #  gzhan med de /
tatra hetu PalayoH taratama BedAt / anuttarasya BAvaH Anuttaryam / kim punar tat iti atas Aha / Anuttarya prapattO hi / iti vistaraH / triviDam Anuttaryam mahAyAne iti / kim punar tat mahAyAnam / etat eva tRtayam pratipattiH Alambanam samudAgamaH ca
# de-la #  rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  gnyis shin-tu #  mchog-tu-gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro / / bla-na-med-pa # 'i dngos-po #  ni bla-na-med-pa #  nyid do / / de-yang #  gang zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  / / bla med nyid ni sgrub-pa #  dang / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so / / theg-pa-chen-po #  ni bla-na-med-pa #  nyid rnam-pa-gsum #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  la / / theg-pa-chen-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  de gang zhe na / / rnam-pa-gsum #  po de-dag-nyid #  de / / sgrub-pa #  dang dmigs-pa #  dang yang-dag-par-'grub-pa # 'o /
tatra pratipatteH anuttarya daSa pAramita anizpAdaka tvAt
# de-la #  sgrub-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  nyid ni pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bcu sgrub-par-byed-pa #  nyid de /
pAramitA nizpAdaka tve boDisattva pratipattiH Anuttaryam ucyate
# pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams sgrub-pa #  la byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi sgrub-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
Alambanasya punar pAramita AdayaH DarmAH DarmaDAtuH ca
# dmigs-pa #  ni pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  dang chos-kyi-dbyings #  te /
anena hi Alambanena boDisattvAnAm aSeza para arTa karaNa samarTA
# dmigs-pa #  'dis byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams gzhan-gyi-don #  ma-lus-par #  mdzad nus-pa # r 'gyur ro /
Bavanti iti atas parArTa karaNa sAmarTya hetu tvam Alambana anuttaryam / kim kAraNam
# de'i-phyir #  gzhan-gyi-don #  byed-nus-pa # 'i rgyu'i dmigs-pa #  ni dmigs-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  nyid do / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
tadvat tvAt tat Alambanam boDisattvAnAm anuttaryam ucyate
# de dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa #  de bla-na-med-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
samudAgamaH gotra aDimukti citta UrpAda AdInAm Palam
# yang-dag-par-grub-pa #  ni rigs dang mos-pa #  dang sems-bskyed-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rnams kyi 'bras-bu #  ste /
samudAgacCanti prApnuvanti gotra AdiByaH tat iti p / samudAgamaH
# de ni rigs la-sogs-pa #  las yang-dag-par-'grub-pa # r 'gyur / / 'thob-par-'gyur-ba # s na yang-dag-par-'grub-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
sa ca tatas anya viSizwa samudAgama aBAvAt anuttaraH iti ucyate
# de-yang #  de-la # s yang-dag-par-'grub-pa #  khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  gzhan med-pa # s na bla-na-med-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
tatas atra tasmAt samudAgamAt anuyaviSizwa aBAva vastu tvam Anuttaryam
# de-bas-na #  'dir yang-dag-par-'grub-pa #  de-la # s khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  gzhan med-pa # 'i dngos-po #  nyid bla-na-med-pa #  nyid do /
atra punar pratipattiH boDisattvAnAm sADAra saPalA ca mahAyAnam / iti uktam Bavati
# 'dir ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi sgrub-pa #  bzhi dang bcas-pa #  'bras-bu-dang-bcas-pa #  la theg-pa-chen-po #  zhes bshad-pa #  yin te /
etat ca triviDena anuttaryeNa anantara ukte na anuttaryam iti ucyate
# de-yang #  bla-na-med-pa #  nyid rnam-pa-gsum #  bshad ma-thag #  pas bla-na-med-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
aTa vA mahAyAnam sarva vikalpa paQca vigatam jQAnam sa samprayogam
# yang-na #  theg-pa-chen-po #  ni rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i spros-pa #  thams-cad #  dang bral-ba # 'i ye shes mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  tshogs dang bcas-pa #  /
sa samBAram sa prayogam sa pRzWa labDa jQAnam sa viSizwa guNam sAla lambanam / sa PalaQca
# sbyor-ba #  dang bcas-pa #  / / rjes-las-thob-pa # 'i ye shes dang bcas-pa #  / / khyad-par-can #  gyi yon-tan #  dang bcas-pa #  / / dmigs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  / / 'bras-bu-dang-bcas-pa # 'o /
tatra Alambanam taTatA
# de-la #  dmigs-pa #  ni de-bzhin-nyid #  do /
Palam apratizWitam nirvANam iti / asya ca mahAyAnasya aBiDAyikA yA sUtra Adi deSanA api mahAyAnam / Bavanti iti granTaH api aDikAraH iva upacaryate / yaTA kaMsa vaDAH maNi haraNaQca / tat ca saptaviDa mahat tva yogAt mahat / yAnti anena prApnuvanti apratizWitam nirvANam iti yAnam
# 'bras-bu #  ni mi-gnas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'o / / theg-pa-chen-po #  'di ston-pa # 'i mdo-sde #  la-sogs-pa #  bshad-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  kyang theg-pa-chen-po #  yin no / / tshig kyang gzhi dang 'dra-bar #  gdags te / / dper-na #  khar-ba #  bsad-pa #  dang rin-po-che #  phrogs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o / / 'dis theg chen mi-gnas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  thob-par-byed-pa # s theg-pa # 'o / / de-yang #  chen-po #  rnam-pa #  bdun dang ldan-pa # s na chen-po # 'o / / de ni theg-pa #  yang yin la chen-po #  yang yin-pas #  theg-pa-chen-po # 'o /
saptaviDam punar mahat tvam / Alambana pratipatti jQAna vIrya upAya prApti karma mahat tvam
# chen-po #  rnam-pa #  bdun ni dmigs-pa #  dang sgrub-pa #  dang ye shes dang brtson 'grus dang thabs-mkhas-pa #  dang 'thob-pa #  dang las chen-po # 'o /
tatra Alambana mahat tvam Sata sAhasrikA Adi ananta sUtra Darma AlambanAt / boDisattva mArgasya
# de-la #  dmigs-pa #  chen-po #  ni stong phrag brgya pa la-sogs-pa #  mdo-sde #  mtha'-yas-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  byang-chub-sems-dpa'i-lam #  gyi dmigs-pa #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
pratipatti mahat tvam sakala sva para arTa pratipattitaH
# sgrub-pa #  chen-po #  ni bdag-dang-gzhan-gyi-don #  mtha'-dag #  sgrub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
jQAna mahat tvam pudgala Darma nErAtmya jQAnAt
# ye shes chen-po #  ni gang-zag #  dang chos-la-bdag-med-pa # r shes-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vIrya mahat tvam trizu kalpa saMKyeyezu aneka duzkara Sata sahasra prayogAt
# brtson 'grus chen-po #  ni bskal-ba #  grangs-med-pa #  gsum du bya-dka'-ba #  brgya stong phrag du-ma #  la sbyor-ba # 'i phyir ro /
upAya kOSalya mahat tvam saMsAra nirvANa pratizWAnAt
# thabs-mkhas-pa #  chen-po #  ni 'khor-ba #  dang mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la mi-gnas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
prAptim ahat tvam / bala vESAradya AveNika udDa Darma Adi prameya saMKyeya guNa aDigamAt
# 'thob-pa #  chen-po #  ni stobs dang mi-'jigs-pa #  dang sangs-rgyas-kyi-chos #  ma-'dres-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yon-tan #  dpag-tu-med-pa #  grangs-med-pa #  'thob-pa # 'i phyir ro /
karma mahat tvam yAvat saMsAraH tAvat boDi aBisandanena / budDa kArya anuzWAnAt
# lam chen-po #  ni 'khor-ba #  ji-srid-pa #  de srid du byang-chub #  mngon-pa # r ston-pa # s sangs-rgyas-kyi-mdzad-pa #  sgrub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
etat eva mahAyAnam anuttaram tat anyasya viSizwayAnasya aBAvAt / tad aBAvaH Anuttaryam
# 'di dag nyid ni theg-pa-chen-po #  bla-na-med-pa #  ste / / de-la # s theg-pa #  khyad-par-can #  gzhan med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tat punar pratipatti Alambana samudAgamAH
# de-yang #  sgrub-pa #  dang dmigs-pa #  dang yang-dag-par-'grub-pa #  ste /
taTA hi tad yogAt mahAyAnam anuttaram ucyate
# 'di-ltar #  de-dag #  dang ldan-pa # s na theg-pa-chen-po #  bla-na-med-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
pratipattiH eva anuttaryam pratipattyAni uttaryam
# sgrub-pa #  nyid bla-na-med-pa #  yin-pas #  sgrub-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  nyid de /
evam Alambana anuttaryam samudAgamAnuttaryaQca veditavyam / etat Anuttaryam yaTAkramam boDisattva mArgam tat aDizWAnam tat / Pala QcA aDikRtya vyavasTApyate
# de-bzhin-du #  dmigs-pa #  dang yang-dag-par-'grub-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  nyid kyang rig-par-bya # 'o / / bla-na-med-pa #  nyid de-dag #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa'i-lam #  dang de'i-gnas #  dang de'i 'bras-bu # 'i dbang-du-byas-te #  / / go-rims-bzhin-du #  rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
etAvat ca budDa vacanena ucyate yat uta pratipattiH Alambanam tat / PalaQca iti / pratipattyA anuttaryam / Alambana pUrvikA pratipattiH iti Alambana pUrva nirdeSanayena pratipattiH
# 'di-lta-ste #  / / sangs-rgyas-kyi-gsung-rab #  kyis kyang sgrub-pa #  dang dmigs-pa #  dang de'i 'bras-bu #  dang 'di rnams tsam zhig bshad-pa # r zad do / / dmigs-pa #  ni sgrub-pa # 'i sngon-du-'gro-ba # s dmigs-pa #  sngar bshad-pa # 'i rigs-pa #  las /
pUrvam uktAH boDisattvAnAm pratipatti sAratA nandana arTam / tatra kaTam pratipattyA anuttaryam iti atas Aha pratipattyAni uttaryam
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams la sgrub-pa #  snying-po # r bya-ba #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir sgrub-pa #  sngar bshad do / / de-la #  ji-ltar #  na sgrub-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  nyid ces bya zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  /
daSa pAramitA pratipattitaH veditavyam iti
# sgrub-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  ni pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bcu la sgrub-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
pAramitA pratipattiH p / pAramitAnuzWAnam
# pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams sgrub-pa #  ni pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams la nan-tan-byed-pa # 'o /
sA ca pAramitA pratipattiH mahAyAne eva nirdizwA na anyatra yAne iti / mahAyAnam eva anuttaram iti darSayati
# pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  sgrub-pa #  de-yang #  theg-pa-chen-po #  nyid-du #  bshad kyi; gzhan ni ma-yin-pa # s na theg-pa-chen-po #  nyid bla-na-med-pa # r ston to /
sA ca pratipattiH yiaH prakArEH pAramitAsu prayujyamAnasya anuttarA / Bavati tAn prakArAn darSayan= Aha
# sgrub-pa #  de-yang #  rnam-pa #  gang-gis #  pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams la sbyor-ba #  ni bla-na-med-pa # r 'gyur-ba'i-rnam-pa #  de-dag #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
pratipattiH tu zaXviDA / iti / paramA pratipattiH
# sgrub-pa #  dag ni rnam drug ste / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so /
sA ca pAramitA pratipattiH na vijQAyate kaTam paramA yAvat kaTam
# pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams la sgrub-pa #  ji-ltar #  na dam-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  nas / / ji-ltar #  na khyad-par-can #  med-pa # 'i bar-du #  'gyur-ba #  mi shes-nas #  /
aviSizwA iti atas Aha tatra paramA dvAdaSa AtmikA iti
# de'i-phyir #  de-la #  /
dvAdaSa prakArA paramA mahatI niruttarA iti arTaH / tat prakAra pradarSana arTam Aha / OdAryam AyatattvaQca p / iti vistaraH
# dam-pa #  bcu gnyis bdag-nyid #  de / / zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / dam-pa #  ni rnam-pa-bcu #  gnyis te / / che-ba #  dang bla na med ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / de'i rnam-pa #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / rgya-che-ba #  dang yun-ring #  dang / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
OdArya parama tA yAvat nizpatti parama tA iti ezA dvAdaSa viDA parama tA
# rgya-che-ba #  dam-pa #  nas 'grub-pa #  dam-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  rnam-pa-bcu #  gnyis-pa #  de-dag #  ni dam-pa # 'o /
tatra OdArya parama tA sarva lOkika sampatti anarTaka tvena utkRzwa tayA ca / veditavyA / sampattiH aByudayaH sa ca dviDA AkAraH prAptaH ca aprAptaH ca
# de-la #  rgya-cher #  dam-pa #  ni 'jig-rten #  gyi phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  thams-cad #  mi-'dod-pa #  dang mchog-tu #  rig-par-bya # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la / / phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mngon-par-mtho-ba # 'o / / de-yang #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  te /
tatra prApte na sajjate aprAptam na prArTayati / sva suKa nirapekza para duHKa apanaya prayukta tvAt / yaTA uktam
# rnyed-pa #  dang ma-rnyed-pa # 'o / / de-la #  bdag-gi-bde-ba #  la mi-chags-pa #  dang gzhan gyi sdug-bsngal-ba-bsal-ba # r zhugs-pa # 'i phyir rnyed-pa #  la mi chags shing ma-rnyed-pa #  mi 'tshol-ba # 'o / / ji-skad-du #  /
puNyam hi yat puNya PalaQca sADoH
# dge-ba #  khyod kyi bsod nams 'bras-bu #  gang /
sarva para arTam tava na Atma hetoH iti
# thams-cad #  gzhan-gyi-don #  te bdag-gi-don #  rgyur min / / zhes 'byung-ba #  lta-bu # 'o /
prahANa jQAna praBAva sampanna budDa tva pala tvAt utkRzwa tvam
# spong-ba #  dang ye shes dang mthu phun-sum-tshogs-pa # 'i sangs-rgyas #  nyid 'bras-bu #  yin pa'i phyir mchog go /
aTavA loke hi dviviDAH eva udAraH ucyate yaH sTUla lakzaH / pratyupakAra aprArTanaH ca
# yang-na #  'jig-rten #  na rgya-che-ba #  ni rnam-pa-gnyis #  su brjod de / / che-ba # r mngon-pa #  dang lan-du-phan-'dogs-pa #  mi-'dod-pa # 'o /
tasmAt boDisattvaH sarva loka sampattya prArTakaH api aDimAtrA aDimAtrAsu / ca dAna Adi pAramitAsu prayujyate iti tat pratipatteH OdAryam ucyate / Ayatat tva para matA Ayata tvena utkRzwatA
# de-ltar-na #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni 'jig-rten #  gyi phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  thams-cad #  mi 'dod kyang sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams la je bas je cher sbyor te / / de-bas-na #  de sgrub-pa #  rgya-che-ba #  nyid ces bya'o / / yun-ring-ba #  dam-pa #  ni yun-ring-ba # 'i phyir mchog ste /
Ayatat tvam punar dAna pAramitA Adizu Ayata aByAsaH / tat ca na jQAyate kiyaQciram iti atas Aha / vikalpa asaMKyeya pariBAvanAt iti
# yun-ring-ba #  nyid kyang sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la yun-ring-por #  goms-par-byed-pa # 'o / / de-yang #  dus ji-srid-pa #  mi shes-nas #  de'i-phyir #  / / bskal-ba #  grangs-med-pa #  gsum du yongs-su-bsgom-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
boDisattvAnAm hi dAna pAramitA Adi BAvanA / kalpa asaMKyeya traya paryavasAna tvAt atyanta mAya tA
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams ni sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bsgom-pa #  bskal-ba #  grangs-med-pa #  gsum gyi mthar-thug-pa # r byed-pa # s shin-tu #  yun-ring-ba #  yin no /
aDikAra parama tA sarva sattva arTa kriyA aDikArAt iti / boDisattvAnAm sva suKa nirapekzANAm dAna Adizu pravRttiH
# ched du bya-ba #  dam-pa #  ni sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi don-bya-ba # 'i ched kyi phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  la / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  bdag-gi-bde-ba #  la mi-chags-pa #  rnams ni /
sarva sattvAnAm hita suKa kriyAm aDikRtya iti atas aDikArataH paramA iti ucyate
# sems-can #  la phan-pa-dang-bde-ba # r bya-ba # 'i ched du sbyin-pa #  la zhugs-pa # s de'i-phyir #  ched du bya-ba #  dam-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
akzaya tva para matA akzaya tvena parama tA
# zad-mi-shes-pa #  dam-pa #  ni mi-zad-pa # 'i phyir dam-pa #  ste /
akzaya tvam punar kutas iti atas Aha mahAboDi pariNAmanayA atyantam / apryAdAnAt iti
# zad-mi-shes-pa #  gang zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  / / byang-chub-chen-po # r yongs-su-bsngos-pa # s / / gtan-du #  yongs-su-gtugs-pa # r mi-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
mahA boDi pariNAmitAH hi dAna AdayaH sarva upapatti Ayatanezu vipAka Palam / dattvA api na atyantam samucCidyante ASraya parAvRtti lakzaNasya
# byang-chub-chen-po # r yongs-su-bsngo-ba # 'i sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ni / / skye pa'i gnas-thams-cad #  du rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  byin yang gtan-du #  rgyun-chad-pa # r mi 'gyur te /
DarmakAyasya nizpAdanAt tasya ca akzayatva nirupADi Seze api nirvANe na
# gnas-gyur-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  chos kyi sku sgrub-pa #  dang de-yang #  mi-zad-pa # s phung-po # 'i lhag-ma #  med-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # r gtan-du #  yongs-su-gtugs-pa # r mi 'gyur gyi /
paryAdIyante SrAvaka Adi boDi pariNAmanayA tu nirupaDi Seze / nirvANa DAtO sarvaTA ASrayasya samucCedAt samucCidyante
# nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i byang-chub #  tu yongs-su-bsngos-pa #  ni phung-po #  lhag-ma #  med-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i dbyings su lus rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  rgyun-chad-pa # s rgyun-chad-pa # r 'gyur ro /
mahA boDi pariNAmanayA vA dAna AdIni akzayANi Bavanti / praBUta vipAka tvAt
# yang-na #  byang-chub-chen-po # r yongs-su-bsngo-ba # s sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  mi-zad-pa # r 'gyur te; rnam-par-smin-pa #  mang-ba # 'i phyir ro /
praBUtam api akzayam ucyate vipAka dAnena atyantam aparyAdAnAt na
# mang-ba #  la yang mi-zad-pa #  zhes bya ste / / rnam-par-smin-pa #  sbyin-pa # s gtan-du #  yongs-su-gtugs-pa # r mi-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
tu evam SrAvaka Adi pariNAmanAyAm akzaya tvam p
# nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i byang-chub #  tu yongs-su-bsngos-pa #  la ni de-ltar #  mi-zad-pa # r mi 'gyur ro /
aTavA satva arTam mahA boDi pariNAmitAni kuSala mUlAni boDisattvAnAm / sattva DAtu vat akzayANi Bavanti iti atas ca sattva DAtu vat na atyantam / paryAdIyante iti / nErantarya parama tA Atma para sama tA aDimokzAt sarva sattva dAna AdiBiH / pAramitA paripUraNAt iti / pramuditAyAm hi BUmO DarmaDAtoH sarvatra gArTO= aboDAt / boDisattvaH Atma para sama tAm aBimucyate / sa sva para sama tA aDimokzAt prahINa sva para vikalpaH sva dAna AdiBiH iva / para dAna AdiBiH api su mudita cittam laBate / tatas pratikzaNam pratimuhUrtam pratidivasam ca nirantaram / dAna Adi pAramitAH paripUryante iti / akRcCra tva para matA anumodanA mAtreNa para dAna AdInAm / pAramitA paripUraNAt iti / taTA boDisattvAH sattvAnAm dAna Adi kuSala mUlAni samuditena
# yang-na #  sems-can #  rnams kyi don-du #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba byang-chub-chen-po # r yongs-su-bsngos-pa #  dang sems-can-gyi-khams #  bzhin-du #  mi-zad-pa #  yin te / / de-bas-na #  sems-can-gyi-khams #  bzhin-du #  gtan-du #  yongs-su-gtugs-pa # r mi 'gyur ro / / rgyun-mi-'chad-pa #  dam-pa #  ni bdag-dang-gzhan #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  du mos-pa # 'i phyir te / / sems-can-thams-cad #  la sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / sa rab-tu-dga'-ba #  la byang-chub-sems #  dpas chos-kyi-dbyings #  kun du 'gro-ba # 'i don rtogs-pa # s bdag-dang-gzhan #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  du mos so / / de bdag-dang-gzhan #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  du mos-pa # 'i phyir bdag-dang-gzhan #  du rnam-par-rtog-pa #  spangs-pa # s / / rang-gi #  sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  gzhan gyi sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s kyang sems shin-tu #  dga'-ba #  thob po / / de-bas-na #  skad-cig #  re-re # 'am yud tsam re-re # 'am nyi-ma #  re-re # r yang rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  de'i sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r 'gyur ro / / tshogs med-pa #  dam-pa #  ni gzhan gyi sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la rjes-su-yi-rang-ba #  tsam gyis pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni ci nas kyang de-dag #  la rjes-su-yi-rang-ba #  tsam gyis sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  de-ltar #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams sems-can #  rnams kyi sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba rnams la rab-tu-dga'-ba # 'i yid kyis rjes-su-yi-rang-ba # r byed do /
manasA anumodayanti yaTA ezAm anumodanA mAtreNa dAna Adi pAramitAH / paripUryante iti / vitta tva para matA gagana gajaQja samADi AdiBiH dAna Adi paripUraNAt iti / boDisattvAH DarmaDAtu prativeDa BAvanayA gaganagaQja saMjQakam
# dbang 'byor-ba #  dam-pa #  ni nam-mkha' #  mdzod kyi ting-nge-'dzin #  la-sogs-pa # s sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams chos-kyi-dbyings #  rtogs-pa #  bsgom-pa # s; ting-nge-'dzin #  nam-mkha' #  mdzod ces bya-ba #  'thob ste /
samADim pratilaBante / tasya pratilamBAt sattvAnAm sarva aBiprAya paripUraNAt dAna pAramitAm
# de thob-pa # s sems-can #  rnams kyi bsam-pa #  thams-cad #  yongs-su-bskang-ba # 'i phyir sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r 'gyur te /
paripUrayanti / tad ADipatyena hi gaganam eva gaQjaH Bavati iti samADiH gagana gaQja
# de'i dbang gis nam-mkha' #  nyid mdzod dam yang-na #  nam-mkha' #  la mdzod 'cha' ba'i ting-nge-'dzin #  la nam-mkha' #  mdzod ces bya-ba # r brjod de /
iti aBiDIyate yasmAt tat RdDyA sarva upakaraNAni gaganAt jAyante
# 'di-ltar #  ting-nge-'dzin #  de'i mthus yo-byad #  thams-cad #  nam-mkha' #  las 'byung-ba # r 'gyur ro /
Adi Sabdena prajQApAramitA Adi sUtra paWitAnAm grahaNam
# sogs-pa # 'i sgras ni shes-rab #  kyi rol tu phyin pa la-sogs-pa #  mdo las 'byung-ba # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  rnams bsdu'o /
parigrahaNa parama tA nirvikalpa jQAna parigRhIta tvAt iti
# yongs-su-bzung-ba #  dam-pa #  ni / / rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyis yongs-su-bzung-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
boDisattvAnAm hi dApaka deya pratigrAhaka traya anupalamBAn nirvikalpam / jQAnam
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes ni sbyin-bdag #  dang sbyin-par-bya-ba #  dang len-pa #  gsum ni dmigs-pa # s rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes so /
evam yAvat jQAtR jQeya jQAna traya anupalamBAn nirvikalpam jQAnam
# de-bzhin-du #  shes-par-byed-pa #  dang shes-par-bya-ba #  dang shes-pa #  gsum gyis bar-du #  mi dmigs-pa # 'i phyir rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes te /
tena parameNa nirvikalpena jQAnena parigRhItA dAna Adi pratipattiH kaTam
# rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye-shes-dam-pa #  des yongs-su-gzung-ba # 'i sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  sgrub po /
tat anuparivartita tvAt tat Alambana tvAt ca iti atas paramA iti ucyate
# ji lta zhe na de'i rjes-su-'brang-ba #  dang de-la #  dmigs-pa # 'i phyir te / / de'i-phyir #  dam-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
AramBa parama tA aDimukti caryA BUmO= aDimAtrAyAm kzAntO= iti / praTama kalpa asaMKye yAnAm aDimukti caryA BUmiH iti ucyate / gotra mitra balena ca utpAdita boDi cittasya svaBAva traya muKena atyarTam
# rtsol ba dam-pa #  ni mos-pas-spyod-pa'i-sa #  la bzod-pa #  cher gyur-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la / / bskal-ba #  grangs-med-pa #  dang-po #  ni mos-pas-spyod-pa'i-sa #  zhes bya ste / / rigs dang bshes-gnyen #  gyi stobs kyis byang-chub #  tu sems bskyed nas /
sarva Darma nErAtmya aDimokzaH aDimAtrA kzAntiH aSradDi Adi vipakzEH / aparAjayaH iti
# ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum gyi sgo nas chos-thams-cad #  la bdag-med-pa # r shin-tu #  mos-pa # 'i bzod-pa #  che-ba #  ste / / ma-dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  mi mthu pa'i phyogs las rgyal-ba #  la bya'o /
sA hi boDisattvasya AramBa avasTA / tatas aDimAtrAyAm kzAntO= AramBa parama tA iti ucyate / pratilamBa parama tA praTamAyAm BUmO= iti / praTamAyAm hi BUmO Darma DAtoH sarvatra gatvA avaboDAt loka uttarAH / pAramitAH pratilaBate pUrvantu praTama BUmi prayoga saFgRhItAH
# de ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i rtsom pa'i dus te / / de'i-phyir #  bzod-pa-chen-po #  ni rtsom pa dam-pa #  zhes bya ste / / 'thob-pa #  dam-pa #  ni sa dang-po # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni sa dang-po #  la chos-kyi-dbyings #  kun du 'gro-ba #  rtogs-pa # s 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams 'thob po /
lOkikAH eva iti atas praTamAyAm BUmO pratilamBa parama tA iti ucyate / nizyanda parama tA tad anyAsu azwAsu iti
# sngar sa dang-po #  la sbyor-ba # s bsdus-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-pa #  nyid de / / de'i-phyir #  sa dang-po #  la 'thob-pa #  dam-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  rgyu-mthun-pa #  dam-pa #  ni de-ma-yin-pa #  gzhan brgyad po dag la'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
praTama BUmi pratilabDAnAm tat anyAsu azwAsu BUmizu / uttara uttara viSizwa pratilamBaH nizyandaH iti nizyanda parama tA
# de-ma-yin-pa #  gzhan sa brgyad po dag la gong-nas-gong-du #  khyad-par-thob-pa #  ni sa dang-po #  la thob-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams kyi rgyu-mthun-pa #  yin-pas #  rgyu-mthun-pa #  dam-pa # 'o /
aTavA aDimukti caryA BUmO pAramitA BAvanA balena / praTama BUmi pratilamBaH pratilamBa parama tA
# yang-na #  mos-pas-spyod-pa'i-sa #  la pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams bsgoms-pa # 'i stobs kyis sa dang-po #  'thob-pa #  ni 'thob-pa #  dam-pa #  ste /
praTamA hi BUmiH boDisattvAnAm darSana mArga saFgRhItA tat / praveSAt ca jAtO p / taTAgatasya utpannaH tat anukUla tad Atmaka Darma pratilamBAt iti
# sa dang-po #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi mthong-ba'i-lam #  du bsdus-pa #  der zhugs na / / de'i-bdag-nyid #  kyi chos rab tu thob-pa # 'i phyir / / de-bzhin-gshegs-pa'i-rigs #  su skyes-pa #  yin no zhes mdo las 'byung ngo /
sUtrapAWaH / pAramitA BAvanA balena pratilabDAyAH praTamAyA BUmeH avaSizwA / BUmayaH nizyanda tvAt nizyanda parama tA / aTavA praTama BUmi pratilabDAnAm pAramitAnAm azwO BU mayaH / nizyanda BUta tvAt nizyanda pramatA
# sa lhag-ma #  rnams pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams bsgom-pa'i-stobs #  kyis thob-pa # 'i sa dang-po # 'i rgyu-mthun-pa #  dam-pa # 'o / / yang-na #  sa brgyad po 'di dag ni sa dang-po #  la rab tu thob-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams kyi rgyun mthun-par #  gyur-pa # s rgyu-mthun-pa #  dam-pa # 'o /
nizpatti para matA daSamyAm BUmO tATAgatyAQca boDisattva nizpattyA / budDa nizpattyA ca
# 'grub-pa #  dam-pa #  ni sa bcu pa dang de-bzhin-gshegs-pa'i-sa #  la / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  'grub-pa #  dang sangs-rgyas #  'grub-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  la /
daSamyAm hi BUmO boDisattvaH sarva boDisattva caryA niryAtaH iti tatra / taTAgatEH yOvarAjye aBizicyate
# sa bcu pa la byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i spyod-pa #  thams-cad #  tshar phyin nas de-bzhin-gshegs-pa #  rnams kyi rgyal chab tu dbang bskur te /
acintya puNya jQAna samBAra paripUrNa tvAt sarva Darma vikalpa vigata tvAt / sarvaTA sva para arTa sampAdaka tvAt ca boDisattvAnAm vizpatti para matA
# bsod nams dang ye-shes-kyi-tshogs #  bsam-gyis-mi-khyab-pa #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa #  dang chos-thams-cad #  la rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang bral-ba #  dang rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  bdag-dang-gzhan-gyi-don #  sgrub-pa # 'i phyir /
tATAgatyAQca BUmO prahANa jQAna praBAva atiSaya lABAt BagavAn / sarvasya jagataH SAstA Bavati iti atas budDa parinizpattyA nizpattiH / kA punar iyam nizpattiH
# sa bcu pa la byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi 'grub-pa #  dam-pa # 'o / / spong-ba #  dang ye shes dang mthu khyad-par-can #  rnams thob-pa # 'i phyir bcom-ldan-'das #  ni 'gro-ba #  thams-cad-kyi #  ston-pa #  yin-pas #  de'i-phyir #  sangs-rgyas #  su 'grub-pa # s 'grub-pa # 'o / / 'grub-pa #  de-yang #  gang zhe na /
boDisattva DarmANAm budDa DarmANAQca sarva prakAra aBinirhAraH
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i chos-rnams #  dang sangs-rgyas-kyi-chos #  rnams rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  mngon-par-sgrub-pa # 'o /
aTavA pAramitAnAm SEkza BUmi saFgRhItAnAm prakarzaH daSamI BUmiH
# yang-na #  slob-pa # 'i sar bsdus-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams kyi phul-du-byung-ba #  ni sa bcu pa ste /
atas tasyAm boDisattva parinizpattiH / aSEkzaBum asi gRhItAnAm kAzWA budDa BUmiH
# de-bas-na #  de-la #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  yongs su 'grub po / / mi-slob-pa # 'i sar bsdus-pa #  rnams kyi phul-du-byung-ba #  ni sangs-rgyas #  kyi sa ste /
tasyAm BUmO pAramitAnAm SEkzA aBAvAt budDa parinizpattyA
# sa de na pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams la slob-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir / / sangs-rgyas #  su yongs-su-'grub-pa # s 'grub-pa #  ste /
parinizpattiH iti evam boDisattva parinizpattyA daSamyAm BUmO / tATAgati aQca budDa parinizpatti para matA veditavyA / tatas ca parama arTena daSa pAramitAH matAH iti / yatas ezA dvAdaSa viDA parama tA boDisattvAnAm dAna Adizu saMvidyate na
# de-ltar #  sa bcur byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i yongs-su-'grub-pa #  dang de-bzhin-gshegs-pa'i-sa # ngs rgyas yongs-su-grub-pa # s 'grub-pa #  dam-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / de'i-phyir #  dam-pa # 'i don-gyis-na #  / / pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bcur 'dod do zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'di-ltar #  dam-pa #  rnam-pa-bcu #  gnyis po 'di dag / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la yod kyi /
SrAvaka AdInAm dAna Adizu tatas param iti anena arTena boDisattvAnAm eva
# nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la ni med-pa #  de'i-phyir #  / / dam-pa #  zhes bya ste /
dAna AdayaH jQAna paryantAH daSa pAramitAH matAH iti nirukti nyAyena iti
# don 'dis byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams nyid kyi sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ye shes la thug-pa #  rnams nges-pa'i-tshig #  gi tshul-gyis #  pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bcu po dag tu ston to /
daSa pAramitAnAm yA pratipattiH sA punar parama tA iti ucyate
# de-bas-na #  pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams la sgrub-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de-yang #  dam-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
p / ekezAm iti yezAm pAramitAnAm nAma mAtram api na vyutpannam tezAm tat / nAma vyutpAdana arTam ucyate
# kha-cig #  ces bya-ba #  ni gang dag pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams kyi ming tsam yang mi-shes-pa #  de rnams la de-dag #  gi ming bstan-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir /
dAnam SIlam kzaMA vIryam DyAnam prajQA upAya tA
# sbyin dang tshul-khrims #  bzod brtson 'grus / / bsam-gtan #  dang ni shes-rab #  thabs /
praNidAnam balam jQAnam etAH pAramitAH daSa iti
# smon-lam #  stobs dang ye shes dang / / 'di dag pha rol phyin bcu'o / / zhes-bya-ba #  brjod de /
aDikAra parama tA sarva tattva arTa kriyA uddeSa Adi yuktam atas ayam praSnaH
# ched du bya-ba #  dam-pa #  ni sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi don-bya-ba # 'i ched kyi phyir ro zhes bshad-pa #  de'i-phyir #  /
kim AsAm pratyekam karma iti / atas Aha / anugrahaH aviDAtaH ca karma tasya ca marzaNam / iti vistaraH
# 'di dag gi so-so # 'i las ci zhe na zhes dris-pa #  de'i-phyir #  / / las ni rjes su 'dzin byed dang / / gnod mi byed dang de-la #  bzod / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
dAnena hi boDisattvaH sattvAn anugRhNAti iti / tatra pUjA anugraha kAFkzayA bAhya Atmika vastuni avadya tvAt
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i sbyin-pa # s ni sems-can #  rnams rjes su 'dzin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-la #  mchod-pa #  dang phan-gdags-pa # r 'dod-pa # s /
pratyupakAra vipAka Adi nirapekzaH yayA cetanayA parityajati / kAya vAc karmANi ca pratipAdayati idam boDisattvasya Amiza dAnam
# phyi dang nang-gi-dngos-po #  kha-na-ma-tho-ba #  med-pa # s lan-du-phan-'dogs-pa #  dang rnam-par-smin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la mi-lta-ba # r sems-pa #  gang-gis #  yongs su gtong zhing lus-dang-ngag-gi-las #  kyis kyang sgrub-pa #  'di ni / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i zang-zing-gi-sbyin-pa #  ste /
anena kzuD pipAsA Adi duHKa apanayanAt sattvAna anugRhNAti
# 'dis bkres-pa #  dang skom-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal #  sel-ba # s sems-can #  rnams rjes su 'dzin to /
sattvAn upaGAtakAnAm AjIva SAstra kalA nipuNAnAm karuNA pUrvakam / upadeSaH sugati mokza mArga upadeSaH ca Darma dAnam
# snying-rje #  sngon-du-btang-ste #  sems-can #  rnams la mi-gnod-pa # 'i 'tsho-ba #  dang bstan-bcos #  dang sgyu rtsal dang bzo rnams ston-pa #  dang bde-'gro #  dang thar-pa # 'i lam-ston-pa #  ni chos-kyi-sbyin-pa #  ste /
anenA api ajIvikA durgati saMsAra duHKa apanayanAt sattvAn anugRhNAti
# 'dis kyang 'tsho-ba-med-pa #  dang ngan-'gro #  'khor-ba'i-sdug-bsngal #  sel-ba # s sems-can #  rjes su 'dzin to /
rAja cOra dAyAda vyAla AdiBiH AGrAtAnAm teByaH vimokzaNam / aBaya dAnam
# rgyal-po #  dang chom-rkun #  dang bgo-skal-la-spyod-pa #  dang gcan-gzan #  la-sogs-pa # s zin-pa #  de-dag #  las thar-par-byed-pa #  ni mi-'jigs-pa #  sbyin-pa #  ste /
anena api jIva Boga putra dAra Adi vipad Baya apanayanAt sattvAn anugRhNAti iti / SIlena upaGAtam ezAm na karoti
# 'dis kyang srog dang longs-spyod #  dang bu-dang-chung-ma #  la-sogs-pa # s phongs-pa # 'i 'jigs-pa #  sel-ba # s sems-can #  rnams rjes su 'dzin to; /
sarva kAya vAc duScarita viratiH loka anuvRttyA ca pratizidDAt vihitasya ca / kAya vAc karmaNaH viratiH anuzWAnaQca SIlam
# tshul-khrims #  kyis ni de-dag #  la gnod-pa # r mi byed do zhes-bya-ba #  ni lus dang ngag gis nyes-par-spyod-pa #  thams-cad #  spyod-pa #  dang 'jig-rten-dang-mthun-pa # 'i bkag-pa #  dang bsgo-ba # s lus-dang-ngag-gi-las #  ldog cing sgrub-pa #  ni tshul-khrims #  te /
asmin SIle vyavasTAnAt sattvezu apakAram duzwa upasaMhAram jIvita hetoH / api svayam na karoti na api kArayati iti
# tshul-khrims #  de-la #  rnam-par-gnas-pa # s sems-can #  la gnod-pa #  dang mi-bde-ba # r sgrub-pa #  srog-gi-phyir #  yang bdag-nyid #  kyang mi byed cing gzhan la yang byed du mi-'jug-pa # 'o /
kzAntyA parEH kRtam upaGAtam marzayati iti / karuNA puraHsareNa cetasA sarva AkAra duHKa marzaNa aDivAsana AtmikA
# bzod-pa #  ni gzhan dag gis gnod-par-byas-pa #  la ji-mi-snyam-pa # r byed do zhes-bya-ba #  ni snying-rje'i-sems #  sngon-du #  btang-ba # s sdug-bsngal-gyi-rnam-pa #  thams-cad-la #  ji-mi-snyam-pa # r byed cing dang-du-len-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  bzod-pa #  ste /
kzAntiH / tena anvitEH hiMsA banDana tA AXana Adi kRtam upaGAtam marzayati / pratyapakArA samIhanAt / vIryeNa guNAn varDayati
# des gzhan dag gis gsod-pa #  dang 'ching-ba #  dang rdeg-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  byas-pa #  la slar gnod-pa #  mi-byed-pa # s ji-mi-snyam-pa # r byed-pa # 'o / / brtson 'grus kyis ni yon-tan #  rnams 'phel-ba # r byed do zhes-bya-ba #  ni sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i phyir spro-ba #  ni brtson 'grus te /
dAna AdIn aDikRtya utsAhaH vIryam / tena dAna Adi guNa aByAsAt viSizwa guNa nizpattiH vRdDiH
# des sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i yon-tan #  goms-par-byas-pa # s yon-tan #  khyad-par-du-'phags-pa # r 'grub-pa #  ni 'phel-ba # 'o /
DyAnena RdDi AdiBiH Avarjya avatArayati iti / Adi Sabdena citta paryAya jQAnam p / parigRhyate
# bsam-gtan #  gyis ni rdzu-'phrul #  la-sogs-pa # s mgu-bar-byas #  te 'dzud do zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgras ni / / sems-kyi-rnam-grangs #  shes-pa #  bsdu'o /
DyAnam samADiH cittasya ekAgra tA
# bsam-gtan #  ni ting-nge-'dzin #  la sems rtse gcig pa'o /
RdDiH AkASa gamana AdikA
# rdzu-'phrul #  ni nam-mkha' #  la 'gro-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
avatAraNam SAsana DarmatA pratipAdanam
# 'dzud-pa #  ni bstan-pa # 'i chos-nyid #  ston-pa #  ste /
DyAna PalAByAm hi RDyA deSanA prAtihAryAByAm AvarjitaH Sakyante / SAsana avatartum
# bsam-gtan-gyi-'bras-bu #  rdzu-'phrul #  dang kun-brjod-pa'i-cho-'phrul #  gnyis kyis mgu-bar-byas #  na bstan-pa #  la 'dzud nus-pa # r 'gyur ro /
prajQayA samyak avavAda dAnAt vimocanAt vimocayati
# shes-rab #  kyis ni yang-dag-pa # 'i gdams-ngag #  byin-pa # s rnam-par-grol-ba # r byed do zhes-bya-ba #  la /
sarva AkAra Darma pravicaya lakzaNA prajQA / tasyAH ca karma samyak avavAda dAnam kleSa prahANam / ca aviparIta anuSAsana pratibadDa mataH prajQayA samyak avavAda dAnAt / vimocayati
# shes-rab #  ni rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  chos rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do / / de'i las ni yang-dag-pa # 'i gdams-ngag #  sbyin-pa #  ste / / nyon-mongs-pa-spong-ba #  yang phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r rjes-su-bstan-pa #  la rag lus pa'o /
upAya kOSalya pAramitayA mahA boDi pariNAmanAt dAna AdIn akzayAn karoti / yasya Darmasya nizpattaye vivRdDaye prAptaye prahANAya vA yAH yuktiH / sa tatra upAyaH tatra kOSalyam vEcakzaNyam upAya kOSalyam
# de-bas-na #  shes-rab #  kyis yang-dag-pa # 'i gdams-ngag #  byin-pa # s rnam-par-grol-ba # r byed do / / thabs-la-mkhas-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # s ni / / byang-chub-chen-po # r yongs-su-bsngos-pa # s / / sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  mi-zad-pa # r byed do zhes-bya-ba #  ni chos gang 'grub-par-bya-ba #  dang rnam-par-'phel-ba # r bya-ba #  dang 'thob-pa # r bya-ba #  dang spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i phyir rigs-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni thabs yin no; / / de-la #  mkhas-pa #  ni thog tu phebs pa ste / / thabs-la-mkhas-pa # 'o /
tasya kRuta upacitAnAm dAna AdInAm maha boDi pariNAmanayA kzaya kAraNAm
# de'i las ni sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  byas-shing-bsags-pa #  rnams byang-chub-chen-po # r yongs-su-bsngos-pa # s mi-zad-pa # r byed-pa # 'o /
mahA boDi pariNAmanayA kuSala mUlAni mahA boDi vat akzayAni Bavanti iti
# byang-chub-chen-po # r yongs-su-bsngos-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba rnams ni byang-chub-chen-po #  bzhin-du #  mi-zad-pa # r 'gyur ro /
praNiDAna pAramitayA anukUla upapatti parigrahAt sarva janmasu / budDa utpAda ArAgaNataH dAna Adizu sadA pravartate / praNiDAnam anekaviDam prArTana Atmaka tvAt / kuSala anukUla upapatti prArTanam atra praNiDAnam aBipretam tasya janmani
# smon-lam #  gyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # s ni mthun-pa # 'i skye-ba #  yongs-su-'dzin-pa # s tshe-rabs-thams-cad-du #  sangs-rgyas-'byung-ba #  mnyes-pa # r byed cing sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la rtag-tu #  'jug go zhes-bya-ba #  la / / smon-lam #  ni rnam-pa-du-ma # r smon-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin mod kyi / / 'dir ni dge-ba #  dang mthun-pa # 'i skye-ba #  la smon-pa # s smon-lam #  du 'dod do /
janmani budDa utpAda ArAgaNataH dAna Adizu sadA pravartanam karma
# de'i las ni tshe-rabs #  tshe-rabs #  su sangs-rgyas-'byung-ba #  mnyam-pa # r byed-pa #  dang sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la rtag-tu #  'jug-pa # 'o /
bala pAramitayA pratisaMKyAna BAvanA balAByAm niyatam dAna Adizu / pravartate vipakzAn aBiBavAt iti / pratisaMKyAnam prajQA
# stobs kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # s ni so-sor-rtog-pa #  dang bsgom-pa'i-stobs #  gnyis kyis mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyis zil-gyis-mi-non-pa # 'i phyir sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la nges-par #  'jug go zhes-bya-ba #  la so-sor-rtog-pa #  ni shes-rab #  po /
BAvanA tu kuSala Darma aByAsaH / tat dvayam vipakzeNa anaBiBUtam balapAramitA iti ucyate
# bsgom-pa #  ni dge-ba'i-chos #  goms-par-byed-pa #  ste / / de gnyis la mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyis zil-gyis-mi-non-pa #  ni / / stobs kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
tasyAH kzaNa nEyamyena dAna Adizu pravRttiH karma
# de'i las ni skad-cig-re-re-la #  yang gdon-mi-za-bar #  sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la 'jug-pa # 'o /
niyata Sabdasya satata paryAya tvAt
# nges-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgras ni rgyun-mi-'chad-pa # 'i rnam-grangs #  so /
na hi pratisaMKyAna BAvanA balAt dAna Adi kuSalam vipakzeNa aBiBUyate / jQAna pAramitayA yaTA ruta Darma sammoha apagamAt / dAna Adi ADipateya Darma samBogaQca pratyanuBavati sattvAn= ca / paripAcayati iti / sarvasmin mahAyAna deSanA Darme yaTAruta sammoha vigata jQAnam / jQAna pAramitA
# so-sor-rtog-pa #  dang bsgom-pa'i-stobs #  dang ldan-pa # 'i sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dge-ba #  la mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  rnams kyis zil gyis mi non to / / ye shes kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # s ni / / chos la sgra ji bzhin-du #  rmongs-pa #  dang bral-ba # s / / sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dbang du mdzad-pa # 'i chos la longs-spyod-pa #  myong-ba #  dang sems-can #  rnams kyang yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed do zhes-bya-ba #  ni theg-pa-chen-po # 'i chos-bstan-pa #  thams-cad-la #  sgra ji bzhin-du #  rmongs-pa #  dang bral pa'i ye shes ni / / ye shes kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'o /
ayam punar yaTA ruta sammohaH kaH
# sgra ji bzhin-du #  rmongs-pa #  de-yang #  gang zhe na /
yena aBiprAyikam arTam tyaktvA yaTArutam eva kalpayati ayam / yaTA ruta sammohaH
# gang-gis #  dgongs-pa'i-don #  spangs-te #  sgra ji bzhin nyid-du #  rtog-pa #  'di ni sgra ji bzhin-du #  rmongs-pa # 'o /
dAnam aDikRtya dAnam Alambya yaH sUtra AdikaH DarmaH deSitaH sa / dAna aDipateyaH / evam SIla kzAnti vIrya Adi ADipateyaH drazwavyaH / mahAyAnam AraBya
# sbyin-pa # 'i dbang du mdzad-pa #  ni sbyin-pa #  la dmigs nas / / mdo la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-bstan-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de sbyin-pa # 'i dbang du mdzad-pa # 'o / / tshul-khrims #  dang bzod-pa #  dang brtson 'grus la-sogs-pa # 'i dbang du mdzad-pa #  de-yang #  de-bzhin-du #  blta-bar-bya # 'o / / sangs-rgyas #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi theg-pa-chen-po #  las brtsams te /
budDa boDisattvena aviparIta sAMkaTya viniScaya kAraNAt sattvAnAm / ca aviparItayA Darma deSanayA paripAcanAt DarmsamBoga anuBavanam / sattva paripAcanaQca jQAna pAramitAyAH karma
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  'brel-pa'i-gtam #  nges-par #  mdzad-pa #  dang sems-can #  rnams la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i chos-bstan-pa # s / / yongs-su-smin-pa # r mdzad-pa # s chos la longs-spyod-pa #  myong-ba #  dang sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r mdzad-pa #  ni / / ye shes kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i las te /
sUtra Adi Darma upadeSasya jQAna pAramitA praBAvita tvAt / manasikAra pratipattiH p
# mdo la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-bstan-pa #  ni / / ye shes kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
parama pratipatti nirdeSa anantaram manasikAra pratipattiH vaktavyA tatas
# dam bsgrub-pa #  bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  yid-la-byed-pa # 'i sgrub-pa #  brjod dgos te / / de'i-phyir #  /
pRcCati manasikAra pratipattiH katametyataH Aha / yaTAprajQaptitaH Darma mahAyAna manaskriyA / iti vistaraH
# yid-la-byed-pa #  sgrub-pa #  gang zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  / / theg-pa-chen-po #  ji-lta-bu # r / / chos-rnams #  btags-pa #  mdzad-pa #  dag / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
dAna AdIni aDikRtya iti dAna SIla kzAnti vIrya AdIni uddiSya
# sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dbang du mdzad nas zhes-bya-ba #  ni sbyin-pa #  dang tshul-khrims #  dang bzod-pa #  dang brtson 'grus la-sogs-pa # 'i ched kyi phyir ro /

# mdo la-sogs-pa #  ji-ltar #  btags-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis rnam-pa #  gang-gis #  sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dbang du mdzad de /

# mdo dang dbyangs kyis bsnyad-pa #  dang lung du bstan-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  gsungs-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  de-dag #  gi don dang tshig-'bru #  la sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur ba 'debs-pa #  med-pa # r yid-la-byed-pa #  ni yid-la-byed-pa #  sgrub-pa #  ste /
manasikAra pratipattiH na anyaTA iti mahAyAne iti na SrAvaka yAne

# mdo la-sogs-pa # 'i chos ji-ltar #  btags-pa #  rnams / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams sgrub-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa #  ni yid-la-byed-pa #  sgrub-pa # 'o /
SrAvakayAne dAna AdIni aDikRtya BAzitAnAm sUtra AdInAm
# nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa # r sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dbang du mdzad de /
manasikaraNam miTyA manasikAra pratipattiH sva arTa mAtra ASraya tvAt iti / jQApitam Bavati / te ca prAyeNa citta samatAm asaktim anunnatim anupalaMBaQca aDikRtya
# gsungs-pa # 'i mdo la-sogs-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa #  ni log-pa # r sgrub-pa #  ste / / rang-gi-don #  tsam la brten-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes bstan-pa #  yin no / / de-dag #  kyang phal-cher #  sems-snyoms-pa #  nyid dang mi-chags-pa #  dang ma khengs-pa #  dang mi dmigs-pa #  rnams kyi dbang du mdzad de gzhag-pa # 'o /
prajQaptAH iti / tatra eya citta samatA yA guNya guNinAm samam upakAra prArTanA
# de-la #  gang yon-tan-can #  dang yon-tan #  med-pa #  rnams la mtshungs-pa # r phan-'dogs-pa # r 'dod-pa #  'di ni sems-snyoms-pa #  nyid do /

# de-la #  gang srid-pa #  dang longs-spyod #  la 'dod-pa #  med-pa # r gzhan-gyi-don #  nyid-du #  sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la sbyor-ba #  'di ni mi-chags-pa # 'o /
tatra iyam anunnatiH yat dAna AdiBiH na AtmAnam manyate na parAn pariBavati

# de-la #  gang sbyin-pa #  dang sbyin-bdag #  dang len-pa #  rnams mi dmigs-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  'khor gsum yongs-su-dag-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  'di ni mi dmigs-pa # 'o /
aBIkzNam iti punar punar / Sruta cintA BAvanA mayyA prajQayA iti tatra Apta vacana prAmANya jaH niScayaH
# thos-pa #  dang bsams-pa #  dang bsgoms-pa-las-byung-ba # 'i shes-rab #  kyis zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  yid-ches-pa # 'i gsung-rab #  las skyes-pa # 'i nges-pa #  ni thos-pa-las-byung-ba # 'o /
Sruta mayI / yukti niDAna jaH cintAmayI / BAvanA jaH BAvanA mayI iti / sarvA hi pravRttiH pralArTam atas pRcCati sA tri prAkarayA
# rigs-pa #  dang nges-par-sems-pa #  las skyes-pa #  ni bsams-pa-las-byung-ba # 'i'o / / bsgoms-pa #  las skyes-pa #  ni bsgoms-pa-las-byung-ba # 'i'o / / rgyun-du #  zhes-bya-ba #  'di yang-dang-yang-du # 'o /
prajQayA manasikriyA kam guNam Avahati iti atas Aha / DAtu puzwyE praveSAya ca arTa sidDEH Bavati asO / DAtuH gotram bIjam / tasya puzwiH vRdDiH / DAtupuzwyA ca AyatyAm viSada maha prajQaH Bavati / tasya Srutasya arTam BAvena praviSati iti
# 'jug-pa #  thams-cad #  ni 'bras-bu # 'i phyir te / / de-bas-na #  shes-rab #  rnam-pa-gsum #  gyis yid-la-byed-pa #  de yon-tan #  ci-zhig #  byed ce na zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir # ; khams brtas byed dang 'jug byed dang / / de yi don rnams 'grub-pa # r 'gyur / / zhes gsungs so / / khams ni rigs dang sa-bon #  no / / de'i brtas-pa #  ni 'phel-ba # 'o / / khams-brtas-pa # s ni tshe-phyi-ma #  shes-rab #  che zhing gsal-ba # r 'gyur ro /
tasya sUtra Adikasya Sruta Darmasya arTe yukti bala utpAditayA cintAmayyA / prajQayA arTa sadBAvam ASayataH praviSati iti / BAvanA mayya arTa sidDim prApnoti / arTa sidDiH tattva aDigamaH
# thos-pa #  de'i don la snying-nas #  'jug-pa # r byed do zhes-bya-ba #  ni mdo la-sogs-pa # 'i chos thos-pa #  de'i don la rigs-pa # 'i stobs-skyed-pa # s / / bsams-pa-las-byung-ba # 'i shes-rab #  kyis don-yod-pa #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  la bsam-pa-thag-pa-nas #  'jug-pa # 'o / / bsgoms-pa-las-byung-ba #  ni don-'grub-pa # r 'gyur te zhes-bya-ba #  la / / don grub-pa #  ni de-kho-na #  khong-du-chud-pa # 'o /
kaTam iti atas Aha BUmi praveSa pariSoDanAt iti

smRti upasTAna Adi pariSudDyA hi BUmim praviSati iti atas
# dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yongs-su-dag-pa # s sa la 'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro /
smRti upasTAna AdiBiH eva BUmim praviSati iti nirdizwam
