praviSati iti arTaH
# sa la 'jug go zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
sA punar iyam manasikAra pratipattiH sa parivArA vijQeyA na kevalA / kaH tat parivAraH / Aha / saMyuktA Darma caritEH sA jQeyA daSaBiH punar iti
# yid-la-byed-pa #  sgrub-pa #  'di yang 'khor dang bcas-pa # r shes-pa # r bya ste / / 'ba'-zhig #  ni ma yin no / / de'i 'khor gang zhe na / / de ni chos spyod rnam bcu dang / / yang dag ldan-pa # r shes-pa # r bya / / zhes gsungs so /
parigRhItA veditavyA iti parivAritA iti arTaH / Darma AtmakAni Darma aDikArikANi p / vA caritAni Darma caritAni / tAni punar na jQAyante iti atas Aha katamat daSaDA Darma caritam iti
# yongs-su-zin-pa # r rig-par-bya-ba #  ste zhes bya ni kun nas bskor-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / chos kyi bdag-nyid #  du'am chos kyi ched du spyod-pa #  dag ni chos spyod-pa #  dag go / / de-dag #  kyang mi shes-nas #  / / de'i-phyir #  / / chos spyod rnam-pa-bcu #  gang zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  /

# sbyin-pa #  ni theg-pa-chen-po #  la zhugs-pa #  gzhan dag la yi-ge # r bris pa'i glegs-bam #  la-sogs-pa #  bsti stang du byas te sbyin-pa # 'o / / gzhan klog-pa #  la nyan-pa #  ni bsti stang du byas te nyan-pa # 'o /
mahatA gOraveNa svayam vAcanam

udgrahaNam mahatA prasAdena AtmasAt karaNam

# tshig dang don 'chad-pa #  ni 'bad-pa #  chen-po # s 'os-pa #  rnams la ston-par-byed-pa # 'o / / kha-ton #  du byed-pa #  ni blangs-pa # 'i phyir zhing goms-par-byed-pa # 'o / / sems-pa #  ni rigs-pa'i-don #  la de'i sgo nas spyod-pa # 'o / / bsgom-pa #  ni mnyam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i shes-rab #  kyis goms-par-byed-pa # 'o / / dang zhes-bya-ba #  ni bsdu-ba # 'i don to /
tatra leKanA pUjanA dAnam SravaNam iti eBiH caturBiH padEH kAya karma / pradarSitam
# de-la #  yi-ge # r 'dri-ba #  dang mchod-pa #  dang sbyin-pa #  dang nyan-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshig bzhi-po #  'di dag gis ni /
vAcanam udgrahaNam prakASanA svADyAyanam iti eBiH caturBiH padEH / vAc karma pradarSitam
# lus-kyi-las #  rab tu bstan to / / klog-pa #  dang len-pa #  dang 'chad-pa #  dang kha-ton #  du byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshig bzhi-po #  'di dag gis ni ngag-gi-las #  rab tu ston to /
cintanA BAvanA ca iti AByAm api manaH karma pradarSitam
# sems-pa #  dang sgom-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  de-dag #  gis ni yid-kyi-las #  rab tu ston to /
ameya puNya skanDam hi caritam tat daSa Atmakam / yat et daSa prakAram Darma caritam uktam tatas ekEkasmAt Darma carita AdyaH / puNya skanDa udBavaH na sa punar svayam pareNa vA pramAtum Sakyate
# spyod-pa #  de bcu'i bdag-nyid #  ni / / bsod nams phung-po #  dpag tu med / / gang chos la spyod-pa #  rnam-pa-bcu #  gsungs-pa #  de-la #  chos spyod-pa #  gcig las bsod nams kyi phung-po #  skye-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de-yang #  shin-tu-mang-ba # 'i phyir /
ati bahu tvAt iti kasmAt punar dAna SIla DyAna Adi Darma nirdeSe tulye
# bdag gam gzhan gyis tshod bzung-ba # r mi nus so / / sbyin-pa #  dang tshul-khrims #  dang bsam-gtan #  la-sogs-pa # 'i chos 'dra-bar #  bstan-pa #  las /
mahAyAnaH eva Darma caritam atyarTam mahAPalam deSyate sUtrezu na punar
# ci'i-phyir #  mdo dag las theg-pa-chen-po #  nyid kyi chos spyod-pa #  shin-tu #  'bras-bu-che-ba # r bstan gyi /
SrAvakayAne / sUtrezu Darma caritam mahA Palam deSyate iti sambaDyate
# nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa #  la ni ma yin zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  ni chos spyod-pa #  'bras-bu-che-ba # r bstan zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro /
dvAByAm kAraNAByAm iti mahA yAne Darma caritam atyarTam mahApalam / deSyate iti sambaDyate / katam AByAm iti atas Aha / viSezAt akzaya tvAt ca iti
# rnam-pa-gnyis #  kyi phyir te zhes-bya-ba #  ni theg-pa-chen-po # 'i chos spyod-pa #  'bras-bu #  shin-tu-che-ba # r bstan to zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro / / rnam-pa-gnyis #  pa gang zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  /
etat api na jQAyate iti atas pRcCati kaTam viSezAt kahtma akzaya tvAt / iti atas Aha / para anugrahataH aSamAt iti
# khyad-par #  phyir dang mi zad phyir / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so / / de nyid kyang mi shes-nas #  de'i-phyir #  khyad-par #  gyi phyir ni ji-lta-bu #  / / mi-zad-pa # 'i phyir ni ji-lta-bu #  zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  / / gzhan la phan 'dogs ma zhi phyir / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so /
mahAyAne hi boDisattvAnAm dAna Adi pratipattiH / sarva sattva arTa karaNa ekam deSyate
# theg-pa-chen-po # r ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyis sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  sgrub-pa # s sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi don-bya-ba # r ro gcig par bstan gyi /
SrAvaka yAne tu Atma arTa praDAna iti atas SrAvakAyAnAn mahAyAnam / para anugraha pravRtta tvAt viSizyate
# nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa #  las ni bdag-gi-don #  gtso bor bshad do / / de-bas-na #  nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa #  las theg-pa-chen-po #  gzhan-la-phan-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir khyad-par #  du 'phags te /
evam tAvat hetu samAKyAnataH SrAvaka yAnAt mahAyAnasya viSizwa tvam
# de-ltar #  rgyu brjod-pa # s nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa #  las theg-pa-chen-po #  khyad-par #  du 'phags so /
acintya puNya jQAna samBAra Palasya tri kAya saMgRhItasya yAvat lokaH
# bsod nams dang ye-shes-kyi-tshogs #  bsam-gyis-mi-khyab-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  sku gsum du bsdus-pa #  /
tAvat sattva hita kriyA pravRttasya nirupaDi Seze api nirvANa DAtO= / anuparatasya asra vaparA vRtti lakzaNasya dyotanAt akzaya tvam / na tu evam SrAvaka yAne
# 'jig-rten #  ji-srid #  du yod-pa #  de srid du sems-can #  la phan-pa # r mdzad-pa # r zhugs-pa #  / / phung-po # 'i lhag-ma #  med-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  na yang rgyun-mi-'chad-pa #  gnas-gyur-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  bstan-pa # s mi-zad-pa #  yin no /
SrAvaka samBAra Palam hi kzaya tvam AKyAtam nirupaDi Seza nirvRtAnAm / sarva AtmanA samucCedAt
# nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa #  ni de lta ma yin te / / nyan-thos #  kyi tshogs kyi 'bras-bu #  ni phung-po # 'i lhag-ma #  med-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  rgyun-mi-'chad-pa # 'i phyir zad-pa # r bshad do /
evam nirvANe api anuparatam Palam dyotanAt SrAvaka yAnAt mahAyAnam / viSizyate p
# de-ltar #  mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  na yang 'bras-bu #  rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  bstan-pa # s / / nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa #  las theg-pa-chen-po #  khyad-par #  du 'phags so /
aTavA mahAyAnasya arTaH dAna AdikaH sarva sattva anugraha pravRttaH na tu evam / SrAvakAna arTaH / SrAvakANAm sva arTa para tvAt
# yang-na #  theg-pa-chen-po # 'i don ni sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / sems-can-thams-cad #  la phan-gdags-pa # r zhugs-pa # 'o / / nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa # 'i don ni de lta ma yin te / / nyan-thos #  rnams rang-gi-don #  la brtson pa'i phyir ro /
dAna AdayaH ca boDisattvAnAm DarmAH anAsravakAya tvena parivRttAH / parinirvANe api na vicCidyante
# sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  dag gi chos-rnams #  zag-pa-med-pa # 'i lus su gyur-pa # s / / mya-ngan #  las 'das kyang rgyun 'chad-pa # r mi 'gyur gyi /
SrAvakANAn tu mArgasya kOlopama tvAt parinirvANe samucCidyate iti na
# nyan-thos #  rnams kyi lam ni gzings lta-bu #  yin-pas #  yongs su mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # r rgyun 'chad-pa # r 'gyur te /
tezAm akzaya tvam
# de-dag #  gis ni mi-zad-pa #  ma yin no /
tasmAt yuktam mahAyAnasA eva Darma caritam mahA Palam na SrAvaka yAnaH iti
# de-bas-na #  theg-pa-chen-po #  nyid kyi chos sbyor pa 'bras-bu-chen-po # r rigs kyi nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa #  ni ma yin no /
anuDarma pratipattiH / manasikAra pratipatti anantaram anuDarma pratipAtiH vaktavyAH iti atas / pRcCataH anuDarma pratipattiH katamet yatas Aha
# de-la #  yid-la-byed-pa #  sgrub-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  rjes-su-mthun-pa'i-chos #  sgrub-pa #  brjod-pa # r bya ste / / de'i-phyir #  rjes-su-mthun-pa'i-chos #  sgrub-pa #  gang zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  / / mi g-yeng phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r / / 'gyur-ba # r rjes-su-mthun-pa'i-chos #  /
avikziptA avAviparyAsa praNatA iva anuDArmikI iti / DyAta vyajQeya Darma anugatA anupravizwa SamaTa vipaSyanABO= AtmikA / pratipattiH anuDarmpratipattiH
# zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so / / bsam-gtan #  du bya-ba #  dang shes-par-bya-ba # 'i chos kyi rjes-su-song-ba #  rjes-su-zhugs-pa # 'i zhi-gnas-dang-lhag-mthong #  bsgoms-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  sgrub-pa #  ni / / rjes-su-mthun-pa'i-chos #  sgrub-pa # 'o /
tatra SamaTa BAvanA AtmikA avikziptA
# de-la #  zhi-gnas-bsgom-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  ni mi g-yeng ba'o /
vipaSyanA BAvanA AtmikA viparyAsa pariNatA
# lhag-mthong-bsgom-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  ni phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r gyur-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ste /
iyam dviviDA anuDarma pratipattiH / avikzepa pariNatA / ayam akAraH bahuzu arTezu vartate iti kahtam avivikzepta iti na vijQAyata
# 'di rnam gnyis ni rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'i cho sgrub-pa # 'o / / mi zhes-bya-ba #  ni don mang zhig tu yang bsnyegs-pa # s mi g-yeng ba zhes-bya-ba #  ji-lta-bu-yin-pa # r mi shes-nas #  /
iti atas Aha tatra zaXviDa vikzepa aBAvAt avikziptA iti / vikzepaH api na jQAyAte kaTam zaXviDaH iti atas Aha zaXviDaH vikzepaH
# de'i-phyir #  / / de-la #  g-yeng ba rnam-pa-drug #  med-pa # 'i phyir mi g-yeng ba'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / g-yeng ba rnam-pa-drug #  mi shes te / / ji-lta-bu #  zhig snyam pa la /
prakRti vikzepaH bahirDA vikzepaH iti vistaraH p
# de'i-phyir #  / / g-yeng ba rnam-pa-drug #  ni zhes rgya-cher #  smos so /
evam api praBeda mAtram darSitam na vikzepa svarUpam iti pRcCati saH eza
# de-ltar #  yang rab-tu-dbye-ba #  tsam zhig bstan gyi g-yeng ba'i rang-gi #  ngo bo ni ma bshad-pa # s na /
zaXviDaH vikzepaH kim lakzaNaH veditavyaH iti atas Aha
# g-yeng ba rnam-pa-drug-po #  'di dag gi mtshan-nyid #  ji-lta-bu # r rig-par-bya #  zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  /
vyutTAnam vizaye sAraH / iti vistaraH / DImatAH iti DaImAn boDisattvaH
# ldang dang yul la 'jug-pa #  dang / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so / / blo ldan zhes-bya-ba #  ni blo can te byang-chub-sems-dpa' # o /
tatra vyutTAnam samADitaH paQcaBiH vijQAna kAyEH iti
# de-la #  ldang-ba #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  lnga rnams kyi ting-nge-'dzin #  las ldang-ba #  ste / / zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
yadA hi samAhitasya punar paQcAnAm cakzuH Adi vijQAnAnAm anyatamat / ekam utpadyate tadA samADitaH vyutTitaH Bavati / ayaQca prakRti vikzepaH bahirmuKa pravRtta tvAt
# gang-gi-tshe #  mnyam-par-gzhag-pa #  la mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  lnga rnams las gang-yang-rung-ba #  gcig cig 'byung-ba #  de'i tshe ting-nge-'dzin #  las langs-pa # r gyur-pa #  'di ni ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi g-yeng ba ste /
paQcAnAm vijQAna kAyAnAm vikzepa Atmaka tvAt paQcaBiH
# phyi-rol-du #  bltas-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs lnga rnams g-yeng ba'i bdag-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir /
vijQAnakAyEH samADitaH vyutTAnam prakRti vikzepaH ucyate
# rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs lnga rnams kyis ting-nge-'dzin #  las ldang-ba # r gyur-pa # s na ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  g-yeng ba zhes-bya'o #  /
vizaye visAraH bahirDAvikzepaH iti
# yul la 'jug-pa #  ni phyi-rol-du #  g-yeng ba zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
yadA samAhitasya samADi AlambanAt akAmakasya Alambana antare
# kha-cig #  na re gang-gi-tshe #  mnyam-par-gzhag-pa #  ting-nge-'dzin #  la dmigs-pa #  las /
manaH vijQAnam pravartate tat Alambana antara saQcArAt bahirDAvikzepa / iti eke
# mi-'dod-bzhin-du #  dmigs-pa #  gzhan la yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  'jug-pa #  de'i tshe / / dmigs-pa #  gzhan la 'phos-pa # s phyi-rol-du #  g-yeng ba'o zhe'o /
samAhitasya samADi Alambanam hitvA manaH vijQAnasya / vizaya antara saQcAraH bahirDA vikzepaH iti apare
# gzhan na re mnyam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi dmigs-pa #  spangs-te #  / / yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  yul gzhan-du #  'phos-pa #  ni phyi-rol-du #  g-yeng ba'o zhe'o /
samADeH AsvAnadAm laya OdDatyam ca aDyAtma vikzepaH iti
# ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi ro myang-ba #  dang bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  ni nang gi g-yeng ba'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
yadi samAhitaH tam eva samADim tRzNA AdinA kleSena AsvAdayati tatas
# gal-te #  mnyam-par-gzhag-pa # s ting-nge-'dzin #  de-nyid-la #  sred-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  nyon-mongs-pa # s ro myangs na /
SudDakAt samADeH vikzepaH Bavati klizwa samADi prati upasTAnAt
# nyon mongs can gyi ting-nge-'dzin #  nye-bar-gnas-pa # 'i phyir-yang #  dag-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  de-la # s g-yeng bar 'gyur ro /
laya OdDatyaQca SamaTa vipaSya nAsam avAhinaH samADeH vikzepaH Bavati / asamAhi tattvAt ca AsvAda anala OdDatyAnAm
# bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  dag gis kyang zhi-gnas-dang-lhag-mthong #  mnyam-pa # r 'jug-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  las g-yeng bar 'gyur ro / / ro myang-ba #  dang bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa # s ting-nge-'dzin #  nyams-par-'gyur-ba # s na /
AsvAdana AdayaH aDyAtma vikzepaH iti ucyante / samBAvana aBisanDiH nimitta vikzepaH / DyAyyayam mahAtmA iti evam samBAvanA Atmani iti anena nimittena samADO / prayuktasya ASaya vilayatvA AlabDAt alabDAt vA kuSala pakzAt vikzepaH / nimittavikzepaH iti ucyate / atra eva kAraNam Aha tat nimittam kRtvA prayogAt iti
# ro myang-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni nang gi g-yeng ba'o / / yid-ches-pa # 'i bsam-pa #  ni mtshan-ma # 'i g-yeng ba ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / bdag la 'di ni bsam-gtan-pa #  ste / / che-ba'i-bdag-nyid-can #  no zhes de-ltar #  yid-ches-pa # r 'gyur ro snyam pa'i mtshan-ma #  des / / ting-nge-'dzin #  la brtson pa ni bsam-pa #  log-par-zhugs-pa # 'i phyir dge-ba'i-phyogs #  thob-pa # 'am / / ma-thob-pa #  las g-yeng bas mtshan-ma # 'i g-yeng ba zhes bya ste; 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  / / de-la #  mtshan-ma # r byas-na # s sbyor-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
jQAtu kAmatayA tam samBAvanA aBisanDiH nimittam kRtvA iti / samBAvana Atmani iti
# shes-kyi-khe #  'dod-pa # s yid-ches-pa # 'i bsam-pa #  de mtshan-ma # r byas-na # s bdag la yid-ches-pa # r 'gyur ro snyam ste /
samADi prayukta tvAt iti
# ting-nge-'dzin #  du zhugs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sa ahaFkara manaskAra tA dOzWulya vikzepaH iti / ASayena samADi guNa arTinaH api sAhaFkara manaskAraH asmin asamam / prayuktaH aham asmi DyAyI iti
# ngar-'dzin-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  ni gnas-ngan-len #  gyi g-yeng ba ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni snying-nas #  ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi yon-tan #  'dod kyang / / bdag ni bsam-gtan-pa # 'o zhes nga'o-snyam-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  dang ldan te /
tatas ca Atma utkarzam anyatra avajQAm karoti iti / kasmAt eza dOzWulya manaskAraH / iti atas Aha dOzWulya vaSena asmi mAnasam udAcArAt iti / etat uktam Bavati dOzWulya praBAvitaH vikzepaH dOzWulya vikzepaH iti / kim punar dOzWulyam / asmin avAsana aparipuzwiH tayA hi asmin samudAcarati iti / tad vaSena asmi mAnasam udAcArAt / satkAya dRzwiH dOzWulyam iti anye / hIna citta tvam manasikAra vikzepaH iti / aniyata SrAvaka Adi gotrasya p
# de'i-phyir #  / / bdag la ni bstod gzhan la ni khyad-du-gsod-pa # s na / / ngar-'dzin-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa # 'o / / ci'i-phyir #  'di-la #  gnas-ngan-len #  gyi yid-la-byed-pa #  zhes bya zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  / / gnas-ngan-len #  gyi dbang gis nga'o-snyam-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  kun-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / de ni 'di-skad-du #  / / g-yeng ba ni gnas-ngan-len #  gyis rab tu phye'o zhes ston-pa # r 'gyur ro / / gnas-ngan-len #  ci zhe na / / nga'o-snyam-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  gyi bag-chags #  yongs su brtas-pa #  ste / / des nga'o-snyam-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  kun du 'byung-ba # s / / de'i dbang gis nga'o-snyam-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  kun du 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / gzhan dag na re 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  ni gnas-ngan-len #  to zhe'o /
mahAyAna manasikAra prayuktasya samsara duHKa BIru tayA / sattva vipratipAna tvena akalyANa mitra nizevaNena ca tat / CrAvaka pratyekabudDa cittam utpadyate / tat cittam hInam sva arTa mAtra parAyaNa tvAt / tat SrAvaka pratyekabudDa cittam mahAyAna manasikAra vikzepaka tvAt / manasikAra vikzepaH kaTyate / atra eva kAraNam Aha hIna yAna manasikAra samudAcArAt iti / hIna yAnam SrAvaka pratyekabudDa yAnam
# dman-pa # 'i sems ni yid-la-byed-pa # 'i g-yeng ba ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rigs su ma-nges-pa #  theg-pa-chen-po #  yid-la-byed-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  'khor-ba'i-sdug-bsngal #  gyis skrag-pa #  dang sems-can #  log-par-zhugs-pa #  dang mi-dge-ba'i-bshes-gnyen #  gyis bsten-pa # s na nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi sems-bskyed-pa # r 'gyur te / / rang-gi-don #  tsam 'dzin-pa # 'i phyir de ni sems dman-pa # 'o / / nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi sems de ni / / theg-pa-chen-po #  yid-la-byed-pa #  las g-yeng bar byed-pa # s yid-la-byed-pa # 'i g-yeng ba zhes bya ste / / 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  / / theg-pa-dman-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa #  kun du 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba # 'o / / theg-pa-dman-pa #  ni nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi theg-pa #  ste /
Atma parinirvANa aDikAra pravRtta tvAt manasikAra samudAcAraH / mahAyAna manasikAreByaH vikzipati iti hInam cittam manasikAra vikzepaH iti / ucyate
# bdag yongs su mya-ngan-las-'da'-ba # r bya-ba # 'i ched du zhugs-pa #  dang yid-la-byed-pa # 'i g-yeng ba kun du 'byung-ba # 'i phyir theg-pa-chen-po #  yid-la-byed-pa #  las g-yeng bar byed-pa # s na / / dman-pa # 'i sems ni yid-la-byed-pa # 'i g-yeng ba zhes-bya'o #  /
evam iyam boDisattvasya zaXviDa vikzepa doza rahitA SamaTa aBAvanA / veditavyA
# de-ltar-na #  'di ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  g-yeng ba rnam-pa-drug #  gi skyon dang bral-ba # 'i zhi-gnas-bsgom-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
aviparyAsa pariNatA / evam avikziptena yaTA viparyAsa pariNatA anugDarma pratipattiH / BAvayitavyA taTA ucyate / aviparyAsa AtmanA pravRttA viparyAsa pariNatA
# de-ltar #  g-yeng ba med-pa # s ji-ltar #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r gyur-pa # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa'i-chos #  sgrub-pa #  bsgom-par-bya-ba #  de-ltar #  'chad de / / phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  du zhugs-pa #  ni phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r gyur-pa # 'o /
tatra yat yaTA vyavasTitam vastu taTA tatra jQAnam aviparyAsaH / tat vastuta punar na jQAyate kativiDe vastunItyate Aha
# de-la #  gang ji-ltar #  gnas-pa'i-gzhi #  de-la #  de-bzhin-du #  shes-pa #  ni phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ste / / gzhi de-yang #  rnam-pa #  du yod mi shes-nas #  / / de'i-phyir #  /
tatra aviparyAsaH daSaviDe vastuni veditavyaH iti / aviparyAsavaH tu pradarSana arTam bravIti yat uta p
# de-la #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni dngos-po #  rnam-pa-bcu # r rig-par-bya #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i gzhi bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / 'di-lta-ste #  /
vyaQjana arTa manaskArA visAre lakzaNa dvaye / iti vistaraH
# yi-ge #  don dang yid byed dang / / mi-'phro-ba #  dang mtshan-nyid #  gnyis / / zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
idAnIm tezu vastuzu yaTA viparyAsaH Bavati tat pradarSana arTam Aha / tatra / saMyogAt saMBavAt ca eva viyogAt api asamBavAt / arTa sattvam asat tvaQca vyaQjane saH aviparyayaH iti / saMyoge sati vyaQjanAnAm iti / saMyogaH hi paraspara saMSlezaH / na ca asO vyaQjanAnAm vidyate yOgapadyA aBAvAt / vyaQjanAnAm yugapad uccAraNam na yujyate / pUrva vikalpAnAm uttara vyaQjana uccaraNa kAle anavasTAnam / uccAraNa anantaram eva vinazwa tvAt iti ASaFkAvi udAsa arTam Aha / avicCinna uccAraNa tayA iti
# da-ni #  gzhi de-dag #  la ji-ltar #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r gyur-pa #  de bstan-pa # 'i phyir de-la #  / / 'brel-pa # 'i phyir dang 'dris phyir dang / / ma 'brel phyir dang ma 'dres phyir / / don-yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  ste / / de ni yi-ge # r ma-log-pa # 'o / / zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / yi-ge #  rnams 'brel te zhes-bya-ba #  la / / 'brel-pa #  ni phan tshun 'byar ba yin na / / cig-car-'byung-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir de-yang #  yi-ge #  rnams la med do / / yi-ge #  rnams la cig-car #  brjod du mi rung ste / / sngar brjod-pa #  rnams ni brjod ma-thag-tu #  zhig-pa # s yi-ge #  phyi-ma #  brjod-pa # 'i dus-su #  mi sdod do snyam pa'i dogs-pa #  bsal-ba # 'i phyir / / rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  brjod-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / de ni 'di-skad-du #  /
etat uktam Bavati aviparyasta avilambita uccAraNam atra vyaQjanAnAm / saMyogaH izyate na tu vyaQjanAnAm paraspara saMSlezaNam iti
# ma nor-ba #  dang ma thogs-pa # r brjod-pa #  la 'dir yi-ge #  rnams 'brel-pa # r 'dod kyi / / yi-ge #  rnams phan tshun 'byar ba ni ma yin no zhes bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro /
asya ca idam nAma iti samBavAt iti / yadi ca asya vastunaH idam nAma iti saFketaH aByastaH Bavati evam anena / prakAra dvayena sArTaka tvam vyaQjanAnAm pratyAyaka tvam iti arTaH
# 'di'i ming ni 'di zhes-bya'o #  zhes 'dris-pa # s zhes-bya-ba #  ni dngos-po #  'di'i ming 'di'o zhes brdal goms-pa # r gyur-pa #  ste / / de-ltar #  rnam-pa #  'di gnyis kyis yi-ge #  rnams don-yod-pa #  nyid-du #  khong-du-chud-pa # r byed do zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
viparyayAt nirarTaka tvam iti
# bzlog-pa #  ni don-med-pa #  nyid do zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnyi-ga #  med-pa # 'am /
uBaya aBAvaH anyatara vEkalyam vA viparyayaH / yat evam darSanam iti jQAnam
# gang-yang-rung-ba #  ma-tshang-ba-med-pa #  ni bzlog-pa # 'o / / de-ltar #  bzlog-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni shes-pa # 'o /
saH aviparyAsaH vyaQjane veditavyaH iti saMvRttyA na tu paramArTataH / paramArTena aviparyAsasya nirvikalpaka tvAt iti anena aviparyAsena
# de ni yi-ge #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni kun-rdzob #  yin gyi / / don-dam-pa # r ni ma yin te / / don-dam-pa # r ni phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
boDisattvaH Sabda arTa rahitAn sarva DarmAn prativiDyati / idAnIm vyaQjana prajQapti nimittaH arTe aviparyAsa pradarSana arTam Aha
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  'dis kyang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  sgra'i don dang bral-ba # 'i chos-thams-cad #  rtogs-pa # r 'gyur ro / / da-ni #  yi-ge # r 'dogs-pa # 'i rgyu'i don la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
dvayena pratiBAsa tvam taTA ca avidyamAna tA / iti vistaraH
# gnyis su snang-bar-gyur-pa #  ni / / de-ltar #  yod-pa #  ma yin te / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
dvayena grAhya grAhaka tvena pratiBAsate / kaH / paratantra svaBAvaH / kasmAt
# gnyis ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r snang-ba #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni gang zhig ce na / / gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  do / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
grAhya grAhaka bIja yukta tvAt
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i sa-bon-dang-ldan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kah punar atra pratiBAsa arTaH iti atas Aha tad AkAra utpattitaH iti / grAhya grAhaka AkAra utpatitaH grAhya grAhaka tvena pratiBAsate na punar / sPAwika vat upaDAna uparAgAt iti
# 'di-la #  snang-ba # 'i don gang zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  de'i rnam-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r 'byung-ba # s gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r snang gi / / shel sgong ltar nye-bar-gzhag-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  lta-bu #  ni ma yin no / / de-ltar #  yod-pa #  ma yin te /
taTA ca na vidyate yaTA pratiBAsate advaya prakRti tvAt / iti evam BrAnti vijQAna utpatti nimitta BUte arTe yat darSanam sa
# zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnyis po med-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  yin-pas #  ji-ltar #  snang-ba # 'i rnam-pa #  de-ltar #  med-pa # 'o / / de-ltar #  'khrul-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung-ba # 'i rgyur-gyur-pa # 'i phyir /
tatra aviparyAsaH sat asat sattva varjana Aditya aBiprAyaH / arTasya sattvena varjitaH iti atra eva kAraNam Aha
# don la mthong-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni de-la #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  spangs-pa # 'i phyir ro snyam-du #  dgongs-pa # 'o / / don gyi yod-pa #  spangs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la / / 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  /
grAhya grAhaka aBAvAt iti / arTasya sattvam p / grAhya grAhaka sadBAvaH
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i dngos-po-med-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba # 'o / / don gyi yod-pa #  ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  yod-pa # 'o /
tena varjitaH grAhya grAhaka AkAreNa SUnya tvAt iti
# de spangs-pa #  ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i rnam-pa # s stong-pa # 'i phyir ro /
asattvena varjitaH / kim kAraNam
# med-pa #  spangs-pa #  ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
tat pratiBAsa BrAnti sadBAvAt iti
# der-snang-ba # 'i 'khrul-pa-yod-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ste /
grAhya grAhaka pratiBAsa BrAnti sadBAvAt iti arTaH
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r snang-ba # 'i 'khrul-pa #  yod do zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
ayam api saMvRttA viparyAsaH ucyate na paramArTataH sa vikalpa tvAt
# 'di yang kun-rdzob #  tu phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  zhes bya'i don-dam-pa # r ni ma yin te / / rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anena aviparyAsa jQAnena boDisattvaH grAhya grAhaka svaBAva rahitAn / sarva DarmAn prativiDyati iti
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r shes-pa #  'dis byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  chos-thams-cad #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  dang bral-ba # r rab tu rtogs so /
idAnIm grAhya grAhaka praKyAna nimitte / AlayavijQAne aviparyAsa pradarSana arTam Aha / tad jalpa BAvitaH jalpam anaskAraH tad ASrayaH / iti vistaraH
# da-ni #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i rgyu kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / rtog-pa #  de yis bsgos-pa #  yi / / rtog-pa #  yid byed de'i-gnas #  ni / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
grAhya grAhaka jalpa pariBAvitaH jalpam askAraH iti / tasmin grAhya grAhaka praKyAna lakzaNe arTe ayam grAhyaH ayam grAhakaH iti
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r rtog-pa # s yongs-su-bsgos-pa #  ni rtog-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r snang-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyi don de-la #  'di ni gzung-ba # 'o /
vAc manoByAm yat aBilapanam sa jalpaH iti ucyate
# 'di ni 'dzin-pa # 'o zhes ngag dang yid kyis brjod-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni rtog-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
anena jalpena pariBAvitaH anAgatat jAtIya jalpa utpAdAya
# rtog-pa #  des yongs-su-bsgos-pa #  ni ma-'ongs-pa #  na / / rigs 'dra-ba # 'i rtog-pa #  bskyed-pa # 'i phyir /
bIja paripozaNam iti pariBAvitaH iti ucyate
# sa-bon #  yongs su brtas-par-byed-pa # s na bsgos-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
saH ayam jalpa pariBAvita tvAt jalpam anaskAraH iti AKyAyate kArye / kAraNa upacArAt
# de ni rtog-pa # 'i yongs-su-bsgos-pa # 'i phyir / / 'bras-bu #  la rgyu btags te rtog-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
jalpa vAsanA tu atra jalpaH
# rtog-pa # 'i bag-chags #  ni 'dir rtog-pa #  ste /
jalpaH atra asti iti ADAra ADeyayoH aBedam kRtvA ADAra Sabdasya vA / grahaNAt jalpamanaskAraH iti ucyate
# de-la #  rtog-pa #  yod-pa # s na rten dang brten-pa #  dbye-ba #  ma-byas-pa # 'i phyir ram / / yang-na #  rten gyi sgra ma smos-pa # 'i phyir rtog-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ste /
tasya grAhya grAhaka vikalpasya jalpa AKyasya bIja ADAra tvAt / punar ca jalpasya tat sanniSrayeNa utpAteH ASrayaH Bavati iti ayam / manaskAre aviparyAse iti aviparItam jQAnam iti arTaH / sa tu manaskAraH na vijNyAte yasmin= aviparyAsaH iti atas pRcCati katam
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  de'i sa-bon #  gyi rten-du-gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-la #  brten-nas #  yang rtog-pa #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / rten yin-pas #  'di ni yid-la-byed-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r shes-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / yid-la-byed-pa #  gang-la #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  de-yang #  mi shes-nas #  /
asmin manaskAre aviparyAse iti / atas manaskAra viSezaNa arTam Aha grAhya grAhaka sampraKyAna kAraNe
# yid-la-byed-pa #  gang-la #  phyin ci ma log ce na zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  yid-la-byed-pa # 'i khyad-par #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r snang-ba # 'i rgyu la ste zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
AlayavijQAna viSeza AtmakaH iti arTaH / yaTA asO grAhya grAhaka sampraKyAna kAraNam Bavati tat pradarSana arTam
# kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i khyad-par #  gyi bdag-nyid #  ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / ji-ltar #  'di gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r snang-ba # 'i rgyur-'gyur-ba #  de bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
Aha sa hi asO jalpam anaskAraH aBilApa saMjQA pariBAvita tvAt iti
# rtog-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa #  ni brjod-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  kyis yongs-su-bsgos-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
grAhya grAhaka praKyAna kAraNam Bavati iti sambaDyate
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r snang-ba # 'i rgyu yin no zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro /
aTavA jalpam anaskAraH iti atas aBiDAna pravRtti nimittam Aha
# yang-na #  rtog-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  zhes brjod-pa-'jug-pa # 'i rgyu yin par bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
aBilApa saMjQA pariBAvita tvAt jalpamanaskAraH ucyate iti
# brjod-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  kyis yongs-su-bsgos-pa # 'i phyir rtog-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
aBilApa samutTA aBilApa samutTApikA vA saMjQA aBilApa saMjQA
# brjod-pa #  las byung-ba # 'am / / brjod-pa #  kun-nas-slong-ba # 'i 'du-shes #  pa ni brjod-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  te /
tayA sa samprayogayA jalpam anaskAre sva bIja paripozaNAt jalpam anasikAraH / pariBAvitaH ucyate
# mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  des / / rtog-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  la rang-gi-sa-bon #  yongs su gsos pas rtog-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa #  yongs-su-bsgos-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
ayam api saMvRttyA eva aviparyAsaH na paramArTataH
# 'di yang kun-rdzob #  tu phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ste; don-dam-pa # r ni ma yin no /
anena ca aviparyAsena boDisattvaH viparyAsa nidAnam / grAhya grAhaka aBiniveSa lakzaNam parivarjayati
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  'dis byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  phyin-ci-log #  gi gzhi gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  yongs su spong ste /
evam tat dOzWulyam suKena varjitam Bavati iti p
# de-ltar-na #  gnas-ngan-len #  de bde blag tu spong-ba # r 'gyur ro /
idAnIm avisAre aviparyAsa pradarSana arTam Aha
# nga ni mi-'phro-ba #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
mAyA Adi vat asattvaQca sattva Qca arTasya tat matam / iti vistaraH
# don gyi med dang yod-pa #  ste / / sgyu-ma #  la sogs bzhin-du #  'dod / / ces rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
yat tad arTasya asattvam sattvaQca anantaram uktam iti / kaTam anantaram uktam iti / dvayena prEBAsa tvam taTA ca avidyamAna tA / arTe sa ca A viparyAsaH sat asat tvena varjtiaH
# don gyi yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  gong-du #  bshad ma-thag #  pa gang-yin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la / / gong-du #  bshad-pa #  gang zhe na / / gnyis su snang-ba # r gyur ba ni / / de-ltar #  yod-pa #  ma yin te / / de ni don la ma-log-pa #  / / yod dang med-pa #  rnam-pa # r spangs /
iti tat amAya Adi vat matam
# zhes-bya-ba # 'o / / de ni sgyu-ma #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  'dod de /
mAyA AdInAm iva mAyA Adi vat
# sgyu-ma #  la-sogs-pa #  dang 'dra-ba # s na / / sgyu-ma #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin no /
etat eva pradarSayan= Aha yaTA mAyA sva Atmani avidyamena
# de nyid bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / dper-na #  sgyu-ma #  ni rang-gi #  bdag-nyid-kyis #  med bzhin-du #  /
hasti Adi AtmanA praKyAnAt na hasti Adi BAvena asti iti / hasti Adi BAvena na asti iti sarvaTA eva na asti / kim tarhi na ca na eva asti tat BrAnti mAtrA astitvAt iti
# glang-po-che #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  du snang-ba # s na / / glang-po-che #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dngos-po # r yod-pa #  yin la zhes-bya-ba #  ni glang-po-che #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dngos-po # r med-pa # s / / rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  med-pa #  yang ma yin te / / de ni 'khrul-pa #  tsam du yod-pa # 'i phyir med-pa # 'ang ma yin te /
tasya hasti Adi AkAreNa praKyAyamAnasya BrAnti mAtrasya astitvAt na / sarvaTA na asti / taTA arTaH api na ca asti yaTA sampraKyAti grAhya grAhaka tvena taTA / na eva asti p / tasya trEDAtuka citta cEtta svarUpasya taTA apraKyAyamAnasya
# glang-po-che #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r snang-ba #  de ni / / 'khrul-pa #  tsam du yod-pa # 'i phyir ye med-pa # 'ang ma yin no / / de-bzhin-du #  yod kyang ji-ltar #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r snang-ba #  ltar yod-pa # 'ang ma yin la / / khams-gsum-pa # 'i sems dang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo de /
BrAnti mAtra astitvAt na api na asti / Adi Sabdena marIci svapna udaka candra AdayaH dRzwAntAH yaTAyogam veditavyA iti / nahi marIci svapna udaka candra AdayaH yaTA strI pumAtmanA praKyAyante / taTA santi na ca santi eva BrAnti mAtrA astitvAt evam arTaH api iti
# de-lta-bu # r snang-ba #  de 'khrul-pa #  tsam du yod-pa # 'i phyir med-pa # 'ang ma yin no / / sogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgras ni smig rgyu dang rmi-lam #  dang chu-zla #  la-sogs-pa #  chu dang skyes-pa-dang-bud-med #  kyi bdag-nyid #  du ji-ltar #  snang-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  yod-pa #  ma yin la / / de-la #  'khrul-pa #  tsam du yod-pa # 'i phyir med-pa # 'ang ma yin no /
vistareNa pratyekam yojayitavyam
# de-bzhin-du #  don la rgya-cher #  so-so # r sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
atra ca Adi Sabdena ganDarvanagara pratiSrutka AdayaH veditavyAH
# 'dir yang sogs-pa # 'i sgras ni dri-za # 'i grong-khyer #  dang brag-ca #  la-sogs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
evam yat mAyA Adi upama arTa darSanAt sattva asattva pakzayoH avisAram cetasaH
# de-ltar #  don la sgyu-ma #  la-sogs-pa #  lta-bu # r mthong-nas #  / / yod-pa #  dang med-pa # 'i phyogs la sems mi 'phro ste /
avikzipta tvam paSyati saH avisAre aviparyAsaH / kaH punar avisAraH / maDyamA pratipad samADiH iti anye
# g-yeng ba med-pa # r mthong-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni mi-'phro-ba #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'o / / mi 'pho-ba #  gang zhe na / / gzhan dag na re dbu-ma'i-lam #  gyi ting-nge-'dzin #  to zhe'o /
yadi evam kaTam avisAre aviparyAsaH iti atas Aha tena
# gal-te #  de lta na ji-ltar #  mi-'phro-ba #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r 'gyur zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  /
BAva aBAvayoH cittasya aviraNAt iti
# des yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  la sems-'phro-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
anena aviparyAsena boDisattvaH / BAva aBAva vikalpa rahitAt SUnyatA
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  'dis byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  yod-pa #  dang med-pa # r rtog-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / stong-pa-nyid #  la dmigs-pa #  las mi g-yeng ste /
tasmAt avisAre viparyAsaH ucyate
# de-bas-na #  mi-'phro-ba #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
ayam api saMvRttyEH vA aviparyAsaH na paramArTataH tasya nirvikalpaka tvAt
# 'di yang kun-rdzob #  tu phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  yin gyi / / don-dam-pa # r ni ma yin te / / de ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
idAnIm sva lakzaNe aviparyAsa pradarSana arTam Aha
# da-ni #  rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
sarvasya nAma mAtra tvam sarva kalpa apravRttaye / iti vistaraH
# rtog-pa #  thams-cad #  mi 'jug phyir / / thams-cad #  ming tsam kho-na #  ste / / zhes-bya-ba #  rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
sarvam idam nAma mAtram yat idam cakzUrUpam yAvat manaH DarmA iti
# gang 'di mig dang gzugs rnams nas / / yid dang chos-rnams #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar 'di dag thams-cad #  ni ming tsam mo /
atas dvAdaSa Ayatana Atmakam jQeyam sarvam nAma mAtram / tatra nAma svaBAva viSeza prajQaptiH / na ca prajQapti asya arTasya prajQapteH vA svaBAvaH asti
# zhes-bya-ba #  ni skye-mched #  bcu gnyis kyi bdag-nyid #  shes-bya-thams-cad #  ni ming tsam mo / / de-la #  ming gi ngo-bo-nyid #  dang khyad-par #  du 'dogs-pa # 'o / / gdags-pa # r bya-ba # 'i don dang btags-pa #  ni ngo-bo-nyid #  med de /
tena AtmanA parikalpita tvAt parikalpitasya ca asattvAt
# de'i-bdag-nyid #  du kun-brtags-pa # 'i phyir ro / / kun-brtags-pa #  yang med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anyaTA nAma nirapekzayA cakzuH Adi tvena grahaNam syAt
# gzhan-du-na #  ni ming la mi ltos-pa # r mig la-sogs-pa # r 'dzin-pa # r 'gyur te /
na ca asti avyutpanna saFketasya grahaNam / tasmAt cakzUrupam ityAdi asya asat svaBAva tvAt nAma mAtram eva
# brda la ma byang-ba # r mi-'dzin-pa #  med do / / de-bas-na #  mig dang gzugs zhes-bya-ba #  de ni / / don gyi ngo-bo-nyid #  ma-yin-pa # s mig dang gzugs nas yid dang chos-rnams #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar dag ni ming tsam mo zhes /
cakzUrUpam yAvat manaH DarmA iti evam yat jQAnam sarva vikalpAnAm / pratipakzeNa ayam sva lakzaNe aviparyAse iti parikalpita Darma muKena
# de-ltar #  gang shes-pa #  ni rnam-par-rtog-pa #  thams-cad-kyi #  gnyen-po #  yin-pas #  'di ni rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni kun-brtags-pa # 'i chos-kyi-sgo #  nas /
sarva Darmezu sarva vikalpa pravRttiH
# chos-thams-cad #  la rnam-par-rtog-pa #  thams-cad #  'jug ste /
atas nAma mAtra prativeDa jQAnam sarva vikalpa pratipakzaH / sva lakzaNe aviparyAse iti uktam / tatra na jQAyate kim parama arTe sva lakzaNe Ahosvit saMvRtO= iti atas / pRcCati katam asmin sva lakzaNaH iti / atas Aha / parama arTe sva lakzaNe / ayam aviparyAsaH / paramArTasya sva lakzaNasya anaBilApya tvAt na saMvRteH / kim kAraNam / saMvRttyA yatas na idam nAma mAtram iti gRhyate aBilApa dvAreNa
# de-bas-na #  ming tsam du rtogs-pa # 'i shes-pa #  rnam-par-rtog-pa #  thams-cad-kyi #  gnyen-po #  ni / / rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  zhes bstan to / / de'ang ci don-dam-pa # 'i rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  la'am 'on te kun-rdzob #  kyi la bya-ba #  mi shes-nas #  / / de'i-phyir #  / / rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  gang-la #  zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  don-dam-pa # 'i rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  la'o zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs te / / 'di ni phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'o / / don-dam-pa # 'i rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  ni brjod-du-med-pa # 'i phyir kun-rdzob #  tu ni ma yin no / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na / / 'di-ltar #  kun-rdzob #  tu ni ming 'di tsam mo zhes 'dzin-pa #  med de /
Darma svarUpe saFkalpa pravRtteH ayam api saMvRtya eva na paramArTataH
# brjod-pa # 'i sgo nas chos-kyi-ngo-bo-nyid #  la kun-tu-rtog-pa #  'jug-pa # 'i phyir / / 'di ni kun-rdzob #  nyid yin gyi don-dam-pa # r ni ma yin te /
nAma mAtram iti vikalpanAt
# ming tsam du rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anena ca aviparyAsena boDisattvaH saMvRti parama arTa kuSalaH Bavati p
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  'dis byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  kun-rdzob #  dang don-dam-pa #  la mkhas-pa # r 'gyur ro /
idAnIm sAmAnya lakzaNe aviparyAsa pradarSanAya Aha / Darma DAtu vinirmuktaH yasmAt DarmaH na vidyate / iti vistaraH
# da-ni #  spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir; chos-kyi-dbyings #  ni ma-rtogs-pa # r / / 'di-ltar #  chos yod ma yin te / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
na hi Darma nErAtmyena vinA kaScid rUpya rUpI vA DarmaH vidyate
# chos la dbang-med-pa #  ma-rtogs-pa # 'i chos / / gzugs-can #  nam gzugs-med-pa #  gang yang med de / / chos-thams-cad #  ni brjod-du-med-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  la /
sarva DarmANAm anaBilApya advaya prakRta tvAt grAha grAhaka BAvena / rahita tvAt / tasmAt DarmaDAtuH sarva DarmANAm sAmAnyam lakzaNam iti / sarva Darmezu apRTaktvena tat sat sAmAnya lakzaNam ucyate / yat evam jQAna mayam sAmAnya lakzaNaH aviparyAsaH saMvRttyA na tu
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i dngos-po #  dang bral-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de-bas-na #  chos-kyi-dbyings #  ni / / chos-thams-cad #  ni spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  do zhes-bya-ba #  ste / / chos-thams-cad #  la bye-brag-med-par #  de yod-pa # 'i spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  ces bya'o / / de-ltar #  shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ste /
paramArTataH / tasya nirvikalpa tvAt
# kun-rdzob #  tu yin gyi don-dam-pa # r ni ma yin te de rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tat anena ca aviparyAsena boDisattvaH viSudDi Alambana kuSalaH Bavati
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  'dis byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams par dag-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  la mkhas-pa # r 'gyur te /
nirvikalpa jQAna vizaya tvAt / viSezaH sAmAnya lakzaNa svalaksaNayoH kaH vidyate
# rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyi yul yin pa'i phyir ro / / rang-dang-spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  gnyis la khyad-par #  ci yod ce na /
aBilApa svaBAva samAropita tvasya pratipakzeNa anaBilApya svaBAva tA / paramArTa lakzaNam
# brjod-pa'i-ngo-bo-nyid #  du sgro-btags-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r brjod-du-med-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  ni don-dam-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do /
parikalpita svaBAvanEH Atmyam punar sarva DarmANAm prakRtiH iti / sAmAnya lakzaNam
# kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi bdag-med-pa #  ni chos-thams-cad #  kyi rang-bzhin #  te / / spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  do /
evam darSana Beda vaSAt viSezaH Bavati na tu arTAt iti
# de-ltar #  mthong-ba #  tha-dad-pa # 'i dbang gis khyad-par #  du gyur gyi / / don las ni ma yin no /
idAnIm Darma DAtu aviSudDi viSudDO= aviparyAsa pradarSana arTam Aha
# da-ni #  chos-kyi-dbyings #  rnam-par-ma-dag-pa #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
viparyasta manaskAra avihAni parihANitaH / iti vistaraH
# phyin-ci-log #  gi yid la byed / / ma-spangs-pa #  dang spangs-pa #  las / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
viparyasta manaskAra prahANam tasya Darma DAtoH aviSudDiH tat prahANam
# phyin-ci-log #  gi yid-la-byed-pa #  ma-spangs-pa #  ni / / chos-kyi-dbyings #  de rnam-par-ma-dag-pa # 'o /
viSudDiH iti / tatra viparyasta manaskAraH AlayavijQAna hetuH viparyaya vikalpaH
# spangs-pa #  ni rnam-par-dag-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  / / phyin-ci-log #  gi yid-la-byed-pa #  ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rgyu phyin-ci-log #  tu rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ste /
tasya aprahANam Darma DAtoH aviSudDiH prahANam viSudDiH
# de ma-spangs-pa #  ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  rnam-par-ma-dag-pa # 'o / / spangs-pa #  ni rnam-par-dag-pa #  ste /
yat evam jQAna mayam aviSudDO viSudDO ca aviparyAsaH yaTAkramam iti
# de-ltar #  shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni rnam-par-ma-dag-pa #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ste / / go-rims #  bzhin no zhes-bya-ba #  la /
viparyasta manaskAra aprahANam tasya Darma DAtoH aviSudDiH iti / DarmaDAtoH aviSudDO= aviparyAsaH
# phyin-ci-log #  gi yid-la-byed-pa #  ma-spangs-pa #  ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  rnam-par-ma-dag-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  rnam-par-ma-dag-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'o /
tasya prahANam viSudDiH iti viSudDO= aviparyAsaH / kim kAraNam
# de spangs-pa #  ni rnam-par-dag-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni rnam-par-dag-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'o / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
DarmaDAtoH Agantukena upakleSena upaklizwa tvAt
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  la glo-bur #  gyi nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # s nyon-mongs-pa # r gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro /
ayam api saMvRttyA eva aviparyAsaH na paramArTataH
# 'di yang kun-rdzob #  tu phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ste / / don-dam-pa # r ni ma yin no /
anena ca aviparyAsena boDisattvaH aprahINa AvaraNam Darma DAtoH / prahANaQca prajAnAti
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  'dis byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i chos-kyi-dbyings #  la sgrib-pa #  spangs-pa #  dang ma-spangs-pa #  rab tu shes so /
idAnIm Darma DAtoH aviSudDeH / viSudDeH ca Agantuka tve aviparyAsa pradarSana arTam Aha
# da-ni #  chos-kyi-dbyings #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  dang rnam-par-ma-dag-pa #  glo-bur-du #  'byung-ba #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
Darma DAtoH viSudDa tvAt prakRtyA vyoma vat punar / iti vistaraH
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  ni rang-bzhin-gyis #  / / rnam-pa # r dag phyir nam-mkha' #  bzhin / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
DarmaDAtoH punar AkASa vat prakRti viSudDita tvAt dvayam / api etat Agantukam aviSudDiH viSudDiH ca paScAt iti
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  nam-mkha' #  bzhin-du #  rang-bzhin-gyis #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i phyir / / rnam-pa # r ma-dad-pa #  dang phyis rnam-pa # r dag ces bya-ba #  'di gnyis kyang glo-bur #  yin zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  /
tatra Darma DAtoH aBUta vikalpa upaklizwa tvAt aSudDiH uktA / paScAt ca pratipakza udayena tat prahANAt viSudDiH / etat dvayam api Darma DAtO= Agantukam / kim kAraNam
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  sa la yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # s rnam-par-ma-dag-pa #  zhes bshad do / / phyis gnyen-po #  byung nas de spangs-pa # s rnam-par-dag-pa #  ste / / de-gnyi-ga #  yang chos-kyi-dbyings #  la glo-bur #  yin no / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
AkASa vat Darma DAtoH prakRti viSudDa tvAt
# nam-mkha' #  bzhin-du #  chos-kyi-dbyings #  rang-bzhin-gyis #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i phyir ro /
prakRti viSudDasya aviSudDiH AgantukI Bavet viSudDeH tu nitya viSudDitaH / kaTam AgantukIBAvaH iti
# rang-bzhin-gyis #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  la rnam-par-ma-dag-pa #  ni glo-bur #  yin grang na rnam-par-dag-pa #  ni rtag-tu #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  yin-pas #  ji-ltar #  glo-bur-du #  'gyur zhe na /
yA mala vigama tA Atma tayA viSudDiH sA atra vivakzitA iti na ayam dozaH
# dri-ma-dang-bral-ba # s rnam-par-dag-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de 'dir brjod-pa # s 'dod-pa # s na nyes-pa #  'di med de /
atas eva uktam viSudDiH ca paScAt iti
# de-bas-na #  'di-skad-du #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  ni phyis rnam-pa # r dag ces bshad do /
yat evam Darma DAtoH jQAnam etat Darma DAtoH viSudDi viSudDyoH / Agantuka tve aviparyAsaH / ayam api saMvRttyA na tu paramArTataH
# de-ltar #  shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  la rnam-par-ma-dag-pa #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa #  glo-bur-du #  byung-ba #  nyid la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'o / / 'di yang kun-rdzob #  tu yin gyi don-dam-pa # r ni ma yin no /
anena ca aviparyAsena boDisattvaH DarmaDAtoH / saFkleSa vyavadAna avasTayoH kRtrima tvam prajAnAti iti p
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  'dis byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  chos-kyi-dbyings #  la kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i dus na bcos-ma-ma-yin-pa # r rab tu shes so /
idAnIm atra Ase anunnatO ca aviparyAsa pradarSana arTam Aha
# da-ni #  mi-skrag-pa #  dang ma khengs-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
saFkleSaH ca viSudDiH ca Darma pudgalayoH na hi / iti vistaraH
# chos-rnams #  dang ni gang-zag #  gi / / kun nas nyon mongs rnam dag med / / ces rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
na hi pudgalasya saFkleSaH na viSudDiH na api Darmasya / saFkleSaH viSudDiH ca iti vartate
# gang-zag #  gis kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med / / rnam-par-dag-pa #  med / / chos kyang med de / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # r bsnyegs so / / 'dir rgyu smos-pa #  /
atra eva kAraNam Aha yasmAt na pudgalaH asti na DarmaH / asti iti anuvartate / yaH saFkleSa vyavadAna vyatirekeNa vidyate yasya saFkleSaH vyavadAnam vA / parikalpayitum yujyate yat pRTaktvena ca saMkleSa viSudDI syAtAm sa / tAdRSaH pudgalaH na asti pratyakza anumAna avizaya tvAt
# 'di-ltar #  gang-zag #  med cing chos med-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ste / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  gnyis kyi dus na / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  ma-gtogs-par #  gang zhig yod-na #  ni / / de'i kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'am rnam-par-byang-ba # r yongs su brtag-tu #  rung ste / / de tha-dad-pa # s 'grib-pa-dang-'phel-ba # r yang 'gyur na / / de-lta-bu # 'i gang-zag #  ni med de / / mngon-sum #  dang rjes-su-dpag-pa # 'i yul-ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
DarmaH api parikalpita AtmakaH na eva asti ekasmin= vastuni eka parikalpa pravRtteH
# dngos-po #  gcig la du-ma # r yongs-su-rtog-pa #  'jug-pa # 'i phyir kun-brtags-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  chos kyang yod-pa #  ma yin te /
na ca ekasya aneka Atmaka tA yujyate atas asattvAt pudgala DarmayoH dvayaH / banDni aputrAt vat na saFleSaH na vyavadAnam / paratantrsya api zuda louki kajQana gocarasya saFkleSa viSudDI na eva izyate / kim kAraNam
# gcig ni du-ma # 'i bdag-nyid #  du mi rung ngo / / de-bas-na #  gang-zag #  dang chos gnyis mo-gsham-gyi-bu #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  med-pa # s na / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  med do / / dag-pa #  'jig-rten-pa # 'i ye shes kyi spyod yul gzhan gyi dbang la ni / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # r mi 'dod do / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
tasya niraBilApya advaya prakRti tvAt
# brjod-du-med-pa #  dang gnyis-su-med-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
yadi paratantrasya api na izyate kasya te syAtAm
# gal-te #  gzhan gyi dbang gi yang ma-yin-pa # r 'dod na go de-dag #  gi yin te /
tasmin= asati saFkleSa parihAre vyavadAna prApti yatna vEyarTyam
# de med na kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  spang-ba #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  thob-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir 'bad-pa #  don-med-pa # r 'gyur ro zhe na /
DarmaDAtoH saFkleSa viSudDI BavataH iti ayam adozaH
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa # r 'gyur-ba # s nyes-pa #  'di med do /
Darma DAtoH api atamyasya eva te vyavasTApyete Darma DAtO tayoH / Agantuka tvAt DarmaDAtoH ca AkASa vat avikArAt
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  de'i-bdag-nyid #  ma-yin-pa #  nyid la de-dag #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ste / / chos-kyi-dbyings #  la de-gnyi-ga #  la yang glo-bur #  yin la chos-kyi-dbyings #  kyang-na # m mkha' bzhin-du #  'gyur-ba-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tatas na saMkleSa pakze kasyacid hAniH na vyavadAna pakze vA kaScid viSezaH
# de'i-phyir #  / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i phyogs la su'i 'grib-pa #  yang med la / / rnam-par-byang-ba'i-phyogs #  la su'i khyad-par-du-'gyur-ba #  yang med na /
yatas trAsaH vA syAt mAnoveti amatrAse anunnatO ca aviparyAsaH iti
# gang-gi-phyir #  skrag-pa # 'am nga-rgyal #  du 'gyur te / / 'di ni skrag-pa #  med-pa #  dang khengs-pa #  med-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'o /
anye tu AhuH na saFkleSa pakze kasyacid hAniH na vyavadAna pakze / viSezaH asti tat uBayavataH kasyacid aBAvAt
# gzhan dag na re kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i phyogs la yang su'i 'grib-pa #  yang med la / / rnam-par-byang-ba'i-phyogs #  la yang su'i khyad-par-du-'gyur-ba #  yang med de /
yatas punar te evam BavataH tatra kim iti trAsaH Bavati ayam me na asti iti
# de-gnyi-ga #  dang ldan-pa #  su yang med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gang-gi-phyir #  de-dag #  ni de-lta-ma-yin-pa # s de-la #  nga'i 'di med do zhes skrag-pa # r 'gyur du'ang ci yod /
kim iti mAnaH Bavati ayam me viSezaH iti p / apare tu manyate pudgalaH tAvat na eva asti
# nga'i khyad-par #  ni 'di yin no zhes nga-rgyal #  du 'gyur du yang ci yod ces zer ro / / gzhan dag ni 'di-snyam-du-sems #  te / / gang-zag #  ni med-pa #  nyid do /
DarmaH api na eva asti / avasTA dvayam yaH anuBavati yasya etat dvayam kalpyeta / kim tarhi pratItyasamutpAda mAtram etat saFkleSa vyavadAnam iti
# gang gnas 'di gnyis myong-ba #  dang 'di gnyis gang-la #  brtag-pa # 'i chos de-yang #  med-pa #  nyid do / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  'di dag ni rten cing 'brel-pa # r 'byung-ba #  nyid-du #  zad do snyam mo /
ayam api saMvRttyA na tu paramArTataH tasya nirvikalpaka tvAt
# 'di yang kun-rdzob #  tu'o don-dam-pa # r ni ma yin te / / de ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anena ca aviparyAsena kzaya vRdDi asat BAvAt avikAri tvam Darma DAtoH / prativiDyati iti
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  'dis chos-kyi-dbyings #  zad-pa #  dang 'phel-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir 'gyur-ba-med-pa # r rab-tu-rtogs-pa # r 'gyur ro /
anena ca aviparyAsena sarvam AvaraNam prahAya nirAvaraNaH niryAti iti anye / aTa vA anena saMvRtya Atmakena daSa viparyAsena parama arTa aviparyAsaH atra / sUcitaH tasya anyaTA nirdeSa anupapatteH / anyaH punar Aha ye ete vyaQjane arTe manaskAre avisAre sva lakzaNe
# gzhan na re phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  'dis sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  / / spangs-te #  / / sgrib-pa-dang-bral-ba # 'i nges-par #  'byung ngo zhe'o / / yang-na #  kun-rdzob #  kyi bdag-nyid #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  'di bcus / / don-dam-pa # 'i phyir ci ma-log-pa #  'di bstan te / / gzhan-du #  ni bstan-pa #  mi 'thad-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sAmAnya lakzaNe aSudDO SudDO= Agantuke atrAse anunnatO ca aviparyAsAH / kalpitAH ASrayAH te svaBAva trayam aDikRtya iti
# gzhan na re gang dag yi-ge #  dang don dang yid-la-byed-pa #  dang mi-'phro-ba #  dang rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  dang spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  dang ma-dag-pa #  dang dag-pa #  dang glo-bur #  dang mi-skrag-pa #  dang khengs-pa #  med-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  de-dag #  ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum gyi dbang-du-byas-pa # 'o zhe'o /
tatra vyaQjana arTa aviparyAsO= atra parikalpitam svaBAvam aDikRtya
# de-la #  yi-ge #  dang don la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste /
saMyoginaH dvaya patitasya ca arTasya kalpita tvAt
# 'brel-pa #  dang gnyis su ltung-ba # 'i don ni brtags-pa # 'i phyir ro /
atattva vizaya tve api sati evam tat dvayam aviparyAsaH eva / aviparyAsaH taTA eva iti
# de-kho-na # 'i yul ma yin-du-zin #  kyang / / de-bzhin-du #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  de-bzhin-nyid #  kyi phyir te / / de gnyis phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  nyid do /
manaskAre aviparyAsaH paratantra svaBAvam aDikRtya
# yid-la-byed-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste /
jalpam anaskArasya prakRtyAH AlayavijQAna Atmaka tvAt
# rtog-pa #  dang yid-la-byed-pa #  gnyis rang-bzhin-gyis #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
avisAre aviparyAsaH parinizpanna svaBAvam aDikRtya
# mi-'phro-ba #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
kutas etat nirvikalpasya jQAnasya BAva aBAvayoH vikzepa vigata tvAt / aviparyAsa parinizpattyA ca parinizpanna svaBAva saMgRhIta tvAt / sva sAmAnya lakzaNayoH aviparyAsaH Darma DAtA eva tasya
# rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes ni / / yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  la g-yeng ba dang bral-ba # 'i phyir dang phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r yongs-su-grub-pa # s yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du bsdus-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rang-dang-spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  nyid la ste /
vikalpa viSayA atikrAnta svarUpa tvAt
# rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i yul las 'das-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi phyir ro /
aSuddO SuddO caviparyAsaH DarmaDAtoH avasTA viSeze / Agantuke aviparyAsaH DarmaDAtO= eva tasya hi AkASa vat
# ma-dag-pa #  dang dag-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  nyid kyi gnas-skabs #  kyi bye-brag #  la'o / / glo-bur #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  nyid la ste /
prakRti viSudDasya citta saFkleSAt citta viSudDyA ca Agantukam etat uBayam / vyavasTApyate
# nam-mkha' #  bzhin-du #  rang-bzhin-gyis #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  de-la #  / / sems kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  'di gnyis ni glo-bur #  yin par rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
atra asAnunna BAva aviparyAsaH Darma DAtO= eva tasya AkASa vat / akRtrima tvAt hAni viSeza aBAvAt / evam ete daSa viparyAsAH svaBAva traye veditavyAH / daSa vajra padAni p
# mi-skrag-pa #  dang khengs-pa #  med-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  nyid la ste / / de nam-mkha' #  bzhin-du #  bcos-ma-ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir 'bri-ba #  dang khyad-par #  du gyur-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-ltar #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  bcu po 'di dag ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum du rig-par-bya # 'o /
ete ca anantara uktAH daSa viparyAsAH sUtra uktezu daSasu vajrapadezu / yaTAkramam yojayitavyAH
# bshad ma-thag #  pa'i phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  bcu po 'di dag ni mdo-sde #  las gsungs-pa # 'i rdo-rje # 'i tshig bcu dag dang go-rims-bzhin-du #  sbyar-ba # r bya ste /
daSa vajra padAni katamAni
# rdo-rje # 'i tshig bcu po gang zhe na /
sat asat tA viparyAsaH ASrayaH mAyA upama tA avikalpana tA / prakRti praBAsvara tA saFkleSaH vyavadAnam AkASa upama tA ahIna tA
# yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  dang phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  dang gnas dang sgyu-ma-lta-bu #  nyid dang rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid dang rang-bzhin-gyis #  'od-gsal-ba #  nyid dang kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  dang nam-mkha' #  lta-bu #  dang 'grib-pa #  med-pa #  dang khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  med-pa # 'o /
aviSizwa tA ca iti / tatra vajram iva vajram sarva viparyAsa Bedi tvAt tEH ca aBedya tvAt
# de-la #  phyin-ci-log #  thams-cad #  'joms pa dang de-dag #  gis mi-choms-pa # 'i phyir rdo-rje #  dang 'dra-ba # s na rdo-rje #  zhes-bya-ba #  ste /
anantara uktam aviparyAsa jQAnam tat ca vajram eBiH pratIyate avagamyata / iti vajra padAni / vajravyAKyAnam iti arTaH
# bshad ma-thag #  pa'i phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i shes-pa # 'o / / rdo-rje #  de ni 'di dag gis rtogs-pa # r byed / / khong-du-chud-pa # r byed-pa # s rdo-rje # 'i tshig rnams te / / rdo-rje # 'i rnam-pa # r bshad-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
aTa punar vyaQjana arTa manaskAra AdayaH eva pada SabDena ucyante tatas vajrasya / padAni Alambana anityarTaH
# ji ste na yang yi-ge #  dang don dang yid la-sogs-pa #  nyid la tshig ces bya-ba # 'i sgrar brjod de / / de'i-phyir #  rdo-rje # 'i tshig rnams te /
aTavA durBeda tayA vajra vat etAni eva padAni vajra padAni iti uccayante
# dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / yang rdo-rje #  bzhin-du #  mi-choms-pa # 'i tshig de-dag #  ni rdo-rje # 'i tshig rnams zhes-bya'o #  /
atra aviparyAsAnAm sUtra yojana arTam vajra pada upanyAsaH
# 'dir phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  rnams mdo-sde #  dang sbyar-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir rdo-rje # 'i tshig rnams bkod do /
vajrapadAnAm va daSaviDA viparyAsa muKena idam vyAKyAnam iti
# yang-na #  rdo-rje # 'i tshig rnams ni phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  rnam-pa-bcu # 'i sgo nas bshad-pa # r bstan-pa # 'o /
pradarSana arTam / tatra vyaQjanAnAm arTa sattvam asattvaQca sat asat tA iti atas vyaQjanezu / aviparyAsaH vajrapadezu sat asat tayA veditavyaH
# de-la #  yi-ge #  rnams kyi don-yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  ni yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  ste / / de-bas-na #  yi-ge #  rnams la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni / / rdo-rje # 'i tshig rnams kyi nang nas yod-pa #  dang med-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
dvaya praBAsaH parikalpitaH sa ca atra arTaH
# gnyis su snang-ba #  kun-brtags-pa #  de ni 'dir don yin te /
sa ca taTA na vidyate iti ayam atra aviparyAsaH iti arTa aviparyAsaH / vajrapadezu aviparyAse yojayitavyaH
# de-yang #  de-ltar #  yod-pa #  ma yin zhes-bya-ba #  'di ni 'dir phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ste / / de-ltar #  don la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni rdo-rje # 'i tshig rnams kyi nang nas phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  dang sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
jalpam anaskAraH eva atra ASrayaH iti atas manaskAre aviparyAsaH / vajrapadezu ASraye yojayitavyaH
# rtog-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  nyid 'dir gnas te / / de-bas-na #  yid-la-byed-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni rdo-rje # 'i tshig rnams kyi nang nas gnas zhes-bya-ba #  dang sbyar ro /
mAyA Adi upamayA yaH cetasaH avisAre aviparyAsaH sa vajrapadezu / mAyA upamatAyAm yojayitavyaH / Darma DAtu sva lakzaNam eva kalpanA rahita tvAt avikalpana tA
# sgyu-ma #  la-sogs-pa #  lta-bu # r gang sems mi-'phro-ba #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  'di ni / / rdo-rje # 'i tshig gi nang nas sgyu-ma-lta-bu #  nyid dang sbyar ro / / chos-kyi-dbyings #  kyi rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  ni rtog-pa #  dang bral-ba # s rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  ste /
tena sva lakzaNa aviparyAsaH nirvikalpa tvena drazwavyaH / DarmaDAtu sAmAnyam prakRti praBAsvara tvam
# de-bas-na #  rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid-du #  blta'o / / chos-kyi-dbyings #  kyi spyi ni rang-bzhin-gyis #  'od-gsal-ba #  ste /
tena sAmAnya lakzaNa aviparyAsaH prakRti praBAsvara tayA saFgRhItaH
# de-bas-na #  spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni rang-bzhin-gyis #  'od-gsal-ba # r bsdus so /
Darma DAtoH aviSudDi viSezaH viSudDi viSezaH ca saFkleSaH p
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  rnam-par-ma-dag-pa # 'i bye-brag #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i bye-brag #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  ste /
vyavadAna QcA iti atas aSudDO viSudDO ca aviparyAsaH / saFkleSa vyavadAna antare saFgRhyate
# de'i-phyir #  ma-dag-pa #  dang dag-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i nang-du #  'dus so /
Darma DAtoH saFkleSa vyavadAnayoH / Agantuka tve aviparyAsaH asO= api AkASa upamatAyAm yojayitavyaH
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  la kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa #  gnyis glo-bur-du #  byung-ba #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  'di yang-na # m mkha' lta-bu #  nyid dang sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
saFkleSa vyavadAna avasTayoH Darma DAtoH kzaya vRdDi aBAvAt
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i dus gnyis na / / chos-kyi-dbyings #  zad-pa #  dang 'phel-ba #  med-pa # s /
atra Ase anunnatO ca aviparyAsaH vajra padezu ahIna aviSizwa tAyAm
# mi-skrag-pa #  dang khengs-pa #  med-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni rdo-rje # 'i tshig rnams kyi nang nas /
yojayitavyaH / evam ete daSa aviparyAsAH daSasu vajrapadezu yaTAkramam yojayitavyAH
# 'grib-pa #  med-pa #  dang khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  med-pa #  dang sbyar ro / / de-ltar #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  bcu po 'di dag ni / / rdo-rje # 'i tshig bcu po dang go-rims-bzhin-du #  sbyar ro /
vajra padAnAm SarIra vyavasTAnam iti yAna arTAn aDikRtya vajra padAnAm
# rdo-rje # 'i tshig rnams kyi lus-rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni don gang dag gi dbang-du-byas-te #  /
pravRttiH te arTAH tezAm SarIram
# rdo-rje # 'i tshig rnams 'jug-pa'i-don #  de rnams de-dag #  gi lus so /
tezAm anu caturDA vyavasTAnam svaBAvataH AlambanataH avikalpanataH / codya parihArataH ca
# de-dag #  kyang rnam-pa-bzhi # r gzhag ste ngo-bo-nyid #  dang dmigs-pa #  dang rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid dang brgal-ba #  dang lan no /
tatra trayaH svaBAvAH parinizpanna parikalpita paratantra AKyAH AdyEH
# de-la #  ngo-bo-nyid #  ni gsum ste yongs-su-grub-pa #  dang kun-brtags-pa #  dang gzhan gyi dbang zhes-bya-ba #  dag ste /
triBiH padEH yaTAkramam iti / tatra AdO BavAni AdyAni tAni punar sat asat tA viparyAsaH ASrayaH ca iti
# tshig dang-po #  gsum dang go-rims #  bzhin no zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  / / dang-po #  ni yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  dang phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  dang gnas zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
tatra sat asat tayA parinizpannaH uktaH
# de-la #  yongs-su-grub-pa #  ni yod-pa #  dang med-pa # r bshad do /
aviparyAsena parikalpitaH uktaH
# kun-brtags-pa #  ni phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r bshad do /
ASraya tvena paratantraH uktaH / kaTam iti
# gzhan gyi dbang ni gnas su bshad do / / ji-ltar #  zhe na /
parinizpannasya sat asattAyAH sat asat tayA nirdeSaH iti kecid
# kha-cig #  na re yongs-su-grub-pa #  ni yod-pa #  dang med-pa # 'i phyir yod-pa #  dang med-pa # r bstan-pa #  yin no zhe'o /
kaTam sadasat lakzaNa tvAt parinizpannasya sat asat tayA aBiDAnam iti eke
# ji-ltar-yod-pa #  dang med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyi phyir yongs-su-grub-pa #  zhe na / / kha-cig #  na re yod-pa #  dang med-pa # r brjod-pa # 'i phyir ro zhe'o /
saMyogAt saMstava AcakzarANAm kalpitena arTena sArTaka tvam paSyan / viparyayAt ca nirarTaka tvam parinizpannaH svaBAvaH anaBilApya iti / avagamyate / atas tat sat asat tA parinizpannaH svaBAvaH iti uktam iti anye
# gzhan dag na re yi-ge #  rnams 'brel-pa #  dang 'dris-pa # 'i phyir rnam-par-brtags-pa # 'i don-gyis #  don-yod-pa #  dang bzlog na don-med-pa # r mthong-ba # s yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  brjod-du-med-pa # r rtogs-pa # r 'gyur te / / de-bas-na #  de yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du bshad do zhe'o /
mahAyAna deSanA DarmaH su viSudDa Darma DAtu nizyanda tvAt / viparyAsa pratipakza Alambana tvAt ca parinizpannaH svaBAvaH iti ucyate
# gzhan na re theg-pa-chen-po #  bstan-pa # 'i chos ni shin-tu #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i chos-kyi-dbyings #  kyi rgyu-mthun-pa #  dang phyin-ci-log #  gi gnyen-po # 'i dmigs-pa #  yin pa'i phyir / / yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  ces bya ste /
saH arTaH kalpita svaBAvasya Bavati na tu parikalpitaH
# rnam-par-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi don yin-du-zin #  kyang kun-brtags-pa #  ma yin te /
atas sat asat tA parinizpannaH iti uktam iti apare
# de'i-phyir #  yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du bshad do zhe'o /
anye tu AhuH sadasattA api viparyasta tvAt parinizpannaH svaBAvaH uktaH
# gzhan dag na re yod-pa #  dang med-pa # r phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i phyir yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du bshad do zhe'o /
aviparyAsena parikalpitaH tasya avidyamAnena dvaya rUpeNa praKyAti / lakzaNAt / ASrayeNa paratas tasya aBiDAnam
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  ni kun-brtags-pa #  ste / / yod-pa #  ma yin yang gnyis po med-pa # 'i ngo bor snang-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  du gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gnas ni gzhan gyi dbang ste /
hetu tvAt ASrayaH iti ucyate Pala tvAt paratantraH iti
# de ni rgyu yin-pas #  na gnas zhes-bya'o # ; / / 'bras-bu #  yin-pas #  na gzhan gyi dbang zhes-bya'o #  /
etat eva svaBAva trayam AlambanataH jQeyam
# ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum po 'di dag nyid shes-par-bya-ba #  yin-pas #  dmigs-pa # 'o /
avikalpanataH iti atra vigraha BedAt Aha yena ca vikalpayati nirvikalpena
# rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid ces bya-ba #  ni 'dir tshig rnam-pa # r sbyar-ba # 'i bye-brag #  gis na / / gang-gis #  rnam-pa # r mi rtog ce na / / rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyis so /
jQAnena yat ca na vikalpayati prakRti praBAsvara tAm / tatra Arya vigraha BedaH na vikalpayati anena iti avikalpanam na vikalpyate / tat iti avikalpanam / tat BAvaH avikalpana tA
# gang-la #  rnam-pa # r mi rtog ce na / / rang-bzhin-gyis #  'od-gsal-ba #  la'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / de-la #  tshig rnam-pa # r sbyar-ba # 'i bye-brag #  ni 'di yin te / / 'dis rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # s na rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  dang de rnam-par-rtog-pa # r bya-ba-ma-yin-pa # s na / / rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  ste / / de'i dngos-po #  ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid do; / / de-ltar #  rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid ni /
evam avikalpana tA dvAByAm vajra padAByAm paridIpitA iti darSayati / tat anena jQeya jQAna vyavasTAnam yaTAkramam veditavyam yat uta triBiH / sva BAvEH avikalpanatayA ca iti
# rdo-rje # 'i tshig gnyis kyis brjod-pa # r bstan to / / de-bas-na #  'di shes-bya #  dang shes-pa #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  'di-lta-ste #  / / ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum dang rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid dang go-rims-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra triBiH svaBAvEH jQeya vyavasTAnam grAhya tvAt
# de-la #  ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum ni gzung-ba #  yin pa'i phyir shes-bya # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
avikalpanatayA jQAna vyavasTAnam grAhaka tvAt
# rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid ni 'dzin-pa #  yin pa'i phyir shes-pa # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
codya parihArataH upayukteByaH SizwAni vajrapadAni / atra kiQcid vajra pradam codyasya parihAraH eva
# brgal-ba #  dang lan ni rdo-rje # 'i tshig bshad-zin #  pa'i lhag-ma #  rnams so / / 'di-la #  rdo-rje # 'i tshig kha-cig #  ni brgal-ba # 'i lan nyid de /
tat yaTA mAyA upama tA AkASa upama tA ahIna aviSizwa tA ca iti p / kiQcid punar ca udyam eva / tat yaTA saMkleSaH vyavadAnam iti / tasmAt ucya parihAraH ca codyasya parihAraH ca codya parihArO / asarUpa eka Sezam kRtvA
# 'di-lta-ste #  / / sgyu-ma-lta-bu #  nyid dang nam-mkha' #  lta-bu #  nyid dang 'grib-pa #  med-pa #  nyid dang khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  med-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / kha-cig #  ni brgal-ba #  nyid de / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  / / de-bas-na #  brgal-ba # 'i lan dang brgal-ba #  ni /
tatra codyam yadi ete parikalpita paratantra lakzaNAH DarmAH na saMvidyante
# brgal-ba #  dang lan te mi-mthun-pa #  gcig ma bcug-pa # 'o / / de-la #  brgal-ba #  ni gal-te #  kun-brtags-pa #  dang gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan-nyid #  kyi chos de-dag #  med na /
grAhya grAhaka tvena iti vAkyaSezaH
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  nyid-du #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshig gi lhag-ma # 'o /
kaTam upalaByante grAhya grAhaka tvena iti aBiprAyaH
# ji-ltar #  dmigs-pa # r 'gyur / / gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  nyid-du #  zhes-bya-ba # r dgongs so /
atas saMvidyante DarmANAm prakRti praBAsvara tA na yujyate / grAhya grAhaka tvAt manAH vidyamAna tvAt / etat ca udyam
# ji ste yod-na #  de lta na go chos-rnams #  rang-bzhin-gyis #  'od-gsal-ba #  nyid-du #  mi rung ste / / gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  du yod-pa # 'i phyir ro / / 'di ni brgal-ba # 'o /
tad mAyA upamatayA pariharati
# de'i lan ni sgyu-ma-lta-bu #  nyid yin te /
yaTA mAyA kRtam na saMvidyate upalaByate ca iti
# dper-na #  sgyu-ma #  byas-pa #  lta-bu #  ni med kyang dmigs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ste /
na hi mAyA upalaByatayA saMvidyate tatas api evam saMvidyate iti jQAtum
# sgyu-ma #  ni dmigs su yod kyang de'i-phyir #  de-bzhin-du #  yod do zhes-bya-ba # r shes-pa # r mi nus so /
Sakyate / yadi parkRti praBA svara tA DarmANAm tat kaTam pUrvam saMkleSaH paScAt / vyavadAnam iti codyam
# gal-te #  chos-rnams #  rang-bzhin-gyis #  'od-gsal-ba #  nyid yin na / / ji-ltar #  sngar kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  phyis rnam-pa # r byang zhes brgal-te #  /
na hi prakRti viSudDe kadAcid saMklizwa tA upapadyate / asya parihAraH saFkleSa vyavadAnam AkASa upama tayA veditavyam
# rang-bzhin-gyis #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  yin na / / nam du yang kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  mi 'thad do zhes-bya-ba #  de'i lan ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  nam-mkha' #  lta-bu # r rig-par-bya-ba #  yin te /
yaTA AkASam prakRti pariSudDam Agantukena upakleSena saMkliSyate tat
# dper-na #  nam-mkha' #  rang-bzhin-gyis #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  la / / glo-bur #  gyi nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # s kun nas nyon mongs so /
apagamAt vyavadIyate ca iti / evam Darma DAtoH prakRti viSudDa tvepya AgantukEH upakleSEH saMkleSaH / tat apagamAt ca vyavadAnam iti yadi aprameya budDa utpAde satya prameyANAm / sattvAnAm kleSa praSamaH tat kaTam anAdi saMsAre pratyekasya api
# de dang bral-ba #  rnam-pa # r byang ngo zhes pa de-bzhin-du #  chos-kyi-dbyings #  rang-bzhin-gyis #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  yang glo-bur #  gyi nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams kyis kun nas nyon mongs so / / de dang bral na rnam-pa # r byang ngo / / gal-te #  sangs-rgyas #  dpag-tu-med-pa #  byung ste / / sems-can #  dpag-tu-med-pa #  dag gi kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  bsal te /
budDa utpAdasya aprameyANAm satvAnam saMsAra apagamAn nirvANa praveSAt
# thog-ma-med-pa # 'i 'khor-ba # r sangs-rgyas-'byung-ba #  re-re # s kyang sems-can #  dpag-tu-med-pa #  dag 'khor-ba #  dang phral te / / mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # r btsud na /
ca na saMsAra samucCedaH na nirvANa vRdDi vA iti codyam / asya ahIna aviSizta tayA parihAraH / aprameya tvAt sattva DAtoH vyavadAna pakzasya ca iti
# de'i-phyir #  / / ji-ltar #  'khor-ba #  rgyun-chad-pa # r mi 'gyur zhing mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  'phel-ba # r mi 'gyur zhes brgal-ba #  de'i lan ni 'grib-pa #  med-pa #  dang khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  med-pa #  nyid yin te /
parimANavataH hi vastunaH hAniH samucCedaH vA prajQAyate aprameyaH ca / sattva DAtuH / tasya hAniH api na prajQAte kutas eva samucCedaH prajQAsyeta AkASa vat
# sems-can-gyi-khams #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba'i-phyogs #  dpag-tu-med-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ste / / tshad dang ldan-pa'i-don # gs po ni 'grib-pa # 'am rgyun-chad-pa # r sngon gyi sems-can-gyi-khams #  dpag-tu-med-pa #  de-la #  ni / / 'grib-pa # r yang mi mngon na rgyun-chad-pa # r ltag la mngon te nam-mkha' #  bzhin no /
vyavadAnasya api aprameya tvAt viSezaH eva na asti tasya kaTam vRdDiH / Bavizyati AkASa vat
# rnam-par-byang-ba #  yang dpag-tu-med-pa # 'i phyir khyad-par #  nyid kyang med na / / de 'phel-ba # r ji-ltar #  'gyur te /
tasya AvaraNa ApagAt AvaraNa aBAvAt ca iti / dvitIyam SarIra vyavasTAnam iti vajrapadAnAm iti aDikRtam / yatra yA ca yatas BrAntiH aBra antiH yA ca yatra ca / BrAnti aBrAnti Pale ca eva paryantaH ca tayoH iti
# nam-mkha' #  sgrib-pa-dang-bral-ba #  dang sgrib-pa #  'byung-ba #  bzhin no / / lus-rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  gnyis ni zhes-bya-ba #  ni rdo-rje # 'i tshig rnams kyi zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro / / gang-la #  gang zhig gang-la # s 'khrul / / ma 'khrul gang zhig gang-la #  dang / / 'khrul dang ma 'khrul 'bras-bu-nyid #  / / de nyid kyi ni tha-ma # 'o /
vajrapadEH BrAnti vizayaH BrAnti svarUpa tA BrAnti hetuH BrAnti Palam / BrAnti paryantaH ca nirdizwaH
# zhes-bya-ba #  ni rdo-rje # 'i tshig rnams kyis 'khrul-pa # 'i yul dang 'khrul-pa # 'i rang-gi #  ngo-bo-nyid #  dang 'khrul-pa # 'i rgyu dang 'khrul-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  dang 'khrul-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  mthar-phyin-pa #  bstan to /
taTA aBra antisva rUpam aBrAnti vizayaH aBra anti Palam tad paryantaH ca iti
# de-bzhin-du #  ma 'khrul-pa # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo dang ma 'khrul-ba # 'i yul dang ma 'khrul-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  dang de'i mthar-phyin-pa #  yang bstan to /
tatra yatra BrAntiH iti sat asattAyAm vyaQjanAnAm
# de-la #  gang-la #  'khrul zhes-bya-ba #  na / / yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  la ste /
sArTaka tva nirarTaka tva lakzaNAyAm aBiDAna aBiDeyayoH tat / sambanDasya ca BAva svarUpeNa parikalpita tvAt / yA ca BrAntiH iti viparyAsaH BrAntiH / sva Atmani avidyamena dvaya AkAreNa praKyAnAt / yatas BrAntiH iti ASrayAt BrAntiH ASrayaH punar jalpa pariBAvitaH / manaskAraH AlayavijQAna AtmakaH
# yi-ge #  rnams kyi don-yod-pa #  dang med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  la rjod pa dang brjod-par-bya-ba #  dang de'i 'brel-pa #  ni dngos-po # 'i ngo bor kun-brtags-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gang zhig 'khrul ces bya-ba #  la / / phyin-ci-log #  ni 'khrul-pa #  ste / / bdag-nyid #  la yod-pa-ma-yin-pa # r / / gnyis kyi rnam-pa # r snang-ba # 'i phyir ro / / gang-la # s 'khrul zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / gnas las 'khrul-pa #  ste / / gnas ni rtog-pa # s yongs-su-bsgos-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  do /
aBrAntiH yA ca iti mAyA Adi vat arTataH sat asat tA visAraH aBra antiH
# ma 'khrul gang zhig ces bya-ba #  ni / / sgyu-ma #  la-sogs-pa #  lta-bu # r don gyi yod-pa #  dang med-pa # r mi-'phro-ba #  ni ma 'khrul-pa # 'o /
BAva aBAva aBiniveSa BrAnti pratipakzaH ca aBra antiH
# dngos-po #  dang dngos-po-med-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  'khrul-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  yang ma 'khrul-pa #  ste /
sA yaTAkramam mAyA upama tayA avikalpana tA ca nirdizwA / yatra ca iti yatra ca p / sA aBra antiH
# de ni sgyu-ma-lta-bu #  nyid dang rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid-du #  go-rims-bzhin-du #  bstan to / / gang-la #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni gang-la #  de sems ma 'khrul-ba # 'o / / de-yang #  rang-bzhin-gyis #  'od-gsal-ba #  nyid la ste /
sA punar prakRti praBA svara tAyAm parinizpanna svaBAva lakzaNAyAm / BrAnti aBrAnti Pale ca eva iti tatra BrAnti Palam hi saFkleSaH / BrAnti nizyandaH iti vAkya SezaH / aBrAnti nizyandAnAyAH BrAnteH aBra anti Pala tvAt / aBrAnti Palam vyavadAnam sa samprayogam iti vAkyaSezaH / eva kAra karaNam tat Pale saFkleSaH vyavadAnam iti anena eva ukte / AkASa upama tayA tu paSyati Darma DAtoH yasya BrAnti aBra anti Palam tat / saFkleSa vyavadAna Atmakam / na idam tat prakRtikam iti pradarSana arTam / paryantaH ca tayoH iti saFkleSa vyavadAnayoH paryantaH nirvANam / tad cahIna anaDika tvena paryantam uktam iti eke / anye tu AhuH saMsArasya aprameya tayA apacaya aBAvAt ahIna tA yuktaH / saFkleSa paryantaH / nirvANasya aprameya tayA upacaya aBAvAt aviSizwa tA yuktaH vyavadAna paryanta iti / etAni daSa vajra padAni aviparyAsa prasaFga dvAreNa uktAni / na tu sUtritAni iti atas tAni antara SlokAByAm saFgRhItAni / sat asat tA aparyAsaH ASrayaH mAyayA upamA / akalpanA prakRtyA ca BAsvara tvam sadA eva hi / saMkleSaH vyavadAnaQcaH AkASa upama tA taTA / ahIna tva aDika tvacaQca daSa vajra padAni hi / atra ca parinizpanna Sabda arTa sambanDa darSanam viparyAsaH / yaTA pratyavaBAsate taTA arTAnAm svaBAva sattA darSanam / viparyAsaH / tat arTa pravRtti kAraNa darSanam viparyAsaH / arTa samAropa apavAda darSanam viparyAsaH / yaTA nAm arTa svaBAva darSanam viparyAsaH / BAvAnAm sva sAmAnya lakzaNayoH vastu tvena darSanam viparyAsaH / svastya svasti saQcArAt viSudDiH aviSudDiH ca iti darSanam viparyAsaH / ekasya eva aSudDi viSudDi darSanam viparyAsaH / saFkleSa vyavadAna prahANa pratilamBayoH hAni viSeza darSanAt / trAsamAna pravRttiH viparyAsaH / iti ete daSa viparyAsAH
# yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  mtshan-nyid #  la'o / / 'khrul dang ma 'khrul 'bras-bu-nyid #  / / ces bya-ba #  de-la #  / / 'khrul-ba # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  ste / / 'khrul-pa # 'i rgyu-mthun-pa # 'i zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshig gi lhag-ma # 'o / / ma 'khrul-ba # 'i rgyu-mthun-pa # 'i ma 'khrul-ba #  ni / / ma 'khrul-pa # 'i 'bras-bu # 'i phyir ma 'khrul-ba # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni rnam-par-byang-ba #  ste / / mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshig gi lhag-ma # 'o / / nyid ces bya-ba #  brjod-pa # s de'i 'bras-bu #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  'dis bshad de / / nam-mkha' #  lta-bu #  nyid ces bya-ba # s ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  gang-gis #  'khrul-ba #  dang ma 'khrul-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  de-dag #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin gyi / / de de'i-rang-bzhin #  ni ma yin no zhes bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de gnyis ni mtha' ma'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / kha-cig #  na re kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  gnyis kyi mtha' ni mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  ste / / de-yang #  'grib-pa #  med-pa #  dang lhag-pa #  med-pa # s mthar-thug-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir bshad do zhe'o / / gzhan dag na re 'khor-ba #  dpag-tu-med-pa # 'i phyir / / 'bri-ba #  med-pa # s 'grib-pa #  med-pa #  dang ldan-pa # s ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i mtha' ma'o / / mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  dpag-tu-med-pa # s 'phel-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir / / khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  med-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  ni rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go zhes zer ro / / rdo-rje # 'i tshig bcu po 'di dag ni phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i zhar la bshad kyi mdor byas-pa #  las ni mi 'byung ngo / / de-bas-na #  / / yod med phyin ci ma log dang / / gnas dang sgyu-ma-lta-bu #  nyid / / mi-rtog-pa #  dang rang-bzhin-gyis #  / / rtag bar 'od-gsal #  nyid dang ni / / kun nas nyon mongs rnam byang dang / / de-bzhin #  nam-mkha' #  lta-bu #  nyid / / 'grib dang med-pa #  lhag med-pa #  / / rdo-rje # 'i tshig ni bcu zhes-bya'o #  / / zhes-bya-ba #  bar gyi tshigs-su-bcad-pa #  gnyis kyis sdud do / / 'di-la #  yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i sgra dang don 'brel-pa # r lta-ba # 'i phyin-ci-log #  dang don rnams ji-lta-bu # r snang-ba #  de-lta-bu # r ngo-bo-nyid #  du yod-pa # r mthong-ba # 'i phyin-ci-log #  dang don de 'byung-ba # 'i rgyu la phyin-ci-log #  dang don la sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-par #  lta-ba # 'i phyin-ci-log #  dang ming ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  don gyi ngo-bo-nyid #  du lta-ba # 'i phyin-ci-log #  dang dngos-po #  rnams kyi rang-dang-spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  la dngos-po #  nyid-du #  phyin-ci-log #  dang bkra-shis #  pa dang bkra-shis #  pa ma-yin-pa #  kun du spyod-pa # s las rnam-par-dag-pa #  dang rnam-par-ma-dag-pa # r lta-ba # 'i phyin-ci-log #  dang gcig kho-na #  la rnam-par-ma-dag-pa #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa # r lta-ba # 'i phyin-ci-log #  dang kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  spang-ba #  dang 'thob-pa #  dang 'grib-pa #  dang khyad-par #  du lta-ba # s skrag-pa #  dang brgyal-ba #  'byung-ba # 'i phyin-ci-log #  ste / / 'di dag ni phyin-ci-log #  bcu'o /
boDisattvasya tat aBAvAt aviparyAsa avasTitasya / yaTA uktezu arTezu ariNatA vidarSanA BAvanA veditavyA / uktA anu Darma pratipattiH / anta dvaya varjane pratipattiH
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  la de-dag #  med-pa # s / / ji-skad #  bshad-pa # 'i don rnams la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r gnas-pa #  ni lhag-mthong-bsgom-pa #  yin par rig-par-bya # 'o /
p / anuDarma pratipatti antaram anta dvaya varjane pratipattiH vaktavyA iti atas
# rjes-su-mthun-pa'i-chos #  sgrub-pa #  bshad-zin #  to / / rjes-su-mthun-pa'i-chos #  sgrub-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  mtha'-gnyis #  spang-ba #  sgrub-pa #  brjod-pa # r bya ste / / de'i-phyir #  /
pRcCati anta dvaya varjane pratipattiH katamet yatas Aha yAH ratna kUwe / nAma Darma paryAyeNa samyak pratipatteH svaBAva pratipAdana arTam / maDyamA pratipad upadizwA
# mtha'-gnyis #  spang-ba #  sgrub-pa #  gang zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  gang dkon-mchog #  brtsegs pa zhes-bya-ba # 'i chos-kyi-rnam-grangs #  las yang-dag-par-sgrub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / dbu-ma'i-lam #  bshad do zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tat yaTA kASyapaH iha mahA ratna kUwe Darma paryAye Sikzitu kAmena / boDisattvena yoni SoDarma prayuktena Bavitavyam
# 'od srungs 'di-lta-ste #  / / dkon-mchog #  brtsegs pa chen-po #  chos-kyi-rnam-grangs #  la slob-par-'dod-pa # 'i byang-chub-sems #  dpas tshul-bzhin-du #  rab tu chos la sbyar-ba # r bya'o; /
katamaH ca yoni SoDarma prayogaH / yat uta sarva DarmANAm BUta pratyavekzA
# tshul-bzhin-du #  chos la sbyor-ba #  gang zhe na 'di-lta-ste #  / / chos-rnams #  la yang-dag-par #  so-sor-rtog-pa #  ste /
yA na Atma pratyavekzA na / sattvana jIvana pozaNa pudgalanam anujana mAnava pratyavekzA / iyam ucyate kASyapa maDyamA p / pratipad iti vistareNa yAvat dvitIya pradIpa udAharaNa paryantaH paWyate
# gang bdag-med-pa # r rtog-pa #  dang sems-can-med-pa #  dang srog med-pa #  dang gso-ba #  med-pa #  dang skyes-bu #  med-pa #  dang gang-zag-med-pa #  dang shed las skyes med-pa #  dang shed bu med-pa # r so-sor-rtog-pa #  'di ni / / 'od srungs dbu-ma'i-lam #  mo zhes-bya-ba #  nas / / mar-me # 'i dpe gnyis-pa #  la thug gi bar-du #  rgya-cher #  'byung ngo /
kasya antasya varjanAt asO veditavyA / katam asya antasya varjanAt maDyamA pratipatteH jQAtavyA iti arTaH / atas Aha
# mtha' gang spangs-pa # s de rig-par-bya #  zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  ni mtha' gang spangs-pa # s dbu-ma'i-lam #  shes-pa # r bya zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / de'i-phyir #  /
pRTak tu eka tvam antar ca tIrTya SrAvakayoH api / iti vistaraH
# tha-dad-pa #  dang gcig mtha' dang / / mu stegs nyan-thos #  gnyis-ka #  dang / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
ayam paQcadaSaviDaH anta dvaya BedaH
# bco lnga po 'di dag ni mtha'-gnyis #  dbye-ba #  ste /
asya varjanAt sA veditavyA
# 'di dag spangs-pa # s de rig-par-bya # 'o /
atra pRTak Adi darSanam antar / ekEka pakza aBinivizwa tvAt kArye kAraNa upacAram kRtvA / tatra rUpa AdiByaH pRTaktvam AtmanaH iti antar ekatvam iti antar
# 'dir tha-dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r lta-ba # 'i mtha' ni phyogs re-re #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i phyir 'bras-bu #  la rgyu gdags-pa # r byas-pa # 'o / / de-la #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  dang bdag tha dad ces bya-ba #  yang mtha'o /
tatra ye rUpa AdIn sknaDAna AyatanAni DAtUn= ca nitya AtmanaH / upaBoga vastu tvena kalpayanti tat rUpa AdiByaH pRTaktvam AtmanaH iti antar
