# gcig ces bya-ba #  yang mtha'o zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  / / gzugs la-sogs-pa #  phung-po #  rnams dang skye-mched #  rnams dang khams rnams ni bdag rtag-pa # 'i spyad-par-bya-ba # 'i 'os su rtog-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  ni gzugs la-sogs-pa #  dang bdag tha dad do snyam pa'i mtha'o /
ye punar ADyAtmikAn saMskArAn rUpa AdInAm Atma tvena pratipannAH yaH
# nang gi 'du-byed #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la bdag-tu-'du-shes #  nas gang mthong-ba #  dang thos-pa #  dang shes-pa #  de ni bdag yin la /
paSyati SRNoti jAnAti saH AtmA iti bAhyAn= ca AtmIya tvena kalpayanti tat / rUpa AdiByaH ekatvam AtmanaH iti antar yat sUtryate a jIvaH tat SarIram / anyaH jIvaH anyat SarIram iti darSanam tat eva atra anta Sabdena uktam
# phyi'i rnams ni bdag-gi #  ba yin par rtog-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni gzugs la-sogs-pa #  dang bdag gcig go zhes-bya-ba # 'i mtha' ste / / gang mdo-sde #  las srog kyang gzhan la lus kyang gzhan-pa #  dang srog de lus de yin zhes-bya-ba # r lta-ba #  nyid 'dir mtha' zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgrar bstan to /
tat parivarjana arTam iti rUpa AdiByaH tattva anyatvAnta parivarjana arTam / AtmanaH
# de yongs-su-spang-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs la-sogs-pa #  dang bdag de nyid dang gzhan gyi mtha' yongs su spang-pa # 'i phyir ro /
maDyamA pratipad yat DarmAtram vizaya BUtam jQAnam
# dbu-ma'i-lam #  gang chos tsam zhig yul du gyur-pa # 'i ye shes so /
etat eva pradarSayan= Aha yA na Atma pratyavekzA / yAvat namAnapratyavekzeti Darma mAtra darSanAt hi vanDyA purtra vat / AtmA na asti iti avagacCat na AtmAnam pratyavekzate na anusarati iti arTaH
# de nyid bstan-pa # 'i phyir gang bdag-med-pa # r so-sor-rtog-pa-na # s shed bu med-pa # r so-sor-rtog-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / chos tsam du mthong-ba # s ni bdag mo-gsham-gyi-bu #  bzhin-du #  med-pa # r khong-du-chud-nas #  bdag-med-pa # r so-so # r rtog ste /
kutas eva tasya rUpa AdiByaH tattvam anya tvam vA gRhyate iti
# rjes su rtogs zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / de dang gzugs la-sogs-pa #  de nyid dam gzhan-du #  'dzin-pa # r lta-ga-la #  'gyur /
Atma Sabdena eva tad arTe avagamyamAne kimarTam
# bdag ces bya-ba # 'i sgra nyid kyis de'i don khong-du-chud-pa # r 'gyur na /
sattva Adi paryAya viSeza aBiDAnam
# ci'i-phyir #  sems-can #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-grangs #  kyi bye-brag #  smos she na /
na sarvasya sarva paryAya vyutpattiH iti atas sarvezAm tad arTa avaboDa arTam / paryAya antara nirdeSaH
# thams-cad-kyi # s rnam-grangs #  thams-cad #  khong-du-chud-pa # r mi 'gyur te / / de'i-phyir #  thams-cad-kyi # s de'i don khong-du-chud-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir rnam-grangs #  gzhan bshad do /
tat kAla vikziptAnAm vA paryAya antareNa tad arTa prApaNa arTaH / tena eva aBiDAnena ucyamAne anyezAm prApaNAt / nityam rUpam iti tIrTikAntaH
# yang-na #  de'i dus-su #  g-yengs pa rnams la rnam-grangs #  gzhan gyis de'i don rtogs-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir te / / brjod-par-bya-ba #  de nyid brjod na ni gzhan dag gis brnyas-par-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
te hi parikalpita rUpAn vastu tvena aBiniveSya nitya tvena kalpayanti / nitya viparyAsa upahata tvAt / anityam iti SrAvakAntaH
# gzugs la-sogs-pa #  rtag go zhes-bya-ba #  ni mu-stegs-can #  gyi mtha' ste / / de-dag #  ni rtag-par #  phyin-ci-log #  gis non-pa # 'i phyir kun-brtags-pa # 'i gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la dngos-po #  kho-nar #  mngon-pa # r zhen nas rtag-pa #  nyid-du #  rtog go / / mi rtag go zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyan-thos #  kyi mtha' ste /
tEH api kalpita svaBAvAnAm rUpa AdInAm vastu rUpeNa anitya tvena / samAropaNAt anta tvam
# de-dag #  kyang kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la dngos-po # 'i ngo bor mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  du sgro-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir mtha' nyid de /
atyanta saMsAra udvega karAt nirvANasya ca anta pAtanAt / anitya darSnasya anta tvam tat uBaya parivarjana arTam iti / nitya anitya darSana parivarjana arTam maDyamA pratipad yA rUpa AdInAm / nanitya pratyavekzA na anitya pratyavekzeti / tat punar kim
# shin-tu #  'khor-ba #  las skyo-bar-byed-pa #  dang mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i mthar ltung-ba # r byed-pa # s mi-rtag-pa # r lta-ba # 'i mtha'o / / de-gnyi-ga #  yongs-su-spang-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni rtag-pa #  dang mi-rtag-pa # r lta-ba #  yongs-su-spang-ba # 'i phyir dbu-ma'i-lam #  ste / / gang gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la rtag-par #  yang mi rtog / / mi-rtag-pa # r yang mi-rtog-pa # 'o /
nirvikalpa jQAnam / yat na rUpa AdIn rUpa Adizu eva nityatvena anitya tvena ca anugacCati / rUpa AdInAm iti Adi Sabdena
# de-yang #  gang zhe na / / rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes te / / gang gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la gzugs la-sogs-pa #  nyid-du #  rtag-pa # 'am / / mi-rtag-pa #  mi-rtog-pa # 'o /
vedanA saMjQA saMskAra vijQAna skanDAnAm / pRTivI ap tejaH vAyu AkASa DAtUnAm / cakzuH Srotra GrANa jihvA kAyam anAyatanAnAm ca grahaNam p / AtmA iti Sabdena pudgala samAropAntaH iti skanDa DAtu Ayatana vyatiriktam
# gzugs la-sogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sgras ni tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang 'du-byed #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i phung-po #  rnams dang sa dang chu-dang-me #  dang rlung dang nam-mkha'i-khams #  rnams dang mig dang rna-ba #  dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi skye-mched #  rnams bsdu'o / / bdag yod ces bya-ba # 'i sgras ni gang-zag #  tu sgro-'dogs-pa # 'i mtha'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni phung-po #  dang khams dang skye-mched #  rnams dang tha-dad-pa # 'am /
avyatiriktam vA vanDyA putra vat asantam AtmAnam dravyataH paSyataH
# tha-dad-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'ang rung ste / / bdag mo-gsham-gyi-bu #  bzhin-du #  rdzas-med-pa # r mthong yang /
pudgalasya AtmanaH vastu rUpa samAropaNam antar
# gang-zag #  la bdag tu dngos-po # 'i ngo bor sgro-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir mtha'o /
nErAtmyam iti apavAda antaH / apavAdaH hi sataH asat parikalpaH iti uktaH
# bdag med ces bya-ba #  ni skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i mtha' ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni yod-pa #  la med-pa # r yongs-su-rtog-pa #  ni skur-pa-'debs-pa #  zhes bya na /
AtmanaH tu asattvAt kaTam nErAtmyam iti apavAda antaH Apadyate iti atas
# bdag ni med-pa # s ji-ltar #  bdag med ces bya-ba #  la skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i mthar 'gyur zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  /
Aha prajQaptisataH api apavAdAt nErAtmyam apavAda antaH iti sambaDyate
# btags-pa'i-yod-pa #  la skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / bdag-med-pa # r skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i mtha' zhes-bya-ba #  dang sbyar ro /
sa punar DarmANAm santAnaH yasmin hetu Pala sambanDaH prajQAyate / samudayaH vA yatra deva manuzya prajQaptiH
# de-yang #  chos-rnams #  kyi rgyun te / / gang-la #  rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  'brel-pa # r mngon-pa # 'o / / yang-na #  spyir gang-du #  lha-dang-mi # r gdags-pa # 'o /
tat parivarjana arTam maDyamA pratipad iti AtmanaH / sat asat tA darSana parivarjana arTam / tasyAH punar yasyAH maDyamAyAH pratipadaH nirUpaNa arTam Aha
# de yongs-su-spang-ba # 'i phyir dbu-ma'i-lam #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni bdag-yod-pa #  dang med-par-lta-ba #  yongs su spang-pa # 'i phyir ro / / da-ni #  dbu-ma'i-lam #  gang-yin-pa #  brtag-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro /
yad AtmanEH AtmyayoH maDyamam iti
# gang bdag dang bdag-med-pa #  de gnyis kyi dbus zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
kim punar tat maDyam / nirvikalpam jQAnam
# de'i dbus ci-zhig #  ce na / / rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes so /
grAhya arTa vikalpasya anta tvam darSayitvA
# gzung-ba # 'i don la rnam-par-rtog-pa #  mtha'o nyid-du #  bstan nas /
grAhaka arTa vikalpasya antatva pradarSana arTam Aha BUtam cittam ityAdi
# 'dzin-pa # 'i don la rnam-par-rtog-pa #  mtha' nyid-du #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / sems yang-dag-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  smos so /
aTavA pudgalasya samAropa apavAda anta tvam darSayitvA Darmasya / samAropa apavAda anta darSana arTam Aha BUtam cittam ityAdi
# yang-na #  gang-zag #  la sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i mtha' bstan nas / / chos la sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i mtha' bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / sems yang-dag-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  smos so /
yaTA pratiBAsate yaTA vA aBilapyate cittam taTA eva BUtam vidyata / iti ayam Darma samAropAntaH aBUtasya citta svaBAva BUta tvena
# sems ji-ltar #  snang-ba #  dang ji-ltar-brjod-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  yang-dag-par #  yod do zhes-bya-ba #  'di ni / / chos la sgro-'dogs-pa # 'i mtha' ste sems kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  la yang-dag-pa-nyid #  du sgro-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
samAropAt / aBUtam cittam iti apavAda antaH
# sems yang-dag-pa #  ma yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i mtha'o /
tasya hi grAhya grAhaka rahita AtmanA niraBilApyena ca vidyamAnam / api aBUtam iti paSyataH sarva AtmanA Darma svaBAva apavAdAt / apavAda antaH
# de ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  dang bral-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  brjod-du-med-pa # r yod kyang med-pa # r mthong-ste #  / / chos-kyi-ngo-bo-nyid #  la rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  skur-pa-'debs-pa # s na skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i mtha'o /
tat parivarjana arTam iti samAropa apavAda rahitasya Darma nErAtmyasya / praviteDa arTam maDyamA pratipad
# de yongs-su-spang-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur-pa-'debs-pa #  dang bral-ba #  la chos-bdag-med-pa # r rtogs-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir / / dbu-ma'i-lam #  ste /
sA yatra nacittam na cetanA na manaH na vijQAnam iti / aBiniveSAH na pravartante iti vAkyaSezaH
# de ni gang-la #  sems med-pa #  dang yid med-pa #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  med-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mngon-par-zhen-pa #  'byung-ba #  med do zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshig gi lhag-ma # 'o /
yatra vA vizaye na cittam sa Asrava vAsanABiH citta Atmakam pravartate na / cetanA aBisaMskAra lakzaNA na manaH manyana AkAram na vijQAnaQca / vikalpanam iyam maDyamA pratipad iti ucyate / tatra cittam AlayavijQAnam sarva srAva Darma vAsanABiH citta tvAt / cetanA manaskarma kuSala akuSala avyAkRtezu citta preraNa karmikA
# yang-na #  yul gang-la #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i bag-chags #  bsags-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  sems mi-'jug-pa #  dang mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyi sems-pa #  med-pa #  dang rlom sems kyi rnam-pa # 'i yid med-pa #  dang rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  med-pa #  'di ni dbu-ma'i-lam #  zhes-bya'o #  / / de-la #  sems ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ste / / zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i chos-thams-cad #  kyi bag-chags #  bsags-pa # 'i phyir ro / / sems-pa #  ni yid-kyi-las #  te / / dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  rnams la sems-'jug-par-byed-pa # 'i las can no /
manaH klizwam manaH / vijQAnam zaXvijQAnakAyAH
# yid ni nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi yid do / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs drug go /
akuSala AdayaH DarmAH saMkleSaH iti vipakzAntaH
# mi-dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  ni / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi mtha'o /
kuSala AdayaH vyavadAnam iti p / pratipakzAntaH
# dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni rnam-pa # r byung-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnyen-po # 'i mtha'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sgras ni /
Adi Sabdena / sAvadyaanavadya lOkika lokottara sAnrava anAsrava saMskRta asaMskRta AdayaH / nirdeSAH sambaDyante / tatra yaTA eva akuSalAH kuSalAH ca DarmAH pratiBAsante aBilapyante ca / taTA eva saMkleSaH vyavadAnaQca iti darSanam vipakzAntaH pratipakzAntaH ca
# kha-na-ma-tho-ba #  dang bcas-pa #  dang 'jig-rten-pa #  dang 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  dang zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa #  dang 'dus byas dang 'dus-ma-byas #  la-sogs-pa #  bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro / / de-la #  dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  ji-ltar #  snang-ba #  dang brjod-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # r lta-ba #  ni / / mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi mtha' dang gnyen-po # 'i mtha'o /
tatra akuSalA akzema arTa tvAt / sAvadyA duScarita samutTApaka tvAt
# de-la #  mi-dge-ba #  ni mi-bde-ba # 'i don to / / kha-na-ma-tho-ba #  dang bcas-pa #  ni nyes-par-spyod-pa #  kun-nas-slong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
lOkikAH viparyasta tvAt / sa Asrave Asrava anuSayita tvAt
# 'jig-rten-pa #  ni phyin-ci-log #  gi phyir ro / / zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  ni zag-pa #  rgyas-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
saMskRtAH pratyaya utpAdi tvAt
# 'dus byas ni rkyen rnams kyis bskyed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tat viparItAH tu kuSala AdayaH veditavyAH / tat parivarjana arTam maDyamA pratipad iti / vipakza pratipakzayoH tad Savadena aBisambanDaH / na maDyamA atra pratipad jQAyate iti atas Aha / yaH syAt tat vayasyA anupagamaH anudAhAraH apravyAhAraH iti
# de-las-bzlog-pa #  ni dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / de yongs-su-spang-ba # 'i phyir dbu-ma'i-lam #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  la / / mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang gnyen-po #  ni de zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra dang sbyar ro / / dbu-ma'i-lam #  mi shes-nas #  / / de'i-phyir #  / / gang mtha' de gnyis khas mi len cing mi brjod mi smra'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tatra anupagamaH vipakza pratipakzayoH anaBiniveSaH
# de khas mi len-pa #  ni mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang gnyen-po #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  med-pa # 'o /
anudAhAraH tasmin vipakza pratipakzA ante parezAm asamAda apanAt / apravyAhAraH vipakza pratipakzAntayoH asaMvarNanAt
# mi brjod-pa #  ni mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang gnyen-po # 'i mtha' de-la #  gzhan dag yang-dag-par #  'dzin du mi-'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro / / mi-smra-ba #  ni mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang gnyen-po #  gnyis mi brjod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tIrTika SrAvaka anta pratipakzeNa maDyamAm pratipadam deSayitvA / boDisattva anta pratipakzeNa maDyamAm pratipadam pratipAdayan= Aha
# mu-stegs-can #  dang nyan-thos #  kyi mtha'i gnyen-po # r dbu-ma'i-lam #  bstan nas / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i mtha'i gnyen-po # r dbu-ma'i-lam #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
asti iti SASvata antaH na asti iti ucCeda antaH tayoH eva pudgala DarmayoH
# gang-zag #  dang chos de gnyis yod do zhes-bya-ba #  ni rtag-pa # 'i mtha'o / / med do zhes-bya-ba #  ni chad-pa # 'i mtha'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
sarvadA sva lakzaNa samArupAt asti iti SASvata antaH
# rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  la rtag-par #  sgro-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir / / yod do zhes-bya-ba #  ni rtag-pa # 'i mtha'o /
sarvaTA svarUpa apavAdAn na asti iti ucCeda antaH
# rang-gi #  ngo bo la rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i phyir med do zhes-bya-ba #  ni chad-pa # 'i mtha'o /
tat parivarjana arTam maDyamA pratipad yat anayoH antayoH maDyam iti / uBaya anta vigamaH atra maDyam aBipretam iti eke
# de yongs-su-spang-ba # 'i phyir dbu-ma'i-lam #  ste / / mtha' de gnyis kyi dbus gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la / / kha-cig #  na re mtha' gnyi-ga #  dang bral-ba #  ni 'dir dbu-ma # r 'dod do zhe'o /
uBaya lakzanam atra dvayoH antayaH maDyam iti apare / kaTam kRtvA
# gzhan dag na re 'di gnyi-ga # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni 'dir mtha'-gnyis #  kyi dbus so zhe'o / / ji lta zhe na /
yaH hi aBUta parikalpa vat DarmaDAtu vat vA jQeyamn aBiDeyam ca vastu / dravyataH paramArTataH ca asti iti aBiniveSaH sa SASvata antaH / tasya tahA asattvAt
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun rtog-pa #  lta-bu # 'am / / chos-kyi-dbyings #  lta-bu # r shes-bya #  dang brjod-par-bya-ba # 'i dngos-po #  rdzas nyid dang don-dam-pa # r yod do zhes mngon-par-zhen-pa #  de ni rtag-pa # 'i mtha' ste / / de ni de-bzhin-du #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tat vA SaSavizANa vat na asti eva iti darSanam ucCeda antaH / kim kAraNam / tasya prajQaptitaH astitvAt
# de-ltar #  ri-bong-gi-rva #  bzhin-du #  med-pa #  nyid-du #  lta-ba #  ni chad-pa # 'i mtha' ste / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na / / de rtag-par #  yod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
atas tat nirAkaraNena ucCeda antaH ucyate
# de-bas-na #  de bstsal-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir chad-pa # 'i mtha' zhes-bya'o #  /
atas ca astitva nAstitvayoH maDyam dravyaH paramArTaH ca nasti / prajQaptitaH asti iti uBaya lakzaNam Bavati
# de'i-phyir #  yod-pa-nyid #  dang med-pa #  nyid kyi dbus rdzas nyid dang don-dam-pa # r med-pa #  la btags-pa # r yod do zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnyi-ga # 'i mtshan-nyid #  yin no /
vipakza pratipakzayoH samAropAntam aDikRtya Aha avidyA grAhyA / grAhakA ca iti antar
# de mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang gnyen-po #  la sgro-'dogs-pa # 'i mtha'i dbang du mdzad de ma-rig-pa #  la gzung-ba # 'o / / 'dzin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni mtha' ste /
evam vidyA saMskArA asaMskRtaQca tat pratipakzaH grAhyam / grAhya paQca iti antar
# de-bzhin-du #  ma-rig-pa #  dang 'du-byed-rnams #  dang de'i gnyen-po #  'dus-ma-byas #  la gzung-ba # 'o / / 'dzin-pa # 'o zhes pa yang mtha' ste /
atra ca yAvat jarA maraNam iti paryanta grahANAt / vijQAna nAma rUpa AdayaH aDyAkzipyante
# 'dir rga shi'i bar la zhes-bya-ba # 'i mtha' smos-pa #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang ming-dang-gzugs #  la-sogs-pa #  yang bsdu'o /
vijQAnam grAhyam grAha kaQcetyantaH
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  la gzung-ba # 'o 'dzin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  yang mtha'o /
evam nAma rUpam zaXa Ayatanam sparSaH vedanA tRzNA upAdAnam BavaH / jAti jarA maraNam grAhyam grAha kaQcA iti antar
# de-bzhin-du #  ming-dang-gzugs #  dang skye-mched-drug #  dang reg-pa #  dang tshor-ba #  dang sred-pa #  dang len-pa #  dang srid-pa #  dang skye-ba #  dang rga shi la gzung-ba # 'o 'dzin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  yang mtha'o /
tatra avidyA satya ratna asaMprakyAna AtmikA / punyA punyA niQja svaBAva cetanA sa punarBAva aBisaMskaraNAt / saMskArAH
# de-la #  ma-rig-pa #  ni bden-pa #  dang dkon-mchog #  mi-shes-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  do / / 'du-byed-rnams #  ni bsod nams dang bsod nams ma-yin-pa #  dang mi g-yo-ba # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  de / / zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i sems-pa # s yang-srid-pa #  mngon-par-'du-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
evam saMkleSa lakzaNa vyAKyAna anusAreNa vijQAna AdayaH api vistareNa / vaktavyAH / vidyA api na Asravam
# de-bzhin-du #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  bshad-pa # 'i tshul du rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yang rgya-cher #  brjod-pa # r bya'o / / rig-pa #  ni zag-pa-med-pa # 'i ye shes so /
saMskArANAm jQAnam eva saMskRtam pratipakzaH
# 'du-byed-rnams #  kyi gnyen-po #  ni 'dus-ma-byas #  kyi ye shes so /
aTa vA anyasmAt asaMskRtAt p / vyavacCeda arTam Aha tat pratipakzaH iti
# de nyid kyi phyir 'dus-ma-byas #  gzhan-las #  dbye-ba # 'i phyir gnyen-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
anye tu anutpattima tvAt asaMskRtam azwaviDam api atra manyante
# gzhan dag ni mi-skye-ba #  can yin-pas #  na / / 'dus-ma-byas #  rnam-pa-brgyad #  car yang 'dir 'dod do /
pratipakzaH tu anAsravA cetanA punar BAvanaBi saMskaraNAt iti
# gnyen-po #  ni zag-pa-med-pa # 'i sems-pa #  ste / / yang-srid-pa #  mngon-pa # r 'du mi-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro snyam-du #  sems so /
tat niroDaH grAhyaH grAhakaH vA iti antar
# de 'gog-pa #  la gzung-ba # 'o 'dzin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  yang mtha' ste zhes-bya-ba #  la /
tat Sabdena vijQAnAt ayaH jarA maraNa paryavasAnAH sambaDyante / niroDaH na vijQAyate kim BAvaH kAraNam vA iti Aha yena tat nAma rUpam / niruDyate iti / kena punar tat nAma rUpam niruDyate
# de zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgras ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  nas rga shi la thug gi bar-du #  sbyar ro / / 'gog-pa #  la yang ngo-bo-nyid #  dam rgyu yin pa mi shes-nas #  / / de'i-phyir #  / / lam gang-gis #  ming-dang-gzugs #  'gag-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / gang-gis #  ming-dang-gzugs #  de 'gag-pa # r 'gyur zhe na /
nAma rUpa pratipakzeNA nAsraveNa mArgeNa / vidyA ca A vidyA ca advayam etat advEDIkAram iti etat eva atra
# ming-dang-gzugs #  kyi gnyen-po #  zag-pa-med-pa # 'i lam gyis so / / rig-pa #  dang ma-rig-pa #  de ni gnyis su med de gnyis su byar med do zhes-bya-ba #  de ni /
sa parivAram mArgaH
# 'dir ye shes 'khor dang bcas-pa #  ste lam mo /
atas ca niruDyate anena iti niroDaH / kaH punar atra antaH / ayam eva grAhya grAhaka aBiniveSaH / kim kAraNam
# de'i-phyir #  'dis 'gag-par-byed-pa # s 'gog-pa # 'o / / de-la #  mtha' gang zhe na / / gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  'di nyid do / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
advaya prakRtizu avidyA Adizu avidyamAna dvaya aDyAropa pravRttavAn
# ma-rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  gnyis med-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  dag la med bzhin-du #  gnyis su sgro-'dogs-pa #  'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro /
evam grAhya grAha kAntaH dviDA kRzNa Sukla pakza Bedena iti
# de-bzhin-du #  nag-po #  dang dkar-po'i-phyogs #  kyi bye-brag #  gis /
tatra kRzNa pakze dvAdaSa Bava aFgAni avidyA yAvat jarA maraNam
# gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # 'i mtha' rnam-pa-gnyis #  so zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  / / nag pa'i phyogs ni ma-rig-pa #  nas rga shi'i bar srid-pa'i-yan-lag #  bcu gnyis so /
evam Sukla pakze api viDi Adi niroDa Bedena dvAdaSa prakAra / eva aviDya aniroDaH yAvat jarA maraNa niroDaH iti
# de-bzhin-du #  dkar-po'i-phyogs #  kyang ma-rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  'gag-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis ma-rig-pa-'gag-pa #  nas / / rga shi 'gag-pa # 'i bar rnam-pa-bcu #  gnyis so /
atra ca niryDyante enAH avidyA AdayaH iti tat pratipakza BUtaH mArgaH eva / niroDa Sabdena uktaH
# de-la #  'dis ma-rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  'gag-pa # r 'gyur-ba # s na / / de'i gnyen-por-gyur-pa #  lam nyid la 'gog-pa # 'i sgrar brjod do /

sA ca na vijQAyate iti atas Aha vidyA cA avidyA ca advayam etat iti
# de-yang #  mi shes te / / de'i-phyir #  rig-pa #  dang ma-rig-pa #  'di ni gnyis su med ces bya-ba #  smos so /

evam saMskArANAm asaMskRtasya ca vijQAnasya tat niroDasya ca yAvat / jarA maraNasya tad niroDasya ca iti vaktavyaH / kA punar atra maDyamA pratipad
# de-bzhin-du #  'du-byed-rnams #  dang 'dus-ma-byas #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang de 'gog-pa #  nas 'gog-pa #  dang rga shi zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  brjod-pa # r bya'o / / 'dir dbu-ma'i-lam #  gang zhe na /
etat eva jQAnam vidyA ca avidyA ca advayam etat avEDIkAram iti na / vidyA utpAdayitavyA nA avidyA niroDayitavyA / na saMskAra AdayaH praheyAH / na tad niroDaH prAptavyaH iti yat evam jQAnam etat avEDIkAram p
# rig-pa #  dang ma-rig-pa #  'di ni gnyis su med de gnyis su byar med-pa # r shes-pa #  de nyid de'i rig-pa #  bskyed-par-bya-ba #  yang med cing ma-rig-pa #  dgag-pa # r byar yang med-pa #  dang 'du-byed-rnams #  spang-bar-bya-ba #  yang med la / / de 'gog-pa #  thob-par-bya-ba #  yang med-pa #  de-ltar #  shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni gnyis su dbyer-med-pa # 'o /

sva para AtmanoH vyAbADa hetu tvAt vA saMkleSaH ucyate

punar kleSa saFkleSasya triDA Beda pradarSana arTam Aha

anantara uktena p / kleSa karma janma saMkleSena pRTak BUta jQeya SUnyatA AdayaH DarmA / jQAna SUnyatA AdiBiH na kriyante / kim kAraNam na kriyante / yasmAt te prakRtyA eva SUnyatA AdayaH iti / prakRtyA eva dRzwi Adi svaBAvAH iti arTaH / kutas etat / atas Aha DarmaDAtoH prakRti asaMklizwa tvAt / atas jQeya SUnyatA AdayaH DarmAH prakRtyA eva SUnyatA AdayaH iti / jQAna SUnyatA AdiBiH na kriyante / yaTAyogam iti ayam atra yaTAyoga arTaH / jQAna SUnyatayA jQeya SUnyatA dRzwi saMkleSena vimuktA virahitA na
# shes-bya #  stong-pa-nyid #  la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  ni bshad ma-thag #  pa'i nyon-mongs-pa #  dang las dang tshe'i kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dag tha-dad-pa # r gyur-pa # 'o / / rang-bzhin-gyis #  stong-pa-nyid #  la-sogs-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / stong-pa-nyid #  shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s stong-pa-nyid #  du mi-byed-pa # 'o / / ci-rigs-par #  zhes-bya-ba #  la / / 'dir rigs-pas #  ni 'di yin te / / stong-pa-nyid #  shes-pa #  shes-bya #  stong-pa-nyid #  lta-ba # 'i kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang mi ldan zhing bral-ba # r mi byed de /

# lta-ba # 'i stong-pa-nyid #  ni bdag-nyid-kyi #  lta-ba # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-bzhin-du #  mtshan-ma-med-pa #  shes-pa # s shes-bya #  mtshan-ma-med-pa #  'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-ma #  rnams dang bral-ba # r mi byed de / / 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-ma # 'i stong-pa-nyid #  ni /
jQAna apraNihitena jQeya apraNihitam na kriyate praNiDAna SUnyatAyAH / prakRtyA eva apraNiDAna lakzaNa tvAt
# bdag-nyid-kyi #  mtshan-ma-med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / smon-pa-med-pa #  shes-pa # s shes-bya #  smon-pa # r mi byed de / / smon-pa # 'i stong-pa-nyid #  ni rang-bzhin-gyis #  smon-pa-med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
jQAna anaBisaMskAreNa jQeya anaBisaMskAraH na kriyate
# mngon-pa # r 'du mi-byed-pa #  shes-pa # s shes-bya #  mngon-pa # r 'du mi-byed-pa # r mi byed de /

# nyon-mongs-pa #  dang las dang tshe'i kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnam-pa #  bdun du phye-ba #  dang shes-bya #  stong-pa-nyid #  la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  kyi nang nas /
DarmANAm yasya Darmasya yena saMkleSa Bedena yogaH sa DarmaH na
# chos gang kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  tha-dad-pa #  gang dang sbyar-ba # r rigs-pa # 'i chos de ni /

# nam-mkha' #  bzhin no /

# mtha' de gnyis yongs-su-spang-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir dbu-ma'i-lam #  ste gang-stong-pa #  nyid rig-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyis #  shes-bya #  stong-pa-nyid #  la-sogs-pa # 'i chos yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi bdag-nyid #  rnams /

# de-bzhin-du #  rig-pa #  yod-pa #  dang de'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  yod-pa #  yang kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  dang bral-ba # r bstan-pa # s / / sgro-btags-pa #  dang bskur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i mtha' spangs-pa #  yin no /

trAsye api kalpaH antar tatas ca trAsyAt Baye api / kim / vikalpaH antaH iti aDikRtam / yatas trAsaH samBavati tat trAsyam ucyate / BIyate asmAt iti Bayam
# skrag-par-bya-ba #  de-la # s 'jigs-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  yang mtha' ste / / gang-la #  'jigs-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  de ni skrag-par-'gyur-ba # 'o zhes-bya'o #  / / de-la # s 'jigs-pa #  byang-ba # s na 'jigs-pa #  ste /
tasmAt yat anizwa Palam tasmin strAsye tasmin= ca Baye yaH vikalpayati / saH antar
# de-la # s mi-'dod-pa # 'i 'bras-bu # 'o / / skrag-par-bya-ba #  de dang 'jigs-pa #  de-la #  gang rnam-par-rtog-pa #  de ni mtha' ste / / ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  /
kaTam iti atas bravIti parikalpita rUpa Adi rasanAt duHKa BIrutayA iti / bAlAH hi parikalpita rUpa AdIn vastutas kalpayitvA teByaH Bayam anizwam / Palam ca kalpayanti
# sdug-bsngal #  gyis khong sngangs pas kun-brtags-pa # 'i gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la skrag-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / byis-pa #  ni kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo bo gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la dngos-po # r kun brtags-nas #  / / de-dag #  la mi-'dod-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  'jigs-pa # r rnam-pa # r rtog go /
tatas ca duHKa BIru tayA teByaH rUpa AdiByaH tat nimitteByaH ca BayAt / trasanti iti
# de'i-phyir #  sdug-bsngal #  gyis khong sdangs [*sdang?] pas / / gzugs la-sogs-pa #  de-dag #  dang de'i mtshan-ma #  rnams kyis 'jigs-shing-skrag-pa # r 'gyur ro /
etasya vikalpa dvaya antasya parivarjana arTam p / citrakara dRzwAntaH
# rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i mtha' de gnyis yongs-su-spang-ba # 'i phyir dpe ri-mo-mkhan #  te / / 'od srungs 'di-lta-ste #  /
tat yaTA kASyapa citrakaraH svayam eva BIzaNam yakza rUpam kRtvA / tasmAt eva BIta srastaH aDomuKaH nipatya sammoham nigacCet / evam eva kASyapa sarva bAla pRTagjanAH svayam eva
# dper-na #  ri-mo-mkhan #  zhig bdag-nyid-kyis #  gnod-sbyin #  gyi gzugs 'jigs 'jigs lta zhig bris nas / / des 'jigs skrag ste / / kha bub tu 'gyel nas brgyal-ba # r gyur-pa #  de-bzhin #  'od srungs byis-pa #  so-so'i-skye-bo #  rnams /
rUpa Sabda ganDa rasa sparSAn kRtvA teByaH saMsAre BrAmyanti na ca tAn / DarmAn yaTABUtam prajAnanti iti
# gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg-pa #  bdag-nyid-kyis-byas-pa #  de-dag #  gis 'khor-ba #  na 'khor yang / / chos de-dag #  yang-dag-pa-nyid #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  rab tu mi shes so zhes 'byung-ba # 'o /
yaTA ca citrakaraH svayaMkRte BIzaNake yakza rUpe miTyA vikalpena
# ji-ltar #  ri-mo-mkhan #  zhig bdag-nyid-kyis #  gnod-sbyin #  gyi gzugs 'jigs 'jigs lta zhig bris pa la log-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa # s /
BUta yakza BAvam aDyAropya tasmAt BItaH sammoham Apadyate
# gnod-sbyin #  gyi dngos-po #  yang-dag-pa # 'o snyam-du #  sgro btags te / / des skrag nas brgyal-ba # r 'gyur-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  /
evam sarve eva bAlAH miTyA vikalpa prasrutAH svayam kRtEH iti vikalpitEH / saMsAre BrAmyante kzaNa avasTA nikAya saBA anavasTita tvAt
# byis-pa #  log-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  la zhugs-pa #  skad-cig #  gi gnas-skabs-thams-cad #  ni / / bdag-nyid-kyis-byas-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  bdag-nyid-kyi #  rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dag gis 'khor-ba #  na 'khor te / / rigs mthun-par #  skad-cig #  kyang mi-gnas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pUrvakaH dRzwAntaH SrAvakAn aDikRtya Ayantu boDisattvAn iti
# dpe snga-ma #  ni nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  las brtsams pa'o / / 'di ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams las brtsams pa'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
SrAvakaH hi SUnyatAyAm akRta paricaya tvAt SUnya tAyAH trasyati
# kha-cig #  na re nyan-thos #  ni stong-pa-nyid #  yongs-su-'dris-pa # r ma-byas-pa # s stong-pa-nyid #  kyis skrag go /
boDisattvaH tu parikalpita Darma vikalpena saMkliSyate
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni kun-brtags-pa # 'i chos la rnam-pa #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  ste /
vikalpa kleSa tvAt iti eke
# rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i phyir ro zhe'o /
na anayoH arTa viSezaH asti api tu varga dvaya vaSAt dvaya aBiDAnam iti anye
# gzhan dag na re 'di gnyis la don-du #  bye-brag #  med mod kyi ris gnyis kyi dbang gis gnyis su brjod do zhe'o /
SrAvakaH SUnyatA trAsAt aDigantavyam na aDigacCati boDisattvaH punar / vikalpita Darma trAsAt iti apare
# gzhan dag na re nyan-thos #  ni stong-pa-nyid #  kyis skrag-pa # 'i phyir rtogs-par-bya-ba #  ma rtogs so / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams ni rnam-par-brtags-pa # 'i chos-kyis #  skrag-pa # 'i phyir ro zhe'o /
pUrvakaH Atma grAha pratipakzeNa ayam punar Darma grAha pratipakzeNa iti kecid / grAhye api vikalpaH antaH grAhake api / vikalpaH antar iti aDikRtam
# kha-cig #  na re snga-ma #  ni bdag-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i gnyen-po # 'o / / 'di ni chos su 'dzin-pa # 'i gnyen-po # 'o zhe'o / / gzung-ba # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  yang mtha'o /
kaTam ete grAhya rUpa AdayaH tat grAhakAH ca vijQAnakAyAH / sva lakzaNataH kAryataH ca gRhyamANAH Atma Adi vat aDyAropita AtmAnaH
# 'dzin-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  yang mtha'o / / gzung-ba #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  dang de-la #  'dzin-pa #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs de-dag #  rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  dang 'bras-bu # s shes-pa # r byar yod-bzhin-du #  / / bdag la-sogs-pa #  dang 'dra-bar #  sgro-btags-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  du ji-ltar #  'gyur zhes /
Bavizyanti iti evam grAhya grAhakayoH vastutas parikalpaH antaH aBipretaH
# de-ltar #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  gnyis la dngos-po # r yongs-su-rtog-pa #  ni 'dir mthar 'dod do /
etasya p / vikalpa dvaya antasya parivarjana arTam mAyA kAra dRzwAntaH d / tat yaTA kASyapa mAyA kAraH puruzaH mAyA kRtam nirmimI iti
# rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i mtha' de gnyis yongs-su-spang-ba # 'i phyir / / dpe sgyu-ma #  bye-ba #  pa ste; 'od srungs 'di-lta-ste #  / / dper-na #  sgyu-ma #  byed-pa # 'i mi zhig gis sgyu-ma #  sprul pa sprul nas /
aTa sa mAyA nirmitaH tam eva mAyA kAram KAdet
# sgyu-ma #  sprul-ba #  des sgyu-ma #  byed-pa #  de nyid zos-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  /
evam eva kASyapa yoga AcAraH BikzuH yat yat eva ArambaNam manaH karoti tat / sarvam asya riktam eva KyAti iti vistaraH
# 'od srungs dge slong rnal-'byor-spyod-pa #  dmigs-pa #  gang-dang-gang #  yid-la-byed-pa #  da dag thams-cad #  de-la #  gsog tu snang ngo zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba # 'o /
kaTam anena evam viDam vikalpa dvaya antam parivarjayanti iti
# ji-ltar #  'dis rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i mtha' 'di gnyis yongs su spong zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  /
atas Aha vijQaptimAtra jQAna kRtam hi arTa aBAva jQAnam
# rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam du shes-pa # s don dngos-po-med-pa # r shes-par-byas-nas #  /
tat ca arTa aBAva jQAnam tat eva vijQaptimAtra jQAnam nivartayati
# don dngos-po-med-pa # r shes-pa #  des kyang rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam du shes-pa #  de nyid rnam-pa # r bzlog go /
arTa aBAve vijQapti asamBavAt iti etat atra sADarmyam iti
# don dngos-po #  med na rnam-par-shes-pa #  mi srid-pa # 'i phyir te / / de-ltar-na #  'di ni 'dir mtshungs so zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
mAyAkAra sTAnIyam vijQapti mAtra tA jQAnam
# sgyu-ma #  byed-pa #  lta-bu #  ni rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam du shes-pa # 'o /
nirmita yakza sTAnIyam arTa aBAva jQAnam
# sprul pa'i gnod-sbyin #  lta-bu #  ni don dngos-po-med-pa # r shes-pa #  ste /
vijQapti mAtra jQAna praBAvita tvAt arTa aBAva jQAnasya / yaTA nirmitaH nirmAtAram Bakzyet evam arTa aBAva jQAnam tat eva / vijQapti mAtra jQAnam Bakzyati / asati arTe vijQaptimAtrasya asaMBavAt arTa upalabDiH vijQaptiH iti / kRtvA / samyaktve api vikalpaH antaH miTyAtve api vikalpaH antaH aDikRtam / nirveDa BAgIya avasTAyAm BUta pratyavekzAm samyaktvena vA / vikalpayataH miTyAtvena vA anta dvayam / kaTam / samyaktvam anAsravAH DarmAH miTyA tvam sa AsravAH / tatra yadi BUta pratyavekzAm samyaktvena eva aDyavasti atyevam
# don dngos-po-med-pa # r shes-pa #  ni rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam du shes-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro / / ji-ltar #  sprul pa byed-pa #  sprul pa zos-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  / / don dngos-po-med-pa # r shes-pa # s kyang rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam du shes-pa #  de nyid zos te / / don-la-dmigs-pa #  ni rnam-par-rig-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # s / / don med na rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam yang med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yang-dag-pa-nyid #  du rnam-par-rtog-pa #  yang mtha'o / / log-pa #  nyid-du #  rnam-par-rtog-pa #  yang mtha' ste / / nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i dus na yang-dag-par #  so-sor-rtog-pa-na #  yang-dag-pa-nyid #  du'am / / log-pa #  nyid-du #  rtogs-pa # 'i mtha'-gnyis #  so / / ji lta zhe na / / yang-dag-pa-nyid #  ni zag-pa-med-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  so / / log-pa #  nyid ni zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  so / / de-la #  gal-te #  yang-dag-par #  so-sor-rtog-pa-na #  dag-pa #  nyid-du #  chags-na #  /
kuSala sa AsravA na BUta pratyavekzA syAt / aTa punar asamyak tva lakzaNam eva evam api miTyAtvam eva upapadyate / trEDAtuka pratisaMyukta kuSala vat iti
# de lta na ni zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i dge-ba #  dang yang-dag-par #  so-sor-rtog-pa # r mi 'gyur ro / / ji ste yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kho-na # 'i snyam na / / de lta yang khams-gsum #  dang ldan-pa # 'i dge-ba #  bzhin-du #  log-pa #  nyid-du #  'gyur te /
etasya anyat vayasya parivarjana arTam kAzWa dvaya agni dRzwAntaH
# mtha' de gnyis yongs su spangs-pa # 'i phyir / / dpe shing gnyis la me 'byung-ba #  de /
tat yaTA kASYapa kAzWa dvayam prati iti agniH jAyate iti jAtaH ca
# 'od srungs 'di-lta-ste #  / / dper-na #  shing gnyis rlung gis drud pa las me byung ste /
samAnaH tat eva kAzWa dvayam dahati
# byung-ma-thag-tu #  shing de gnyis tshig-pa # r byed-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  /
evam eva kASyapa BUta pratyavekzAm pratItya Aryam prajQA indriyam jAyate
# 'od srungs yang-dag-par #  so-sor-rtog-pa #  yod-na #  'phags-pa # 'i shes-rab #  kyi dbang-po #  skye ste /
jAtam ca tAm eva BUta pratyavekzAm dahati iti
# skyes ma-thag-tu #  yang-dag-par #  so-sor-rtog-pa #  nyid tshig-pa # r byed do zhes 'byung ngo /
ama mAtra arTaH yaTA kAzWa dvayAt anagni lakzaNAt agniH jAyate
# de'i don ni 'di yin te / / dper-na #  me'i mtshan-nyid #  ma-yin-pa #  shing gnyis las me 'byung ste /
jAtaH ca kAzWa dvayam dahati iti / evam eva asaMtattva lakzaNAyAH BUta pratyavekzAyAH samyaktva lakzaNam / Aryam prajQA indriyam jAyate
# byung nas kyang shing gnyis tshig-pa # r byed do / / de-bzhin-du #  yang-dag-pa-nyid #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  ma-yin-pa #  yang-dag-par #  so-sor-rtog-pa #  las / / yang-dag-pa-nyid #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  'phags-pa # 'i shes-rab #  kyi dbang-po #  skye ste /
jAtaH ca tAm eva BUta parati avekzAm dahati / viBAvayati iti arTaH
# skyes nas kyang yang-dag-par #  so-sor-rtog-pa #  nyid tshig-pa # r byed de / / rnam-pa # r 'jig-pa # r byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
sA hi viBAvanAt eva dagDA iva dagDA iti ucyate vikRti darSanAt / iyaQca BUta pratyavekzA sa AsravA api satI samyaktva AnukUlyAt
# rnam-pa # r 'jig-pa #  de-yang #  tshig-pa #  dang 'dra-bar #  byed-pa # s na tshig-pa # r byed ces bya ste / / gyur-pa # r mthong-ba # 'i phyir ro / / yang-dag-par #  so-sor-rtog-pa #  'di zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  yin yang /
BUta pratyavekzeti ucyate iti / vyApRtO= api vikalpaH antar avyApRtO= api
# yang-dag-pa-nyid #  kyi rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'i phyir-yang #  dag-pa # r so-sor-rtog-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # r ston to / / byed-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  yang mtha'o /
vikalpaH antaH iti aDikRtam
# mi-byed-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  yang mtha' ste /
kaTam iti atas Aha jQAnasya budDi pUrvAm kriyAm niHsAmarTyam vA
# ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / ye shes ni blo sngon-du-'gro-ba # s byed-pa # 'am /
kalpayate iti / yadi p
# mthu-med-pa # r rtog-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
jQAnam idam ajQAnam prajahAmi iti avaDArya tat prahANAya pravartata / iti ayam vyApRtO vikalpaH antar
# gal-te #  ye shes 'dis mi-shes-pa #  spong ngo snyam-du #  rtogs-nas #  de spang-ba # 'i phyir 'jug go zhes-bya-ba #  'di ni byed-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i mtha'o /
jQAnasya kzaNika tvAt na prahANa vyApAra kAle saMBavaH
# ye shes ni skad-cig-pa #  yin-pas #  spyod-pa #  byed-pa # 'i dus na mi srid de /
atas ajQAna prahANasya niHsAmarTyam tiyayam avyApRtO vikalpaH antar
# de-bas-na #  mi-shes-pa #  spang-ba # 'i mthu med do zhes-bya-ba #  'di ni mi-byed-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i mtha'o /
etasya vikalpa dvaya antasya parivarjana arTam tEla pradyota dRzwAntaH / tat yaTA kASyapa tEla pradyote kRte tamaH anDakAram vigacCati na Kalu
# rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i mtha' de gnyis yongs-su-spang-ba # 'i phyir dpe mar-me #  ste / / 'od srungs 'di-lta-ste #  / / dper-na #  mar-me #  byung na mun-pa #  mun-nag #  thams-cad-med-pa # r 'gyur yang /
punar kASyapa tEla pradyotasya evam Bavati aham sarvam anDakAram / viDamAm iti / api tu Kalu tEla pradyotam pratItya tamaH anDakAram vigacCati iti / evam eva kASyapa jQAne utpanne ajQAnam vigacCati na Kalu punar
# 'od srungs mar-me #  'di-ltar #  bdag-gis #  mun-pa #  mun-nag #  thams-cad #  bsal lo snyam-du #  mi sems mod kyi / / 'on-kyang #  mar-me #  la brten-nas #  mun-pa #  mun-nag #  med-par-'gyur-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  'od srungs ye shes skyes na ni mi-shes-pa #  med-pa # r 'gyur te /
kASyapa jQAnasya evam Bavati aham ajQAnam viDamAm iti / api tu Kalu jQAnam pratItya ajQAnam vigacCati iti / etat uktam Bavati yaTA pradIpaH vyApAra SUnyaH
# ye shes ni 'di snyam-du #  bdag-gis #  mi-shes-pa #  bsal lo snyam-du #  mi sems mod kyi / / 'on-kyang #  ye shes la brten-nas #  / / mun-pa-med-pa # r 'gyur ro zhes 'byung-ba # 'o / / 'di-skad-du #  bstan-pa # r 'gyur te /
tamaH anDakAra vyudAsa aBiprAya rahitaH ca punar yasmin pradeSe kriyate
# dper-na #  mar-me #  ni byed-pa # s stong zhing mun-pa #  mun-nag #  bsal-ba # r bsam-pa #  med kyang /
tasmAt pradeSAt pradIpa sattA mAtreNa sarvatamaH anDakAram vigacCati iti
# phyogs dang du byung-ba # 'i phyogs der mar-me #  yod-pa #  tsam gyis mun-pa #  mun-nag #  thams-cad-med-pa # r 'gyur ro /
evam eva yasmin santAne nirvikalpam jQAnam utpadyate tat / sattA mAtra sadBAvAt eva tasmAt santAnAt ajQAnam vigacCati / jQAnasya nirvikalpa tvAt kriyA arTa iti / evam jQAnasya vyApAra aBAvAt sAmarTya aBAvAt sAmarrTya aBAvaH / pradIpa vat sattA mAtreNa pratipakza nirAkaraNAt iti / ajanmatve api vikalpaH antar sama kAla tve api
# de-bzhin-du #  rgyud gang-la #  rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes skyes-pa # r gyur na de yod-pa #  tsam gyis rgyud de-la # s mi-shes-pa #  med-pa # r 'gyur te / / ye shes ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  dang dpyod-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-ltar #  ye shes ni byed-pa # 'i mthu med la / / mar-me #  bzhin-du #  yod-pa #  tsam gyis mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  sel to / / skye-ba #  med-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  yang mtha'o /
vikalpaH antaH iti anuvartate / kaTam iti atas Aha yadi pratipakzasya anutpattim vA kalpayati yaTeya tA
# dus mnyam-pa-nyid #  du rnam-par-rtog-pa #  yang mtha'o / / ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / gal-te #  gnyen-po #  ma-skyes-pa # 'am zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
kAlena na utpanna pUrvaH pratipakzaH taTA idAnIm api na utpatsyate iti ayam / ajanmatve vikalpaH antar
# de-ltar #  dus-ji-srid-du #  sngon gnyen-po #  ma-skyes-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  da yang mi skye'o snyam pa 'di ni skye-ba #  med-pa # r rtog-pa # 'i mtha'o /
saFkleSasya vA dIrGa kAla tvam iti / na hi ajQAne jQAna pratiyoginI avasTitaH eva jQAnam utpattum samarTam / aTa api kaTaQcid utpadyeta taTA api cira kAla virudDa tvAt ajQAnasya na / jQAnena tat kzaNikena vyudAsaH Sakyate kartum
# yang-na #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  yun-ring-ba #  nyid-du #  rtog-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mi-shes-pa #  dang ye shes mi-mthun-par-gnas-pa # s ye shes 'byung-ba # 'i mthu med do / / ji ste brgya-la #  skyes su zin na yang mi-shes-pa #  de yun-ring-po-nas #  gnas gnas-pa # 'i phyir / / ye shes skad-cig-pa #  des bsal-ba # r bya mi nus so /
tatas ca saFkleSa vyavadAnayoH samAna kAla tvam iti / etasya vikalpa dvaya antasya parivarjana arTam dvitIyaH / tEla pradyota dRzwAntaH iti
# de-bas-na #  nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  gnyis dus mnyam-pa-nyid #  do snyam pa'i rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i mtha' de gnyis yongs-su-spang-ba # 'i phyir mar-me # 'i dpe gnyis-pa #  ste /
tat yaTA kASyapa gRhe vA layane vA avacarake vA varza sahasrasya atyayAn / na kenacid tEla pradyotaH kutas Bavati / aTa tatra kaScid eva puruzaH tEla pradyotam kuryAt / tat kim manyase kASyapa api tu tamaH anDa AkArasya evam Bavet / varza sahasra saQcitaH aham na aham atas vigamizyAmi iti / Aha naH Bagavat na hi tamaH anDakArasya SaktiH asti tEla pradyote kRte na / vigantum avaSyam tena vigantavyam
# 'od srungs 'di-lta-ste #  / / dper-na #  khyim mam khang-pa # 'am khang phran lo brgya stong 'das-pa # r sus kyang lan 'ga' yang mar-me #  ma bus pa der mi la-la-zhig #  gis mar-me #  bus na / / 'od srungs de ji snyam-du #  sems / / mun-pa #  mun-nag #  de 'di-ltar #  bdag ni lo brgya stong du bsags-pa #  yin te / / bdag 'di-nas #  mi 'gro'o snyam-du #  sems sam / / gsol ba bcom-ldan-'das #  mi sems te / / mar-me #  byung na mun-pa #  mun-nag #  la mi mchi ba'i nus-pa #  ma mchis kyi / / gdon mi 'tshal-ba # r ma mchis par 'gyur ro /
BagavAn Aha evam eva kASyapa kalpa Sata sahasra saQcitaH api karma kleSa / ekena yoni SomanaskAreNa vigacCati
# bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis bka'-stsal-pa #  / / 'od srungs de-bzhin-du #  las dang nyon-mongs-pa #  bskal-pa-brgya #  stong du bsags-pa #  yang tshul-bzhin #  yid-la-byed-pa # 'i so-sor-rtog-pa #  gcig gis med-pa # r 'gyur ro /
tEla pradyotaH iti kASyapa p / Aryasya etat prajQA indriyasya aDivacanam
# 'od srungs mar-me #  zhes-bya-ba #  de ni 'phags-pa # 'i shes-rab #  kyi dbang-po # 'i tshig bla dags so /
tamaH anDakAraH iti Sabalasya etat karma kleSasya aDivacanam iti
# 'od srungs mun-pa #  mun-nag #  ces bya-ba #  ni las dang nyon-mongs-pa # 'i tshig bla dags so zhes 'byung-ba # 'o /
nidarSanena pratipakzasya anutpattim pariharati pratyaya pratibudDa tvAt tat / utpatteH saFkleSa tulya kAla tAQca
# de-lta-bas-na #  'dis ni skye-ba #  rkyen las rag-las-pa # 'i phyir gnyen-po #  mi-skye-ba #  dang kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i phyogs dang dus mnyam-pa-nyid #  kyi lan-btab #  pa ste /
kRzNa pakzasya durbala tvAt balavat tvAn ca tat pratipakzasya / tamaH anDakAra pradIpa vat iti / uktAnta dvaya varjane pratipattiH / viSIzwA ca aviSizwA ca pratipattiH / anta dvaya varjana pratipatteH anantaram viSizwA ca aviSizwA ca pratipattiH / uddizwA iti atas anta dvaya varjana pratipatti nirdeSa anantaram pRcCati viSizwA / ca aviSizwA ca pratipattiH kaTam eti / atas Aha / viSizwA ca aviSizwA ca jQeyA daSasu BUmizu
# nag-po'i-phyogs #  stobs chung zhing gnyen-po #  de stobs-dang-ldan-pa # 'i phyir mun-pa #  mun-nag #  dang mar-me #  bzhin no / / mtha'-gnyis #  spangs-pa #  sgrub-pa #  bshad-zin #  to / / mtha'-gnyis #  spangs-pa #  sgrub-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  khyad-par-can #  dang khyad-par-med-pa #  sgrub-pa #  smos-pa # s / / de'i-phyir #  mtha'-gnyis #  spangs-pa #  sgrub-pa #  bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  khyad-par-can #  dang khyad-par-med-pa #  sgrub-pa #  gang zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang de'i-phyir #  / / khyad-par-can #  dang khyad med ni /
tAsu daSasu BUmizu ekEkaSas dvi prakArA api pratipattiH
# sa bcu dag tu shes-pa # r bya / / zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so / / sa bcu po de-dag #  re-re #  la yang sgrub-pa #  rnam-pa #  gnyi-ga # 'o /
kaTam iti atas Aha yasyAm BUmO yA pAramitA atirikta tarA Bavati iti
# ji lta zhe na de'i-phyir #  / / sa gang-la #  pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  gang-gi #  shas-che-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  rgya-cher #  smos so /
vistaraH / yasyAm boDisattva BUmO vyavasTitaH boshi sattvaH yasyAm pAramitAyAm / ADikyena prayujyate sA tasyAm boDisattva BUmO= itarAByaH / pAramitA eByaH atirikta tarA Bavati iti viSizwA ucyate
# byang-chub-sems-dpa'i-sa #  gang-la #  gnas-pa # 'i byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  gang-la #  lhag-par-spyod-pa #  de ni / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  sa de-la #  pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  / / gzhan dag-pa # s shas-cher #  gyur-pa # s na khyad-par-can #  zhes bya ste /
tat yaTA praTamAyAm BUmO dAna pAramitA atirikta tarA Bavati iti
# 'di-ltar #  sa dang-po #  la sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  shas-che-ba #  yin te /

# de-la #  sgrub-pa #  khyad-par-can #  zhes-bya'o #  /

# de-bzhin-du #  sa bcu pa la ye shes kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o /
aviSezeNa SezAsu sarvAsu pAramitAsu tasyAm BUmO samudAgacCati iti / tAsu pratipattiH aviSizwa ucyate
# sa de-dang-der #  pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  lhag-ma #  thams can la yang / / khyad-par-med-pa # r yang-dag-par-sgrub-pa #  ni de-dag #  la sgrub-pa #  khyad-par-med-pa #  zhes bya ste /
yaTA uktam pramuditAyAm BUmO dAnapAramitA atirikta tarA Bavati iti / na ca SezAsu na samudAgacCati yaTAbalam yaTABAjamAnam iti
# ji-skad-du #  sa rab-tu-dga'-ba #  la sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i shas-che-ba #  yin te / / lhag-ma #  rnams kyang ci-nus #  kyi 'os su yang-dag-par #  mi sgrub-pa #  ma yin no zhes gsungs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
evam SezAsu BUmizu yaTA sUtram nirdeSaH veditavyaH / uktam pratipattya anuttaryam / Alambana anuttaryam p / idAnIm Alambana anuttaryam nirdeSa avasaraH iti atas Aha
# de-bzhin-du #  sa lhag-ma #  rnams la yang mdo las ji-skad #  bshad-pa #  bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / sgrub-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  nyid bshad-zin #  to / / da-ni #  dmigs-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  nyid bshad-pa # 'i skabs su bab ste /

# chos rnam-pa # r khong-du-chud-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni sa de nyid na mdo la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-kyi-mtshan-ma # 'i rnam-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  dang bral pa'i sgo nas chos rnam-pa # r khong-du-chud-pa # s na rnam-pa # r khong-du-chud-pa # 'o / / de nyid ni bsgom-pa'i-lam #  zhes bya ste / / sa bdun pa nyid-du # 'o / / rnam-pa # r khong-du-chud-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni / / rnam-pa # r khong-du-chud-pa # 'i dmigs-pa # 'o / / bcu gcig pa ni sa brgyad pa la'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / mtshan-ma #  dang 'bad-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  thams-cad #  dang bral nas rang-gi #  tshul-gyis #  rnal du 'dug-pa # s 'jug-pa # 'i phyir te / / bsgom-pa'i-lam #  de-nyid-la #  rnal du 'dug-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / rnal du 'dug-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni / / rnal du 'dug-pa # 'i dmigs-pa # 'o /

# dmigs-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  nyid bshad-zin #  to / / da-ni #  yang-dag-par-'grub-pa #  bra na med-pa #  nyid kyi skabs su bab-pa # s de bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
samudAgamaH katamaH iti
# yang-dag-par-'grub-pa #  gang zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
tayA tayA pratipattyA samudAnIyate iti samudAgamaH
# sgrub-pa #  de-dang-de # s yang-dag-par-'grub-pa # s na yang-dag-par-'grub-pa # 'o /
tat anyeByaH samudAgameByaH viSizwa tvAt tatas ca anyasya samudAgamasya / viSizwa aBAvAt Anuttaryam ucyate / tat pradarSana arTam Aha / avEkalyA apratikzepaH vikzepaH ca prapUraNA / iti vistaraH
# de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i yang-dag-par-'grub-pa #  rnams las khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  dang yang-dag-par-'grub-pa #  khyad-par-can #  de-la # s gzhan med-pa # 'i phyir bla-na-med-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / de bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / ma tshang med dang mi spong dang / / mi g-yeng ba dang rab rdzogs dang /
tatra pratyayO= Ekalyam AraBya yAvat boDi sandarSanam iti eza daSaviDaH / samudAgamaH
# zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so / / de-la #  rkyen ma-tshang-ba-med-pa #  nas brtsams te / / byang-chub #  kun du ston-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  rnam-pa-bcu-po #  de-lta-bu #  ni yang-dag-par-'grub-pa # 'o /
tatra pratyayO= Ekalyam gotra samudAgamaH iti / pratyayAnAm avEkalyam samagrANAm sAnniDyam
# de-la #  rkyen ma-tshang-ba-med-pa #  ni rigs yang-dag-par-'grub-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la / / rkyen rnams ma-tshang-ba-med-pa #  ni thams-cad #  tshogs-pa # 'o /
tezu AhRtezu gotram samudAgaccyati sPItam tat viSizwataram / Bavati iti arTaH
# de-dag #  tshogs na rigs yang-dag-par #  'grub ste / / rgyas-pa #  dang khyad-par-can #  du 'gyur zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
tat punar sat puruza saMsevA sadDarma SravaNam yoniSas manaskAraH iti evam / AdayaH
# de-yang #  skyes-bu-dam-pa #  la brten-pa #  dang dam-pa'i-chos-nyan-pa #  dang tshul-bzhin #  yid-la-byed-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
tezAm tat gotra mitra Adi vEkalyAt vEkalyam
# rigs dang bshes-gnyen #  la-sogs-pa #  de-dag #  ma-tshang-ba # 'o /
mahAyAna apratikzepaH aDimukti samudAgamaH iti / yadi gAmBIrya OdArya lakzaNa mahAyAna Darmam na pratikzipati evam asya
# theg-pa-chen-po #  mi-spong-ba #  de ni mos-pa #  yang-dag-par-'grub-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / gal-te #  zab cing rgya-che-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  theg-pa-chen-po # 'i chos mi spong na /
niScayasya DAraNA AtmikAyAH aDimukteH puzwiH Bavati
# de lta na de'i nges-par-'dzin-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  mos-pa #  rgyas-pa # r 'gyur ro /
hIna yAna avikzepaH citta UrpAda samudAgamaH iti
# theg-pa-dman-pa # r mi g-yeng ba ni sems-bskyed-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'gyur-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
yat utpAdita boDi cittasya satsu api boDi citta vyAvRtti pratyayezu / SrAvaka yAne pratyekabudDa yAne vA cittam asya na krAmati evam asya tat
# gal-te #  byang-chub #  tu sems bskyed la / / byang-chub #  kyi sems las ldog-pa # 'i rkyen yod-du-zin-kyang #  / / nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa # 'am / / rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi theg-pa # r des sems mi 'jug na /
boDi cittam puzwim Apadyate
# de lta na byang-chub #  kyi sems de brtas-pa # r 'gyur ro /
pAramitA paripUraNA pratipatti samudAgamaH iti
# pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa #  ni 'grub-pa #  yang-dag-par-'grub-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
utpAdita boDi cittAnAm tad vaSAt dAna Adi pAramitAnAm paripUryA / sarvajQa tA pratipatti puzwiH Bavati
# byang-chub #  kyi sems-bskyed-pa #  dag de'i dbang gis sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # s thams-cad-mkhyen-pa-nyid #  sgrub-pa #  rgyas-pa # r 'gyur ro /
Arya mArga utpAdaH nyAm avakrAnti samudAgamaH iti
# 'phags-pa'i-lam #  bskyed-pa #  ni / / skyon-med-pa # r 'jug-pa #  yang-dag-par-'grub-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
praTamatas eva apUrvasya Arya mArgasya utpAdaH nyAm avakrAntiH Bavati
# thog-ma #  nyid-du #  sngon ma-skyes-pa # 'i 'phags-pa'i-lam #  bskyed-pa # s skyon-med-pa #  la 'jug-pa # r 'gyur ro /
AmaH ucyate dozaH kzayaH vA / sa yatra na asti sA nyAmA nivAta vadana AsravAH BUmiH / nyAm AyAma vakrAntiH nyAm avakrAntiH praveSaH iti arTaH p / niyama avakrAnti pAWe api niyamaH eva niyamaH / taTA hi utpanna darSana mArgaH niyataH Bavati sugatO nirvANe ca iti
# skyon zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyes-pa # 'am zag-pa #  ste / / gang na de med-pa #  de ni skyon-med-pa #  ste / / rlung med-pa #  bzhin te zag-pa-med-pa # 'i sa'o / / nges-par #  'jug-pa #  zhes 'byung-ba #  yang nges-pa #  nyid nges-pa #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  mthong-ba'i-lam #  skyes na / / bde-'gro #  dang mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  nyid-du #  nges-par #  'gyur ro /
kuSala mUla nirUXiH dIrGa kAla paricayAt sattva paripAka samudAgamaH iti / labDa darSana mArgANAm tat pRzWa labDasya BAvanA mArgasya
# dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba 'phel-ba #  ni yun-ring-po-nas #  'dris-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir / / sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-pa #  yang-dag-par-'grub-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni mthong-ba'i-lam #  thos-nas #  /
dIrGa kAla paricayAt aByAsAt kuSala mUla vRdDiH kuSala mUla nirUXiH
# de'i-rjes-la # s thob-pa #  bsgom-pa'i-lam #  la yun-ring-por #  'dris-pa # r byas goms-par-byas-pa # s / / dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba 'grub-pa #  ni dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba 'phel-ba # 'o /
tayA sattva paripAcana samarTaH Bavati
# des sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-nus-pa # r 'gyur te /
atas kuSala mUla nirUXiH sattva paripAka samudAgamaH
# de'i-phyir #  dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba 'phel-ba #  ni / / sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-pa # r yang-dag-par-'grub-pa # 'o /
anye tu AhuH evam asya sattva paripAkaH samudAgataH BavatiH yadi anena
# gzhan dag na re de'i sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-pa #  yang-dag-par-'grub-pa #  ni 'di-lta-bu #  yin te / / 'di-ltar #  'dis yun-ring-po-nas #  goms-par-byed-pa #  la brten-nas #  /
dIrGa kAla aByAsam Agamya sattva santAnezu kuSala mUlam dRXIkRtam
# sems-can #  rnams kyi rgyud la dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba brtan-po # r byas-pa # r 'gyur-pa # 'o zhes zer ro /
citta karma jQa tA kzetra pariSudDi samudAgamaH iti
# sems-las-su-rung-ba #  ni zhing yongs-su-dag-pa #  yang-dag-par-'grub-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
evam BAvanayA vivRdDa kuSala mUlAnAm eka Ayatana mArga vipakzayoH / nimitta ABogayoH vigamAt cittasya karma jQa tA / yat karma jQa tA ADipatyena yaTecCam sPawika Adi mayam budDakzetram / darSayati atItyaH citta karmaNya tA kzetra pariSrudDi samudAgamaH / yAnAm uttara piNxa arTaH p / yAnAn uttarasya piNXa arTaH iti pUrvam piNXa arTa AKyAna prayojanam ucyate / samAsatas triviDam Anuttaryam iti vyAsataH anantam iti / pratipattiH yat uktam / Anuttaryam prapattO hi / pratipatti ADAraH yat uktam / punar Alambane iti / pratipatti Palam yat uktam / samudAgamaH uddizwam iti / sA ca pratipattiH yAdRSI paramA iti / paramA dvAdaSa AtmikA / iti uktam / yena iti / yaTAprajQaptitaH Darma mahAyAna manaskriyA p / iti evam AdinA iti / boDisattvasya satatam prajQayA tri prakArayA / iti vacanAt / taTA ca / saMyuktA Darma caritEH sA jQeyA daSaBiH punar iti / yaTA yena prakAreNA avikzepa pariNatA ca SamaTa BAvanayA iti / zaXviDa vikzepa aBAvAt / aviparyAsa pariNatA ca vipaSyana aBAvanayA iti vyaQjana Adizu daSasu / viparyAsa aBAvAt / yat arTaQca maDyamayA pratipadA niryANa arTam iti anta dvaya varjane / pratipattiH / yatra ca iti yAsu / daSasu BUmizu / kim iti atas Aha / viSizwA ca aviSiztA ca iti / aviparyAsAnAm piNXa arTaH / punar vyaQjanA viparyAsena SamaTa animittam prativiDyati iti / saMyoga svaBAva vigatam sAkzAt karoti / arTa aviparyAsena vipaSyana animittam dvayam api BrAnti mAtra tvena / prativiDyati / manaskAra aviparyAsena viparyAsa nidAnam Alaya vijQAna Ahitam / dvaya aBiniveSa bIjam parivarjayati / aviasAra aviparyAsena viparyAsa nimittam mAyA Adi vat / sat asat tva anaBiniveSena saMgRhItam karoti / sva lakzaNa aviparyAsena tat pratipakzeNa avikalpam aBilApa rahitam / Darma sva lakzaNa vizayam mArgam BAvayati / sAmAnya lakzaNa aviparyAsena vyavadAna prakRtim sarva Darma sAmAnya tayA / prativiDyati / aSudDi SudDi manaskArA viparyAsena tad AvaraNa prahINa aprahINa tAm

 la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # s de'i gnyen-po #  rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  brjod-pa #  dang bral-ba #  chos kyi rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  kyi yul la-la # m bsgom-pa #  dang spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # s chos-thams-cad #  spyir rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i rang-bzhin #  du rtogs-pa #  dang ma-dag-pa #  dang dag-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # s de'i sgrib-pa #  ma-spangs-pa #  dang spangs-pa # r rab tu shes te /
prajAnAti prakRti praBAsvarasya Darma DAtoH Agantu kopa kleSa klizwa tvAt
# chos-kyi-dbyings #  rang-bzhin-gyis #  'od-gsal-ba #  la glo-bur #  gyi nyon-mongs-pa # s nye-bar-nyon-mongs-pa # r gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tadA Agantuka tva aviparyAsena saMkleSa vyavadAnam prajAnAti iti / prakRti praBAsvarasya anyaTA saMkleSasya vyavadAnasya ca asamBavAt / atra asAnunnati aviparyAsena pudgala Darma anaBiniveSataH nirAvaraNaH / niryAti iti / samAptA ca iyam Agama anusAriNI maDyAnta viBAgawIkA
# de'i glo-bur-du #  byung-ba #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # s kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba #  bzhin rab-tu-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / rang-bzhin-gyis #  'od-gsal-ba #  la gzhan-du-na #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # r 'gyur mi srid-pa # 'i phyir ro / / mi-skrag-pa #  dang khengs-pa #  med-pa #  la phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # s / / chos dang gang-zag #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  med de / / sgrib-pa-med-pa # r nges-par-'byung-ba # 'o / / bstan-bcos #  dbus dang mtha' rnam-par-'byed-pa #  las / / theg-pa #  bla-na-med-pa # 'i le'ur bcad-pa #  lnga'i 'grel bshad de / / slob-dpon #  blo brtan gyis mdzad-pa #  rdzogs so /
